40001001	Chitabu cho lukolo lwa Yesu Kilisito, imwana wa Daudi, imwana wa Ibulahimu.
40001002	Ibulahimu hakamweleka Isaka, Isaka hakamweleka Yakobo, Yakobo hakamweleka Yuda na Wanduguse,
40001003	Yuda hakamweleka Pelesi na Sela kwa Tamali, Pelesi hakamweleka Esilomu, Esilomu hakamweleka Alamu,
40001004	Alamu hakamweleka Aminadabu, Aminadabu hakamweleka Nashoni, Nashoni hakamweleka Salimoni,
40001005	Salimoni hakamweleka Boasi kwa Lahabu, Boasi hakamweleka Obedi kwa Lusi, Obedi hakamweleka Yese,
40001006	Yese hakamweleka Mundewa Daudi. Daudi hakamweleka Sulemani kwe muke wa Uliya,
40001007	Sulemani hakamweleka Lehoboamu, Lehoboamu hakamweleka Abiya, Abiya hakamweleka Asa,
40001008	Asa hakamweleka Yehoshafati, Yehoshafati hakamweleka Yolamu, Yolamu hakamweleka Usiya,
40001009	Usiya hakamweleka Yosamu, Yosamu hakamweleka Ahasi, Ahasi hakamweleka Hesekia
40001010	Hesekia kamweleka Manase, Manase kamweleka Amoni, Amoni hakamweleka Yosia,
40001011	Yosia hakamweleka Yekonia na wanduguse, ugele wo kusanyiligwa Babeli.
40001012	Kusanyiligwa Babeli kukahele, Yekonia hakamweleka Shelitieli, Shelitieli kamweleka Selubabeli,
40001013	Selubabeli hakamweleka Abihudi, Abihudi hakamweleka Eliyakimu, Eliyakimu hakamweleka Asoli,
40001014	Asoli hakamweleka Sadoki, Sadoki hakamweleka Akimu, Akimu hakamweleka Eliudi,
40001015	Eliudi hakamweleka Eliesa, Eliesa hakamweleka Matani, Matani hakamweleka Yakobo,
40001016	Yakobo hakamweleka Yusufu, mulume wa Maliamu yamweleke Yesu yekwinangigwa Kilisito.
40001017	Hambiya, ifyeleko fyose kulawa Ibulahim mpaka Daudi hafyuwa fyeleko ikumi na fine, na kulawa Daudi mpaka kusanyiligwa Babeli fyeleko ikumi na fine; na kulawa kusanyiligwa Babeli mpaka Kilisito hafyuwa fyeleko ikumi na fine.
40001018	Kwelekigwa kwa Yesu Kilisito hakuwa nhafi; Maliamu ing'ina ugele woyowile katumisigwa na Yusufu, ugele wasinati wakitole, hakoneka kena inda kwa udaha wa Muhe Musunhile.
40001019	Na Yusufu, kosoko hakowa munhu wechawelu nghendile kumuguma chinyala, hakona yamuleke chinyelenyele.
40001020	Hambiya, ugele foyendeyodoga aso; langa, malaika we Mundewa hakamwijila musinjosi, yakugamba, “Yusufu gomwana wa Daudi, unghogohe kumulonda Maliamu imukago, kosoko iinda yakwe ni kwa udaha wa Muhe Musunhile.
40001021	Naye yakwenda yeleke mwana, nagwe komwinanga disina dyakwe Yesu, kosoko imwene noyakwenda yawahonye awanhu wakwe na uwihi wawo.”
40001022	Ago gose ganheifo, uleke imbuli iya iyalongigwe ne Mundewa kwa njila ye inonga ye mugonesi yagambile,
40001023	“Langa bikila yakwinula inda, naye yakwenda yeleke mwana. Nawo wakwenda wamwinange disina dyakwe Imanueli” (nong'amba, “Imulungu kahamwedu nase”).
40001024	Yusufu yakenuke musinhongo hakagolosa nheifiya fina foyalongile imalaika we Mundewa. Hoyomutola.
40001025	Nghagendile naye ka, mpaka yakweleka imwanagwe; kamwingha disina dyakwe Yesu.
40002001	Mundewa Yesu foyelekigwa Betelehemu ku iisi ya Uyahudi ugele we Mundewa Helode, langa, mamajusi wa ulwandi lwa kundawilo ye dijuwa, haweja Yelusalemu wakugamba,
40002002	“Kowa hoki iMundewa wa Wayahudi yelekigwe? Kosoko hachiyona inyelesi yakwe kundawilo yedijuwa, nase chija, uleke chimufugamile.”
40002003	Kamei Mundewa Helode yakahulike nheifo, hakasinanghala, na wanhu wose wa Yelusalemu hamwedu naye.
40002004	Hoyokwinanga ifilongosi wose wa makuhani, na watulumi yawosa fina, “Kilisito yakwelekigwa hoki?”
40002005	Nawo howomugamba, “kuBetelehemu ya Uyahudi; Kosoko nofo itulumigwe ne Mugonesi,
40002006	‘Nagwe Betelehemu muisi ya Yuda, mu wakulu wa Yuda, iyakwenda yawadime wanhu wangu Isilaeli.’”
40002007	Kamei Helode hoyowenanga awaya mamajusi hanghanda, hoyopata ichawelu kulawa fowakongile kuyona inyelesi iya.
40002008	Hoyowegala Betelehemu, hoyogamba, “Yandamileni injila ino, mkosilise lugano simbuli se mwana yuyo, munghafulusa kumona munitamile uleke nani nilute nikamufugamile.”
40002009	Nawo wakahulike simbuli, se Mundewa, howolongosa injila, kamei inyelesi iya yowonile kundawilo ye dijuwa hoiwalongolela, hoikwima ahanhu hoyowile imwana.
40002010	Fowayonile inyelesi iya hawowa na chinyemi chikulu lugano.
40002011	Howokwingila kugati, howomwona imwana hamwedu na Maliamu ing'ina, howomusegelela, howomufugamila, wakamale kudohola sihasina sawo, howomulafila simhongesi sawo, sahabu, ufumba, na manemane.
40002012	Nawo wakamale kutamiligwa na Mulungu musinjosi wanghamuwile Helode; howogenda njila ingi.
40002013	Awaya wakafuluse kuleuka, kamei imalaika we Mulungu hoyomwijila Yusufu musinjosi, hakagamba, “Leuka, umulonde imwana hamwedu ne ing'ina, utijile Misili, wikale uko mpaka nikutamile, kosoko Helode yakuhananga yamulangise imwana uleke yamukome.”
40002014	Hakenuka, hoyomulonda mwana ne ing'ina nechilo; hoyoluta Misili;
40002015	hoyokwikala uko mpaka foyafile Helode; uleke yoneke fina chawelu imbuli yalongigwe ne Mundewa kusimbuli salongigwe na wagonesi wagambile, “Kulawa Misili hanimwinanga imwanangu.”
40002016	Helode yakone kadanhilisigwa na waya mamajusi, hakasuha lugano; hoyotuma wanhu hoyowakoma awana we chigosi wose, awoile ako Betelehemu, ne filunga fyose fikihakane na Betelehemu, kukongela wana we minyaka mili mpaka awasinati wafike minyaka mili, kwandamila fowalongile awaya mamajusi.
40002017	Hoiliganila imbuli yoyalongile imugonesi Yelemia.
40002018	“Chililo chihulikika Lama, Laheli yakuwalilila wanagwe, kosoko wahechaka.”
40002019	Kamei Helode yakafe, noho malaika we Mundewa yamwijila Yusufu musinjosi uko Misili,
40002020	yakugamba, “Handiko leuka, umulonde imwana ne ing'ina, ulute mpaka kuisi ya Isilaeli; kosoko awahanange ichidoga che imwana wafulusa kufa.”
40002021	Yaleuka na kumulonda imwana hamwedu ne ing'ina, howoluta mpaka iisi ya Isilaeli.
40002022	Yakahulike fina Alikelao yakudima ako Uyahudi ahanhu ha Helode iBabakwe, yaluta ulwandi lwa Galilaya,
40002023	Hakaluta, hakekala mukaya yendeikwinangigwa Nasaleti; Uleke iliganile imbuli yoyalongile imugonesi “Kokwinangwa Munasalayo.”
40003001	Mumajuwa gago yalawanisa Yohana mubatisaji yakuhubili munyika ya Uyahudi, yakugamba,
40003002	“Mulambe; Kosoko undewa wa kulanga usegelela.”
40003003	Kosoko ayo no yalongigwe ne mugonesi Isaya, yakugamba, “Dijwi dye imunhu yakujoja mwibalangu, Igoloseni injila ye Mundewa, Musigolole si njila sakwe!”
40003004	Naye Yohana imwecho hakafala suke igolosigwe na singa se ngamia, na mukanda wa nghingo, muchuno chakwe; na chakudiya chakwe hachuwa sige na uuki wa kumbago.
40003005	Weja wamulutila awanhu wose wa Yelusalemu na Uyahudi na si isi sose sisungulute Yolodani;
40003006	Hakawabatisa mulwanda lwa Yolodani, akuno wakulamba u wihi wawo.
40003007	Yakone matewa ga Mafalisayo na Masadukayo, wakwijila ubatiso wakwe, yawagamba, “Anyeye muwana wa majoka nani yamujanjaluseni kutija inyono ikwija?”
40003008	Hambiya, mweleke mamudyo gakonesa kulamba, “Munghakidanhilise mufidoga fyenu fina, china Baba yetu Ibulahimu,” kosoko nikumutamilani fina Mulungu mumawe agano yekudaha kumwinulila Ibulahimu wana.
40003009	Munghakidanhilise mufidoga fyenu fina, china Baba yetu Ibulahimu; kosoko nikumutamilani fina Mulungu mumawe agano yakudaha kumwinulila Ibulahimu wana.
40003010	Inhemo ifulusa kwikigwa hamasina ga mabiki; chila ibiki disikweleka mamudyo maswanu, dikung'enyigwa na kugumigwa mumoto.
40003011	“Chawelu aniye nikuwabatisa na meji kosoko yo kulamba; amba iyakwija kunyuma yangu kena ludole kusuma niye, kahi aniye sikudaha hata kulonda ifilwatu fyakwe; imwene yakwenda yamubatiseni kwa Muhe Musunhile na kwa moto.
40003012	Imwene diselo dyakwe kenadyo mumikono yakwe, naye yakweda yasunhe ahanhu hakwe; ingano yakwe yakuilunda mukano, makohele yakwenda yagasome no moto uusikusima.”
40003013	Ugele uwo Yesu hoyokwija kulawa Galilaya mpaka Yolodani kwa Yohana uleke yabatisigwe.
40003014	Ninga Yohana hoyohananga kumulemesa, yakugamba, “Aniye nikuhananga nibatisigwe na gweye, agweye nagwe ukwija ukwangu?”
40003015	Mundewa Yesu yamubidula yagamba, “Fumila du hambiya; kosoko ikuhanangigwa kwandamila ichelu yose.” Kamei hoyofumila.
40003016	Yesu yakamale kubatisigwa yalawa mulwanda; kamei, ulanga weja wagubuka na kumona, Muhe we Mulungu kifana huwa yakuhumuluka mchanhya yakwe;
40003017	kamei, dijwi kulawa kulanga dikugamba, “Ayuno no Mwanangu, mwendigwa wangu, wonyendesigwe naye.”
40004001	Kamei Yesu hoyolongosingwa na Muhe hoyomwigala kunyika, uleke yagesigwe ne luhoma
40004002	Hoyokwikala bila kudiya majuwa makumi mane chilo ne misi, hoyokona njala.
40004003	Imugesa hoyomwijila hoyomugamba, “Nghonaga gweye no Mwana we Mulungu, gagambe amawe gano gowe mikate.”
40004004	Ninga hoyomubidula hoyogamba, “Itulumigwa fina imunhu nghakudaha kuwa mumi kosoko yo mukate muhala, ninga kwa chila mbuli ikulawa mumulomo we Mulungu.”
40004005	Kamei Luhoma hoyomulonda mpaka ikaya isunhile, hoyomwika kuchisusu chisololoke kuchanhya ye dihekalu,
40004006	hoyomugamba, “Nghonaga gwe no Mwana we Mulungu kilagase hasi; kosoko itulumigwa, Yakwenda yatume malaika wakwe; Wakwenda wakuhokele mumikono yawo; Unghakibulage umugulu wako mwiwe.”
40004007	Yesu yamugamba, “Kahi itulumigwa, ‘Unghamugese Mundewa Mulungu wako.’”
40004008	Kamei Luhoma hoyomulonda mpaka kwitunda ditali lugano, hoyomonesa, undewa wose we chilunga, na uswanu wakwe,
40004009	yamugamba, “Aga gose nikwenda nikwinghe, unghogwa na kunifugamila.”
40004010	Kamei Yesu hoyomugamba, “Halawe, Shetani!” Kosoko itulumigwa, “Umufugamile Mundewa Mulungu wako, umufugamile imwene muhala!”
40004011	Kulawa baho Luhoma hoyomuleka; kamei, howokwija malaika kumutogomela.
40004012	Kamei Yesu yakahulike fina Yohana kohigwa, hakaluta mpaka Galilaya;
40004013	Hakaleuka Nasaleti, hoyejakwikala Kapelinaumu, ikaya yuwile munhika ye bahali muundewa wa Sabuloni na Nafutali;
40004014	uleke iliganile imbuli yalongigwe ne Mugonesi; Isaya yagambile,
40004015	“Iisi ya Sabuloni na iisi ya Nafutali, Injila ye bahali, umwambu wa Yolodani, iGalilaya ya Mataifa,
40004016	Awanhu waya awekale muchisa wona ujelu mukulu, Nawo wekale muisi ya dinyefu dya difa ujelu uwahulumukila.”
40004017	Kulawa ugele uwo Yesu hakakonga kuhubili, na kugamba, “Lambeni, kosoko undewa wa kulanga usegelela.”
40004018	Naye foyendeyogenda munghanda ye bahali ya Galilaya, hakona wandugu weli, Simoni yekwinangwa Petulo ne munduguse Andelea, wakuguma ulwafu lwao mubahali, kosoko hawowa walowaji wa somba.
40004019	Yawagamba, “Munyandamile, nikuhananga niwagolose muwe walowa wanhu.”
40004020	Chimwande howoleka sinyafu sawo, howomwandamila.
40004021	Yogendelela kumwande, yakawona wamonga wandugu weli, Yakobo wa Sebedayo ne munduguse Yohana, wowile mu chiya hamwedu ne Baba yawo Sebedayo, wendewogolosa sinyafu sawo; yawenanga.
40004022	Chimwande howoleka chiya chawo ne Baba yawo howomwandamila.
40004023	Naye yendeyosunguluta Galilaya yose, yakufusa mumasinagogi gawo na kuhubili simbuli siswamu so undewa wa kulanga, na kuwahonya wanhu na matamu gose.
40004024	Simbuli sakwe hosihulikika ako Shamu yose howomwigalila awanhu wose wowile na si nhamu, awowile na sinhamu se hayo hayo ne magayo, wowile na magini, wowile ne chisilisi, na wowile na utamu wa kuholola, hoyowahonya.
40004025	Matewa ga wanhu wengi howomwandamila kulawa Galilaya, Dekapoli, Yelusalemu na Uyahudi na umwambu wa Yolodani.
40005001	Naye yakawone matewa, yakwila kwitunda; yakafuluse kwikala hasi, wefusa wakwe howomwijila;
40005002	Yagubula umulomo wakwe, na kukonga kuwafusa, yakugamba,
40005003	“Ibeka awakiwa mufidoga, Kosoko undewa wa kulanga wawo!
40005004	Ibeka wena usungu; Kosoko wakwenda waholesigwe!
40005005	Ibeka awaholo; Kosoko awene wakwenda wahale iisi!
40005006	Ibeka wena injala na inghilu ya chelu; Kosoko awene wakwenda wegusigwe!
40005007	Ibeka awena ubasi; Kosoko awo wakwenda woneligwe ubasi!
40005008	Ibeka awena mimoyo miswanu; Kosoko awo wakwenda wamone Mulungu!
40005009	Ibeka awalamusi; Kosoko wakwenda wenangigwe wana we Mulungu!
40005010	Ibeka awakugaya kwa kugolosa foyakwenda Mulungu; Kosoko undewa wa kulanga wawo!
40005011	Ibeka anyeye ghona wakwenda wamubeseni na kumugoloselani fibi, na kumulongani, na kumusigani mabuli gehile kwa udasi, kosoko yangu.
40005012	Sekeleleni na kwanga, kosoko digelo dyenu ikulu kulanga. Kosoko nofowawagolosele fibi awagonesi awawalongolele nyeye.”
40005013	“Anyeye no umunyu we chilunga; ninga umunyu unghabanika wogumigwa choni ukolele? Usikunoga ka, isigalila kutagigwa kunje na kujatigwa na wanhu.
40005014	Anyeye no ujelu we chilunga. Ikaya isikudaha kifisa inghowa muchitunda muchanhya.
40005015	Kahi awanhu wasikwasa itaa na kuigubika, ninga wakuika muchigwaso, ikuwamulikila wose awoile munyumba.
40005016	Nheifo ujelu wenu umulike kumwande ya wanhu, uleke wone sinhenda senu si swanu, uleke wamutunye iBaba yenu yowile kulanga.”
40005017	“Munghadoge fina nija nileusa itolati ama awagonesi, ng'o, sijile kuleusa ninga kumemelesa.
40005018	Kosoko chawelu nikumutamilani, mpaka ulanga ne iisi fileuke, chisikuleuka ng'o chinhu chidodogi chimwedu che tolati mpaka gose gamemelesigwe.
40005019	Hambiya imunhu yakubesa dilagiso dimwedu du musino si ndodogi, na kuwafusa wanhu wandamile nheifo yakwenda yenangigwe mudodogi mu undewa wa kulanga, ninga imunhu yekusigolosa na kuwafusa wamonga wandamile nheifo, yakwinangigwa mukulu ku undewa wa kulanga.
40005020	Kosoko nikumutamilani fina uswanu wenu ughaleka kusuma wa watulumi na Mafalisayo, musikudaha kwingila ng'o mu undewa wa kulanga.”
40005021	“Muhulika wanhu wa katali fowagambigwe fina, ‘Unghakome! Na imunhu yanghakoma yowisiligwe.’
40005022	Ninga niye nikugamba chila munhu yakumonela nyono imiyagwe yagila yowisiligwe; na munhu yakuliga imiyagwe, ‘Dibwalata’ yagila yengisigwe mu moto wa majuwa gose.
40005023	Unghegala isadaka yako hokufugila, kamei unghagelegela fina imunduguso kena mbuli na gweye.
40005024	Uileke isadaka yako hadifugilo, ulute, ukakifumilise ne munduguso, noho uye ulafe isadaka yako.
40005025	Kifumilise ne munghondo wako, yanghakwigale kwe mulamusi; ne mulamusi yakwigale ku wasilikali, wakugume kuchifungo.
40005026	Huwila, nikukutamila, nghukulawa mo mpaka ulihe isendi yo ndumo.”
40005027	“Muhulika awanhu wakatali fowagambigwe, ‘Unghagolose dihabwa!’
40005028	Ninga niye nikugamba, ‘Chila munhu yakumulanga imwanamuke kwa kumusulumila, kafulusa kugona naye muchidoga chakwe.
40005029	Digiso dyako dyo kulume dinghakwambusa ugolose wihi ding'ole uditage kutali nagwe, kosoko yagila ichilungo chako chimwedu chagilile, uleke umutufi wako wose unghatagigwe kumoto uusikusima.
40005030	No mukono wako wo kulume unghakuhosa ugolose wihi udumule uutage kutali nagwe, kosoko yagila chilungo chako chimwedu chagilile, uleke umutufi wako wose unghatagigwe jehanamu.’”
40005031	“Kahi igambigwa, ‘Imunhu yanghamuleka imuke yamwinghe baluwa ya malekeni.’
40005032	Ninga niye nikugamba, ‘Chila munhu iyakumuleka imuke, inghowa si kosoko ye dihabwa, yakumugolosa fina yakwingililigwa; ne munhu yakumutola yuya yalekigwe yakuwa kengilila.’”
40005033	“Kahi muhulika wanhu wa katali fowagambigwe, ‘Unghakilahe kwa udasi ninga umugolosele, Mundewa fina foukilahile.’
40005034	Ninga niye nikugamba: Unghakilahe ng'o, kahi kwa ulanga, kosoko no digoda dyo undewa we Mulungu;
40005035	Kahi kwa iisi, kosoko noho yakwika imigulu yakwe, kahi kwa Yelusalemu, kosoko no kaya ye Mundewa mukulu;
40005036	Kahi unghakilahile ditwi dyako, kosoko nghukudaha kulugolosa ulujwili lumwedu luwe lujelu ama lutitu.
40005037	Ninga simbuli senu suwe Heye; heye, si nheifo, si nheifo; sose isikupulutisa sikulawa kwa yuya iyehile.”
40005038	“Muhulika fina igambigwa, ‘Igiso kwa igiso, na igego kwa igego.’
40005039	Ninga niye nikugamba, ‘Munghakikushe ne munhu yehile, ninga imunhu yanghakutowa ifunda yo kulume, mubidusile na ya keli.
40005040	Ne munhu yakuhananga kukusongesa na kukuhoka inghasu yako, mulekele na dijoho nadyo.
40005041	Ne munhu yakukudindilisa utali wa chipisi chimwedu, luta naye fipisi fili.
40005042	Iyakukutasa, mwinghe; iyakuhananga kukopa ukwako, unghamwinghe chigosigosi.’”
40005043	“Muhulika fina igambigwa, ‘Umwende imiyago, umusule imunghondo wako.’
40005044	Ninga niye nikugamba, wendeni awanghondo wenu, muwatasile wakumutendani fibi.
40005045	Uleke muwe wana we Baba yenu iyowile kulanga; kosoko imwene yakwalisa dijuwa dyakwe kuwehile na waswanu, yakuwatonyesela ifula awaswanu na wehile.
40005046	Kosoko munghawenda awakumwendani nyeye mopata igeleko dyaki? Aho awaya awakuhokela ikodi togoleni nawo wasikugolosa nheifo?
40005047	Kahi munghawalamusa awandugusenu du, mugolosa nhenda yaki yongeseke? Aho awanhu wa mataifa wasikuwagolosela fina nheifo!
40005048	Hambiya anyeye mokuwa muliganile fina Baba yenu yowile kulanga foyaliganile.”
40006001	“Langisiseni munghagolose uswanu wenu, mumeso ga wanhu, kosoko mulangigwe na awene, kosoko munghagolosa nheifo mukuswela igeleko kwi Baba yenu iyowile kulanga;
40006002	Hambiya, agweye nghona ukulafa isadaka yako unghakitowele igunda kumwande yako fina wanhu awena chimwefe fowakugolosa mumasinagogi na musinjila, uleke watunyigwe na wanhu.
40006003	Chawelu, nikumutamilani, wafulusa kuhokela digeleko dyawo. Ninga gweye ghona ukulafa isadaka yako, umukono wako wo kumoso unghamanye umukono wo kulume choukugolosa;
40006004	isadaka yako yuwe ku chifiso; Baba iyakona ichifiso yakwenda yakumemese.”
40006005	“Kahi ghona mukutasa, munghowe fina wanhu we chimwefe, kosoko awene wakwenda kutasa wemilenyima mumasinagogi na musinjilamhanda, uleke wonigwe na wanhu. Chawelu, nikumutamilani wafulusa kuhokela digeleko dyawo.
40006006	Ninga agweye nghona ukutasa, ingila kuchaisi unghafulusa kuhinda dibakwa dyako, utase kumwande ye Babako yowile kuchifiso; ne Babako iyakona kuchifiso kokumemelesa.
40006007	Nanye munghowa mukutasa, munghabagebage fina wanhu we chilunga; kosoko awene wakona fina wohulikigwa kosoko ye simbuli sawo fo ni nyingi.
40006008	Ninga anyeye munghowe fina awene, kosoko Baba yenu kamanya gomukuhananga ugele musinati mutase.
40006009	Nanye taseni nhafi: Baba yetu uwile kulanga: Disina dyako ditunyigwe; Undewa wako wije;
40006010	Kwenda kwako kugoloseke. Ahano ha chilunga fina ako kulanga.
40006011	Uchinghe diyelo chakudiya chetu cho kuchigutisa.
40006012	Uchilekelele uwihi wetu fina seye nase fochikuwalekelela awachigolosele wihi,
40006013	Na unghachingise mumagesa, ninga uchihonye na uwihi. Kosoko, undewa ni wako, no ludole, ne ditunyo, majuwa gose hano.
40006014	“Kosoko munghawalekelela wanhu uwihi wawo, ne Baba yenu wa kulanga yakuhananga yamulekeleni na nyeye uwihi wenu.
40006015	Amba munghaleka kuwalekelela awanhu uwihi wawo, na iBaba yenu nghakwenda yawalekelele uwihi wenu.”
40006016	“Kahi fomukufunga, munghowe fina wechimwefe wena fihanga fisinanghale, kosoko yokiyonesa ifihanga fyawo, uleke wonigwe na wanhu fina wafunga. Chawelu nikumutamilani, wafulusa kuhokela digeleko dyawo.
40006017	Ninga agweye nghonaukufunga, ukibake mafuta mwitwi, unawe chihanga;
40006018	Uleke unghoneke na wanhu fina kufunga, ninga iBabako yowile muchifiso yakwenda yakumemese.”
40006019	“Mughakiikile sigafu muchilunga, sinondo ne ikanga fikubana, na wahiji wakubena na kuhija;
40006020	mukiikile sigafu kulanga, kusikubanika chinhu, kwichaka sinondo kahikanga, kahiwahiji wasikubena kahiwasikuhija;
40006021	kosoko isigafu yako hoyuwile, noho umoyo wako houkuwa.”
40006022	“Digiso no taa yo mutufi; digiso dyako dinghowa iswanu, mutufi wako wose ukuwa na ujelu.
40006023	Ninga digiso dyako dinghowa dibanike, umutufi wako wose wokuwa na chisa. Ninga awuya ujelu uwile kugati yako unghowa chisa, chititu tukutuku!”
40006024	“Kwechaka munhu iyekudaha kutogomela wakulu weli; kosoko yekumusula yuno, na kumwenda ayuno, nhagela yekiyandamila nayu, na kumubesa ayuno. Musikudaha kumutogomela Mulungu no ugoli.
40006025	Kosoko iyo nikumutamilani, munghakiidase no uumi wenu, modiya choni, kahi mokunywa choni; kahi imitufi yenu, mufale choni. Uumi si mukulu kujumha chakudiya, no mutufi si mukulu kujumha sisuke?
40006026	Filangeni fidege fya Mulanga, fisikuhanda kahi fisikugola, kahi fichaka kano; ne Baba yenu wa kulanga yekufigutisa. Togoleni! Anyeye si ibeka kujumha ifyene?
40006027	Yehoki ukwenu imwene kwakiidasa yekudaha kiyongesela utali wakwe hata mukono umwedu?
40006028	“Nhani mukiidasile sisuke? Gelegeleni amaluwa ga kumigunda, ifene fo ga kukula; gasikugolosa milimo yoyose, kahigasikubota;
40006029	Nanyeye nikumutamilani, hata Sulemani muditunyo dyakwe dyose nghafasigwe fiswanu kifana dimwedu dyawo.
40006030	Kamei inghowa Mulungu yekugafasa nhaifo amanyagala ga kumbago agebaho diyelo, na nhosiku gakutagigwa kwikusisi, togoleni! Nghodaha lugano kuwafasa nyeye mwina dihuwi dikefu?
40006031	“Munghakiidase mukugamba, Chodiya choni? Ama chokunywa choni? Ama chofala choni?
40006032	Kosoko ago gose awe chilunga wekugahananga; kosoko Baba yenu wa kulanga kamanya fina mukugahananga ago gose.
40006033	Ninga uhanangeni undewa wakwe, no uliganisi wakwe, nago gose mukwenda mongeseligwe.
40006034	Ninga munghakiidase na ganhoosiku, kosoko aganhoosiku gakakiidasila agecho. Leka amagayo ge dijuwa gamemelekele mwijuwa dyakwe.”
40007001	“Munghaliganise, uleke anye nanye munghaliganiswe.
40007002	Kosoko kukuliganisa akuya komukuliganisa nofo nanye mukwenda muliganisigwe. Nacho ichipimo chomukupimila, nocho mukwenda mupimiligwe.
40007003	Nhani ukulanga ichibasi chuwile mwigiso dye munduguso, na dibiki duwile mudigiso dyako gomwecho nghukudyona?
40007004	Kahi komulonga nhani imunduguso, Nileke nileguse ichibasi ichuwile mwigiso dyako; ugele! Mwina dibiki mwigiso dyako go mwecho?
40007005	Kwina chimwefe gweye! Yenda kuleusa dibiki dyuwile mwigiso idyako go mwenecho noho udahe kona fiswamu kuleusa achiya ichibasi mwigiso dye munduguso.
40007006	Munghagenghe mabwa ichinhu chisunhile, kahi munghakubitile silulu senu kumwande ye singuluwe, singheje sisijata ne migulu yawo, hosimubidukilani nyeye, na kumulumani.”
40007007	“Taseni, nanye mokwinghigwa; hanangeni, nanye mokona; gong'ondeni, nanye mokumuliligwa;
40007008	kosoko chila yekutasa, yakuhokela; naye yekuhananga, yakona; naye yekugong'onda, yekukumuliligwa.
40007009	Kahi kwina munhu nani ukwenu imwene imwanagwe yanghatasa mukate komwingha diwe?
40007010	Kahi yanghatasa isomba, komwingha dijoka?
40007011	Inghowa, anyeye mwihile, mumanya kuwengha awana awenu ifinhu fiswanu; togoleni! Si chawelu iBaba yenu wakulanga, yakwenda yawenghe maswanu awakumutasa?
40007012	Gose gomukuhananga mugoloseligwe na wanhu, anyeye nanye muwagolosele nheifo; kosoko ayo no tolati na wagonesi.”
40007013	“Ingileni kwa kugendela umulango umusisili; kosoko umulango mugalamu, ne njila ni ngalamu iikuluta kukwagilila, nawo awekwingila kumulango uwo ni matewa
40007014	Ninga mulango musisili, na injila ilongoka kuumi, nawo awakuyona wakefu.”
40007015	“Kilangisiseni na Wagonesi wo udasi, awanhu awakuwejila wafala suke sa ngholo ninga kugati yawo mausi makali.
40007016	Mowatanga kosoko ye sinhenda sawo. Togoleni! Awanhu wekubawa sabibu mumabiki ge miwa; ama tini mu mibaluti?
40007017	No nheifo chila dibiki diswanu dikweleka mamudyo maswanu, dibiki dihile dikweleka amamudyo gehile.
40007018	Dibiki diswanu disikudaha kweleka mamudyo gehile.
40007019	Chila ibiki idisikweleka mamudyo maswanu dikung'enyigwa na kugumigwa kumoto.
40007020	Hambiya mowatanga kosoko ye sinhenda sawo.”
40007021	“Siyo chila munhu yekunigamba Mundewa, Mundewa, iyakudaha kwingila mu undewa wa kulanga; ninga iyakugolosa ifyene foyakwenda Baba yowile kulanga.
40007022	Matewai wakuhananga weje wanigambe dijuwa diya, Mundewa, Mundewa! Aniye salafile ugonesi kudisina dyako na kugolosa majumo mengi?
40007023	Kamei nikwenda nije niwagambe, Anyeye siwamanyile ka, Halaweni hano, anyeye mukugolosa gehile!”
40007024	“Hambiya chila iyakuhulika simbuli sangu, na kusigolosa, yekuliganisigwa ne munhu iyena misungu, yajengile inyumba yakwe mwiwe.
40007025	Ifula hoitonya, amafaluko hogokwingila mengi, imheho hoitowa, ipumunha inyumba iya, isogwile; kosoko inghindiso yakwe hayuwa mwiwe.
40007026	“Na chila yakuhulika simbuli sangu yanghagolose, yakuliganisigwa ne munhu imubwalasi, yajengile inyumba yakwe mwisanga;
40007027	ifula hoitonya, amafaluko hogokwingila, imheho hoipumunha, hoitowa inyumba iya, hoikugwa, inyugwa yakwe hoikuwa nghulu!
40007028	Kamei, Yesu yakamale simbuli siso, amatewa ga wanhu hogojuma lugano kosoko ya amafuso gakwe;
40007029	kosoko yendeyofusa kifana munhu yena udaha; siyo fina watulumi wawo.”
40008001	Naye foyadulike kulawa kwitunda, matewa mengi hogomwandamila.
40008002	Ulange, hoyokwija imunhu yena ukoma hakamufugamila, na kumugamba, “goMundewa,” unghenda ukudaha kunihonya.
40008003	Yesu hoyogolola umukono wakwe hakamukwafa, hakagamba, “Nikwenda hona.” Baho ni baho ukoma wakwe houhona.
40008004	Yesu hoyomugamba, “Ulangisise, unghamutamile munhu, ulute ukakiyonese kwa kuhani, ukalafe digelo fina foyalongile Musa, uwe uhomelesi ukwawo.”
40008005	Yakengile Kapelinaumu, akida yumonga yamwijila,
40008006	na kumugongelesa yakugamba, “Mundewa imutumishi wangu kagona ukaya, mutamu wa kuholola, yakutamigwa lugano.”
40008007	Yesu yagamba, “Nokwija nimuhonye.”
40008008	Ayuya iakida, yamubidula, yakugamba, “Mundewa, Isinyagile aniye agweye wingile hasi ye ikano yangu; ninga longa mbuli du imutumishi wangu yakwenda yahone.
40008009	Kosoko ani nani na munhu nuwile hasi ya udaha, nina wasilikali hasi yangu, ninghamugamba ayuno, ‘Luta,’ yekuluta; na ayuno, ‘Wije,’ yekwija, ne mutumwa wangu, ‘Golosa nhafi,’ yekugolosa.”
40008010	Yesu yakahulike simbuli siso, yajuma, yakuwagamba awaya wendewomwandamila, “Sinati nyone ihuwi ikulu fina dino mu Isilaeli.
40008011	Chawelu, nikumutamilani, fina wengi wakwenda weje kulawa kundawilo ye dijuwa, wakwenda wekale hamwedu na Ibulahimu, na Isaka na Yakobo mu undewa wa kulanga;
40008012	amba awana wo undewa wakwenda watagigwe ku chisa cha kunje; ukwene kukuwa chililo na kugwegwejula meno.”
40008013	Kamei Yesu hoyomugamba ayuya ichilongosi wa wasilikali igana, “Luta, yuwe ukwako fina fouhuwile.” Imutumishi wakwe hoyohona ichigele chichiya.
40008014	Kamei Yesu foyafikile ukaya kwa Petulo, yamona imukwewe wa Petulo, inghina we muke, kagona mwisasi kena mhungo.
40008015	Hakamukwafa umukono, imhungo hoimuleuka; hoyokwinuka hoyomutogomela.
40008016	Ikafike hegulo, wejawamwijila matewa awena simhepo, hoyosilafa kwa kulonga imbuli yakwe, hakawahonya wose awowile watamu,
40008017	uleke imemelesigwe imbuli yalongigwa ne mugonesi Isaya, yekugamba, “Imwenyecho hakalonda usokesi wetu, Nakulonda matamu getu.”
40008018	Imwene Yesu foyejayona amatewa ga wanhu gekumusunguluta, yalagisa walute umwambu.
40008019	Imutulumi yumwedu hoyomulutila, yamugamba, “Mwalimu, Nokwandamila kokose kowukwenda ulute.”
40008020	Yesu yamugamba, “Mabwasiko gena mapango, fidege fya mulanga fina mafulu, Ninga imwana we munhu kechaka hokugonesa ditwi dyakwe.”
40008021	Yumwedu wa wefusa wakwe yamugamba, “Mundewa, ninghe luneka nilute nikamusike iBabangu.”
40008022	Ninga Yesu yamugamba, “Nyandamile, waleke wafile wasike awafile wawo.”
40008023	Yakengile muchiya, awefusa wakwe wejawamwandamila.
40008024	Hakuwa musingisiko mukulu mubahali, hata ichiya hochigubikigwa na meji, imwene hakowa yagonile sinhongo.
40008025	Awefusa wakwe wejawamulutila, na kumwinusa, wakumugamba, “Mundewa, chihonye, chikufa!”
40008026	Yawagamba, “Nhani mukogoha anyeye we dihuwi dikefu?” Chimwande, yekwinuka na kuyigombela hoyoigombela imheho ne bahali; hoisalama lugano.
40008027	Awanhu waya wejawajuma wakugamba, “I munhu yuno munhu waki! Imwene imheho ne ibahali fikumuhulika?”
40008028	Naye foyafikile umwambu kuisi ya Wagelasi, wanhu weli wena simhepo weja wakitang'anyila naye, wakulawa kufilalo, wakali lugano, awanhu wasendewodaha kugenda injila iyo.
40008029	Langa wejawatula chowe, wakugamba, “China choni na gweye go Mwana we Mulungu? Togola! Kwija kuchisambasa ugele wetu unghali?”
40008030	Hatali na baho hahowa na itewa dya nguluwe itewa sikudiya.
40008031	Magini gaya gejagamutesa, gakugamba, “Unghachilafe chileke chilute chikengile mwitewa dye singuluwe.”
40008032	Hakagamba, “Luteni Hogelawa,” hogekwingila musinguluwe; kamei ditewa dyose hodidulika kwigenge mpaka kubahali, hosikunywa munghabu hosikufa.
40008033	Awadimi howotija, howoluta ukaya, howokwanjasa simbuli sose, na sawaya wowile na simhepo.
40008034	Langa ikaya yose hoilawa kwija kumusingila iMundewa Yesu; kamei wakamwone, howomutasa yaleuke muisi yawo.
40009001	Yakengile muchiya, hoyoloka, umwambu hoyokwingila mukaya iyawo.
40009002	Langa, howomwigalila imunhu yena utamu wo kuholola, kagona mwisasi, imwene Yesu yakone dihuwi dyawo, hoyomugamba yuya yaholole, “Kiinghe moyo mukulu, mwanangu!” kulekeleligwa uwihi wako.
40009003	Langa, awamonga wa Watulumi howolonga kufidoga fyawo, “Ayuno yakubesa!”
40009004	Ninga Yesu hakamanya fowakudoga, hoyogamba, “Nhani mukudoga gehile mufidoga fyenu?
40009005	Dihufu no dihoki, kugamba, ‘Kulekeleligwa uwihi wako,’ ama kugamba, ‘Inuka ulute?’
40009006	Ninga mumanye fina Imwana we Munhu kena udaha muisi wokulekelela uwihi.” Yakumulonga ayuya yaholole inuka, ukitwike disasi dyako, ulute ukaya ukwako!
40009007	Hoyokwinuka, hoyoluta ukaya ukwakwe.
40009008	Amatewa gakone nheifo howomemigwa na ditisi, hogamutunya Mulungu, iyawenghile awanhu udaha kifana uwo.
40009009	Kamei Yesu foyagendage yakulawa uko hakona munhu ahanhu hakulihiligwa ikodi, yakwinangwa Matayo, hoyomugamba, “Nyandamile.” Hoyokwinuka na kumwandamila.
40009010	Yakengile kugati kudiya chakudiya, langa, wakonghosa kodi itewa na awena uwihi haweja, na kwikala hamwedu na Yesu na wefusa wakwe.
40009011	Mafalisayo, wakone nheifo, hawawagamba awefusa wakwe, “Nhani imwalimu wenu yakudiya hamwedu na wakonghosa kodi na wena uwihi?”
40009012	Imwene yakahulike, yawagamba, “Awomi wasikuhananga muganga, ninga awatamu.”
40009013	Ninga luteni mukakifuse isoko ye simbuli sino: “Nikuhananga ubasi, ninga si igelo. Kosoko sijile nikwinanga awanhu awaswamu, ninga awena uwihi.”
40009014	Ugele uwo wefusa wa Yohana howomulutila, howogamba, “Nhani aseye na Mafalisayo chikufunga, ninga awefusa wako wasikufunga?”
40009015	Yesu yawagamba, “Awenangigwe kuhalusi wodaha nhani kulila, ugele imwenye halusi kahamwedu nawo? Ugele uukwija wo kuleusiligwa imwenye halusi; aho noho wakwenda weje wafunge.
40009016	Hechaka munhu iyakuguma indame ya suke nyisha musuke ing'ono, kosoko aiya indame ikwenda idege isuke iya ilalile, na haya ahadegeke hakwenda hongeseke.
40009017	Kahi awanhu wasikuguma difai nyisha mufiya filalile; wanghagamba wagume mufiya ifilalile fikwenda fitulike, idifai ikwenda itike, ne ifiya fikwenda fibanike; ninga wakuguma idifai nyisha mufiya ifisha, kamei fyose fisikubanika.”
40009018	Ugele fo yalongage nawo gago, langa, hoyokwija jumbe yumonga, hoyomufugamila, yekugamba, “Imwanangu we chike kafa hambiya baha; ninga wije, wike imikono yako umwakwe naye yakwenda yowe mumi.”
40009019	Hoyoleuka Yesu, hoyomwandamila hamwedu na wefusa wakwe.
40009020	Langa, imwanamuke yejayowa na utamu wa kulawa sakame kwa miyaka ikumi na mili, hoyokwija kunyuma, hoyokwafa dipindo dye suke yakwe,
40009021	kosoko hakagamba muchidoga chakwe, “Ninghakwafa du dipindo dye isuke yakwe nikuhona.”
40009022	Yesu hoyobiduka, hoyomona, hoyomugamba, “Kiinghe moyo mukulu, mwanangu we chike! Dihuwi dyako dikuhonya.” Imwanamuke yuya hoyohona kulawa ugele uwo.
40009023	Yesu yakafike ukaya kwa yuya ijumbe, hakona wanhu wakutowa sifilimbi, na matewa wakuhongesa.
40009024	Hoyowagamba, “Leukeni! Kosoko ayuno imundele nghafile, kagona du.” Howomuseka lugano.
40009025	Ninga amatewa fowaleusigwe, hoyokwingila, hoyomukola umukono, ayuya imundele hoyokwimanyima.
40009026	Simbuli sino hosikwenela iisi iya yose.
40009027	Yesu foyagendage kulawa uko, wanhu wemudula weja wamwandamila wakwinula majwi, wakugamba, “Uchonele ubasi Mwana wa Daudi!”
40009028	Naye yakafike ukaya, awaya fidula howomulutila; Yesu hoyowagamba, “Mukuhuwila fina nodaha kugolosa dino?” Howogamba, “Heye, Mundewa!”
40009029	Hoyowakwafa ameso gawo, hoyogamba, “Ifene fomuhuwile muhokele!”
40009030	Ameso gawo hogogubuka; Imwene Yesu hoyowasigilila kwa ludole, “Langisiseni, hata munhu yumwedu yanghamanye.”
40009031	Ninga hawaleuka, howokwenesa simbuli sakwe mu isi iya yose.
40009032	Ugele awaya fowaleukage, hawamwigalila munhu chibubu iyena imhepo.
40009033	Imhepo ikalafigwe, ichibubu yalonga, amatewa hogojuma lugano, wakugamba, “Isinati yoneke nheifino mu Isilaeli ugele wowose.”
40009034	Amba Amafalisayo howogamba, “Kuludole lwe mukulu we simhepo yakulafa simhepo.”
40009035	Ne mwene Yesu yende yosunguluta mu sikaya ne fikaya fyose, yakufusa mumasinagogi gawo na kuhubili imbuli iswanu yo undewa, na kuhonya sinhamu sose na usokesi wowose uya.
40009036	Foyawonile amatewa, hakawonela ubasi kosoko hawasoka kifana ngholo sichaka mudimi.
40009037	Noho yawagambile awefusa wakwe, “Ugolaji mwingi, ninga wagolosaji wakefu.
40009038	Mutaseni Mundewa wo ugolaji, yegale wagolaji ku ugolaji wakwe.”
40010001	Yawenanga awefusa wakwe ikumi na weli, hoyowengha udaha wa kulafa simhepo sihile, na kuhonya sinhamu sose na usokesi wowose uya.
40010002	Na masina ga wefusa ikumi na weli no gano: Wa bosi Simoni yakwinangigwa Petulo, na Andelea imunduguse; Yakobo mwana wa Sebedayo, na Yohana imunduguse;
40010003	Filipo, na Batolomayo; Tomaso, na Matayo imukonghosa kodi; Yakobo mwana wa Alufayo, na Tadayo;
40010004	Simoni Mukananayo, na Yuda Isikalioti, ayo noyeja yamusongesa.
40010005	Awo ikumi na weli Yesu hoyowatuma, hoyowalagisa fina, “Kusinjila sa Mataifa munghalute, kahi injila yoyose ya wowose Wasamalia munghengile.
40010006	Ibeka mukole injila yokusilutila singholo sagilile se inyumba ya Isilaeli.
40010007	Mung'enda yenu hubilini, mugambe, Undewa wa kulanga usegelela!
40010008	Honyeni awatamu, inuleni awofile, wahonyeni awena ukoma, lafeni simhepo, muhokela chaka, lafeni chaka.
40010009	“Munghalonde sahabu, kahe fesa, kahe shaba mumisipi yenu;
40010010	kahi umufuko we nhambo, kahi ghasu mbili, kahi filwatu, kahi mhando, kosoko iyakugolosa milimo imwagila yenghigwe ichakudiya chakwe.
40010011	Ne ikaya yoyose ama chikaya chochose chomukwingila, hanangeni no nani umo imunhu yekudaha kuhuwilika; mwikale ukwakwe mpaka fomukuleuka.
40010012	Nanye munghengila munyumba muilamuse.
40010013	Ne inyumba iyo inghagiligwa digoya dyenu diwafikile; ninga honaga isagiligwe digoya dyenu dimuwileni muwecho.
40010014	Imunhu yanghaleka kumuhokelani kahi kusitegelesa simbuli senu, nghona mukulawa munyumba iyo, ama ikaya iyo, kung'unheni dinghundi duwile mumigulu yenu.
40010015	“Chawelu, nikumutamilani, ikwenda yuwe ibeka ku iisi ya Sodoma na Gomola kufinyilisa magayo gakwe dijuwa dye kuliganiswa, kusuma ikaya iyo.”
40010016	“Mulange, aniye nikumutumani, kifana ngholo muchiligati cha mausi, muwe ne misungu kifana majoka, na waholo kifana huwa.
40010017	Kilangisiseni na awanhu; kosoko wakwenda wawegale kumabalasa, na kumasinagogi gawo, wakwenda wamutoweni;
40010018	nanye mukwenda mwigaligwe ku maliwali na wandewa kosoko yangu, uwe uhomelesi ukwawo na kumataifa.
40010019	Ninga baho nghona wakumwigalani, munghadogedoge chomukwenda mulonge, kosoko mukwinghigwa ugele uwo gokulonga.
40010020	Kosoko siyo nyeye mukulonga, ninga ni Muhe we Baba yenu yakulonga mugati yenu.
40010021	“Ne imundugu yekumusongesa imunduguse uleke yakomigwe, ne baamunhu imwana, awana wekuwenukila awaweleke, na kuwakoma.
40010022	Nanye mukwenda musuligwe na wanhu wose kosoko ye disina dyangu, ninga iyakwenda yafinyilise mpaka kundumo noyakwenda yahone.
40010023	Ninga fowakuwawinga mukaya ayino, mutijile kuyimonga; kosoko, chawelu nikumutamilani, musikumala sikaya sa Isilaeli, mpaka yeje Imwana we Munhu.
40010024	“Imwifusa ghakumusuma imufusa wakwe, kahi imutumwa nghakumusuma iMundewa wakwe.
40010025	Yagila imwifusa yowe fina imwalimu wakwe, mutumwa yowe fina imukulu wakwe. Nghonaga wamwinange imwenye nyumba Belisebuli, isikuwa lugano kuwaya awoile munyumba yakwe.”
40010026	“Munghawogohe, kosoko kwa chaka mbuli ikifisile iyene isikwenda imanyike.
40010027	Dyonikumutamilani mu chisa, dilongeni mu ujelu; na dyomukuhulika kuchifiso, mudihubili munyumba muchanhya.
40010028	Munghawogohe awakukoma umutufi, wasikudaha kukoma ne chidoga; ibeka mumogohe ayuya iyakudaha kubana umutufi ne chidoga nacho mu jehanamu.
40010029	Togoleni ifindebwa fili fisikuguligwa kwe sendi imwedu? Ninga hata chimwedu chisikugwa hasi Baba yenu yaleke kumanya;
40010030	Ninga nyeye, hata si njwili sa mumatwi genu sitaligwa sose!
40010031	Munghogohe, ibeka nyeye kusuma findebwa itewa.”
40010032	“Ninga chila munhu yakwenda yanifumile kumwande ya wanhu, aniye nani nikwenda nimufumile kumwande ye iBabangu yowile kulanga.
40010033	Ninga imunhu wowose yakwenda yanikane kumwande ya wanhu, ani nani nikwenda nimukane kumwande ye iBabangu yowile kulanga.”
40010034	“Munghagambe fina nigala igoya muisi; ng'o! Sijile kwigala igoya, ninga ipanga.
40010035	Kosoko nija kuwatemanula imunhu ne Babakwe, imwana we chike ne ing'ina, imukwemulima ne mukwewe.
40010036	Awanghondo we munhu no waya wowile munyumba yakwe.
40010037	Iyakwenda iBabakwe ne ing'ina kusuma niye, nghakunyendesa; kahi iyakwenda imwanagwe we chigosi ama wechike kusuma niye nghakunyendesa.
40010038	Ninga imunhu inghakulonda umusalaba wakwe na kunyandamila, nghakunyendesa.
40010039	Iyakuchona chidoga chakwe yakuchagilisa; ninga ayuya iyakwagilisa chidoga chakwe, kosoko yangu yakwenda yachone.”
40010040	“Iyakuwahokelani nyeye yakunihokela niye, iyakunihokela niye, yakumuhokela ayuya iyanitumile.
40010041	Iyakumuhokela mugonesi kosoko ni mugonesi, yakwenda yapate digeleko dya mugonesi, naye iyakumuhokela imunhu we chawelu, kosoko ni munhu we chawelu, yakwenda yapate digeleko dye munhu wa chawelu.
40010042	Ne munhu wowose yakwenda yamunywise yumwedu wa awano awadodogi hata chinghowa chikombe cha meji gemheho, kosoko ni mwifusa, huwila, nikumutamilani, nghakwagililigwa na digeleko dyakwe ng'o.”
40011001	Kamei Yesu yakamale kuwasigilila awefusa wakwe ikumi na weli, hoyoleuka kuluta kufusa na kuhubili kusikaya sawo.
40011002	Yohana yakahulike ako kwigelesa sinhenda sa Kilisito, hoyotuma awefusa wakwe, wamuse,
40011003	“Agweye noyuya yakwija ama chimulangilile yungi?”
40011004	Yesu yabidula, na kuwagamba, “Luteni mukamutamile Yohana agene gomukuhulika, na gomukona:
40011005	awemudula wakona, ifiwete wakugenda, awena ukoma wakuhona, ifihuli wakuhulika, awafile wakwinuligwa, na awakiwa wakuhubiliigwa imbuli swanu.
40011006	Naye ibeka imunhu wowose yuya inghakunyona fina niha.”
40011007	Kamei awaya wakaleuke, Yesu yakonga kulonga na matewa simbuli sa Yohana, “Hamulawa kuluta kunyika kulanga choni? Chibago chikusingiswa ne imheho?
40011008	Ninga hamulawa kwijalanga choni? Munhu yafalile suke swamu lugano? Langa awanhu awakufala sisuke siswamu lugano, wowa musinyumba sa wandewa.
40011009	Ninga nhani mwalawile? Nikona mugonesi? Heye, nikumutamilani imukulu kusuma imugonesi,
40011010	langa, nikumutuma mutumigwa wangu, ‘Kumwande ye chihanga chako. Iyakwenda yagolose injila yako kumwande yako.’
40011011	Chawelu nikumutamilani, nghenati yoneke munhu mu fyeleko fya wanawake imukulu kusuma Yohana Mubatisaji; ninga imudodogi mu undewa wa kulanga no mukulu kusuma imwene.
40011012	Kulawa ugele wa Yohana Mubatisaji mpaka hambiya undewa wa kulanga ukulondigwa kwa ludole, nawo awena ludole wakuwulonda.
40011013	Kosoko wagonesi wose na tolati watamila mpaka ugele wa Yohana.
40011014	Munghahananga kufumila, imwene no Eliya iyakwenda yeje.
40011015	Iyena singhutwi, yahulike!
40011016	“Ninga icheleko chino nochiliganisa na choni? Chikifana wana wekwikala kwisoko, wakuwenanga wayao wakugamba,
40011017	‘Chiwatowela filimbi ninga musifinile! Chimba nyimbo so usungu kahi musililile!’
40011018	Kosoko Yohana hakeja, nghakudiya kahi nghakunywa, wagamba Kena mhepo yuno!
40011019	iMwana we Munhu keja yakudiya na kunywa, wagamba, ‘Mulafi yuno, na mulefi, wo ugimbi mbwiya yawo awakonghosa kodi na wena uwihi!’ Ne imisungu imanyika fina ina chawelu kumilimo yakwe.”
40011020	Hokakonga kusigombela sikaya siya sene soyagolose majumo mengi mugati yakwe, kosoko sisalambile.
40011021	“Usungu wako Kolasini! Usungu wako Betisaida! Kosoko amajumo agagolosigwe ukwenu nhanga gagolosigwe Tilo na Sidoni, howowa wakulamba katali na kufala magunia na kibaka difu.
40011022	Ninga nikumutamilani ikuwa ibeka Tilo na Sidoni kufinyilisa ditoso dyawo dijuwa dyo kuliganiswa kusuma nyeye!
40011023	Agwe nagwe Kapelinaumu, togola! Kokwinuligwa mpaka kulanga? Ukwenda udulisigwe mpaka kusimu! Kosoko amajumo agagoloseke ukwako nhanga gagoloseke Sodoma, ikaya iyo nhanga inghali mpaka diyelo.
40011024	Ninga nikumutamilani, ikwenda yuwe ibeka kwa Sodoma kufinyilisa uliganiso wakwe kusuma nyeye!”
40011025	Ugele uwo Yesu hakabidula yakugamba, “Nikukulumba, Baba wo ulanga ne iisi, kosoko ye simbuli siso, hakuwafisa wene ubala na wena misungu, na kuwagubulila wana wadodogi.
40011026	Heye, Baba, kosoko nofoyagile kumwande yako.”
40011027	Hoyogamba, “Ninghigwa fyose ne Babangu; kahi hechaka iyamumanyile Imwana, ninga Baba; kahi hechaka yamumanyile Baba ninga Mwana, na wowose imwene iMwana woyakwenda kumugubulila.
40011028	Mwije ukwangu, anye wose, mukwidasigwa na kusumigwa na makanda, aniye nikwenda niwabwihiseni.
40011029	Faleni umugwato, mukifuse ukwangu; kosoko niye na muholo munhu we digoya dye chidoga, nanye mukwenda muwe na kubwihila mufidoga fyenu.
40011030	Kosoko ulugwato lwangu lutelemeko, na dikanda dyangu ihufu.”
40012001	Ugele uwo Yesu yendeyogenda mumigunda dijuwa dye sabato; awefusa wakwe howokona njala, howokonga kukwanyula masamhu, na kudiya.
40012002	Amafalisayo wakone nheifo, howomugamba, “Langa, awefusa wako wakugolosa chinhu chene si chiswamu kugolosa dijuwa dye sabato!”
40012003	Hakawagamba, “Musasomile foyagolose Daudi, foyowile ne njala, imwene na wayagwe?
40012004	Ifyene foyengile munyumba ye Mulungu, na kudiya imikate ilafigwe kwa Mulungu, iyene si fiswanu imwene kudiya kahi awayagwe waya, ninga makuhani wemwene?
40012005	Kahi musisomile mutolati ifina awatambiki dijuwa dye sabato wakuibana isabato wanghowe na wihi?
40012006	Ninga nikumutamilani, ahano kabahano imukulu kusuma dihekalu.
40012007	Ninga nhanga mumanyile isoko ye simbuli sino, Nikuhananga ubasi, siyo igelo. Musowile mukuwagamba wabana awechaka wihi;
40012008	Kosoko Mwana we Munhu no Mukulu we sabato.”
40012009	Yaleuke uko, na kwingila mwisinagogi dyawo.
40012010	Langa, hamuwa na munhu iyena mukono uholole; weja wamusa, wakugamba, “Togola! Yagila kuhonya munhu dijuwa dye sabato?” Uleke wamusongese.
40012011	Hakawagamba, “No yehoki mugati yenu imwene ingholo yakwe imwedu inghahubugila mwikolongo dijuwa dye sabato, nghakuikola na kuilafa?
40012012	Togoleni! Imunhu si ibeka kusuma ingholo mikangha mingahi! Ninga ni fiswanu kugolosa amaswamu dijuwa dye sabato.”
40012013	Kamei yamugamba imunhu yuya, “Golola umukono wako.” Hakagolola, houhona, houkuwa mumi fina uyagwe wa keli.
40012014	Ninga awaya Mafalisayo, howolawa, howokuwa na mulundo kosoko yakwe, ifene fowakwenda wamukome.
40012015	Imwene Yesu yakagamanye ago, yaleuka uko; na wanhu itewa howomwandamila; hoyowahonya wose.
40012016	Hakawalemesa wanghamutamilise kuwanhu.
40012017	uleke iliganile imbuli yalongigwe ne mugonesi Isaya, yakugamba:
40012018	“Langa, imutumigwa wangu wonisagule, Mwendigwa wangu, umoyo wangu wendeswa naye. Nikuguma muhe wangu umwakwe, Yakwenda yawatamilise Amataifa uliganiso.
40012019	Nghakuwa na lukani kahi chowe, kahi imunhu nghakwenda yamuhulike munjila.
40012020	Ichibwade chitulike nghakuchibena, kahi ichikoloboyi chikulawa umosi nghakuchisima, Mpaka hona yakwigala uliganiso usume.
40012021	Disina dyakwe Amataifa wakwenda wadihuwile.”
40012022	Ugele uwo hakegaliligwa munhu yena magini, mudula, kahi chibubu, yamuhonya, kamei yuyuya chibubu yalonga na kona.
40012023	Matewa gose hagajuma, wakugamba, “Ayuno so mwana wa Daudi?”
40012024	Mafalisayo wakahulike, hawagamba, “Ayuno nghakulafa simhepo chaka, ninga kwa Belisebuli mukulu we simhepo.”
40012025	Kamei Yesu yakamanye fowakudoga, yawagamba, “Chila undewa ukigawile uwecho kwa uwecho, ukwenda ubanike; na kwachaka kaya iikitemanula iyenyecho ikudaha kwima.
40012026	Na Luhoma yanghamulafa Luhoma, yakibanila imwecho kwa imwecho, undewa wakwe wokwima nhani?
40012027	Nghona aniye nikulafa simhepo kwa Belisebuli, togoleni! Awana wenu wakumulafa kwa yehoki? Kosoko iyo awene nowakwenda wamuliganiseni!
40012028	Ninga niye ghona nikulafa simhepo kwa Muhe wa Mulungu, undewa wo Mulungu ufulusa kumwijilani.
40012029	“Ama kodaha nhani imunhu kwingila kunyumba ye munhu yena ludole na kufilonda ifinhu fyakwe, nghonaga nghakongile kumoha ayuya iyena uludole? Noholo yakonge kuhoka inyumba yakwe.
40012030	Imunhu inghehamwedu naniye kachinyume naniye; ne imunhu inghekukunjagisa hamwedu na niye yakwanjasa.
40012031	Kosoko iyo nikuwagambani, chila wihi na chila mbuli yo kubesa wakwenda walekeleligwe wanhu, ninga kwa kumbesa Muhe Musunhile wasikulekeleligwa.
40012032	Naye munhu wowose yakwenda yalonge mbuli muchanhya yo mwana wa Munhu yakwenda yalekeleligwe. Ninga Imunhu wowose yakwenda yalonge mbuli muchanhya ya Muhe Musunhile nghakwenda yalekeleligwe muchilunga chino hambiya na achiya chikwija.”
40012033	“Digoloseni dibiki dyuwe iswanu, na mamudyo gakwe maswanu; ama digoloseni dibiki dyuwe diha, na mamudyo gakwe geha; kosoko kwa mamudyo gakwe dibiki dikumanyika.
40012034	Anyeye mu wana wa majoka, modaha nhani kulonga maswanu nghonaga mwihile? Kosoko umulomo we munhu ukulonga agamemile mu moyo wakwe.
40012035	Munhu muswanu mu sigafu yakwe iswanu, yakulafa maswanu, na munhu yehile musigafu yakwe ihile yakulafa gehile.
40012036	Hambiya, nikumutamilani, chila mbuli ye chibwalasi yowakulonga wanhu, wakwija wolafa nhaguso yakwe dijuwa dyo kuliganiswa.
40012037	Kosoko kwa simbuli sako kotaligwa kuwa muswamu, na ku simbuli sako koliganiswa.”
40012038	Baho awamonga, awatulumi na Mafalisayo howomubidula, wakugamba, “Mwalimu Chikuhananga kona chitangilo ukwako.”
40012039	Hawabidula na kuwagamba, “Cheleko chihile na chechilanga, chikuhananga chitangilo? Wala chisikwinghigwa chitangilo, ninga ichitangilo che mugonesi Yona.
40012040	Kosoko fina Yona foyejayowa majuwa madatu misi ne chilo mudida dye nyamungumi, nonheifo foikuwa iMwana we Munhu foyakwenda yowe majuwa madatu imisi ne chilo mu moyo we iisi.
40012041	Wanhu wa Ninawi wakwija wokwima dijuwa dyo uliganiso na wanhu we cheleko chino, nawo wakwenda wawaliganise fina wabana; kosoko awene hawalamba kwa mahubili ga Yona; na ahano kabaha imukulu kusuma Yona:
40012042	Imalikia wa kwikulu yakwenda yeme dijuwa dyo uliganiso hamwedu na wanhu we cheleko chino, naye yakwenda yawaliganise fina wabana; kosoko imwene yeja kulawa ulwandi lwe ndumo we chilunga uleke yahulike ubala wa Sulemani; na hano kabahano imukulu kusuma Sulemani.”
40012043	“Imhepo ihile, foikulawa mwe munhu, ikugendela ahanhu hechaka meji, ikuhananga hanhu hakubwihila, inghaswela.
40012044	Kamei, ikugamba, ‘Nikuya ukaya ukwangu konilawile,’ nghonaikwija, ikuifika yechaka munhu, ishagiligwa, na ihambigwa.
40012045	Chimwande ikuluta ikalonda mhepo mufungate isihile kusuma iyene naso sokwingila na kwikala umo; na imunhu yuya inyuma yakwe ya ndumo ikuwa ihile kusuma aiya ya kunghonga. Nofo ikwenda yuwe kucheleko chino chihile.”
40012046	Ugele woyalongage na matewa, langa, ing'ina na wanduguse hawowa wemile kunje, wakuhananga kulonga naye.
40012047	Imunhu yumonga yamutamila, “Langa, ing'inako na wanduguso wowa kunje, wakuhananga kulonga nagwe.”
40012048	Kabidula yekumugamba, “Ayuya yamwigalile imbuli, Ing'inangu nonani, na awandugusangu?”
40012049	Hakawagololela umukono awefusa wakwe, yakugamba, “Langa, ing'inangu na wandugu sangu!”
40012050	Kosoko wowose iyakwenda yagolose foyakwenda iBaba yowile kulanga, ayu no mundugu sangu, lumbu dyangu, ne ing'inangu.
40013001	Dijuwa diya Yesu hoyoleuka ukaya, hoyokwikala hanghingi ye bahali.
40013002	Howomwijila matewa mengi, hoyokwingila mumunhumbwi, hoyokwikala; agaya matewa gose hogokwima kunghingi ye bahali.
40013003	Hoyolonga nawo mbuli nyingi kwa mbasi, hoyogamba, “ “Langa, imuhandi yaluta kuhanda.
40013004	Kamei foyendeyonyaga, simbeyu simonga silagala habehi ne njila; ifidege hofikwija hofisidiya;
40013005	simonga hosilagala mwikangalawe, ahechaka ulongo mwingi; hosikota chimwande kosoko ulongo usingile hasi;
40013006	dijuwa dikalike hosilakala; na kosoko sichaka misisi hosinyala.
40013007	Simonga hosilagala ahena imiwa; imiwa iya hoikula, hoisikanhamisa;
40013008	Simonga hosilagala hena ulongo muswanu, hosikweleka, imonga, igana, makumi mutandatu, imonga makumi madatu.
40013009	Iyena singhutwi yahulike!”
40013010	Howokwija awefusa wakwe howomugamba, “Nhani ukulonga nawo kwa mbasi?”
40013011	Yabidula, yekugamba, “Anyeye mumotesigwa kufimanya ififiso fyo undewa wa kulanga, ninga awene wasimotesigwe.
40013012	Kosoko wowose iyena ichinhu, yakwenda yongeseligwe, naye yakwenda yamemesiligwe telele: Ninga ayuya iyechaka chinhu; hata achiya choyenacho yakwenda yahokigwe.
40013013	Kosoko iyo nikulonga nawo kwa mbasi; kosoko wanghalanga wasikona, na wanghategelesa wasikuhulika, kahi kumanya.
40013014	Imbuli ye mugonesi Isaya ikuliganiswa ukwawo, iikugamba: ‘Kuhulika mohulika, ninga musimanya; Kulanga molanga, ninga musikona.
40013015	Kosoko imimoyo ya wanhu wano igaluka misito, Na kusinghutwi sawo wasikuhulika fiswanu, Ameso gawo wafinya; Wangheje wokona kwa meso gawo, Howohulika kwa nghutwi sawo, Howomanya mumiyoyo yawo. Howobiduka honiwahonya.’
40013016	Ninga ibeka ameso genu, kosoko gakona, ne singhutwi senu, kosoko sikuhulika.
40013017	Kosoko chawelu, nikumutamilani, wagonesi wengi na waswanhu hawenda kugona gomukona nyeye, ninga wasagonile, na wasagahulike gomukuhulika nyeye wanghagahulike.”
40013018	“Hulikiseni imbasi ye muhandi.
40013019	Chila munhu nghona yakuhulika imbuli ya undewa nghona nghakuimanya, yakwija ayuya iyehile, yakuidondola iihandigwe mumoyo wakwe. Ayo noyahandigwe habehi ne injila.
40013020	Na yuya iyahandigwe mumakangalawe, no yuya yakuihulika imbuli yakuihokela kwa chinyemi;
40013021	ninga kusiyakwe kechaka misisi, yakugendelela chipisi chiguhi, inghalawanisa nyidaswa kosoko ye imbuli iyo, chimwande yakuileka.
40013022	Iyahandigwe hamiwa, no yuya iyakuhulika imbuli; kamei simbuli se chilunga, na udasi wo ugoli we chilunga, fikuikanhamisa imbuli iya; kamei isikweleka.
40013023	Ayuya yahandigwe haulongo muswanu no yuya yakuhulika iyo imbuli, na kuimanya: Na chawelu yakweleka mamudyo na kulafa igana dimwedu, na makumi mutandatu, na imonga makumi madatu.”
40013024	Hoyowalafila mbasi ingi, yakugamba, “Undewa wa kulanga uligana na munhu yahandile mbeyu swanu mumugunda wakwe:
40013025	awanhu wakagone hakeja imunghondo wakwe na kuhanda mabago mugati ye ingano, na kuleuka.
40013026	Hanyuma, ingano ikakule na kweleka, hogoneka na mabago gengi mugatigati ye ingano.
40013027	Awatumwa wakwe imwenye kaya howoluta kumutamila, ‘Mundewa, nghwahandile mbeyu swanu mu mugunda wako; galawa hoki amabago?’
40013028	Hakowagamba, ‘Imunghondo noyagolose nhaifi!’ Awatumwa hawamugamba, ‘Ukuhananga chikagalunde hamwedu?’”
40013029	Hakagamba, “Ng'o, Mungheje mung'ola mabago, na kung'ola ingano hamwedu nago.
40013030	Filekeni fyose fikule fifike ku ugele wokududula; nikaniwatamila awakududula, Kongeni kugalunda amabago, madulu na kugasoma; ingano muyigale kukano yangu.”
40013031	Hakawalafila mbasi ingi: Yakugamba, “Undewa wa kulanga ukifana ne imhule ye haladali, imunhu yailonda, hoyoihanda mumugunda wakwe;
40013032	nayo ndodogi kusuma simbeyu sose; amba inghakula ikuwa nghulu kusuma mabiki gose, dikuwa ibiki ikulu fidege fya kulanga fikwija na kujenga mafulu gawo mumanhambi gakwe."
40013033	Hoyowatamila mbasi ingi: “Undewa wa kulanga ukifana inungo yoyalondile imwanamuke, hoyoiguma mu simhishi ndatu so usage, kamei usage wose housasa.”
40013034	Ago gose Yesu hoyowatamila amatewa kwa mbasi, ninga bila mbasi nghawatamile mbuli.
40013035	Uleke iliganile imbuli iyalongwa ne mugonesi, iyagamba, “Nogubula umulomo wangu kwa mbasi; Nikugatambula agakifisile kulawa kunghonga.”
40013036	Kamei Yesu yakawaleke amatewa, hoyokwingila munyumba; awefusa wakwe howomwijila, wakugamba, “Chibulile imbasi ya mabago ga mumugunda.”
40013037	Hoyowabidula, hoyowagamba, “Iyakunyaga asiya simbeyu si swanu no Imwana we Munhu;
40013038	umugunda uya no chilunga; simbeyu siswanu no wana wa undewa; agaya amabago no wana wa yuya yehile;
40013039	ayuya imunghondo yahandile no Luhoma; kukududula no kuhela kwe chilunga, na waya awakududula no malaika.
40013040	Kamei; fina mabago fogakulundigwa na kusomigwa mumoto; nofo ikwenda yuwe kukuhela kwe chilunga.
40013041	Imwana we Munhu yakwija yakutuma malaika wakwe, nawo wakwenda wawakonghole kulawa mu undewa wakwe wose awena uwihi, na wose awakugolosa gehile,
40013042	na kuwaguma mwililimba dyo umoto; kukwende kuwe chililo na kugwegwejula meno.
40013043	Noho awanhu awaswamu wakwenda wake fina dijuwa mu undewa we Baba yawo. Yena singhutwi yahulike!”
40013044	“Kahi undewa wa kulanga ukifana na ugoli ukifisile mumugunda; imunhu yakawone, hoyoufisa; na kwa chinyemi chakwe hoyoluta hoyolafa ifinhu fyakwe fyose hofiguligwa, kamei hoyogula umugunda uya.”
40013045	“Kahi undewa wa kulanga ukifana munhu mwambasi iyekuhananga lulu swanu.
40013046	Kamei yakone lulu imwedu ya iliho lugano, hakaluta na kulafa ifinhu fyakwe fyose figuligwe, hoyoigula.”
40013047	“Kahi undewa wa kulanga ukifana ulwafu lugumigwe mubahali, kamei houkwega sisomba sa matalago gose.
40013048	Lukameme, howolukwega kunje; howokwikala, howosagula si swanu howosiguma mufiya, isihile howositaga.
40013049	Nofo ikaikuwa kukuhela kwe chilunga; malaika wakwenda walawanise na kuwabagula awehile na awaswanu,
40013050	na kuwakubita mwililimba dyo umoto; kukwende kuwe chililo na kugwegwejula meno.”
40013051	Yesu hoyowosa, “Mugamanya agano gose?” Howomugamba, “Heye.”
40013052	Hoyogamba, “Ninga kosoko iyo chila mutulumi yena umanyi wa undewa wa kulanga, kakifana imunhu imwenyenyumba iyakulafa mufinhu fyakwe ifingi ifinhu fisha ne figono.”
40013053	Kamei Yesu yakamale simbasi siso, hoyolawa,
40013054	Yakafike kuiisi yakwe, hakawafusa mwisinagogi dyawo, howojuma, wakugamba, “Ayuno kapata hoki imisungu ino na amajumo gano?
40013055	Ayuno si mwana we muselemala? Ing'ina si yuya yekwinangwa Maliamu? Na awandugusakwe si cha Yakobo, na Yusufu, na Simoni, na Yuda?
40013056	Na walumbuse wose wasibaha ahetu? Hambiya yuno kapata hoki gose gano?”
40013057	Hawamusula. Yesu hakawagamba, “Imugonesi nghakuswela chogoho, ninga kuisi yakwe imwecho na munyumba yakwe.”
40013058	Kamei nghagolose majumo mengi makulu uko, kosoko yakuleka kuhuwila kwawo.
40014001	Ugele uwo iMundewa Helode hoyohulika simbuli se Mundewa Yesu, yawatamila awatumishi wakwe,
40014002	“Ayo no Yohana Mubatisaji kenuka mudifa, kosoko udaha ukugolosa milimo mugati yakwe.”
40014003	Kosoko Helode hakowa yamukolile Yohana, hoyomoha, hoyomuguma mwigelesa, kosoko ya Helodia imuke wa Filipo imunduguse.
40014004	Kosoko Yohana yamugamba, “Fina isinogele agweye kuwa naye.”
40014005	Naye yakahanange kumukoma, hakawogoha awanhu, kosoko hawamona Yohana fina mugonesi.
40014006	Dikafike dijuwa dye sikukuu yo kwelekwigwa kwakwe Helode, imwanagwe we chike wa Helodia hoyofina fiswanu kumwande ya wanhu, hoyomwendesa Helode,
40014007	hakamuhuisa kwa kilaha fina komwingha chochose cho yakuhananga.
40014008	Kwa kusongesigwa ne ing'ina, yagamba, “Ninghe bahano, mwisahani ditwi dya Yohana Mubatisaji!”
40014009	iMundewa, hakona usungu lugano, ninga kosoko ye nyilaha yakwe, na kosoko ya waya awowile naye hachakudiya, hakalagisa yenghigwe;
40014010	hakatuma munhu, howomudumula ditwi Yohana amuya mwigelesa.
40014011	Ditwi dyakwe hadigaligwa mwibakuli, hoyokwinghigwa imwana yuya we chike; hoyodigala kwe ing'ina.
40014012	Awefusa wakwe hawaluta, howolonda umutufi uya, howowika, muchilalo; kamei howoluta kumutamila Yesu.
40014013	Ninga Yesu yakahulike gago, hoyoleuka uko muchiya, hoyoluta hanhu hechaka wanhu, ye imwene chinyele. Amatewa wakahulike, howomwandamila kwa migulu kulawa mukaya sawo.
40014014	Yesu hoyolawa hoyokona, itewa ikulu dya wanhu, hoyowonela ubasi, hoyowahonya sinhamu sawo.
40014015	Ikafike hegulo, awefusa wakwe howamulutila, wokugamba, “Ahanhu hano nyika muhala, ne chigele chiloka, uwelage amatewa walute kusikaya wakakigulile fyakudiya.”
40014016	Yesu hoyowagamba, “Hechaka soko ya kuleuka, Wengheni nyeye chakudiya!”
40014017	Howomugamba, “Chichaka chinhu hano ila mikate mishano na somba mbili du.”
40014018	Hoyogamba, “Nigalileni hano.”
40014019	Hoyowalonga amatewa wekale mumbago: Hoyoilonda aiya imikate mishano na sisomba si mbili, hoyolanga kulanga, hoyoitasila mboto, hoyoibendula imikate iya, hoyowengha awefusa wakwe; awefusa howowengha amatewa.
40014020	Howodiya wose howokwiguta; howodondola ifibesu fye mikate fisigale, fisege ikumi na fili fimemile.
40014021	Nawo awadiile hawowa wagosi figulu fishano, kuleka wanawake na wana wadodogi.
40014022	Chimwande hoyowadindilisa awefusa wakwe wengile muchiya, na kulongola kumwande yakwe kuloka umwambu ugele imwene yakilaga na amatewa.
40014023	Kamei yakamale kilaga na matewa, hoyokwila kwitunda yemwene, kutasa. Ikafike hegulo, hakowa uko yewaimwene.
40014024	Ne chiya chiya chifika muchiligati che bahali, chikwidasigwa lugano na meji gakujubajuba, kosoko imheho yende itowa muchiya kwa ludole.
40014025	Kumalile kucha ninga kukali chilo, Yesu hoyowejila, yakugenda nemigulu mubahali.
40014026	Awefusa wakwe wakamone yakugenda mubahali, howokogoha, howogamba, “Inyefu! Howotula chowe kosoko ya uwoga.”
40014027	Chimwande Yesu hoyolonga, hoyowagamba, “Kiingheni moyo; No niye. Munghogohe.”
40014028	Petulo hoyomubidula, yakugamba, “Mundewa, nghona nogweye, nilonge uleke nije ukwako mumeji muchanhya.”
40014029	Hoyomugamba, “Wije!” Petulo hoyohumuluka muchiya, hoyogenda kwa migulu mumeji kumulutila Yesu.
40014030	Ninga yakone imheho hoyokogoha; hoyokonga kudidimila, hoyotula chowe, “Mundewa, nihonye!”
40014031	Chimwandemwande Yesu hakagolola umukono wakwe, hakamukola, na kumugamba, “Agwe go we dihuwi dikefu! Nhani wowile na manhonge?”
40014032	Nawo wakengile muchiya, imheho hoiposika.
40014033	Nawo awowile muchiya howomufugamila howogamba, “Chawelu agweye no umwana we Mulungu!”
40014034	Wakafuluse kuloka, hawengila mu iisi ya Wagenesaleti.
40014035	Na awanhu wa hanhu haya wakamutange, howotuma wanhu kuluta ku si iisi sose sisungulute hawamwigalila wose wowile ne sinhamu;
40014036	nawo hawamutasa fina wakwafe du; dipindo dye isuke yakwe; na wose wakwafile howohona.
40015001	Baho Mafalisayo na Watulumi kulawa Yelusalemu howomulutila Yesu na kugamba,
40015002	“Nhani awefusa wako wakubana ijadi? Kosoko wasikunawa imikono nghona wakudiya chakudiya.”
40015003	Hoyowabidula yakuwagamba, “Nhani anye nanye mukubana imisigililo ye Mulungu kosoko ya ijadi yenu?
40015004	kosoko Mulungu yagamba, ‘Mogohe iBabako, ne ing'inako, na Iyakuliga iBabakwe, ama ing'ina, yakomigwe chelu.’
40015005	Ninga anyeye mukugamba, ‘Iyakwenda yamulonge iBabakwe ama ing'ina, Chochose chiwagile kutasigwa kulawa ukwangu niye ni cha Mulungu. Kechaka soko ya kumogoha iBabakwe.’
40015006	Kamei mukuibesa imbuli ye Mulungu kosoko ye ijadi yenu.
40015007	Anye mwina ichimwefe, ni fiswanu foyalongile mugonesi Isaya kosoko yenu, yekugamba,
40015008	‘Awanhu wano wakunyogoha kwa milomo; Ninga imimoyo yawo ya hatali naniye.
40015009	Nawo wakufuga chaka, Wakufusa amafuso ge misigililo ya Wanhu.’”
40015010	Hoyowenanga matewa hoyowagamba,
40015011	“Hulikiseni, mumanye! Siyo ichikwingila kumulomo ichikumuguma imunhu uwafu; nanga ichikumulawa kumulomo nochikumuguma imunhu uwafu.”
40015012	Noho awefusa wakwe wamulutile wakugamba, “Kumanya fina Mafalisayo fowahulike imbuli iya hawasuha?”
40015013	Hakabidula, “Chila mbeyu iisihandigwe ne Babangu wa kulanga ikung'oligwa.
40015014	Walekeni! Awene ni filongosi mudula, wa mudula; na mudula yanghamulongosa imudula miyagwe, wakwenda wahubugile mwikolongo wose foniweli.”
40015015	Kamei Petulo hakabidula yakugamba, “Chitamile, imbasi iyo.”
40015016	Yesu hoyowagamba, “Hata nyeye nanye mwikali mwechaka misungu?
40015017	Munghati mumanye fina chila chikwingila kumulomo chikuloka kunda, na kuluta kutagigwa kucholo?
40015018	Ninga ifikulawa kumulomo fikulawa kumoyo; nofikumuguma imunhu uwafu.
40015019	Kosoko kumoyo kukulawa magelegela gehile, kukoma, dihabwa, uhiji, uhomelesi wa udasi, na maligo;
40015020	ago nanga gekumwingha imunhu uwafu, ninga kukudiya na mikono isinawigwe kusikumwingha imunhu uwafu.”
40015021	Yesu yakaleuke uko hoyoluta ulwandi lwa Tilo na Sidoni.
40015022	Langa mwanamuke yumonga Mukananayo we simhaka sa kuya hoyomwijila, hoyokwinula dijwi, na kugamba, “Unyonele ubasi, Mundewa mwana wa Daudi. Mwanangu we chike, kekaliligwa lugano na simhepo.”
40015023	Kahi Yesu nghamubidule mbuli. Awefusa wakwe howomulutila, howomutasa, wakugamba, “Muleke yaleuke, kosoko yakuchijojela kunyuma yetu.”
40015024	Hakabidula, yekugamba, “Nhumigwa kusingholo sagilile du, se nyumba ya Isilaeli.”
40015025	Naye hoyokwija hoyomufugamila hoyogamba, “Mundewa nitase!”
40015026	Hakabidula yekugamba, “Siyo fiswanu kulonda ichakudiya cha wana na kugakubitila amabwa.”
40015027	Hoyogamba, “Heye, Mundewa, ninga hata amabwa gakudiya chakudiya che sigafu ichikulagala musimesa se wandewa wawo.”
40015028	Kamei Yesu hoyobidula yekugamba, “Mayi, dihuwi dyako ikulu.” Na yuwe ukwako fina fo ukuhananga. Imwanagwe we chike hoyohona kulawa ugele uwo.
40015029	Yesu hakaleuka uko, na kufika ulwandi lwa bahali ya Galilaya; hoyokwila kwitunda, hoyokwikala hasi uko.
40015030	Hawamulutila matewa wakumwigalila fiwete, fidula, fibubu, filema, na wamonga itewa hawaweka hamigulu yakwe; hoyowahonya;
40015031	Kamei amatewa howajuma, wakone fibubu wakulonga, filema wakuhona, fiwete wakugenda; na fidula wakona; howomutunya Mulungu wa Isilaeli.
40015032	Yesu hakawenanga wefusa wakwe hoyogamba, “Nikuwonela ubasi amatewa, kosoko gafika majuwa madatu wekala hamwedu na niye, kahi wechaka chinhu cho kudiya; kuwelaga wafungile sikwenda, wangheje wosilika munjila.”
40015033	Awefusa wakwe howogamba, “Chopata hoki mikate ahano hanyika, yo kudigutisa ditewa dikulu fina dino?”
40015034	Yesu hoyowosa, Mwina mikate mingahe? Howogamba, “Mufungate, Na fisomba fikefu.”
40015035	Hoyowalagisa amatewa wekale hasi;
40015036	hoyoilonda iya imikate mufungate ne fisomba fiya, hoyolumba, hoyoibendula, hoyowengha awefusa wakwe, awene nawo howowengha amatewa.
40015037	Howodiya wose, howokwiguta, howodondola ifibendu fisigale fye mikate fisege mufungate, fimemile.
40015038	Nawo awadiile hawowa wagosi figulu fine, leka wanawake na wana.
40015039	Hoyowelaga amatewa, hoyokwila mu chiya, hoyoluta ulwandi lwa Magadani.
40016001	Howomwijila Mafalisayo na Masadukayo, kumugesa, howomuhananga yawonese chitangilo chikulawa kulanga.
40016002	Hoyobidula, hoyowagamba, “Hona ni hegulo, mukugamba, ‘Kukuwa kuswanu; kosoko ulanga mudunghu.’
40016003	Na nhosikusiku, mukugamba, ‘Diyelo kukuwa mheho ya luputa; kosoko ulanga mudunghu, kahi kukudidima.’ Mumanya kutanga ulanga fowuwile; ninga, musikudaha kutanga ifitangilo fya ugele uno.
40016004	Cheleko chihile cha dihabwa chikuhananga chitangilo? Wala! Chisikwinghigwa chitangilo kusuma chiya cha Yona.” Hoyowaleka, hoyoleuka.
40016005	Nawo awefusa wakwe howoluta mpaka umwambu, howosimilwa kulonda mikate;
40016006	Yesu hoyowagamba, “Mukilangisise ne inungo ya Mafalisayo na Masadukayo.”
40016007	Howokonga kusimulila awecho kwa wecho, wakugamba, “Kosoko chisigale mikate.”
40016008	Ninga Yesu yakamanye, hoyowagamba, “Nhani mukuwanga nyenye kwa nyenye, anyeye we dihuwi dikefu, kosoko mwichaka mikate?
40016009	Mukali kumanya? Kahi musikugelegela aiya imikate imishano ku wanhu figulu fishano, homudondola fisege fingahi?
40016010	Na aiya mikate mufungate, na waya wanhu figulu fine, homudondola fisege fingahe?
40016011	Yanhani musikumanya fina si kosoko ye mikate nimutamilani? Ninga mukilangisise na inungo ya Mafalisayo na Masadukayo.”
40016012	Noho wamanyile fina nghalongile wakilangisise ne nungo ya mukate, ninga na mafuso ga Mafalisayo na Masadukayo.
40016013	Yesu yaluta ulwandi lwa Kaisalia-Filipi, hoyowosa awefusa wakwe yakugamba, “Awanhu wakugamba fina Imwana we Munhu no nani?”
40016014	Howogamba, “Wamonga wakugamba Yohana Mubatisaji, wamonga Eliya, wamonga Yelemia, nhagela yumwedu wa Wagonesi.”
40016015	Hoyowagamba, “Anyeye mukugamba niye no nani?”
40016016	Simoni Petulo hokabidula, “Agweye no Kilisito Imwana we Mulungu imumi.”
40016017	Yesu hoyobidula, hoyomugamba, “Ibeka gweye Simoni Bal-yona! Kosoko umutufi ne sakame fisikugubulile adino, ninga iBabangu iyowile kulanga.”
40016018	Nani nikukugamba, “Agweye no Petulo, na muchanhya ya diwe dino nikudijenga dikanisa dyangu; kahi imilango ya kusimu isikudisuma.
40016019	Nani nikukwingha gweye sifunguo sa undewa wa kulanga, dyodose dyoukuhinda hasi dihindigwe na kulanga, na dyodyose dyo ukukumula hasi hano, dikukumuligwa kulanga.”
40016020	Kamei hoyowalemesa awefusa wakwe wanghamutamile munhu wowose fina imwene no Kilisito.
40016021	Kulawa ugele uwo Yesu hakakonga kuwatamila awefusa wakwe na kuwagamba ikuhanangigwa yalute Yelusalemu na kitang'anyila na masambasiko mengi, kulawa kuwasehe na Makuhani, na watulumi na kukomigwa na dijuwa dya kadatu kwinuligwa muchilalo.
40016022	Petulo hoyomulonda, hoyokonga kumugombela, yakugamba, “Mulungu yalegusile kutali Mundewa! Agano ganghakwijile ng'o.”
40016023	Hakabiduka, na kumugombela Petulo, “Luta kunyuma yangu Shetani! Kwa chikwakwalisi ukwangu; kosoko nghukudoga aga Mulungu, ninga ge chimunhumunhu.”
40016024	Ugele uwo Yesu yawatamila awefusa wakwe, “Munhu wowose iyakwenda kunyandamila, yakikane mwecho, yakitwike umusalaba wakwe, yanyandamile.
40016025	Kosoko imunhu yakuhananga kuhonya chidoga chakwe kosoko yangu; yakuchagilisa, iyakwenda yagilise chidoga chakwe kosoko yangu, yakuchihonya.
40016026	Imunhu kopata chinhu chaki yanghapata ichilunga chose, ninga yagilise ichidoga chakwe? Kahi munhu yakudaha kulafa choni ahanhu he chidoga chakwe?
40016027	kosoko Mwana we Munhu yakwija mwitunyo dye Babakwe hamwedu na malaika wakwe; noho yakwenda yamulihe chila munhu kuligana na sinhenda sakwe.
40016028	Chawelu nikumutamilani, hena wanhu wamonga wemile hano, awene wasikufa ugele wasinati wamone iMwana we Munhu yekwija mu undewa wakwe.”
40017001	Gakaloke majuwa mutandatu, Yesu hakawalonda Petulo na Yakobo, na Yohana imunduguse, hoyowegala kwitunda kuchanhya wemwene;
40017002	Hakabiduka ichihanga chakwe, kumwande yawo, ichihanga chakwe hachikonga kwakaika fina dijuwa.
40017003	Langa hawalawanisa Musa na Eliya, wakusimulila naye.
40017004	Petulo hakabidula yakumugamba Yesu, “Mundewa, nifiswamu chuwe bahano; unghenda nigolose fibanda fidatu, chimwedu chako gweye, chimonga cha Musa, na chimonga cha Eliya.”
40017005	Ugele yakulonga go, langa, difunde dijelu dyawagubika, kamei dijwi hodilawa mwifunde diya, dikugamba, “Ayuno no Mwanangu Mwendigwa wangu, wonikwendesigwa naye, mumutegelese imwene!”
40017006	Ninga awefusa wakwe wakahulike, hawogwa funama, na kogoha lugano.
40017007	Yesu hakawejila, na kuwakwafa, hoyowagamba, “Inukeni, kahi Munghogohe!”
40017008	Howokwinula ameso gawo, wosonile munhu ila Yesu yemwene.
40017009	Ugele foweja wadulikaga kulawa kwitunda, Yesu hoyowalagisa, hoyogamba, “Munghamutamile munhu wowose si mbuli sa gago gomonile mpaka Imwana we Munhu yenuke muchilalo.”
40017010	Awefusa wakwe howomusa, wakugamba, “Ninga nhani awatulumi wakugamba fina yakulongola Eliya?”
40017011	Naye hoyobidula, yakuwagamba, “Eliya yakwija, Naye koliganisa gose,
40017012	ninga nikumutamilani, fina Eliya kafulusa kwija, howoleka kumutanga, ninga howomugolosela gose gowendile kumugolosela. Nheifo Imwana we Munhu naye yakuluta kudumangiswa mumikono yawo.”
40017013	Noho awaya awefusa wamanyile fina yakulonga nawo simbuli sa Yohana Mubatisaji.
40017014	Kamei wakadifikile ditewa, munhu yumonga hoyomwijila, hoyomufugamila, yakugamba,
40017015	“Mundewa, umonele ubasi imwanangu! Kosoko kena chisilisi, na yakwidasigwa lugano, kosoko chila ugele yakugwa mumoto, na chila ugele mumeji.
40017016	Nimwigala kuwefusa wako, walemeligwa kumuhonya.”
40017017	Yesu hoyobidula hoyomugamba, “Anyeye cheleko chichaka dihuwi! Ichagilile, nokwikala hamwedu nanye mpaka milaki? Nimufinyiliseni mpaka milaki? Mwigaleni akuno ukwangu.”
40017018	Yesu hoyoigombela imhepo, nayo hoilawa; imwanike yuya hoyohona kulawa ichigele chicho.
40017019	Noho awaya awefusa wakwe howomulutila Yesu wemwene kwa chinyele howogamba, “Nhani seye chalemeligwe kuilafa?”
40017020	Yesu hoyowagamba, “Kosoko yo ukefu we dihuwi dyenu, kosoko chawelu nikumutamilani, Munghowa na ihuwi idodogi kifana mhule ya haladali, modaha kudilonga ditunda dino, ‘Leuka hano ulute akuya,’ nadyo dikwenda dileuke. Kahi kusikuwa na mbuli iyene isikudahika ukwenu!”
40017021	Ninga ifanile ino isikulawa ila kwa kutasa na kufunga.
40017022	Nawo fowakitang'anyile Galilaya, Yesu hoyowagamba, “iMwana we Munhu yakagumigwa mumikono ya wanhu,
40017023	nawo wakumukoma, na dijuwa dya kadatu yakwinuka muchilalo.” Howokuwa na usungu lugano.
40017024	Kamei fowafikile Kapelinaumu, awaya awende wakonghosa ikodi ya nusu shekeli hawamulutila Petulo, wakugamba, “Togola! iMwalimu wenu yakuliha kodi?” Hakawagamba, “Heye.”
40017025	Naye yakengile munyumba, “Yesu hakakonga kumusa.” Yakugamba, “Ukona nhani Simoni? Awandewa we chilunga chino wakulonda ikodi au maliho kuwanhu wenhani? Kuwana wawo ama wanhu wengi?”
40017026	Naye yakagambe, “Kuwanhu wengi.” Yesu yagamba, “Nghona noneifo, basi awana wasikulafa.
40017027	Chingheje chiwakwakwalisa, luta kubahali, ukagume induwano kamei ulonde isomba iya yowukwenda ukole kunghonga, unghagubula umulomo wakwe kokona shekeli, ilonde iyo ukawenghe, kosoko yako na kosoko yangu.”
40018001	Ichigele chichiya awefusa wakwe howomulutila Yesu howogamba, “No nani imukulu mu undewa wa kulanga?”
40018002	Hoyokwinanga imwana yumwedu, hoyomwika mugati yawo,
40018003	hoyowagamba, “Chawelu nikumutamilani munghaleka kubiduka na kuwa kifana fyana fidodogi, musikudaha kwingila ng'o mu undewa wa kulanga.
40018004	Hambiya wowose iyakihungusa imwecho fina imwana ayuno, ayo no mukulu mu undewa wa kulanga.
40018005	Na wowose yekwenda yamuhokele imwana yumwedu kifana yuno kosoko ye disina dyangu, yakunihokela niye.”
40018006	“Ninga iyakwenda yamwagilise yumwedu wa wadodogi wano awakunihuwila, iwagila yohigwe musingo ulwala na kutubugisigwa muchiligati che bahali.
40018007	Usungu we chilunga kosoko ya simbuli sokwagilisa! Kosoko gakwenda geje mabuli gakwagilisa; ninga usungu wakwe imunhu yuya iyakwigala simbuli sokwagilisa!
40018008	Hambiya umukono ama umugulu wako unghakugolosa ugolose wihi, udumule, uutage kutali nagwe! Ibeka kwingila mu undewa wa kulanga kuhungukiligwa mukono ama mugulu, kusuma kuwa na mikono mili na migulu mili, na kutagigwa kumoto wa majuwa gose.
40018009	Na digiso dyako dinghakugolosa ugolose wihi, ding'ole uditage kutali nagwe, ibeka kwingila ku undewa wa kulanga kwina igiso dimwedu, kusuma kuwa na meso meli na kutagigwa kumoto uusikusima.”
40018010	“Mulangisise munghamubese yumwedu wa awadodogi wano; kosoko nikumutamilani fina malaika wawo kulanga majuwa gose wakulanga ichihanga che Babangu yowile kulanga.
40018011	Kosoko Mwana we Munhu keja yochihonya chagilile.
40018012	Mukona nhani? Imunhu yanghowa na ngholo igana, imwedu inghagilila, togola! Nghakusileka siya makumi ikenda na ikenda, hoyoluta kwitunda, na kuihananga aiya yagilile?
40018013	Ninga yanghayona, chawelu, nikumutamilani, yakuisekelela aiya lugano kusuma asiya makumi ikenda na ikende isene si sagilile.
40018014	No nheifo isikwendesa kumwande ye Babangu yowile kulanga fina yumwedu wa awadodogi wano yagilile.”
40018015	“Ne munduguso yanghakugolosela wihi, luta ukamulolese, agweye ne imwene mwiwene, yanghakuhulika, kumupata imunduguso.
40018016	Ninga, nghona nghakuhulika, londa hamwedu nagwe munhu yumwedu ama weli uleke kwa milomo ya wahomelesi weli ama wadatu.
40018017	Yanghaleka kuwahulika awene, ditamile dikanisa; na yanghaleka kudihulikisa dikanisa nadyo, yowe ukwako kifana munhu wa mataifa na mukonghosa kodi.”
40018018	“Chawelu nikumutamilani: Gogose gomukoha muisi, gakohigwa na kulanga; na gogose gomukugadoholela muisi, gakudoholigwa na kulanga.
40018019	Kahi nikumutamilani: Weli wenu wanghakifumilisa mbuli yoyose muisi, imbuli yoyose yowakwenda watase, wakwenda wagoloseligwe ne Babangu yowile kulanga.
40018020	Kosoko howowile weli ama wadatu wakitang'anyile kudisina dyangu, nani nabaho mugati yawo.”
40018021	Kahi Petulo hoyomulutila hoyomugamba, “Mundewa, mundugusangu yanigolosele uwihi kengahe nimulekele? Mpaka mikangha mufungate?”
40018022	Yesu hoyomugamba, “Sikukugamba mpaka mikangha mufungate, ninga mufungate mikangha makumi mufungate.
40018023	Kosoko iyo undewa wa kulanga ukifana na Mundewa yumonga yahananga kutala si mali sakwe na watumwa wakwe.
40018024	Yakakonge kuigolosa, hoyokwigaliligwa munhu iyakudaigwa talanda figulu ikumi.
40018025	Naye yakaswele chokuliha, iMundewa hoyogamba yaguligwe, imwene, ne muke, na wanagwe, na finhu fyose foyenafyo, uleke dideni diya dilihigwe.
40018026	Kamei imutumwa yuya, hakamufugamila yakugamba, ‘Mundewa nyonele ubasi, naniye nikwenda nikulihe fyose figima!’
40018027	iMundewa we mutumwa yuya yamonela ubasi, na kumudoholela, na kumulekelela dideni diya.
40018028	Imutumwa yuya yakalawe yamona yumonga imiyagwe woyendeyomudayi dinali igana du, hakamukola, mwilaka, yakugamba Unilihe dideni dyangu dyonikukudai!
40018029	Kamei imiyagwe hoyokugwa hamigulu yakwe, hoyomutasa, hoyogamba, ‘Nyonele ubasi, nani nokuliha!’
40018030	Ninga nghendile; hoyoluta, hoyomuguma muchifungo, mpaka yalihe dideni diya.
40018031	Kamei awayagwe wakone agagoloseke, howokalala lugano howoluta kumutamila iMundewa wawo gose gene gagoloseke.
40018032	Kamei iMundewa wakwe hoyomwinanga, hoyomugamba, ‘Agweye go mutumwa wihile! Nikulekelela di deni diya dyose, fowanitasile.
40018033	Agwe nagwe isagile kumonela ubasi imiyago, fina niye fonikonele ubasi agweye.’
40018034	iMundewa wakwe hoyokona nyono, hoyomwigala kuwakusambasa wanhu, mpaka yalihe dideni diya dyose.
40018035	Nofo iBaba wa kulanga yakwenda yamugoloseleni anyeye, munghaleka kuwalekelela kwa mimoyo yenu yose chila munhu ne munduguse.”
40019001	Kamei Yesu yakamale simbuli siso, hoyoleuka Galilaya, hoyekwingila kusimhaka sa Uyahudi, umwambu wa Yolodani.
40019002	Matewa makulu hogomwandamila, hoyowahonya uko.
40019003	Baho Amafalisayo howomulutila, howomugesa, howomugamba, “Togola fiswanu imunhu kumuleka imuke kosoko yoyose?”
40019004	Hoyobidula, hoyowagamba, “Musisomile fina yawombile kunghonga hakomba munhu mugosi na mwanamuke?
40019005	Hoyogamba, ‘Kosoko iyo imunhu yakumuleka iBabakwe ne ing'ina, yakiyandamile ne muke; na wano aweli wakuwa mutufi umwedu?’
40019006	Awano si weli kahi, ninga mutufi umwedu woyahasile Mulungu, imunhu yanghawatemanule.”
40019007	Howomugamba, “Hayuwa nhani Musa hakalagisa kumwingha ibaluwa ya malekeni, na kumuleka?”
40019008	Hoyowagamba, “Musa kosoko ya ukugutu we fidoga fyenu, kafumila muwaleke awake senu; ninga kulawa kunghonga isowile nheifo.
40019009	Aniye nikumugambani anyeye, chila munhu iyakumuleka imuke, ninga kosoko ya dihabwa, hoyotola yungi, yekwingilila; ayuya naye iyekumutola yalekigwe naye kengilila.”
40019010	Awefusa wakwe howomugamba, “Nghonaga simbuli se munhu ne muke nofosuwile nheifo, isagile kutola.”
40019011	Ninga imwene hoyowagamba, “Si wose wakudaha kuhokela imbuli ino, ninga awaya awakudahisigwa ne Mulungu.
40019012	Hena wanhu awekigwe ne Mulungu wowe mhende kulawa muinda ya wang'ina sawo, wabaho watendigwe na wanhu wowe mhende, na wabaho wakitendile mhende kosoko ya undewa wa kulanga. Iyekudaha kuihokela imbuli ino leka yaihokele.”
40019013	Kamei hoyokwigaliligwa wana wadodogi uleke yawekile mikono yakwe muchanhya yawo na kuwatasila; awefusa wakwe howowagombela.
40019014	Ninga Yesu hoyogamba, “Walekeni wana wadodogi weje ukwangu; munghawalemese, kosoko awafanile wawo, undewa wa kulanga ni wawo.”
40019015	Hoyowekila mikono muchanhya yawo, hoyoleuka uko.
40019016	Langa, imunhu yumonga hakamulutila hoyomugamba, “Mwalimu, nigolose chinhu chaki chiswanu uleke niupate uumi wa majuwa gose?”
40019017	Hoyomugamba, “Nhani ukunyusa imbuli ya uswanu? Imuswanu yumwedu du. Ninga unghahananga kwingila kuumi, ugakole amalagiso.”
40019018	Kamugamba, “Agehoki?” Yesu hoyogamba, “Agano, Unghakome, Unghengilile, Unghahije, Unghamuhomelele miyago udasi.
40019019	Wogohe iBabako ne ing'inako; Mwende imiyago fina fowukiyenda gomwecho.”
40019020	Imujelelo yuya hoyomugamba, “Ago gose nigakola nihungukiligwa na choni kahi?”
40019021	Yesu hoyomugamba, “Unghahananga uwe munhu yaliganile ulute ukambase ifinhu fyako fyose figuligwe, uwenghe awakiwa, kamei kokuwa na ugoli kulanga; kamei nyagula unyandamile.”
40019022	Imujelelo yuya yakahulike imbuli iyo, hoyoleuka na usungu, kosoko hakowa na finhu fingi.
40019023	Yesu hoyowagamba awefusa wakwe: “Chawelu, nikuwatamilani, ikuwa fikugutu kwe imugoli kwingila ku undewa wa kulanga.
40019024	Nikumutamilani kahi: Ni fihufu ingamia kwingila muchihengele che sing'ano, kusuma imugoli kwingila ku undewa we Mulungu.”
40019025	Awefusa wakwe wakahulike, siso howojuma lugano, howogamba, “Ninga nani iyakudaha kuhona?”
40019026	Yesu hoyowakumhulila ameso, yakugamba, “Kuwanhu adyo disikudahika. Ninga kwe Mulungu gose gakudahika.”
40019027	Noho Petulo yabidula yakugamba, “Langa aseye chileka fyose chikwandamila, chopata choni?”
40019028	Yesu hoyowagamba, “Chawelu, nikumutamilani, fina anyeye munyandamile niye, muchilunga ichisha, nghona yakayokwija Imwana we Munhu mu digoda dye ditunyo dyakwe, anye nanye mukwikala mumagoda ikumi na meli, mowaliganisa amakabila ikumi na meli ga Isilaeli.
40019029	Na chila munhu iyalekile nyumba, ama munduguse wa chigosi, ama wachike, ama iBabakwe, ama ng'ina, ama wana, ama migunda, kosoko ya disina dyangu, yakwenda yahokele mikangha igana, na kuhala undewa wa majuwa gose.
40019030	Ninga wengi awoile we nghonga; wakuwa we ndumo; na wendumo wakuwa we nghonga.”
40020001	“Kosoko undewa wa kulanga ukifana na imwenyenyumba, yelawile nhosikusiku kuhananga walimisi wakagolose milimo kumugunda wakwe we misabibu.
40020002	Naye hoyokifumilisa nawo kuwengha kwa ijuwa dinali imwedu, hoyowegala kumugunda we misabibu.
40020003	Hoyolawa kahi chigele cha saa tatu, hoyowona wamonga wemile hesoko wechaka milimo;
40020004	awene nawo hoyowagamba, ‘Luteni nanyeye kumugunda wangu we misabibu, na digelo dyenu nomwinghani. Howoluta.’
40020005	Hoyoleuka kahi muchipisi cha saa mutandatu, na saa ikenda, hoyogolosa nheifiya.
40020006	Ikafike saa ikumi na imwe, hoyoleuka, hoyofika wamonga wemile, hoyowagamba, ‘Nhani nyeye mwimile hano imisi yose bila milimo?’
40020007	Howomugamba, ‘Kosoko hachaka munhu yachinghile milimo.’ Hoyowagamba, ‘Luteni nanyeye kumugunda wangu we misabibu.’
40020008	“Dikoswe, ayuya imwenye mugunda hoyomulonga imunyamhala wakwe, wenange awalimisi, uwalihe digelo dyawo, ukongele wakunyuma mpaka wa kunghonga.”
40020009	Wakeje awaya wa saa kumi na imwedu, howohokela chila munhu dinali.
40020010	Awaya wa kunghonga wakeje hawamanya fina wohokela nyingi kusuma waya; awene nawo howohokela chila munhu dinali.
40020011	Wakamale kuhokela, howomukalalila imwenye nyumba,
40020012	wakugamba, “Awano wa kunyuma wagolosa milimo saa imwedu du, nagwe kuwaliganisa na seye chifinyilise misi yose?”
40020013	“Hakamubidula yumwedu wawo, yamugamba, ‘Mbwiyangu, sikonele hata, sichilagane na niye kwa dinali.
40020014	Londa iyako uleuke, nikwenda kumwingha yuno wa kunyuma fina gweye.
40020015	Isinogele niye kugolosa neifyangu fina fonikwenda nimwecho? Ama digiso dyako digaluka diha kosoko yaniye kuwa muswanu?’
40020016	No nheifo we ndumo wokuwa wa kunghonga, na wakunghonga wokuwa we ndumo.”
40020017	Baho Yesu yakowe yekugenda kuluta Yelusalemu, hoyowalonda awaya awefusa wakwe ikumi na weli we imwene; munjila hoyowagamba,
40020018	“Langisiseni! Chikukwila Yelusalemu, Imwana we Munhu yakwijagumigwa mumikono ya Makuhani na Watulumi, nawo wakwijamuliganisa yakomigwe;
40020019	Kamei wakumwigala kuwamataifa nawo uleke wamuseigile, kumutowa mikotya, na kumutungika; na dijuwa dya kadatu yakwinuka muchilalo.”
40020020	Noho ing'ina yawo awana wa Sebedayo yamulutila hamwedu na wanagwe, yakumufugamila, na kumutasa mbuli.
