40020021	Hoyomugamba, “Ukuhananga choni?” Hoyogamba, “Ulagise fina awanangu wano aweli wekale iyumonga umukono wako wo kulume, na iyumonga umukono wako wo kumoso, mu undewa wako.”
40020022	Yesu hoyobidula, hoyogamba, “Musimanyile dyomukutasa. Togoleni! Mukudaha kunywila ichikombe chonikunywila niye?” Howogamba, “Chikudaha.”
40020023	Hoyowagamba, “Chawelu mokunywila ichikombe changu; ninga kwikala umukono wangu wo kulume na mukono wangu wo kumoso, nechaka udaha wa kuwengha, ninga wakwinghigwa wekiligwe ne Babangu.”
40020024	Nawaya ikumi wakahulike howowasuhila awaya awandugu aweli.
40020025	Ninga Yesu hoyowenanga, hoyowagamba, “Mumanya fina awakulu wa Mataifa wakuwalongosani kwa ludole, na wakulu wawo, wakonesa uludole lwawo ukwawo.
40020026	Ninga isikuwa nhaifo ukwenu, ninga imunhu wowose yekuhananga kuwa mukulu ukwenu, na yowe mutumwa wenu;
40020027	imunhu wowose yakuhananga kuwa wa kunghonga ukwenu, na yowe mutumwa wenu;
40020028	fina imwana we Munhu fonghejile kutogomeligwa ninga kutogoma na kulafa uwumi wakwe uwe iliho dya wengi.”
40020029	Wakowe wekulawa Yeliko, itewa ikulu hodiwandamila.
40020030	Langa, mudula weli wekala hanghanda ye njila, nawo wakahulike fina Yesu yekuloka, hawekwinula majwi, wakugamba, “Uchonele ubasi, Uchonele ubasi, Mundewa, go Mwana wa Daudi!”
40020031	Amatewa howowagombela, wanyamale. Ninga awene howokongesa kwinula majwi, wekugamba, “Uchonele ubasi, Mundewa go Mwana wa Daudi!”
40020032	Yesu yeja yema, na kuwenanga, yakugamba, “Mukuhananga nimugoloseleni choni?”
40020033	Hawamugamba, “Mundewa, chikuhananga ameso getu gagubuligwe.”
40020034	Yesu yawonela ubasi, yawakwafa ameso gawo; baho ni baho howona, na kumwandamila.
40021001	Kamei wakasegelele Yelusalemu, na kwija Betifage, muditunda dya Miseituni, noho Yesu yawatuma awefusa wakwe weli, yakuwagamba,
40021002	“Luteni mpaka he chikaya chiya chi hamwande yenu, baho mokona dipunda dyohigwe hamwedu ne mwanagwe: Gadoholeni chimwande munigalile.
40021003	Na munhu yanghawosa mbuli, gambeni, ‘iMundewa yekugahananga,’ yakwenda yagowise chimwande.”
40021004	Aga gose galawanisa, uleke iliganile imbuli yalongigwe ne imugonesi yakugamba,
40021005	“Mutamileni Biti Sayuni, Langa iMundewa wako yakwija ukwako! Muholo, naye kakwila dipunda, Ne mwanagwe we dipunda, ichana che dipunda.”
40021006	Awaya awefusa wakwe howoleuka, howogolosa fina Yesu foyawatumile:
40021007	Howomwigalila dipunda ne mwanagwe, howokwika sisuke sawo muchanhya yawo, naye hoyokwikala muchanhya yakwe.
40021008	Amatewa makulu howotandalisa sisuke sawo mwibalabala, na wamonga howotema mahupi kulawa mumabiki na kugatandalisa mwibalabala.
40021009	Na amatewa agamulongolele na gamwandamile hogokwinula majwi “Hosana Mwana wa Daudi! Kamotesigwa ayuya iyakwija kudisina dye Mundewa! Hosana kuchanhya kulanga.”
40021010	Yakengile Yelusalemu, ikaya yose hoisingisika, wanhu wekugamba; Nani yuno?
40021011	Amatewa howogamba, “Ayuno no yuya imugonesi, Yesu, wa Nasaleti ya Galilaya.”
40021012	Yesu yengila kugati ye dihekalu dye Mulungu, na kuwawinga wose wende wokwambasa, na wende wogula mwihekalu, na kusibidula si mesa sa wendewobadilisha mapesa, na magoda gawo awende wakwambasa sinjiwa.
40021013	Hakawagamba, “Itulumigwa, ‘Inyumba yangu ikwinangwa nyumba ya kufugila.’ Amba nyeye muigolosa mhango ya wahiji.”
40021014	Ne midula, ne fiwete howomulutila umuya mwi hekalu, hakawahonya.
40021015	Ninga awakulu wa Makuhani na Watulumi, wakone majumo goyagolose, na wana wakwinula majwi gawo mwi hekalu, wakugamba, “Hosana, Mwana wa Daudi!” Hawasuha wakumugamba,
40021016	“Ukuhulika wanhu fowakulonga?” Yesu hakawagamba, “Heye, musinati musome kwa milomo ya wana wadodogi na wakongha kumemelesa ditunyo?”
40021017	Yakawaleke, hakalawa kunje ye kaya mpaka Betania, hakagona uko.
40021018	Ugele wa nhosikusiku foyoyage kwikaya, hakowa na njala.
40021019	Hakona musada hanghanda ye injila na kuulutila, hoyokona mwachaka chinhu ninga manyagala du. Kamei hoyogamba, “Ungheleke mamudyo. Kahi kulawa diyelo na majuwa gose.” Umusada hounyala baho ni baho.
40021020	Awefusa wakwe wakone, howokisina, howogamba, “Yanhani umusada unyalile baho ni baho?”
40021021	iYesu yabidula, na kuwagamba, “Chawelu, nikumutamilani, Munghowa na ihuwi, munghaleka kuwa na manhonge, mukwenda mugolose si didyo du dyo mutini, ninga mu kudaha kudigamba ditunda dino ‘Ng'oka ukatagigwe kubahali,’ ikwenda igoloseke.
40021022	Na dyo dyose dyomukutasa mumawombi genu, munghahuwila, mukuhokela.”
40021023	Kamei yakengile mwihekalu awakulu wa Makuhani, na wasehe wa wanhu, howomulutila ugele foyendeyofusa, howogamba, “Kwa udaha waki ukugolosa gano go ukugolosa? Naye nani yakwinghile udaha uwo?”
40021024	Yesu hoyobidula hoyowagamba, “Aniye nani nikumusani mbuli imwedu, ninga munghabidula, nikwende nimutamileni kwa udaha wani nikugolosa gano.
40021025	Ubatiso wa Yohana haulawa hoki? Haulawa kulanga ama ku wanhu?” Howokonga kuwa na lukani awecho kwa wecho, wakugamba, “Chinghagamba ulawa kulanga, yakwenda yachigambe, ‘Nhani musamuhuwile?’
40021026	Na chinghagamba, ‘Ulawa ku wanhu,’ chikogoha amatewa, kosoko awanhu wose wakumona Yohana fina ni mugonesi.”
40021027	Howomubidula Yesu howogamba, “Chisimanyile.” Naye hoyowagamba, “Aniye nani sikumutamilani anyeye ni kwa udaha waki nikugolosa gano.”
40021028	“Ninga, mukonanhani? Munhu yumonga hakowa na wana weli; kamulutila yuya we nghonga, hoyomugamba, ‘Mwanangu diyelo ulute ukagolose milimo kumugunda we misabibu.’
40021029	Hoyobidula na kugamba, ‘Nema!’ Ninga hanyuma hoyelamba na kuluta.
40021030	Hoyomulutila ayuya iwakeli, hoyolonga naye nheifiya, naye hoyobidula hoyogamba, ‘Nikuluta Mundewa,’ ninga hoyoleka kuluta.
40021031	Togoleni! Mu wano aweli no yehoki yagolose foyakwenda iBabakwe?” Howogamba, “Ayuya we nghonga.” Kamei Yesu, hoyowagamba, “Chawelu, Nikumutamilani, awakonghosa kodi na wedihabwa wakwenda walongole kumwande yenu kukwingila ku undewa we Mulungu.
40021032	Kosoko Yohana hakeja ukwenu kwa njila ya chawelu, anyeye homuleka kumuhuwila; ninga awakonghosa kodi na wadihabwa howomuhuwila, anye hata fomonile, nheifo musalambile mumuhuwile.”
40021033	Tegeleseni mbasi ingi, “Hakuwa na munhu imwenye nyumba, iyahandile mugunda wakwe we misabibu, hoyojengela ikigo, hoyokata ikolongo dyo kukamila si sabibu, hoyojenga ilingo, hoyokwika wanhu wo kugolosa milimo, hoyoluta nhambo.
40021034	Ugele sisabibu sikakonge kuwa habehi na kwifa; hoyowatuma awatumwa kuwaya awakwimilisa mugunda, wahokele umudyo.
40021035	Awaya awemilisi howowakola awatumwa wakwe, ayuno howomutowa, na yumonga howomukoma, yumonga howomutowa na mawe.
40021036	Hakatuma kahi watumwa wengi kusuma awaya wa kunghonga, hawawatenda nheifiya.
40021037	Kundumo hakamutuma imwanagwe ukwawo, yakugamba, ‘Wakwenda wamogohe imwanangu,’
40021038	Ninga awemilisi wakamone ayuya imwana hawalonga, awecho kwa wecho, ‘Ayuno no muhasi; handikoni chimukome! Kamei chilonde uhasi wakwe.’
40021039	Hawamukola, hawamulafa kunje yo mugunda we misabibu, howomukoma.
40021040	Nghona yakwija ayuya imwenyemugunda we misabibu kowatenda nhani awemilisi?”
40021041	Howomugamba, “Yakwenda yawakome fibi awaya awemilisi wehile No umugunda we misabibu yakwenda yawenghe wemilisi wengi, awakwenda wamwinghe si sabibu ku ugele wakwe.”
40021042	Yesu hakawagamba, “Musinati musome mu matulumo? ‘Diwe dyowalemile awajengaji, Adyo digaluka diwe dikulu dye inghindiso!’
40021043	Kosoko iyo nikumutamilani, Undewa wa Mulungu, ukuleusigwa ukwenu, wakwenda wenghigwe ditaifa dingi idikweleka mamudyo gakwe.
40021044	Naye yakwenda yogwe mudiwe didyo, yakudumuka fiponge ponge; na yuya imwene dikwende dimugwile dikumutiginha tiki tiki.”
40021045	Awakulu wa Makuhani na Mafalisayo, wakahulike si mbasi sakwe, hawatanga fina yakuwalonga awene.
40021046	Ninga fowahanangage kumukola, howokogoha amatewa, kosoko awene hawamona fina mugonesi.
40022001	iYesu hakabidula, hakawatamila kahi kwa mbasi, yakugamba,
40022002	“Undewa wa kulanga ukifana Mundewa yumonga, yamugolosela imwanagwe halusi.
40022003	Hoyowatuma awatumwa wakwe wawenange awaya awagonekigwe kwija kuhalusi; nawo howolema kwija,
40022004	Hoyotuma kahi watumwa wengi, yakugamba, ‘Watamileni awaya awagonekigwe, Langeni, nifulusa kugolosa ifyakudiya fyangu; sing'ombe sangu na finonile fifulusa kuchinjigwa, na fyose fifuluka, mwije kuhalusi.’
40022005	Ninga hawona si chinhu, howoleuka, yumonga kaluta kumugunda wakwe: Yumonga kubiyashala yakwe,
40022006	awasigale howowakola awatumwa wakwe, howowatenda fibi na kuwakoma.
40022007	Kamei iMundewa yuya hoyosuha; hoyokwigala wasilikali wakwe we inghondo, howowakoma awakomaji waya na kuisoma ikaya yawo.
40022008	Kamei, hoyowagamba awatumwa wakwe, ‘Ugele we halusi ufika, ninga awaya awagonekigwe wasagiligwe.
40022009	Handikoni luteni kusinjila mhanda sa mabalabala, na wose womukona wenangeni weje kudikumbo.’
40022010	Awatumwa waya hawalawa na kulata kusinjila singhulu, howowalonda wose wowawonile, awehile na waswanu; dikumbo dye halusi hadimema wageni.
40022011	“Ninga foyengile iMundewa yuya kuwalanga awageni wakwe, hoyokona umuya munhu yumwedu yechaka suke ye halusi.
40022012	Hakamugamba, ‘Mbwiyangu, kwingila nhani muno nagwe kwechaka suke ya halusi?’ Hoyonyamala twi.
40022013	iMundewa hoyowagamba awatumwa wakwe, ‘Moheni, imikono ne migulu, mulondeni mukamutage kuchisa cha kunje, no kukwenda kuwe chililo na kugwegwejula meno.’
40022014	Kosoko wengi awakwinangigwa, amba wakusaguligwa wakefu.”
40022015	Noho Mafalisayo howoluta, howogolosa mulundo, uleke wamutege kwa simbuli sakwe.
40022016	Howotuma ukwakwe awefusa wawo hamwedu na Mahelodi, hawagamba, “Mwalimu, chimanya agweye kwa munhu wa chawelu ne injila ya Mulungu ukuifusa mu chawelu kahi nghukogoha ukulu we munhu wowose, kosoko nghukulanga sifuta sa wanhu.
40022017	Haya chitamile, Ukona nhani. Ni fiswanu kumwingha Kaisali kodi, ama si fiswanu?”
40022018	Ninga iYesu hakamanya uwihi wawo, hakagamba, “Nhani mukunigesa anyeye mwine ichimwefe?
40022019	Nyoneseni ifesa ye kodi!” Howomwigalila dinali.
40022020	Hakawagamba, “Isanamu ino yani, ne anuwani ino?”
40022021	Howomugamba, “Ni ya Kaisali.” Hakawagamba, “Basi muliheni Kaisali age Kaisali, ne Mulungu age Mulungu.”
40022022	Wakahulike, hawajuma; hawamuleka, na kuleuka.
40022023	Dijuwa didyo, Masadukayo, wanhu wakugamba kwichaka kwinuka awanhu wafile, howomulutila, howomusa,
40022024	wakugamba, “Mwalimu, Musa yagamba fina, imunhu yanghafa, nghona nghalekile mwana, imunduguse yamutole imwigane yuya yowe muke, kosoko yamwelekele imunduguse cheleko.
40022025	Hambiya, ukwetu hakuwa wandugu mufungate, iwenghonga hoyotola, hoyokufa, kosoko nghalekile mwana, hoyomulekela imunduguse imuke,
40022026	Nheifo na wakeli naye, na wakadatu mpaka wose mufungate.
40022027	Hanyuma ya wose ayuya mwanamuke naye hoyokufa.
40022028	Dijuwa dye ndumo ye chilunga yakwenda yowe muke wa yehoki? Kosoko wose mufungate hawowa naye.”
40022029	Yesu hoyobidula, hoyowagamba, “Mwagilila! Kosoko musimanyile matulumo kahi udaha we Mulungu.
40022030	Kosoko ku ndumo ye chilunga wasikutola kahi wasikutoligwa, ninga wakuwa kifana malaika wa kulanga.
40022031	Kahi, imbuli ya wafile kwinuka, musisomile imbuli ilongigwe na Mulungu, yakugamba,
40022032	‘Aniye na Mulungu wa Ibulahimu, na Mulungu wa Isaka, na Mulungu wa Yakobo.’ Si Mulungu wa wafile, ninga wa womi.”
40022033	Na matewa wakahulike, howojuma kosoko ya mafuso gakwe.
40022034	Na Amafalisayo wakahulike fina Yesu kawanyamasa Masadukayo, hawakitanganyila hamwedu.
40022035	Yumwedu wawo, mulahi, hoyomusa, kwa kumugesa,
40022036	“Mwalimu, Mu tolati ligasilo dikulu no dihoki?”
40022037	Hakamugamba, “Umwende Mundewa Mulungu wako kwa umoyo wako wose, na chidoga chako chose, na misungu yako yose.
40022038	Adino no dilagiso dikulu, kahi no dya kunghonga.
40022039	Na dya keli dikifana na didino, nadyo no dino: ‘Umwende imiyago fina foukiyenda agweye gomwecho.’
40022040	Malagiso gose ga Musa na mafuso ga wagonesi gakwegamila mumalagiso agano ameli.”
40022041	Amafalisayo wakakitanganyile hamwedu, Yesu hoyowosa, yekuwagamba,
40022042	“Anyeye mukona nhani muchanhya ya Kilisito? Togoleni ni mwana wani? Howomubidula, wa Daudi.”
40022043	Yesu hoyowagamba, “Ikudahika nhani fina kwa udaha wa Muhe Daudi yakumwinanga imwene Mundewa? Yekugamba,
40022044	‘Mundewa hoyomutamila Mundewa wangu, Ikala ukulume kwangu, mpaka niweke awanghondo wako hasi ye migulu yako.’
40022045	Daudi hona yakumwinanga Kilisito iMundewa, yakuwa nhani mwanagwe?”
40022046	Hachaka munhu kahi yadahile kumubidula. Na kulawa dijuwa didyo hechaka yadahile kumusa iswali.
40023001	Kamei Yesu hakawagamba amatewa na wefusa wakwe, fina,
40023002	“Awatulumi na Mafalisayo wekala mwigoda dya Musa,
40023003	ninga, gose gawakumutamilani mugakole na kugagolosa, ninga kusinhenda sawo munghagolose; kosoko awene wakulonga ninga wasikugolosa.
40023004	Awene wakoha makanda masito na kuwatwika awanhu mu mayega gawo; awene awecho wasikwenda kugasegesa makanda gaya ne fidole fyawo.
40023005	Kahi sinhenda sawo sose wakugolosa uleke wonigwe na wanhu, wakufala mikanda mikulu ina simbuli sa Mulungu siandikigwe, wakugalamula amapindo ga makasu gawo.
40023006	Wakwenda amagoda ga kumwande mumajuwa ge sikukuu na kwikala kumwande mumasinagogi;
40023007	na kulamusigwa mumagulilo, na kwinangigwa na wanhu, ‘Labi’.
40023008	Ninga anyeye munghenangigwe ‘Labi’, kosoko iMwalimu wenu yumwedu anye wose mwa ndugu.
40023009	Munghamwinange munhu ‘Baba’, muchilunga, kosoko mwina Baba yenu yumwedu, iyowile kulanga.
40023010	Kahi munghenangigwe Filongosi, kosoko ichilongosi wenu yumwedu, imwene no Kilisito.
40023011	Mukulu wenu yakuwa mutumwa wenu.
40023012	Na wowose iyakiinula yakudulisigwa, na wowose iyekidulisa, yekukwisigwa.”
40023013	“Usungu wenu, watulumi na Mafalisayo! Mwine chimwefe! Kosoko mukuwa hindila awanhu undewa wa kulanga, anye muwecho musikwingila, na awaya awakuhananga kwingila musikuwaleka wengile!
40023014	Usungu wenu watulumi na Mafalisayo, mwine chimwefe! Kosoko mukudiya musinyumba sa wegane na kwa chimwefe mukutasa nhasa nhali; kosoko iyo mukupata uliganiso mukulu lugano.
40023015	Usungu wenu watulumi na Mafalisayo! Mwine chimwefe! Kosoko mukusunguluta kuisi na kubahali kumugolosa munhu yabiduke na kumwandamilani, kamei nomoyabiduke yakuwa mwana wa jehanumu mikangha mili kusuma anyeye muwecho.
40023016	“Usungu wenu mufilongosi mudula, anyeye mukugamba, imunhu yekilaha kwa dihekalu, siyo chinhu; ninga iyakilaha kwa sahabu ya kwi hekalu, kakiyoha.
40023017	Mubwalata nyeye! Kahi mwa mudula inghulu no ihoki, aiya hefugilo, ama adiya dihekalu idikuisunha hefugilo?
40023018	Kahi anyeye mukugamba imunhu yakilaha kwa mumasabahu si chinhu; ninga yanghakilaha kwa digelo duwile mu masabahu, yakiyoha.
40023019	Mwafidula nyeye! Kosoko inghulu no ihoki, adiya digelo, ama amafugilo agakusunha digelo?
40023020	Basi ayuya yakilaha kwa mafugilo, yakilaha kwa iyo na kwa ifinhu fyose fuwile muchanhya yakwe;
40023021	naye iyakilaha kwa dihekalu, yakilaha kwa didyo, na kwa yuya iyakwikala mugati yakwe;
40023022	na iyakilaha kwa ulanga, yakilaha kudigoda dyo undewa we Mulungu, na kwa imwene iyakudikalila.
40023023	“Usungu wenu watulumi na Mafalisayo! Mwine chimwefe! Kosoko mulafa filafywa fya munanaa, bisali na jila, ninga muleka simbuli singhulu se malagiso naso no usindamafu, ubasi, na dihuwi; ago iwagila kugagolosa, ninga gaya gamonga munghagaleke.
40023024	Filongosi mudula mukuchuja ujuguni mukumesa ingamia!
40023025	Usungu wenu watulumi na Mafalisayo! Mwine chimwefe! Kosoko mukusunha kunje ye fikombe na mabakuli kugati yakwe fimema uhiji na upujili.
40023026	Agwe Gomufalisayo chidula! Yenda kusunha, kugati ye chikombe, ne sahani uleke kunje yakwe nako kuwe kuswanu!
40023027	“Usungu wenu, watulumi na Mafalisayo, mwine chimwefe! Kosoko mukifana filalo fibakigwe swakaya, nafyo kunje fikoneka fiswanu, ninga kugati fimema maguha ga wanhu wafile na uwafu wose.
40023028	No nheifo anye nanye, kwa kunje mukoneka fina wanhu waswanu, ninga kugati mumema chimwefe na wihi.”
40023029	“Usungu wenu watulumi na Mafalisayo! Mwine chimwefe! Kosoko mukujengela ifilalo fya wagonesi na kuhamba ifilalo fya wanhu waswamu;
40023030	mukugamba, ‘Nhanga aseye chowile uko ugele wa waBaba setu, chisowile chikihasa nawo musakame ya wagonesi.’
40023031	Mukihomelela muwecho fina anyeye mwa wana wawo awawakomile awagonesi!
40023032	Chimemeleseni ichipimo cha wababasenu!
40023033	Anyeye mumajoka, cheleko cha majoka! Moitija nhani iliganiswa kwa jehanumu?
40023034	Kosoko iyo, mulangisise, aniye nikwigala ukwenu awagonesi na wena imisungu na watulumi; wamonga mukwende muwakome na kuwatungika, na wamonga mukwenda muwatowe mumasinagogi genu, na kuwawinga kulawa kaya mpaka kaya;
40023035	kwa nheifo ikwija muchanhya yenu isakame yose ya wanhu waswanu iitike mu iisi, kukongela sakame ya Habili, ayuya iwechawelu mpaka isakame ya Sakalia imwanagwe wa Balakia, yomwakomile hagati gati ya ahasunhile na masabahu.
40023036	Chawelu, nikumutamilani: Simbuli siso sose sikwenda sije muchanhya ye cheleko chino!”
40023037	“Agwe Yelusalemu, Yelusalemu! Go ukukoma awagonesi, na kuwatowa na mawe awaya awatumigwe ukwako! Ni mikangha mingahi nihananga kukunyatila hamwedu awanago fina inghuku foikukunyagisa hamwedu ifyanagwe hasi ye mabawa gakwe, ninga musendile!
40023038	Mulangisise, Inyumba yenu ikusimiligwa na kulekigwa.
40023039	Kosoko nikumutamilani, Musikwenda munyone kahi kulawa hambiya, mpaka fomukwija mugamba, ‘Kamotesigwa iyakwija kwe disina dye Mundewa.’”
40024001	Yesu hakaleuke, mwihekalu; awefusa wakwe hawamulutila, uleke wamonese amajengo ge dihekalu.
40024002	Imwene hakawabidula, “Mukugona agano gose? Chawelu, nikumutamilani: Disikusigala ahano diwe muchanhya ye diwe idyene disikumoligwa.”
40024003	Hata foyeja yekala muditunda dya Miseituni, awefusa wakwe howomwijila kwa chinyele, wakugamba, “Chitamile simbuli sino sikuwa milaki. Ne chitangilo cho kwija kwako chikuwa choni, na indumo ye chilunga?”
40024004	Yesu yabidula, yakuwagamba, “Mulangisise imunhu yanghawadanhiliseni.
40024005	Kosoko wengi wakwenda weje kwi disina dyangu, wakugamba ‘Aniye no ni Kilisito!’ Nawo wakwenda wawadanhilise wengi.
40024006	Mohulika simbuli se singhondo; na fununu se singhondo; mulangisise, munghogohe; kosoko ago gakwenda galawanise; ninga indumo iyecho inghali.
40024007	Kosoko ditaifa dimwedu dikwinuka na dikitowa na ditaifa dingi; undewa kitowa na undewa; kukwenda kuwe na njala, na disingisi dye iisi kose kose.
40024008	Ago gose no nghonga ya usungu kifana wakweleka kwa mwanamuke.
40024009	“Ugele uwo wakwenda wamugumeni mu magayo, nawo womukomani, nanye mukuwa wanhu wasuligwe na wanhu wose kosoko ya disina dyangu.
40024010	Noho wengi wokuya kunyuma, kisongesa na kisula.
40024011	Wagonesi wengi wa udasi wakwija walawanisa, na kuwadanhilisa wengi.
40024012	Kosoko ya kongeseka uwihi, uwendo wa wanhu wengi ukwija uhola.
40024013	Ninga iyakufinyilisa mpaka kundumo, noyakwenda yahone.
40024014	Kahi imbuli iswanu ya undewa ikwija ihubiliigwa muchilunga yuwe uhomelesi ku mataifa gose; aho noho iya indumo ikwija.”
40024015	“Ugele womukamukona Disinhu dihile dya kubana, adiya dyalongigwe ne mugonesi Danyeli, dima ahanhu asunhile (iyakusoma yamanye).
40024016	Noho wowile Uyahudi watijile kumatunda,
40024017	na yowile ukano yanghahumuluke kulonda ifinhu fuwile munyumba yakwe,
40024018	yowile kumugunda yanghoye ukaya kulonda si suke sakwe;
40024019	Usungu wawo awena siinda na wakonghesa majuwa gago!
40024020	Mutase uleke kutija kwenu kunghowe ichigele che imheho au dijuwa dye sabato!
40024021	Kosoko ugele uwo kukwija kukuwa lwidaso lugano, agene gasinati goneke gafanile gago kulawa kunghonga ye chilunga mpaka ugele uno, kahi isikwijaikuwa nheifo kahi.
40024022	Nhanga amajuwa gago woile gasahunguligwe, nghowile yakuhona munhu wowose yuya; ninga kosoko ya wasaguligwe majuwa ago gohunguligwa.
40024023	“Ugele uwo imunhu yanghawagamba, ‘Langa Kilisito! Kowa hano’, ama ‘kowa kuya’, munghahuwile.
40024024	Kosoko gakwenda galawanise Makilisito ga udasi, na wagonesi wa udasi, wogolosa fitangilo fingi na majumo; wawagilise, inghadahika du hata waya awasaguligwe.
40024025	Langa! Nifulusa kumutamilani gasinati galawanise.
40024026	Waghamugambani, ‘Langa kowa kunyika!’ Munghaleuke; ‘kowa kumabuha ga kugati!’ Munghahuwile.
40024027	Kosoko fina ulumwemwe foukoneka kulawa kundawilo ye dijuwa mpaka kukuswila dijuwa, nofo kukwenda kuwe kukwija kwakwe Imwana we Munhu.
40024028	Hena umufimba noho sikitanganyila si numba.”
40024029	“Chimwande, kulawa kwidasigwa kwa majuwa gago, dijuwa dikugumigwa chisa, umwesi nawo usikwijalafa ujelu wakwe, na sinyelesi sikwija silagala kulawa kulanga, uludole lwa kulanga losingisika,
40024030	Noho chikwija chikoneka ichitangilo chakwe iMwana we Munhu kulanga; noho amataifa gose ge chilunga gakwija golila, wekwija wamona iMwana we Munhu yakwija mumafunde ga kulanga na ludole na ditunyo ikulu.
40024031	Yakwija yowatuma malaika wakwe ne dijwi dikulu dyo lwinango nawo wakwenda wawakonghole awasagulwe kulawa si sandi sose ine, we digunda kulawa ulwandi luno lwe ndumo yo ulanga mpaka ulwandi luya lwe indumo yo ulanga.”
40024032	“Kwibiki dyo mutini mukifuse imbasi; manhambi gakwe ganghalafa na kusanhula manyagala, mukutanga fina ugele we dibahu wahabehi;
40024033	anye nanye nhaifo, fomukugona ago gose, mutange fina kahabehi, hamulango.
40024034	Chawelu, nikuwatamilani, Icheleko chino chisikuloka, mpaka ago gose gamemelesigwe.
40024035	Ulanga ne chilunga fikuloka; ninga simbuli sangu sisikuloka ng'o.”
40024036	“Ninga dijuwa diya na ugele uya hechaka iyamanyile, kahimalaika wowile kulanga, kahiiMwana; ninga iBaba yemwene.
40024037	Kosoko fina mumajuwa ga Nuhu nofo kukuwa kukwija kwakwe iMwana we Munhu.
40024038	Kosoko fina amajuwa gaya Difaluko foduwile dikali, awanhu fowendawodiya, na kunywa, wakutola na kutoligwa, mpaka dijuwa diya doyengila Nuhu musafina;
40024039	wasamanyile mpaka Digalika fodejile, hodiwalonda wose, nofo kukwenda kuwe kwakwe iMwana we Munhu.
40024040	Ugele uwo wanhu weli wokuwa kumugunda; yumonga yakulondigwa, yumonga yekulekigwa;
40024041	wanawake weli wakuwa wakusaga: Yumonga yakulondigwa, yumonga yakusigala.
40024042	Mwikale meso; kosoko musimanyile dijuwa dihoki dyo yakayokwija Mundewa wenu.
40024043	“Ninga mumanye imbuli ino; imwenyenyumba nhanga yamanyile dijuwa dyo yakwija imuhiji, nhanga yekale meso, nghowile yakuleka inyumba yakwe ibenigwe.
40024044	Kosoko iyo anye nanye, ikaleni meso, kosoko isaa yo musimanyile Mwana we Munhu yakwija.”
40024045	“No nani imutumwa, yekuhuwiligwa, na yene misungu. Imwene yalekeligwe ne Mundewa wakwe inyumba yakwe, yawenghe wanhu ichakudiya ku ugele wakwe?
40024046	Ibeka imutumwa yuya imwene, iMundewa wakwe foyakwija yamufike yakugolosa nheifo.
40024047	Chawelu, kumutamilani, yakwenda yamwike kulangisisa ifinhu fyakwe fyose.
40024048	Ninga imutumwa yuya yehile yanghagamba mu moyo wakwe, ‘iMundewa yekuchelewa,’
40024049	yanghakonga kuwatowa wayagwe na kudiya na kunywa hamwedu na walefi.
40024050	iMundewa wakwe imutumwa yuya yakayakwija dijuwa dyonghamanyile na isaa yonghamanyile.
40024051	Yakumudumula mahindi meli, na kumwika hamwedu na wechimwefe, no kokuwa chililo na kugwegwejula meno.”
40025001	“Noho undewa wa kulanga ukwija uliganiswa na wali ikumi, awalonda sitaa sawo, howolawa kuluta kumuhokela bwana halusi.
40025002	Washano wawo howokuwa wabwalasi, na washano wena misungu.
40025003	Awaya awabwalasi howolonda sitaa sawo, howoleka kulonda na mafuta;
40025004	ninga awaya awene misungu howolonda sitaa sawo na mafuta gasigafu mufiya fyawo.
40025005	Kamei ibwana halusi yakachelewe kwija, wose howasisila howogona.
40025006	Ninga muchilo gati, hokuwa na chowe, ‘Handikoni, ibwana halusi keja mumuhokele!’
40025007	“Chimwande, hawaleuka, awali waya wose na kugolosa sitaa sawo.
40025008	Awaya awabwalasi howowalonga awene misungu, ‘Chingheni amafuta genu makefu du, kosoko sitaa setu sikusima.’
40025009	Ninga waya wene misungu hawawabidula wakugamba, ‘Kaa, gasikuchenela aseye na nyeye; ibeka mulute kumaduka, mukagule.’
40025010	Ugele awaya wakalute kukugula; ibwana halusi keja. Awaya awowile baho howokwingila hamwedu naye kuhalusi, umulango howuhindigwa.
40025011	“Howokwija awamonga waya, wakugamba, ‘Mundewa, Mundewa! Chikumulile!’
40025012	Hakawabidula, yakuwagamba, ‘Chawelu, nikumutamilani, siwamanyileni nyeye.’
40025013	Mwikale meso, kosoko musimanyile dijuwa kahi ugele.”
40025014	“Kosoko ikifana imunhu yakuluta kunhambo, hakawenanga awatumwa wakwe, hakeka isawo yakwe ukwawo.
40025015	Hakamwingha yumonga talanda shano, yumonga talanda mbili, yumonga talanda imwedu; chila yumwedu kaliganiswa ifene fyo yakudaha, kamei hakaluta.
40025016	Chimwande ayuya yenghigwe talanda shano, hakaluta kwambasa na si talanda siya, na kupata talanda singi shano.
40025017	Nheifo ayuya naye we simbili, naye hakapata talanda singi mbili.
40025018	Ninga ayuya yahokele talanda imwedu, hakaluta na kufukula hasi, na kufisa italanda ye Mundewa wakwe.
40025019	“Gakaloke majuwa mengi hakeja, iMundewa wa watumwa waya, hakatala ifesa iya hamwedu nawo.
40025020	Yakeje ayuya yahokele talanda shano, na kwigala talanda singi shano, hakagamba, ‘Mundewa hakwika ukwangu talanda shano, Langa nipata talanda singi shano.’
40025021	iMundewa wakwe hakamugamba, ‘Fiswamu, mutumwa muswamu, na wakuhuwilwa! Hakuhuwiligwa kwa makefu, nikwenda nikwike muchanhya ya mengi. Ingila mu chinyemi che Mundewa wako!’
40025022	“Hakeja ayuya iyahokela sitalanda mbili, hakagamba, ‘Mundewa, hakwika ukwangu talanda mbili. Langa nipata talanda singi mbili.’
40025023	iMundewa wakwe hakamugamba, ‘Fiswamu, mutumwa muswamu na wakuhuwilwa! Hakuhuwiligwa kwa makefu, nikukwika muchanhya ya mengi. Ingila mu chinyemi che Mundewa wako!’
40025024	“Kamei hakeja na ayuya iyahokele italanda imwedu, hakagamba, ‘Mundewa, hanimanya agweye kwa munhu mukugutu; ukugola honghuhandile, ukulunda honghwanjase.
40025025	Kamei hanyogoha, haniluta na kufisa italanda yako musanga. Langa! Aino no iiya iyako.’
40025026	“Mundewa wakwe yabidula, yakumugamba, ‘Agwe kwa mutumwa wihile na mudoba! Hakumanya fina nikugola hosihandile, nikulunda, hosanjase;
40025027	Haikwagila kwikisa isawo yangu ku wakwambasa na kulafa nyongesa, nani fonikwija nipate iyangu ne nyongesa yakwe.
40025028	Muhokeni italanda iyo, mwingheni ayuya iyenaso ikumi.
40025029	Kosoko chila iyena chinhu yekwinghigwa, na kongesigwa telele; ninga iyechaka, hata achiya cho yenacho yakuhokigwa.
40025030	Na imutumwa yuya yehile, mumutage kutali ku chisa cha kunje, no kukuwa chililo na kugwegwejula meno.’”
40025031	“Nghona yakwija iMwana we Munhu mu ditunyo dyakwe, hamwedu na malaika wasunhile wose, noho yekwikala mwigoda dyakwe dya ditunyo dya undewa wakwe;
40025032	kumwande yakwe wakwenda wakitang'anyile awanhu wa mataifa gose, naye yakwenda yawabagule fina imudimi foyakubagula singholo na simhene;
40025033	yakusika singholo umukono wakwe wo kulume na simhene umukono wakwe wo kumoso.
40025034	Kamei Mundewa yakuwagamba awaya awowile kumukono wakwe wokulume; ‘Wijeni, anyeye mulugutiswe ne Babangu! Muhale undewa womwikiligwe kulawa kukumbigwa kwe chilunga;
40025035	kosoko hanuwa na njala, homuningha chakudiya, hanuwa na nghilu homunigha meji go kunywa; hanuwa mugeni, hamunihokela.
40025036	Hanuwa mwasi; hamunifasa, hanuwa mutamu; hamwija munilanga, hanuwa kuchifungo; homunijila.’
40025037	“Noho awanhu waswamu, womubidula, ‘Mundewa, milaki fochakonile kwina njala, hochikwingha chakudiya, ama kwina nghilu hochikwingha meji?
40025038	Kahi milaki fochakonile kwa mugeni, hochikukalibisha, ama kwa mwasi hochikufasa?
40025039	na kahi milaki chakonile umutamu, kahi kwa muchifungo, hochikwijila?’
40025040	iMundewa yakuwabidula yekuwagamba, ‘Chawelu, nikumutamilani, ifyene fyomumugolosele yumwedu wa wano awandugusangu awadodogi, munigolosela niye.’
40025041	“Kamei yakuwalonga awaya awowile umukono wakwe wo kumoso, ‘Leukeni ukwangu, muligitiswe, mulute ku umoto wa majuwa gose! Woyafuluse kwikiligwa iLuhoma na malaika wakwe;
40025042	kosoko hanuwa na njala, musaninghile chakudiya; hanuwa na nghilu; musaninghile meji;
40025043	hanuwa mugeni; musanihokele, hanuwa mwasi; musanifasile, hanuwa mutamu na muchifungo; musejile kunilanga.’
40025044	“Kamei nawo wakubidula, wakugamba, ‘Mundewa milaki, fochakonile agweye kwina njala kahe kwina nghilu, kahe kwa mugeni, kahe kwa mwasi, kahe kwa mutamu, kahe kwa muchifungo, hochileka kukutogomela?’
40025045	Yakwenda yawabidule, yekugamba, ‘Chawelu nikuwatamilani, ifyene fo musimugolosele yumwedu wa awa awadodogi, musinigolosele niye.’
40025046	Kamei awo nawo wakwenda walute kwingila mu usungu wa majuwa gose; ninga awanhu waswamu wakuluta ku wumi wa majuwa gose.”
40026001	Yesu yakamale kulonga simbuli siso sose, hoyowagamba awefusa wakwe,
40026002	“Mumanya fina fogakuloka majuwa meli ikuwa Pasaka, ne Mwana we Munhu yakwenda yasongesigwe na kukomigwa kwa kutungikigwa mwibiki.”
40026003	Ugele uwo awakulu wa makuhani na wasehe wa wanhu, weja wakitang'anyila mudijumba dye Kuhani Mukulu, iyenangagwa Kayafa;

40026005	Ninga howogamba, “Unghowe ugele we sikukuu, ungheje ulawanisa mugogolo ku wanhu.”
40026006	Imwene Yesu hoyokuwa Betania munyumba ya Simoni mukoma,
40026007	mwanamuke yene chichupa cha mafuta ga malihamu, ga diliho ikulu lugano hakamusegelela na kumwitilila mwitwi dyakwe ugele yekale hachakudiya.
40026008	Awefusa wakwe wakone nhaifo, howosuha, howogamba, “Hasala yaki ino?
40026009	Kosoko amafuta gano hagowa gakudaha kuguligwa kwa mapesa mengi howogawiligwa awakiwa.”
40026010	Yesu yakamanye, hoyowagamba, “Nhani mukumwidasa imwanamuke? Kosoko kanigolosela chinhu chiswanu.
40026011	Kosoko majuwa gose awakiwa mwinawo hamwedu nanye, ninga niye si hamwedu nanye majuwa gose.
40026012	Kosoko kwa kunyitilila umutufi wangu amafuta gano, kagolosa nhaifo kosoko ya kutandila amasiko gangu.
40026013	Chawelu, nimukuwatamilani, chila ahakuhubiliigwa imbuli iswamu muchilunga chose, ichinhu chino choyagolose chotambuligwa, kosoko ya kumugelegela.”
40026014	Ugele uwo iyumonga wa waya ikumi na weli, disina dyakwe Yuda Isikalioti, hakawalutila awakulu wa makuhani,
40026015	hakagamba Moningha choni, ninghamulafa ukwenu? Howomuliha fipande makumi madatu fya fesa.
40026016	Kulawa ugele uwo yende yohananga luneka lwa kumusongesa.
40026017	Dijuwa dya kukonga dye mikate isigumigwe nungo, awefusa wakwe hawamulutila Mundewa Yesu, na kumugamba, “Ukuhananga chigolose hoki uleke ukadiile iPasaka?”
40026018	Hakagamba, “Luteni ukaya kwa munhu yumonga, Mukamugambe: ‘Mwalimu yekugamba; ugele wangu wahabehi; ukwako nikuhananga nigolose iPasaka hamwedu na wefusa wangu.’”
40026019	Awefusa hawagolosa fina Yesu foyawasigilile kamei hawaitandila iPasaka.
40026020	Ikowe hegulo hakekala hachakudiya hamwedu na waya wefusa wakwe ikumi na weli.
40026021	Fowendewodiya, hakagamba, “Chawelu nikumutamilani, Yumwedu wenu yakunisongesa.”

40026024	Imwana we Munhu yakuluta ifene foyaandikiigwe, ninga usungu wakwe imunhu yuya imwene yekumusongesa imwana wa Munhu! Hayuwa ibeka kwe munhu yuyo yowile nghelekigwe!”
