41001012	Chimwande Muhe Musunhile kamulongosa kunyika.
41001013	Naye yowa uko kunyika kwa majuwa makumi mane; yakugesigwa na Luhoma, yowaga na makewe ga kumbago, na malaika wende womutogomela.
41001014	Hambiya, Yohana yakohigwe, Yesu yeja Galilaya, yakuhubili imbuli swanu ye Mulungu
41001015	yakugamba, “Ugele wija, undewa we Mulungu usegelela, Mulambe, na kuihuwila imbuli swanu.”
41001016	Ugele foyagendage munghingi ye bahali ya Galilaya, yamona Simoni ne munduguse Andelea, wakuguma ulwafu lwawo mubahali, kosoko hawowa walowaji wa somba.
41001017	Yesu yawagamba, “Nyandamileni, nani nowagolosa muwe walowa wanhu.”
41001018	Kamei chimwande wejawaleka si nyafu sawo na kumwandamila.
41001019	Hawaluta hamwande habehibehi, hawamona Yakobo wa Sebedayo, na Yohana imunduguse, nawo nheifiya hawowa mu chiya, wakusigolosa si nyafu sawo,
41001020	Kamei chimwande, yeja yawenanga; howomuleka iBaba yawo Sebedayo mu chiya hamwedu na wanhu we maliho, na kumwandamila.
41001021	Wejawaluta Kapelinaumu, chimwande dijuwa dye sabato yejayengila mwisinagogi na kufusa.
41001022	Wejawajuma lugano kosoko ya mafuso gakwe, kosoko yendeyofusa fina munhu yena udaha, kahi si fina watulumi.
41001023	Kamei chimwande, hamuwa na munhu yena digini dihile umo mwisinagogi dyawo;
41001024	kamei hakajoja China choni nagweye, “Yesu wa Nasaleti? Togola kwija uchimalagise? Nikumanya gwegwe no Imusunhile we Mulungu.”
41001025	Ninga Yesu yaigombela yakugamba, “Nyamala na umulawe!”
41001026	Kamei dyamuguma chisilisi, na kujoja kwa ijwi ikulu na kumulawa.
41001027	Wose wejawajuma, wakiyusa, wakugamba, “Choni chino? Ifuso isha! Kwa udaha yakulagisa hata magini gehile nago gakumuhulika.”
41001028	Simbuli sakwe hosikwenela chimwande ku si iisi sose sikusunguluta Galilaya.
41001029	Kamei chimwande wakalawe mwisinagogi, wejawengila ukaya kwa cha Simoni na Andelea, hamwedu na Yakobo na Yohana.
41001030	Imukwewe wa Simoni, ing'ina we imuke, hakowa mwisasi, kena mhungo; kamei chimwande wejawamutamila simbuli sakwe.
41001031	Hoyamusegelela, na kumwinula kwa kumukola umukono, imhungo haimuleka, na kuwatogomela.
41001032	Hegulo iya dijuwa dikoswe, wejawamwigalila wose awowile na sinhamu na wowile na magini.
41001033	Awanhu wose we ikaya iya howokwija howomema hamulango.
41001034	Hakawahonya matewa na matamu ga hayo hayo, na kulafa magini itewa, nghagalekile magini galonge, kosoko hagamumanya.
41001035	Nhosikusiku, kwikali malisalisa, yejayenuka na kuluta kunhu kwichaka wanhu, uko yowa na mawombi.
41001036	iSimoni na wayagwe hawamwandamila,
41001037	na kumona hawamugamba, “Awanhu wose wakukuhananga.”
41001038	Yawagamba, “Chigendeni kwingi, kufikaya fihamwande, uleke nihubili uko nako kosoko iyo nochileka nejile.”
41001039	Yaluta kuhubili, iisi yose ya Galilaya mumasinagogi gawo na kulafa magini.
41001040	Yamwijila munhu yena ukoma, yakumugongelesa kwa kumufugamila, yakugamba, “Unghenda ukudaha kunihonya.”
41001041	Naye yamonele ubasi, na kugolola umukono wakwe, na kumukwafa, yakugamba, “Nikwenda, uhone.”
41001042	Kamei chimwande ukoma wamuleuka hakahonyigwa.
41001043	kamei Yesu yamugamba yalute chimwande
41001044	na kumugamba, “Langa, unghamutamile munhu mbuli yoyose; nanga ulute ukakiyonese ku watambiki, go mwenyecho ukalafe isadaka foyalagisa iMusa, kosoko ya kuhona kwako; chuwe chitangilo ukwawo.”
41001045	Ninga, hakalawa na kukonga kuibwambwasa na kuyenesa imbuli iya mpaka isidahike kahi kwa Yesu kwingila mukaya yakoneke na wanhu. Ninga hakasigala kunje ahanhu hasowile na wanhu, hawamulutila kulawa chila ulwandi.
41002001	Gakaloke majuwa makefu, yoya kahi Kapelinaumu, hawahulika fina kowa ukaya.
41002002	Wanhu itewa weja welunda hamwedu mpaka hamulango, hokukuwa chaka luneka kosoko yawo; naye yendeyowahubili imbuli yakwe.
41002003	Haweja wanhu wegale mutamu yaholole, kenuligwa na wanhu wane.
41002004	Wakalemeligwe kumusegelela kosoko ya matewa, Howaimola ikano, ahaya hoyowile. Wakamale kuitobola hawamuhulumusa mwisasi dyoyagonele ayuya iyaholole.
41002005	Kamei Yesu yakone dihuwi dyawo, hakamugamba ayuya iyaholole, “Mwanangu kuleusiligwa uwihi wako.”
41002006	Awamonga wa Watulumi awowile uko, hawekala na kudoga mufidoga fyawo,
41002007	“Nhani yuno yakulonga nhafi? Yakutofula. No nani yakudaha kuleusa uwihi langa yu mwedu du naye no Mulungu!”
41002008	Chimwande Yesu, yakamanye muchidoga chakwe fina wakudoga nheifo mufidoga fyawo, yawagamba, “Nhani mukudoga nhafi mufidoga fyenu?
41002009	Chihufu no chihoki, kumugamba yaholole, ‘Kuleusiligwa uwihi wako,’ ama kugamba, ‘Inuka, kitwike disasi dyako, ulute?’
41002010	Ninga mumanye fina Mwana we Munhu kena udaha muchilunga wo kuleusa uwihi.” Kamei yamugamba ayuya yaholole
41002011	Nikugamba, “Inuka kitwike disasi dyako ulute ukaya ukwako.”
41002012	Chimwande hakenuka, na kitwika disasi dyakwe na kulawa kumwande yawo wose. Wose wejawajuma na kumutunya Mulungu, wakugamba, “Chisinati chone chinhu fina chino ugele wowose!”
41002013	Hakaleuka kahi na kuluta kunghingi ye bahali, ditewa dyose hodimusunguluta, hoyowafusa:
41002014	Foyalokage, yamona Lawi imwana wa Alifayo, kekala hachibanda cho kulihila kodi, hakamugamba, “Nyandamile. Hakenuka na kumwandamila.”
41002015	Ugele foyekale wakudiya kunyumba yakwe ditewa dye wakonghosa kodi na wena uwihi hawekala hamwedu na Yesu, na wefusa wakwe, kosoko hawowa itewa wamwandamilage.
41002016	Watulumi na Mafalisayo fowamonile yakudiya hamwedu na wakonghosa kodi na wena uwihi, hawawagamba awefusa wakwe, “Nhani yakudiya hamwedu na wakonghosa kodi na wena uwihi?”
41002017	Yesu yakahulike hoyowagamba, “Awomi wasikuhananga muganga ninga awatamu. Sijile kwinanga awomi ninga awene wihi.”
41002018	Awefusa wa Yohana na Wamafalisayo weja wafungaga; kamei, haweja, wakumugamba, “Nhani awefusa wa Yohana na wefusa wa Mafalisayo wakufunga, ninga awefusa awako wasikufunga?”
41002019	Yesu hakawagamba, “Awowile mu halusi wakudaha kufunga nhani ugele ibwana halusi kahamwedu nawo?” Ichigele chose nghona ibwana halusi ye hamwedu nawo, wasikudaha kufunga.
41002020	Ninga amajuwa gakwija iBwana halusi yakwija yoleusigwa, dijuwa dyo noho wakawofunga.
41002021	Hechaka munhu yakusona ndame nyisha mu suke ya katali, yanghasona, achiya ichisha chikuigolosa idegeke aiya isuke ya katali, ahaya ahadegeke hakongeseka kudegeka.
41002022	Kahe hechaka munhu yakuguma difai nyisha muchibuyu cha katali, yanghaguma aiya idifai nyisha ikwenda ifitule ifibuyu fiya, ninga difai nyisha ikugumigwa mufibuyu fisha.
41002023	Yakowe yakuloka mumigunda ye ngano dijuwa dye sabato; fowaleukage awefusa wakwe hawakonga kukwanyula masanja ge ingano.
41002024	Mafalisayo hawamugamba, “Langa, nhani wakugolosa dilemesigwe kugolosa mwijuwa dye Sabato?”
41002025	Kamei yawagamba, “Musinati musome hohose foyagolose Daudi, foyowile na njala, imwene na wayagwe:
41002026	ifene foyengile mu nyumba ye Mulungu, ugele we mutambiki mukulu Abiyasali, na kudiya imikate iya yokonesa iyene isikudiigwa na wanhu wowose ninga na watambiki du, na kuwenghawayagwe?”
41002027	Hoyowagamba, “Isabato haigoloseka kosoko ye munhu; siyo imunhu kosoko ye isabato.
41002028	Ninga Mwana we Munhu no Mundewa we sabato nheifia.”
41003001	Yengila kahi mwisinagogi; umo hamuwa munhu yena mukono uholole.
41003002	Wende womutegela uleke wone nghona yomuhonya dijuwa dye sabato; uleke wamukole chikono.
41003003	Kamei yamugamba ayuya yena umukono uholole nyagula
41003004	Hakawagamba, “Ni fiswanu dijuwa dye sabato kugolosa maswanu ama gehile, Kuhonya chidoga ama kukoma?” Ninga hawanyamala.
41003005	Hakawakumhulila meso kose kose kwa nyono, yena usungu kosoko yo ukugutu we fidoga fyawo. Yakumugamba ayuya imunhu, “Golola umukono wako. Naye hakaugolola, na umukono wakwe houhona.”
41003006	Amafalisayo hawalawa na chimwande haweka njama hamwedu na Mahelodiya kosoko yakwe uleke wamukome.
41003007	Yesu yaleuke hamwedu na wefusa wakwe, kuluta kunghingi ye bahali na wanhu itewa kulawa Galilaya weja wamwandamila; kahi kulawa Uyahudi,
41003008	na Yelusalemu, na Idumaya, na umwambu wa Yolodani, na ulwandi lwa Tilo na Sidoni. Itewa ikulu, wakahulike simbuli sose soyagolose, hawamwijila.
41003009	Hakawalonga awefusa wakwe fina wamwikile chiya habehi naye, kosoko ya ditewa dya wanhu, wangheje womukanhamisa;
41003010	Kosoko hakahonya matewa, hata awaya awowile na sinhamu, weja wakisegesaga uleke wamukwafe.
41003011	Na wena magini gehile chila fowakumona, wakugwa na kujoja, wakugamba, “Agweye no umwana we Mulungu.”
41003012	Hakawalemesa lugano, wanghamubwambwase kuwanhu.
41003013	Kahi hakakwila kwitunda na kuwenanga wose woyendile howomwijila..
41003014	Kamei yawasagula ikumi na weli, wowe hamwedu naye, uleke yawatume kuhubili.
41003015	Kahi wowe na udaha wa kulafa magini:
41003016	Simoni yamwingha disina dya Petulo;
41003017	Yakobo imwana wa Sebedayo, na Yohana imunduguse wa Yakobo, yoyawengha disina dya Boanege, nong'amba, “Wana we ididimo;”
41003018	Andilea na Filipo, na Batolomayo, na Matayo, na Tomaso, na Yakobo imwana wa Alufayo na Tadei na Simoni Mukananayo,
41003019	na Yuda Isikalioti, iyamusongesa. Kamei hakaluta ukaya.
41003020	Ditewa dya wanhu dyakitang'anyila kahi, hata awene wasapata luneka lwa kudiya.
41003021	Awanduguse wakahulike simbuli so, hawamulutila uleke wamukole; kosoko hawagamba, “Ditwi dyakwe dijuguma.”
41003022	Na Watulumi awadulike kulawa Yelusalemu, hawagamba, “Kena Belisebuli, na yakulafa simhepo kwa udaha we mukulu wa magini.”
41003023	Hakawenanga, na kuwatamila kwa mbasi: “Iluhoma kodaha kumulafa Luhoma?
41003024	Nghona Undewa unghakitemanula uwecho kwa wecho usikudaha kugendelela.
41003025	Na inyumba inghakitemanula iyecho kwa iyecho, inyumba yo isikudaha kugendelela.
41003026	Iluhoma yanghakisuhila imwecho na kigawa nghekudaha kugendelela, ninga indumo yakwe ija.
41003027	Kwechaka munhu yekudaha kwingila kunyumba ye munhu yena ludole na kulonda ifinhu fyakwe, mpaka yakonge kumoha imunhu wo ludole; noho yakudaha kulonda inyumba yakwe.
41003028	Chawelu, nikumutamilani, uwihi wose wa awanhu wakudaha kuleusiligwa, na matofulo gose gowekulonga;
41003029	Ninga imunhu iyakwenda yamutofule Muhe Musunhile yakuwa na wihi wa majuwa gose.”
41003030	Kosoko wagambile fina Kena magini gehile.
41003031	Haweja ing'ina ne wanduguse: Wema kunje, walagisa munhu yamwinange.
41003032	Amatewa hawowa wekale, wamusunguluta, wamugamba, “Langa, ing'inako na wanduguso, wowa kunje wakukuhananga.”
41003033	Yawabidula, yekugamba, “Imayi na wandugu sangu no chenani?”
41003034	Yawalanga awaya awekale na kumusunguluta kose kose na kuwagamba, “Langa! Imayi na wandugu sangu!
41003035	Kosoko imunhu wowose iyakugolosa foyakuhananga iMulungu, ayo no mundugusangu, no lumbu dyangu no ng'inangu.”
41004001	Yakonga kahi kuwafusa kunghingi ye bahali. Ditewa ikulu lugano dya wanhu, dyamusunguluta, imwene yengile muchiya, na kwikala muchiya ulwandi lwe bahali, ditewa hodikuwa kunje ye bahali, kuisi kwichaka meji.
41004002	Yawafusa mbuli nyingi kwa mbasi, mumafuso gakwe yawagamba:
41004003	Hulikiseni! “Imuhandi yaluta kuhanda.
41004004	Kamei ugele foyahandage imbeyu imonga hoilagalila munghanda ye njila, ifidege hofiidiya.
41004005	Imonga hailagala hena diwe, hahowa na ulongo mukefu. Chimwande hoikota kosoko ya ulongo mukefu.
41004006	Kamei dijuwa dikalawe, hailakala, na kosoko ichaka misisi hainyala.
41004007	Isimonga hosilagala ahena imiwa, imiwa iya yakula na kuikanhamisa, hoileka kweleka mhule.
41004008	Simonga hosilagala hena ulongo umuswanu hosikweleka, hasota na kukula, na kweleka: Imonga mhule makumi madatu, imonga makumi mutandatu, na mhule imonga igana dimwedu.
41004009	Yena singhutwi so kuhulika yahulike!”
41004010	Naye yakowe ye imwene awaya awanhu awamusungulute na waya ikumi na weli, howomusa difuso dye mbasi.
41004011	Yawagamba, “Anyeye mumotesigwa kumanya imbuli ifisigwe ya undewa we Mulungu, ninga kwa waya wowile kunje gose gakugolosigwa kifana mbasi,
41004012	uleke hata wanghalanga, walange wanghone, ‘Na wanghahulika, wahulike wanghamanye, Wangheje wobiduka na kulekeleligwa.’”
41004013	Kahi yawagamba, “Musikuimanya imbasi ino? Simbasi simonga mosimanya nhani?
41004014	Imuhandi ayo yakuhanda imbuli.
41004015	Awano no wowile munghanda ye injila ichigele choikuhandigwa imbeyu; awene, wanghahulika imbuli, chimwande yakwija Luhoma na kuileusa aiya imbuli ihandigwe mufidoga fyawo.
41004016	Nheifo awa nawo nowaya wahandigwe mu mawe, awene wakuhulika iya imbuli. Chimwande waihokela kwa chinyemi.
41004017	Ninga wachaka misisi mugati yao, wakugendelela chipisi chiguhi. Kughalawanisa migogolo kosoko ya iya imbuli, wakuleka kuhuwila.
41004018	Na wano nowaya wakuhandigwa mumiwa. Ni wanhu wakuihulika imbuli,
41004019	na simbuli se chilunga, na udasi we mali, na kukwegigwa na finhu, sikukanhamisa iya imbuli mpaka imbuli iya isikudaha kweleka.
41004020	Na wano nowaya wahandigwe mu ulongo muswanu, no wanhu wakuihulika imbuli na kuihokela, na kweleka si mhule: Aino makumi madatu, aino makumi mutandatu, na aino igana dimwedu.”
41004021	Yawagamba, “Itaa ikwija igubikigwe? Si kwikigwa muchigwaso?
41004022	Kosoko kwechaka mbuli ifisigwe ninga kosoko ije imanyike, kahi kwechaka difisigwe ninga dije dyoneke pwi, pwi, pwi.
41004023	Imunhu nghona yena nghutwi sa kuhulika yahulike.”
41004024	Hakawagamba, “Mulangisise go mukuhulika, imhishi iya yo mukupima, noyo mukamupimiligwa na kahi mukongeseligwa.
41004025	Kosoko yena chinhu yakwenda yenghigwe, na ayuya yechaka chinhu, hata chiya choyenacho yakuhokigwa.”
41004026	Yagamba, “Undewa we Mulungu ukifana munhu yanyagile imbeyu musanga,
41004027	yakugona na kwinuka, chilo ne imisi, na imbeyu hoikota na kukula, fonghamanyile.
41004028	Kosoko iisi ikweleka iyecho, ikukonga dinyagala, kamei chida, kamei disanja dye ingano ikangale mwisanga.
41004029	Inghakangala, yakwingisa ihengo yakwe kosoko ugele wokududula ufika.”
41004030	Yagamba, “Chiliganise na choni undewa we Mulungu? Kahi chiugume mu mbasi yaki?
41004031	Ikifana imbeyu yo umheja, iyene foikuhandigwa mu ulongo ni ndodogi kusuma si mbeyu sose suwile mu chilunga;
41004032	ninga inghahandigwa, ikukula kusuma amabiki gose, ikuwa na matambi makulu mpaka amadege ga kulanga gakujenga amafulu gawo mwipeho dyakwe.”
41004033	Kwa mbasi nyingi sifanile ino, hakalonga nawo imbuli fowadahile kuhulika.
41004034	Ninga bila mbasi nghalongile nawo, kamei yawatamila awefusa wakwe we imwene.
41004035	Dijuwa diya ikowe hegulo, yawagamba, “Chiloke mpaka umwambu.”
41004036	Na fowadilekile ditewa dya wanhu kunyuma, hawamulonda imwene hamwedu nawo muchiya nheifiya foyowile. Na Ifiya fimonga, hafyua baho hamwedu naye.
41004037	Lwalawa luputa lukulu lwa imheho, amawingo hagatowa ichiya, na kukonga kumema meji.
41004038	Imwene hakowa kunyuma ye ichiya kagona mu muto. Hawamwinusa, wakumugamba, “Mwalimu, nghukona ubasi aseye fochikufa?”
41004039	Hakenuka, na kuigombela imheho, yakuigamba ibahali, “Nyamala twi!”
41004040	Hakawagamba, “Nhani mukogoha? Mwichaka ihuwi?”
41004041	Hawengiligwa na chogoho chikulu, na kukonga kulonga awecho kwa wecho, “Ayuno nani, imwene imheho ne bahali fikumuhulika?”
41005001	Hawaloka umwambu we bahali, mpaka muiisi ya Wagelasi.
41005002	Yakahulumuke mu chiya, chimwande, haketang'anyila ne munhu, yalawile kufilalo, yena imhepo ihile;
41005003	ukalo wakwe hauwa kufilalo; hahowa chaka munhu wowose yadahile kumoha kahi, hata kwa minyolo;
41005004	kosoko hakohigwa kengi na kengi kwa mhingu ne minyolo na kuidumula aiya iminyolo, na kusitulatula asiya simhingu; kahi hahowa chaka munhu wowose yadahile kumusuma.
41005005	Na majuwa gose, chilo ne misi hakowaga kufilalo na kumatunda, yakutula chowe na kitema tema na mawe.
41005006	Yakamone Yesu kwa hatali; yabilima na kumufugamila.
41005007	Yakujoja kwa dijwi dya muchanya, yekugamba, “Nina choni nagweye, Yesu, Mwana we Mulungu! Yowile kuchanhya? Nikutasa kwedisina dye Mulungu unghanidumangise!”
41005008	Kosoko hakadigamba digini diya, “Agwe go digini dihile mulawe imunhu yuno!”
41005009	Hakadyusa, “Disina dyako nani? Hodibidula Disina dyangu nene Legioni kosoko cha itewa!”
41005010	Hadimugongelesa yanghagegale kutali ne iisi iya.
41005011	Baho hetunda hahowa itewa dya nguluwe sikudima;
41005012	Kamei amagini gose hagamugongelesa, gakugamba, “Chigale kusinguluwe uleke chisingile isene.”
41005013	Naye hoyogengha luneka amagini gehile hogelawa, na kwingila musinguluwe siya. Ditewa dyose dyadulika chimwandemwande kwigenge, na kwingila mubahali, hasuwa figulu fili nhafi; hosikunywa munghabu.
41005014	Awadimi wew singuluwe hawatija, na kuwatamilisa simbuli so mukaya na kunje ye ikaya. Awanhu hawalawa uleke wone imbuli igoloseke.
41005015	Hawamulutila Yesu; hawamona yuya yowile na magini, kekala, kafala suke, kena misungu yakwe; naye noyowile na diya ditewa howokogoha.
41005016	Na waya awonile hawawatamila simbuli sagoloseke kwe munhu yuya wa magini, na simbuli se singuluwe.
41005017	Kamei wejawakonga kumutasa Yesu yaleuke muisi yawo.
41005018	Naye foyendeyokwingila muchiya, ayuya yowile na magini hakamutasa fina yowe hamwedu naye.
41005019	Ninga Yesu nghamufumile. Yamugamba, “Luta ukaya kuwambwiyasako, ukawahubili wa ukwenu kawatamile simbuli singhulu iMundewa soyakugolosele na ifene foyakonele ubasi.”
41005020	Hakaluta, na kukonga kuhubili mu isi ya Dekapoli simbuli singhulu isene Yesu soyamugolosele, wanhu wose hawakisina.
41005021	Yesu yakafuluse kuloka kuya umwambu muchiya, hawamwijila itewa ikulu, naye hakowa munghingi ye bahali.
41005022	Hakeja munhu yumonga mu wakulu wa disinagogi, disina dyakwe Yayilo; yakamone, yamufugamila.
41005023	Hakamugongelesa lugano, yakugamba, “I mwanangu we chike imudodo mutamu lugano kahabehi na kufa. Nikukutasa wije umwikile umukono wako muchanhya yakwe, uleke yahone, na yowe mumi.”
41005024	Yaluta hamwedu naye. Itewa ikulu dyeja dyamwandamila wakumufinhafinha.
41005025	Kamei mwanamuke yumonga yena utamu wa kulawa sakame kwa minyaka ikumi na mili,
41005026	hakaluta kuwaganga wengi lugano, na kupata magayo mengi. Hakamala imali yakwe yose, ninga kusamutasile hata hadodogi, inyuwa yakwe hoigendelele kwiha kusuma foyowile kunghonga.
41005027	Yakahulike simbuli sa Yesu, yagenda muchiligati che ditewa kwa kunyuma, na kukwafa isuke yakwe;
41005028	kosoko hakagamba, “Ninghasikwafa sisuke sakwe du, nikuhona.”
41005029	Chimwande inhyoko ye sakame yakwe yanyala; naye hakamanya mumutufi wakwe fina kahona utamu wakwe.
41005030	Kamei Yesu yakamanye fina udaha umulawa umwakwe, chimwande yabiduke mu ditewa, hoyogamba, “Nani yanikwafile?”
41005031	Awefusa wakwe hawamugamba, “Togola nghukona amatewa fowakukukanhamisa ulwandi lwose; nagwe ukugamba Nani yanikwafile?”
41005032	Yalanga ulwandi lwose uleke yamone iyagolose didyo.
41005033	Na yuya imwanamuke yengilwa na chogoho na kuchichima, yakamanye chigoloseke umwakwe, yeja na kumugwila na yakumutamila yose.
41005034	Yamugamba, “Mundele dihuwi dyako dikuhonya. Ugende mheho, uwe mumi, unghowe na utamu wako kahi.”
41005035	Ugele foyalongage, haweja wanhu kulawa kwa yuya imukulu wa disinagogi, wakugamba, “Imwanago we chike kafulusa kubanika. Nhani ugendelele kumwidasa imwalimu?”
41005036	Ninga Yesu yakahulike imbuli iyo ikulongigwa, yamugamba imukulu wa disinagogi, “Unghogohe, huwila du.”
41005037	Hakawalemesa awanhu wanghamwandamile, ninga Petulo, na Yakobo, na Yohana imunduguse wa Yakobo.
41005038	Fowengile kugati kwa yuya imukulu wa disinagogi, yona wanhu wengi wakulila, na kuhongesa lugano,
41005039	yakafuluse kwingila yagamba, “Nhani mukujoja na kulila? Imundele yuno nghafile, ninga kagona du!”
41005040	Hawamuseka lugano. Yakawalafe kunje wose, hakamulonda iBabakwe ne ing'ina wa yuya imundele, na waya awowile hamwedu na kwingila kugati koyowile imundele yuya.
41005041	Hakamukola umukono imundele yuya, na kumugamba, “Talita kumi,” no ng'amba, “Mundele nikukugamba Inuka!”
41005042	Chimwande imundele yuya yemanyima na kugenda, (kosoko hakowa mukulu wa minyaka ikumi na mili.) Chimwande weja wajuma ijumo ikulu.
41005043	Yawalemesa lugano, wanghatamile munhu imbuli iyo. Yawalonga, wamwinghe chakudiya.
41006001	Yaleuka uko na kuluta kuiisi ya ukwawo, awefusa wakwe wejawamwandamila.
41006002	Ikowe sabato, yakonga kufusa mwisinagogi. Matewa wakahulike wejawakisina, hawagamba, “Ayuno kapata hoki agano? Na misungu yaki ino yoyenghigwe yuno? Kahi yakugolosa amajumo gano goyakugolosa kwe mikono yakwe?
41006003	Ayuno si yuya muselemala imwana wa Maliamu na, mundugu sawo wa cha Yakobo, na Yose, na Yuda na Simoni na walumbuse wasibaha ahetu?” Hawamulema.
41006004	Yesu yagamba, “Imugonesi yakwinghigwa chogoho chila hanhu ninga kuisi yakwe ka imwecho na kuwanhu wo lukolo lwakwe na inyumba iyakwe.”
41006005	Nghagolose ijumo dyodyose uko, ninga hakeka imikono yakwe muwatamu wakefu, hakawahonya.
41006006	Hakajuma kosoko yo kuleka kuhuwila kwawo. Yesu yasunguluta mufikaya fiya na kufusa.
41006007	Yawenanga awaya ikumi na weli, na kukonga kuwatuma weli weli, na kuwengha udaha muchanhya ya magini gehile.
41006008	Yawalemesa wanghalonde chinhu chochose cha munjila, ninga mhandodu; kefana mikate, mufuko wa nghingo, mapesa ga mumifuko.
41006009	Ninga wafale filwatu, kahi wanghalonde nghasu ya sigafu ninga mhando du.
41006010	Hakawagamba, “Kunyumba yomukwingila mwikale baho mpaka fomukuleuka.
41006011	Na hanhu hohose wanghaleka kumuhokelani ama kuwategelesa hona mukuleuka uko, mukung'unhe dinghundi dyuwile mumigulu yenu, yuwe chitangilo chokumulemani.”
41006012	Hawalawa kuhubili fina awanhu walambe.
41006013	Hawalafa magini mengi, na kuwabaka mafuta wanhu wengi na kuwahonya.
41006014	Mundewa Helode yakahulike simbuli so, kosoko disina dya Yesu hadimanyika kosekose, awamonga hawagamba, “Yohana Mubatisaji kenuligwa mu wanhu wafile; nochanghone uludole lwakwe lukiyonesa mumilimo yakwe.”
41006015	Wamonga weja wagamba, “Ayuno Eliya.” Na wamonga hawagamba, “Ayuno ni mugonesi fina yumwedu wa wagonesi wa katali.”
41006016	Ninga Helode yakahulike, yagamba, “Yohana, wonadumule ditwi, kenuka.”
41006017	Kosoko Helode imwecho yatuma wanhu, hawamukola Yohana, na kumoha mwigelesa, kosoko ya Helodia, imuke wa Filipo imunduguse, kosoko hakamutola.
41006018	Kosoko Yohana hakamulonga Helode fina, “Si fiswanu agweye kuwa ne muke we mukuluwo.”
41006019	Ihelodiya hakowa na finju na Yohana, na hakahananga kumukoma. Ninga nghapatile luneka,
41006020	kosoko Helode yendeyomwogoha Yohana; hakamanya fina ni munhu we chawelu na musunhile, na hakamwika hanhu haswanu. Foyamuhuwile hakakisina lugano, kahi hakenda kumuhulikisa kwa chinyemi.
41006021	Ichigele hachifika, ugele Helode yakagolose sikukuu ya dijuwa dyo kwelekigwa kwakwe, yawagolosela madiya, wakulu wa wasilikali ne filongosi, na wanhu awena undewa wa Galilaya.
41006022	Noho imwanagwe we chike wa Helodia, yengila na kufina, yamwendesa Helode na wose wowile naye hachakudiya chiya. iMundewa yamugamba imundele yuya, “Nitase chochose cho ukuhananga ani nikukwingha.”
41006023	Yamwilahila, “Chochose choukutasa nikukwingha, hata ulwandi lyo undewa wangu!”
41006024	Kamei hakaluta na kumusa ing'ina, “Nitase choni?” Naye yamugamba, “Ditwi dya Yohana Mubatisaji.”
41006025	Kamei yengila chimwandemwande kumwande ye Mundewa, hoyotasa, yakugamba, “Nikuhananga uninghe hambiya hano ditwi dya Yohana Mubatisaji mwisahani.”
41006026	iMundewa yona usungu lugano, ninga kosoko ye nyilaha yakwe na kosoko ya waya awowile hechakudiya, yasumwa kulema.
41006027	Chimwande yamutuma musilikali iyowile mu samu na kumugamba yegale ditwi dya Yohana. Kamei yaluta na kumudumula ditwi amuya mwigelesa;
41006028	Yegala ditwi dyakwe mwisahani na kumwingha imundele yuya, naye imundele hakamwingha ing'ina.
41006029	Awefusa wakwe wakahulike imbuli iyo haweja na kulonda umutufi wakwe na kumusika.
41006030	Awefusa hawoya kwa Yesu; na kumutamila agaya gose gowagolose, na kufusa.
41006031	Kamei hakawagamba, “Mwije anyeye mwikale hanhu haposike mukabwihile hadodo.” Kosoko hahowa na wanhu wengi, wakwija na kuleuka, awene howoswela luneka lwa kudiya.
41006032	Hawaluta awene muhala muchiya ahanhu howile chaka wanhu.
41006033	Awanhu hawawona wakuluta, na wengi hawamanya hawaluta uko kwa lumangho kulawa sikaya sose na kuwalongolela.
41006034	Yakahumuluke muchiya, hoyokona itewa ikulu, akawonela ubasi, kosoko hawowa kifana ngholo sichaka mudimi. Kamei hakakonga kuwafusa mbuli itewa.
41006035	Chikaloke chipisi chitali cha nemisi, awefusa wakwe hawamulutila wakugamba, “Ahanhu hano nyika muhala, dijuwa nadyo duswa;
41006036	uwelage awanhu wano, uleke walute kufikaya fya munghanda wakakigulile chakudiya.”
41006037	Ninga hakawagamba, “Wengheni nyeye chakudiya.” Wamugamba, “Togola chilute chikagule mikate ya dinali magana meli uleke chiwenghe chakudiya?”
41006038	Yawagamba, “Mwinayo mikate mingahi?” Luteni mukalange. Wakafuluse kumanya weja wagamba, “Mishano na somba mbili.”
41006039	Yawatuma wawagambe awanhu wekale wose, fitewa tewa, mumbago injolo.
41006040	Howokwikala kwa misitali ahano igana, ahano makumi mashano.
41006041	Foyailondile aiya imikate mishano na siya sisomba si mbili, yenula meso kuchanya kulanga, na kuilugutisa na kuibendula imikate iya na kuwengha awefusa wakwe wawagawile wanhu na siya sisomba si mbili hawawagawila wose.
41006042	Awanhu wose hawadiya na kwiguta.
41006043	Hawalonda ifibendu fye mikate na sisomba sasigale na kumemesa fisege ikumi na fili.
41006044	Wadiile imikate yiyo hawowa wagosi figulu fishano.
41006045	Chimwande yawalonga awefusa wakwe wengile muchiya, wamulongelele kuluta Betisaida, umwambu we bahali, ugele imwene foyakilagage ditewa dya wanhu.
41006046	Yakamale kilaga na wanhu, hakakwila kwitunda kutasa.
41006047	Ikafike hegulo ichiya hachuwa muchiligati ye bahali, imwene hakowa yemwene kuiisi, kunje ye bahali.
41006048	Hokawona awefusa wakwe wakugaya na kuyusigwa muchiya chawo kosoko imheho yendeitowa kwa ludole kulawa kowakuluta. Habehi na kucha, yawejila yakugenda mubahali, na kuhananga kuwaloka,
41006049	Nawo wakamone yakugenda mumeji ge bahali; hawamanya nhagela ni isoki, hawatula chowe;
41006050	kosoko wose hawamona hawogoha. Chimwande yalonga nawo, “Sangalaleni noniye, munghogohe.”
41006051	Yengila muchiya chiya; imheho yanyamala na kisina; howokisina lugano mufidoga fyawo,
41006052	kosoko wasatangile simbuli se mikate iya, ninga fidoga fyawo hafyuwa fikugutu.
41006053	Wakafuluse kuloka, hawafika iisi ya Genesaleti, kamei hawemisa ichiya chawo baho.
41006054	Wakafuluse kulawa mu chiya, chimwande wanhu hawamutanga.
41006055	Hawabilima lumangho musikaya sose sihabehi na kukonga kuwegala awatamu mumasasi kuluta chila hanhu howahulike fina kauko.
41006056	Chila koyalutile yengila kufikaya na kusikaya ama kumigunda, haweka watamu mumagulilo, wakumutasa fina wakwafe hata dihepu du dye suke yakwe; na wose wamukwafile howahona.
41007001	Kamei Amafalisayo na wamonga wa watulumi kulawa Yelusalemu, fowejile ukwakwe.
41007002	Hawona awamonga wa wefusa wakwe wakudiya ne mikono ichuchile.
41007003	(Kosoko Amafalisayo na Wayahudi wose wanghaleka kunawa imikono ichiganja chose wasikudiya; wakolelesa amahokelo ga wasehe wawo;
41007004	Kahi wanghalawa kwigulilo, wanghaleka kusunha imigulu wasikudiya na gauko mengi gowakolile, fina kusunha ifikombe, na madumu, ne fiya fya shaba.)
41007005	Awaya Mafalisayo na Watulumi howomusa Yesu, “Nhani awefusa wako wasikwandamila amahokelo gawasehe ninga wakudiya ne mikono ichuchile?”
41007006	Kamei hakawagamba, “Mugonesi Isaya hakalonga fiswanu muchanya yenu! Anyeye mwine chimwefe! Fina foitulumwe: ‘Awanhu wano wakunitunya kwa milomo yawo, Amba fidoga fyawo fya kutali na niye.
41007007	Nawo wakufuga chaka, na kufusa amafuso ga malagiso ga wanhu!’
41007008	Anye mukuleka amalagiso ge Mulungu na kukola amahokelo ga wanhu.”
41007009	Hakawagamba, “Fiswanu!” mukulema amalagiso ge Mulungu uleke mukole amahokelo genu!
41007010	Kosoko iMusa hakagamba, “Uwahulike iBabako ne ng'inako, na iyakumuliga iBabakwe ama ing'ina kufa na yafe.
41007011	Ninga anyeye mukugamba imunhu yanghamugamba iBabakwe ama ing'ina Ni kolibani, (nong'amba nikwika chinhu changu cha kulafa kwa Mulungu, ichikwenda chimutase hechaka mbuli.)
41007012	Kahi musikutuma hanyuma ya gago kumugolosela mbuli iBabakwe au ing'inakwe.
41007013	Ako ni kubesa imbuli ya Mulungu kwa mahokelo genu gomukuhokela; kahi mukugolosa mbuli nyingi kifana siso.”
41007014	Hakawenanga amatewa kahi yekuwagamba, “Mhulikeni mose na kumanya.”
41007015	Kwechaka chinhu chuwile kunje ye munhu ichikudaha kumugolosa yowe na wihi. Ninga afiya ifikulawa mugati ye munhu, nofikumuguma uwihi.
41007016	Imunhu ghona kena nghutwi sa kuhulika yahulike.
41007017	Yakengile kugati kadileka ditewa kunje, awefusa wakwe weja wamusa muchanya ye imbasi iya.
41007018	Yawagamba, “Hata nyeye mwechaka misungu? Musikumanya fina chila chinhu chuwile kunje ye munhu chinghamwingila, chisikudaha kumwingha uwihi;
41007019	Kosoko chisikumwingila muchidoga, ninga, munda du, kamei chikulawa kucholo?” (Kwa kulonga nhaifo kafitenda fyakudiya fyose fuwe fiswanu.)
41007020	Yagamba, “Ichikumulawa imunhu nochikumuguma uwihi.
41007021	Kosoko mufidoga fya wanhu mukulawa magelegela gehile, dihabwa,
41007022	uhiji, kukoma, ugoni, kusulumila kwihile, migogolo, udasi, chimwefe, chigiso, maligo, usisi, ubwalasi
41007023	Agano gose gehile gakulawa kugati, nago gakumuguma imunhu uwihi.”
41007024	Yakaleuke uko, yaluta umwambu kuisi ya Tilo na Sidoni. Yengila nyumba imonga, yahananga yanghamanye munhu wowose, ninga isadahike kifisa.
41007025	Ninga, chimwande, mwanamuke, imwene imwanagwe we chike hakowa na igini dihile, yahulika simbuli sakwe, yeja na kumugwila hamigulu yakwe.
41007026	Naye imwanamuke yuya hakowa Muyunani, dikabila dyakwe Musilofoinike. Yamutasa, yailafe imhepo mwe mwanagwe we chike.
41007027	Yamugamba, “Waleke awana wende kwiguta, kosoko siyo fiswanu kuchilonda ichakudiya cha wana na kugakubitila mabwa.”
41007028	Ninga yabidule, yakugamba, “Heye, Mundewa, Ninga hata amabwa gowile hasi ye imesa, gakudiya fowakulagasa awana.”
41007029	Hakemugamba, “Kosoko ye imbuli iyo, Luta, imhepo imulawa imwanago we chike.”
41007030	Yaluta ukaya ukwakwe, na kumufika ayuya imundele katambalala mwisasi; na digini diya difulusa kumuleuka.
41007031	Yaleuka mumihaka ya Tilo, yagenda mugatigati ya Sidoni, na kupulutila mpaka kubahali ya Galilaya, kupulutila Dekapoli.
41007032	Hawamwigalila munhu nghakuhulika chihuli, kahi nghakulonga, hawamugongelesa yamwikile mikono.
41007033	Hakamusegesa kunghanda ne ditewa yemwene, na kuguma ifidole fyakwe musinghutwi sakwe na kuguma mate, na kumukwafa mwilimi,
41007034	ghakalanga kuchanhya, na kugula, na kugamba, “Efata, nong'amba Kumuka!”
41007035	Chimwande singhutwi sakwe hasigubuka, ichifundo cha dilimi dyakwe, hachilegela na kulonga fiswanu.
41007036	Hakawalemesa wanghamutamile munhu; ninga foyagendelele kuwasigilila, nofowagendele kubwambwasa simbuli.
41007037	Howakisina lugano kusuma fowasowele, wakugamba, “Kagolosa finhu fyose fiswanu! Wasikuhulika kawagolosa wahulike, ne fimumu walonge.”
41008001	Mumajuwa gago, itewa dya wanhu wengi fowakitanganyile. Na hawowa wechaka chakudiya, yawenanga awefusa wakwe, yakuwagamba,
41008002	“Nikuwonela ubasi amatewa kosoko wekala hamwedu na niye, gafika majuwa madatu, na wechaka chinhu cha kudiya.
41008003	Ninghawelaga walute kusikwawo, wafungile, wakusilika munjila, na wamonga walawa kutali.”
41008004	Awefusa wakwe wamusa, wakugamba, “Togola kwina munhu yakudaha kuwegusa mikate awanhu ahano hanyika?”
41008005	Kawosa, “Mwina mikate mingahi?” Hawagamba, “Mufungate.”
41008006	Yawalonga wanhu wekale hasi, na kulonda imikate iya mufungate, yamulumba Mulungu, na kwibendula, na kuwengha awefusa wakwe wawagawile wanhu ditewa.
41008007	Hawowa na fisomba fikefu hakafilungutisa na kuwagamba wawagawile afyo nafyo.
41008008	Weja wadiya na kwiguta na kudondola ifibedu fye mikate fisigale, fisege mufungate fimemile.
41008009	Awanhu awadiyile wakufika figulu fine. Hakawelaga.
41008010	Chimwande hakakwila muchiya, hamwedu na wefusa wakwe, na kuluta ulwandi lwa Dalumanusa.
41008011	Howalawanisa Mafalisayo, na hawakonga kuwa na lukani naye, wakuhananga kulawa ukwakwe ijumo dikulawa kulanga, wakumugesa.
41008012	Hakona usungu muchidoga chakwe, “Nhani icheleko chino chikuhananga ijumo? Chawelu nikumutamilani! Chisikwinghigwa chitangilo icheleko chino!”
41008013	Hakawaleka, na kwingila kahi muchiya, hakaluta mpaka umwambu;
41008014	Hawasimilwa kulonda mikate, kahi muchiya hawowa chaka ninga mukate umwedu du.
41008015	Hakawajama, yakugamba, “Muwe meso ne inungo ya Mafalisayo na ya Helode.”
41008016	Hawowa na lukani wene kwa wene yagamba Chichaka mikate.
41008017	Yesu hakamanya, hoyowagamba, “Nhani mwina lukani kosoko mwechaka mukate? Musinati mumanye, kahi musikutanga? Togoleni! Fidoga fyenu fisito?
41008018	Mwina meso musikona. Mwina nghutwi musikuhulika; kahi musikugelegela.
41008019	Fonabendule haya imikate mishano na kuwengha awaya wanhu figulu fishano hamulonda fisege fingahi fimemile ifibendu?” Wamugamba, “Ikumi na fili.”
41008020	Na iya mufungate na kuwengha wanhu figulu fine, Hamulonda fisege fingahi fimemile fibesu? Howomugamba, “Mufungate.”
41008021	Yawagamba, “Musinati mumanye, mukali?”
41008022	Hawafika Betisaida, wamwigalila munhu nghakona, wamutasa yamukwafe.
41008023	Hakamukola mukono, hakamusegesa kunje ye chikaya na kumutwila mate kumeso, yamwikila mikono yakwe, yamusa, “Ukona chinhu?”
41008024	Hakalanga kuchanhya hoyogamba, “Nikona wanhu kifana mabiki gakugenda.”
41008025	Hakeka kahi mikono yakwe mumeso gakwe, na kulanga lugano; na kuwa mumi, hakona ifinhu fyose fiswanu.
41008026	Yesu hakamugamba yalute ukaya ukwakwe, na kumugamba, “Unghengile kahe mufijiji fya munjila.”
41008027	Yesu hakaleuke na wefusa wakwe, na kuluta ku fikaya fya Kaisalia, Filipi, munjila yawosa awefusa wakwe, yakugamba, “Awanhu wakunigamba niye nene nani?”
41008028	Hawamubidula wakugamba, “Yohana Mubatisaji, wamonga Eliya, wamonga, yumwedu wa wagonesi.”
41008029	Yawosa: “Anyeye mukugamba niye nene nani?” Petulo hakamubidula, yekumugamba, “Agweye no Kilisito.”
41008030	Hakawalemesa wanghamutamile munhu wowose simbuli sakwe.
41008031	Hakakonga kuwafusa fina: Imwagila iMwana we munhu yapate magayo mengi, na kulemigwa na wasehe, na wakulu wa watambiki, na watulumi. Na kukomigwa, na fogakuloka majuwa madatu yakwinuka muchilalo.
41008032	Yendeyolonga imbuli iyo bila chifiso. iPetulo hakamulonda na kukonga kumugombela.
41008033	Hakabiduka, yakuwalanga awefusa wakwe na kumugombela Petulo, yakugamba, “Luta kunyuma yangu Luhoma, Kosoko nghukudoga simbuli se Mulungu ninga sa wanhu!”
41008034	Hakawenanga ditewa hamwedu na wefusa wakwe, hakawagamba, “I munhu wowose iyekuhananga kunyandamila yakileme imwecho na yalonde umusalaba wakwe, yanyandamile.”
41008035	Kosoko imunhu iyakuhananga kuhonya ichidoga chakwe, yakuchagilisa, imunhu yakwagilisa chidoga chakwe kosoko yangu na kosoko ya imbuli iswanu, ayo yakuchihonya.
41008036	Kosoko ikwenda imutase nhani imunhu yanghapata ichilunga chose na kwagilisa ichidoga chakwe?
41008037	Kahe imunhu yalafe choni ahanhu hokulafa ichidoga chakwe.
41008038	Kosoko chila munhu yakunyonela chinyala, aniye na simbuli sangu mucheleko chino ichisikumuhuwila Mulungu na wihi, iMwana we Munhu yakwija yomonela chinyala imunhu yuyo nghona yakiyokwija mu ditunyo dye Babakwe, hamwedu na malaika wasunhile.
41009001	Hakawagamba, “Chawelu, nikuwatamilani, mu wanhu wemile hano hena wanhu awene wasikwenda wafe ugele wanghali kuwona undewa we Mulungu ukwija kwa ludole.”
41009002	Gakaloke majuwa mutandatu, Yesu hakawalonda Petulo, na Yakobo, na Yohana, yawegala kuditunda ditali wemwene, hakahiluka ifuta yakwe, kumwande yao,
41009003	sisuke sakwe hasikonga kwakaika, njelu swe, kwechaka munhu mu iisi yakudaha kusigolosa suwe njelu nheifo.
41009004	Kamei hawalawanisila Eliya, hamwedu na Musa, awene wawo wakusimulila na Yesu.
41009005	Petulo hakabidula, yakumugamba: “Mukulu, ni fiswamu aseye chuwe hano. Chijenge fibanda fidatu, chimwedu chako gweye, chimwedu cha Musa, na chimwedu cha Eliya.”
41009006	Kosoko, nghamanyile choyakulonga, kosoko hawengiligwa na itisi ikulu.
41009007	Hadilawanisa ifunde, hadiwagubika, dijwi hadilawa umuya mwifunde, “Ayuno no Mwanangu mwendigwa, mumuhulike imwene.”
41009008	Ugele uwo wakalange kuno na kuno wasonile munhu hamwedu nawo; ninga Yesu du yemwene.
41009009	Ugele fowadulikage kulawa kwitunda, hakawalemesa wanghamutamile munhu wowose gowonile, mpaka iMwana we Munhu ugele woyakuwa kafulusa kwinuka kulawa kuwanhu wafile.
41009010	Hawaikola imbuli iya, wakiyusa awecho kwa wecho, “Akuno kukwinuka kulawa kuwafile no choni?”
41009011	Hawamusa wakugamba, “Awatulumi wakugamba fina iwagila Eliya yakonge kwija?”
41009012	Hakawabidula, yawagamba, “Chawelu, Eliya yakulongola kwija, na kugolosa usha finhu fyose, ninga, hamwedu na gago, foyatulumigwe nhani Mwana we Munhu fina yakwende yadumangisigwe madumangiso mengi na kubesigwa?
41009013	Ninga nikumutamilani, fina Eliya kafulusa kwija, nawo wamugolosela gose gowendile fina foitulumigwe.”
41009014	Ugele fowejile kuwefusa wamonga hawona itewa ikulu diwasunguluta na watulumi wena lukani nawo.
41009015	Chimwande ditewa dyose wakamone hawakisina, hawamubilimila, kumulamusa.
41009016	Hakawosa, “Mwina lukani lwa choni nawano?”
41009017	Imunhu yumonga kulawa muditewa hakabidula, “Mwalimu nimwigala imwanangu ukwako, kena igini kahi chimumu.”
41009018	Chila ugele foikumwijila ikumukinya hasi, yakulawa ifulo kumulomo na kugwegwejula meno kahi yakugagamala. Nilonga na wefusa wako wadilafe digini, waduga.
41009019	Hakabidula yakuwagamba, “Anyeye cheleko chichaka dihuwi! Nikale nanyeye mpaka milaki? Nimulondeni fomuwile mpaka milaki? Mwigaleni ukwangu!”
41009020	Hawamwigala imujelelo ukwakwe. Kamei digini dikamone hadimuguma chisilisi na kugwa mpaka hasi, hakasambalagata na kulawa ifulo kumulomo.
41009021	Yesu hakamusa iBabakwe, “Kakongigwa milaki?” Hakagamba, “Kulawa udodo.”
41009022	Ugele mwingi dimuguma mumoto na mumeji uleke dimukome, ninga unghadaha mbuli yoyose, uchonele ubasi na uchitase!
41009023	Yesu yamugamba, “Unghadaha! Gose gakudahika ukwakwe yena dihuwi.”
41009024	Chimwande iBabakwe we mujelelo yuya yenula dijwi, yakugamba, “Nikuhuwila, nitase kusumigwa kuhuwila kwangu!”
41009025	Yesu yakone ditewa dikubilima dikwija, hakadigombela digini diya dihile, yakugamba, “Agwe go digini, chimumu na chihuli,” nikukugamba, “Mulawe yuno, kahi unghamuwile!”
41009026	Hakalapa, hadimuguma chisilisi lugano na kulawa. Naye hakowa kifana kafa, hata wengi hawagamba, “Kofa!”
41009027	Ninga Yesu hakamukola mukono na kumwinula, naye hakemanyima.
41009028	Yakengile munyumba, awefusa wakwe hawamusa wemwene, “Nhani seye chisadahile kuilafa?”
41009029	Hoyawagamba, “Digini difanile dino disikulawa kwa njila yoyose iya, ninga kwa mawombi du.”
41009030	Hawaleuka uko hawalokela mugatigati ya Galilaya. Nghahanange munhu wowose yamanye,
41009031	kosoko yendeyowafusa awefusa wakwe: Yakuwagamba, “Mwana we Munhu yakuluta kugumigwa mumikono ya wanhu. Nawo wakumukoma, yanghafulusa kukomigwa, ganghaloka majuwa madatu yakwinuka muchilalo.”
41009032	Ninga wasaimanyile imbuli iyo, hawogoha kumusa.
41009033	Hawaje Kapelinaumu, yakowe munyumba hakawosa, “Mwende mutowa lukani lwaki munjila?”
41009034	hawanyamala, kosoko munjila wendewotowa lukani awecho kwa wecho, imukulusi no nani.
41009035	Hoyokwikala hasi, na kuwenanga awaya ikumi na weli na kuwagamba, “I munhu yakuhananga kulongola yakuwa wa kunyuma kusuma wose, mutogomi wa wose.”
41009036	Hakalonda chana chidodogi, na kuchika muchiligati chawo. Hakachidinghula, na kukawagamba,
41009037	“I munhu yanghachihokela chana chimwedu fina chino kwi sina dyangu, kanihokela niye; na imunhu yanghanihokela niye, yakumuhokela, si niye du, ninga ayuya imwene yanitumile.”
41009038	Yohana kamubidula, yakugamba, “Mwalimu, chimona munhu yakulafa simhepo kwa disina dyako, hachimulemesa kosoko nghakiyandamila naseye.”
41009039	Yesu hakagamba, “Munghamulemese. Kosoko kwachaka munhu yakudaha kugolosa ijumo kwa disina dyangu kahi ugele uwo na kunilonga mbuli sihile.
41009040	Kosoko inghowile chinyume chetu ka ulwandi ulwetu.
41009041	Kosoko wowose iyakumwinghani ichikombe cha meji, kosoko nyeye mwina disina dya Kilisito, chawelu; nikumutamilani, nghakuswela digelo dyakwe.”
41009042	“Ne munhu yakwenda yamugolose yumwedu wa wadodogi wano awanihuwile yagolose wihi, kagiligwa yohigwe ulwala musingo yakwe na kukubitigwa mubahali.
41009043	Na umukono wako unghakugolosa ugolose wihi, udumule! Ibeka kwingila kuumi kwina mukono umwedu, kusuma kuwa na mikono yose mili na kuluta Jehanumu.
41009044	Namo umo sinhende sakwe sisikufa ninga umoto wakwe uusikusima
41009045	Na umugulu wako unghakugolosa ugolose wihi, udumule! Ibeka kwingila kuumi na kwina mugulu umwedu, kusuma kuwa na migulu mili na kutagigwa kwi jehanumu.
41009046	Namo sinhende sakwe sisikufa kahiumoto usikusima
41009047	Na digiso dyako dinghakutenda ugolose wihi, ding'ole uditage! Ibeka kwingila kuundewa wa Mulungu kwina igiso dimwedu, kusuma kuwa na meso meli na kutagigwa kwi jehanumu.
41009048	Amo umo Sinhende sakwe sisikufa, kahiumoto wakwe usikusima.
41009049	Kosoko chila munhu kokwikigwa digoya kwa munyu na kusunhigwa kwa moto.
41009050	“Umunyu muswanu; ninga umunyu unghasusuka, si munyu kahi wogumigwa choni ukolele? Muwe munyu mugati yenu, mukekale kwa digoya muwecho kwa wecho.”
41010001	Yesu yaleuka uko yaluta ulwandi lwa Uyahudi, yaloka ulwandi lwa Yolodani. Ditewa dya wanhu dyawandamila, kahi fina foyasowela yakonga kuwafusa.
41010002	Amafalisayo weja wamulutila, wakumusa, “Togola! Ni fiswanu imunhu kumuleka imuke? Wakumugesa.”
41010003	Naye yawabidula yekugamba, “I Musa hakawalagisa choni?”
41010004	Hawagamba fina, “Musa hakafumisa fina munhu yawandike kalatasi ya malekeni kumuleka.”
41010005	Yesu yawagamba, “Kosoko ya ukugutu we fidoga fyenu hakamwinghani dilagiso dino.
41010006	Ninga kulawa kukumba iisi Mulungu hakagolosa mugosi na mwanamuke.
41010007	‘Kosoko iyo imunhu yakumuleka iBabakwe ne ing'ina wakiyandamila ne imuke.
41010008	Nawo aweli wakuwa mutufi umwedu. Wagaluka si weli kahi, ninga mutufi umwedu.’
41010009	Choyahasile Mulungu, imunhu yanghachitemanule.”
41010010	Wakowe ukaya kahi awefusa wakwe hawomusa muchanhya ye simbuli siso.
41010011	Hakawagamba, “Chila munhu yakumuleka imuke na kutola mwanamuke yungi, basi yakugolosa ugoni na yuya.
41010012	Na imwanamuke yanghamuleka imulume na kutoligwa na mugosi yungi, yakugolosa ugoni naye.”
41010013	Kamei, hawamwigalila awana wadodogi uleke yawakwafe, awefusa wakwe hawawagombela.
41010014	Yesu yakone nheifo hakona nyono lugano, hakawagamba, “Walekeni awana wadodogi weje ukwangu, munghawalemese, kosoko awana fina wano undewa wa Mulungu ni wao.
41010015	Chawelu, nikumutamilani, imunhu inghakuhokela undewa wa Mulungu kifana mwana mudodogi, nghakuwingila ng'o.”
41010016	Hakawadinghula, na kwika mikono yakwe muchanhya yawo na kuwalugutisa.
41010017	Ugele foyalawage kuluta kunjila, munhu yumonga hakamwijila lumangho, na kumufugamila, yakumusa, “Mwalimu muswamu nigolose nhani uleke niuhokele uwumi wa majuwa gose?”
41010018	Yesu hakamugamba, “Nhani ukuninanga muswamu?” Kwachaka imunhu muswanu ninga yumwedu du ni Mulungu.
41010019	Kugamanya amalagiso: “Unghakome; unghagolose dihabwa; unghahije; unghamusigile munhu udasi, Wogohe iBabako ne ng'inako.”
41010020	Hoyomugamba, “Mwalimu! Aga gose nigakola kulawa udodo wangu.”
41010021	iYesu yamukumhulila meso, hakamwenda na, kumugamba, “Kuhungukiligwa na mbuli imwedu. Luta ukambase fyose fyowinafyo, uwenghe awakiwa imali yako, nagwe ukuwa na ugoli kulanga; kamei wije unyandamile.”
41010022	Ninga imwene hakakunyanghala ichihanga chakwe kosoko ye imbuli yo, hakaleuka kwa usungu kosoko hakowa na sawo nyingi.
41010023	Yesu hoyalanga kose kose, hakawagamba awefusa wakwe, “Foikuwa nghugutu ku wanhu wagoli kukwingila kuundewa we Mulungu!”
41010024	Awefusa hawakisina kosoko ya simbuli siso isakwe. Yesu hakawabidula kahi, yakugamba: “Mowana, fikugutu lugano kwingila ku undewa wa Mulungu!
41010025	Fihufu inhembo kwingila muchihengele che singano, kusuma imugoli kwingila mu undewa we Mulungu.”
41010026	Nawo hawakisina lugano, wakumugamba, “No nani yekudaha kuhona?”
41010027	Yesu yawakumhulila meso, yagamba, “Ku wanhu isikudahika, ninga kwa Mulungu si nhaifo; kosoko gose gakudahika kwa Mulungu.”
41010028	Petulo yakonga kumugamba, “Langa, aseye chileka fyose chikwandamila gweye.”
41010029	Yesu hakagamba, “Chawelu nikumutamilani Hechaka munhu yalekile nyumba, ama wanduguse wagosi, ama walumbu sakwe, ama ng'ina, ama Babakwe, ama wanagwe, ama migunda, kosoko yangu na kosoko ya imbuli swanu.
41010030	Inghakwinghigwa mikono igana muchigele chino cha hambiya; nyumba, na wandugu wagosi, na wechike, wang'ina munhu, na wana, na migunda hamwedu ne migogolo. Na muchilunga chikwija uwumi wa majuwa gose.
41010031	Ninga wengi wakunghonga wakuwa wakunyuma, na wakunyuma wakuwa wa wakunghonga.”
41010032	Nawo hawowa munjila wakukwila kuluta Yelusalemu, na Yesu, hakowa yawalongolele, hawakisina, awaya fowamwandamilage hawogoha. Hakawalonda kahi awaya ikumi na weli hakakonga kuwatamila agakwenda gamupate.
41010033	Hakagamba, “Langeni chikuluta Yelusalemu, iMwana we munhu yakwenda yagumigwe mumikono ya wakulu wa watambiki na watulumi, nawo wakulamula fina yakomigwe, wakumuguma mu mikono ya wamemb,
41010034	nawo, wakwenda wamuhowe na kumutwila mate, kumutowa na mikotya, na kumukoma; ganghaloka majuwa madatu yekwinuka muchilalo.”
41010035	Yakobo na Yohana, awana wa Sebedayo, hawamulutila, wakugamba, “Mwalimu! Chikuhananga uchigolosele dyo dyose dyochikukutasa.”
41010036	Yawagamba, “Mukuhananga niwagoloseleni choni?”
41010037	Hawamugamba, “Uchinghe seye kwikala, yumonga kumukono wako wo kulume na yumonga kumukono wako wokumoso muditunyo dyako.”
41010038	Yesu hakawagamba, “Musimanyile chomukutasa. Mukudaha kunywila ichikombe chonikunywila niye? Kahe kubatisigwa ubatiso wonikubatisigwa niye?”
41010039	Hawamugamba, “Chikudaha.” Yesu hakawagamba, “Ichikombe chonikunywila niye mukuchunywila, na ubatiso wonikubatisigwa niye mobatiswa.
41010040	Ninga imbuli yo kwikala ku mukono wangu wo kulume ama wo kumoso, si dyangu kuwenghani, ninga wakwenda wenghigwe awafulusa kwikiligwa.”
41010041	Awaya ikumi wakahulike hawakonga kuwasuhila Yakobo na Yohana.
41010042	Yesu hakawenanga, na kuwagamba, “Mumanya fina awaya awakutaligwa kuwa wakulu wa Mataifa, wakutawala kwa ludole, na wakulu wawo wakuwatumagisa.
41010043	Ninga isikuwa nhaifo ukwenu;
41010044	ninga imunhu yakuhananga yowe mukulu kwenu, yakuwa munhu mutogomi wenu.
41010045	Kosoko iMwana we munhu naye nghejile kutogomeligwa; ninga kutogoma na kulafa uumi wakwe udahe kuhonya wengi.”
41010046	Wakafike Yeliko, yakowe yekuleuka kulawa Yeliko, hamwedu na wefusa wakwe, ditewa ikulu dya wanhu, imwana wa Timayo, Batolomayo, ayuya imutasaji imudula, hakekala hanghanda ye injila.
41010047	Naye yakahulike fina no Yesu Munasaleti, Hakakonga kutula chowe na kugamba, “Mwana wa Daudi, Yesu, Nyonele ubasi!”
41010048	Wengi hawamugombela uleke yanyamale. Ninga hakongesa kwinula dijwi, “Mwana wa Daudi nyonele ubasi!”
41010049	Yesu hakema, yokugamba, “Mwinangeni.” Hawamwinanga ayuya imudula, wakumugamba, “Kiinghe moyo! Inuka, yakukwinanga.”
41010050	Hakakubita dikasu dyakwe, na kujumha, na kumulutila Yesu.
41010051	Yesu yamubidula, yamugamba, “Ukuhananga nikugolosele choni?” Ayuya imudula yamugamba, “Mwalimu wangu! Nikuhananga nidahe kona.”
41010052	Yesu hakamugamba, “Luta, dihuwi dyako dikuhonya.” Chimwande hakona; hakamwandamila Yesu munjila.
41011001	Ichigele fowasegele habehi na Yelusalemu, Betifage na Betania, habehi ne ditunda dya Miseituni, baho hawatuma weli wa wefusa wakwe
41011002	hoyawagamba: “Luteni kuchikaya chiya chuwile kumwande yenu. Fomukwingila umo mofika mwana we dipunda, dyohigwe, idyene disinati dikwiligwe na munhu. Didoholeni munigalile.
41011003	Ne munhu yanghamusani Nhani mukutenda nheifo, gambeni, iMundewa yakudihananga yakwenda yadyuwise lulubaha.”
41011004	Kamei howoluta, na kudyona dipunda diya didodogi, dyohigwa hamulango, kunje, hawadidohola,
41011005	awanhu awemile uko weja wawagamba, “Mukugolosa choni kudidohola dipunda didodogi?”
41011006	Hawawatamila fina Yesu foyawasigilile, nawo howowengha.
41011007	Hawamwigalila Yesu dipunda diya didodogi, na kutandika sisuke sawo muchanhya yakwe.
41011008	Wanhu itewa hawatandalike sisuke sawo munjila, na wamonga amatambi gowabenile mumigunda.
41011009	Na awanhu awalongole na waya awandamile kunyuma howokwinula amajwi, “Hosana! Noyamotesigwe iyakwija kudisina dye Mundewa!
41011010	Umotesigwa na undewa ukwija we Baba yetu Daudi! Hosana kuchanhya kulanga!”
41011011	Naye hakengila Yelusalemu mpaka kugati ya dihekalu, yakafuluse kulanga kose kose. Kosoko hayuwa ugele wa hegulo, hakalawa, hakaluta Betania hamwedu nawaya ikumi na weli.
41011012	Dijuwa dyandamile fowalawile Betania, hakowa na njala.
41011013	Hakona kwa hatali musada wina manyagala, hoyoluta kosoko, nhegela kokona chinhu muchanhya yakwe. Yakafike bahaya nghonile chinhu ila manyagala; kosoko usowile ugele wo kwifa kwa masada.
41011014	Hakaugamba nhafi, “Kulawa diyelo na majuwa gose imunhu yanghadiye imudyo ukwako.” Awefusa wakwe hawahulika.
41011015	Hawafika Yelusalemu, naye foyengile kwihekalu, yakonga kuwawinga awaya awenda wokwambasa na wenda wogula kwihekalu kugati. Hakasibidula si mesa sawaya awende wobadili mapesa, na magoda gawo wambasage si njiwa,
41011016	ninga nghalekile munhu yalonde chinhu mwihekalu.
41011017	Hakawafusa, hakagamba: “Togoleni! Isitulumigwe, fina, ‘Inyumba yangu yokwinangigwa nyumba ya kutasila ku mataifa gose.’ Ninga anyeye muyigolosa kifana ipango dya wahiji!”
41011018	Awakulu wa watambiki na watulumi hawahulika, hawahananga njila ya kumukoma kosoko hawamogoha. Kosoko amatewa gose hawajuma ku mafuso gakwe.
41011019	Ikafike hegulo hakaleuka mukaya.
41011020	Nhosikusiku wakowe wakuloka howowona umusada uya unyala kulawa kwisina.
41011021	iPetulo hakagelegela, hakamugamba, “Labi, langa, dibiki dowaligitise dinyala nya.”
41011022	Yesu hakabidula, “Muhuwileni Mulungu.”
41011023	Chawelu nikumutamilani, wowose yakugamba ditunda dino Ng'oka ukakubitigwe kubahali yaleke kuwa na manhonge muchidoga chakwe ninga yahuwile gago goyalongile gogoloseka, gakuwa gakwe.
41011024	Kosoko iyo nikumutamilani: Gogose gomukutasa huwileni fina mukugahokela.
41011025	Nanye chila fomukwima na kufuga, lekeleleni hona mwina mbuli yoyose na munhu, uleke iBaba yenu yowile kulanga yawalekelele nanyeye kubana kwenu.
41011026	Ninga nghonaga nyeye musikulekelela, iBaba yenu yowile kulanga nghakumulekelelani na nyeye kubana kwenu.
41011027	Kahi haweja Yelusalemu. Kamei foyagendage mwihekalu, howomulutila awakulu wa watambiki na watulumi, na wasehe,
41011028	wakumugamba, “Kwa udaha waki ukugolosa gano? No nani yakwinghile udaha uwo ugolose gano?”
41011029	Yesu hakawagamba, “Nikumusani mbuli imwedu, munibidule, kamei nikwenda niwatamileni kwa udaha waki nikugolosa gano.
41011030	Ubatiso wa Yohana haulawa kulanga ama kuwanhu? Nhamileni.”
41011031	Howokonga kuwanga awecho kwa wecho wakugamba fina chinghagamba, “Haulawa kulanga,” yakwenda yachigambe, “Nhani musamuhuwile?”
41011032	Chinghagamba, “Haulawa kuwanhu,” (Hawogoha wanhu, kosoko awanhu wose hawona iYohana fina mugonesi we chawelu.)
41011033	Hawamubidula Yesu, wakugamba, “Chisimanyile.” Yesu hakawagamba, “Aniye nani sikuwatamilani nyeye ni kwa udaha waki nikugolosa gano.”
41012001	Hakakonga kulonga nawo kwa mbasi, “Munhu yumonga yahanda mugunda wakwe wa misabibu, hakasungulusila ikigo, na kukata ikolongo dya kukamila, hakajenga ilingo, hoyokwika wemilisi, hoyoluta ku iisi ya kutali.
41012002	Ugele wakwe ukafike hakatuma imutumwa wakwe kuwaya wakwimilisa umugunda wakwe, yamwigalile si sabibu.
41012003	Hawamulonda, hawamutowa, hawamutaga kunje, mikono muhala.
41012004	Hakatuma kahi ukwawo mutumwa yungi, ayu naye hawamubulaga na kumuguma malonda mwitwi na kumugolosela wihi.
41012005	Hakatuma yungi, ayo hawamukoma; na wamonga wengi hawawatowa, na wamonga kumukoma.
41012006	Hakowa na yumwedu yasigale, imwanagwe mwendigwa wakwe, ayuno naye hakamutuma ukwawo kundumiliso yakugamba, ‘Wakwenda wamogohe imwanangu,’
41012007	Ninga awaya awakwimilisa umugunda, hawakitamila wakugamba, ‘Ayuno no muhasi. Handikoni chimukome, na uhasi ukuwa wetu!’
41012008	Hawamukola na kumukoma, na kumutaga kunje yo mugunda we misabibu.
41012009	“Kamei yatende nhani ayuya iMundewa, imwenyemugunda we misabibu? Yakwija na kuwakoma awemilisi waya, na umugunda uya we misabibu yakwende yeke wemilisi wengi.
41012010	Diwandiko dino musinati mudisome? ‘Isumbi yalemigwe na wajengaji iyo igalukagaluka no sumbi inghulu ya hagati.
41012011	Imbuli ino ilawa kwe Mundewa; Nadyo ni ijumo mumeso getu!’”
41012012	Nawo hawahananga kumukola ninga hawogoha amatewa, kosoko hawamanya fina imbasi iya kawalonga awene. Hawamuleka na kuleuka.
41012013	Howotuma ukwakwe wamonga wa Mafalisayo na Mahelode, uleke wa mutegele kwa simbuli sakwe.
41012014	Baho fowamufikile, hawamugamba, “Mwalimu, chimanya fina agweye kwa munhu wa chawelu, kahi nghukogoha ukulu wa munhu, kosoko nghukulanga sifuta sa wanhu, ninga muchawelu ukuifusa injila ye Mulungu. Togola ni fiswanu kuliha kodi kwa Kaisali ama si nheifo?
41012015	Chimwinghe, chinghamwinghe?” Naye yakamanye ichimwefe chawo, hakawagamba, “Nhani mukunigesa? Nigalileni ifesa niilange.”
41012016	Hawegala. Kamei hakawagamba, “Isanamu ino lubonoto lunolwani?” Hawamugamba, “Lwa Kaisali,”
41012017	Yesu hakabidula yekugamba, “Mwingheni Kaisali aga Kaisali, na ge Mulungu mwingheni Mulungu.” Hawamwisina lugano.
41012018	Kamei amasadukayo, wanhu wakugamba fina kwachaka kwinuka awafile, hawamulutila, na kumusa wekugamba,
41012019	“Mwalimu, Musa hakachiwandikila, ‘Fina imunduguse we munhu yangafa yanghamuleka imuke kachaka mwana, imunduguse yamulonde imwanamuke yuya uleke yamwelekele imunduguse wana.’
41012020	Heja howa na wanhu mufungate we ndugu; imukulu hakatole mwanamuke, na kufa, ngheleke naye.
41012021	Iwakeli naye hakamulonda, hoyokufa, naye nghalekile mwana. Na wakadatu naye nheifia,
41012022	hata wose mufungate, wasalekile wana. Kundumo, ayuya imwanamuke naye hoyokufa.
41012023	Mukwinuka wafile kokuwa muke wa yehoki? Kosoko wose mufungate hawamutola.”
41012024	Yesu hakabidula, yekugamba, “Togoleni musikwagilila kosoko musimanyile amawandiko kahi udaha we Mulungu?
41012025	Kosoko awanhu ma wakwinuka kulawa kuwafile, wasikutola kahiwasikutoligwa, ninga wakuwa fina malaika wowile kulanga.
41012026	Na fina awafile wakwinuligwa: ‘Musisomile muchitabu cha Musa, sula ye chibiki?’ Fina iMulungu foyamutamile yakugamba, ‘Aniye na Mulungu wa Ibulahimu, na Mulungu wa Isaka, na Mulungu wa Yakobo.’
41012027	Si Mulungu wa wafile, ninga wa womi, kwa nheifo mukwagilila lugano.”
41012028	Yumonga wa watulumi hakeja na kuwahulika wakulonga naye. Hakona fina kawabidula fiswamu, hakamusa: “Mumalagiso gose dilagiso dihoki no dikumwande ya gose?”
41012029	Yesu hakamubidula yekumugamba, “Dye nghonga nodi 'Hulika gweye Isilaeli! iMundewa Mulungu wetu ni Mundewa yumwedu.
41012030	Nagwe umwende iMundewa Mulungu wako, no umoyo wako wose, ne chidoga chako chose, ne misungu yako yose, no ludole lwako lwose.'
41012031	Na dyakeli no dino: 'Umwende imiyago fina foukiyenda gomwecho.' Hechaka ilagiso dingi dikulu kusuma gano.”
41012032	Ayuya imutulumi yamugamba “Chawelu, Mwalimu! Kulonga fiswanu fina iMulungu ni yumwedu, ninga kwachaka yungi, ninga imwene du.
41012033	Na kumwenda imwene kwa moyo wose, na umanyi wose, na kwa ludole lose; na kumwenda imiyago fina fyo ukiyenda gomwecho. Imbuli nghulu kusuma kumulafila iMulungu nhambiko yokusomigwa na kwingha kose.”
41012034	Naye Yesu yakone fina kabidula kwa misungu, yamugamba “Agweye ghwihatali na undewa wa Mulungu.” Kulawa baho hachaka munhu wowose yagesile kumusa mbuli kahi.
41012035	Ugele Yesu foyafusage mwihekalu, hakawagamba, “Awatulumi wakugamba Kilisito ni Mwana wa Daudi?
41012036	iDaudi imwecho kwa udaha wa Muhe wa Musunhile hakagamba: ‘Mundewa yamugamba iMundewa wangu: Ikala umukono wangu wo kulume, mpaka niweke awanghondo wako, wowe hasi ye migulu yako.’”
41012037	Daudi imwecho yakugamba, “Mundewa aho kagaluka mwanagwe nhani?” Na ditewa dyose wende womutegelesa kwa chinyemi.
41012038	Mumafuso gakwe hakawagamba, “Muwe meso na watulumi, awakwenda kugenda wafalile makasu matali na kulamusigwa mumagulilo,
41012039	na kwikala kumwande mumasinagogi, na magoda ga kumwande mufyakudiya fye si sikukuu.
41012040	Wakudiya kusinyumba sa wegane, na kwa chimwefe wakuwomba mawombi matali. Awano wakwija wapata iliganiso dikulu dijuwa dye ndumo.”
41012041	Naye yekale kulanga disanduku dyowakuguma fowakumulafila Mulungu, kalanga amatewa fowaguma amapesa musanduku. Wagoli wengi hawaguma mengi;
41012042	yeja mwanamuke yumwedu mwigane, mukiwa, yalafa sendi mbili, kifana nusu ya dipesa.
41012043	Yawenanga awefusa wakwe, yawagamba, “Chawelu nikumutamilani, Ayuno imwanamuke, imwigane imukiwa kaguma nyingi kusuma wose wakuguma musanduku.
41012044	Kosoko awo wose waguma sigafu; ninga yuno mu ukiwa wakwe, kaguma fyose foyenafyo ne chakudiya chakwe chose nacho.”
41013001	Ugele foyalawage mwihekalu, yumwedu wa wefusa wakwe, hakamugamba, “Mwalimu Langa, uswanu wa amawe na majengo gano!”
41013002	Yesu hoyobidula, yamugamba, “Ukugona amajengo gano amakulu? Disikwenda disigale iwe muchanhya ya diwe idyene disikwenda dije dimoligwe.”
41013003	Yakekale mwitunda dya miseituni, kumwande ye dihekalu, Petulo na Yakobo na Yohana na Andelea hawamusa wemwene.
41013004	Chitamile simbuli sino sikuwa milaki, nacho ichitangilo ni choni cha ugele wa ago gose kumemelesigwa?
41013005	Yesu yakonga kuwatamila, “Mulangisise imunhu yanghawadanhilise.”
41013006	Matewa gokwija mwisina dyangu, wakugamba, “Ani no niye!” nawo wakwenda wawadanhilise wengi
41013007	Nanye munghahulika simbuli sa inghondo, na minong'ono ye inghondo, munghogohe, ago gakwenda galawanise. Ninga indumo yecho ikali.
41013008	Kosoko ditaifa dikulewa nghondo na undewa ukulawa nghondo. Kukuwa na dimasingisa dye iyisi ako nako, kukuwa na njala. Ago no nghonga ya usungu fina wo kweleka chali.
41013009	Nanye mukilangisise muwenyecho. Kosoko wakwenda wamwigaleni kumabalasa. Na kumasinagogi mukutowigwa; nanye mukwende mwigaligwe ku majumbe na wandewa kosoko yangu, kuwa uhomelesi ukwawo.
41013010	Na imbuli swanu, ikwenda ihubiliigwe ku mataifa gose.
41013011	Na fowakuwalonda nyeye na kuwasongesa, munghadoge go mukwenda mulonge; ninga dyo dyose dyomukwinghigwa ugele uwo, dilongeni. Kosoko si nyeye mukulonga; ninga ni Muhe Musunhile.
41013012	Kahi indugu yakumusongesa imunduguse uleke yakomigwe na Baba yakumusongesa imwanagwe. Kahi awana wakuwenukila awaweleke na kuwakoma.
41013013	Nanye mukwenda musuligwe na wanhu wose kosoko ya disina dyangu. Ninga iyakugendelela mpaka kundumo, ayo noyakuhona.
41013014	“Munghona ludeso lwima ahanhu ahene lusikuhanangigwa lwima (iyakusoma yamanye).” Noho awowile, “Uyahudi watijile kumatunda.
41013015	Na imunhu yowile mukano yanghahumuluke, kahi yanghengile kulonda chinhu munyumba yakwe.
41013016	Naye yowile kumugunda yanghoye ukaya kulonda suke yakwe.
41013017	Usungu wawo awasokesi, na waya awakonghesa amajuwa gago!
41013018	Mutase unghowe ugele we inyota!
41013019	Kosoko amajuwa gago gakuwa na mugogolo, uwo usinati uwe kulawa inghonga ya kumba, foyombile iMulungu mpaka hambiya. Ninga isikuwa nheifo kahi.
41013020	Mhali iMundewa nghagadumukise amajuwa gago; hasowile hakuhona munhu wowose, ninga kosoko ya wasaguligwe woyawasagule. Kagadumukisa amajuwa go.”
41013021	Na ugele uwo imunhu yanghawagamba, “Langa, Kilisito!” kowa akuno ama akuya munghahuwile.
41013022	Kosoko wakwenda wenukile Makilisito ga udasi, na wagonesi wa udasi, wakonesa fitangilo na majumo, uleke wawadanhilise, kulonga chelu hata na wasaguligwe.
41013023	Ninga anyeye mukilangisise, nifulusa kuwatamila, ugele fisinati filawanise.
41013024	“Ninga amajuwa gago, unghaloka umugogolo uwo, dijuwa dikutukuwala, umwesi nao usikumulika,
41013025	sinyelesi sa kulanga solagala, na uludole lwa kuchanhya losingisika.”
41013026	Baho noho wakiyawomona iMwana we Munhu yakwija mumafunde kwa ludole mwingi na ditunyo.
41013027	Noho yakayotuma malaika na kuwakonghola awasagulwa wakwe kulawa si sandi sose ine, kulawa ulwandi lwa kundumo lwe yisi mpaka ulwandi lwe ndumo yo ulanga.
41013028	“Mukifuse difuso dyo musada. Amanhambi gakwe fogakuwa majolo jolo na kukonga kutuguta, mukutanga fina ugele wo kuhanda wahabehi;
41013029	Nanye nheifiya fomukona simbuli so sikukonga, manyeni fina kahabehi mumilango.
41013030	Chawelu, nikuwatamileni, Icheleko chino chisikuloka mpaka ago gamemelesigwe.
41013031	Ulanga na iisi fikuloka, ninga simbuli sangu sisikuloka ng'o.”
41013032	“Ninga imbuli ya ugele uya, ne chipisi chiya, hachaka yamanyile, hata malaika awowile kulanga, kahii Mwana; ninga Baba.
41013033	Mulangisise, Muwe meso, kosoko musimanyile ugele wuya wokuwa milaki.
41013034	Imbasi yakwe ni kifana imunhu yekuluta nhambo, kaileka inyumba yakwe, kawalekela awatumwa wakwe malagiso, na chila munhu no umulimo wakwe, naye kamulagisa imwimilisi wa hamulango yowe meso.
41013035	Muwe meso, kosoko, musimanyile imwenye nyumba yakwija ugele waki, yokuwa hegulo ama muchilo mugati, ama ugele wo kwika dijogolo, ama nhosikusiku.
41013036	Yangheje yolawanisa chimwande na kumufikani mugonile.
41013037	Na dyonikumutamilani nyeye, nikuwatamila wose: Muwe meso!”
41014001	Gakaloke majuwa meli hadyuwa ijuwa ikulu dye Pasaka, na dijuwa dikulu dye mikate isilungigwe. Awakulu wa watambiki na watulumi hawahananga njila ya kumukola kwa chifiso na kumukoma.
41014002	Kosoko hawagamba, “Inghowe ugele we sikukuu, ingheje ikuwa nghondo mu wanhu.”
41014003	Yakowe Betania munyumba ya Simoni mukoma, yakudiya chakudiya, hoyokwija mwanamuke yena chichupa cha mafuta ge mhungile gakwinangigwa nalido ge iliho ikulu. Hakachitula na kumwitilila Yesu mwitwi dyakwe.
41014004	Hahowa na wanhu awene wasuhile mufidoga fyawo wakugamba, “Nhani kwagilisa mafuta ge diliho nhaifino?
41014005	Kosoko mafuta ge diliho dino hagowa gakudaha kuguligwa kwa dinali magana madatu ama na musapu, na kugawiligwa awakiwa!” Hawamusuhila lugano imwanamuke yuya.
41014006	Yesu hakagamba, “Mulekeni! Nhani mukumwidasa? Kanigolosela chinhu chiswanu.
41014007	Kosoko majuwa gose mwenawo wakiwa hamwedu nanye, na chila fomukwenda mukudaha kuwagolosela maswanu. Ninga niye si hamwedu nanye majuwa gose.
41014008	Kagolosa foyadahile; kalongola kuubaka umutufi wangu malihamu kosoko ya kusikigwa kwangu.
41014009	Chawelu, nikumutamilani, chila koikuhubiliigwa imbuli swanu, muchilunga chose na dino doyagolose yuno dyotambuligwa kwa kumugelegela.”
41014010	Yuda Isikalioti, yumwedu wa waya ikumi na weli, yaluta kuwakulu wa watambiki, uleke yamusongese ukwawo.
41014011	Nawo wakahulike hawasekelela lugano, na kulagana naye wamwinghe mapesa. Hakahananga luneka lwa kumusongesa.
41014012	Dijuwa dye nghonga dye mikate isilungigwe, wakachinje ingholo ye iPasaka, awefusa wakwe wamugamba, “No hoki koukuhananga chikugolosele udiile iPasaka?”
41014013	Hawatuma weli mu wefusa wakwe, yakuwagamba, “Luteni ukaya, mokitang'anyila na mugosi yakitwikile ibiga dya meji. Mwandamileni
41014014	na hohose hoyakwingila, mumugambe imukaya: Mwalimu yakugamba, ‘Chuwa hoki ichibuha changu ichawageni, nidiye iPasaka umo hamwedu na wefusa wangu?’
41014015	Naye imwecho yakwenda yamoneseni chibuha chikulu che golofa, chifulusa kuhambigwa, muchitengele umo.”
41014016	Awefusa hawaleuka, hawaluta ukaya, hawona kifana fowasigililigwe; na kutenga chakudiya che sikukuu ye Pasaka.
41014017	Ikafike hegulo, iYesu hakeja hamwedu na waya ikumi na weli.
41014018	Wakekale hachakudiya wakudiya, Yesu hakagamba, “Chawelu, nikumutamilani yumwedu wenu iyakudiya hamwedu na niye yakunisongesa.”
41014019	Hawakonga kona usungu, na kulonga yumwe yumwe. Togola no niye?
41014020	Kawagamba, “Ni yumwedu wa anyeye ikumi na weli, iyakusanhisa hamwedu na niye mwibakuli.
41014021	Kosoko iMwana wa munhu yakuluta fina foyawandikiligwe; ninga usungu wakwe imunhu yuya iyakumusongesa iMwana wa munhu! Hayuwa ikuwa ibeka kwi munhu yuyo nhanga nghelekwe!”
41014022	Ugele fowadiyage, yalonda umukate, na kuulugutisa na kuumogola, kawengha, yakugamba, “Londeni mudiye, auno no mutufi wangu.”
41014023	Yalonda ichikombe, yakamale kulumba; hakawengha; na wose hawonywila.
41014024	Hakawagamba, “Aino no sakame yangu ya dilagano, iikwitika kosoko ya wengi.
41014025	Chawelu, nikumutamilani nyeye, Sikunywa kahi cheleko cho musabibu, mpaka dijuwa diya donikanikunywa umusha mu undewa wa Mulungu.”
41014026	Nawo wakamale kwimba, howolawa kuluta kuditunda dya Miseituni.
41014027	Yesu yawagamba, “Anye mose monileka ichilo cha diyelo,” Kosoko nofyo iwandikwe, “Nikumutowa imudimi, na singholo sikiyagala.
41014028	Ninga ninghafulusa kwinuka kulawa muchilalo, nikuwalongolela kuluta Galilaya.”
41014029	Petulo hakamugamba, “Hata wose wakuleke aniye sikukuleka!”
41014030	Yesu yamugamba, “Chawelu nikukutamila gweye, ichilo cha diyelo, ugele dijogolo disinati dike keli, ukuwa unikanile kadatu.”
41014031	Naye yagendelela kulonga, “Hata inghowa kufa hamwedu nagwe, sikwenda nikukane ng'o!” Wose hawalonga nheifo.
41014032	Kamei haweja kumululu iikwinangigwa Getisemane na kuwagamba awefusa wakwe, “Kaleni hano ugele fonikuwomba.”
41014033	Hoyamulonda Petulo, na Yohana, na Yakobo hamwedu naye. Yakonga kona usungu muchidoga chakwe na kugaya,
41014034	hoyowagamba, “Ichidoga changu china usungu mwingi habehi na kufa. Ikaleni hano mwikale meso.”
41014035	Yakalute kumwande chidodogi, hokogwa funama, yakuwomba, fina inghadahika ichipisi chicho chimuleukile.
41014036	Hakagamba, “Tate, go Babangu! Gose gakudahika ukwako. Unileusile ichikombe chino, si fina fonikwenda niye, ninga, foukwenda agweye.”
41014037	Yakwija yakuwafika wagona sinhongo, yamugamba Petulo, “Togola Simoni kugona? Kulemeligwa kwikala meso hata disaa dimwedu?”
41014038	Ikaleni meso muwombe, munghengile mumagesa. Chidoga chikudaha amba umutufi wachaka ludole.
41014039	Hakaluta kahi, kuwomba, yakulonga imbuli iya.
41014040	Hakeja kahi hakawafika wagona; kosoko ameso gawo hagowa masito. Kahi wasamanyile dya kumubidula.
41014041	Hakeja kahi lwakadatu, hakawagamba, “Mwikali timbula nhongo du na kubwihila? Ifuluka ugele nouuno! Langeni, iMwana we Munhu yakugumigwa mu mikono yawo awena uwihi.
41014042	Inukeni, chigendeni, langeni ayuya yakunisongesa kasegelela.”
41014043	Baho ugele yakulonga, Yuda hakeja, yumwedu wa waya ikumi na weli hamwedu naye itewa. Wena mapanga na mapulo, walawa ku wakulu wa watambiki, na watulumi, na wasehe.
41014044	Ayuya musongesi kawengha chitangilo: Yakugamba, “Wonikamunonela, no mwene. Mukoleni mumulonde kwa kumwimilisa.”
41014045	Kamei yakeje, chimwande hoyomulutila, hoyagamba, “Mukulu!” hoyomunonela.
41014046	Hawagolola imikono yawo na kumukola.
41014047	Yumwedu wawo yowile baho, hakakwega dipanga dyakwe hakamunghenya mutumwa wa mutambiki mukulu na kumudumula inghutwi.
41014048	Yesu hakabidula yekuwagamba, “Nhafo! Mwija mukola muhiji na mapanga na mapulo kunilonda niye?
41014049	Chila ijuwa hanuwa hamwedu na nyeye mwihekalu nikufusa, musanikolile. Ninga adino dilawanisa uleke amatulumo gamemelesigwe.”
41014050	Baho hawamuleka, na kutija wose.
41014051	Na mwanike yumonga hakamwandamila, kegubika suke ya bafuta. Hawamukola,
41014052	hakaleka aiya isuke yakwe ye bafuta hakatija mwasi.
41014053	Hawamulonda Yesu, hawamwigala kwa mutambiki mukulu, hawamumemelela wose, awakulu wa watambiki na wasehe na watulumi.
41014054	Petulo yamwandamila kwa kutali, mpaka kugati ku dikumbo dye mutambiki mukulu. Yekala hamwedu na wemilisi, yakotela moto.
41014055	Baho awakulu wa watambiki na dibalasa dyose hawahananga uhomelesi muchanhya ya Yesu uleke wamukome, ninga hawaswela.
41014056	Kosoko wengi hawahomelesa udasi, ninga hawaswela uhomelesi wawo usaligane.
41014057	Kamei wamonga hawema na kumuhomelela udasi wakugamba:
41014058	Aseye hachimuhulika yakugamba, “Aniye nikudimola dihekalu dino dijengigwe kwa mikono, na fogakuloka majuwa madatu nikujenga dingi idisikugolosigwa kwa mikono.
41014059	Hata nheifo, uhomelesi wawo usaliganile.”
41014060	Kamei imutambiki Mukulu hakema muchiligati, yokumusa Yesu yakugamba, “Nghukubidula mbuli? Awano wakukuhomelesa choni?”
41014061	Ninga hakanyamala kahe nghamubidule mbuli. Imutambiki Mukulu yamusa kahi, yekumugamba, “Agweye no Kilisito, Imwana we Yamotesigwe?”
41014062	Yesu yagamba, “Heye, noniye! Nanye mukamumona iMwana we Munhu, yekale ku mukono wo kulume wo ludole, yakwija mumafunde gakulanga!”
41014063	iMutambiki mukulu yadega si suke sakwe, yakugamba, “China soko yaki yakuhananga wahomelesi?
41014064	Muhulika ulubeso lwakwe. Mukona nhani nyeye?” Wose hawalamula fina iwagila yakomigwe:
41014065	Wamonga, hawakonga kumutwila mate, hawamugubika ichihanga, na kumutowa, na kumugamba, “Haya tanga!” Hata awasilikali nawo hwamuhokela kwa kumutowa makofi.
41014066	Petulo hakowa kwikumbo; hakamwijila mutogomi we chike we mutambiki mukulu.
41014067	Hakamona Petulo yakotela moto, hakamukumhulila meso yakumugamba, “Agwe nagwe hakuwa hamwedu na yuya iYesu Munasaleti.”
41014068	Hokakana na kugamba, “Simanyile kahi sikuhulika so ukulonga gweye, hoyolawa kunje mpaka kwilango.” Dijogolo hodikwika Yakana. Dijogolo hodikwika.
41014069	Na yuya imutumishi we chike hoyomona kahi, hoyokonga kuwatamila awemile bahaya, “Ayuno yumwedu wawo!”
41014070	Hoyokana kahi. Chipisi chidodogi kahi awaya awemile bahaya howomugamba Petulo, “Chawelu agweye kwa yumwedu wawo, kosoko kwa Mugalilaya gweye.”
41014071	Hoyokonga kuligitisa na kilaha, “Simumanyile imunhu yuno yo mukumulonga!”
41014072	Chimwande dijogolo dyeka keli. Petulo hoyogelegela aiya imbuli iyalongigwe na Yesu, “Ugele dijogolo disinati dike lwakeli ukuwa unikanile kadatu.” Na yakakonge kudoga hoyolila.
41015001	Chimwande nhosikusiku awakulu wa watambiki hawekala hebalasa hamwedu na wasehe wa watulumi na dibalasa dyose, hawamoha Yesu, hawamulonda, hawamwigala kwa Pilato.
41015002	Pilato yamusa, “Agweye no gwegwe go, Mundewa wa Wayahudi?” Yabidula yakumugamba, “Agwe kuilonga.”
41015003	Awakulu wa watambiki wende womuhomelela mbuli nyingi.
41015004	Pilato kamusa kahi yakugamba, “Nghukubidula? Langa ni mbuli nyingahi sowakukuhomelesa.”
41015005	Ninga Yesu nghabidule mbuli kahi, Pilato hakakisina!
41015006	Ugele we sikukuu yakowadoholela mufungwa yumwedu, wowakumutasa.
41015007	Hahowa na munhu yakwinangigwa Balaba, kohigwa hamwedu na wanhu awagolose finju na kukoma mufinju iyo.
41015008	Amatewa howokwija hawakonga kutasa yawatendele fina foyasowele,
41015009	Pilato yawabidula, yakugamba, “Togoleni mukuhanaga niwadoholeleni iMundewa wa Wayahudi?”
41015010	Kosoko hakamanya fina awakulu wa watambiki hawamulafa kwa chimwefe.
41015011	Ninga awakulu wa watambiki howowasonghesa amatewa fina ibeka yawadoholele Balaba.
41015012	Pilato yawabidula kahi yakuwagamba, “Nimutende nhani ayuno yo mukumugamba Mundewa wa Wayahudi?”
41015013	Hawatula chowe kahi wakugamba, “Mudumangise!”
41015014	Pilato yawagamba, “Kwina wihi waki woyagolose?” Weja wagendelele kutula chowe, “Musambase!”
41015015	Pilato yakende kuwendesa matewa, hakewadoholela Balaba; yakafuluse kumujola ne mikotya hakemulafa Yesu yadumangiswe.
41015016	Awasilikali hawamulonda hawamwigala kwi kumbo dikwinangwa Plaitolia. hawawalonda chitewa chose.
41015017	Hawamufasa isuke idunghundunghu, hawaluka nghofia ya miwa, hawamufasa mwitwi dyakwe.
41015018	Hawakonga kumulamusa: “Baho hako Go Mundewa wa Wayahudi!”
41015019	Hawamutowa ne chigwami mwitwi, hawamutwila mate, hawafugama, wakumufunamila.
41015020	Wakamale kumuseyigila, hawamuhambula dikasu diya didunghudunghu, hawamufasa sisuke sakwe imwecho. Hawamulafa kunje uleke wamudumangise.
41015021	Kamei hawamudindilisa imunhu yalokage kulawa kumugunda, Simoni Mukilene, Baba yawo cha Isikanda na Lufo, uleke yaudinghule musalaba wakwe.
41015022	Hawamwigala ahanhu hakwinangigwa Goligota, nong'amba, Ahanhu he diguha dye ditwi.
41015023	Hawamwingha difai ihanganisigwe manemane, ninga ghayunywile.
41015024	Hawamutungika, na kugawa si suke sakwe, hawatowa kula chila munhu yapate choni.
41015025	Hayuwa chipisi cha saa ya kadatu, hawamutungika mumusalaba.
41015026	Hahowa na anuwani muchanhya yakwe, “MUNDEWA WA WAYAHUDI.”
41015027	Hamwedu naye hawatungikigwa wahiji weli, yumonga kumukono wakwe wokulume, na yumonga kumukono wakwe wokumoso.
41015028	Uleke diwandiko dimemelekele idikugamba, “Yasambaswa hamwedu na wehi.”
41015029	Wagendage munjila howomuliga, hawafumila kwa kusingisasingisa amatwi gawo wakugamba, “Ahaa! Agweye ukudaha kudimola dihekalu na kudijenga kwa majuwa madatu!
41015030	Kihonye gomwecho, uhumuluke mumusalaba!”
41015031	Awakulu wa Watambiki nawo hawamuseyigila awecho kwa wecho, hamwedu na watulumi wakugamba, “Hakahonya wamonga,” nghakudaha kihonya imwecho!
41015032	Kilisito iMundewa wa Isilaeli na hayahulumuka hambiya mumusalaba uleke chone, chimuhuwile! Awaya nawo awatungikigwe hamwedu naye howomuliga.
41015033	Ikowe saa ya mutandatu hokukuwa chisa, iisi yose mpaka saa ya dikenda,
41015034	Ikafike saa ya dikenda, Yesu yekwinula dijwi dyakwe kwa ludole, “Eloi, Eloi, lama sabakitani?” No kugamba, “Mulungu wangu Mulungu wangu nhani unilekile?”
41015035	Awamonga awemile baho awahulika na kugamba, “Langa, yakumwinanga Eliya!”
41015036	Yumonga hayabilima lumangho, na kutubwisa didodoki na kudifabika musiki. Hakamwingha yonywe, yakugamba, “Lekeni! Chilange nghonaga Eliya kokwija kumuhulumusa!”
41015037	Naye Yesu yalafa ijwi ikulu, kamei na kufa.
41015038	Dipasiya dya hekalu dyadegeka fibemhe fili, kulawa kuchanya mpaka hasi.
41015039	Yuya iyakida, iyemile baho yakumulanga, yakone kafa kwanjila iyo. Hoyagamba, “Chawelu ayuno hakowa Mwana wa Mulungu!”
41015040	Hahowa na wanawake wakulanga kwa hatali. Mugati yawo hakowa Maliamu Magidalene, na Maliam ing'ina yawo cha Yakobo imudodo na Yose, na Salome.
41015041	Awo nowakiyandamile naye ako Galilaya, na kumutogomela. Na wamonga wengi awejile naye mpaka Yelusalemu.
41015042	Ikowe hegulo, kosoko ni Matandilo, nadyo ijuwa dikulongolela isabato.
41015043	Hakaluta Yusufu munhu wa Alimataya, munhu mukulu, munhu wa dibalasa dya mahonge. Imwene imwecho yakugojela undewa we Mulungu, yagolosa chigosi, yekwingila kwa Pilato, na kumutasa umutufi wakwe Yesu.
41015044	Pilato yekisina lugano kosoko fina kafulusa kufa. Hakamwinanga iyakida yuya, na kumusa fina kufa kafulusa katali.
41015045	Yakafuluse kupata ichawelu kwi Akida yuya, na kumwingha Yusufu umutufi wa Yesu.
41015046	Naye hakagula sanda ya bafuta, hakamuhulumusa, na kumufasa isanda iya, yamwika muchilalo chisongoligwe mudiwe. Hakafingilisa diwe kumulango we chilalo.
41015047	Naye Maliamu Magidalene na Maliamu ng'inakwe wa Yose, hawalanga ahaya hoyekigwe.
41016001	Isabato ikaloke Maliamu Magidalene, na Maliamu ing'ina wa Yakobo, na Salome, hawagula mafuta gena mhungile swanu wakamubake.
41016002	Kwikali lwisalwisa, dijuwa dye inghonga dye dijuma, hawaluta kuchilalo ugele dijuwa fodyakongage kutonhomoka.
41016003	Hawakonga kulonga awecho kwa wecho, “Nani yakuchifingilisila diwe diya hamulango we chilalo?”
41016004	Wakalange na kona diwe diya difulusa kufingilisigwa; nadyo hadyuwa ikulu lugano.
41016005	Hawengila kuchilalo, na kona mwanike yekale ulwandi lo kulume kafala suke njelu, hawakisina.
41016006	Yawagamba, “Munghakisine! Mukumuhananga Yesu Munasaleti, iyatungikigwe. Kenuka muchilalo! Kahechaka hano, halangeni howamwikile.
41016007	Ninga luteni mukawatamile awefusa wakwe, na Petulo: Fina kawalongolela kuluta Galilaya, mukamona uko fina foyamutamileni.”
41016008	Hawalawa kunje, hawabilima kulawa hachilalo, kosoko wakutetema na kisina. Kahi wasamutamile munhu mbuli kosoko hawogoha. [
41016009	Naye yakenuke nhosikusiku dijuwa dye inghonga dye kukonga dye dijuma, hoyokiyonesa kunghonga kwa Maliamu Magidalene, imwene wo yamulafa simhepo mufungate.
41016010	Aye hoyoluta hoyowatamila awaya awowile hamwedu naye. Nawo wakali hongesa na kulila;
41016011	Ninga awene fowahulike fina mumi, naye kawona, wasahuwile.
41016012	Kahi hakakiyonesa na weli wawo na kena futa ingi; nawo wende wagenda wakuluta kumugunda.
41016013	Awa nawo hawaluta hawawatamila awaya wamonga, awene nawo hawaleka kuhuwila.
41016014	Hanyuma, hakoneka na waya ikumi na yumwedu fowende wodiya. Hokawagombela kosoko ya kuswela dihuwi kwawo na ukugutu we fidoga fyawo, kosoko wasawahuwile awaya awamwonile foyenuke muchilalo.
41016015	Hakawagamba, “Luteni kuchilunga chose mukahubili imbuli swanu kwa chila munhu.
41016016	Iyakuhuwila na kubatisigwa yakuhona; inghakuhuwila yakulamuliligwa.
41016017	Fitangilo fino fikwende fikiyandamile na awaya awakuhuwila. Kwi sina dyangu wolafa si mhepo; wolonga kwa nonga nyisha;
41016018	wokola majoka, hata wanghadiya chinhu cha kukoma chisikuwabulaga ng'o; wokwika imikono yawo muwatamu, nawo wakuhona.”
41016019	Basi Mundewa Yesu yakamale kulonga nawo, hakenuligwa kulanga na kwikala umukono wo kulume we Mulungu
41016020	Nawo awaya hawalawa hawaluta kuhubili kosekose, iMundewa yakugolosa milimo hamwedu nawo na kumemelesa aiya imbuli kwa fitangilo ifyakiyandamile nayo. Hano.]
42001001	Kosoko wanhu wengi waguma mikono kwika hamwedu simbuli sigoloseke ukwetu,
42001002	fina fowachisimulila awaya wowile watogomi we imbuli kulawa kunghonga,
42001003	nyona fiswanu kwandika kusoko aniye nani nyandamila simbuli sose kwa habehi, sa ugele ulokile, kwandika hamwedu fina fosilawanise Mutunyigwa Teofilo;
42001004	udahe kumanya chawelu simbuli so utamiligwe.
42001005	Ugele wo undewa wa Helode, Mundewa wa Uyahudi heja howa na mutambiki yumwedu disina dyakwe Sakalia wo ugele wa Abiya, na imukagwe yowa Elisabeti wo ulukolo lwa Haluni.
42001006	Na wose foniweli hawowa wachawelu mumeso ge Mulungu, hawekala fiswanu, hawagendelela kuikola misigililo ye Mundewa bila kubana chochose.
42001007	Nawo weja wowa wechaka mwana, kosoko Elisabeti yowa mugumba hawowa wasehe lugano.
42001008	Hambiya foyatogomage mumulimo wo utambiki hamwande ye Mulungu, foyowile muugele wakwe,
42001009	kwa kwandamila sinhenda se chitambiki, ikula haimugwila imwene kwingila mwihekalu dye Mundewa kufunghisa ufumba.
42001010	Ugele wo kufunghisa amatewa gose ga wanhu hagowa kunje gekutasa.
42001011	Baho Sakalia hakalawiligwa na Malaika we Mundewa, Kema nyima ulwandi lo kulume lwa Hefugilo dyo kufunghisa.
42001012	Kamei Sakalia hakedasika na kogoha lugano foyamonile Malaika.
42001013	Ninga, “Malaika kamutamila Sakalia, ughogohe kusoko kutasa kwako kuhulikigwa na imukago Elisabeti kokweleka mwana we chigosi, nagwe komwinanga disina dyakwe Yohana.
42001014	Nagwe kokuwa na chinyemi na kubwedelela na matewa wonyemuka ugele wo kwelekwa kwakwe.
42001015	Kosoko kokuwa mukulu mumeso ge Mundewa, na imwene nghekunghwa difai kahigimbi mukali, naye komemeswa Muhe Musunhile kulawa munda mwe ng'ina.
42001016	Kawowisa matewa ga wana wa Isilaeli kwe Mundewa Mulungu wawo,
42001017	na komulongolela Mundewa, kolongosigwa ne Muhe na ludole lwa Eliya. Kubidula imimoyo ya waBabamunhu ku wana, kowagolosa awechaka chogoho wowe na madoga ga uchawelu, kuwatandila awanhu kusoko ye Mundewa.”
42001018	Sakalia kamusa Malaika yakugamba, “Nomanya nhani? Aniye namusehe ne mukangu mudaha lugano.”
42001019	Na Malaika kamugamba, “Aniye na Gabilieli, nikwima ahanhu he Mulungu, nhumigwa kulonga na gweye na kukwigalila mbuli swanu fina ino.
42001020	Langa nghudaha kulonga mpaka dijuwa diya gogekwija gelawanisa agano gonikutamile, kusoko nghusifumile simbuli sangu sikwija silawanisa mu ugele wakwe.”
42001021	Wanhu wenda wemugojela Sakalia na hawesina kusoko hakekalisa kwi hekalu.
42001022	Na foyalawile kunje nghadaha kulonga nawo, howemutanga fina kona majumo kugati ye dihekalu; kawengha chitangilo na kugendelela kuwa chimumu.
42001023	Foyafuluse amajuwa go mulimo wakwe, hakoya ukaya ukwakwe.
42001024	Kulawa ugele uwo imuke Elisabeti hakeyoha. Hakefisa kugati kwa chigele cha minyesi mishano, yakugamba,
42001025	“Nhafi no Mundewa foyanigolosele muchigele choyanyonile, kanilegusila chinyala changu mumeso ga wanhu.”
42001026	Mumwesi wa mutandatu kulawa kwiyoha kwa Elisabeti; Malaika Gabilieli hakatumigwa ne Mulungu mukaya ya Galilaya disina dyakwe Nasaleti.
42001027	Kwa bikila yatumisigwe na munhu disina dyakwe Yusufu, wa lukolo lwa Daudi, na disina dya bikila yuyo ni Maliamu.
