42001030	Malaika kamugamba, “Unghogohe Maliamu, kusoko kwinghiwa Dihewa na Mulungu.
42001031	Nagwe kokiyoha na kweleka Mwana we chigosi, na disina dyakwe kokwinangigwa Yesu.
42001032	Kokuwa Mukulu na kokwinangigwa Mwana wa yowile Kuchanhyasi. iMundewa Mulungu komwingha idigoda dyo undewa we Babakwe Daudi.
42001033	Naye kodima awanhu wa Yakobo majuwa gose na undewa wakwe ukuwa wichaka ndumo.”
42001034	Maliamu kamubidula Malaika yakugamba, “Yokuwa nhani mbona simanyile mugosi?”
42001035	Malaika kamubidula kamugamba, “Muhe Musunhile kokwijila muchanhya yako na ludole wa yowile kuchanhyasi wokugubika kosoko yo imwana yekwelekigwa kokwinangigwa musunhile, Mwana we Mulungu.
42001036	Kahi langa imunduguso Elisabeti muudala wakwe Kakiyoha mwana wa chigosi, na auno mwesi wa mutandatu ukwakwe ayuya yowile mugumba.
42001037	Kosoko chila chinhu chikudahika kwe Mulungu.”
42001038	Maliamu kabidula yakugamba, “Langa niye na mutumwa we Mundewa, leka yuwe ukwangu fina foulongile.” Malaika kamuleka, kaluta.
42001039	Ichigele chicho Maliamu hoyekinuka hoyeluta kwa chimwande mpaka isi ya fitunda, mukaya ya Yuda.

42001042	Elisabeti hakalonga kwa dijwi ikulu yakugamba, “Agweye kupata mboto kusuma wanawake wose na cheleko chako chipata mboto!

42001044	Kosoko dijwi dyo mulamuso wako fodyengile munghutwi sangu, ichali chidodogi hachijumha kwa chinyemi mugati ye sinda sangu.

42001046	Maliamu kagamba, “Umoyo wangu ukumutunya Mundewa.
42001047	Na muhe wangu wonela kosoko ye Mulungu mwihula wanguq
42001048	Kosoko kamulanga kwa ubasi mutumwa wakwe muholo, na langa kulawa hambiya awanhu wose woninanga mumoti.

42001055	Fina foyawatamila awakulu setu, hakalonga Abulahamu na weleko wakwe majuwa gose.

42001068	“Yatunyigwe Mundewa Mulungu wa Isilaeli, kusoko kawejila wanhu wakwe, na kuwahonya.
42001069	Kachingha ihembe dya uhonya mwelekwa wa Daudi mutogomo wakwe.
42001070	Fina foyalonga kulawa kunghonga kwa njila ya wagonesi wakwe wasunhile.
42001071	Uleke chihonyigwe kulawa ku wanghondo wetu. Na kulawa mumikono ya awekuchisuhila.
42001072	Kuwonela ubasi awaBaba setu, na kudigelegela dilagano dyakwe disunhile.
42001073	Inyilaha yoyamwilahila iBaba yetu Ibulahimu
42001074	Chihonyigwe kulawa mumukono wa wanghondo wetu, chitogome chichaka kogoha.

42001077	Kuwatamila awanhu wose fina wahonyigwa, kwa kulekeligwa uwihi wawo.

42001079	Awaya wakwikala muchisa, awagubikigwe na dipeho dye difa, kuchilongosa mu njila ye digoya.”
42001080	Kamei, imwana hakakula, hoyopata ludole lwe chimuhe, hoyokwikala kunyika mpaka dijuwa dyo kwiyonesa kwakwe ku Isilaeli.
42002001	Muchigele chicho dilagiso dyalawa kwa Kayisali Agosito ikugamba, “Awanhu wose muchilunga wandikwe masina gawo.”
42002002	Aino yowa nyandikwa ya bosi yalawanise ugele wo undewa wa Kilenio yowile Mundewa wa Silia.

42002004	Yusufu naye hakakwila kulawa Galilaya, Mukaya ya Nasaleti kaluta Yudea mukaya ya Daudi ikwinangigwa Betelehemu, kosoko imwene ni wa lukolo lwa Daudi.
42002005	Hakaluta kiandikisha hamwedu na Maliamu mutumisigwa wakwe naye hakeyoha.
42002006	Ichigele chicho fowowile uko, majuwa gakwe gokidohola geja gafika.
42002007	Kamei hakedohola nhula hanju naye hakowa mugosi, kamufasa sisuke se mwana, kamugonesa ahanhu hokudiila sing'ombe, kwasoko wasapata luneka musinyumba sa wageni.
42002008	Na muisi iiya kweja kowa na wadimi wekwikala kwidimo ne isawo yawo hechilo.
42002009	Malaika we Mundewa hoyowalawila, kema hagati yawo, utunyi we Mundewa houwamulikila, nawo howokwingilwa na itisi ikulu.

42002012	Achino no chitangilo chenu, mokona mwana mudodogi kafasigwa suke sa chali, kagoneswa hanhu hakudiila sing'ombe.”

42002021	Majuwa munana gakaloke, na ugele wo kumufina haufika, howomwinanga Yesu disina dyakwe, ifene foyenangwa na Malaika kabla ya kwifunga kwe ing'ina.

42002023	(Fina foyandikwe muchitabu che malagiso ge Mundewa, “Mwana nhula hanju we chigosi kokwinangigwa musunhile kwe Mundewa).”
42002024	Kahi hawaluta kulafa filafwa ifene dilagiso dye Mundewa fodilongile, “Huwa mbili hagela makinda ge njiwa.”

42002026	Imuhe Musunhile hakamugubulila fina nghodaha kufa mpaka yamone Kilisito we Mundewa.

42002028	Simioni yamudinghula imwana, hoyomutunya Mulungu yakugamba,
42002029	“Hambiya Mundewa kumulekela imutumwa wako, Yaleguke digoya ifene diwandiko dyako fodilongile.

42002031	Ninga awanhu wose wowona uhonya wako woutandile mumeso ga wanhu wose.

42002033	iBabakwe ne ing'ina weja wakisina kosoko ya simbuli salongigwe soko ye imwana.
42002034	Simioni kuwamotesa na kumutamila Maliamu ing'ina fina, “Imwana yu kekigwa kwa kugwa na kwinuka wengi wowile Isilaeli, na chitangilo che wanhu womulema.
42002035	Nagwe gomwecho idipanga dyokwingila mumoyo wako uleke gagubuligwe madoga ga mimoyo itewa.”
42002036	Kweja kowa na Mugonesi yumwedu we chike disina dyakwe Ana mwana wa Fanueli wa lukolo lwa Asheli. Hakekala na mugosi minyaka mufunghate kulawa munhole yakwe.
42002037	Kahi hakasigala mwigane mpaka ugele wuwo foyowile mudala wa miyaka makumi munana na mine, nghekuleuka mihekalu ye Mulungu yekutasa kuleka kudia chigele chose.
42002038	Ugele wuwo hoyolawanisa, hoyomutunya Mulungu na kulonga simbuli se mwana ku wanhu wose wagojelage uhonya wa Yelusalemu
42002039	iBabakwe ne ing'ina fowamalile kugolosa gose fina fodyendage dilagiso, hawoya ukwawo Nasaleti mumukoa wa Galilaya.
42002040	Imwana hoyokula, hoyokongeseka ludole, kamema misungu, na Dihewa dya Mulungu hadyuwa umwakwe.
42002041	Chila mwaka iBabakwe ne ing'ina wenda weluta Yelusalemu fina fowasowele ugele we sikukuu ya Pasaka.
42002042	Imwana foyafika miyaka ikumi na mili, howolutanya Yelusalemu fina fowasowele.
42002043	Fowafulusa isikukuu, isikukuu ye Pasaka wejawakonga inhambo ya kuya ukwawo, amba Iyesu hoyosigala Yelusalemu, na iBabakwe ne ing'ina wasamanyile;
42002044	Awene wamanya kaumo mwitewa, howogenda mpaka dijuwa duswa, wakonga kumuhananga kuwambwiya sawo na wayawo.
42002045	Kosoko wasamonile, howokuya Yelusalemu kumuhananga.
42002046	Dijuwa dya kadatu howomufika mwihekalu kekala hagatigati ya wafusaji yakuwategelesa na kuwosa.
42002047	Wose wamuhulike hawesina lugano kwasoko ye misungu na mbidula yakwe swamu.
42002048	iBabakwe ne ing'ina fowamonile hawesina, ing'inakwe kamusa yakugamba, “Gomwana kuchitenda nhani? iBabako na niye chenda chikukongha kwa usungu.”
42002049	Imwene hakabidula yekugamba, “Nhani mukunihananga? Musamanyile fina inyagila kwikala munyumba ye Babangu?”
42002050	iBabakwe ne ing'ina wasamanyile simbuli sowatamiligwe.
42002051	Hoyokuya hamwedu nawo mpaka Nasaleti, hoyogendelela kuwahulika. Ing'ina hoyofundika gose mumoyo wakwe.
42002052	Na iYesu hoyogendelela kukula kwa misungu na chimo, hoyowendesa wanhu ne Mulungu.
42003001	Hawuwa mwaka wa kumi na shano wa undewa wakwe Kaisali Tibelio. Pondio Pilato hakowa Mundewa wa Uyahudi, Helode Mundewa mudodo wa Galilaya na imunduguse Filipo hakowa Mundewa mudodo wa mikoa ya Itulea na Tilakoniti; na Lusania Mundewa mudodo wa Abilene,
42003002	Anasi na Kayafa hawowa Makuhani wakulu. Imbuli ye Mulungu hoimwijila Yohana mwana wa Sakalia uko kunyika.
42003003	Kamei Yohana hoyeluta mumhelo ya ulwanda wa Yolodani. Hoyohubili ubatiso wo kulamba kosoko yo kulekeleligwa uwihi.
42003004	Fina foyandikwe muchitabu cha Mugonesi Isaya: “Dijwi dya munhu dihulikika kunyika, ‘Igoloseni injila ye Mundewa; gololeni injila yakwe!
42003005	Chila ilolo difukiswe, chila itunda na kitongo iduliswe. ahagonjile hagoloke, sinjila sihile sigoloswe na kuwa swamu.
42003006	Na chila munhu kowona uhonya we Mulungu.’”
42003007	Wanhu matewa haweja kubatisigwa na Yohana, kawosa yakugamba, “Anyeye cheleko cha majoka nani yawafundile muitije inyono ye Mulungu?
42003008	Mweleke mamudyo gakonesa fina mulamba, kahi munghakonge kugamba: ‘Chinaye Baba Ibulahimu,’ kosoko nikuwatamila Imulungu yakudaha kumwinulila Ibulahimu wana kulawa mumawe gano.
42003009	Muchigele chino inhemo ikigwa mumasina ga mabiki, idibiki disikweleka mamudyo maswamu, dikung'enyigwa na kusomigwa.”
42003010	Awanhu wamusa wakugamba, “Chigolose nhani seye?”
42003011	Hoyowabidula yakugamba, “Iyena makoti meli na yamwinghe iyechaka; na iyena chakudiya yagolose nhaifo.”
42003012	Awakonghosa we ikodi nawo howokwija kubatisigwa, howomusa, “Mwalimu chigolose nhani seye?”
42003013	Kawagamba, “Munghakongose chinhu kujumha fomusigililigwe.”
42003014	Awasilikali nawo howomusa wekugamba, “Ase nase chigolose nhani? Kawagamba Munghapujile munhu, kahi munghamubalalile munhu, na mwigutiswe na maliho genu.”
42003015	Awanhu fowowile mukugoja agelawanisa, wose wakudoga mufidoga fyawo isimbuli sa Yohana, nhegela imwene no Kilisito.
42003016	Yohana kawabidula yekugamba, “Aniye nikubatisa kwa meji, ninga yekwija munhu iyena ludole kujumha niye, kai aniye sagilwe kohola sisigi sa filwatu fyakwe. Ayo kowabatisa kwa Muhe Musunhile na kwa moto.
42003017	Diselo dyakwe dya mumukono yakwe, naye koshagila uluga lwakwe, na kukunjagisa ngano mukano yakwe, ninga amakohelele kogasoma mumoto usikusima.”
42003018	Kahi kwa mbuli nyingi hoyowahubilia wanhu mbuli swanu.
42003019	Ninga iMundewa Helode yagombelwa na Yohana kosoko yamulonda Helodia imuke we munduguse na kumutenda mukagwe, kahi no uwihi wose woyagolose.
42003020	Kahi Helode yongesa uwihi wakwe kwa kumoha Yohana.
42003021	Ninga awanhu wose wakamale kubatisigwa, na Yesu yakafuluse kubatisigwa yendeyotasa, ulanga wagubuka,
42003022	Kamei Muhe Musunhile yadulika muchanhya yakwe kefana njiwa, dijwi dyalawa kulanga, “Agweye no mwanangu mwendigwa wangu nyendesigwe nagwe.”
42003023	iYesu foyakonga umulimo wa kufusa, yowa fina minyaka makumi madatu nhafia hakamanyika fina mwana wa Yusufu wa Heli,
42003024	mwana Matati, mwana wa Lawi, mwana wa Meliki, mwana wa Janai, mwana wa Yusufu,
42003025	mwana wa Matatiya, mwana wa Amosi, mwana wa Nahumu, mwana wa Esili, mwana wa Nagai,
42003026	mwana wa Maati, mwana wa Matatia, mwana wa Semei, mwana wa Yoseki, mwana wa Joda.
42003027	Joda hakowa mwana wa Yohanani, mwana wa Lesa, mwana wa Selubabeli, mwana wa Shealitieli, mwana wa Neli,
42003028	Neli hakowa mwana wa Meliki, mwana wa Adi, mwana wa Kosamu yowile mwana wa Elimodamu, mwana wa Eli.
42003029	Eli hakowa mwana wa Yoshua, mwana wa Elieseli, mwana wa Yolamu, mwana wa Matati, mwana wa Lawi.
42003030	Lawi hakowa mwana wa Simoni, mwana wa Yuda, mwana wa Yosefu, mwana wa Yonamu, mwana wa Eliakimu,
42003031	Eliakimu hakowa mwana Melea, mwana wa Mena, mwana wa Matasa, mwana wa Nasani, mwana wa Daudi,
42003032	Daudi hakowa mwana wa Yese, mwana wa Obedi, mwana wa Boasi, mwana wa Sala, mwana wa Nashoni,
42003033	Nashoni yowa mwana wa Aminadabu, mwana wa Adimini, mwana wa Alini, mwana wa Hesiloni, mwana wa Pelesi, mwana wa Yuda.
42003034	Yuda yowa mwana wa Yakobo, mwana wa Isaka, mwana wa Ibulahimu, mwana wa Tela, mwana wa Naholi,
42003035	Naholi hakowa mwana wa Selugi, mwana wa Lewu, mwana wa Pelegi, mwana wa Ebeli, mwana wa Shela.
42003036	Shela hakowa mwana wa Kainani, mwana wa Alifokisadi, mwana wa Shemu, mwana wa Nuhu, mwana wa Lameki,
42003037	Lameki yowa mwana wa Mesusela, mwana wa Henoki, mwana wa Yaledi, mwana wa Mahalale, mwana wa Kainani,
42003038	Kainani hakowa mwana wa Enoki, mwana wa Seti, mwana wa Adamu yowile mwana wa Mulungu.
42004001	Foyamema Muhe Musunhile hoyokuya kulawa Yolodani, kalongoswa na Muhe
42004002	chigele cha majuwa makumi mane kunyika, yagesigwa na Luhoma. Na majuwa gose ngadiya chinhu, gakahele hakowa na njala
42004003	Luhoma kalonga naye yakugamba, “Nghona gweye ni Mwana we Mulungu, dilonge idiwe adi dyuwe mukate.”
42004004	Yesu hakamubidula, “Yandikigwa fina, ‘Munhu nghakuhuwila mukate wimwene.’”
42004005	Na iluhoma hoyomukwisa kuchanhya na kumunesa undewa wa muchilunga kwa chipisi chiguhi,
42004006	na kumugamba, “Nokwingha gweye Undewa na Ukulu wakwe ne ditunyo kosoko galafigwa ukwangu, nani nikumwingha wowose ifene fonikwenda.
42004007	Ninga gweye unghanifugamila, ai yose ikuwa yako.”
42004008	Na iYesu kamubidula yakugamba, “Yandikigwa Komufugamila, Mundewa Mulungu wako na imwene du komutogomela!”
42004009	Na iLuhoma hakamulonda mpaka Yelusalemu na hakamwika muchisusu che dihekalu na kumugamba, “Inghowa gweye kwa mwana we Mulungu, lagala hasi kulawa hano.
42004010	Fina yandikigwa, ‘Kokwingha malaika wakwe wakwimilise,
42004011	na mumikono yawo wokudinghula ungheje utowa mugulu wako nghwalo mwiwe.’”
42004012	Na iYesu kamubidula yakugamba, “Ilongigwa unghamugese Mulungu Mundewa wako.”
42004013	Na iLuhoma yakamale chila igesa, hoyomuleka kwa chipisi.
42004014	Na iYesu hakowa Galilaya yamemesigwe ne ludole lwa Muhe Musunhile, simbuli sakwe seja senela muchilunga chose cha munghanda ya Galilaya.
42004015	Hoyofusa mumasinagogi gawo, yatunyigwa na awanhu wose.
42004016	Na iYesu hoyokwija Nasaleti ahanhu hoyakulila, mwijuwa dye Sabato hakaluta kwisinagogi fina foyasowela. Hakema kosoko.
42004017	Na bahaya hakenghigwa chitabu cha Mugonesi Isaya. Hoyogubula ichitabu, hoyopata hanhu handikigwe,
42004018	“Muhe wo Mundewa kamuchanhya yangu, kosoko kanibaka mafuta kuwahubilia awakiwa mbuli swanu. Kanituma kutamila kulekeleligwa kwa amateka, kona kwa waya wasikona, kuwengha kulekeleligwa awaya awakoneligwa,
42004019	na kutamilisa umwaka we Mundewa ufumiligwe.”
42004020	Na hakagubika ichitabu, hoyomuwisila imutumishi na hoyokwikala hasi, na awanhu wose wowile mwisinagogi howomung'olela meso.
42004021	Hoyokonga kulonga nawo, “Diyelo ditulumo dino dimemelesigwa musinghutwi senu.”
42004022	Na wose hawalonga fiswanu kosoko yakwe na kwisina simbuli swanu silawile mumulomo wakwe; nawo hawagamba, “Ayu si mwana wa Yusufu?”
42004023	Kawatamila, “Hechaka manhonge fina molonga nonga ayi, ‘Gomuganga kihonye gomweecho, gose gochihulike kugolosa Kapelinaumu, golosa hano naho haisi yako gomweecho.’”
42004024	Na iYesu hakawagamba, “Chawelu nikumutamilani, hechaka Mugonesi iyekufumiligwa muisi yakwe.
42004025	Ninga, chawelu nikumutamilani, hakuwa na wegane wengi Muislaeli ugele wa Eliya, ugele ulanga fowohigwa miyaka midatu na miyesi mutandatu bila kutonya fula. Muchigele chicho njala nghulu haingila muisi,
42004026	na Eliya nghatumigwa kwa yoyose, amba kwa Seleputa, muisi ya Sidoni, kwe mwanamuke yowa mwigane.
42004027	Na hahowa na awena ukoma matewa Muislaeli ugele we Mugonesi Elisha, na hechaka yoyose yasunhigwa, ila Naamani wa Siliya.”
42004028	Ninga fowahulike gago, hawadeseka wose wowile mwisinagogi.
42004029	Nawo howekwinuka na kumulafa kunje ye ikaya, na kumulongosa ditwi kung'enge ye chitunda chajengigwe ikaya yawo, kosoko wamukubite hasi,
42004030	Ninga imwene kapuluta mugatigati yawo hoyoleuka.
42004031	iYesu hoyohulumuka Kapelinaumu, kaya yuwile Galilaya. Na yenda yewafusa mwijuwa dye Sabato.
42004032	Nawo hawesina kosoko ye mafusa gakwe, simbuli sakwe hasuwa na udaha.
42004033	Na mwisinagogi mowa na munhu yena magini, hoyolila kwa ijwi ikulu,
42004034	“Koo! China choni na gweye Yesu Munasaleti? Kwija kuchimalagisa? Nikumanya kwa nani gweye, Musunhile we Mulungu.”
42004035	Yesu kaigombela imhepo yekugamba, “Nyamala na umulawe. Na yakakinyigwe hasi ne imhepo mugatigati ya wanhu, imhepo hoilawa, ninga isimugolose dihile.”
42004036	Na wose hawesina wakilongelesa wakugamba, “Aino mbuli yaki? Kosoko kwa udaha na ludole yakugombela simhepo sihile naso sikulawa.”
42004037	Simbuli sakwe seja senela chila hanhu munghandanghanda ye iisi iya.
42004038	Hakenuka na kuleuka mwisinagogi, hoyokwingila munyumba ya Simoni. Ninga imukwewe Simoni hakowa mutamu, yakoligwa na ipwipwi ikali, na howomutasa kosoko yakwe.
42004039	Hoyokwima hanghanda yakwe, hoyedigombela dipwipwi, na hodimuleka, na chimwande hoyokwinuka na kuwatogomela.
42004040	Ninga dijuwa dikoswe, awanhu wose wowile na watamu, howomwigalila awanhu wose awakutamwa sinhamu mbalimbali; naye hoyokwika mikono yakwe muchanhya ya chila mutamu hoyowahonya.
42004041	Na simhepo naso hasiwalawa matewa, hositowa chowe, “Agweye kwa mwana we Mulungu!” Ninga hoyosigombela na nghasifumise kulonga, kosoko hasimumanya fina no Kilisito.
42004042	Housiku yakwe dijuwa dikalawe, hoyoleuka na kuluta ahanhu hachinyele. Awanhu howomuhananga na kwija ukwakwe, howokwenda kumulemesa kuleuka ukwawo.
42004043	Ninga hayowagamba, “Inyagila kuhubili imbuli swanu ya undewa we Mulungu musikaya singi kahi, kosoko iyo hanitumigwa.”
42004044	Na yenda yefusa mumasinagogi ga Yudea.
42005001	Ugele awanhu wakelunde na kumumemelela kutegelesa imbuli ye Mulungu, hakowa yemile munghanda ya dilamba dya Genesaleti.
42005002	Na hakona minhumbwi mili habehi na dilamba, ninga awalowa somba hawalawa muminhumbwi na wenda wesunha sinyafu sawo.
42005003	Hakakwila mumunhumbwi umwedu no wakwe Simoni, hakamutasa yawile mumeji kidogo kulawa kunghingi. Na hakekala na kuwafusa wanhu kulawa mumunhumbwi.
42005004	Yakafuluse kulonga, hoyomugamba Simoni, “Guma kuchiligati, na ulafe sinyafu sako ulowe somba.”
42005005	Simoni hoyobidula, “Mundewa chigolosa kasi yo kusokesa chilo chose chinghapate chinhu. Ninga kwa imbuli yako nohulumusa sinyafu.”
42005006	Ninga wakahulumuse sinyafu, hawapata somba nyingi lugano, sinyafu sawo hosikonga kudumuka.
42005007	Hawawenanga awayawo wowile mumunhumbwi wa keli weje kuwatasa. Haweja na kumemesa minhumbwi yose mili, ninga haikonga kusama.
42005008	Ninga Simoni Petulo yakone nhaifo, hakogwa mumigulu ya Yesu yakugamba, “Leuka ukwangu go Mundewa, kosoko aniye na munhu wa wihi.”
42005009	Kosoko hakesina imwene hamwedu na waya wowile naye kosoko ya uwingi we sisomba sowapatile;
42005010	na baho kahi weja wowa Yakobo na Yohana, wana wa Sebedayo, wowile wayagwe wa Simoni Petulo. Na iYesu hoyomutamila Simoni, “Unghogohe kulawa hambiya kokuwa mulowa wanhu.”
42005011	Nawo fowafuluse kwigala minhumbwi yawo kunghingi, howoleka fyose na kumwandamila.
42005012	Ugele foyowile mukaya imonga, baho keja munhu iyena ukoma, na foyamonile Yesu yogwa funama kededela yakugamba, “Mundewa nghona ukuhananga ukudaha kunihonya.”
42005013	Naye yagolola umukono wakwe hoyomukwafa yakugamba, “Nikuhanga, hona baho ni baho ukoma houhona.”
42005014	Na hakamulemesa yanghamutamila munhu, ninga, “Luta gomweecho ukeyonese kwa mutambiki, na ukalafe digelo fina foyalongile Musa uwe uhomelesi ukwawo.”
42005015	Ninga simbuli so seja senela lugano kola hanhu na matewa mengi hawetang'anyila kutegelesa na kuhonyigwa sinhamu sawo.
42005016	Imwene hoyoleuka hoyoluta kunyika kutasa.
42005017	Mwijuwa dimonga dya majuwa gago, foyendeyefusa, heja howa na Mafalisayo na walimu we malagiso wekale naye, awo nowejile kulawa chila kaya ya Galilaya, na Yudea na kulawa Yelusalemu, na uludole lwe iMundewa hauwa naye kuhonya.
42005018	Langa, wanhu hawegala munhu yaholole mwisasi, wahananga wamwingise kugati na kumwika kumwande ya Yesu.
42005019	Ninga fowonile hechaka njila ya kumwingisa kosoko ya matewa, howokwila munyumba muchanhya howotobola na kumwingisa na disasi dyakwe kupulutila mukano mpaka kugati kumwande ya Yesu.
42005020	Yakone dihuwi dyawo hakagamba, “Mwanangu uwihi wako ulekeleligwa.”
42005021	Na Watulumi na Mafalisayo howakonga kiyusa, wakugamba, “Ayuno nani yakulonga lubeso? Nani yakudaha kulekelela uwihi ninga Mulungu yemwene!”
42005022	Ninga Yesu hakatanga amahweso gawo hakawagamba, “Nhani mukihwesa mumimoyo yenu?”
42005023	Imhufu no ihoki? Kugamba, “Kulekeleligwa uwihi wako ama kugamba leuka ulute?”
42005024	Ninga uleke mumanye fina mwana we munhu kena udaha muchilunga wa kulekelela uwihi. Hakalonga ne munhu yaholole, Nikukugamba, “Inuka winule disasi dyako ulute ukaya.”
42005025	Baho ni baho kenuka kumwande yawo, na hakalonda achiya choyagonele, na kuluta ukaya akuno yakumutunya Mulungu.
42005026	Na itisi ikulu hadiwengila wose, na hawamutunya Mulungu na hawamema lutwitwi wakugamba, “Diyelo chona mbuli ya ijumo.”
42005027	Hoyoleuka na kumona mukonghosa kodi yakwinangigwa Lawi, kekala ahanhu ho kulihila kodi, hoyomugamba, “Nyandamile.”
42005028	Na hoyoleka fyose, na kumwandamila.
42005029	Na Lawi hoyomugolosela chakudiya chikulu ukaya ukwakwe, na heja howa na mulundo mukulu wa wakonghosa kodi na wamonga wekale mumesa na wene.
42005030	Amafalisayo na Watulumi wawo hawawakalalilaga awefusa wakwe wakugamba, “Nhani mukudiya na kunywa hamwedu na wakonghosa kodi na wena uwihi?”
42005031	Yesu hoyowagamba, “Awomi wasikumuhananga Muganga, ninga awaya iwatamu.”
42005032	Sijile kuwenanga awaswanu ninga awena uwihi wadahe kulamba.
42005033	Na hawamugamba, “Awefusa wa Yohana wakufunga mikangha mingi na wakutasa, nheifo awefusa wa Mafalisayo, ninga awako wakudiya na kunywa.”
42005034	Na iYesu hakawagamba, “Mukudaha kuwagolosa awageni we halusi wohe ugele imwenye halusi kahamwedu nawo?
42005035	Amajuwa gokwija, hona imwenye halusi yekuleusigwa ukwawo, noho wakwenda wafunge mumajuwa gago.”
42005036	Kawatamila mbasi yakugamba, “Hechaka munhu iyekudega ndame ya suke nyisha na kuguma musuke ing'ono, yanghagolosa nhaifo, yakudega inyisha, na indame kulawa inyisha fisikiyagila na ing'ono.
42005037	Kahi hechaka munhu yakuguma difai nyisha mufiliba filalile, yanghagamba yagume idifai nyisha, yotula ifiliba na difai yokitika na ifiliba fyobanika.
42005038	Ninga idifai nyisha ikuhanangigwa igumigwe mufiliba fisha.
42005039	Kosoko hechaka munhu yakunywa difai yakatali hoyosulumila difai nyisha, kosoko yakugamba, ‘Chakatali kiswanu.’”
42006001	Mwijuwa dye Sabato Yesu foyendayogenda mumigunda ye ngano, awefusa wakwe wadudula masamhu, wafigisa mumikono yawo wa kudiya.
42006002	Ninga awamonga wa Mafalisayo wagamba, “Nhani mukugolosa chinhu chene chilemesigwe mwijuwa dye Sabato?”
42006003	Yesu hoyobidula, “Musisomile adiya dyo yagolose Daudi foyowile na njala, imwene hamwedu na waya awowile naye.
42006004	Foyengile munyuma ye Mulungu hoyolonda imikate ya konesa na kudiya, yene si fiswamu kudiigwa na wowose ninga Makuhani, kahi hoyowengha awaya woyowile nawo.”
42006005	Hoyowagamba, “Imwana we munhu no Mundewa we Sabato.”
42006006	Mwijuwa dingi dye Sabato, foyendae kwingila Mwisinagogi na kufusa, heja howa na munhu yaholole umukono wakwe wo kulume.
42006007	Na Watulumi na Mafalisayo weja wamunyembela, kona fina komuhonya mwijuwa dye Sabato, kosoko wapate mbuli ya kumusongesa.
42006008	Ninga hoyotanga madoga gawo, hakamugamba ayuya iyena umukono uholole, “Wije wime hano.” Hakenuka na kwima haya.
42006009	Na Yesu hakawagamba, “Nikuwosani togoleni! Ikuhanangigwa dijuwa dye Sabato kugolosa maswamu ama gehile? Kuhonya ugima ama kuubana?”
42006010	Hakawakongholela meso wose, na kumugamba ayuya imunhu, “Golola umukono wako. Hakagolosa nheifiya na umukono wakwe hauhona.”
42006011	Ninga weja wamemwa na nyono na kiyusa wene kwa wene wamugolose nhani Yesu.
42006012	Mumajuwa gago hakakwila kufitunda kutasa; hakatasa kwe Mulungu chilo chose.
42006013	Hosiku yakwe hakawenanga wefusa wakwe, na kuwasagula ikumi na weli kulawa mwiwefusa wawo, hakawenanga watumigwa;
42006014	Simoni, yamwinanga disina dya keli Petulo, na Andelea imunduguse, na Yakobo na Yohana, na Filipo na Batolomayo,
42006015	na Matayo, na Tomasi na Yakobo imwana wa Alufayo, na Simoni yenangigwe Selote,
42006016	Na Yuda mwana wa Yakobo, na Yuda Isikalioti yabiduke kuwa musongesi.
42006017	Hoyohulumuka nawo na kwima hanhu hatindimale, hamwedu na itewa dya wefusa wakwe na matewa ga wanhu walawile Yudea yose na Yelusalemu na mhwani ya Tilo na Sidoni, awejile kumutegelesa na kuhonyigwa sinhamu sawo,
42006018	na wose wedasigwagwe na simhepo sihile weja wahonyigwa.
42006019	Na amatewa wose hawahananga kumukwafa, kosoko uludole wenda umulawa kuwahonya wose.
42006020	Yesu hakenula meso gakwe hoyowalanga awefusa wakwe na kugamba, “Ibeka nyeye muwakiwa; kosoko undewa wa Mulungu ni wenu!
42006021	Ibeka nyeye mufungile hambiya; kosoko mokigutisigwa! Ibeka nyeye gomukulila hambiya; kosoko moseka!
42006022	Ibeka nyeye awanhu wanghawasula, kahi wanghawabagula, na kuwaliga na kuwabanila disina dyenu fina mbuli ihile kosoko ye Mwana we Munhu!
42006023	Sekeleleni dijuwa diya na kujumhajumha kosoko digelo dyenu ikulu kulanga, kosoko awaBaba sawo weja wawagolosa nhaifo awagonesi.
42006024	Ninga usungu wenu anyeye muwagoli; kosoko mufulusa kupata imhoso yenu!
42006025	Usungu wenu gomwigute hambiya; kosoko mokona njala! Usungu wenu anyeye gomukuseka hambiya; kosoko molombola na kulila!
42006026	Usungu wenu awanhu wose wanghawatogola; kosoko awaBaba sawo hawawagolosela nhaifo awagonesi wa udasi.”
42006027	“Ninga nikumutamilani anyeye mukunitegelesa, wendeni wanghondo wenu, muwagolosele maswamu awaya wakumusulani,
42006028	muwamotese awaya wakuwaligita, mutase kosoko ya waya wakuwabesa.
42006029	Kwa yuya yakukutowa munjeje mubidulile na ya keli, na yuya iyakulonda dikoti dyako unghamulemese inghasu nhaifiya.
42006030	Mwinghe chila munhu iyakukutasa, na iyakupokola finhu fyako unghahanange yakuwisile.
42006031	Na fina fomukuhananga wanhu wawagolosele anyeye, muwagolosele nhaifo.
42006032	“Nghona mukuwenda awaya awakuwenda nyeye, mukonesa uswamu waki? Kosoko hata awena uwihi wakugolosa nhaifo.
42006033	Na nghona mukuwagolosela uswamu awaya wakuwagolosela maswamu, mukupata igelo dyaki? Kosoko hata awena uwihi wakugolosa nhaifo.
42006034	Na nghona mukuwakopesha awaya wene womumanyile fina mohokela, mukugolosa uswamu waki? Hata awena uwihi wakuwakopesha awena uwihi kuhokela kahi.
42006035	Ninga wendeni awanghondo wenu, goloseleni fiswamu, kopesheni bila kugojela chochose kulawa ukwawo, na digelo dyenu dyokuwa ikulu na mokuwa wana wa ye kuchanhyasi, kosoko imwene muswanu kwa awasikumulumba na awakiyenda wenyecho.
42006036	Muwe na ubasi, ninga fina iBaba yenu foyena ubasi.”
42006037	Munghalamule; nanye musilamuligwa, munghatofule; nanye musitofuligwa, mulekelele; nanye molekeleligwa.
42006038	Wengheni; nanye mokwinghigwa chipimo chiswamu cha kumema na kukandisa na kusingisigwa hata kwitika chokwikigwa muchifa chenu. Kosoko ichipimo chomukulafa no chicho chomukupimiligwa.
42006039	Kahi hoyowatamila mbasi, “Togoleni! Imudula kodaha kumulongosa Mudula? Wasihubugila wose mwikolongo?
42006040	Imwifusa nghakumusuma imwalimu wakwe, ninga kila munhu yanghafusigwa fiswanu yakuwa fina imwalimu wakwe.
42006041	Nhani ukuchona ichibasi chuwile mwigiso dye munduguso, ninga nghukutanga dibiki dyuwile mwigiso dyako gomwecho?
42006042	Ama kodahaje kumugamba imunduguso, sekulu, leka nileuse ichibasi chuwile mwigiso dyako, nagwe gomwenecho nghukudyona dibiki duwile mwigiso dyako? Agwe wechimwefe! Konga kuleusa dibiki mwigiso dyako, baho kokona fiswamu kuleusa ichibasi chuwile mwigiso dye imunduguso.”
42006043	“Kosoko hechaka ibiki iswamu dikweleka mamudyo gehile, kahi kwichaka ibiki dihile dikweleka mamudyo maswamu.
42006044	Kosoko chila ibiki dikumanyika kwa mamudyo gakwe, kosoko amasada sigakubawigwa mumiwa, kahi sisabibu sisikubawigwa kulawa mumisega.
42006045	Imunhu muswamu kulawa musigafu ya umoyo wakwe yakulafa maswamu, na imunhu yehile kulawa musigafu ya uwihi wakwe yakulafa gehile; kosoko kulawa gaya agemile mumoyo wakwe umulomo wakwe ukulonga.”
42006046	“Nhani mukuninanga, ‘Mundewa,’ Mundewa, na musikugolosa agaya gonikumutamilani?
42006047	Chila munhu yekwija ukwangu na kuhulika simbuli sangu na kusigolosa nomutamilani foyakuliganiswa:
42006048	Yakuliganiswa na munhu yakujenga nyumba, iyakukata mpaka kusi, na kwika inghindiso mwiwe. Amafaluko gangheja, ameji gakutowa munyumba na gasikudaha kuisingisa kosoko ijengigwa fiswanu.
42006049	Ninga ayuya yakuhulika na kuleka kusigolosa kakifana munhu yakujenga nyumba mwisanga bila nghindiso, ameji gakuitowa na kuibena, na baho ni baho ikugwa, na inyugwa yakwe ikuwa nghulu.”
42007001	Foyafuluse kuwatamila gaya goyendage wanhu wahulike, hakengila Kapelinaumu.
42007002	Ninga Chilongosi wa wasilikali igana hakowa na mutumwa yowile mwendigwa wakwe, hakowa mutamu habehi na kufa.
42007003	Foyahulike simbuli sa Yesu, hakawatamila wasehe we Chiyahudi kumutasa yeje na kumuhonya imutogomi.
42007004	Nawo fowejile kwa Yesu howokidedela wakugamba, “Yendesigwa umugolosele dino.
42007005	Kosoko yakuwenda wanhu wetu na kachijengela disinagogi dyetu.”
42007006	Na Yesu hakaluta nawo. Foyowile habehi ne inyumba, “Ichilongosi wa wasilikali igana hakatuma wambwiya ukwakwe wakugamba Mundewa unghakiidase, kosoko aniye sagiligwe agweye wingile hasi he ikano yangu,
42007007	kosoko iyo hanikiyona sagiligwe nimwenecho kwija ukwako. Ninga longa mbuli du na imutumwa wangu yakuhananga yahone.
42007008	Kosoko ani nani na munhu mukulu nina wasilikali hasi yangu, na nighamulonga yumwedu, ‘Luta na yakuluta,’ na kwa yumonga, ‘Nyagula na yakwija,’ na kwa mutumwa wangu, ‘Golosa dino na yakugolosa.’”
42007009	Foyahulike nhaifo, Yesu hoyekisina lugano kosoko yakwe, hoyobiduka na kuwatamila matewa wamwandamilage, “Nikumutamilani hata Muisilaeli singhati nyone ihuwi fina dino.”
42007010	Na waya watumigwe fowowile ukaya, hawamufika imutumwa yuya mumi togi.
42007011	Chigele chiguhi hakaluta mukaya imonga ikwinangigwa Naini, hamwedu na wefusa wakwe na itewa ikulu hadikilongosa naye.
42007012	Foyeja yasegelela mumulango umukulu we ikaya iya, langa munhu yafile yenda yelafigwa kunje, ni mwana ye imwene we ing'inakwe yowile mwigane, na itewa ikulu kulawa kukaya iya hawowa naye.
42007013	Na iMundewa yakamone, hoyomonela ubasi hakamugamba, “Unghalile.”
42007014	Hoyokwija na kudikwafa dijenesa na waya wadipikile howokwima, hoyogamba, “Gomujelelo nikulonga na gweye, inuka.”
42007015	Na yuya yofile hoyekwinuka na kukonga kulonga, Yesu hoyomwingha ing'ina we imujelelo.
42007016	Itisi hadiwengila wose, na hawamutunya Mulungu wakugamba, “Mugonesi mukulu kalawanisa mugati yetu na Mulungu kawejila wanhu wakwe.”
42007017	Imbuli ayo hoyikwenela muisi yose ya Uyahudi na muisi sose sa munghanda yakwe.
42007018	Awefusa wa Yohana hawamutamila gose gano.
42007019	Yohana hakawenanga wefusa wakwe weli, hakawatuma kwa Mundewa wamuse, “Agweye no yuya iyekwija hegu chimugoje yungi?”
42007020	Kamei awanhu waya fowejile ukwakwe hawagamba, “Yohana Mubatisaji kachituma ukwako yakugamba, ‘Agweye noyuya yakwija hegu chimugoje yungi?’”
42007021	Muugele uya hoyowahonya wanhu matewa na sinhamu sawo, na sinhato sawo, na magini gehile, na wengi wowile wasikona hakawowisila kona kwawo.
42007022	Yesu hakagamba, “Luteni mukamutamile Yohana agene gomukona na kuhulika: Mudula wakona, fiwete wakugenda, wakoma wakusunhigwa, na fihuli wakuhulika, wafile wakwinuligwa, awakiwa wahubiligwa mbuli swamu.
42007023	Ibeka imunhu iyechaka manhonge kosoko yangu.”
42007024	Awatumigwe na Yohana wakaleuke, hakakonga kulonga na amatewa muchanhya ya Yohana. “Hamulawa kuluta kunyika kulanga choni?” Chibwade chikusingiswa ne imheho?
42007025	Ninga hamuluta kulanga choni? Munhu yafasigwe suke swamu? Langa, awaya wakufala sisuke se ditunyo na kwikala kwa kubwedelela wowa musinyumba sa undewa.
42007026	Ninga hamuluta kwija langa choni? Mugonesi? Heye! Nikumutamilani mukulu kusuma mugonesi.
42007027	Ayo yoyaandikiligwa gano, langa nikumwigala mutumigwa wangu kumwande yako yakugolosele injila.
42007028	Nikumutamilani mu wanhu wose welekigwe na wanawake hechaka mukulu kusuma Yohana, hata nheifo ayuya imudodogi mu undewa wa Mulungu ni mukulu kujumha Yohana.
42007029	(Fowahulike gago awanhu wose na wakonghosa kodi hawamufumila Mulungu, na kutunya kubatisigwa ubatiso wa Yohana;
42007030	Ninga Mafalisayo na walamusi we malagiso weja walema inyenda ye Mulungu ukwawo, kosoko wasabatisigwe na Yohana.)
42007031	“Nowaliganisa na choni awanhu wa cheleko chino? Nawo wakifana choni?
42007032	Wakifana wana awekale kwigulilo na kiinanga, ‘Hachiwatowela filimbi, nanye musafinile! Chiwembila nyimbo sa usungu, nanye musililile!’
42007033	Kosoko Yohana Mubatisaji keja nghakudiya mukate na kunywa difai, hamugamba, ‘Kena magini!’
42007034	Mwana we munhu keja yakudiya na kunywa, na mukugamba Langeni muhongho yuno na mulefi! Mbwiya yawo wakonghosa kodi na wena uwihi!
42007035	Ninga imisungu ikufumiligwa na wanagwe wose.”
42007036	Mufalisayo yumonga hoyomugoneka kudiya hamwedu naye, hoyoluta kunyumba ye Mufalisayo, na kwikala hamesa.
42007037	Kahi imwanamuke we ikaya iya iyeja yowa na uwihi, foyahulike fina hakekala mumesa munyumba ye Mufalisayo, hoyokwigala chichupa cha mafuta ge imhungile.
42007038	Kamei foyemile hanyuma yakwe hamigulu ya Yesu, hakalila, hakakonga kumutwinhesela imigulu yakwe na masosi, na kuihamusa na sinjwili sa muditwi dyakwe, na kuinonela migulu yakwe na kuibaka agaya mafuta ge mhungile swanu.
42007039	Hambiya Imufalisayo yuya yamugoneke yakone nhaifo, yalonga mumoyo wakwe, “Imunhu ayu mhali ni Mugonesi hakowa yakutanga fina imwanamuke yuno no nani kahi kanhani! Ayuya yakumukwafa, fina ni munhu wa uwihi.”
42007040	Kamei iYesu kamubidula kamugamba, “Simoni, nina chinhu cha kulonga na gweye.” Naye hoyomubidula, “Chinhu chaki Mwalimu?”
42007041	Yesu hakawagamba, “Mukopeshaji wa mapesa yumwedu yeja yowa na wanghokwa wakwe weli, yumwedu yakopa magana mashano, na wakeli makumi mashano.
42007042	Fowadugile kuliha hoyowalekelela wose. Hambiya yehoki yemwendesa yuya imukopeshaji?”
42007043	Simoni kamugamba, “Nikudoga fina ayuya yalekeleligwe inghokwa inghulu.” Hoyomugamba, “Kulamula fiswamnu.”
42007044	Baho hakamubidukila imwanamuke, yakumugamba, “Simoni ukumona imwanamuke yono? Ningila munyumba yako, nghuninghile meji ga kunawa migulu yangu, ninga yuno kanidonhesa migulu yangu na masosi na kuihamusa na sinjwili sakwe.
42007045	Nghuninonele, ninga ayuno kulawa fonengile nghalekile kuninonela migulu yangu.
42007046	Nghunibakile mafuta ditwi dyangu, ninga imwene kanibaka migulu yangu na mafuta ge mhungile swanu.
42007047	Kosoko iyo nikumutamilani, kalekeleligwa uwihi wakwe wowile mwingi, kosoko hakenda lugano, ninga iyakulekeleligwa chidodogi yakwenda chidodogi.”
42007048	Hoyomugamba, “Uwihi wako ulekeleligwa.”
42007049	Kahi awaya wowile naye hamesa hawakonga kihwesa, “Ayuno no nani yakulekelela hata uwihi?”
42007050	Na hakamugamba imwanamuke, “Dihuwi dyako dikuhonya. Genda mheho.”
42008001	Kulawa baho hoyoleuka kugendela mumakaya ne fijiji, yekuhubili na kwigala mbuli swanu ya undewa we Mulungu. Na waya ikumi na weli hawowa hamwedu naye.
42008002	Kahi wanawake wamonga awahonyigwe kwa kulafigwa simhepo na sinhamu. Maliamu yanangigwe Magidalena, yalafigwe simhepo mufungate,
42008003	na Yoane imuke wa Chusa mutumwa wa Helode, na Susana, na wamonga wengi wawatogomele kwa isawo yawo.
42008004	Amatewa wakeje hamwedu na wanhu kulawa kaya kwa kaya, hakalonga kwa mbasi.
42008005	“I muhandi hakaleuka kuhanda imbeyu, kamei foyahandage, simonga hasilagala munjila, na wagendanjila hawasijata, na fidege hofisidiya.
42008006	Na simonga hosilagala mwikangalawe, na fosakulile, hasinyala kosoko hasiswela ujolo.
42008007	Na simonga hasilagala mumiwa, na imiwa haikulanaso na kusikanhamisa.
42008008	Na kamei simonga hasilagala muulongo muswamu na kukula na kweleka kocho! Iyena singhutwi sa kuhulika na yahulike.”
42008009	Kamei wefusa wakwe wakamuse difuso dye imbasi,
42008010	hakawagamba, “Anyeye mwinghigwa udaha wa kumanya ififiso fye undewa we Mulungu, ninga kwa wamonga ukutamiligwa kwa mbasi, kosoko wanghalanga wanghone na wanghahulika wanghamanye.”
42008011	“Difuso dye imbasi nodi: Imbeyu no imbuli ye Mulungu.
42008012	Awaya we habehi ne injila no waya waihulike imbuli, ninga Iluhoma yakwija na kuilonda imbuli kulawa mumimoyo yawo, kosoko wangheje wehuwila na kuhona.
42008013	Awaya wowile mwikangalawe no waya wene fowakuhulika imbuli, wakuihokela kwa chinyemi, ninga wano wechaka misisi, wakuhuwila kwa chigele chiguhi na ugele wa magesa wakugwa.
42008014	Asiya salagale mumiwa, no waya wakuihulika imbuli, ninga fowakugendelela wakukanhamisigwa na ugoli we chilunga, na mamudyo gawo gasikukangala.
42008015	Na kwa siya silagale muulongo muswamu, awo no waya waihulike imbuli, na kuikola mumimoyo yawo miswamu na kweleka mamudyo kwa ufinyilisi wawo.”
42008016	“Hechaka munhu yekwasa taa na kuigubika ama kuigubika na idebe, ninga yakuika muchigwaso, kosoko awekwingila wadahe kona ujelu wakwe.
42008017	Hechaka mbuli ifisigwe uleke ikakiyonese, kahi chinhu che chifiso chisimanyika na koneka hajelu.
42008018	Mulangisise gomukuhulika, kosoko iyenacho kokwinghigwa, na iyechaka hata chiya choyekudoga kenacho kohokigwa.”
42008019	Kahi ing'inakwe Yesu ne wanduguse howomwijila, ninga wasafikile ukwakwe kosoko ye ditewa.
42008020	Hakatamiligwa, “Ing'inako ne wanduguso wema kunje, wakuhananga kukona.”
42008021	Hoyowabidula, “Ing'inangu na wandugu sangu no waya awakuhulika mbuli ye Mulungu na kuigolosa.”
42008022	Ijuwa dimonga Yesu na wefusa wakwe hawakwila mumunhumbwi, hakawagamba, “Lekeni chiloke umwambu ye dilamba.” Howoleuka.
42008023	Na ifene fowalutage Yesu hakakoligwa na nhongo na kugona. Na imheho yo luputa hoitowa mwilamba, ameji hagakonga kumema mumunhumbwi, na hawowa habehi kudidimila.
42008024	Hawaluta na kumwinusa wakugamba, “Mundewa, Mundewa! Chikufa!” Kamei hakenuka na kuigombela imheho na mawingo gajojage, hofinyamala na kuposika posi.
42008025	Hoyowagamba, “Dihuwi dyenu dyuwahi?” Hawogoha, na kisina wekulonga chila munhu na miyagwe, ninga yuno munhu waki? Iyakugombela hata imheho na meji, nafyo fikumuhulika!
42008026	Kahi howofika muisi ya Wagelasi yuwile umwambu wa Galilaya.
42008027	Foyajatile hasi kulawa mumumhumbwi, hakatang'anyila na munhu kulawa kwikaya yowile na mhepo, kwa chigele chitali nghafalile suke, nghekalage munyumba ninga mufilalo.
42008028	Foyamonile Yesu, hakatula chowe na kugwa kumwande yakwe, na kutowa lwangi, “Choni choukuhananga unigolose, Yesu Mwana we Mulungu iyekuchanhyasi? Nikukutasa unghanisambase.”
42008029	Kosoko Yesu yasidindilisa si mhepo kumulawa imunhu yuya. Ugele mwingi hasimukola, hakemilisigwa, na kohigwa kwa minyolo na simhingu, ninga hakedumula minyolo ne simhingu na kulongoswa na magini.
42008030	“Ninga Yesu hayamusa Disina dyako nani?” Hoyogamba, “Itewa,” kosoko mhepo itewa hasimwingila.
42008031	Kahi hasikinenela yanghasilafe na kuluta kwikolongo.
42008032	Baho heja howa na itewa dya nguluwe dikudima muluduli, simhepo hasikinenela yasileke singile musinguluwe. Hoyofumila.
42008033	Simhepo hosilawa kwe imunhu na kwingila kusinguluwe, kamei ditewa hodikulumhuka kuluduli lwe inghingi ye dilamba na kunywa munghabu.
42008034	Awadimi wakone dyalawanise, hawatija, na kutamilisa mwikaya na mufijiji.
42008035	Awanhu watamiligwe hawaleuka kulanga dyalawanise, na kwija kwa Yesu, howomufika ayuya yalafigwe simhepo yekale mumigulu ya Yesu, kafala suke na mahala gakwe maswamu, na howokogoha.
42008036	Awaya wonile hawawatamila foyowile ayuya yakoligwe ne simhepo na fene foyahonyigwe.
42008037	Na wanhu wose wa si isi sa munghanda ya Genesaleti hawamutasa yaleuke ukwawo kosoko hawengiligwa na itisi ikulu, baho hakengile mumunhumbwi na kuya.
42008038	Imunhu yalafigwe simhepo hakakinenela fina yamwandamile Yesu, ninga Yesu nghamufumise ila kamugamba,
42008039	“Yuya ukaya ukwako, ukatamilise fina Imulungu foyakugolosele.” Hoyoluta na kwanjasa mwikaya dyose fina foyagoloseligwe na Yesu.
42008040	Ninga iYesu yakoye, awanhu wose hawamuhokela kosoko wose wenda womugojela.
42008041	Baho hakeja munhu disina dyakwe Yailo, yowile mukulu we disinagogi, hoyofugama hamigulu ya Yesu, hoyomutasa kwija ukaya ukwakwe,
42008042	kosoko hakowa na mwanagwe yemwene we chike, yena minyaka ikumi na mili nhafi, naye hakowa mutamusi. Foyaluta awanhu hawelunda kumusunguluta.
42008043	Na imwanamuke yowile na utamu wo kulawa sakame kwa minyaka ikumi na mili na hechaka munhu yadahile kumuhonya.
42008044	Hoyokwija kulawa kunyuma ya Yesu na kukwafa dihepu dye isuke yakwe, na baho ni baho inhamu yakwe hoihona.
42008045	Yesu hoyogamba, “Nani yanikwafile?” Wose fowakanile Petulo hakagamba, “Mundewa, amatewa wakusunguluta na kukuumbilila.”
42008046	Ninga Yesu hoyogamba, “Yumonga kanikwafa, kosoko nyona fina ludole lunilawa.”
42008047	Na imwanamuke yakone fina nghodaha kifisa hakeja yakutetema na kugwa kumwande yakwe na kumutamila mumeso ga wanhu wose ichilekile yomukwafa na ifyene fyoyahonile baho ni baho.
42008048	Yesu hoyomugamba, “Mudala dihuwi dyako dikuhonya, genda mhepo.”
42008049	Foyalongage gago, munhu kulawa kwe mukulu we disinagogi keja na kugamba, “Imundele wako kafulusa kufa, unghamwidase Mwalimu.”
42008050	Ninga Yesu foyahulike gago hakamubidula, “Unghogohe, huwila du, naye kokuwa muswamu.”
42008051	Foyafika ukaya nghamufumile munhu wowose kwingila naye kugati, ninga Petulo na Yohana na Yakobo na iBabakwe ne ing'ina we imwana.
42008052	Na wose wendewolila na kuhongesa, ninga hoyogamba, “Munghalile; kosoko nghafile ila kagona.”
42008053	Howomuseka, kosoko hawamanya fina kofa.
42008054	Ninga hakamukola na umukono wakwe, na kumwinanga yakugamba, “Gomwana inuka.”
42008055	Umuhe wakwe howumuwila, na kwimanyima chimwande, Yesu hakalagisa yenghigwe chakudiya.
42008056	iBabakwe ne ing'ina hawakisina lugano; ninga hakawalemesa wanghamutamile munhu wowose agalawanise.
42009001	Yesu hakawenanga awefusa ikumi na weli na kuwengha ludole na udaha muchanhya ya simhepo na kuhonya sinhamu.
42009002	Hakawatuma awefusa kuhubili undewa we Mulungu na kuhonya.
42009003	Hakawagamba, “Munghalonde chochose kosoko ya inhambo yenu, si mhando kahimukoba kahimukate kahidipesa,” na munghowe na makasu meli.
42009004	Munyumba yoyose yomukwingila, mwikale baho, na kulawa baho mugendelele ne inhambo.
42009005	Na ikaya yoyose yene ina wanhu wasikuwahokela, fomukuleuka mukaya iyo kunghunheni amanghundi gowile mumigulu yenu chuwe chitangilo ukwawo.
42009006	Howoleuka na kugendela mufijiji, wakutamilisa mbuli swamu na kuhonya chila hanhu howagendile.
42009007	Kahi iMundewa Helode hakahulika gose gagoloseke, hakedasika kosoko hailongigwa na wamonga fina, “Yohana kenuligwa kulawa mudifa.”
42009008	na wamonga, “Eliya hakeyonesa, na wamonga yumwedu wa Wagonesi wakatali kenuka.”
42009009	Helode hoyagamba, “I Yohana hanimudumula ditwi, ninga ayuno nani yene ifinhu fya itisi?” Hoyohananga kumona.
42009010	Munyuya yawo awatumigwa hawamutamila gowagolose. Yesu hoyowalonda awefusa ikumi na weli na kuluta kukaya yenangigwe Betisaida.
42009011	Amatewa wakahulike howomwandamila, hoyowahokela na kulonga nawo simbuli sa undewa we Mulungu, na kuwahonya awaya wendage kuhonyigwa.
42009012	Ninga dijuwa hadikonga kuswa, na waya ikumi na weli howokwija na kulonga naye, “Uwelage amatewa walute kufijiji na sikaya sa munghanda, wakagone na kupata chakudiya kosoko ayi nyika isikwikaligwa na wanhu.”
42009013	Hawagamba, “Wengheni nyeye chakudiya.” Howogamba, “Chichaka chinhu kujumha ino mikate mishano na somba mbili, nghona chisilutile na kugula chakudiya kosoko ye ditewa dino!”
42009014	Kosoko hahowa na wanhu fina figulu fishano nhafi. Hoyowatamila awefusa wakwe, “Wagambeni wanhu wekale hasi mufilundolundo fya wanhu makumi mashano nhafi.”
42009015	Awefusa hawagolosa nhaifo, awanhu wose hawekwikala hasi.
42009016	Hakailonda aiya imikate mishano na siya sisomba simbili, hakenula meso kuchanhya kulanga, na kulumba. Hakaibendula aiya imikate na sisomba na kuwengha awefusa wawagawile wanhu.
42009017	Na wanhu wose hawadiya na kwiguta. Na kudondola ifyasigale, fisege ikumi na fili fya fibendu.
42009018	Ugele foyejayowa yakutasa ye imwene, awefusa wakwe hawowa hamwedu naye, hakawosa, “Awanhu wakunigamba niye nene nani?”
42009019	Hawamubidula, “Yohana Mubatisaji, wamonga Eliya, Wamonga Yumwedu wa Wagonesi.”
42009020	Hakamosa yakugamba, “Anyeye nanye mukugamba niye nene nani?” Petulo hakamubidula yakugamba, “Agweye no Kilisito we Mulungu.”
42009021	Hakawalemesa wanghamutamile munhu wowose imbuli iyo;
42009022	yakugamba, “Imwagila Mwana we Munhu kitang'anyila na magayo mengi na kulemigwa ne wasehe na wakulu wa watambiki na Watulumi na kukomigwa, na mwijuwa dya kadatu kwinuka.”
42009023	Kamei hoyowatamila wose Nghona munhu wowose yakuhananga kunyandamila, yakileme imwenyecho na kulonda umusalaba wakwe chila ijuwa na kunyandamila.
42009024	Kosoko wowose yakuhananga kuhonya uumi wakwe yakuwagilisa, na ulomo yakuhananga kwagilisa uumi wakwe kosoko yangu, kouhonya.
42009025	Kosoko imunhu kopata chambusi chaki yanghapata ichilunga chose na kiyagilisa imwenecho?
42009026	Kosoko chila yakunyonela chinyala aniye na imbuli yangu, imwana we imunhu naye komonela chinyala ugele wayakwija mwitunyo dyakwe, mwitunyo dye Babakwe na dya Malaika Wasunhile.
42009027	Ninga chawelu nikumutamilani, wabaha wamonga wemile hano awene wasidyona difa mpaka wawone undewa we Mulungu.
42009028	Gakaloke majuwa munana, kufulusa kulonga gago, hoyowalonda Petulo na Yohana na Yakobo hamwedu naye na kuluta kwitunda kutasa.
42009029	Ugele woyatasage inyoneka ye chihanga chakwe haibiduka na sisuke sakwe hosikwakaika swee!
42009030	Langa wanhu weli wendewolonga naye, hawowa awagonesi Musa na Eliya.
42009031	Woneka mwitunyo ikulu na kulonga soko ye difa dyakwe dikuhananga dilawanise Yelusalemu.
42009032	Petulo na wayagwe wowile naye hawowa na nhongo, ninga howokwinuka na kona ditunyo dyakwe na wanhu weli wemile hamwedu naye.
42009033	Na wanhu waya fowamulekage Yesu, Petulo hoyomugamba Yesu, Mundewa, ni fiswamu fina cha hano, leka chigolose fibanda fidatu, chimwedu chako, chimwedu cha Musa, chimwedu cha Eliya. Nghamanyile choyalongage.
42009034	Foyalongage nhaifo, ifunde hodikwija na kuwagubika, nawo hawogoha fowengile mwifunde.
42009035	Na dijwi hadilawa mwifunde dikugamba, “Ayuno no mwanangu wonimusagule; mutegeleseni!”
42009036	Na dijwi diya dikahulikike, Yesu hoyokoneka yemwene. Nawo howonyamala na wasamutamile yoyose gowonile mumajuwa gago.
42009037	Mwijuwa dya keli, fowadulike kulawa kwitunda, itewa ikulu hodikitang'anyila naye.
42009038	Langa munhu kulawa mwitewa yenula dijwi yakugamba, “Mwalimu nikukutasa umulange imwanangu, kosoko no yuyuno yumwedu.
42009039	Langa imhepo imukinya, na baho ni baho hoyotowa chowe, dimuguma chisilisi mpaka kalawa ifulo, na disikumulekela chimwande.
42009040	Haniwatasa wefusa wako wadilafe, ninga hawaduga.”
42009041	Yesu hoyobidula, “Anye icheleko kichaka dihuwi, chagilile nokikala na nyeye, na kuwafinyilisa mpaka milaki? Mwigale imwanago ahano.”
42009042	Kamai foyendeyokwija dipepo hodimukinya na kumuguma chisilisi. Ninga iYesu hoyodigombela dipepo dihile na kumuhonya imujelelo na kumwingha keli iBabakwe.
42009043	Na wose howokisina kosoko ya udaha ukulu we Mulungu. Ninga wose fowesinage soko ya kila chinhu choyagolose, hoyolonga na wefusa wakwe,
42009044	“Lekeni simbuli sino singile musinghutwi senu, kosoko imwana we munhu kolafigwa kumikono ya wanhu.”
42009045	Ninga wasaimanyile inonga iyo, na hoifisigwa ukwawo, wanghaitange, nawo wende wokogoha kumusa Yesu soko ye inonga iyo.
42009046	Na howokwingila mumawango mugati yawo, nani imukulu kusuma wose?
42009047	Ninga iYesu foyatanga amadoga ge mimoyo yawo, hoyolonda mwana mudodogi na kumwika habehi naye,
42009048	na hoyowagamba, “Wowose yakumuhokela imwana yuno kwisina dyangu, yakunihokela niye, na wowose yakunihokela niye, yakumuhokela ayuya yanitumile, kosoko ayuya imudodogi mugati yenu wose ayo no mukulu.”
42009049	Yohana hakabidula, “Mundewa hachona munhu yakuwinga magini kwa disina dyako, na hachimulemesa kosoko nghakiyandamila na seye.”
42009050	Ninga Yesu hoyomugamba, “Munghamulemese, kosoko inghowile chinyume chetu kaulwandi lwetu.”
42009051	Amajuwa gakasegelele kwe imwene kwinuligwa kulawa muchilunga, hoyohananga kuluta Yelusalemu.
42009052	Na hoyotuma watumigwa kumulongolela, awo hawaluta na kwingila muchijiji cha Wasamalia kosoko wamugolosele hanhu.
42009053	Ninga awakaya wasamuhokela kosoko hakalongosa injila kuluta Yelusalemu.
42009054	Kamei awefusa wakwe Yakobo na Yohana fowonile imbuli iyo hawagamba, “Mundewa ukuhananga chilagise moto kulawa kulanga uwalakase?”
42009055	Ninga iYesu hakabiduka na kuwagombela.
42009056	Kamei hakawagombela na kugamba, “Musimanyile mwina chidoga chaki chihile kosoko imwana we Munhu nghejile kukoma uumi wa wanhu ninga kuwahonya. Kamei hawaluta mukaya ingi.”
42009057	Ninga fowendowogenda munjila, munhu yumwedu hoyomugamba, “Nokwandamila hohose howukuluta.”
42009058	Na iYesu hoyomugamba, “Amabwasiko gena makolongo na fidege fya mulanga fina mafulu, ninga imwana we munhu kechaka hanhu hokugona.”
42009059	Kwa yumonga kagamba, “Nyandamile,” ninga imwene kagamba, “Mundewa leka nghonge kumusika iBabangu.”
42009060	Ninga Yesu hoyomugamba, “Waleke wofile wawasike wayawo wofile; amba gweye leuka ukatamilise undewa we Mulungu.”
42009061	Yumonga kamugamba, “Mundewa nokwandamila, ninga leka nghonge kuwelaga awanhu wa ukaya ukwangu.”
42009062	Yesu hoyomugamba, “Munhu iyagumile umukono wakwe kulima, kayi yekulanga kunyuma, nghagiligwe kuundewa we Mulungu.”
42010001	Kulawa baho iMundewa hoyosagula makumi Mufungate na weli, na kuwegala wamulongolele weli weli musikaya na hanhu hoyendoyohananga kuluta.
42010002	Hakawagamba, “Uludyo kumugunda mwingi, ninga awagolaji wakefu; mutase iMundewa wa uludyo yegale awagolaji mumugunda wakwe.
42010003	Sanghanyeni, mulangisise nikumutumani nyeye fina ngholo mugati ya mausi.
42010004	Munghalonde mufuko kahi mukoba, kahifilwatu, na munjila munghamulamuse munhu.
42010005	Munyumba yoyose yo mukwingila kunghonga gambeni dihewa dyuwe hamwedu ne inyumba ayino!
42010006	Inghowa mwana wa uswamu kabaho, dihewa dyenu dyokwikala hamwedu naye, ninga nghona kechaka, dihewa dyenu dyomuwilani.
42010007	Musigale munyumba imwedu, mudiye na kunywa fowakumwinghani, kosoko imutogomi kagiligwa maliho gakwe; munghasungulute kulawa inyumba imwedu kuluta ingi.
42010008	“Mukaya yoyose yomukwingila na wanghawahokela, diyeni fikwikigwa kumwande yenu.
42010009	Honyeni watamu wawo na kuwagamba, ‘Undewa we Mulungu wija habehi yenu.’
42010010	Ninga mukaya yoyose yomukwingila wanghaleka kuwahokela, mulute musinjila sawo na kugamba,
42010011	‘Hata dinghundi dye ikaya yenu idinamatile mumigulu yetu chikudikunghuna chuwe chitangilo ukwenu; ninga manyeni fina undewa we Mulungu usegelela.’
42010012	Nikumutamilani yokuwa fihufu ku Sodoma kufinyilisa mwijuwa diya kujumha ikaya iya.”
42010013	“Usungu wako Kolasini! Usungu wako Betisaida! Kosoko mhali majumo ago agagoloseke ukwenu, gagoloseke Tilo na Sidoni, hawowa wekulamba katali, no kufala suke sa magunia na kwikala mudifu.
42010014	Ninga yokuwa fihufu kufinyilisa diliganiso, kosoko ya Tilo na Sidoni kusuma nyeye.
42010015	Na gweye Kapelinaumu, togola! Kokwisigwa mpaka kulanga? Koduliswa mpaka kusimu.
42010016	Iyakuwahulika nyeye, yakunihulika niye, na yuya yakuwalema nyeye, yakunilema niye, na iyakunilema niye, yakumulema ayuya yanitumile.”
42010017	Awaya makumi mufungate na weli howokuya kwa chinyemi, wakugamba, “Mundewa, hata simhepo sikuchogoha seye ku disina dyako.”
42010018	Hoyowagamba, “Hanimona Shetani yakulagala fina lumwemwe kulawa kulanga.
42010019	Langeni, niwengha udaha wa kujata majoka na fisuswe, ne udaha wose muchanhya ye imunghondo, na hechaka chinhu chidaha kuwabulaga.
42010020	Hata nheifo munghasekelele kosoko simhepo sikuwogoha, ninga musekelele kosoko amasina genu gawandikigwa kulanga.”
42010021	Ugele uwo Yesu hakonela mwi Muhe Musunhile, hoyosekelela na kugamba, “Nikukulumba, Baba, Mundewa we iisi na Ulanga, kosoko simbuli sino kuwafisa awena misungu na umanyi na kuwagubulila wana wadodogi. Heye Baba, kosoko nofowendile.”
42010022	Kawatamila wanhu yakugamba, “Ninghigwa finhu fyose na Babangu, kahi hechaka yamumanyile Mwana ila Baba, kahi hechaka yamumanyile Baba ila Mwana, na wowose imwana yoyakuhananga kumugubulila.”
42010023	Kahi hakawabidukila awefusa wakwe na kulonga nawo kwa chinyele, “Ibeka ameso agekona gomukona nyeye!
42010024	Kosoko nikumutamilani nhafi, wagonesi na Wandewa wengi hawasulumila kona gomukona nyeye, wanghagone na kugahulika.”
42010025	Langa! Mulamusi yumwedu hoyokwima kumugesa, yakugamba, “Mwalimu, nigolose nhani niuhale uumi wa majuwa gose?”
42010026	Hakamugamba, “Iwandikigwa choni mwilagiso? Ukusoma nhani?”
42010027	Kamei hakamubidula, “Umwende iMundewa Mulungu wako kwa umoyo wako wose, na ichidoga chako chose, na uludole lwako lwose, na imisungu yako yose, na iyehabehi nagwe fina gomwenecho.”
42010028	Naye kamugamba, “Kubidula fiswamu, Golosa nhaifo, nagwe kokuwa mumi majuwa gose.”
42010029	Ninga imwene hakahananga kiyonesa muswamu, hakamusa Yesu, “Na iyehabehi na niye noyehoki?”
42010030	Yesu hakamubidula, “Munhu yumwedu yeja yadulikaga kulawa Yelusalemu kuluta Yeliko, hoyokoligwa na wahiji hawamuhambula na kumutowa, na kumuleka habehi na kufa.
42010031	Ninga kwa bahati, Kuhani yumwedu yendoyedulika kupulutila injila iiya, na foyamonile hoyogenda kunghanda.
42010032	Kahi ne Mulawi nheifiya, foyafikile baho na kumona hoyogenda kunghanda.
42010033	Ninga Musamalia yumwedu munghenda yakwe, yafika baho hoyowile, na foyamonile, hakamonela ubasi,
42010034	hakamulutila, kamubaka mafuta na miti na kumoha filonda fyakwe, kahi hoyomukwisa mwipunda dyakwe na kumwigala kunyumba ya wageni, na hoyomulagula.
42010035	Na dijuwa dya keli yalafa dinali mbili na kumwingha imwenye nyumba yakugamba, ‘Mulangisise yuno, na chochose chowukwenda ulafe kusuma ino, nokuwisila nghona nikuya.’
42010036	“Togola! Yehoki mudatu wawo, yeyonese fina kahabehi na yuya yatowigwe na wahiji?”
42010037	Hoyogamba, “Ayuya yamonele ubasi.” Na Yesu hoyomugamba, “Luta nagwe ukagolose nhaifo.”
42010038	Ninga Yesu na wefusa wakwe, fowowile munhambo, Yesu hoyokwingila muchikaya chimonga, na imwanamuke disina dyakwe Malita hoyomuhokela munyumba yakwe.
42010039	Malita hakowa na mufunakwe yenangagwe Maliamu, imwene yekala mumigulu ya Yesu na kutegelesa amafuso gakwe.
42010040	Ninga Malita hakedasika na utogomi mwingi, hoyomulutila na kumugamba, “Mundewa, ukona fiswanu fonikidasika niimwene, imufunangu kanileka nikutogoma niimwene? Mugambe ninga yanitase.”
42010041	iMundewa hoyomubidula, “Agwe Malita, ukugaya na kiidasika na finhu fingi,
42010042	chinhu chimwedu chikuhanangigwa. Imaliamu kasagula chinhu ichiswamu, nacho chisileusigwa ukwakwe.”
42011001	Yesu yeja yowa hanhu hamonga yakutasa, foyamalile kutasa yumwedu wa wefusa wakwe hoyomugamba, “Mundewa, chifuse kutasa fina Yohana foyawafusile awefusa wakwe.”
42011002	Hakawagamba, “Nghona mukutasa gambeni: Baba, Disisina dyako ditunyigwe; Undewa wako wije.
42011003	Uchinghe chila ijuwa chakudiya chetu,
42011004	na uchilekelele uwihi wetu, kosoko seye nase chikuwalekelela awachigolosele uwihi. Na unghachigume mumagesa.”
42011005	Kamei hakawagamba, “No nani ukwenu yena mbwiyakwe yomulutila muchilo gati na kulonga naye, mbwiyangu ninghe mikate midatu,
42011006	‘Kosoko nijiligwa na mbwiyangu yekulawa nhambo, nani nichaka chinhu cha kumwingha yadiye,’
42011007	naye komubidula kulawa kugati, ‘Unghanidase, dibanhi difulusa kuhindigwa, aniye ne wanangu chifulusa kugona, sidaha kwinuka na kukwingha chochose.’
42011008	Nikumutamilani, hata nghona nghekwinuka na kumwingha chochose kosoko ni mbwiyakwe, ninga kosoko yakugendelela kumutasa kokwinuka na kumwingha chochose choyakuhananga.
42011009	“Nikumutamilani, Taseni, mokwingigwa, hanangeni; mopata, gong'ondeni; nanye mokumuliligwa.
42011010	Kosoko chila yakutasa yakuhokela, na kwa yuya yakugong'onda yakukumuliligwa.
42011011	Hena Baba yehoki ukwenu imwanagwe yanghamutasa somba komwingha ijoka?
42011012	Ama yanghatasa ditagi komwingha chisuswe?
42011013	Nghona nyeye gomwina uwihi mumanya kuwengha awana wenu finhu fiswamu, iBaba yenu wa kulanga kamanya mikangha mingahi kuwengha Muye Musunhile awaya awekumutasa!”
42011014	Baho yendoyolafa imhepo yowile imutendile imunhu chimumu, imhepo foyalawile ichimumu hoyolonga, na awanhu howokisina lugano.
42011015	Ninga wamonga hawagamba, “Yekulafa simhepo kwa udaha wa Belisebuli, imukulu wa simhepo.”
42011016	Baho awamonga wakumugesa wakuhananga chitangilo kulawa kulanga.
42011017	Ninga imwene yamanya amadoga gawo, hoyowatamila yakugamba, “Chila undewa ukigawa uwecho kwa uwecho usikwima na nhaifo ulukolo kwa ulukolo.
42011018	Nghona Shetani yakigawa imwenecho, undewa wakwe wokwima nhani? Kosoko mukugamba nikulafa simhepo kwa ludole lwa Belisebuli.
42011019	Kahi nghona nikulafa simhepo kwa ludole lwa Belisebuli, togoleni awana wenu wakulafa kwa ludole lwani? Kosoko yo, awene nowowoliganisa.
42011020	Ninga inghowa kwe ludole lwa Mulungu, nikulafa simhepo, ninga mutange fina undewa we Mulungu ufulusa kuwejila.
42011021	Ugele munhu yena uludola yakiyohile ifilama fyakwe na kwimilisa ikaya yakwe, ifinhu fyakwe fikala digoya.
42011022	Ninga imunhu iyena ludole kusuma imwene yanghamulutila na kumutowa, yakumuhoka ifilama fyakwe foyahuwile na kufigawa ku wayagwe.
42011023	Wowose nghowile na niye nghehamwedu nami; na wowose nghakukunjagisa na niye yakwanjasa.”
42011024	“Imhepo ihile foikumulawa munhu, ikugenda muluwala kuhananga hanhu hakubwihila, na inghaleka kona ahanhu hokwikala, ikugamba Nokuya kukaya yangu, akuya konilawile.
42011025	Na inghoya ikuifika ikaya yakwe ishagiligwe na kuhambigwa fiswanu.
42011026	Baho yakuluta na kwigala simhepo singi mufungate sihile kusuma iyene, na sikwingila na kwikala umo, na imunhu yuya nyuwa yakwe ya kundumo ikuwa iha kujumha ya nghonga.”
42011027	Foyalongage nhaifo, mwanamuke yumonga mwitewa yatowa ikenje na kugamba, “Ibeka imwanamuke yakweleke, na matombo gowonghile.”
42011028	Imwene hakagamba, “Heye, ninga ibeka awekuihulika imbuli ye Mulungu na kuikola.”
42011029	Na amatewa fowongesekage, hoyokonga kugamba, “Icheleko chino ni cheleko cha wihi, chikuhananga chitangilo, ninga hechaka chitangilo chochikwinghigwa ninga achiya cha Yona.
42011030	Kosoko fina Yona foyowile chitangilo kwe wanhu wa Ninawi, nhaifo nofoyekuwa imwana we munhu kucheleko chino.
42011031	Malikiya wa kwekulu kokwinuka mwijuwa dya kuliganisigwa hamwedu na wanhu we cheleko chino na kuwaliganisa, kosoko imwene yeja kulawa ulwandi lwe ndumo ye chilunga, uleke yahulike ubala wa Sulemani, na hano hena munhu mukulu kusuma Sulemani.
42011032	Awanhu wa Ninawi wokwinuka mwijuwa dya kuliganiswa hamwedu na cheleko chino na kuchiliganisa, kosoko awene hawalamba kwa mahubili ga Yona, langa ahano hena mukulu kusuma Yona.”
42011033	“Hechaka munhu iyakwasa taa na kuifisa ama kuigubika ne isege, ninga yakuika muchigwaso, kosoko awekwingila wone ujelu wakwe.
42011034	Digiso dyako no taa yo umutufi wako, digiso dyako dinghowa dikona, umutufi wose winawo ujelu, ninga nghona disikona umutufi wako wina chisa.
42011035	Ninga langisisa ujelu uwile umwako ungheje ukuwa chisa.
42011036	Ninga inghowa umutufi wako wose umema ujelu, hechaka hanhu hena chisa, wokuwa na ujelu muhala, fina itaa foikumulika na ujelu wakwe.”
42011037	Ugele wuwo woyalongage, Mufalisayo yumwedu hakamugoneka kudiya naye ukwakwe, hakaluta na kwikala hamesa.
42011038	Imufalisayo hakesina kumona kakonga kudiya chakudiya cha nhegulo nghenati yanawe.
42011039	Kamei iMundewa hakamugamba, “Hambiya anyeye Mafalisayo mukusunha kunje ye fikombe na sisahani, ninga kugati mumema upujilaji na wihi.
42011040	Anye mubwalate! Iyombile fya kunje soyombile fya kugati?
42011041	Ninga lafeni ku wakiwa fyose fuwile kugati na kila chinhu chokuwa chiswanu ukwenu.
42011042	“Usungu ukwenu Mafalisayo! Kosoko mukutosa wanhu saka hata musunga na munafu na mabago gengi, na kuno mukuleka ichawelu na uwendo we Mulungu; agano hayagila mugakole kahi munghaleke agamonga.
42011043	Usungu wenu Mafalisayo! Kosoko mukwenda amadoga ga kumwande Mumasinagogi na kulamusigwa mumagulilo.
42011044	Usungu wenu! Kosoko mukifana filalo ifisikoneka, na awanhu wakugenda muchanhya yawo bila ya kutanga.
42011045	Yumwedu wa walimu wa shelia hoyomubidula, Mwalimu kwa kulonga nhafi kuchiliga na seye nheifiya.”
42011046	Hoyogamba, “Usungu wenu nanye muwalamusi we isheliya! Kosoko mukuwengha wanhu misigo misito, nanye muweecho musikukwafa ga makanda na chimwedu che fidole fyenu.
42011047	Usungu wenu! Kosoko mukushagila fiswanu mifilalo fya wagonesi wakomigwe ne waBaba senu.
42011048	Mukuhomelela na kuifumila imilimo ya wasehe wenu; Kosoko hawawakoma, nanye mukujengela ifilalo fyawo.
42011049	Na kosoko ubala we Mulungu ukugamba, ‘Nowatumila Wagonesi na watumigwa, awamonga wowakoma na kuwasambasa,’
42011050	na sakame ye Wagonesi itike kulawa kunghonga ye chilunga, yohanangigwa kucheleko chino.
42011051	Kulawa isakame ya Habili mpaka isakame ya Sakalia, iyakomigwe hagati ye hanhu hasunhile na hakulafila filafwa. Heye nikumutamilani yohanangigwa mucheleko chino!”
42011052	“Usungu wenu! Wanhu we malagiso, kosoko muleusa chikumulilo ye misungu; anye muweecho musingile na muwalemesa awaya wendowekwingila!”
42011053	Foyaleukage kulawa haya, Watulumi na Mafalisayo hawakonga kumwidasa na kumwanda yalonge mbuli nyingi,
42011054	Kumugojela wamukole muchinhu choyedaha kulonga.
42012001	Muchigele chicho, wanhu matewa kwa matewa hawakilunda hamwedu mpaka wendewokijata, hakakonga kulonga ne wefusa wakwe kunghonga, “Muwe meso na inungo ya Mafalisayo, nayo no chimwefe.
42012002	Hechaka chigubikwe chisigubuligwa, kahi chifisigwe ichene chisikamanyika.
42012003	Chochose chomulongile muchisa, chohulikika kuujelu, na chomulongile chinyele kuchumba kugati chotamiliswa munyumba muchanhya.”
42012004	“Nikumutamilani wambwiya sangu, munghogohe awaya wakukoma umutufi, kulawa baho wechaka dyowokudaha kugolosa.
42012005	Ninga nomutamilani nonani wokumwogoha: Mumogohe ayuya, yanghafulusa kukoma, kena udaha wa kuguma munhu kujehanamu, heye! Nikumutamilani mogoheni!
42012006	Togoleni ifindewa fishano fisikuguligwa kwa sendi mbili? Na hechaka chimwedu chikusimiligwa kumwande ye Mulungu.
42012007	Nhani, hata sinjwili sa matwi genu sitaligwa sose. Munghogohe anyeye mukwendigwa lugano kusuma findebwa fingi.”
42012008	“Na nikumutamilani wowose yekunifumila kumwande ya wanhu, imwana we munhu nheifiya komufumila kumwande ya Malaika we Mulungu.
42012009	Amba yuya yekunilema kumwande ya wanhu, kolemigwa kumwande ya Malaika we Mulungu.
42012010	Na chila munhu iyekumutofula Mwana we Munhu ngholekeleligwa, amba iyekumutofula Muhe Musunhile nghelekeleligwa.
42012011	Na wanghawegala anyeye kumwande ya masinagogi na wandewa na wena udaha munghowe na manhonge ifene fomubidula, hegu fomulonga;
42012012	Kosoko Muhe Musunhile kowafusa nyeye muchigele chicho agawagile kulonga.”
42012013	Munhu yumwedu mwitewa diya hoyomugamba, “Mwalimu mutamile mundugu sangu yanigawile ichipe changu.”

42012053	Wokitemanhula iBaba munhu ne imwanagwe, na imwana ne iBabakwe; ing'ina ne imwanagwe we chike, na imwana we chike ne ing'ina; ng'ina fyala ne muke mwana, kahi muke mwana ne ingina fyala.”

42023018	Ninga awanhu wose howojoja hamwedu, Chileusile imunhu ayu na uchidoholele Balaba.
42023019	Munhu yagumigwe kugati kosoko ye finju yalawanise mwikaya, na kwa ukomaji.
42023020	Pilato hakahananga kumohola Yesu, hakalonga nawo keli;
42023021	ninga hawatowa chowe Yasambasigwe, musambase!
42023022	Kahi lwakadatu hoyolonga nawo, “Nhani, kagolosa choni chihile? Sonile umwakwe mbuli yoyose ihile imwagile kufa; kosoko yiyo nomujola na kumudohola.”
42023023	Ninga hawakonya kuhananga kwa majwi makulu fina yasambasigwe. Na majwi gawo hagasuma.
42023024	Pilato yalamula fina ingwina yawo igoloseka.
42023025	Hakamoholela imunhu yagumigwe kugati kosoko ye ulefi na ukomaji, wowamuhanange, ninga iYesu hakamulafa yakomigwe fina fowendile.
42023026	Fene fowamulongose kulawa kwa Pilato, hawamukola munhu disina dyakwe Simoni wa Kilene yalawage kumugunda, na kumutwika umusalaba yaupike kunyuma ya Yesu.
42023027	Na baho hadimwandamila itewa ikulu dya wanhu, hamwedu na wanawake walilage na kuhongesa.
42023028	Ninga Yesu yayabidukila na kuwagamba, “Muwanawake wa Yelusalemu, munghanililile niye ninga mukililile muweecho na mulile kosoko ye iwana wenu.
42023029	Kosoko langeni! Amajuwa gekwija nawo wekwija welonga, Ibeka awechaka cheleko, na sinda siseleke, na matombo gasonghese!
42023030	Nawo wakonga kulonga na matunda, Chugwileni na fitongo Chigubikeni.
42023031	Nghona wagolose dino mwibiki dideke yokuwa nhani mwibiki dinyalile?”
42023032	Kahi hawawalonda wanhu weli wowile wabanaji, hawawalongosa wawakome hamwedu na Yesu.
42023033	Na fowejile ahanhu hekinangigwa Iguha dya ditwi, baho howomusambasa na waya wabanaji, yumwedu kulume na yumonga kumoso kwakwe.
42023034	Na Yesu hakagamba, “Baba uwonele ubasi kosoko wasimanyile chowakugolosa. Na hawegawila sisuke sakwe kwa kutowa kula.”
42023035	Na wanhu hawema baho na kulanga, ninga, ifilongosi hawamujowa wakugamba, “Hakahonya wamonga; lekeni yakihonye imwenecho, nghona imwene no mubakigwa we Mulungu yasaguligwe!”
42023036	Wasilikali nawo hawamogelela, haweja na kumwingha siki,
42023037	wakugamba, “Nghona gweye uMundewa wa Wayahudi kihonye gomwecho!”
42023038	Muchanhya yo musalaba hahowa na matulumo AYUNO NO MUNDEWA WA WAYAHUDI.
42023039	Yumwedu wa waya wabani watungikigwe hakamuliga yakugamba, “Agweye so Kilisito? Kihonye gomwecho na seye.”
42023040	Ninga iyumonga hakamugombela yakugamba, “Nghukumogoha Imulungu, nagwe kuwa munamulwa iyo?
42023041	Naseye ichagila, kosoko chikuhokela amaliho ge sinhenda setu, amba imunhu ayu nghagolose dyodyose dihile.”
42023042	Na hakagamba, “Yesu unigelegele no maa ukwingila muundewa wako.”
42023043	Na Yesu hakamugamba, “Chawelu, nikukutamila, diyelo ukuwa na niye kulanga.”
42023044	Hachuwa chigele cha saa mutandatu, hakuwa na chisa muisi yose mpaka saa ikenda;
42023045	dijuwa fyodyadugile kwalika; na dipasia dye dihekalu dyadegeka fipande fili.
42023046	Baho Yesu hakalila kwa ijwi ikulu yakugamba, “Baba mumikono yako nikwika ichidoga changu! Na foyalongile nhaifo hakatajika.”
42023047	Ayuya imukulu wa wasilikali yakone galwanise, hakamutunya Mulungu na kugamba, “Chawelu, imunhu ayu hakowa muswamu.”
42023048	Na amatewa wose watang'anyile kosoko yo kona imbuli ayo yo usungu, fowonile chagoloseke, hawoya ukaya wakwitowatowa mumhambaga.
42023049	Wengi wamumanyile, na awanawake wamwandamile kulawa Galilaya hawema hatali na kona fiswamu imbuli ayo.
42023050	Hahowa na munhu disina dyakwe Yusufu kulawa mukaya ye Chiyahudi ya Alimataya. Hakowa yumwedu wa wasehe we dibalasa, munhu muswanu na muchawelu,
42023051	imwene nghefumilise ne weyagwe soko ya diya dyowalamule na kugolosa, na yendeyongojela undewa we Mulungu.
42023052	Imunhu ayu hakaluta kwa Pilato na kuutasa umutufi wa Yesu.
42023053	Hoyouhumulusa na kuwoha musanda na kuwika muchilalo chowile mwiwe, nacho chisinghati chisikigwe munhu.
42023054	Hadyuwa ijuwa dya maandaliwo, ne sabato hayuwa habehi na kukonga.
42023055	Awanawake walawile Galilaya hamwedu naye hawamwandamila Yusufu na kuchona ichilalo na fowamusikile;
42023056	kahi howokuya, na hawagolosa mafuta ge mhungileu. Mwijuwa dye sabato hawabwihila fina foyalagisigwe.
42024001	Ninga dijuwa dye inghonga ye dijuma, hawaluta kuchilalo, na kulonda amafuta ge imhungile swamu gowagolose.
42024002	Hawona idewe dyo kuhindila difingilisigwa kulawa muchilalo.
42024003	Ninga fowengile kugati, wasawonile umutufi wa Yesu.
42024004	Fowedasikage kosoko ye imbuli ayo, langa! Wanhu weli wema habehi nawo wena suke njelu swee;
42024005	na fowowile na chogoho na kukinya ameso gawo hasi, awanhu waya hawawagamba, “Nhani mukumulangisa imumi kuwanhu wafile?
42024006	Kahechaka hano, ninga kenuka. Gelegeleni fina foyawatamile foyowile yekali Galilaya,
42024007	fina, Imwana we munhu, kolafigwa mumikono ye wanhu wena uwihi, nawo womusambasa, na mwijuwa dya kadatu kokwinuka.”
42024008	Baho hawagelegela simbuli sakwe,
42024009	na wakoye kulawa kuchilalo, hawawatamila gose go awaya ikumi na yumwedu na wose wasigale.

42024011	ninga simbuli asi hasoneka ni sa ubwalasi ukwawo na wasasihuwile.
42024012	Ninga Petulo hakenuka na kubilima ku chilalo, hakenama na kulanga kugati hakona isanda iimwene, na hakoya ukaya yakwisina kwa soko ya dilawanise.
42024013	Mwijuwa didyo weli wa wefusawakwe wenda weluta muchijiji chikwinangigwa Emau, utali wa isaa dimwedu nhafi kwa migulu kulawa Yelusalemu,
42024014	na wenda wesimulila awecho soko ye simbuli sose silawanise.
42024015	Fowasimulilage na kuwanga hamwedu, Yesu imwecho hakawejila na kwilongosa nawo.
42024016	Ninga ameso gawo hagahindigwa wanghamutange.
42024017	Hakawagamba, “Mbuli saki sino somukugenda mulonga?” Hawema, wakunyahala ifihanga fyawo.
42024018	Yumwedu wawo yekinangigwa Kileopa, hoyomubidula, “Agweye kwa mugeni we mwene ku Yelusalemu nghumanyile imbuli ilawanise kuya mumajuwa gano?”
42024019	Kawagamba, “Mbuli yaki?” Hawamugamba, “Imbuli ikumuhusu Yesu wa Nasaleti, yowile mugonesi yena udaha mu go yakulonga na kugolosa kumwande ye Mulungu na wanhu,
42024020	na ifyene wakulu wa Makuhani na wakulu wetu fowamulafile yahokele indamulwa ye difa, kahi yasambasigwe.
42024021	Ninga hachihuwila fina imwene hakowa yakuwakombola Isilaeli. Heye, na kuleka gago gose, diyelo ni ijuwa dija kadatu kulawa gano galawanise.
42024022	Hamwedu na gago, awanawake wamonga wamwandamilage fina seye, wachitinhusa; hawaluta kuchilalo nhousikusiku.
42024023	Na wasawonile umutufi wakwe, na woya wakugamba fina hawalawiligwa na malaika, wawatamile fina ni mumi.
42024024	Awamonga wowile na seye hawaluta kuchilalo na kona fina awanawake fowalongile, ninga imwene wasamonile.”
42024025	Hakawagamba, “Anye mu wanhu muwabwalasi! Na wakugutu wa kuhuwila gose galongigwe na wagonesi?
42024026	Togoleni, isamwagile imubakigwa, yapate magayo gano na kwingila ku undewa wakwe?”
42024027	Yakonga kulawa Musa na wagonesi wose, kawagubulila mumatulumo masunhile simbuli sose simwagile imwene.
42024028	Kahi hawachisegelela ichijiji chowalutage. Imwene hakakigolosa fina yakuhananga kugendelela kumwande;
42024029	ninga hawamulemesa wakugamba, “Ikala na seye, kosoko dijuwa diswa.” Baho hakaluta na kwikala nawo.
42024030	Foyowile muchakudiya hamwedu nawo, hakalonda umukate kuumotesa, na kaubendula na kuwengha.
42024031	Na ameso gawo hagagubuka na hawamutanga; naye hakaleuka mumeso gawo.
42024032	Hawakiyusa, Imimoyo yetu isakile mugati yetu foyalongage na seye munjila, foyachigubulilage amatulumo masunhile?
42024033	Kamei hawenuka muchigele chichiya na kuya Yelusalemu; na hawawafika awaya ikumi na weli wetang'anyile hamwedu na waya wose wowile nawo,
42024034	wagambile, iMundewa kenuka chawelu na keyonesa kwa Simoni!
42024035	Baho, awatumigwa aweli hawawatamila galawanise munjila na fyene fowamutangile mu kuubendula umukate.
42024036	Fowalongage gago, Yesu imwecho hakema mugati yawo na kuwagamba, “Digoya dyuwe ukwenu.”
42024037	Ninga hawatinhuka na kwingilwa na manhonge, na hawamanya fina wona isoki.
42024038	Na hakawagamba, “Nhani mukiidasika, na nhani mukiyusa mumimoyo yenu?
42024039	Langeni imikono ne migulu yangu, fina no niye nimwenecho, nyalabaseni munilange, kosoko umusikule wechaka nyama na maguha fina fomukona ninafo.”
42024040	Na yakalonge gago, hakawonesa imikono ne imigulu.
42024041	Na fowowile wenghali kuhuwila kosoko ye inyemo na kukisina, hakawagamba, “Mwina chochose hano chakudiya?”
42024042	Hawamwingha chibendu cha somba ibanikigwe,
42024043	na hakakilonda na kudiya mumeso gawo.
42024044	Kahi hakawagamba, “Asi no simbuli sonalongile na nyeye, fonowile nikali na nyeye, fina chila chinhu chitulumigwe muchanhya yangu mutolati ya Musa na wagonesi na Musabuli ikuhanangigwa chimemelekele.”
42024045	Noho yawagubulila imisungu yawo wadahe kugatanga amatulumo,

42024047	na fina kulamba na kulekeleligwa uwihi fikuhanangigwa fihubiliigwe mudisina dyakwe kuMataifa gose kukongela Yelusalemu.
42024048	Anyeye mwa wahomelesi wa simbuli asi.
42024049	Langeni, nomwigalilani ayuya iBaba woyalongile; ninga mwikale mukaya mpaka mufasigwe uludole kulawa kuchanhya.”
42024050	Kahi hakawalongosa kuluta mpaka Betania, hakenula mikono yakwe na kuwamotesa.
42024051	Foyeja yowa mukuwamotesa, hoyokwitemanula nawo na hakenuligwa kulanga kuchanhya.
42024052	Awene hawamufugamila na hawoya Yelusalemu kwa chinyemi chikulu,
42024053	Hawekala chigele chose mwihekalu wakumutunya Mulungu.
43001001	Uko kunghonga hakuwa na Mbuli, naye Mbuli hakowa ne Mulungu.
43001002	Imwene kunghonga hakowa na Mulungu;
43001003	ifinhu fyose hafigoloseka kwa njila ya imwene, na kuswela imwene kwichaka chochose chene chagolosigwe chowile chikugoloseka.
43001004	Mugati yakwe no mowile na uwumi; na uwumi uya hawuwa ujelu wa wanhu.
43001005	Ujelu ukumulika muchisa, na ichisa chisikudaha kuwusima.
43001006	Kweja kowa munhu yatumigwe kulawa kwe Mulungu, disina dyakwe Yohana.
43001007	Hakeja kosoko yo uhomelesi, kuuhomelela ujelu, uleke wose wahuwile kwa njila yakwe.
43001008	Imwene nghowile ujelu uya, ninga hakeja yauhomelele ujelu.
43001009	Ujelu we chawelu uwukumulikila chila munhu wokwija muchilunga.
43001010	Hakowa muchilunga, ne chilunga hachigolosigwa kwa njila yakwe, ninga ichilunga chisamumanyile.
43001011	Hakeja kukaya yakwe imwenyecho, ninga awanhu wakwe wasamuhokele.
43001012	Ninga ku wose awamuhokele, awahuwile disina dyakwe hakawengha udaha wogoloseke wana we Mulungu.
43001013	Awelekigwe, si kwa sakame hegu kwenda kwa munhu kwa chimutufi, ninga kwa Mulungu.
43001014	Imbuli hoikuwa mutufi, hoyokwikala muchilagati yetu, kamema dihewa ne chawelu; chidilanga ditunyo dyakwe, ditunyo fina dye imwana yemwene kulawa kwe Baba.
43001015	Yohana hakowa na uhomelesi muchanhya yakwe, na kujoja, “Ayuno no yuyuya wonagambile fina, ‘Iyakwenda yeje kunyuma yangu, imukulu kusuma niye, kosoko hakowa kumwande yangu.’”
43001016	Kulawa mukumema kwake ase wose chohokela dihewa muchanhya ya dihewa.
43001017	Kosoko dilagiso hadija kwe njila ya Musa; dihewa ne chawelu fija kwa njila ya Yesu Kilisito.
43001018	Hechaka yamonile Mulungu, ugele wowose uya; iMwana muhala, yowile mu chifa cha Baba, noyamugolose yamanyigwe.
43001019	Na uno no uhomelesi wa Yohana, ugele Wayahudi fowatumile awatambiki na Walawi kulawa Yelusalemu wamuse, “Agweye no nani?”
43001020	Hakafumila kahi ngalemile, ninga hakalonga fina, “Aniye siyo no ni Kilisito.”
43001021	Howomusa, “Aho gwegwe nani gweye? Aho gwe no Eliya? Hoyobidula Siniye ka. Agweye no yuya imugonesi? Hoyobidula, ka.”
43001022	Hawamusa, “Aho gwegwe nani? Chitamile uleke chiwabidule awaya awachitumile ukugambaki muchanhya yako?”
43001023	Hakagamba, “Aniye no dijwi dye iyakujoja munyika: Igololeni injila ye Mundewa, fina foyalongile imugonesi Isaya.”
43001024	Wawo awatumigwe hawalawa kumafalisayo.
43001025	Hawamusa, “Aho nhani ukubatisa, nghonaga nghu Kilisito, kahi nghu Eliya, nghwi mugonesi?”
43001026	Yohana hakawabidula, “Nikubatisa na meji; muchiligati chenu kema imwene anyeye musimumanyile.
43001027	Ayuya iyakwija kunyuma yangu, aniye sikudaha kudohola isigi ye chilwatu chakwe.”
43001028	Agano hagogoloseka Betania umwambu wa Yolodani, hoyabatisilage Yohana.
43001029	Dijuwa dya keli yakwe hakamona Yesu yakwija ukwakwe; hakagamba, “Langeni iMwana Ngholo we Mulungu, iyakulewusa uwihi we chilunga!
43001030	Ayuno noyonalongile nikugamba, ‘Kunyuma yangu yakwija munhu imwene yowile kumwande yangu, kosoko hakuwa uko ugele aniye sinati nyuwe.’
43001031	Aniye nimwenyecho samumanyile, ninga kosoko yiyo hanija nikubatisa kwa meji, uleke yoneke ku Waisilaeli.”
43001032	Na Yohana hakahomela, “Hanyona Muhe yakuhulumuka kulawa kulanga kifana huwa, hoyosigala umwakwe.
43001033	Aniye nimwecho samumanyile; ninga ayuya iyanitumile kubatisa kwa meji kanigamba, ‘Ayo yo ukona Muhe yakudulika muchanhya yakwe na kusigala u mwakwe no yakubatisa kwa Muye Musunhile.’
43001034	Aniye nyona kahi nikuhomelela fina ayuno no Mwana we Mulungu.”

43001039	Hakawagamba, “Mwije mulange Howoluta hawona hoyekalage,” howokwikala naye dijuwa dyo kosoko hayuwa kifana saa kumi ya hegulo.

43002016	Hakawagamba waya awambasage si njiwa, Galeuseni gano ahano, musikudaha kuigolosa inyumba ye Babangu kuwa igulilo.
43002017	Awefusa wakwe howogelegela fina itulumigwa, Uwendo we nyumba yako wombulaga.

43002019	Yesu hakawabidula, Moleni Dihekalu dino, aniye kwa majuwa madatu nikudinula.
43002020	Wayahudi wagamba, “Dihekalu dino dijengigwa kwa minyaka makumi mane na mutandatu, agwe ukudaha kudinula kwa majuwa madatu?”
43002021	Ninga imwene hakalonga dihekalu dyo umutufi wakwe.
