43002025	kosoko hakawamanya wanhu wose nghahanange munhu wowose kuhomelela simbuli sa munhu; kosoko imwene imwecho hakamanya isuwile mugati ye munhu.
43003001	Hambiya, heja howa na munhu yumonga wa Mafalisayo, yakwinangwa Nikodemo, mukulu wa Wayahudi.
43003002	Munhu yuno yamwijila Yesu nechilo na kugamba, “Labi, chimanya gweye fina kwa mwalimu na kulawa kwa Mulungu, kosoko hechaka munhu yakudaha kugolosa fitangilo fina fino foukugoloa gweye, inghowa iMulungu nghehamwedu naye.”
43003003	Yesu hoyomubidula, “Chawelu chawelu nikukutamila, imunhu yanghaleka kwelekwa kwa usha, nghodaha kuwona undewa we Mulungu.”
43003004	Nikodemo yamugamba, “I munhu yakudaha kwelekigwa nhani yanghowa musehe? Yakudaha kwingila kahi munda mwe ing'ina na kwelekigwa?”
43003005	Yesu hakamubidula, “Chawelu, chawelu nikumutamilani imunhu yanghaleka kwelekigwa kwa meji na Muhe, ghodaha kwingila ku undewa we Mulungu.
43003006	Achiya chelekigwe kwa mutufi ni mutufi, na chiya chelekigwe kwa Muhe ni muhe.
43003007	Unghakisine kosoko nikugambile fina, yagila kwelekigwa kwa usha.
43003008	Imheho ikutowa foikwenda iyecho, mukuhulika dibumo dyakwe, ninga musikumanya ikulawa hoki kahi ikuluta hoki; nheifo nofoyuwile ku chila muunhu yelekigwe kwa Muhe.”
43003009	Nikodemo hakamugamba, “Yodahika nhani kuwa nheifo?”
43003010	Yesu yabidula yakugamba, “Agweye kwa mwalimu wa Isilaeli na simbuli sino nghusimanyile.
43003011	Chawelu, chawelu nikukutamila fina, chikulonga adiya dyo chimanyile, na kukuhomelela kugaya gochonile, ninga nyeye musikuhokela uhomelesi wetu.
43003012	Nghonaga nimutamileni simbuli sa muisi nanye musikuhuwila, mohuwila nhani ninghamutamilani simbuli si kulanga.
43003013	Kwechaka munhu wowose yakwilile kulanga ninga ayuya do yadululike kulawa kulanga iMwana wa Munhu.
43003014	“Kahi fina iMusa foyenula dijoka diya munyika, nheifo iMwana we Munhu kokwinuligwa.
43003015	Uleke chila munhu iyakumuhuwila yowe na uwumi wa majuwa gose.
43003016	Mulungu kachenda ichilunga lugano, hoyomulafa iMwanagwe iyumwedu du uleke chila munhu iyakumuhuwila yang'hagilile ninga yowe na uwumi wa majuwa gose.
43003017	Kosoko Mulungu nghamwigale iMwanagwe amuno muchilunga, uleke yachilamule ichilunga, ninga ichilunga chihonyigwe ne imwene.
43003018	Iyakumuhuwila imwene nghakuliganisigwa; inghakumuhuwila imwene kafulusa kuliganisigwa, kosoko nghadihuwile disina dye iMwana yumwedu we Mulungu.
43003019	“Auno no ulamusi, fina ujelu wija muchilunga awanhu howokwenda ichisa kusuma ujelu, kosoko sinhenda sawo hasuwa sihile.
43003020	Kosoko chila munhu yakugolosa gehile yakuudesekela ujelu, kahi nghakwija ku ujelu sinhenda sakwe singhonigwe.
43003021	Ninga ayuya iyakugolosa ichawelu yakwija kuujelu, uleke yoneke hajelu fina kagolosa kwa Mulungu.”
43003022	Kulawa baho Yesu na wefusa wakwe hawaluta kuisi ya Uyahudi, hakasinda uko hamwedu nawo na kubatisa.
43003023	Yohana naye yendeyobatisa, ako Ayinoni, habehi na Salimu kosoko uko hakuwa na meji mengi, awanhu wendewomulutila na kubatisigwa.
43003024	Kosoko Yohana hakowa nghenati yagumigwe kuchifungo.
43003025	Howolawanisa nyikusha mugati ya wefusa wa Yohana na Muyahudi yumonga kosoko ya usunhaji.
43003026	Howomulutila Yohana na kumugamba, “Labi ayuya yowile nagwe umwambu wa Yolodani, wowahomelele, kabahano, yakubatisa, na wose wakumulutila imwene.”
43003027	Yohana hakabidula, “I munhu ng'hakudaha kuwa na chinhu chochose ichene chonghenghigwe kulawa kulanga.
43003028	Anye muwecho mukudaha kuhamelela, fina hanigamba, ‘Aniye siyo no Kilisito, ninga nigaligwa nimulongolele!’
43003029	Iyenaye mutoligwa, no mutolaji. Imbwi yakwe we mutolaji, iyakwima na kumutegelesa, yakusekelela lugano foyakuhulika dijwi dye mutolaji. Kosoko iyo ichinyemi changu hambiya chimemelesigwa.
43003030	Imwene yongeseke ninga aniye nihunguke.”
43003031	“Imwene iyekwija kulawa kulanga ni mukulu kusuma wose. Ayuya wa hachilunga ni munhu wa hachilunga na yakulonga simbuli sa hachilunga, ayuya yakulawa kuchanhya, kamuchanhya ya gose.
43003032	Yakuhomelela agaya goyonile na kugamelela na kugahulika, ninga hechaka iyakuhokela uhomelesi wakwe.
43003033	Iyakuhokela uhomelesi wakwe yakufumilisa fina Mulungu ni chawelu.
43003034	Kosoko iyatumigwe na Mulungu yakulonga simbuli sa Mulungu; kosoko Mulungu ng'hakulafa Muhe kwa chiliganiso;
43003035	iBaba yakumwenda iMwana, naye kamulekela finhu fyose mumikono yakwe.
43003036	Iyakumuhuwila iMwana kena uwumi wa majuwa gose; inghekwandamila simbuli sakwe nghakwenda yawone uwumi, ninga inyono ye Mulungu ikumwikalila.”
43004001	Hambiya iMundewa yakamanye fina Mafalisayo hawahulika fina Yesu yakugolosa wefusa wengi na kuwabatisa kusuma Yohana. (ninga
43004002	Yesu mwecho nghabatise nanga awefusa wakwe.)
43004003	Hakaleuka Samalia hoyoluta kahi Galilaya.
43004004	Haimwagila yalokele Samalia.
43004005	Hakafika ku kaya imonga ya Samalia ikwinangwa Sikali, habehibehi no mugunda Yakobo wo yamwingha imwanagwe Yusufu.
43004006	Chisima cha Yakobo hachuwa baho, Yesu kosoko hakasoka ne inhambo hakekala hasi baho hachisima. Hachuwa chigele cha saa ya mutandatu nhafi.
43004007	Hakeja mwanamuke Musamalia kunega meji, Yesu hoyomugamba, “Ninghe meji nunywe.”
43004008	Kosoko awefusa wakwe hawaluta ku ikaya kugula chakudiya.
43004009	Imwanamuke Musamalia yamugamba, “Yanhani agweye go Muyahudi, utase ameji ukwangu, ni mwanamuke we Chisamalia? Kosoko Wayahudi wasikuhanga na Wasamalia.”
43004010	Yesu hakamubidula, Nhanga umanyile ichinghwa che Mulungu no nani iyakukugamba, “Ninghe meji nunywe, hakuwa ukumutasa, imwene hakowa yakukwingha ameji ga uwumi.”
43004011	Imwanamuke hoyomugamba, “Mukulu, kwechaka chinhu cha kunegela, ne chisima ni chitali, ukupatahi ago ameji ga uwumi?
43004012	Agweye kwa mukulu kusuma iBaba yetu Yakobo, iyachighile ichima chino, na imwene imwecho hakonywa meji ge chisima chino, na wanagwe, na sawo sakwe?”
43004013	Yesu yamugamba Chila munhu yakunywa ameji gano yakwenda yone nghilu kahi,
43004014	ninga chila munhu iyakunywa ameji gonikumwingha nghakwenda yone nghilu ka! Ameji gaya gonikumwingha gakuwa kugati yakwe nhyoko ya meji gakubwiluka ku wumi wa majuwa gose.
43004015	Imwanamuke yamugamba, “Mukulu, ninghe niye ameji gano, uleke ninghone nghilu, kahi kwija hano kunega meji.”
43004016	Yesu hoyomugamba, “Luta kamwinange imulumako, mwije hano.”
43004017	Imwanamuke hakabidula nechaka mugosi, Yesu kamugamba, “kulonga ichawelu fougambile, Nechaka mugosi;
43004018	Kosoko hakuwa na wagosi washano, na ayuno yowinaye hambiya, si mulumako; aho nanga kulonga ichawelu.”
43004019	Imwanamuke yamugamba, “Mukulu nikona agweye kwa mugonesi.
43004020	Awababa setu wafungaga mwitunda adino; amba nyeye mukugamba Yelusalemu no kunhu kokufugila.”
43004021	Mundewa Yesu yamugamba, “Go mwanamuke unihuwile niye, ichigele chikwija ichene awakufuga wasikufugila mwitunda dino kahi si Yelusalemu, mukwende mumufuge iBaba.
43004022	Anyeye mukufuga cho musimanyile, aseye chikufuga cho chimanyile, kosoko uhonya ukulawa kuWayahudi.
43004023	Ninga ichigele chikwija, na hambiya chabahano, awakumufuga Mulungu chawelu wakumufuga iBaba mu muhe na chawelu, awo iBaba nowoyakuhananga wamufuge.
43004024	Mulungu ni Muhe, nawo awakumufuga inogela wamufuge kwa Muhe na kwa chawelu.”
43004025	Ayuya imwanamuke hakamugamba, “Nimanya fina Imasiya yakwija; (iyakwinangwa Kilisito); ma yakwija, yakayochones simbuli sose.”
43004026	Yesu kamugamba, “Aniye nikulonga nagwe no nene.”
43004027	Chimwande awefusa wakwe howokwija. Hawakisina kosoko yendeyosimulila ne mwanamuke, ninga hechaka yamusile Ukuhananga choni? Nhani ukulonga naye?
43004028	Kamei imwanamuke hakaleka dibiga dyakwe, hakaluta kwikaya, yawagamba awanhu,
43004029	Mwije, mulange munhu yanitamile ifinhu fyose fonigolose. Ayuno yakudaha kuwa no Kilisito?
43004030	Hawalawa kunje ye kaya na wende womwijila imwene.
43004031	Ugele uwo awefusa wakwe wakuhananga yadiye, wakugamba, “Labi udiye!”
43004032	Ninga kawagamba, “Nina chakudiya ichene anyeye msichimanyile.”
43004033	Kameyi awefusa wakiyusa wecho kwa wecho, Hena yumonga yamwigalile chakudiya?
43004034	Yesu kawagamba, “I chakudiya changu ni kugolosa ifyene foyakwenda ayuya yanitumile, na kumalagisa ikasi yakwe.
43004035	Mwina ulosi, ukugamba Ikali minyesi mine ukuwa ugele wokugola, ninga nikumutamilani, langisiseni imigunda; simhule sikangala ugele wokugola ufika!
43004036	iyekugola yakuhokela digelo dyakwe, yakulunda figoligwe fiya ku uwumi wa majuwa gose; kwa neifo imunhu yahandile na yuya yakugola wakusekelela wose.
43004037	Inonga ino ni chawelu, ‘Munhu yumwedu yakuhanda, munhu yumonga yakugola.’
43004038	Hanimutumani kugola afiya ifyene fomusagolosele milimo; wamonga hawagolosa, anye mwingila mu milimo yawo.”
43004039	Matewa ga Wasamalia mukaya iya wamuhuwila Yesu kosoko imwanamuke hakagamba, “Mwije mulange imunhu yanitamile ifinhu fyose fonigolose.”
43004040	Kamei Awasamalia wakeje ukwakwe, howomutasa yekale nawo; hoyokwikala uko majuwa meli.
43004041	Na wengi lugano hawamwihuwila kosoko ya imbuli yakwe,
43004042	hakamugamba imwanamuke, Sikosoko ya simbuli sako du ilekile chihuwila, kosoko aseye chiwecho chimuhulika, na chimanya fina ayuno chawelu nao Mwihula we chilunga.
43004043	Yakamale kwikala majuwa meli hoyoluta Galilaya.
43004044	Kosoko Yesu mwecho hakalonga fina imugonesi nghakupata itunyo muisi yakwe imwecho.
43004045	Nheifo yakeje Galilaya, awanhu wa Galilaya, howomuhokela, kosoko wonile gose agene goyagolose Yelusalemu ugele we dijuwa dikulu kosoko awene nawo hawaluta kusikukuu.
43004046	Kahi Yesu hoyoluta ku Kana ya Galilaya, koyagaluse meji kuwa difai. Baho Kapelanaumu hahowa mukulu yumonga wa Selekali, imwene hakowa na mwanagwe mutamu.
43004047	Hakahulike fina Yesu keja kulawa Uyahudi hata Galilaya, hoyaluta na kumutasa walutanye yakamuhonye mwanagwe, kosoko hakowa mutamu lugano, habehi na kufa.
43004048	Yesu kosoko iyo hoyomugamba, “Munghaleka kona fitangilo na majumo muisi kuhuwila.”
43004049	Imukulu yuya hoyogamba, “Mundewa wije imwanangu nghenati yafe.”
43004050	Yesu hakamugamba, “Luta imwanago yakuhona!” Imunhu yuya hoyohuwila imbuli yoyalongile Yesu ukwake hoyaluta.
43004051	Foyalutage, imutogomi wakwe hakakitanganyila na kumutamila fina imwanagwe kahona.
43004052	Hakosa ichigele choyakongile kuwa mumi, howomugamba, “Digulo chigele cha saa mufungate, imhungo imuleuka.”
43004053	iBabamunhu hoyogelegela fina ichigele chiya no chigele Yesu choyagambile, Imwanago yakuhona. Imwene imwecho hoyohuwila, we inyumba yakwe yose.
43004054	Achino hachuwa chitangilo chakeli choyagolose Yesu yakoye kulawa Uyahudi na kuya Galilaya.
43005001	Hanyuma yakwe kweja kowa ihuwa ikulu dye Wayahudi. Yesu hakakwila Yelusalemu.
43005002	Uko Yelusalemu habehi na dilango dya Singholo hahowa ne ilamba dikwinangwa munonga ye Chiyebulaniya Betisasa, dina deha shano.
43005003	Mugati ya siso sideha mwina awesikidaha, mudula, fiwete na watamu wokuholola, wakugojela ameji gatibuke;
43005004	(kosoko imalaika we Mundewa yendeyohumuluka ugele umonga na kwingila mwilamba, na kugatibula ameji; iyekukonga kwingila mwilamba, ameji ghonagatibuke yakuhona utamu wakwe wowose woyowile nawo.)
43005005	Munhu yumonga hakowa baho, yowile mutamu kwa minyaka makumi madatu na munane.
43005006	Yesu yakamone na kukumanya hakowa na utamu na kugona bahaya kwa ugele mwingi hoyomugamba, “Ukuhananga kuhonywa?”
43005007	Imunhu mutamu yuya hoyomubidula, Mukulu; nachaka munhu wa kuniguma mwilamba ameji fogakutibuligwa, ghona nikugesa kuluta munhu yungi yakulongola kwilamba kumwande yangu.
43005008	Yesu hoyomugamba, “Inuka, kitwike disasi dyako, na ugende.”
43005009	Chimwande imunhu yuya hakonywa, hoyolonda disasi dyakwe na kugenda. Dijuwa didyo hadyuwa ijuwa dye sabato,
43005010	awakulu wa Wayahudi howomulonga imunhu yahonyigwe, Diyelo ni sabato sifiswamu agweye kwinula disasi dyako.
43005011	Ninga hoyobidula, munhu iyanihonyile kanigamba, “Inula disasi dyako, ulute!”
43005012	Howomusa, Imunhu yakugambile ukitwike disasi dyako ulute nani?
43005013	Hambiya imunhu yuya yahonyigwe nghamumanyile Yesu, kosoko Yesu hakaleuka anhu baya, kosoko hahowa itewa dya wanhu ahanhu baho.
43005014	Hanyuma yakwe Yesu hoyomufika kwihekalu hoyomugamba, “Hulika, kwa mumi mambiya; unghagolose wihi kahi; dinghakwijile dihile lugano kusuma dino.”
43005015	Imunhu yuya hoyoluta kuwatamila aWayahudi fina Yesu noyonihonyile.
43005016	Aino nochileka Awayahudi wamwidasage Yesu, kosoko yagolose didyodijuwa dye sabato.
43005017	Yesu hoyowabidula, iBabangu yakugolosa milimo ugele wose, aniye nani inyagila nigolose.
43005018	Aino haiwagolosa Wayahudi wagendelele kuhananga kumukoma, si kosoko yo kubana isabato du, kahi na kumwinanga Mulungu fina Babakwe, yakigolosa fina kaligana ne Mulungu.
43005019	Yesu hakawagamba nikumutamilani ichawelu; iMwana nghakudaha kugolosa chochose yemwene; yakugolosa agaya do goyakona iBabakwe yakugolosa. Goyakugolosa iBaamunhu, iMwana naye nogoyakugolosa.
43005020	Kosoko iBaba yakumwenda iMwana na yakumonesa gose agene goyakugolosa imwene, yakumonesa na milimo mikulu kusuma aino, nanye mose mukwenda mukisine.
43005021	Fina iBaba foyakuwenula wafile na kuwengha uwumi, no nheifo iMwana naye yakuwengha uwumi awaya woyakwenda kuwengha.
43005022	Kahi iBaba nghakulamula munhu wowose, kamwingha iMwana udaha wose wo kulamul.
43005023	Wose wamogohe iMwana, fina fowakumogoha iBabamunhu. Wowose inghakumogoha iMwana nghakumogoha Baba iyamwigale.
43005024	Nikumutamilani ichawelu; imunhu wowose iyakuhulika simbuli sangu na kumuhuwila yanitumile kena uwumi wa majuwa gose; nghakwingila kukulamuligwa, ninga kaloka kulawa kudifa na kwingila kuuwumi.
43005025	Chawelu, chawelu, nikumutamilani, ichigele chikwija, na hambiya chabaha, ugele uwene awafile wakuhulika dijwi dye iMwana we Mulungu na awaya awakuhulika wakwenda wenuke mudifa.
43005026	Kosoko fina iBaba foyena uwumi mugati yakwe no nheifo kamwingha iMwana naye kuwa na uwumi mugati yakwe,
43005027	na kamwingha udaha wokogolosa ulamusi, kosoko ni Mwana we munhu.
43005028	Munghakisine kosoko yadino, ichigele chikwija awene wose wowile mufilalo wakawohulika dijwi dyakwe
43005029	na kulawa kunje, awagolose maswanu kukwinukila mu uwumi, awagolose gehile kukwinukila mukulamulwa.
43005030	Sikudaha kugolosa chinhu chochose kwa udaha wangu nimwecho; fonikuhulika, nofonikulamula; na ulamusi wangu uliganila, kosoko sikuhananga kugolosa fonikwenda niye, ninga kwenda kwakwe iyanitumile.
43005031	Hona nikihomelela nimwenecho uhomelesi wangu si wachawelu;
43005032	kwina yungi iyakuhomelela muchanhya yangu na nimanya fina uhomelesi wakwe woyakuhomelela muchanhya yangi ni wachawelu.
43005033	Hamutuma wanhu kwa Yohana, na hoyolafa uhomelesi kuchawelu.
43005034	Si kosoko niye nikuhokela uhomelesi ukulawa kuwanhu; ninga nikulonga sino uleke mohone.
43005035	Hakowa taa ikwaka na kumulika, nanye hamudaha kusekelela kwa chipisi chiguhi mu ujelu wakwe.
43005036	Ninga uhomelesi wo ninawo ni mukulu kusuma awuya wa Yohana; kosoko imilimo iBaba yoyagambile niigose na kumale, imilimo iyino yonikugolosa, ikunihomela fina iBaba kanituma.
43005037	Ne Baba imwecho yanitumile kalafa uhomelesi muchanhya yangu. Dijwi dyakwe musinati mudihulike, ifuta yakwe musinati muyone;
43005038	na mwachaka imbuli yakwe ikwikala kugati yenu, kosoko mudikumuhuwila ayuya iyagaligwe ne mwene.
43005039	Mukugahena hena matulumo kosoko mukudoga fina mugati yakwe mwina uwumi wa majuwa gose, nogo agene ga kuhomelela;
43005040	ninga mukulema kwija ukwangu uleke muwe na uwumi.
43005041	Aniye sikuhokela ditunyo kulawa kuwanhu.
43005042	Ninga nimanya anyeye mwechaka uwendo wao kumwenda Mulungu mufidoga fyenu.
43005043	Aniye nija mwisina dye iBabangu; anyeye musikuhihokela, ninga, yumonga yangheja kwa disina dyakwe imwecho, mukwenda mumuhokele.
43005044	Mohuwila nhani anyeye mukihokelesa ditunyo muwecho kwa wecho, ninga musikuhananga ditunyo dikulawa kwe Mulungu?
43005045	Munghagambe fina nikwenda niwasongese kwa Baba, iMusa noyakuwasongesa, imwene womumwikile dihuwi dyenu.
43005046	Nanga mwamuhuwile Musa hamuwa mukunihuwila na niye kosoko hakatuluma muchanya yangu.
43005047	Ninga ghonanga musikuhuwila goyatulume, mohuwila nhani sonikulonga?
43006001	Hanyuma yakwe Yesu hakaloka umwambu we bahali ya Galilaya no ya Tibelia.
43006002	Itewa ikulu dya wanhu howomwandamila, kosoko hawona amajumo gakwe gokuhonya watamu.
43006003	Yesu hoyokwila kwitunda, hoyokwikala hasi hamwedu na wefusa wakwe.
43006004	Na ugele we juwa dikulu dye Pasaka haduwa habehi.
43006005	Yesu hakenula meso hakalanga ako nako, hakona itewa dya wanhu wakumwijila, hakamusa Filipo, Chikudaha kugula hoki chadiya chakuwegusa awanhu wose wano?
43006006	Hakalonga neifo kumugesa Filipo; ichawelu iyecho imwecho hakamanya choyakwenda yagolose.
43006007	Filipo hakamubidula, Uleke chila munhu yapate chidodogi du ikunangigwa chuwe na mikate ya mapesa dinali magana meli nhafi.
43006008	Yumwedu wa wefusa wakwe, Andulea, munduguse wa Simon Petulo hoyogamba,
43006009	“Hena mwana bahano yene mikate mishano ye shaili na fisomba fili. Ninga chawelu fisikudaha kwigusa awanhu wose wano.”
43006010	Yesu hoyowagamba, “Walongeni awanhu wekale hasi. Hanhu baho hahowa na mbago nyingi.” Kosoko iyo awanhu wose howokwikala hasi, hawowa wanhu wafikile figulu fishano awagosi.
43006011	Yesu hoyoilonda imikate, hoyomulumba Mulungu, howogawiligwa wanhu awekale baho. Hakalumba kosoko ya sisomba, na wose howokwiguta.
43006012	Awanhu wose wakegute, hakawagamba awefusa wakwe Dondoleni ifibendu fyose ifisigale, chinghagilele hata chimwedu.
43006013	Hawamemesafikonghola fyose, howomemesa fisege ikumi na fili kulawa kumikate iya mishano ye shaili iyadiyigwe na wanhu.
43006014	Wakone dijumo dino doyagolose Yesu, awanhu weja wagamba howogamba Chawelu ayuno no Mugonesi yagambigwe yakwija muchilunga.
43006015	Yesu yakamanye fina wanhu wendewohananga weje wamukole uleke wamugolose kuwa Mundewa kwa ludole; hoyoleuka hoyoluta kwitunda kahi yemwene.
43006016	Ikowe hegulo, awefusa wakwe hawadulika kubahali,
43006017	howokwingila mu ngalawa hawakonga kuloka ibahali kuluta Kapelanaumu. Hachuwa chisa chingile, na Yesu hakowa nghenati yeje kuwa hamwedu nawo.
43006018	Ameji hogokonga kutunhumuka kosoko imheho nghulu yapumunhage.
43006019	Awefusa wakwe hawakwega makasia utali wa maili ine au shano nafi howomona Yesu kukugenda mumeji, yakusegelela ingalawa, howokogoha.
43006020	Yesu hoyowagamba, “Munghogohe, no niye!”
43006021	Kameyi kwa chinyemi howomwingisa mungalawa, na baho ingalawa hoifika muisi bahaya howalutage.
43006022	Dijuwa dya keli yakwe amatewa ulwandi lwa keli lwe bahali hawamanya fina kwina ngalawa imwedu du ulwandi lowowowile. Hawamanya fina Yesu nghengile mungalawa iya hamwedu na wefusa wakwe, ninga hawaleuka awene du wenumwene.
43006023	Minhumbwi imonga, kulawa Tibelia, haija mhwani habehi na bahaya ahene awanhu hawadiya imikate yongeseke yakamale kulumba Mundewa Yesu.
43006024	Amatewa wawakone Yesu kahechaka, hamwedu na wefusa wakwe, howokwingila musingalawa, howoluta Kapelinaumu, wakumuhananga.
43006025	Awanhu wakamone Yesu ulwandi lwa keli lwa bahali, hawamugamba, “Mwalimu kwija milaki kuno?”
43006026	Yesu hoyowabidula yakugamba, “Nikumutamilani ichawelu; mukunihananga kosoko hamudia mikate muwecho fomwahanange, homukwiguta, sikosoko hamona amajumo gangu.
43006027	Munghakiidase ne chakudiya ichene chikubanika; ninga mchigolosele milimo ichakudiya cha ugele wose ku uwumi wa majuwa gose. Achino no chakudiya ichene imwana we Munhu yakumwinghani, kosoko Mulungu, iBaba, kaguma chitangilo chakwe cha kumufumila.”
43006028	Kosoko iyo wejawamusa, “Chitende choni noho chigolose imilimo ye Mulungu yoyakuhananga chigolose?”
43006029	Yesu yawabidula, iMulungu choyakuchanga mugolose ni kumuhuwila ayuya yatumigwe ne mwene.
43006030	Yesu kawagamba, “Nikuwafamilani chawelu. iMusa choyamwinghileni usowile mukate kulawa kulanga; iBabangu noyakumwinghani umukate we chawelu kulawa kulanga.
43006031	Awagono wetu hawadiya mana munyika, fina amatulumo fogakulonga, Hakawengha mukate kulawa kulanga wadiye.”
43006032	Yesu kawagamba, “Nikuwatamilani chawelu, iMusa choyamwinghileni usowile mukate kulawa kulanga; iBabangu no yakumwinghani umukate we chawelu kulawa kulanga.
43006033	Kosoko umukate, iMulungu woyakulafa ni yuya yakudulika hasi kulawa kulanga na kuchigalila ichilunga uwumi.”
43006034	Hawamutasa, “Mukulu, Chinghe aseye umukate wuwuno majuwa gose.”
43006035	Yesu hoyowagamba, “Aniye no ni mukate wa uwumi; iyakwija ukwangu ifi nghakona njala; iyakunihuwila niye ifinghakona nghilu.
43006036	Ninga nimutamilani fina munyona nanyi musikuhuwila.
43006037	Wose woyakuningha iBaba wakwija ukwangu sikumutaga kunje ng'oo,
43006038	kosoko nidulika muyisi kulawa kulanga, si kugolosa fina fonikwenda niye, ninga kwenda kwakwe ayuya iyanitumile;
43006039	na kuno nokwenda kwake ayuya yanitumile, ninghamwagilise wowose mu waya woyaninghile, ninga nimwinule (muchilalu) dijuwa dye indumo.
43006040	Akuno no kwenda kwake iBabangu, fina chila munhu iyakumona iMwana na kumuhuwila yowe na uwumi wa majuwa gose; nani nikwenda nimwinule dijuwa dye indumo.”
43006041	Awayahudi hawakonga kumung'ung'unikila, kosoko yagambile, Aniye no ni mukate ulawile kulanga.
43006042	Howogamba, “Ayuno si Yesu, mwana wa Yusufu, iBabakwe ne ing'ina si chiwamanya. Yakudaha nhani kugamba, ‘Hambiya nihulumuka kulawa kulanga?’”
43006043	Yesu yawagamba Muleke kung'ung'ulika nyenye kwa nyenye.
43006044	Hechaka munhu yekudaha kwija ukwangu honaga nghakwegigwe ne Baba yanitumile niye; nani nikanimwinula mudijuwa dye ndumo.
43006045	Itulumigwa muchitabu cha wagonesi Na wose wakawawafusigwa ne Mulungu! Chila munhu yafusigwe na kuhulika kulawa kwa Baba yakwija ukwangu.
43006046	Kwechaka munhu wowose yamonile Baba, ninga ayuya yalawile kwa Mulungu, noyamonile Baba.
43006047	Chawelu, chawelu, nikuwatamilani, iyakuhuwila kwna uwumi wa majuwa gose.
43006048	Aniye no ni mukate wa uwumi.
43006049	Awababa senu hawadiya imana munyika, howokufa.
43006050	Auno no mukate ukudulika kulawa kulanga, uleke imunhu yandiye yanghafe.
43006051	Aniye no ni mukate wo uwumi, mudulike kulawa kulanga, wowose iyakudiya mukate uno, nghakufa ng'oo; na mukate wonikulafa kosoko yo uwumi we chilunga ni umutufi wangu.
43006052	Awayahudi, baho, wejawakonga kuwanga awenyecho, wakugamba, “I munhu yuno kodaha nhani kuchingha aseye umutufi wakwe chidiye?”
43006053	Kamei Yesu hoyowagamba, “Chawelu, chawelu nikuwatamila, Munghalekadiya umutufi we Mwana we munhu na kunywa isakame yakwe mwachaka uwumi kugati yenu.
43006054	Ayuya imwene yakudiya umutufi wangu na kunywa isakame yangu kena uwumi wa majuwa gose. Nani nikwija nimwinula dijuwa dye ndumo.
43006055	Kosoko umutufi wangu ni chakudiya cha chawelu, na isakame ni chinywaji chachawelu.
43006056	Iyakudiya umutufi wangu na kunywa sakame yangu yakwikala umwangu ani nani umwakwe.
43006057	Fina iBaba imumi foyanitumile niye, nani na mumi kosoko ya Baba. No neifo ayuya yakunidiya niya yakuwa mumi kosoko ya niye.
43006058	Awuno no mukate wadulike kulawa kulanga, siyo fina yowadiyile waBaba senu hawakufa, ayuya yakudiya mukate uno yakwikala majuwa gose.”
43006059	Hakalonga sino yowile mwisinagogi, ugele foyafundishage Kapelanaumu.
43006060	Wengi wa wefusa wakwe, wakahulike nheifo, howogamba, “Aino mbuli nghugutu nani yakwenda yaihulike?”
43006061	Ninga Yesu yakamanye fina awefusa wakwe wakuing'ong'olekela inonga iyo, yawagamba, “Musuha kosoko ya ino?”
43006062	Togoleni yokuwa nhani munghamona Mwana we munhu yakukwila koyowile ugele nghenati yeje?
43006063	iMunye noyakwingha uwumi, umutufu wechaka chinhu; simbuli sonilongile nanyi ni muhe kahi ni wumi.
43006064	Ninga wamonga wenu wasikuhuwila. Kosoko Yesu hakamanya kulawa kunghonga awaya awene wasahuwile, chenani awakwenda wamusongese.
43006065	Hoyowagamba, “Kosoko ino no chileka namutamileni kwechaka yakwija ukwangu nanga ayuya yekwihigwa udaha wokwija ne Babangu.”
43006066	Kulawa baho wengi wa wefusa wakwe howokuya kunyuma wasamwandamile kahi.
43006067	Yesu hoyowalonga awaya awefusa wakwe ikumi na weli, “Anye nanye molewuka?”
43006068	Simoni Petulo hakamubidula, “Mukulu, chilute kwani? Agweye kwina simbuli sa uwumi wa majuwa gose;
43006069	na chihuwila, na chifulusa kumanya, fina agweye no u Imusunhile yumwedu we Mulungu.”
43006070	Yesu hakawabidula, “Sawasaguleni ikumi na weli, na yumwedu wenu ni luhoma?”
43006071	Hakalonga muchanhya ya Yuda imwana wa Simoni Isikalioti, kosoko, imwene yumwedu wa waya ikumi na weli, noyowile wo kumusongesa.
43007001	Hanyuma yakwe Yesu hoyuluta ako nako Mufalilaya, nghadahile kugendagenda ako nako mu Uyahudi, kosoko Wayahudi wendewohananga kumukoma.
43007002	Hambiya, isikukuu ya Wayahudi ye Fibanda hayuwa habehi.
43007003	Awanduguse howomugamba, “Leuka hano ulute Uyahudi, uleke awefusa wako wone imilimo yo ukugolosa.”
43007004	Hechaka munhu yakugolosa kwa chifiso hona yakuhananga yamanyike kwa wose. Hona ukugolosa simbuli sino kiyonese kuchilunga.
43007005	Kahi na awanduguse nawo wasamuhuwile.
43007006	Yesu hoyowagamba, “Ichigele changu chisinati chifike, ugele uwenu wabaha majuwa gose.
43007007	Ichilunga chisikudaha kuwasula nyeye, ninga chikunisula niye kosoko nichihomelela kuwa sinhenda sakwe sa wihi.
43007008	Luteni nyeye kusikukuu, aniye sikuluta kusikukuu, kosoko ugele wangu wokuluta usinati umemelekele.”
43007009	Yakalonge nheifo, hoyosigala Galilaya.
43007010	Awanduguse wakafuluse kuluta kusikukuu, kame naye hoyoluta, ninga si kwa konigwa na wanhu nanga kwa chinyele.
43007011	Awayahudi wende womuhananga hasikukuu, wakugamba, “Kowahi?”
43007012	Hakuwa na mang'ung'uliko mengi muwanhu kosoko yakwe ugele wamonga wakugamba, “Ni munhu muswamu,” wamonga wakugamba, “Hata, yakwagilisa wanhu.”
43007013	Ninga kosoko yo kuwogoha Wayahudi hechaka munhu yadahile kulonga achawelu muchanhya yakwe nonga kufumbafumba.
43007014	Mugatigati ya majuwa ge sikukuu Yesu hoyokwingila mudihekalu na kufusa.
43007015	Awayahudi howokisina, wakugamba, “Yanhani, imunhu yuno kena umanyi, naye nghapatile mafuso?”
43007016	Yesu hoyawabidula, amafuso gangu si gangu niye, ninga gakwe iyanitumile;
43007017	inghowa inyenda ye munhu ni kugolosa inyenda yakwe, yakwenda yamanye fina mafuso gano gakulawa kwa Mulungu hegu nikulonga kwa udaha wangu nimwecho.
43007018	Iyakulanga mu udaha wakwe imwecho yakuhananga kutunyigwa imwene, ninga ayuya iyakuhananga ditunyo dya yuya yamutumile, mugati yakwe mwechaka udasi.
43007019	iMusa nghamwinghileni Malagiso? Hata nheifo hechaka yakugakola. Nhani mukuhananga kunikoma?
43007020	Awanhu hawamubidula, Kwina ipepo! Nani yakuhananga kuukoma?
43007021	Yesu hayawabidula Nigolosa nhenda imwedu, mose mukisina kosoko ya iyo.
43007022	Musa hakamwing'hani dikumbi(si kugamba dilawa kwa Musa ninga kulawa kuwa Baba senu) nanyi mukwigala munhu kikumbi dijuwa dye sabato.
43007023	Hona dijuwa dye sabato imunhu yakwigaligwa kikumbi, uleke dilagiso dya Musa dinghabenigwe, musuha na niye kosoko yo mumuhonya munhu umutufi wakwe wose kuwa mumi mudijuwa dye sabato?
43007024	Munghalamule kugaya gomukulanga na meso, ninga mulamule kwa kuliganisa ha kwa chawelu.
43007025	Wanhu wamonga wa Yelusalemu wejawagamba, “Ayuno so imunhu wowakuhanga kukoma?
43007026	Ayuno hano, yakulonga chila munhu yakutuhulika, na wasikulonga dyodyose ukwakwe, ikudaha kuwa fina awakulu wamanya chawelu fina yuno no Kilisito?
43007027	Ninga ichimanya ayuno koyalawile; ninga; iKilisito ma yakwija yakoneka kwechaka munhu yakiyomanya woyalawile.”
43007028	Kwa nheifo Yesu hayalonga, ugele foyendeyofundisha mudihekalu, Aniye munimanya, na mumanya konikulawa? Aniye sijile kwa kusagula kwangu nimwecho; iyanitumile ni wachawelu, naye musimumanyile.
43007029	Aniye nimumanya, kosoko nilawa ukwake, na noyanitumile.
43007030	Hawahananga kumukola, ninga hachaka munhu yagolole mikono yakwe kumukola; kosoko ichigele chakwe hachuwa chisinati chifike.
43007031	Ninga wengi wa wanhu howomwihuwila, howogamba, “Hona Kilisito yakayokoneka, kogolosa majumo mengi kusuma goyagolose imunhu yuno?”
43007032	Mafalisayo wakahulike amatewa gakulongalonga muchanhya yakwe, awatambiki wakulu na Mafalisayo, howotuma wasilikali wamukole,
43007033	Yesu, baho yagamba, “Nikwenda nuwe nayi chipisi chitali chidodogi, kameyi nikuluta kwa yuya iyatumile;
43007034	monihananga ninga musinyona, honuwile musikudaha kwija.”
43007035	Imunhu yuno yakula hoki uko kochisikudaha kumona? Yakuhananga yalute kumugawanyiko wa Wayunani mugatigati ya Wayunani na kuwafusa Wayunani?
43007036	Kena mana yaki ma yakugamba, “Monihananga ninga musinyona, na, Honyuwile niye musikudaha kwija?”
43007037	Dijuwa diya dye indumiliso dye isikukuu, dijuwa dikulu, iYesu hakema na kutula chowe yakugamba, “Imunhu yanghona nghilu yeje ukwangu
43007038	Iyakunihuwila aniye fina amatulumo fogakulonga, sisanda sa meji ga uwumi sikwende sidulike kulawa mumoyo wakwe.”
43007039	Hambiya hakalonga sino muchanhya ya Muhe, imwene awaya awakumuhuwila wakuhokela; kosoko Muhe hakowa nghenati yalafigwa kwa fiya Yesu hakowa nghenati yatunyigwe.
43007040	Wakahulike simbuli siso, wanhu wamonga wakugamba, “Ayuno chawelu no mugonesi.”
43007041	Wamonga wagamba, “Ayuno no Kilisito!” Ninga wamonga wakugamba, “iKilisito yakulawa Galilaya?”
43007042	Togoleni matulumo gasigambile fina fina iKilisito yakulawa mulukolo lwa Daudi, na kulawa Betelehemu, ikaya oyowile Daudi?
43007043	Kosoko iyo hokukuwa na mutemanuko mugati ya wanhu muchanhya yakwe.
43007044	Wamonga hawahananga kumukola ninga hechaka yagolole mikono yakwe yamukole.
43007045	Awasilikali howokuya kuwakulu wa makuhani na Mafalisayo awawagambile, Nhani musijile naye?
43007046	Awasilikali howobidula, Nghenati yalonge munhu fina yuno foyakulonga.
43007047	Mafalisayo howawabidula, Anye nanye mwagilila nheifia?
43007048	Kwina wowose mu filongosi na Mafalisayo yakumuhuwila?
43007049	Ninga ditewa dino dya wanhu awasimanyile amalagiso, waligitigwa.
43007050	Nikodemo, iyamulutile ugele ulokile, yowile yumwedu wawo, hoyowagamba,
43007051	“Togoleni, dilagiso dyetu, dikuchituma chimulamule munhu ugele chisinati chimuhulike na kifusa goni goyakugosa?”
43007052	Wejawabidula, “Agwe nagwe kulawa Galilaya? Hananga ulange mumatulumo ukwenda wowe fina mwichaka mugonesi yakwenda yalawe Galilaya.”
43007053	Chila munhu hakaluta ukaya ukwakwe.
43008001	Ninga Yesu hoyoluta kwitunda dya Miseituni.
43008002	Kukoche nhosikusiku hoyokwija kahi kudihekalu; wanhu wose hawamwijila hakakonga kuwafusa.
43008003	Awatulumi na Mafalisayo hawekwigala mwanamuke yafikililigwe muchitendo cha ugoni, hawamwika muchiligati.
43008004	Hawamugamba, “Mwalimu, imwanamuke yuno kakoligwa ugoni.”
43008005	Mumalagiso Musa kachigamba munhu wa fina yuno yatowigwe mawe, ukugambaki agweye muchanhya yakwe?
43008006	Hawalonga imbuli yo kumugesa, uleke wapate mbuli ya kumusongesela, Yesu hakafunama hakandika hasi ne chidole.
43008007	Fowagendelele kumusa maswali, hakenuka na kuwagamba, “Mugati yenu, ayuya yechaka wihi no yakonge kumukubitila diwe.”
43008008	Hakafunama kahi na kwandika hasi.
43008009	Ninga wakahulike, hawaleuka, yumweyumwe, kukongela imukulu kusuma wose, Yesu hoyosigala yemwene nayuya imwanamuke yemile kumwande yakwe.
43008010	Yesu yenula meso yamugamba, “Mwanamuke, wahoki, hachaka yakulamule?”
43008011	Hakagamba, “Hachaka mukulu.” Na Yesu yagamba, “Ani nani sikukulamula; luta, na unghagolose wihi kahi.”
43008012	Yesu hakalonga nawo kahi yakugamba Aniye no no ujelu we chilunga, wowose yanyandamila yakuwa na ujelu wo uwumi na nghakwenda yagende muchisa kahi.
43008013	Mafalisayo yamugamba, “Hambiya ukihomelela gomwecho; go ukulonga si chawelu.”
43008014	Hata, Yesu hoyobidula, Aniye nikihomelela nimwecho, uhomelesi wangu ni wa chawelu, kosoko nimanya konilawile na nimanya konikuluta ninga anyeye musimanyile kunilawile kahi konikuluta.
43008015	Mukulamula kwa kwandamila umutufi, aniye sikulamula munhu wowose.
43008016	Aniye ninghalamula, ulamusi wangu ni wachawelu, kosoko siniye nimwene nikulamula, ninga aniye na yuya yanitumile.
43008017	Mu malagiso genu itulumigwa, uhomelesi wa wanhu weli ni chawelu;
43008018	Aniye nikihomelela nimwecho, na iBaba yanitumile yakunihomelela.
43008019	Kameyi hawamugamba, “Aniye musinimanyile na Baba musimumanyile, nanga mwanimanyile niye, hamuwa mukumumanya ne Baba naye.”
43008020	Simbuli sino hakasilonge yowile mu chumba cho wakwika ifilafywa mudihekalu, ugele foyendeyofusa, hechaka munhu yamukolile, kosoko ugele wakwe hauwa ukali.
43008021	Kahi Yesu hoyowagamba, “Nikuleuka; monihananga, ninga mukufa mu uwihi wenu. Musikudaha kwija konikuluta niye.”
43008022	Kameyi Wayahudi hoyogamba Togoleni kokikoma, kosoko yakugamba, “Konikuluta musikudaha kwija?”
43008023	Hoyowagamba, “Anyeye mulawa hasi, aniyenilawa kuchanhya, anye ni we chilunga chino, aniye si chilunga chino.
43008024	Nimutamilani fina mukufa mu uwihi wenu, kosoko mukufa mu uwihi wenu munghaleka kuhuwila fina aniye no yeye.”
43008025	Howomugamba, “Agwe no nani?” Yesu hoyowagamba, “Nheifia fonimutamileni kulawa kunghonga.”
43008026	Nina mengi ga kulonga muchanhya yenu na mengi gakulamula, ninga ayuya yanitumile no wachawelu, na nikutamila kuchilunga asiya sonihulike ukwakwe.
43008027	Wasamanyile fina yakulonga nawo muchanhya ya Baba.
43008028	Baho Yesu yagamba, “Fomukwija mumwinula Mwana we munhu, noho mukamutanga fina noniye, na kahi sikugolosa mbuli yoyose kwa kwenda kwangu aniye nimwecho ninga ifene iBaba foyakufusa nofonikulonga.
43008029	Na imwene yanitumile kahamwedu nani; nghanilekile nimwene, kosoko majuwa gose nikugolosa agakumwendesa.”
43008030	Foyalongile nheifo wengi hawamuhuwila.
43008031	Kameyi Yesu hoyowalonga awaya Awayahudi awamuhuila, Munghekala mumbuli yangu, mukuwa wefusa wangu chelu,
43008032	mukwenda muimanye ichawelu nayo ikumwikani kuwa walekeligwe.
43008033	Hawamubidula, Aseye cha cheleko cha Ibulahimu, chisinati chuwe watumwa kwa munhu wowose. Ukagamba, “Nhani gweye fina mukwende mukuwa walekeleligwe?”
43008034	Yesu yawagamba, “Chawelu, chawelu, nikumutamilani chila munhu yakugolosa uwihi ni mutumwa wa wihi.
43008035	Mutumwa nghakwikala munyumba majuwa gose; imwana yakwikala majuwa gose.
43008036	Kwa nheifo imwana yanghakulekelela, ukuwa kulekeleligwa chawelu.
43008037	Nimanye fina anyeye mwa cheleko cha Ibulahimu; ninga mukuhananga kunikoma, kosoko simbuli sonikulonga sachaka luneka mugati yenu.
43008038	Nikulonga fonyonile kwa Baba, anye nanye mukugolosa fina fomuhulike kwi Baba yenu.”
43008039	Howomubidula, Ibulahimu no Baba yetu. Yesu hoyowagamba, “Nanga mu wana wa Ibulahimu, hamuwa mukugolosa foyagolose Ibulahimu,
43008040	ninga niwatamileni ichawelu chonihulike kwa Baba, achino sochonghagolose Ibulahimu.
43008041	Anye mukugolosa foyagose iBaba yenu.” Howomugamba, “Aseye chiselekigwa kwa ihabwa; china Baba yumwedu, naye ni Mulungu.”
43008042	Yesu yawagamba, “Mulungu nanga ni Baba yenu, hamuwa mukunyenda niye, kosoko nilawa uko na kwija kuno kulawa kwa Mulungu; sijile kwa kwenda kwangu nimwecho, ninga hakanituma.
43008043	Nhani musikumanya sonikulonga? Kosoko musikudaha kutegelesa na kuhokela imbuli yangu.
43008044	Anyeye ni we Baba yenu luhoma, na kwenda kwenu ni kugolosa fina foyakwenda imwene. Hakowa mukomaji kulwa kung'honga, kachaka chawelu, kosoko umwakwe mwachaka chawelu. Mayakudanha yakulonga fina foyowile imwene imwecho, kosoko imwene mudasi na Baba wa udasi.
43008045	Ninga, aniye kosoko nikulonga ichawelu, musikunihuwila.
43008046	No nani muchiligati yenu yekudaha konesa fina ni wihi? Hona nikulonga ichawelu nhani musikunihuwila?
43008047	Ayuya imwene wa Mulungu yakuhulika simbuli sa Mulungu; isoko ikuleka anyeye musikuhulika ni kosoko anyeye musi wa Mulungu.”
43008048	Wayahudi howomubidula, Togola chisikulonga sawa ma chigumba fina agweye kwa Musamalia kahi kwina mhepo?
43008049	Yesu hoyowabidula, Nachaka mhepo; nikumogoha Baba anyeye musikunyogoha niye.
43008050	Aniye sikuhananga itunyo dyangu nimwecho, kwina yumwedu iyakudihananga, noyakuwa imulamusi.
43008051	Chawelu, chawelu, nikuwatamilani, imunhu yanghaikola imbuli yangu, nghakwenda yone difa.
43008052	Kameyi Awayahudi howomugamba, “Hambiya chimanya fina kwina ipepo. Ibulahimu kafa, na wagonesi, nagwe ukugamba Imunhu yanghaikola imbuli yangu, ngahakwenda yanomole difa.
43008053	Agweye kwa mukulu kusuma iBaba yetu Ibulahimu, iyafa? Na wagonesi wafile! Ukugamba gweye fina no nani?”
43008054	Yesu yabidula, Ninghakifuna nimwecho kitunya kwangu, kwechaka dyodyose; iBabangu noyakunitunya, womukugamba fina Mulungu wenu.
43008055	Ninga musimumanyile; aniye nimumanya. Nanganigambile, simumanyile, hanuwa nikuwa mudasi fina nyeye; ninga niye nimumanya na niikola imbuli yakwe.
43008056	iBaba yenu Ibulahimu hakasekelela kosoko yokudyona dijuwa dyangu; hakadyona hoyosekelela.
43008057	Awayahudi hawamugamba, “Nghwinati ufike minyaka makumi mashano, kumona Ibulahimu?”
43008058	Yesu yawagamba, “Chawelu, chawelu, nikuwatamilani, ugele Ibulahimu nghenatiyowe, ani noniye.”
43008059	Hawadondola mawe mamukubitile; ninga Yesu hoyokifisa, hoyolawa kunje ye dihekalu.
43009001	Foyagendage, hoyomona munhu mudula kulawa kwelekigwa kwakwe.
43009002	Awefusa wakwe howomusa, Mwalimu, yatendile uwihi nani, imunhu yuno hegu awamweleke, ilekile yakwelekigwa mudula?
43009003	Yesu yawabidula, Si kosoko imunhu yuno kagola wihi, kahi si awamweleke, ninga imilimo ya Mulungu na udaha wa Mulungu woneke umwakwe.
43009004	Ichagila chigolosa imilimo yakwe iyanitumile, ugele kukali misi; ichilo chikwija, ugole uwene hachaka yakudaha kugolosa milimo.
43009005	Ugele uno wonuwile muchilunga, aniye no ujelu we chilunga.
43009006	Yakalonge nheifo hakotwa mate hasi, hakagolosa itope dya mate na kumubaka imunhu yuya mumeso na ditope,
43009007	na kumugamba, “Luta kanawe mwibwawa dya Siloamu” (nong'amba yatumigwe). Hakaluta, hakanawa hakoya yakona.
43009008	Awanhu wa habahi behi, na waya awamonage yakutasa, hawagamba, “Ayuno so munhu yakalage haya na kutasa?”
43009009	Wamonga hawagamba, “No yeye.” Wamonga hawagamba, “Hata, ninga kakifana ne imwene.” Yawagamba, “No niye.”
43009010	Hawamusa, “Ameso gako gakumukakumuka nhani?”
43009011	Yawabidula, “Imunhu yakugambigwa Yesu kagolosa itope na kunibaka mumeso na kunigamba, ‘Luta Siloamu na ukanawe.’ Ninga imunhu yuno, honiluta, honinawa honikonga kona.”
43009012	Howomugamba, “Kahoki Hoyogamba Ani simanyile.”
43009013	Howomwigala Kumafalisayo imunhu yowile mudula.
43009014	Hadyuwa ijuwa dya Sabato Yesu doyagolose ditope na kumugubula meso gakwe.
43009015	Mafalisayo howomusa kahi ifyene foyadahile kona. Yawagamba, “Kaguma itope mumeso gangu, kamei honinawa, na nikona.”
43009016	Wamonga wa Mafalisayo hawagamba, “I munhu yuno nghalawile kwa Mulungu, kosoko nghakolile Isabato.” Ninga wamonga hawagamba, “Ikudahika nhani imunhu yakugolosa wihi yagolose ijumo fina dino?” Hokuwa mutemanuko mugati yawo.
43009017	Baho Amafalisayo hawamusa kahi imunhu yuya, “Ukugambaki kosoko kakuhonya udula?” Ni mugonesi.
43009018	Awayahudi wasafumile kuwa hakowa chipofu na kuwa hakadaha kona, mpaka fowawenanga awamweleke yuya yowile mudula hambiya yakona,
43009019	na kuwosa, Ayuno ni mwana wenu, womukugamba hakelekigwa mudula? Yanhani kuwa yakona hambiya?
43009020	Awaya wamweleke hawagamba, “Chimanya seye, ayuno ni mwana wetu na fina hakelekigwa chipofu,
43009021	ninga foyakona hambiya hata seye chisimanyile, no nani yamugubule meso. Mudeni mwecho; imwene ni mukulu mugima, kokilongela imwecho.”
43009022	Awamweleke wajawalonga nheifo kosoko wejawawogoha Wayahudi, kosoko Wayahudi hawakifumilisa fina munhu yanghamufimila fina Kilisito yekuleusigwa mudisinagogi.
43009023	Kosoko iyo awaya wemeleke hawagamba, “Imwene ni mukulu mugima musene mwecho.”
43009024	Hawamwinanga kahi lwakeli ayuya imunhu yahonyigwe upofu, hawamugamba, “Mwinghe Mulungu ditunyo; ase chimanya imunhu yuno kena wihi.”
43009025	Hakabidula, “Hona yena wihi, ani simanyile, chinhu chimwedu chonimanyile, aniye hanuwa chipofu ninga hambiya nikona.”
43009026	Hawamugamba, “Hakakutendela nhani Hakagubula nhani ameso gako?”
43009027	Hoyowabidula, “Nifulusa kuwatamilani, musendile kutegelesa, Nhani mukuhananga kuhulika kahi? Anye nanyi mukuhananga kuwa wefusa wakwe?”
43009028	Howomuliga wakugamba, “Agwe no umwifusa wakwe, aseye cha wefusa wa Musa.
43009029	Chimany fina Mulungu kalonga na Musa, ninga yuno chisimanyile kayalawile!”
43009030	Imunhu hakabidula, “Nhani, Adino ni ijumo! Anyesi musimanyile koyalawile naye kanigubula meso gangu.
43009031	Chimanya fina Mulungu nghekuwahulika awena uwihi ninga imunhu iyakumwenda na kumufuga Mulungu na kugolosa foyakwenda Mulungu, Mulungu yakumuhuwila.
43009032	Hata nheifo kulawa ichilunga fochanga ilihulikigwa fina munhu wowose kagubula ameso ge munhu yelekigwe chipofu.
43009033	Hona imunhu yuno nghalawile kwa Mulungu, nghowile yakudaha chochose.”
43009034	Howomubidula, “Agwe kwelekigwa muwihi muhala, ukudaha kuchifusa seye?” Howomulafa kunje.
43009035	Yesu yakahulike fina wamulafa kunje, na yakamone yagamba, “Togola ukumuhuwila Mwana we munhu?”
43009036	Yabidula, “Naye no nani, Mukulu, uleke nimuhuwile?”
43009037	Yesu yamugamba, “Kumona, noniye nikulonga nagwe.”
43009038	Hoyogamba, “Mundewa nikuhuwila, hoyomufuga.”
43009039	Yesu yagamba, “Kosoko ya kulamula hija kuchilungu chino awaya awasikona wone na awa awakona wowe fipofu.”
43009040	Wamonga wa Mafalisayo wowile habehi hawamuhulika howomugamba, “Ase nase chafidula?”
43009041	Yesu hakawagamba, “Nanga mowile mudula musowile mukuwa na wihi;” ninga hambiya mukugamba, “Chikona uwihi wenu ukwikala.”
43010001	Chawelu, chawelu, nikuwatamilani, imunhu inghakulokela kumulango kukwingila mwidewa dye singholo, ninga yakukwilila kwingi, imunhu yo muhiji kahi muhokaji
43010002	Ninga ayuya iyakwingilila kumulango no mudimi we singholo.
43010003	Ayo mwimilisi yakumukumulila umulango; singholo sikuhulika dijwi dyakwe, na yekusinanga singholo sakwe kwa masina na yekusilafa na kusilongosa kunje.
43010004	Yanghafulusa kusilafa kunje sose isakwe, yakusilongolela, na singholo sikumwandamila, kosoko sidimanya dijwi dyakwe.
43010005	Imugeni sisikumwandamila, kahi sikumutija, kosoko sisimanyile amajwi ga wageni.
43010006	Yesu hakalonga imbasi ino, ninga wasatangile choyalongage nawo.
43010007	Yesu kahi hakawagamba, “Chawelu, chawelu, nikuwatamilani, aniye no nimulango we singholo.
43010008	Wose awanilongolele ni wahiji na wahokaji, ninga singholo sisawahulikise.
43010009	Aniye no ni mulango; wowose iyakwila kulokela ukwangu, yakwenda yahone, yakwingila na kulawa na kupata madimilo.
43010010	Imuhiji yakwija kuhija na kukoma na kubana; aniye nija uleke wowe na uwumi na wowe nawo telele.
43010011	“Aniye no nimudimi muswanu. Mudimi muswanu yakulafa uwumi wakwe kosoko ya singholo.
43010012	Munhu yakudimu kosoko yo maliho, siyo mudimi, singholo si sakwe, yakona diwusi dikwija, yakusileka singholo yakudija, diwusi dikusikola na kusagalisa.
43010013	Yakutija kosoko ni munhu wa iliho na kechaka usungu ne singholo.
43010014	Aniye no nimudimu muswanu, nisimanya singholo sangu naso sinimanya,
43010015	fina Baba foyanimanyile naniye, fonimumanyile Baba; na nikulafa uwuni wangu kosoko ya singholo.
43010016	Ninga nina ngholo singi, aso si sa ditewa dino; aso naso inyagila nisigale, naso sohulika dijwi dyangu. Kosoko yiyo kukuwa na itewa dimwedu, na mudimi yumwedu.
43010017	“Kosoko iyo iBaba yakunyenda niye, kosoko nikulafa uwumi wangu, uleke ni ulonde kahi.
43010018	Hachaka munhu yekudaha kunihoka, ninga nina udaha wa kuulafa, na kuulonda hahi; dilagiso dino nidihokela kulawa kwa Baba.”
43010019	Hagalawanisa matemanuko mugati ya Wayahudi kosoko ya simbuli siso.
43010020	Matewa hawagamba, “Kena igini, na kena chilalu; waki womukumutegelesa.”
43010021	Wamonga hawagamba, “Asino siyo nonga sa munhu yena digini, digini dikudaha kugubula meso gemudula?”
43010022	Hayuwa ijuwa nikulu dya kukumula ako Yelusalemu;
43010023	ichigele che inyota, na Yesu yendeyogenda Mwihekalu, mwikumbo dya Sulemani.
43010024	Awayahudi hawamusunguluta na kumugamba, “Kogendelela kuchidasa mpaka milaki? Nghonaga agweye no ni Kilisito chitamile unghachifisefise.”
43010025	Yesu hakawabidula, “Nimutamilani ninga musikuhuwila. Imilimo yonikugolosa mu disina dya Baba, ayo no ikunihomelela;
43010026	ninga musikuhuwila, kosoko nyeye musuwile musingholo sangu.
43010027	Singholo sangu sikuhulika dijwi dyangu, na nisimanya, isene naso sinimanya;
43010028	nani nikusingha uwumi wa majuwa gose; na sisikudaha kwagilila, na kwechaka munhu yakudaha kunihoka kulawa mumukono wangu.
43010029	iBabangu iyaninghile siso ni mukulu kusuma wose, na hachaka yakudaha kumuhoka, kulawa mumikono yakwe.
43010030	Aniye na Baba ni chinhu chimwedu.”
43010031	Awayahudi hawadondola mawe kahi uleke wamutowele nago.
43010032	Yesu hoyowabidula, “Nimonesani milimo mingi miswanu kulawa kwa Baba; kosoko ya ihoki mu yiyo yomukunitowela mawe?”
43010033	Awayahudi hawamubidula wakugamba, “Si kosoko ye milimo miswanu ikuleka chikutowa na mawe, ninga kosoko yo kutofula kosoko agweye, go wi munhu ukitenda fina kwa Mulungu.”
43010034	Yesu yawabidula, “Isitulumigwe mu malagiso genu, Hanigamba, ‘Anye mwa milungu?’
43010035	Ghonaga yawenange milungu awaya awejiligwe ne imbuli ya Mulungu na matulumo gasukudaha kubenigwa,
43010036	Mukumugamba, ‘Ayuya imwene iBaba kamusagula na kumulafa na kumutuma kuchilunga. Agweye ukutofula kosoko nigambile Aniye no ni Mwana we Mulungu?’
43010037	Nghonaga niye sikugolosa imilimo ya Baba, munghanihuwile;
43010038	Ninga hona nikuigolosa, inghowa musikunihuwila niye, ihuwileni imilimo iyecho, uleke mutange na kumanya fina, iBaba kamugati yangu na niye nuwa mugati ya Baba.”
43010039	Kahi howogesa kumukola, ninga hoyochulupuka kulawa mumikono yawo.
43010040	Hakaleuka kahi yaluta umwambu wa Yolodani ahanhu ahene Yohana Mubatisaji hakakongela kubatisa, hoyokuwa baho.
43010041	Wengi hawamwijila; hawagamba, “Yohana chawelu nghagolose ijumo dyodyose, ninga chila mbuli yoyalongile muchanhya ye munhu yuno ayuwa ya chawelu.”
43010042	Na wengi howomuhuwila.
43011001	Hambiya munhu yumonga yowa mutamu, Lasalo wa Betania, ikaya Maliamu ne dada yakwe Malita.
43011002	Ayuno no Maliamu yeja yamubaka iMundewa mafuta maswanu na kumuhamusa migulu yakwe na sinjwili sakwe, awene mukulu wawo Lasalo yowile mutamu.
43011003	Na kosoko iyo awalumbuse howokwigala mbuli, wakugamba, “Mundewa, ayuya wo ukumwenda mutamu.”
43011004	Ninga Yesu yakahulike hakagamba, “Utamu uno si wakufa; ninga ni kwa ditunyo dye Mulungu, uleke Mwana we Mulungu yatunyigwe kosoko ya uwo.”
43011005	Hambiya, Yesu hakamwenda Malita na idada yakwe na Lasalo.
43011006	Foyahulike fina hakowa mutamu, yejayekala majuwa meli ahanu bahaya hoyowile.
43011007	Hanyuma yakwe kawagamba awefusa wakwe, “Chigendeni Uyahudi kahi.”
43011008	Awefusa wakwe hawagamba, “Labi.” Wayahudi wendewohananga wakutowe na mawe luluno, ukuluta uko kahi?
43011009	Yesu hakabidula, “Sisaa sa nhemisi si kumi na mbili? Na imunhu yanghagenda nemisi ghakukobadika, kosoko yakuwona ujelu we yisi ino.
43011010	Ninga munhu wowose honayakugenda muchisa yakukobadika, kosoko ujelu umwakwe mwachaka.”
43011011	Yalonga nheifo, kameyi hakawagamba, “Imbwiyayetu Lasalo kagona, nikuluta nikamwinuse musinhongo.”
43011012	Awefusa wakwe howomugamba, “Mundewa, honayagonile nhongo kokwinuka.”
43011013	Ninga Yesu hakalonga muchanhya yo kufa kwakwe, awene hawamanya yakulonga kugona kwa kibwihisa du musinhongo.
43011014	Kamei Yesu hoyowatamila chawelu, “Lasalo kafa,
43011015	kosoko yenu nikonela fina sowile baho, uleke muchuwile. Ninga chigendeni ukwakwe.”
43011016	Tomasi iyakwinangwa ipasa, kagamba kuwefusa wayagwe, “Chigendeni naseye uleke chikafe hamwedu naye.”
43011017	Ugele foyafikile Yesu, Lasalo hakowe yasikigwe muchilalo majuwa mane.
43011018	Betania hayuwa habehi na Yelusalemu, utali wa maili mbili,
43011019	na Wayahudi wengi haweja kwa Malita na Maliamu kuwahongesa kosoko ye difa dye mundugu sawo.
43011020	Malita yakahulike fina Yesu yakwija, hoyolawa kwija muhokela, ugele Maliamu hakasigala mu nyumba.
43011021	Malita hakamugamba Yesu, “Mundewa nanga wowile baha, mundugusangu nghowile yakufa.
43011022	Ninga hata hambiya nimanya chochose choumutasa Mulungu, Mulungu yakukwingha.”
43011023	Yesu yamugamba, “I mundugusa yakwenda yenuke kahi.”
43011024	Malita hakamugamba, “Nimanya yakwenda yenuke dijuwa dyo kwina awanhu wose dyo indumo ye chilunga.”
43011025	Yesu hakamugamba, “Aniye nokwinuka wafile kahi no ni uwumi, iyakunihuwila niye yanghafa kokuwa na uwumi;
43011026	na imumi iyakunihuwila aniye nghakufa ng'oo. Ukuhuwila gonikulonga.”
43011027	Hakamugamba, “Heye, Mundewa, nikukuhuwila fina agweye no Kilisito, Mwana we Mulungu, iyakwija kuchilunga.”
43011028	Yakamale kulonga siso hoyemwinanga Maliamu chinyenele, “Mwalimu kabahano kahi yakukwinanga.”
43011029	Yakahulike nheifo hakenuka chimwandemwande hakemulutila.
43011030	Yesu hakowa nghenati yengile mukaya yawo, hakowa yenghali bahaya Malita hoyamufikile.
43011031	Awayahudi waya wowile hamwedu naye kugati, wakumuhongesa wakone Maliamu kenuka chimwandemwande, na kulawa kunje hawamwandamila, wagamba nhagela yakuluta kuchilalo yikalile ukuya.
43011032	Maliamu yakeje hoyowile Yesu yakamwone hakogwa hamigulu yakwe, yakumugamba, “Mundewa, nanga wowile baha mundugu sangu nghowile yakufa.”
43011033	Yesu yakamone yakulila na Wayahuhi wajile naye nawo wakulila, hakona usungu muchidoga chakwe na kwidasika;
43011034	Hakawagamba, “Mumwika hoki?” Hawamugamba, “Mundewa wije ulange.”
43011035	Yesu hakakonga kulila.
43011036	Awayahudi hawagamba, “Langeni, foyamwendile!”
43011037	Ninga awamonga hawagamba, “Ayuno yagubule ameso ge mudula kalemeligwa kumugolosa yuno yanghafe?”
43011038	Noho Yesu, hoyokuwa na usungu lugano kahi, hoyofika kuchilalo; hachuwa cha mhango, hachigubikigwa na diwe.
43011039	Yesu hoyogamba, “Dileuseni diwe,” Malita ilumbudye wa yuya yafile, hoyumugamba, “Mundewa kwa ugele uno kwina ibofu, kosoko kafa majuwa mane galokile.”
43011040	Yesu hoyomugamba, “Sikugambile fina unghahuwila kokona ditunyo dye Mulungu?”
43011041	Kamei howoleusa diwe, Yesu hoyokwinula meso gakwe kuchanhya hoyogamba, “Baba nikukulumba kusoko ukunihulika.
43011042	Hanimanya fina agweye ukunihulika majuwa gose, ninga nilonga sino kosoko ya wanhu wano awemile hano, uleke wahuwile fina agweye no unitumile.”
43011043	Yakamale kulonga nheifo, hakalonga kwa ijwi dikulu, “Lasalo lawa kunje!”
43011044	Imunhu yafile hakenuka imikono yakwe ne migulu yakwe yohigwe sisanda chihaga chakwe chigubikigwa na sisanda, Yesu hoyowagamba, “Mudoholeni mulekeni yalute.”
43011045	Kosoko yiyo wengi wa Wayahudi awejile hamwedu na Maliamu na wonile doyagolose, hawamuhuwila;
43011046	Ninga wamonga howoluta ku Mafalisayo, na kuwatamila foyagolose Yesu,
43011047	Baho makuhani wakulu na Mafalisayo hawakikonghola na kitang'anyila, hawagamba, “Chochikugolosa choni? Yakugolosa majumo mengi!
43011048	Chinghamuleka yagendelele nheifino, chila munhu yakwenda yamuhuwile, na Walumi wakwenda weje kuchibanila ahanhu hetu hasunhile na ditaifa dyetu!”
43011049	Ninga yumwedu wawo Kayafa yowile kuhani mukulu umwaka uya, hoyowagamba, “Anye musimanyile chochose;
43011050	musimanyile fina inogela kosoko yenu munhu yumwedu yafe kosoko ya wanhu, uleke ditaifa dyose dinghagilile.”
43011051	Nghalongile didyo kosoko ya misungu yakwe imwecho, ninga kosoko yowile mutambiki mukulu umwaka uya hakonesigwa na Mulungu fina Yesu yafe kosoko ya ditaifa,
43011052	na si kosoko ya ditaifa du lakini kuwakonghola hamwedu awana wa Mulungu awenele ako nako.
43011053	Kukongela dijuwa didyo wendewohananga njila ya kumukoma.
43011054	Kosoko iyo Yesu nghadahile kugenda yakonigwa na wanhu mugati ya Wayahudi, ninga hoyoluta kulawa iyisi iyo mpaka kubehi behi na kunyika, ku ikaya ikwinangwa Efulaimu; na hakekala uko hamwedu na wefusa wakwe.
43011055	Idijuwa dikulu dya Wayahudi dye Pasaka hadyuwa habehi, na wengi hawakwila Yelusalemu kulawa kufilunga wasunhe fidoga fyawo ugele dijuwa dye Pasaka disinati difike.
43011056	Wenda womuhananga Yesu na wakiyusa awecho kwa wecho ugele wemile mudihekalu, “Mukona nhani? Nghokwija ku sikukuu?”
43011057	Hambiya, amekuhani wakulu na Mafalisayo hawalafa malagiso hona munhu wowose yamanyile koyowile, yawatamile wamanye, uleke wamukole.
43012001	Fogasigale majuwa mutandatu kufika dijuwa dya Pasaka, Yesu hoyokwija Betania, ahowile Lasalo, imwene yenuligwe na Yesu kulawa mu difa.
43012002	Baho hawamugolosela chakudiya; Malita yendeyotogoma, na Lasalo hakuwa yumwedu wawo awekale hamesa hamwedu naye.
43012003	Maliamu hoyolonda chichupa cha mafuta ge mhungile swanu hakamubaka mumigulu ya Yesu na hamusa imigulu yakwe kwa sinjwili sakwe, na inyumba hoimema mhungile swanu ya mafuta.
43012004	Ninga, Yuda Isikalioti yumwedu wa wefusa wakwe ayuya yowile wo kumusongesa, hoyogamba,
43012005	“Nhani amafuta gano gasambasigwe kwa dinali magana madatu na kuwegha awakiwa?”
43012006	Hakalonga nhaifo, sikosoko hakowa na ubasi na wakiwa, ninga kosoko hakowa muhiji, kosoko noyowile ne chisanduku cha mapesayendeyolonda amapesa gagumagwe umo.
43012007	Yesu yagamba, “Mulekeni, yageke kosoko ya dijuwa dya masiko gangu.
43012008	Awakiwa mwenawo majuwa gose hamwedu nanye, ninga aniye musihamwedu nani majuwa gose.”
43012009	Ditewa dikulu dya Wayahudi wakamanye fina kabaho, howoluta uko, si kosoko ya Yesu du ninga wendewahanana kumona na Lasalo, yenulinuligwe na Yesu kulawa mudifa.
43012010	Kosoko awatambiki wakulu hawahananga njila ya kumukoma Lasalo,
43012011	kosoko matewa ga Wayahudi wendewoleuka ukwawo na kumulutila Yesu na kumuhuwila.
43012012	Dijuwa dya keli itewa ikulu dya wanhu awejile kusikukuu hawahulika fina Yesu yakwija Yelusalemu.
43012013	Howobena matambi ge mitende howoluta kumuhokela wakujoja, “Hosana! Kamotesigwa ayuya iyakwija mudisina dye Mundewa wa Isilaeli!”
43012014	Na Yesu iMundewa hoyolangisa dipunda didodogi, na kwikala muchanhya yakwe; fina foitulumwe,
43012015	“Unghogohe biti Sayuni; Langa; iMundewa yakwija kekala mwi mwana we dipunda.”
43012016	Awefusa wakwe wasatangile chino kunghonga; ninga Yesu yakatunyigwe, Kamei howogelegela fina haitulumigwa nheifo kosoko yakwe, fina imemelesigwa ukwakwe.
43012017	Ditewa dyowile hamwedu naye ugele foyamwinange Lasalo kulawa kuchilalo na kumwinula kulawa kuwafile howolafa uhomelesi.
43012018	Chileka amatewa galutile kumuhokela ni kosoko hawahulika fina hakagolosa ichitangilo chicho.
43012019	Amafalisayo howokigamba awecho kwa wecho, “Mukona fina anyeye musikudaha dyodyose; langeni, ichilunga chikumwandamila.”
43012020	Mu wanhu walutile Yelusalemu kufuga ugele wa sikukuu hawowa Wayunani.
43012021	Awene wawo howomulutila Filipo yalawile Betisaida ya Galilaya, wagamba, “Mukulu aseye chikuhanga kumwona Yesu.”
43012022	Filipo kejamutamila Andelea; Andelea na Filipo wejamutamila Yesu,
43012023	Yesu kawabidula kagamba, “Ugele ufika we Mwana we Munhu kutunyigwa.
43012024	Chawelu, chawelu nikumutamilani imhule ye ngano inghaleka kulagala hasi musanga na kufa, ikusigala imwene, ninga inghafa ikweleka singi nyingi.
43012025	Iyakwenda uwumi wakwe yakuwagilisa, na yuya iyekulema uwumi wakwe muchilunga chino yakuupata ku uwumi wa majuwa gose,
43012026	munhu wowose yanghanitogomela, imwagila yanyandamile; na honuwile niye, baho noho yakwenda yowe imutogomi wangu, imunhu yanghanitogemela, iBabangu yakwenda yalumbe kosoko yakwe.”
43012027	“Hambiya ichidoga changu chikwidasika nani nigambeki? ‘Baba, unihonye ne chipisi chino?’ Hata, ni kosoko iino nija kuchipisi chino.
43012028	Baba, uditunye disina dyako. Baho hodikwija dijwi kulawa kulanga, Niditunya, na nikwenda niditunye kahi.”
43012029	Matewa awemile baho hawahulika howogamba fina ididima. Wamonga howogamba, “Malaika kalonga naye.”
43012030	Yesu yabidula, “Dijwi dino dija kosoko yenu, si kosoko yangu.
43012031	Hambiya no chigele cho kulamuligwa ichilunga chino, hambiya imukulu we chilunga chino yakutagigwa kunje;
43012032	na niye ninghafulusa kwinuligwa muchanhya kulawa hasi, nikuwakwega wanhu wose ukwangu.”
43012033	Hakalonga sino konesa ni ifa dyaki dyoyakufa.
43012034	Amatewa weja wamubidula kugamba, “Chihulika mumalagiso fina Kilisito yakwikala majuwa gose. Kodaha nhani kugamba Mwana we munhu yakwenda yenuligwe kuchanhya? Ayo Mwana we munhu no nani?”
43012035	Yesu hoyowagamba, “Ujelu wa hamwedu nanye kwa chipisi chitali chidodogi. Mugende ugele mwenawo ujelu, ichisa chingheje chiwasumani, iyakugenda muchisa nghamanyile hoki koyakuluta.
43012036	Ugele mwenawo ujelu, huwileni mu ujelu, uleke muwe wana wa ujelu.” Baho Yesu yakalonge nheifo, hakaleuka hakakifisa kulawa ukwawo.
43012037	Hamwedu na majuwa gose goyagolose kumwande ya meso gawo, ninga wasamuhuwile;
43012038	hayuwa uleke imbuli yalongigwe ne mugonesi Isaya imemelesigwe: “Mundewa, nani yahuwile imbuli yetu na kwa chinani ugubuligwa umukono we Mundewa?”
43012039	Kosoko iyo wasadahile kuhuwila kosoko Isaya hakalonga kahi,
43012040	“Kawatula ameso gawo na kaigolosa imiyoyo yawo kuwa mikugutu, uleke wanghone kwa meso gawo na kona kwa miyoyo yawo, na kunibidukila niwahonye.”
43012041	Isaya hakalonga siso kosoko hanona ditunyo dyakwe hoyolonga kosoko yakwe.
43012042	Hata nheifo, wengi wa wakulu howomwihuwila, ninga kosoko ya kuwogoha Mafalisayo, wasadahile kulonga chimesomeso, uleke wanhalafigwe mumasinagogi.
43012043	Kosoko hawenda ditunyo dya wanhu kusuma ditunyo dye Mulungu.
43012044	Yesu yenula dijwi yekugamba, “Wowose yakunihuwila niya, nghakunihuwila niye du, ninga ayuya iyanitumile.
43012045	Na yakunyona niye yakumona na yuya yanitumile.
43012046	Nija kuwa ujelu we chilunga, uleke ayuya iyakunihuwila yanghasigale muchisa.
43012047	Hona kwina wowose yakuhulika simbuli sangu, na nghakusikola, aniye sikumuliganisa; kosoko sijile kuliganisa ichilunga ninga kuchihonya ichulunga.
43012048	Imwene iyakunilema niye na nghakuhokela simbuli sangu, kena mulamusi, simbuli sonilongile no sikasimuliganisa mudijuwa dye indumo.
43012049	Kosoko niye silongile kwa udaha wangu nimwecho; Baba iyanitumile kanigha dilagiso, nilonge choni na nisimulile choni.
43012050	Na nimanya fina dilagiso dyakwe ni uwumi wa majuwa gose. Kosoko iyo chonikulonga, nikulonga ifyene Baba foyanitumile.”
43013001	Hambiya dijuwa dikulu dye Pasaka fodowile disinati difike Yesu hakamanya fina ichigele chokuleuka muchilunga na kuluta kwe Baba chifika. Hakawenda awakwe wowile muchilunga, hakawenda mpaka ndumo.
43013002	Ichigele chokudiya, Ishetani yakowe kaguma muchidoga cha Yuda Isikalioti, mwana wa Simoni, kumusongesa.
43013003	Yesu yakamanye fina Baba kamwingha ifinhu fyose mumikono yakwe, na fina kalawa kwe Mulungu,
43013004	hoyokwinuka hoyekale, hakeka sisuke sakwe hanghanda, hoyokiyoha na chitambala.
43013005	Kameyi hoyogida ameji mwibakuli, hakakonga kusunha imigulu ya wefusa wakwe, na kuwahamusa ne chitambala chakwe choyakiyohile muchuno.
43013006	Hakeja kwa Simon Petulo, iPetulo hoyomugamba, “Mundewa agweye ukunisunha migulu?”
43013007	Yesu hakamubidula, “Chonikugolosa nghukudaha kumanya hambiya, ninga hanyuma ukaumanya.”
43013008	Petulo hoyomugamba, “Agweye ukwija uninashe migulu yangu nghukunasha ng'oo.” Yesu hoyomubidula, “Ninghaleka kukunasha nghumuhangi naniye.”
43013009	Simoni Petulo hoyomugamba, “Mundewa si imigulu yangu du ninga ne mikono yangu ne ditwi dyangu.”
43013010	Yesu hoyomugamba, “Iyafuluse kiyoga kechaka soko ya kiyoga kahi nanga kunawa migulu ninga musafi umutufi wose; nanye mwa wasafi, ninga si nyeye mose.”
43013011	Kosoko hakamanya no nani yakwende yamusongese; nochileka yagambile, “Anye mose musi safi.”
43013012	Yakafuluse kusunha migulu yawo, na kulonda si suke sakwe, na kwikala haukalo wakwe, hoyowagamba, “Mumanya chonigolose ukwenu?
43013013	Mukuninanga, ‘Mwalimu’ na ‘Mundewa,’ na mukulonga chelu, nofo nuwile.
43013014	Honaga aniye ni Mundewa ne Mwalimu wenu, niwanashani migulu yenu, anye nanye imwagilani kinasha migulu nyeye kwa nyeye.
43013015	Kosoko nifulusa kumonesani nanye mugolose fonimoneseni.
43013016	Chawelu lugano, nikumutamilani imutumwa si mukulu kusuma iMundewa wakwe, kahi ayuya yatumigwe si mukulu kusuma iyamutumile.
43013017	Hona munghamanya, ifinhu fino, ibeka ukwenu hona mukufigolosa.
43013018	“Sikulonga kosoko yanyeye mose; niwamanya woniwasaguleni; uleke simbuli sa Mulungu simemelesigwe, ‘Ayuya yadiyile umukate wangu kanyinulila ichisinyagilo chakwe.’
43013019	Nikumutamilani ino hambiya, ugele isinati ilawanise, uleke hona ikulawanisa, muhuwile fina aniye no nene.
43013020	Chawelu, chawelu, nikumutamilani, iyakumuhokela wowose wonikumutuma yakunihokela niye; naye yakunihokela niya yakuhokela iyanitumile niye.”
43013021	Yesu yakalonge nheifo, hoyokuwa na lwidaso muchidoga chakwe hoyohomelela, “Chawelu, chawelu nikuwatamilani, yumwedu wenu yakwenda yanisongese.”
43013022	Awefusa wakwe howokilanga, wasatangile chawelu fina yakulonga nani.
43013023	Mwifusa wakwe yumwedu, yendigwe na Yesu, hakegemila muchifa cha Yesu.
43013024	Baho Simon Petulo hoyomukonyesa, na kugamba, “Chitamile no yehoki imwene woyakulonga.”
43013025	Iyegamile muchifa cha Yesu hoyomugamba, “Mundewa, no yehoki?”
43013026	Yesu hoyobidula, “No yuya yonikwenda nimwinghe ichibendu cho mukate chonichanise mwibakuli.” Kamei yakachanise ichibendu chiya, hoyomwingha Yuda, mwana wa Simon Isikalioti.
43013027	Yakalonde ichibendu chiya, Shetani hoyomwingila, Yesu hoyomugamba, “Dyo ukuhanga kugolosa, golosa chimwande.”
43013028	Hamesa hachaka yatangile nhani yalongile nheifo ukwakwe.
43013029	Wamonga hawana nhagela kosoko Yuda noyowile ne chisanduku cha mapesa, Yesu yendeyomutuma, Kagule fyene fyochikuhananga kosoko ye sikukuu ino; Nhagela chinhu cha kuwengha wakiwa.
43013030	Kwa nheifo yakahokele ichibendu chiya, chimwande hoyolawa kunje; hachuwa chilo.
43013031	Yakaleuka, Yesu hoyogamba, “Hambiya Mwana we Mulungu yakutunyigwa, na mugati yakwe Mulungu yakutunyigwa.
43013032	Mulungu yanghatunyigwa u mwakwe, Mulungu naye yakwenda ya mutunye umwakwe imwecho, na kumutunya chimwande.
43013033	Wana wadodogi, kwa chipisi chiguhi na hamwedu nanye. Mwonihananga; fina fonalongile kuwayahudi nikulonga ukwenu nako, Konikuluta misikudaha kunyandamila.
43013034	Dilagiso disha nikumwinghani, mukiyende, fina fonimwendileni niye anye nanye mukiyende nheifo.
43013035	Munghakiyenda awanhu wose womanya fina anyeye mwa wefusa wangu.”
43013036	Simoni Petulo hoyomugamba, “Mundewa, ukwijahe?” Yesu hoyomubidula, “Konikuluta nghukudaha kunyandamila hambiya; ninga ukudaha kunyandamila hanyuma.”
43013037	Petulo hoyomugamba, “Nhani nileke kukwandamila hambiya? Nikuulafa uumi wangu kosoko yako.”
43013038	Yesu hoyomubidula, “Kolafa uumi wako kosoko yangu? Chawelu chawelu, nikukutamila, ugele dijogolo disinati dike, ukuwa unikanile kadatu.”
43014001	“Mughadasike mufidoga fyenu; muhuwileni Mulungu, nihuwileni na niye.
43014002	Munyumba ya Baba mwina fibuha fingi; nanga si nheifo hanuwa nikumutamilani fina nikamwikilani ukalo?
43014003	Ninghaluta na kumwikilani ukalo, nokwija niwalondeni chilutanye ukwangu, uleke honuwile niye anye nanye muwe baho.
43014004	Na muimanya injila yonikulutila.”
43014005	Tomasi hoyomugamba, “Mundewa chisimanyile koukuluta choimanya nhani injila?”
43014006	Yesu hoyomugamba, “Aniye no ni njila, ne chawelu no uwumi; kwachaka munhu yakwija kwa Baba inghakulokela ukwangu.
43014007	Nanga unimanyile niye hakuwa u kumumanya ne Babangu nheifiya; hambiya mumumanya na mufulusa kumona.”
43014008	Filipo hoyomugamba, “Mundewa, chonese iBaba noyochikuhananga du chokwiguta.”
43014009	Yesu hoyomugamba, “Nikala nagwe majuwa gose gano, ninga agwe hunimanyile Filipo? Iyanyonile niye kamona ne Baba; ukudaha nhani kugamba, chonese Baba
43014010	Nghukuhuwila fina aniye na mugati ya Baba na Baba kamugati yangu? Simbuli sonikulonga ukwenu sikulonga kwa udaha wangu; ninga iBaba yowile mugati yakugolosa milimo yakwe.
43014011	Huwileni, aniye na mugati ya Baba na Baba kamugati iyangu; hona si nheifo munihuwile kosoko ye milimo iyeecho.
43014012	Huwileni, huwileni nikumutamilani, imunhu iyakunihuwila imilimo yonikugolosa, niye yakwenda yagolose kahi yakudaha kugolosa mikulu kusuma ino, kosoko nikuluta kwa Baba.
43014013	Chochose chomukutasa kwe disina dyangu, nigolose, uleke iBaba yatunywigwe mu iMwana;
43014014	Munghatasa chinhu chochose mu disina dyangu nikwenda nigolose.”
43014015	“Mughanyenda, mukukola malagiso gangu.
43014016	Na nikumutasa Baba, yakwenda yamwigheni mutasi yungi, yekale nanyi majuwa gose.
43014017	No Muhe we chawelu, imwene ichilunga chino chisikudaha kumuhokela; anye mukumumanya, kosoko yakwikala hamwedu nanye na yakuwa kugati yenu.
43014018	Sikumulekani mwi wemwene; mukumwijilani.
43014019	Ninga chipisi chiguhi ichilunga chisikwenda chinyone kahi, ninga anyeye mukweda munyone; kosoko niye ni mumi, anye nanye mukuwa womi.
43014020	Dijuwa dyo, mukamumanya fina aniye nuwa mugati ya Baba ne Baba na nyeye muwa mugati yangu, na niye muwa mugati yangu, na niye mugati yenu.
43014021	Iyena malagiso gangu na kugagolosa, aye no yakunyenda, na iyakunyenda yakwenda yendigwe ne Babangu nami nikwenda nimwende na kigubula ukwakwe.”
43014022	Yuda, (si Isikalioti) hoyomugamba, “Mundewa yanhani fina ukuhananga kigubula ukwetu ninga si kuchilunga?”
43014023	Yesu hoyomubidula, na kumugamba, “Awakunyenda wakukola imbuli yangu, na iBaba yakwenda yawende, nase chikwija ukwakwo na kugolosa ukalo wetu umwawo.
43014024	Ayuya imwene inghakunyenda nghakukola simbuli sangu, na imbuli yomukuhulika si yangu ninga ni ya Baba iyanitumile.
43014025	Simbuli sino nilonga nanye, ugele nikali hamwedu nanyi.
43014026	Ninga, Imutasi, Muhe Musunhile iyekwenda yegaligwe na Baba ku disina dyangu, yakwenda yawafuse finhu fyose, na kuwagelegesa gose goniwafusile.
43014027	“Digoya nikumulekelani; digoya dyangu nikumwinghani; sifina ichilunga fochikulafa; aniye nikumwinghani fidoga fyenu finghedasike, kahi finghogohe.
43014028	Hamunihulika nikumugambani, ‘Nikuleuka, ninga nikwenda nimwijileni!’ Hona mukunyenda, nanga mukunyenda hamuwa mukusekelela, kosoko iBaba ni mukulu kusuma niye.
43014029	Na hambiya nimutamilani ugele unghali kufika, uleke maukufika muhuwile.
43014030	“Sikulonga mbuli nyingi kahi nanyeye, kosoko imukulu we chilunga chino yakwija. Kachaka udaha wowose ukwangu;
43014031	ninga nikugolosa fina iBaba foyanilagise, uleke ichilunga chimanye fina nikumwenda iBaba. Inukeni, chigendeni kuya.”
43015001	“Aniye no ni musabibu wa chawelu, na iBabangu no mulimi.
43015002	Chila inhambi idisikweleka, yakudileusa, na chila inhambi idikweleka mamudyo yakudihungulila uleke digendelele kweleka lugano.
43015003	Anyeye mufulusa kwela kosoko ye imbuli yonilongile ukwenu.
43015004	Ikaleni mugati iyangu, na niye mugani yenu. Fina dinhambi fodisikudaha kweleka diimwene, ikuhanangigwa dikale mumusabibu, anye nanye nheifo musikudaha kweleka munghaleka kwikala u mwangu.
43015005	“Aniye no ni musabibu, anyeye no mumanhambi. Iyakwikala mugati yangu, na niye mugati yakwe, no yuyo iyakweleka mamudyo mengi, kosoko munghaniswela musikudaha kugolosa chochose.
43015006	Imunhu nghona ngakwikala umwangu, yakutagigwa kunje kifana itambi na kunyala; na matambi gakulundigwa, na kukubititigwa mumoto na kusomigwa.
43015007	Munghekala umwangu, na simbuli sangu singhekala mugati yenu, taseni chochose chomukuhananga, na mukwenda mugoloseligwe.
43015008	Kwa nheifo iBaba yakutunyigwa, kosoko mukweleka mamudyo mengi, mukiyonesa chawelu fina mwa wefusa wangu.
43015009	Fina iBaba foyanyendile ani, nani nofonimwendileni; mugendelele kwikala mu wendo wangu.
43015010	Munghagakola amalagiso gangu, mwukwenda mugendelele kwikala mu wendo wangu, fina niye fonikolile amalagiso ga Baba na kwikala mu wendo wakwe.
43015011	“Simbuli sino nisilonga ukwenu uleke ichinyemi changu chuwe ukwenu, uleke ichinyemi chenu chimemelekele.
43015012	Adino no dilagiso dyangu, mukiyende fina aniye fonimwendileni anyeye.
43015013	Kwechaka wendo mukulu kusuma uno, we imunhu kulafa uwumi wakwe kosoko ya wambwiya sakwe.
43015014	Anyeye mwawambwiya sangu honaga mukugolosa fonimulagiseni.
43015015	Sikuwenanga kahi imutogomi kosoko imutogomi nghamanyile imukulu wakwe yakugolosa choni, ninga nimwinangani nyeye wambwiya sangu, kosoko gose gokunihulike kulawa kwa Baba niwatamilani.
43015016	Sinyeye mwanisagule, ninga aniye nonawasaguleni na kuwegala mulute mukeleke mamudyo na mamudyo genu gagendelele, uleke chochose chomukumutasa iBaba mudisina dyangu yamwingheni.
43015017	Dilagiso dyangu nodino, mukiyende.”
43015018	“Ichilunga chinghamusulani, mugelegele fina hachikonga kunisula niye.
43015019	Munghowa wanhu we chilunga, ichilunga chikumwendani kosoko mwawanhu wakwe. Ninga hanimusagulani kulawa muchilunga chino, anye mu si wanhu we chilunga; nochileka ichilunga chikuwasula.
43015020	Mugelegele, imbuli yonamutamileni, ‘Imutumishi si mukulu kusuma imukulu wakwe, nghonaga niye hawanisambase, womusambasani na nyeye, nghona waikolile imbuli yangu,’ wakola iyenu nayo.
43015021	Ninga wowagolosela gose gano kosoko yangu, kosoko wasimumanyile ayuya iyanitumile.
43015022	Nanga sejile nakulonga nawo, hawowa wakuwa chaka wihi; ninga hambiya wechaka chinhu cha kuwalongela, kosoko yo uwihi wawo.
43015023	Ayuya iyakunisula niye yakumusula na Baba neifia.
43015024	Nhanga gagolose muchiligati yawo imilimo yene hechaka wowose yakudaha kugolosa, wasowile wakuwa na wihi, ninga hambiya wona na wanisula niye hamwedu na Baba.
43015025	Kukumemelesa imbuli itulumigwe mwilagiso dyawo, ‘Wanisula chaka.’
43015026	“Ninga, nghona Imulolesi yakwija, wonikwenda nimwigale kulawa kwa Baba, Muhe we chawelu, iyakulawa kwa Baba, yakwenda yowe muhomelesi wangu;
43015027	anye nanye mwa wahomelesi, kosoko hamuwa hamwedu na niye kulawa kunghonga.”
43016001	“Nimutamilani sose sino uleke munghaleke dihuwi dyenu.
43016002	Wakumuwingani mumasinagogi chawelu, ichigele chikwija ichene wowose yuya yakumukomani yakona fina yakumutogomela Mulungu itunyo.
43016003	Na wakwenda wagolose nheifo kosoko wasimumanyile iBaba na niye nheifia.
43016004	Ninga nilonga sino ukwenu, ugele nomoo ukwija mugelegele fina hanimutamutamilani.” “Salongile simbuli sino kulawa kunghonga kosoko hanyuwa hamwedu nanye.
43016005	Ninga hambiya nikuluta ukwakwe iyanitumile; hechaka munhu yekunyusa, ukwijahe?
43016006	Ninga kosoko nilongile simbuli sino ukwenu, usungu umema mufidoga fyenu.
43016007	No nheifo, nikumutamilani ichawelu: Ni fiswanu kwa ulwandi ulwenu fina nikuleuka, kosoko ninghaleka kuleuka, Imulolesi nghakwija ukwenu; ninga ninghaluta nikwenda nimwigale.
43016008	Ugele woyekwija, yakuchonesa ichilunga muchanhya ya uwihi, ichawelu, na kuliganiswa.
43016009	Muchanhya ya uwihi kosoko wasanihuwile;
43016010	muchanhya ya chawelu kosoko nikuluta kwa Baba, na musikwenda munyone kahi;
43016011	muchanhya yo kuliganiswa kosoko, imukulu we chilunga chino kaliganiswa.
43016012	“Nina finhu fingi fya kulonga ukwenu, ninga musikudaha kufihokela hambiya.
43016013	Nghona iMuhe we chawelu yakwija, yakayomulongosani kuchawelu chose; nghakwenda yalonga kwa udaha wakwe imwecho, ninga sose soyakuhulika nosoyakulonga, na yakumutamilani ifinhu fikwija ugele fisinati fije.
43016014	Kanitunya niye, kosoko yakulonga ifyangu na kumutamilani nyeye.
43016015	Fose foyenafyo iBaba ni fyangu, kosoko iyo nigamba yakulonda ifyangu, na kumutamilani anyeye.”
43016016	“Chipisi chidodogi musinyona, kahi chipisi chidodogi, monyona.”
43016017	Wefusa wakwe wamonga hawakiyusa, “Choni chichi cho yakulonga ukwetu, ‘Chipisi chiguhi, monyona; na kosoko nikuluta kwa Baba?’
43016018	Hawagamba, ‘Yakulonga choni foyakugamba, chipisi chiguhi?’ Chisikumanya choyakulonga.”
43016019	Yesu hakamanya fina wakwenda wamuse; yawagamba, “Achino nochomukiyusa, fina chonikulonga choni ma nigamba chipisi chiguhi musinyona na kahi chipisi chiguhi monyona?
43016020	Chawelu chawelu nikumutamilani, molila na kuhongesa, ninga ichilunga chosekelela; mokuwa na usungu, ninga usungu wenu wobiduka kuwa chinyemi,
43016021	Imwanamuke nghonaga yakweleka, kena usungu, kosoko ichigele chakwe chifika, ninga yanghamala kweleka ichali, nghakugelegela kahi usungu uya kosoko ye chinyemi fina ichali chelekigwa muchilunga.
43016022	Kosoko mwina usungu hambiya, ninga namonani hanyuma na fidoga fyenu fokuwa na chinyemi, hachaka yakudaha kuleusa ichinyemi chenu.
43016023	Dijuwa didyo musikuwa na soko ya kusa chinhu ukwangu. Chawelu chawelu nikumutamilani munghamutasa Baba chinhu chochose mwisina dyangu komwinghani.
43016024	Mupaka hambiya musitasile chinhu chochose mudisina dyangu; taseni, mohokela, ichinyemi chenu chimeme.”
43016025	“Nilonga sino ukwenu kwa mbasi; Ichipisi chikwija, ugele uwene sikulonga nanye kwa mbasi kahi, ninga kumutamilani chimesomeso muchanhya ya Baba.
43016026	Dijuwa dyo mukamutasa mudisina dyangu na sikugamba fina nikanimutasilani kwa Baba;
43016027	kosoko iBaba imwecho yekumwendani, kosoko nyeye munyenda niye na muhuwila fina nija kulawa kwa Baba.
43016028	Hanija kulawa kwa Baba, na nija kuchilunga; kahi, nikuchileka ichilunga; na kuluta kwa Baba.”
43016029	Awefusa wakwe hawagamba, “Haa, hambiya ukulonga chimeso meso si kwa mbasi.
43016030	Hambiya chimanya fina kumanya finhu fyose, kwechaka soko ya munhu wowose kukusa, kwa nheifino chikuhuwila fina hakulawa kwe Mulungu.”
43016031	Yesu yawabidula, “Hambiya nohomukuhuwila?
43016032	Ichipisi chikwija, chawelu, chija, ugele womukwenda mukiyagale, chila munhu ukaya ukwakwe, na monileka niye nimwene; ninga, si imwene; kosoko iBaba kahamwedu nani.
43016033	Nilonga sino ukwenu, uleke umwangu muwe na digoya. Muchilunga mwina magayo; ninga musangalale aniye nichisuma ichilunga.”
43017001	Yesu yakamale kulonga simbuli siso, hoyokwinula ameso gakwe kulanga na kugamba, “Baba, ugele ufika umutunye iMwanago uleke iMwana naye yakutunye gweye,
43017002	kosoko gweye ukumwingha udaha muchanhya ya wose wene mutufi, yawenghe uwumi wa majuwa gose awaya wo umwinghile.
43017003	Na uno no uwumi wa majuwa gose, fina wakumanye gweye go Mulungu yumwedu we chawelu ne Yesu Kilisito imwene wo umutumile.
43017004	Nikutunya muchilunga, nikamale umulimo wa wanitumile nigolose;
43017005	hambiya Baba, unitunye kumwande yako na ditunyo dyonowile nadyo hamwande yako na didunyo dyonowile hamwedu nagweye ugele ichilunga chisinati chumbigwe.
43017006	“Nidigolosa disina dyako dimanyigwe wowaninghile kulawa kuchilunga. Hawowa wako, houningha niye. Wagolosa fina imbuli yako foikulonga,
43017007	na hambiya wamanya fina chila chinhu chowaninghile chikulawa ukwako.
43017008	Niwengha imbuli iya yowaninghile niye, na waihokela; wamanya chawelu nilawa ukwako, na wakuhuwila fina hakunituma.
43017009	“Nikuwatasila; sikuchitasila ichilunga ninga awaya awene wouninghile, kosoko ni wako;
43017010	awangu wose wako, na awako wangu, na nikutunyigwa mugati yawo.
43017011	Na hambiya si umuno kahi muchilunga, ninga awene wamuno muchilunga, aniye nikwija ukwako. Baba musunhile, uwakole mudisina dyako, dyouninghile uleke wowe na umwedu, kifana seye fochimwedu.
43017012	Fonowile hamwedu du nawo, haniwakola mudisina dyako dyo waninghile, niwemilila hachaka yagilile hata yumwedu nanga imwana wo kwagilila, uleke matulumo gamemelesigwe.
43017013	Ninga hambiya nikwija ukwako; na simbuli sino nikusilonga muchilunga, uleke ichinyemi changu chimemelesigwe mugati yako.
43017014	“Niwengha imbuli yako; ichilunga chiwasula kosoko awene si we chilunga, fina niye fo si we chilunga.
43017015	Sikutasa fina uwaleuse muchilunga, ninga uwemilile na yuya iyehile.
43017016	Awene si wechilunga fina niye fo si wechilunga.
43017017	Uwasunhe ne chawelu, imbuli yako no chawelu.
43017018	Fina agweye fowanitumile muchilunga, ani nani nheifiya niwatuma muchilunga.
43017019	Na kosoko yawo nikilafa nimwecho, uleke nawo wowe wakilafile muchawelu.
43017020	“Sikuwatasila awano du, ninga na awakwenda wahuwile kosoko ye imbuli yawo,
43017021	uleke wowe na umwedu, fina agweye, Baba, fowuwile mugati yangu, na niye mugati yako, awene nawo wowe mugati iyetu, uleke ichilunga chihuwile fina agweye nounitumile.
43017022	Ditunyo dyouninghile niwengha awene, uleke wowe na umwedu fina aseye fochina umwedu:
43017023	Aniye mugati yawo na agweye mugati yangu, uleke wakangale muumwedu, uleke ichilunga chimanye fina agweye kunituma na kuwenda ifyene fyo ukunyenda niye.
43017024	“Baba! Nikwenda, awaya awene wo uninghile, wowe hamwedu nani baho honyuwile, wadyone ditunyo dyangu dyo uninghile kwa uwendo wako ukwangu ugele ichilunga chisinati chumbigwe.
43017025	Baba ni wachawelu, ichilunga chisikumanyile, ninga aniye nikumanya; na wano wamanya fina hakunituma.
43017026	Niwatamila disina dyako, na nikwenda nigendelele kuwatamila, uleke uwendo uwene wo ukunyenda nawo uwe mugati yawo, na niye nuwe mugati yawo.”
43018001	Yesu yakamale kulonga simbuli siso hakaleuka na kuloka ichikolongo cha Keduloni, uko hakuwa na busitani, Yesu na wefusa wakwe howokwingila mubusitani.
43018002	Hambiya, Yuda ayuya yamusongese, hakahamanya ahanhu haya; kosoko Yesu hakasowela kuluta baho na wefusa wakwe.
43018003	Kamei Yuda hakalonda chitewa cha wasilikali, na watogomi kulawa ku makuhani wakulu, na Mafalisayo howowalutila wena na mwenje na mamuli na filama.

43018005	“Hawamubidula Yesu wa Nasaleti.” Yesu hawagamba, “No niye, Yuda, iyamusongese, hakema hamwedu nawo.”
43018006	Yakawagambe, “No niye hawoya chisengelenyuma na kugwa hasi.”

43018020	Yesu, hoyomubidula, “Nilonga ne chilunga chimesomeso, majuwa gose nifusa mumasinagogi na mudihekalu, hawakitang'anyila Wayahudi wose; Silongile chochose kwa chifiso.
43018021	Nhani ukunyusa niye? Wose awano, awanihulike, hanilonga nawo choni; wamanya hanilonga choni.”
43018022	Yakalonga nheifo, imutogomi yumonga yemile habehi naye hoyomutowa Yesu kofi na mukono wakwe, yakugamba, “Afo nofoukumubidula kuhani mukulu?”
43018023	Yesu, hoyomugamba, “Hona nilongile fibi, homelela imbuli ihile; ninga hona nilongile fiswanu, choni cho ukunitowela?”
43018024	Anasi, baho hoyomutuma yohigwe kwa Kayafa kuhani mukulu.

43019024	Howokigamba, “Chighadidege, ninga chiditowele kula, dyuwe dyani.” Hayuwa nheifo uleke Mawandiko gamemelesigwe, “Hawagawa sisuke sangu mugati yawo, na isuke yangu howoyitowela kula.”
