43021014	Auno hauwa ugele wa kadatu wa Yesu kiyonesa kuwefusa wakwe yakafuluse kwinuka kulawa kuwafile.
43021015	Wakamale kudiya chakudiya cha nhosikusiku, Yesu hoyomugamba Simoni Petulo, “Simoni mwana wa Yohana, agwe ukunyenda kusuma wano?” Hoyomugamba, “Heye, Mundewa, kumanya fina nikukwenda.” Yesu hoyomugamba, “Ufinghe chakudiya ifikolo fyangu.”
43021016	Lwakeli kahi hoyomulonga, “Simoni mwana wa Yohana, ukunyenda?” Hoyogamba, “Heye, Mundewa, kumanya fina nikukwenda.” Yesu hoyomugamba, “Dima singholo sangu.”
43021017	Hoyomulonga kahi lwakadatu, “Simoni, mwana wa Yohana, ukunyenda?” Petulo hakona usungu kosoko yalongile naye lwakadatu, “Ukunyenda?” Na hoyomugamba, “Mundewa, kumanya fina nikukwenda!” Yesu homugamba, “Usinghe singholo sangu chakudiya.
43021018	Chawelu, chawelu, nikukutamilani fowowile mujelelo, wende ukiyoha gomwecho na kuluta koukuhananga; ninga foukuwa musehe, ukwenda ugolole imikono yako na munhu yungi kohutasa na kulongosa uhunhu ko nghukwenda kuluta.”
43021019	(Hakalonga nheifo konesa ni kwa difa dya nhani doyakayomutunyila Mulungu.) Sikahele siso hoyomugamba, “Nyandamile!”
43021020	Petulo hoyobidula hoyomona imwifusa yumonga yakuwandamila, ayuya iyendigwe na Yesu, iyegamile muchifa chakwe ugele we chakudiya na yagambile, Mundewa no nani yakukusongesa?
43021021	Petulo yakamone hoyomulonga Yesu Mundewa yanhani imunhu yuno naye?
43021022	Yesu yamugamba, “Nghona nikwenda yekale mpaka ugele wonikuya inachoni ukwako? Nyandamile!”
43021023	Inonga hayenela kuwandugu fina imwifusa yuno nghakufa, ninga Yesu nghalongile nheifo ukwakwe fina nghakufa, ninga, Honaga nikwenda ayuno yakale mpaka nuye ina choni ukwako?
43021024	Ayono no mwifusa yakuhomelela simbuli sino; na chimanya fina uhomelesi wakwe ni chawelu. Kumalagisa
43021025	Ninga kwina mbuli nyingi soyagolose Yesu, kusigwa sose sandikigwe, hata Ichilunga chose sichowile chikudaha kwika ifitabu fyose fitulumwe.
44001001	Ichitabu achiya che inghonga hanichiandika Teofilo simbuli sose soyagolose na kufusa Yesu kulawa kunghonga ye milimo yakwe
44001002	hata dijuwa diya dyoyenuligwe kuluta kulanga. Ugele nghenati yenuligwe kuluta kulanga hakawalekela misigililo kwa njila ya Muhe Musunhile, awaya awatumigwa wakwe woyawasagule.
44001003	Ukwawo hakakionesa imwenyecho yemumi foyamalile amagayo gakwe kwa uhomelesi mwingi, hoyokiyonesa ukwawo kwa majuwa makumi mane na kulonga simbuli se undewa wa kulanga.
44001004	Fowowile hamwedu hakawalagisa nhafi: Munghaleuke Yelusalemu ninga mugojele achiya choyawahuwise iBaba “ichene, choyalongile”, chomuhulike kulawa ukwangu;
44001005	Kosoko Yohana hakabatisa kwa meji, ninga nyeye fogakuloka majuwa makefu, anyeye mukubatisigwa kwa Muhe Musunhile.
44001006	Awefusa, wakakitanganyile na Yesu howomusa, “Togola Mundewa ugele uno noho ukuuwisa undewa ku Isilaeli?”
44001007	Hakawagamba simulimo wenu kumanya, ugele hegu chipisi chikigwe na Baba kwa udaha wakwe imwenyecho,
44001008	Ninga mohokela ludole foyakumwijilani Muhe Musunhile muchanhya yenu nanye mokuwa wahomelesi wangu ahano Yelusalemu, Muyahudi yose na Samaliya mpaka kundumo ye chilunga.
44001009	Yakamale kulonga nheifo, fowagendelelage kulanga hakenuligwa kuluta kulanga na difunde hodimulonda mumeso gawo
44001010	Na foyakwilage kulanga hawakumhula meso gawo kulanga chimwande wanhu weli wafalile suke njelu howokwima habehi nawo
44001011	howogamba, “Anye Muwagalilaya, nhani mwimile ho mukulanga kuchanhya? Yesu yuno, iyalondigwe kulawa ukwenu kuluta kulanga, yakayokwija nheifo fomumonile yakuluta kulanga.”
44001012	Kamei hawoya Yelusalemu kulawa kwitunda dye miseituni idihabehi na Yelusalemu chitambo cha nghanyo igana nhafi;
44001013	wakengile mwikaya hawaluta kuchibuha cha kuchanya, mowekalage Petulo, Yohana, Yakobo, Andelea, Filipo na Tomaso Batolomayo na Matayo, Yakobo imwana wa Alifayo, Simoni Selote na Yuda imwana wa Yakobo.
44001014	Wose wano hawagendelela hamwedu kutasa, hamwedu na wanawake, na Maliamu ing'ina wa Yesu, na wanduguse.
44001015	Mumajuwa gago, Petulo hoyokwima muchiligati ya awandugu (wose hamwedu hawafika wanhu igana dimwedu na makumi meli), hoyogamba,
44001016	“Wandugu sangu ditulumo hayagila dimemelisigwe, idilongigwe ne Muhe Musunhile, kwa simbuli sa Daudi, hakalonga muchanhya ya Yuda iyawalongose awaya awejile kumukola Yesu;
44001017	Yuda hakowa yumwedu wetu, kosoko hakasaguligwa yowe hamwedu nase mu mulimo wetu.”
44001018	(Hambiya imunhu yuno hakagula umugunda na mapesa gaya goyapatile kulawa munhenda yakwe ihile, hoyokugwa hasi, na kutulika utumbu wakwe wose houlawa kunje.
44001019	Chila munhu mu Yelusalemu hoyohulika imbuli kwa nonga yakwe howowinanga umugunda uya Hakelidama no ng'amba, “Mugunda wa Sakame.”)
44001020	“Iwandikigwa mu chitabu cha Sabuli: ‘Uwikalo wakwe usigale mahame; Munhu wowose yanghekale umo.’ Kahi iwandikigwa, ‘Munhu yungi yalonde ahanhu hakwe haugolosaji.’
44001021	Kamei yumwedu wa wanhu awendewochandamila muugele wose iMundewa Yesu woyendeyokwingila na kulawa mugati yetu,
44001022	kukogela muubatiso wa Yohana mpaka mwijuwa dyoyalondigwe kulawa ukwetu kuluta kuchanhya yumwedu wa wanhu wawo yowe hamwedu na seye, muhomelesi wo kwinuka kwakwe.”
44001023	Baho howotambula masina ga wanhu weli wa kunghonga Yusufu iyakwinangwa Balisaba disina dyakwe dya keli Yusto, na Matiya.
44001024	Kamei, hawatasa, wakugamba, “Mundewa, gowumanyile imimoyo ya wanhu wose, chonese no yehoki woumusagule mu wano aweli,
44001025	uleke yalonde ahanhu ho umulimo na utumigwa hoyaleke Yuda na kuluta kunhu kwakwe imwenyecho.”
44001026	Howotowa kula; ikula na kumugwila Matiya naye hoyokongesigwa kulafigwa hamwedu na awaya ikumi na imwedu.
44002001	Dijuwa dye Pendekosite fodiyifikile, wose hawowa wakilundile hanhu hamwedu.
44002002	Kamei chimwande hoihulikika kifana mheho ya ludole kulawa kulanga na kumemela munyumba yose yowowekale
44002003	Kamei hagoneka kumeso gawo malilimba go moto gakigawile, na kumwikalila chila munhu.
44002004	Wose howomemesigwa Muhe Musunhile, howokonga kulonga kwa nonga ingi, ifyene iMuhe foyawenghile udaha wokulonga.
44002005	Kamei hahowa na Wayahudi wakwikala Yelusalemu wanhu wena chogoho kwe Mulungu kulawa chila itaifa hasi ya ulanga.
44002006	Dijwi didyo fodyahulikwe matewa howokitang'anyila, howokwingila itisi, kosoko chila munhu hakawahulika wakulonga mu nonga yakwe imwecho.
44002007	Howokisina na kujuma wakugamba, “Awa wose wochikuhulika wakulonga nheifino si Wagalilaya?
44002008	Ya nhani, hambiya, chila yumwedu wetu yakuwahulika wakulonga kunonga yakwe imwecho?
44002009	Wamonga wetu ni Wapalitiya, Wamedi na Waelamu; wamonga wakaya wa Mesopotamiya, Uyahudi, Kapadokia, Pondo na Asiya,
44002010	Filigiya na Pamufiliya, Misili na ulwandi lwa Libiya habehi na Kilene; Wamonga wetu ni wageni kulawa Loma.
44002011	Wayahudi na wanhu wabidukile idini ye Chiyahudi na wamonga walawa Kilete na Alabiya ase chose chikuwahulika wakulonga ku nonga setu chiwecho mbuli ghulu sa Mulungu.”
44002012	Wose howokisina na kogoha, ukuno wakiyusa, “Ayi nayo yoni?”
44002013	Ninga awamonga hawogelela wakugamba, “Awanhu wano wonywa difai nyisha.”
44002014	Ninga Petulo hoyokwima hamwedu na waya ikumi na yumwedu, hoyokwinula dijwi dyakwe hoyokonga kulonga: “Wandugu sangu Wayahudi, na nyeye mose mukwikala hano Yelusalemu; munitegelese fonikulonga simbuli sangu.
44002015	Awanhu wano wasilewile, fina fomukudoga, kosoko digaluka isaa dya kadatu du dye dijuwa;
44002016	ichawelu ni kugamba imbuli ino no iya yoyalongile imugonesi Yoeli:
44002017	‘Mumajuwa go kundumo, yakulonga iMundewa, nikuwetilila awanhu wose Muhe wangu. Awana wenu we chigosi na we chike wakwenda walafe ugonesi, na wajelelo wenu wokona magubulo na wasehe wenu walota njosi.
44002018	Heye, na awatogomi wana we chigosi na we chike nokuwetilila Muhe wangu majuwa gago nawo wakwenda walafe ugonesi.
44002019	Nogolosa majumo kwichanhya mulanga na chitangilo hasi muchilunga, Kukuwa na sakame, moto na mosi musito;
44002020	dijuwa dyokugumigwa chisa, umwesi ukuwa mudunghu kifana sakame, ugele disinati difike, adiya dijuwa dikulu dye ditunyo dye Mundewa.
44002021	Baho, wowose iyakwinanga kwe disina dye Mundewa, yakuhonyigwa.’
44002022	“Anye Waislaeli mutegelese simbuli sino! Yesu wa Nasaleti, imunhu imwene udaha wakwe we chilungu hawoneka ukwenu kwa njila ya majumo, gokwisina na ifitangilo foyagolose Mulungu mugati yenu kwa njila yakwe fina fomumanyile.
44002023	Imunhu yuno hakalafigwa kwandamila iMulungu imwecho foyadumula mbuli kulawakatali, na kwa kumanya kwakwe, kuwa Yesu kogumigwa kumikono yenu nanye homumuguma mumiko ya wanhu wihile howomutungika na kumukoma
44002024	imwene, Mulungu kamwinula kulawa mudifa, hoyoudohola, usungu we difa, isadahile yakoligwe nawo.
44002025	Kosoko iDaudi yakutambula simbuli soko ye imwene, Hanimona iMundewa kumwande yangu majuwa gose, kosoko kowa ulwandi iwo mukono wangu wo kulume ninghasingisike.
44002026	Kosoko iyo umoyo wangu houkwendeswa dilimi dyangu hodisekelela; kamei umutufu wangu haukwikala mudihuwi.
44002027	Kosoko nghukuchileka ichidoga changu kusimu, nghukumulafa imusunhile wako yone kukubanika.
44002028	Kunyonesa injila ya uwumi kuwakwako hamwedu naniye kanimemesa chinyemi.
44002029	“Wandugu sangu nikumutamilani muchawelu ku iBaba yetu Daudi. Yejayafa, hoyosikigwa, na ichilalo chakwe chabahano ahetu mpaka diyelo nhafi.
44002030	Ninga kosoko Daudi yowile mugonesi, hakamanya kuwa Mulungu hakimulahila fina yakwenda yumwedu we cheleko chakwe kuwa Mundewa ahanhu hakwe.
44002031	Daudi hakona katali Mulungu cho yakwenda yagolose kosoko iyo hoyolonga muchanhya ya kwinuka mwichilalo kwa Kilisito, ugele foyagambile: Nghalekigwe kusimu, umutufi wakwe usadodile.
44002032	Mulungu hakamwinula muchilalo yuyo Yesu ase chose cha wahomelesi we imbuli yo.
44002033	Yesu yakafuluse kwinuligwa na kwikigwa na Mulungu ulwandi lwakwe lwo kulume, hoyohokela kulawa kwa Baba ayuya Muhe Musunhile, imwene woyachihuwise, kachitilila yuyo Muhe, acho nocho mukona hambiya na kuhulika.
44002034	Kosoko Daudi mwecho, ghakwilile mpaka kulanga; ninga imwene hakagamba: ‘Mundewa hakamulonga Mundewa, Ikala ulwandi lwo kulume kwangu
44002035	mpaka niwagolose awanghondo wako wowe hasi ya migulu yako.’
44002036	Wanhu wose wa nyumba ya Isilaeli inogela wamanye kwa chawelu ayo Yesu womwamutungike, no yuyo, Mulungu woyamugolose fina Mundewa na Kilisito.”
44002037	Wakahulike simbuli siso howotamigwa mumoyo yawo, howomusa Petulo na waya awatumigwa wamonga, “Aho chitende nhani wandugu setu?”
44002038	Petulo hoyobidula, “Mulambe na chila munhu yumwe yumwe yabatisigwe mu disina dya Yesu Kilisito, uleke muleusiligwe uwihi wenu na kuhokela ichinghwa che Muhe Musunhile.
44002039	Kosoko dihuwiso dino hadyuwa kosoko yenu na kosoko ya wana wenu kosoko ya wose wowile kutali na kosoko ya chila munhu imwene Mundewa Mulungu wetu yakumwinanga ukwakwe.”
44002040	Na kwa mbuli nyingi du Petulo hoyolonga kwa ludole na kuwasongesa wanhu yakugamba, “Mukihonye ne cheleko chino cha uwihi.”
44002041	Wengi howosifumila simbuli sakwe, howobatisigwa. Awanhu wafikile figulu fidatu howokongeseka muchitewa chiya dijuwa dyo.
44002042	Awa wose howogendelela kifusa kulawa kuwatumigwa, kwikala hamwedu chindugu, kumega mukate na kutasa.
44002043	Chila munhu hakengiligwa itisi, kosoko ya fitangilo na majumo mengi gagoloseke na watumigwa.
44002044	Na wose wahuwile hawowa hamwedu na kuwa ne finhu fyose muhangi.
44002045	Howokwambasa isimali sawo ne finu fyawo kamei howogawa ifesa kwandamila chila munhu foyakuhanga.
44002046	Na chila ijuwa hawagendelela kitang'anyila mwihekalu kwa moyo umwedu na mega umukate musinyumba sawo, wakudiya chakudiya chawo kwa chinyemi na kwa moyo mujelu,
44002047	howomutogola Mulungu, howokwendigwa na wanhu wose. Chila ijuwa iMundewa hoyokongesa dikanisa kwa waya awendile kuhonyigwa.
44003001	Dijuwa dimonga wugele we saa ya dikenda ya nhemisi, Petulo na Yohana wendewoluta kwihekalu, ichigele cho kufuga.
44003002	Ugele wuwo awanhu hawamwinula munhu imwene nghenati yagende kulawa kwelekigwa kwakwe. Awanhu wawo wendewomwinula na kumwika hamulango ukwinangigwa, “Mulango Muswanu,” uleke yatase chokwinghwa na awaya awakwingila kwihekalu.
44003003	Yakawone Petulo na Yohana wakowe wakwingila mwihekalu, hoyowatasa wamwinghe chinhu chochose chiya.
44003004	Howomukumhulila meso, kamei, Petulo hoyogamba, “Chilange seye!”
44003005	Kamei hoyowalanga yakuhuwila kuhokela chinhu kulawa ukwawo.
44003006	Ninga Petulo hoyomugamba, “Nachaka mapesa hegu sahabu, ninga nikukwingha choninacho: Mwisina dya Yesu wa Nasaleti nikukugamba winuke na kugenda!”
44003007	Kamei hoyomukola umukono wokulume hoyomutasa kwinuka. Chimwande imugulu yakwe na simwegele sakwe hosikuwa na ludole;
44003008	hoyojumha, na kwima kwa mimigulu yakwe, hoyokonga kugenda yakusunguluta. Kamei hoyokwingila mwihekalu hamwedu nawo, yakugenda na kujumha na kumutunya Mulungu.
44003009	Awanhu baho howomwona yakugenda na kumutunya Mulungu,
44003010	wakamutange fina no yuya imutasaji yekalage ha Mulango Muswanu, wose howokisina lugano ku chinhu chigoloseke ukwakwe.
44003011	Ugele foyendeyowandamila Petulo na Yohana, wanhu wose howokikonghola howobilima kudikumbo idikwinangwa Dikumbo dya Sulemani. Wakisina lugano.
44003012	Kamei Petulo yakone nheifo hoyowabidula awanhu waya, Anyeye Waislael, nhani mukuching'olela meso aseye, kifana aseye chimugolosa ayuno yagende kwa udaha wetu seye?
44003013	Mulungu wa Ibulahimu na wa Isaka na wa Yakobo, wa waBaba setu, kumutunya imutumishi wakwe Yesu imwene anyeye hamumutungika na kumukana kumwande ya Pilato, ugele foyalafile ulamusi wakwe fina yadoholeligwe.
44003014	Ninga anyeye homumukana ayuya Imusunhile, ayuya Imuswamu; homuhananga mwinghigwe imukomaji;
44003015	Homumukoma ayuya imukulu wa uwumi, imwene yenuligwe na Mulungu kulawa mu wafile; na seye na chiwahomelesi wakwe
44003016	ku disina dyakwe, kwa kudihuwila disina dyakwe, dimugolosa imunhu ayuno wo mukumona womumumanyile, na kwa dihuwi didyo duwile umwakwe imwene, dimwingha ayuno uwumi umemelekele kumwande ya meso genu anyeye mose.
44003017	Ninga hambiya wandugusangu, nimanya fina hamugolosa nheifo kosoko musamanyile fina na wakulu wenu fowatendile.
44003018	Ninga agaya iMulungu goyalongile kulawa katali kwa milomo ya wagonesi wakwe wose, fina Kilisito yakwija yadumangisigwa kagamemelesa naifo.
44003019	Hambiya, mulambe na kumubiduchila Mulungu, uleke uwihi wenu uleusigwe, wije ugele wo kuhola mufidoga,
44003020	kulawa kwa Mundewa, yekumutuma Kilisito Yesu womwikiligwe kulawa katali;
44003021	imwene hayagila kuhokeligwa kulanga na kuwa uko mpaka ifinhu fyose fogolosigwe usha fina foyalongile Mulungu kwi milomo ya wagonesi wakwe kulawa katali.
44003022	Kosoko Musa hakagamba Mundewa iMulungu wenu yakumwigalilani mugonesi, fina foyanigale niye, naye yakuwa yumwedu wa wanhu awenu muwecho: Iwagila mwandamile chila choyakulonga mugolose.
44003023	Imunhu wowose inghakumuhulikisa foyakulonga yakubaguligwa na wanhu wa Mulungu na kubanigwa.
44003024	Awagonesi wose, kukongela Samweli na waya wamwandamile hawalonga simbuli sino isene sikugoloseka majuwa gano.
44003025	Amahuwiso kwa njila ya wagonesi ni kosoko yenu, na mukuhangila dilagano iMulungu dyoyagolose na wakuku senu, fina foyamutamila Ibulahimu. Kunjila ye cheleko chako, ifyeleko fyose fye chilunga fyomotesigwa.
44003026	iMulungu kamwinula kulawa mudifa imutogomi wakwe, mbuli swanu kosoko yenu, kunghonga, hoyomutuma yamwigalile imboto kwa kumugolosa chila yumwedu wenu yabiduke kulawa kuwihi
44004001	Petulo na Yohana fowalongage na wanhu, watambiki ne chilongosi we dihekalu na Masadukayo hawawejila,
44004002	wadeseke kosoko wendewowafusa wanhu na kuhubili fina mu Yesu awafile wakwija wokwinuligwa kulawa mu difa.
44004003	Howowakola, howowaguma mwigelesa mpaka nhosiku yakwe nhosikusiku, kosoko hauwa ugele wa hegulo.
44004004	Ninga wengi mu waya awahulike iyo imbuli howohuwila; mu wawo wahuwile wakudaha kuwa figulu fishano.
44004005	Nhosiku yakwe, wakulu na wasehe na watulumi howokitang'anyila Yelusalemu,
44004006	hamwedu na Mutambiki Mukulu Anasi na Kayafa, na Yohana na Isikanda, na wose wose waya awene howawa wo lukolo lwa kuhani Mukulu.
44004007	Kamei hawaweka hagati yawo, na kuwosahowowosa Kwa ludole lwaki ama kwa isina dyake mugolosa dino?
44004008	Kamei Petulo yakameme Muhe Musunhile, hoyowagamba Anyeye Filongosi na wasehe wa wanhu:
44004009	Hona chikusigwa diyelo mu ichitendo ichiswamu choyagoloseligwe ayuya ichiwete yahonyigwe na kuwa mumi,
44004010	imanyike ukwenu nyeye wose, na kwa wanhu wose wa Isilaelii, fina imunhu yuno kama kumwande yenu diyelo, mumi, telele, kwa udaha wa disina dya Yesu wa Nasaleti imwene anyeye hamumutungika, ninga Mulungu kamwinula kulawa mudifa.
44004011	Ayuno no yakulongigwa na Matulumo Masunhile fina Isumbi yomulemile nyeye mukujenga, hambiya igaluka sumbi nghulu ye nghindiso.
44004012	Kwachaka uhonya kwa yeyose yuya, kosoko kwachaka isina dyodyose hasi ya ulanga, dyowenghigwe awanhu dikuchagila kuhonyigwa nadyo aseye.
44004013	Wakone ing'inyo ya Petulo na Yohana na kumanya fina hawowa wanhu wachaka chisomo, howomanya fina hawowa na Yesu.
44004014	Ninga wakamwone yuya imunhu yahonyigwe kema hamwedu nawo howoswela mbuli ya kulonga
44004015	baho, howowagamba walawe kunje ya ibalasa, awene howosigala kugati wakusimulila kwa Chifiso.
44004016	Howokiyusa Chitende nhani na awanhu wano? Kosoko ijumo ikulu digolosigwa kwa njila yawo na dimanyikana na wanhu wose wa Yelusalemu, chisikudaha kuikana imbuli ino.
44004017	Ninga uleke imbuli ino inghagendelele kwenela kuwanhu, chiwagambe wanghalonge na munhu wowose kudisina dya Yesu.
44004018	Howowenanga kahi kugati howowelagisa wanghalonge kahi kahiwanghafuse wanhu kwa disina dya Yesu.
44004019	Ninga Petulo na Yohana howowabidula, Mulamule anyeye muwecho, hona ni fiswamu kumwande ya Mulungu kuwahulikisa anyeye kusuma Mulungu.
44004020	Kosoko chisikudaha kuleka kulonga simbuli so chonile na kuhulika.
44004021	Kamei wakawagume chogoho na kuwagombela, howowalekelela. Howolemeligwa kuwatenda chinhu kosoko awanhu wose wendewomutunya Mulungu kosoko ya didyo dya goloseke.
44004022	Imunhu yuyo yagoloseligwe dijumo didyo dyokuhonyigwa hakowa mukulu mugima yena minyaka kujumha makumi mane.
44004023	Chimwande, fowalekeligwe, Petulo na Yohana howokuya kuwayawo, howowatamila agaya gowalongigwe na watambiki wakulu na wasehe.
44004024	Wakahulike simbuli so, Howomwinulila Mulungu majwi gawo kwa moyo umwedu, wakugamba, “Mundewa Mukulu, agweye no Mulungu wumbile ulanga ne iisi, ne bahali na fyose fuwile umo;
44004025	nagwe hakulonga kwa mulomo we mutogomi wako Baba yetu Daudi, kwa udaha wa Muhe Musunhile: ‘Nhani awamembe wakugolosa ukali Na makabila gakudoga hechaka chinhu?
44004026	Na wandewa we chilunga wakiika fiswanu, uleke wamuleme Mundewa na Masiha wakwe.’
44004027	“Kosoko chawelu nofyo Helode, Pontio Pilato, na wanhu wa Isilaeli na wanhu wa wamembe fowakitang'anyile bahano mukaya iino, kumulema imutogomi wako musunhile Yesu, imwene wowamugumile mafuta,
44004028	uleke wagolose gose agene umukono wako na kwenda kwako kulawa hatali hakuhananga gagoloseke.
44004029	Hambiya, Mundewa ulange kogohesa kwawo, uwenghe awatumwa wako kuilonga imbuli yako kwa ludole;
44004030	golola umukono wako kuhonya, fitangilo na majumo gagoloseke ku disina dya Mutumishi wako musunhile Yesu.”
44004031	Wakamale kumutasa Mulungu, ahanhu haya howakitang'anyile hohosingisika wose howomemesigwa na Muhe Musunhile, howolonga imbuli ya Mulungu kwa ludole.
44004032	Na awanhu awahuwile hawowa na moyo umwedu na chidoga chimwedu; hachaka munhu wowose yagambile fina ichinhu chochose cho yenacho ni mali yakwe imwecho; ninga hawowa ne finhu fyose muhangi;
44004033	awatumigwa howolafa uhomelesi wa kwinuka kwakwe Yesu kulafa mudifa kwa ludole lukulu, na dihewa ikulu hadyuwa hamwedu nawo wose.
44004034	Kusowile na munhu mugati yawo yowile kachaka chinhu choyakuhanga, kosoko awanhu wose wowile na fiwanja ama nyumba wawafyambasa, howokwigala diyombe dye finhu fiya fyo fyaguligwe,
44004035	howofika hamigulu ya watumigwa; chila munhu hoyogawiligwa fina foyakuhanga.
44004036	Na Yusufu iyenangigwe na watumigwa Balinaba (nong'amba: Mwana wa usindamafu, “Mulawi, nghonga yakwe ni munhu wa kupono”).
44004037	Hokowa na mugunda houguligwa, hoyokwigala ifesa yose, hoyoika hamigulu ya watumigwa.
44005001	Ninga munhu yumonga hamwedu ne muke Safila howousa umugunda.
44005002	Hoyofisa isehemu ye fesa ilawile mumugunda kwa chifiso, imuke naye hakamanya, hayokwika sehemu ndodogi na kwiigala hamigulu ya watumigwa.
44005003	Petulo hogamba, “Anania nhani Ishetani yamemese umoyo wako, kumutamila udasi Muhe Musunhile? Na kufisa isehemu ya imali ilawile mumugunda?
44005004	Fowowile ukwako usowile wako? Na chikamale kuguligwa imali yakwe isowile mu udaha wako? Hayuwa yuwa nhani noho wike imbuli iino muchidoga chako? Nghumudanhilise munhu, ninga Mulungu.”
44005005	Anania yakahulike simbuli sino hoyokugwa hasi, hoyokufa. Chogoho chikulu hochiwapata awanhu wose awahulike simbuli sino.
44005006	Awanike howoleuka, howomuguma mu sisanda howeja musika.
44005007	Chipisi cha saa ndatu hanyuma yakwe, imuke naye hoyokwingila, na hamanyile dyodyose muchanhya ya simbuli silokile.
44005008	Petulo hoyomubidula yakumugamba, “Nitamile, hamuusa umugunda kwa diliho didyo?” Hoyogamba, “Heye, kwa diliho didyo.”
44005009	Hayuwa nhani mulagane kumugesa Muhe Musunhile we Mundewa? Langa, imugulu yawo wamusikile imugosi wako yuwa hamulango, nawo wakwenda wakulonde agwe nagwe.
44005010	Chimwande hoyokugwa hamigulu yakwe hoyokufa. Awaya awanike howokwingila howomufika yafile, howomulafa kunje, howomusika hamwedu na mulume.
44005011	Chogoho chikulu hochiwengila, dikanisa dyose na wanhu wose awahulike simbuli siya.
44005012	Kwa mikono ya Watumigwa hogogoloseka mengi ga majumo na kisina muchiligati cha wanhu. Awahuwile hawekala hamwedu mwikumbo dya Sulemani.
44005013	Hechaka munhu yungi wowose imwene inghahuwile yadahile kihasa nawo, ninga awaya du awawatunyage.
44005014	Kamei awamuhuwile iMundewa wagosi kwa wanawake hawongeseka lugano.
44005015	Kamei hawawenula awatamu hata awoile musikaya, kamei na kuwagonesa musinghingo na mumikeka, uleke dinyefu dya Petulo diwogwile awamonga ichigele foyalokage.
44005016	Na wanhu wa sikaya sa munghanda ya Yelusalemu howokikonghola, wakwigala watamu, na wendewokwidasigwa na simhepo sihile na wose howohonyigwa.
44005017	Kamei Imutambiki mukulu na wose wowile hamwedu naye, (awo no wamasehebu ga Mafalisayo), wamema wifu.
44005018	Howowakola watumigwa howowaguma imwigelesa.
44005019	Ninga imusungula we Mundewa hoyokumula umulango wa digelesa nechilo, hoyowalafa, hoyogamba,
44005020	“Luteni mukeme mwi hakalu na kuwatamila awanhu si mbuli sa uumi uno.”
44005021	Nawo wakahulike howoluta nhosikusiku kwihekalu, howokonga kufusa. Hoyokwija Ikuhani Mukulu na waya wowile hamwedu naye, howowakusanya awanhu wa dibalasa, na wasehe wose wa Isilaeli, howotuma wanhu kwigelesa wakawalonde.
44005022	Ninga awatogomi waya fowafikile wasawonile kwigelesa, howokuya howowatamila,
44005023	wakugamba Digelesa chifika dihindigwe fiswanu, na awemilisi wema kumwande ye milango, ninga chikakumule chisonile munhu kugati!
44005024	Kamei ichilongosi we dihekalu na wakulu wa watambiki wakahulike nheifo, howokwila manhonge kosoko yawo, imbuli ino yokuwa nhani.
44005025	Munhu yumonga hoyokwija hoyowatamila fina, awanhu waya womwawekile kwigelesa wowa kwihekalu, wemanyima wekufundisha wanhu.
44005026	Noho yuya ichilongosi we dihekalu hoyoluta hamwedu na watogomi waya, howowegala, ninga si kwa ludole, kosoko hawogoha wanhu wangheje wowatowa na mawe.
44005027	Wakawegale, howoweka mudibalasa. Ikuhani Mukulu hoyowosa,
44005028	yakugamba, “Togoleni, chisawagambile kwa udaha kuwa munghafuse kusisina dino?” Nanye langeni mumemesa Yelusalemu na mafuso genu, na mukuhananga kuigala isakame ye munhu yuya muchanhya yetu.
44005029	Petulo na watumigwa howobidula wakugamba, “Ichagila kumuhulikisa Mulungu kusuma wanhu.
44005030	Imulungu wa WaBabaset hakamwinula Yesu kulawa muchilalo, imwene anyeye hamumukoma kwa kumutungika mwibiki.
44005031	Imunhu yuno iMulungu kamwinula kumukono wakwe wo kulume yowe Chilongosi na Muhonya yawenghe wa Isilaeli dilumbo dya chawelu na kulekeligwa uwihi.
44005032	Na seye cha wahomelesi wa simbuli siso, hamwedu na Muhe Musunhile imwene Imulungu yakuwengha awanhu wose awakumuhulika.”
44005033	Awene wakahulike howokwafigwa mufidoga fyawo; howogola njama yakuwakoma.
44005034	Ninga munhu yomonga, Falisayo, Gamalieli, mwalimu wa tolati, yakogohigwa na wanhu wose, hoyokwima mwibalasa, na kulagisa watumigwa wekale hanghanda kwa chipisi chiguhi,
44005035	hoyowagamba, “Anye wagosi wa Isilaelii, muchilangisise fomukuwatendela awanhu wano.
44005036	Kosoko ugele wawo fowowile usinati ufike hakalawanisa Teuda, hokigamba imwene munhu mukulu, wanhu wafikile magana mane howomwandamila. Naye hakachinjigwa na wose awamuhuwile howokwaganika howokuwa si chinhu.
44005037	Hanyuma yakwe hoyolawanisa Yuda wa Mugalilaya, ugele uya wokutala wanhu, hoyowakwega wanhu wengi howomwandamila, naye hoyokwagilila na wose wamwandamile howokwaganika.
44005038	“Hambiya, nikumugambani nhafi, Mukinege na wanhu wano, walekeni; kosoko imbuli iino no mulimo uno hona ulawile kuwanhu, ukwenda ubanike uwecho,
44005039	ninga hona ulawile kwa Mulungu musikudaha kuubana; mungheje mukoneka fina mukulewa na Mulungu.
44005040	Howofumila simbuli sakwe; kamei wakawenange awatumigwa, howowatowa, howowalemesa, wanghalonge ku disina dya Yesu; kamei howowaleka ku disina dya Yesu; kamei howowaleka walute.
44005041	Nawo hawaleuka mwibalasa diya, na chinyemi, kosoko watalikwa, kugumigwa chinyala, kosoko ya disina didyo.
44005042	Na chila ijuwa, mwihekalu na musinyumba sawo, wasalekile kufundisha na kuhubili si mbuli si swanu sa Yesu kuwa ni Kilisito.”
44006001	Hambiya mumajuwa gago, chigele awefusa fowendewakongeseka, hakulawanisa kung'ung'ulika mugati ya waya wakulonga Chiyunani na waya wakulonga Chiebulaniya. Awaya wakulonga Chiyunani howonghunghulika fina awegane wao wendewosimiligwa ugele wokugawiligwa amahitaji gawo ga chila ijuwa.
44006002	Kosoko iyo, awaya awatumigwa ikumi na weli howokwinanga mulundo wa wanhu wose awahuwile howogamba, “Si fiswanu aseye chileke kuhubili imbuli ya Mulungu, uleke chishugulikie kugawa amahitaji.
44006003	Kosoko iyo, wandugu setu, saguleni wanhu mufungate, awakoneka wanhu waswanu, wamemile Muhe na misungu, uleke chiwenghe u mulimo uwo.
44006004	Ninga, aseye, chuwe no mulimo wa mataso na kuhubili imbuli ya Mulungu.”
44006005	Imbuli ino hoiwendesa ditewa dyose, kamei howowasagula Sitefano, munhu yena ihuwi ikulu na yamemesigwe na Muhe Musunhile, Filipo, Polokoni, Nikanola, Timona, Palimena na Nikolao wa Andiyokiya imwene yabidukile idini ye Chiyahudi kunghonga.
44006006	Howoweka kumwande ye watumigwa, nawo howowatasila na kuwechila mikono.
44006007	Imbuli ya Mulungu hoigendelela kongeseka na matewa ga wanhu awahuwile ako Yelusalemu hoikongeseka lugano, na matewa makulu ga watambiki howohuwila.
44006008	Kamei hoyomwingha Sitefano yamemile ihewa ikulu na ludole, hoyomwigha udaha mwingi; hoyodaha kugolosa fitangilo na majumo mugati ya wanhu.
44006009	Ninga wanhu wamonga awoile we disinagogi dya walekeleligwe fina fodyenangwa, wakilene, Walekisandaliya, na wamonga kulawa Kilikiya na Asiya, hawema na kuwanga na Sitefano.
44006010	Ninga wasadahile kumusuma kosoko ye misungu yakwe na Muhe yamulongose kukulanga.
44006011	Kosoko iyo howowafupa wanhu Awagambile chimuhulika imunhu yuno yakulonga mbuli sa kumuliga Musa na Mulungu.
44006012	Howowasongesa awanhu na wasehe na watulumi, howomulutila, howomukola, howomwigala kwibalasa.
44006013	Howokwinula wahomelesi wa udasi wagambile, Munhu yuno ghakuleka kulonga simbuli si kubesa ahanhu hano hasunhile na malagiso ga Musa.
44006014	Kosoko chimuhulika yakugamba ayo iYesu wa Nasaleti yakwenda yahabane lugano ahanhu ahano na kugaleusa ijadi yetu yochinghigwe kulawa kwa Musa
44006015	Wose wowile mumulundo uya we dibalasa howomukumhulila amaso Sitefano, howokona ichihanga chakwe kifana chihanga cha malaika.
44007001	Kamei imutambiki mukulu hoyomusa, Togola simbuli sino ni chawelu?
44007002	Naye Sitefano hoyogamba, “Wandugu sangu na waBaba sangu munitegelese! Mulungu hakailawanisa kwi Baba yetu Abulahamu foyowile kuya Mesopotamiya ugele ghenati yakekale Halani.
44007003	iMulungu hoyomugamba, ‘Leuka muisi yako, waleke awanhu wo lukolo lwako, ulute ku isi yonikwenda nikonese.’
44007004	Kosoko iyo Abulahamu hoyosama iisi ya kalidayo, hoyejakwikala Halani. iBabakwe yakafe. Mulungu hoyomuleusa kahi Halani hoyokwija na kwikala mu isi ino yomukwikala hambiya.
44007005	iMulungu nghamwinghile hata uhasi we iisi ino hata nghanyo imwedu uwe mali yakwe; hata nheifo, hoyomuhuwisa fina yakwenda yamwinghe iisi ino yuwe yakwe ne cheleko chakwe, hata fina ugele uwo hakowa chaka mwana.
44007006	Mulungu hakalonga nhafi: ‘Icheleko chako wakwigaligwa ku isi ukutawaligwa na wanhu wengi, na uko wakagolosigwa watumwa, na kugoloseligwa fihile, kwa minyaka magana mane.
44007007	Ninga niye nikuhananga nidiliganise ditaifa didyo dikuwagolosani watumwa. Kamei nikwenda niwaleuse mu isi iyo uleke weje wanifuge ahanhu ahano.’
44007008	Hanyuma iMulungu hoyogolosa dilagano dye dikumbi kwa nheifo Ibulahimu hakowa Baba wa wa Isaka na kufinigwa mwijuwa dye munane na Isaka naye yagaluka Babakwe wa Yakobo na Yakobo Baba wa wakuku ikumi na weli.
44007009	“Awaya awakulu wetu howomonela finju Yusufu, howomusambasa, hoyoguligwa kuutumwa Misili Ninga iMulungu hoyokuwa hamwedu naye,
44007010	hoyomuhonya mumagayo gakwe gose. Mulungu hoyomwingha ihewa na misungu kumwande ya Falao, iMundewa wa Misili, iFalao hoyomwika kuwa mukulu wa iisi ne inyumba ye chindewa.
44007011	“Baho hakulawanisa njala nghulu mu isi yose ya Misili na Kanaani, hoikwigala magayo makulu lugano. Awababu setu howolemeligwa kupata chakudiya chochose,
44007012	Ninga iYakobo yakahulike fina ako Misili kwina chakudiya, hoyowatuma wanangwe, awaBaba setu weje uko Misili ichipango cha kunghonga.
44007013	Inhambo yawo iyakeli Yusufu hoyokiyonesa kuwanduguse na Falao hoyowamanya awanduguse wa Yusufu.
44007014	Kamei Yusufu hakawatuma na kumwinanga Baba yawo Yakobo na wandugu sakwe wose wamwijile, hawowa kifana magana mufungate na na shano wose.
44007015	Kamei Yakobo hakadulika Misili. Imwene imwenyecho hakafila ukuya hamwedu na waBaba setu,
44007016	kamei imitufi yawo hoikwigaligwa mpaka Shekemu, hosikigwa mu chilalo cha Abulahamu choyagulile kuwa kwi kabila dya Hamoli kwa chayasi fulani cha mapesa.
44007017	“Ugele wo kumemelesa dihuwi dya Abulahamu, ukowe habehi ditewa dya wanhu waya akuya Misili hadyongeseka na kuwa ikulu lugano.
44007018	Hanyuma yakwe, hoyotawala Mundewa yumonga imwene nghamumanyile Yusufu, ako Misili.
44007019	Hoyodigolosela ditaifa dyetu Lwidaso, hoyowatendela wababu setu fihile, kwa kuwagamba wawatage awana wawo we chigosi uleke wafe.
44007020	“Musa hoyokwelekigwa ugele uwo. Hokowa mwana muswanu lugano. Hoyoleleligwa ukaya kwa chipango kwa minyesi midatu,
44007021	yakalafigwe kunje, imwana we chike wa Falao hoyomulonda, hoyomulela kifana mwanagwe.
44007022	Musa hoyofusigwa finhu fyose na misungu yose ya Wamisili, hoyokuwa munhu wa itunyo na chogoho kwa sinhenda na simbuli.
44007023	“Yakowe munhu wa minyaka makumi mane, hoyolamula kwijawalanga awanduguse Awaislaeli.
44007024	Uko hokomona yumwedu wawo yakutendeligwa fihile, hoyoluta kumuhonya, na kwa kuliha chisasi hoyomukoma ayuya iMumisili.
44007025	(Hakamanya nhagela Waislaeli wayagwe womanya fina iMulungu kumutumiya imwene kuwakombola, ninga wasatangile nheifo.)
44007026	“Nhosiku yakwe howona Waislaeli weli wakitowa, hoyogesa kuwapatanisha yakugamba, ‘Yoloko anye mwa ndugu, nhani mukulemana muwecho kwa wecho?’
44007027	Ayuya yamufowage miyagwe hoyomukundugisa Musa kughanda, yakugamba: Nani yakwikile gweye kuwa chilongosi na mulamusi wetu?
44007028	‘Togola ukuhanga unikome fina fowamukomile iMumisili digulo?’
44007029	Yakahulike nheifo iMusa hoyotija, hoyeja kwikala ku isi ya Midiani na uko hoyopata wana weli.
44007030	“Minyaka makumi mane iyilokile, imalaika we Mundewa hakamwijila Musa muchisinghu chendechikwaka moto akuya kunyika habehi na ditunda dya Sinai.
44007031	iMusa hoyokisina lugano kukona kona ichinhu fina chino, hoyosegela habehi uleke yalange fiswanu; ninga hoyohulika dijwi dye Mundewa.
44007032	‘Aniye no ni Mulungu wa waBaba sako; Mulungu wa Abulahamu, Isaka na Yakobo.’ Musa hoyotetema kwa chogoho kahinghagendelele kulanga kahi.
44007033	“iMundewa hoyomugamba: ‘Hambula ifilwatu fyako kosoko ahano howimile ni hanhu hasunhile.
44007034	Niyona agehile gowakugoloseligwa awanhu wangu akuya Misili. Nihulika ichilolo chawo, nani nija niwahonye. Kosoko iyo wije hano nikulagise ulute Misili.’
44007035	Ayuno iMusa no yuya awanhu wa Isilaelii wowamulemile fowagambile: ‘Nani yakwikile gweye uwe chilongosi wetu na mulamusi wetu?’ Kwa soko ya yuya imalaika yamulawanisile muchihulo chendechikwaka moto, iMulungu hakumutuma iMusa yuyo yowe chilongosi mwihula kwa njila ya yuya malaika yamulawanisile muchisinghu chendechikwaka moto..
44007036	No yawalongose awa awanhu walawe Misili kwa kugolosa mengi ga majumo na gakisina mu isi ya Misili mu bahali ya Shamu na munyika kwa chipango cha minyaka makumi mane.
44007037	“iMusa noyagambile awanhu wa Isilaelii, ‘iMulungu yakwenda yamusagulileni mugonesi fina niye kulawa mugatigati ya wandugu senu mwecho.’
44007038	Ugele awanhu wa Isilaelii fowakitanganyile akuya kunyika, iMusa noyowile uko hamwedu nawo. Hokowa uko hamwedu na waBaba setu na yuya imalaika isalongile naye akuya kwitunda dya Sinai; noyenghigwe asiya simbuli sikwigala uumi yachinghe seyee
44007039	“Ninga imwene no yuyo awakuku setu yowalemile kumuhulikisa; howomukundugisa kunghanda, howohananga kuya Misili.
44007040	Howomugamba Haluni: ‘Chigolose milungu ikudaha kuchilongosa munjila, kosoko chisimale chimupatile iMusa iyachilongose kulawa Misili.’
44007041	Baho noho wakigolosele isanamu ye indama, wakuitambichila na kugolosa chinyemi, ichinhu chowagolose kwa mikono yawo awecho.
44007042	Ninga iMulungu hoyoleuka mugati yawo, hoyowaleka wafuge sinyelesi sa kulanga, fina foiandikigwe mu chitabu che mugonesi: ‘Anye wanhu wa Isilaelii! Siniye womwanichinjile sinyama na kunitambichila kwa chipisi cha minyaka makumi mane akuya kunyika.
44007043	Anyeye hamwinula dihema dya Moleki ne inyelesi ye mulungu wenu Lefani; sisanamu sowagolose nosoukufuga; kosoko iyo nikukwigala kukutagigwa kutali kusuma Babeli.’
44007044	“AwaBaba setu hawowa na diya dihema dya homelele akuya kunyika fina Mulungu foyawalongose chigele Mulungu foyamusigilile Musa yadigolose, kifana foyonesigwe ne Mulungu.
44007045	Kamei awaBabasetu howokihokela awecho kwa wecho mpaka ugele wa Yoshua, foyailondile iisi iya ya wamembe waya wawingigwe ne Mulungu kumwande yawo. Hodikwikala baho mpaka ugele wa Daudi.
44007046	Daudi hakendigwa na Mulungu kusuma wayagwe wose, hoyomutasa Mulungu luneka lwa kumujengela nyumba imwene iMulungu wa Yakobo.
44007047	Ninga Sulemani noyamujengele Mulungu nyumba.
44007048	“Hata nheifo, iMulungu Mukulu nghakwikala musinyumba sijengigwe na wanhu; fina foyakulonga imogonesi.
44007049	iMundewa yakugamba: ‘Ulanga no digoda dyangu dya ditunyo, na chilunga no digoda dyangu dya kwichila migulu. Ni nyumba inhani yomukudaha kunijengela? Na hoki honikudaha kubwihila?
44007050	Ifinhu fono fyose aniye nonifigolose, aho si nheifo?’
44007051	“Anyeye mwichaka chihuliko! Singhutwi si fidoga fyenu sifana awanhu wasimumanyile Mulungu, anyeye mukifana na awaBabasenu. Majuwa gose mukusilema simbuli sa Muhe Musunhile.
44007052	Togoleni, kwina mugonesi wowose imwene awaBabasenu wasamudumangise? Hawawakoma awaya awatumigwe ne Mulungu weje watamile kwija kwakwe ayuya imunhu we chawelu. Hambiya anyeye homumusongesa, homumukoma.
44007053	Anyeye hamuhokela adiya dilagiso degaligwe ukwenu ne Malaika, ninga musagolose fodikulonga!”
44007054	Awaya wasehe we dibalasa wakahulike nheifo, howosuha lugano, howogwegwejula meno kwa nyono.
44007055	Ninga Sitefano yakameme Muhe Musunhile, hoyokwinula ameso gakwe kulanga, hoyokona ditunyo dye Mulungu na Yesu kekala ulwandi lwo kulume lwa Mulungu.
44007056	Hoyogamba Langeni! Nikona ulanga ugubuka ne iMwana we Munhu kema ulwandi lwo kulume lwa Mulungu.
44007057	Baho, awanhu wose awowile mwi Balasa, howotula chowe na kwingisa fidole fyawo kusinghutwi kusihinda. Kamei howomujumhila wose hamwedu,
44007058	howomulafa kunje ye ikaya, howomutowa na mawe. Awaya wahomelesi howokwika si amako gawo kwimilisigwa na mujelelo yakwinanga Sauli.
44007059	Howogendelela kumutowa Sitefano na mawe, ugele imwene yakuwomba: Mundewa Yesu chihokele chidoga changu!
44007060	Hoyotowa mafindi hasi, hoyokwinula dijwi dyake: Mundewa ungawatalilile wihi muchanhya yawo. Yakamale kulonga nheifo, hoyokufa.
44008001	Na Sauli hakendesigwa na kukomigwa kwakwe Sitefano. Dijuwa didyo hokulawanisa lwidaso lukulu lugano kwikanisa diya Yelusalemu. Awahuwile wose ninga awaya awatumigwa du, howokiyagala kusiisi sa Uyahudi na Samalia.
44008002	Awanhu awakumogoha Mulungu howomusika Sitefano na kumugolosela mohongesi makulu.
44008003	Ugele uwo, Sauli hoyogesa kudibana dikanisa. Hoyoluta kwa chila nyumba, hoyowalafa kunje awahuwile, wagosi kwa wanawake, hoyowaguma kwi gelesa.
44008004	Awaya awahuwile awakiyagale, howoluta kose kose wakuhubili imbuli iya.
44008005	iFilipo hakadulika mukaya ya Samalia na kumuhubili Kilisito ku wakaya wa baho.
44008006	Awanhu howokihasa kwa chinyemi kuutegelesa simbuli sa Filipo na kona majumo gaya goyagolose.
44008007	Kosoko simhepo sihile isawekalile wanhu wengi, hosilawa sikutula chowe chikulu; kahi na wanhu wengi wowile na utamu wa kuholola vilungo fyawo no filema howohonyigwa.
44008008	Hokukuwa na chinyemi mukaya iya.
44008009	Baho, hahowa na munhu yumonga yakwinangwa Simoni, imwenye yagolose uhayi wakwe mukaya iyo ku majuwa galokile, na kuwatenda wanhu wa Samalia wakisine lugano, yakiyona imwene ni munhu mukulu.
44008010	Awanhu wose wakulu na wadodo, hawamutegelesa wakugamba, “Munhu yuno ni udaha uya mukulu we Mulungu.”
44008011	Hawakwegigwa lugano ne imwene kosoko hawakisina uhayi wakwe kwa majuwa mengi.
44008012	Ninga wakahuwile inonga ya Filipo mchanhya ya Imbuli iswanu yo undewa we Mulungu na disina dya Yesu Kilisito, howobatisigwa wanawake na wagosi.
44008013	Hata Simoni imwenyecho hoyohuwila; yakamale kubatisigwa hoyokiyandamila na Filipo, hoyokisina amajumo gagolosagwe na Filipo.
44008014	Awaya watumigwa wowile Yelusalemu wakahulike fina awakaya wa Samalia waihokela imbuli ya Mulungu, howowatuma ukwawo Petulo na Yohana.
44008015	Wakafike howowawombela awahuwile uleke wahokele Muhe Musunhile;
44008016	kosoko ugele uwo Muhe Musunhile hakowa nghenati yamwingile hata yumwedu wao muchiligati yao; ninga hawowa wabatisigwe du mudisina dye Mundewa Yesu.
44008017	Petulo na Yohana howowechila mikono awaya wahuwile, awo howohokela Muhe Musunhile.
44008018	Baho Simoni yakone fina kwa kwikiligwa mikono na watumigwa wanhu wakuhokela Muhe Musunhile. Kosoko iyo hoyoweng'a Petulo na Yohana mapesa,
44008019	yakugamba Ningheni na niye udaha uwo uleke wowose wonikumwichila mikono yahokele Muhe Musunhile.
44008020	Ninga Petulo hoyomubidula, Wagilile kutali na mapesa gako kosoko kumanya simboto sa Mulungu sikuguligwa kwa mapesa!
44008021	Kwachaka mugawo wowose, kahi ifungu dyodyose mumulimo uno kosoko umoyo usiliganile kumwande ya meso ge Mulungu.
44008022	Kwa nheifo, ulambe uwihi wako uno na umutase Mundewa naye yakudaha kukonela ubasi amawaso fina gago.
44008023	Nikukona kumama wifu mukali na kohigwa na uwihi!
44008024	Simoni hoyobidula, Dedede, nitasileni kwe Mundewa dinghanipata dyodyose mugago gomulongile.
44008025	Petulo na Yohana wakamale kulafa uhomelesi wao na kutamula imbuli ya Mundewa, howokuya Yelusalemu. Ugele fowoyage hawahubili imbuli swamu mu fikaya fingi fya Wasamalia.
44008026	Malaika we Mundewa hoyomugamba Filipo, Winuke, ulute kwikulu kwandamila injila ikulawa Yelusalemu kuluta Gasa, (Injila iyo ikugendela munyika)
44008027	Kamei, hakenuka na kuluta. Ugele wuwo hokuwa na Mwesiyopiya yumwedu, yemhende, munhu yuyo hakowa munyamhala mukulu we sawo ye Kendake, iMundewa we chike we Chiyesiyopiya hakowa munhambo kulawa Yelusalemu kukufuga.
44008028	Kamei yendeyokuya ukaya hokowa yakwilile umukokoteni ukukwegigwa, munhambo yakwe yendeyosoma chitabu che Mugonesi Isaya.
44008029	Baho Muhe Musunhile hoyomugamba Filipo, Luta habehi ne mukokoteni uya ukukwegigwa, ukiyandamile nawo
44008030	Filipo hoyobilimila habehi na digali didyo, hoyomuhulika ayo imunhu yakusoma muchitabu cha Isaya. Baho Filipo hoyomusa, Togola, ukutanga ago go ukosoma?
44008031	Imunhu yuyo hoyobidula, Nodaha kutanga nhani bila munhu kunilongosa? Baho hoyomwinanga Filipo yakwile mwigali dyakwe, yekale naye.
44008032	Hambiya, difungu dya matulumo masunhile dyoyasomage hadyuwa dino: Hakowa kifana ngholo ikwigaligwa kuchinjigwa; fina ichana che ingholo fochikunyamala posi ugele chikugetigwa, nghagubule mulomo wakwe.
44008033	Hakagumigwa chinyala na koneligwa. Hachaka yakudaha kulonga muchanhya ye cheleko chakwe, kosoko uumi wakwe ulewusigwa muchilunga. Imwene naye nghalafile dijwi dyakwe hata chidodogi.
44008034	Ayo Mwisiyopiya hoyomugamba Filipo, Nitamile, iMugonesi yuno yalonga kosoko yani? Yakulonga kosoko yakwe imwecho ama kosoko ya munhu yungi?
44008035	Kamei, Filipo hoyokongela baho mu matulumo Masunhile, hoyomutamila simbuli si swanu muchanhya ya Yesu.
44008036	Fowowile wakugendelela ne inhambo, howofika ahanhu hena meji, kamei imukulu yuya hoyogamba, “Ahanhu hano hena meji mengi: Togola, kwina chochose ichikudaha kunemesa nighabatisigwe?”
44008037	[Filipo hoyogamba, “Honaga ukuhuwila kwa moyo wako wose ukudaha kubatiswa.” Imwene hoyobidula, “Heye, nikuhuwila fina Yesu Kilisito ni Mwana wa Mulungu.]”
44008038	Kamei Imukulu yuya hoyolagisa mukokoteni uya wime; awene wose aweli howohumuluka, ayuya imukulu na Filipo hoyomubatisa.
44008039	Wakalawe mumeji Muhe we Mundewa hoyomutenda Filipo yaleuke bila koneka na yuya Muwesiyopiya nghamonile kahi; ninga hoyogendelela na nhambo yakwe yamemile chinyemi lugano.
44008040	Filipo hotangila kowa Asoto, hoyogenda musikaya sose yakuhubili Imbuli swanu hata foyafikile Kaisalia.
44009001	Ninga ichigele chicho iSauli hakagendelela kongesa itisi ikulu kwa kuwakoma awamuhuwile Mundewa, hoyoluta kwa mutambiki mukulu,
44009002	hoyotasa yanghigwe baluwa sa kumanyigwa ku masinagogi ge Chiyahudi gowile Damesiki, uleke yanghafika uko wagosi ama wanawake awakwandamila injila ye Mundewa yawakole na kukwila nawo Yelusalemu.
44009003	Ninga foyowile munjila, habehi na kufika Damesiki, chimwande ujelu kulawa kulanga howumumulike kosekose.
44009004	Hoyokugwa hasi na kuhulika dijwi dikumugamba Sauli; Sauli! Nhani ukunyidasa?
44009005	Imwene naye Sauli hoyokusa Agwe no nani, Mundewa? Dijwi diya hodibidula, Aniye no Yesu imwene agweye ukunyidasa!
44009006	Ninga hambiya Inuka, wingile mukaya, na uko ukwende utamiligwe dyokugolosa.
44009007	Awaya awanhu awende woluta hamwedu na Sauli howokwima bahaya, howowa chaka dya kulonga; howohulika dijwi diya ninga wasonile munhu.
44009008	Sauli hoyokwinuka, yakagubule ameso gakwe nghadahile kona chochose; kwa nheifo awanhu waya howomulongosa kwa kumukola mukono mpaka kukaya ya Damesiki.
44009009	Sauli hoyokwikala majuwa madatu bila kona, na ugele uwo nghadiile kahi kunywa chochose.
44009010	Kamei, uko Damesiki hakuwa mwifusa yumwedu yakwinangwa, “Anania. iMundewa hoyumugamba mumagubulo, Anania.” Hoyokwidika, “Nuwa hano Mundewa.”
44009011	Naye Mundewa hoyomugamba, “Kiyohe ulute kwibalabala dikwinangwa digoloke, kwinyumba ya Yuda ukamuhanange munhu yumonga kulawa Talso yakwinangwa Sauli. Hambiya yakutasa,
44009012	na mumagubulo, kona munhu yakwinangwa Anania yakwingila kugati na mwichila mikono uleke yadahe kona.”
44009013	Ninga Anania hoyobidula, “Mundewa, nihulika simbuli sa munhu yuyo kulawa kwa wanhu wengi, nihulika agihile mene goyawagolosele wanhu wako ako Yelusalemu.
44009014	Na keja hano yena udaha kulawa kwa watambiki wakulu kuwakola awanhu wose awakuwomba kudisina dyako.”
44009015	Ninga iMundewa hoyomugamba, “Luta du, kosoko nimusagula yowe chiya changu, yadingase disina dyangu ku mataifa na wandewa wao na kwa wanhu wa Isilaelii.
44009016	Aniye nimwecho nikuhanga nimonese mengi goyakwenda yedasigwe kosoko ya disina dyangu.”
44009017	Kamei, Anania hoyoluta, hoyokwingila munyumba iyo. Kamei hoyokwika mikono yakwe muchanya ya Sauli, hoyogamba, “Mundugusangu Sauli, Mundewa, iYesu imwecho yakiyonese ukwako fowowile munjila kwija hano kanituma uleke udahe kona kahi, na kumemesigwa Muhe Musunhile.”
44009018	Chimwande finhu kifana makangha hofilagala kuulawa kumeso ga Sauli, hoyodaha kona kahi. Hoyokwima hoyobatisigwa;
44009019	yakamale kudiya, si ngufu sakwe hosimuwila. Sauli hoyokwikala majuwa makefu hamwedu na wefusa uko Damesiki.
44009020	Chimwande hoyokonga kuhubili Mumasinagogi fina, “Yesu ni Mwana wa Mulungu.”
44009021	Wanhu wose wamuhulike howokisina lugano, wakugamba, “Munhu yuno so yuyuya yawakomile waya wawombage ku disina dino akuya Yelusalemu? Hakeja hano uleke yawakole awanhu wawo na kuwegala kuwatambiki?”
44009022	Sauli hoyogendelela kupata ludole na kuwagolosa wafumile aWayahudi wekalage Damesiki kwa kuhomela fina Yesu no Kilisito.
44009023	Majuwa mengi gakaloke, Wayahudi howokikonghola hamwedu na kugolosa njila ya kumukoma Sauli,
44009024	ninga Sauli hoyohulika imbuli iyo. chilo ne misi hawemilisa hemulango wo kwingilila mukaya uleke wamukome.
44009025	Ninga ugele wa nechilo awefusa wakwe howomulonda, howomuhulumusa mudisege dikulu kulokela muluneka lowile mulukasi.
44009026	Sauli yakafike Yelusalemu hoyogesa kihasa na wefusa. Ninga wose hawamogoha, na wasahuile fina naye kagaluka mwifusa.
44009027	Baho Balinaba hoyokwija hoyomulonda Sauli na kumwigala ku Watumigwa na kuwatamila ifyene foyamonile Mundewa munjila na fye ne foyasimulile naye. Hoyowatamila Suli foyahubili bila woga akuya Damesiki.
44009028	Kamei Sauli hoyokwikala hamwedu nawo, hoyoigendela Yelusalemu yose yakuhubili imbuli ye Mundewa bila kogoha.
44009029	Kamei hakalongaga na kuwanga chinyume na Wahelenisiti ninga wendewahananga kumukoma.
44009030	Awaya awandugu wakamanya imbuli iyo, howogolosa njila ya kumulonda Sauli, howomwigala Kaiselia, howomuleka yule Talso.
44009031	Kamei dikanisa muisi yose ya Uyahudi na Galilaya na na Samalia, hodijengeka na kukula na kugendelela kumogoha Mundewa na kulongosigwa na Musunhile.
44009032	Petulo foyendeyoluta chila hanhu, hoyofika nheifo ku wanhu wa Mulungu awendewokwikala Luda.
44009033	Uko hoyomufika munhu yumonga yakwinangwa Enea, imwene yuya kagona mwisasi kwa miyaka ikumi na munana kwa utamu wa kuholola.
44009034	Petulo hoyumugamba, “Yesu Kilisito yakuhonya. Inuka utandike disasi dyako. Enea hoyokwinuka chimwande.
44009035	Awakaya wose wa Luda na Saloni howomwona Enea, nawo wose howomubiduchila Mundewa.”
44009036	Hakuwa na mufusigwa yumonga mukaya ya Yopa yakwinangwa Tabisa (kwa Chiyunani ni Dolika, nong'amba Chipala). Imwanamuke yuno yendeyogolosa maswanu na kuwatasa wakiwa wengi ugele wose.
44009037	Ugele uwo hayuwa fina hakatamigwa, hoyokufa. Awanhu howousunha umutufi wakwe, howomutambalisa muchumba cha kuchanhya.
44009038	Yopa si hatali sana na Luda, kwa nheifo awefusa wakahulike fina Petulo kuwa Luda, howotuma wanhu weli ukwakwe na imbuli, Wije ukwetu chimwande lugano foikudahika.
44009039	Kamei Petulo hoyokilongosa nawo. Yakafike howomwigala kuchumba cha kuchanhya kwigolofa, uko wanawake wegane wengi howomusunguluta Petulo wakulila na kumonesa makoti na sisuke soyendeyogolosa ugele foyowile mumi.
44009040	Petulo hoyowalafa wose kunje, hoyofugama, hoyowomba. Hanyuma hoyomubiduchila ayuya yafile, hoyogamba Tabisa inuka! Naye hoyogubuka meso na yakamwone Petulo, hoyokwikala.
44009041	Petulo hoyomutasa kwimanyima, kamei hoyowenanga awaya awanhu wa Mulungu na waya wegane, hoyomuleka mumikono yao, ugele ni mumi.
44009042	Imbuli iyo yagoloseke baho, hoikwenela chila hanhu uko Yopa na wanhu wengi howomuhuila Mundewa.
44009043	Petulo hoyokwikala majuwa mengi uko Yopa, hoyokwikala na munhu yumonga mugolosaji wa nghingo yakwinangwa Simoni.
44010001	Uko Kaisalia hakuwaga na munhu yumonga yakwinangwa Kolinelio Mukulu wa chikosi chimonga chikwinangwa, “Chikosi cha Italia.”
44010002	Hakowa munhu muswamu; imwene hamwedu na wa munyumba yakwe wose wendewomogoha Mulungu. Yendeyogolosa mengi kuwatasa awakiwa we Chiyahudi na yende yomuwomba Mulungu ugele wose.
44010003	Hayuwa kifana saa kenda nhafi ya nemisi, hoyokona chimesomeso, kagubuliligwa, malaika wa Mulungu hoyokwingila kugati hoyomugamba, “Kolinelio!”
44010004	Kolinelio hoyomukumhulila meso yuyo malaika kwa chogoho, hoyomugamba, “Kwina choni Mundewa?” Ayo imalaika hoyomugamba, “Amawombi hamwedu na kulafa kwako kuwatasa wakiwa kufika kuchanhya kuwa ngelegesi kwe Mulungu.
44010005	Hambiya, watume wanhu Yopa wakamwinange munhu yumonga yakwinangwa Simon, disina dimonga Petulo.
44010006	Kowa munyumba ya Simon mugolosaji wa singhingo, nyumba yakwe yuwile habehi ne bahali.”
44010007	Kamei malaika yalongile siso hakafulusa kuleuka na kuluta, Kolinelio hoyowenanga awatogomi weli wa munyumba yakwe na yumwedu wa wasilikali wakwe yendeyomogoha Mulungu,
44010008	hoyowatamila gose galawanise, hoyowatuma Yopa.
44010009	Nhosiku yakwe dijuwa dya keli, awanhu wawo wadatu wakali munhambo, ninga behi na kufika Yopa, Petulo hoyokwila kwipala dye inyumba kuchanhya, ku saa mutandatu ya nemisi uleke yawombe.
44010010	Hakona njala, hoyokwenda kupata chakudiya; ugele ichakudiya fochendechigolosigwa, hoyapatigwa na nhongo sito, hoyokona diono chimesomeso.
44010011	Hakona ulanga ugubuligwa na chinhu kifana isuke ikulu ikudulisigwa dikoligwa musimhembe sakwe sose ine.
44010012	Kugati yakwe kwina fiyumbe fyose: Si nyama se migulu mine, sinyama sikutambala hasi, ne fidege fya mulanga.
44010013	Hoyohulika dijwi dikumugamba: Petulo, Inuka uchinje sinyama sino udiye!
44010014	Petulo hoyobidula, Hata, Mundewa; aniye sinati nidiye chinhu chochose ichene chikusemunigwa ama chihile.
44010015	Dijwi diya hodihulikika kahi dikugamba, “Unghafigambe fichafu ifinhu ifyene Mulungu foyasunhile.”
44010016	Imbuli ino hoyigoloseka kadatu, kamei adiya disuke hodikwinuligwa kulanga.
44010017	Petulo foyendeyokisina isoko ye digubulo didyo dyoyonile, awaya awanhu watumigwe na Kolinelio, wakaitange inyumba ya Simoni, howofika hamulango,
44010018	howokwinanga kwa ijwi: Togoleni, hena mugeni bahano yakwinangigwa Simoni Petulo?
44010019	Petulo hakowa nghenati yamanye magubulo gano, na baho Muhe hoyomugamba, “Tegelesa! Hena wanhu wadatu hano, wakukuhanga.
44010020	Dulika chimwande na unghowe na manhonge kiyandamila nawo, kosoko aniye noniwatumile.”
44010021	Kamei, Petulo hoyodulika hasi, hoyowagamba awanhu wawo, Aniye nowomukuhanga. Nhani mwijile?
44010022	Awene howomubidula, Imukulu we chikosi cha wasilikali, Kolinelio; munhu muswanu, yakumogoha Mulungu na yakutunyigwa na Wayahudi wose, kachituma. Hakagambigwa na malaika Musunhile yakwinange ukaya ukwake uleke yategelese chochose chiwinacho cho kulonga.
44010023	Petulo hoyowakalibisha kugati, hoyowengha hanhu haguna ichilo chia. Nhosiku yakwe, Petulo hoyokonga inhambo hamwedu nawo, na wamonga wa wandugu wa Yopa howokiyandamila naye.
44010024	Dijuwa dya keli yakwe, howofika Kaisalia, na uko Kolinelio yendeyowagojela hamwedu na wandugu na wambuya, awene woyagoneke.
44010025	Petulo yakowe yakwingila Kolinelio, hoyolawa kunje kumuhokela, hoyofugama kumwande yakwe na funamana hasi.
44010026	Ninga Petulo hoyomwinula, hoyomugamba, “Inuka kosoko aniye na munhu du.”
44010027	Petulo hoyogendelela kusimulila na Kolinelio ugele wakwingila kunyumba koyafikile wanhu wengi wakikonghola.
44010028	Petulo hoyowagamba, “Anye muwecho mumanya fina Muyahudi wowose yakulemesigwa na malagiso ge dini yakwe yanghakihase na wanhu wa wamembe gengi. Ninga Mulungu kanyonesa nileke kumwona munhu wowose kuwa yakusemunigwa ama muchafu.
44010029	Kosoko iyo, fomuninange nija, bila kulema. Hambiya, nimusani, Nhani muninange?”
44010030	Kolinelio hoyogamba, “Majuwa madatu galokile ichigele kifana chino, saa ya dikenda ya nemisi, nendeniwomba kuchumba changu. Chimwande munhu yafalile suke sikwakaika kema kumwande yangu,
44010031	hoyogamba, ‘Kolinelio! Amawombi gako na kulafa kwako na kuwatasa kwako wakiwa fihokeligwa na Mulungu.
44010032	Mutume munhu Yopa yakamwinange munhu yumonga yakwinangwa Simoni, disina dimonga Petulo; kowa kunyumba ya Simoni mgolosaji wa singhingo behi na bahali.’
44010033	Kosoko iyo hanikutumila wanhu baho ni baho nagwe kutenda fiswanu kwija. Hambiya, aseye cha hamwande ya Mulungu, kuhulikisa chochose ichene Mulungu kakulagisa ulonge.”
44010034	Baho Petulo hoyokonga kulonga; Hambiya nimanya chawelu Mulungu kechaka ubagusi.
44010035	Munhu wa ditaifa dyodyose yakumogoha Mulungu na kugolosa simbuli se chawelu, Mulungu yakuhokeligwa naye.
44010036	Aino no imbuli Mulungu yo yawegalile wanhu wa Isilaelii, yakutamila Imbuli swanu iikwigala digoya kwa njila ya Yesu Kilisito imwene no Mundewa wa wose.
44010037	Anye mumanya imbuli iya yagoloseke mu isi yose ya Uyahudi kukongela woyahubili Yohana.
44010038	Mumanya Yesu wa Nasaleti ifyene Mulungu foyamusagule kwa kumwitilila Muhe Musunhile na ludole. Mulungu hakowa hamwedu naye; holuta ako nako na kugolosa maswanu na wose awoneligwe na Luhoma.
44010039	Aseye cha wahomelesi wa simbuli sose soyagolose mu isi ya Uyahudi na Yelusalemu. Howomukoma kwa kumutungika mumusalaba.
44010040	Ninga Mulungu hoyomwinula dijuwa dya kadatu, hoyomugolosa yonigwe,
44010041	si kuwanhu wose, ninga kwa waya awene awasaguligwe wowe wahomelesi wakwe, no seye chanywile na kudiya hamwedu naye yamale kwinuka kulawa kuwafile.
44010042	Kachituma chihubili imbuli swanu ku wanhu wose na kuhomela fina imwene noyasaguligwe na Mulungu yowe mulamusi wa womi na wafile.
44010043	Wagonesi wose hawalonga simbuli sakwe fina chila munhu yakumuhuwila yakuleusiligwa uwihi wakwe kudisina dyakwe.
44010044	Ugele Petulo hoyowile yakalilonga simbuli siso, Muhe Musunhile hoyowahumuluchila wose wategelesage imbuli iyo.
44010045	Awaya Awayahudi wahuwile awejile na Petulo kulawa Yopa howokisina kuhona Mulungu hakawetilila ichipawa che Muhe Musunhile wanhu wa wamataifa gengi nheifiya.
44010046	Kosoko hawawahulika wakulonga kwa nonga sa hayo hayo wakumutunya Mulungu. Baho Petulo hoyogamba,
44010047	“Awanhu wano wahokela Muhe Musunhile fina seye chiwecho fochihokele. Togoleni kwina wowose yakudaha kulemesa awanhu wano wanghabatisigwe kwa meji?”
44010048	Kamei, Hoyogamba wabatisigwe kwa disina dya Yesu Kilisito. Baho howomutasa yekale nawo kwa majuwa makefu.
44011001	Hambiya awatumigwa na wandugu akuya Uyahudi howohulika fina awamembe nawo waihokela imbuli ya Mulungu.
44011002	Kamei, Petulo yakalute Yelusalemu, awaya Awayahudi wahuwile awendage awanhu wamataifa gamonga wagaligwe kwikumbi, howomugamba kabana, wakugamba,
44011003	“Agweye kwijakwikala na walajoni mpaka kudiya nawo.”
44011004	Baho Petulo hoyowatamila chila chinhu, simbuli siya sagoloseke kulawa kunghonga:
44011005	Dijuwa dimonga nendeniwomba mukaya ya Yopa, honikona iono; honikona chinhu kifana isuke ikulu dikudulisigwa hasi kulawa kulanga dikoligwa mu simhembe sakwe ine, hodikwikigwa hanghanda yangu.
44011006	Honisungilila kugati kwa fiswanu honikiona umo si nyama se migulu mine, sinyama sa kumbago, sinyama sikuhambala na fidege fya kulanga.
44011007	Baho honihulika dijwi dikunigamba Petulo, inuka, uchinje, udiye.
44011008	Ninga aniye honigamba; Hata, Mundewa! Kosoko chochose chikusemunigwa na chihile chisinati chingile mumulomo wangu.
44011009	Dijwi diya hodihulikika kahi kulawa kulanga: Unghafigambe fikusemunigwa ifinhu fisunhigwe na Mulungu.
44011010	Imbuli hogoloseka kadatu, kamei fyose hofikuwisigwa kuchanhya kulanga.
44011011	Chimwande wanhu wadatu awene watumigwe ukwangu, howofika kunyumba yonyendenikwila.
44011012	Muhe hoyonigamba nikuyandamile nawo nilekekuwa na manhonge. Awo no awandugu mutandatu howakiyandamila nani kuluta Kaisalia, na uko hochikwingila munyumba ya Kolinelio.
44011013	Imwene hoyochitamila ifyene fyoyamonile malaika yemile kunyumba yakwe yakumugamba, “Mutume Munhu Yopa yakamwinange munhu yumonga yakwinangwa Simoni kwa disina dimonga Petulo.
44011014	Imwene hokutamila simbuli isene agweye na wayago wose mukwende muhonyigwe.”
44011015	Kamei, nikakonge du kulonga, Muhe Musunhile hoyowawadulichila fina foyachidulikile aseye kunghonga.
44011016	Baho honigelegela simbuli siya iMundewa soyalongile: Yohana hakabatisa kwa meji, ninga anyeye mukubatisigwa kwa Muhe Musunhile.
44011017	Hambiya, honaga Mulungu yawenghile wanhu wa wamembe gamonga ichipawa chichiya choyachinghile seye fochamuhuwile Mundewa Yesu Kilisito, togola aniye no nani mpaka nidahe kumupinga Mulungu?
44011018	Wakahulike simbuli siso howoleka lukani, howomutunya Mulungu wakugamba, “Mulungu kawengha wanhu wa wamembe gamonga luneka lwo kulamba na kuwa na uumi!”
44011019	Kosoko ya magayo galwanise ugele foyakomigwe Sitefano, wahuwile howokiyagala. Wamonga howoluta mpaka Foinike, Kupulo, na Andiyokiya wakuhubili imbuli iya kuwayahudi du.
44011020	Ninga wamonga wa wahule kulawa Kupulo na Kulene, howoluta Andiyokiya, howotamila simbuli siso kuwanhu wa wamembe gengi wakuhubili aiya imbuli swanu ye Mundewa Yesu.
44011021	Mundewa hoyowatasi na itewa ikulu dya wanhu hodihuwila na kumubiduchila Mundewa.
44011022	Simbuli siso hosihulikigwa akuya kwi kanisa dya Yelusalemu. Kosoko iyo howomutuma Balinaba yalute Andiyokiya.
44011023	Yakafike uko na kona Mulungu foyawamotese awanhu waya, hoyokonela na kuwaguma moyo wose wagendelele kuwa wanhu wa dihuwi kwi Mundewa.
44011024	Balinaba hakowa munhu muswamu na yamemile Muhe Musunhile na digoya. Itewa ikulu dya wanhu howokwegigwa kwi Mundewa.
44011025	Kamei Balinaba, hoyoluta Talso kumuhananga Sauli.
44011026	Yakamwone hoyokwija naye Andiyokiya. Nawo wose weli howokwikala na dikanisa diya kwa mwaka wose mugima, wakufusa itewa ikulu dya wanhu. Ako Andiyokiya noko kunghonga, awefusa kwinangigwa Wakilisito.
44011027	Ugele uwo wagonesi wengi howokwija Andiyokiya kulawa Yelusalemu.
44011028	Yumwedu wawo iyakwinangwa Agabo hoyokwima kwa udaha wa Muhe Musunhile, hoyolonga gakwende kalawanise fina kukwende kuwa na njala nghulu mu isi yose.
44011029	Awahuwile howokifumilisa chila yumwedu, kwa udaha wakwe yegale chochose uleke wawatase awandugu waye wekalage Uyahudi.
44011030	Kamei, howogolosa nheifo na kwigala kuwasehe wedikanisa umusada wawo kwa mikono ya Balinaba
44012001	Ugele uwo Mundewa Helode hakakonga kuwedasa wanhu we dikanisa.
44012002	Hoyomukoma kwa ipanga Yakobo, munduguse wa Yohana.
44012003	Yakone Wayahudi wendesigwa na chitendo chakwe chicho, hoyogendelela, hoyomukola na Petulo. (Ayo haigoloseka ugele we sikukuu ye mikate isigumigwe nungo.)
44012004	Yakakoligwe, hoyokwikigwa, kulangiligwa na wasilikali fitewa fine fya wasilikali wanewane. Helode hakahananga kumulafa kumwande ya wanhu honaimalile kuloka ikikukuu ye Pasaka.
44012005	Petulo fowile kwigelesa, dikanisa dyende dimuwombela kwa Mulungu kwa moyo.
44012006	Nechilo dijuwa dya longolele dijuwa Helode yahanangage yamulafe Petulo kunje kumwande ya wanhu wose, Petulo hohowa yagonile hagati ya wasilikali weli. Hakowa yohigwe minyolo mili, na wemilisi wendewokwimilisa dilango dya digelesa.
44012007	Chimwande malaika we Mundewa hoyokwima habehi naye, no ujelu houmulika ichumba ichiya chose che digelesa. Malaika hoyomukwafa hambafu hoyomwinusa hoyogamba, “Inuka chimwande!” Baho ni baho iminyolo yamohile mikono hoidumuka na kulagala hasi.
44012008	Malaika hoyomugamba, “Fala umukanda wako, fala filwatu fyako.” Hoyotenda nheifo. Kamei Malaika yuya hoyomugamba, “Fala dikoti dyako, unyandamile.”
44012009	Petulo hoyomwandamila kunje, ninga nghamanyile fina ago gagolosigwe ne malaika hagowa ga chawelu, hakawa yalota nyosi.
44012010	Howoloka ichituwo cha nghonga cha wimilisi na cha keli, hanyuma howofika kumulango we chuma wokwingilila mukaya. Umulango houkumuka uwecho du, awene howolawa kunje. Howokuwa wakugenda mwibalabala dimonga chimwande, ayuya Malaika hoyomuleka Petulo yamwene.
44012011	Ako noho Petulo yatangile choni chigoloseke, hoyogamba, “Hambiya nimanya chawelu fina Mundewa katuma Malaika wakwe na kunihonya mumikono ya Helode na simbuli sose awana wa Isilaelii sowende wa gojela.”
44012012	Yakatange nheifo hoyula kunyumba ya Maliyamu ing'ina wa Yohana iyakwinangwa Mlk o, umo wanhu wengi hawakikonghola wakuwomba.
44012013	Petulo hoyotowa hodi kumulango wa kunje, na mutumishi yumonga we chike yakwinangwa Loda, hoyoluta hamulango kwidika.
44012014	Ayo imwana we chike hoyotanga dijwi dya Petulo hosekelela lugano, ahanhu hokukumula auya umulango hoyobilima kugati na kuwatambila Petulo kema kunje hamulango.
44012015	Howomugamba ayuya imwana we chike, “Kwina chilalu!” Ninga imwene hoyokasana kuwa ni chawelu nofoyuwile. Nawo howomugamba, “Ayo ni Malaika wakwe.”
44012016	Ugele uwo Petulo yakugendelela kutowa hodi. Hanyuma yakwe howokumula u mulango, howomwona, howokisina.
44012017	Kamei hakawapungila umukono wanyamale, hoyowatamila ifene Mundewa foyamulafile mwigelesa. Kamei hoyowagamba wagale imbuli kwa Yakobo na ku awandugu wamonga. Kamei hoyoleuka hoyoluta hanhu hengi.
44012018	Ikafike nhousikusiku hahowa na lutemanuko mugati ya awasilikali kosoko ye imbuli yagoloseke ya Petulo.
44012019	Ichigele Helode foyamukonghile na kuleka kumona, hakawosilisa awasilikali na kulagisa wakomigwe. Kamei hakadulika kulawa Yudea mpaka Kaisaliya na kwikala uko.
44012020	Helode hakasuha sana na watu wa Tilo na Sidoni. Ninga wene howomwigalila wanhu. Awene wawo howomupata kunghonga, Blasito yowe ulwandi ulwawo, Blasito hakowa mumyamhala mukulu munyumba ye Mundewa. Kamei howomulutila Helode, howomutasa kuwa na igya kosoko ye iisi yawo haihula iisi ye Mundewa ku chakudiya.
44012021	Dijuwa dimwedu dyasaguligwe, Helode hoyofala si suke sakwe sechindewa hoyokwikala mwigoda dyakwe dye chindewa hoyolonga na wanhu.
44012022	Wanhu waya howotula chowe cha chinyemi howogamba, “Adino ni ijwi dyo Mulungu si dya Munhu!”
44012023	Baho ni baho Malaika we Mendewa hoyomukinya Helode hasi.
44012024	Imbuli ya Mulungu hoigendelela na kukula.
44012025	Balinaba na Paulo wakamale kugolosa umulimo wawo, howolewuka kahi Yelusalemu howomulonda na Yohana iyakwindigwa kahi Mlk o.
44013001	Kwi kanisa dya Andiyokiya hakuwa na wanhu wamonga wagonesi na walimu; mugati yawo hakowa Balinaba, Simoni yakwinagwa hanyuma Mutitu (Nigel) Lukio wa Kilene, Manaeni imwene yaleligwe hamwedu na Mundewa Helode, na Sauli.
44013002	Wawagolosage kumufugila Mulungu na kufunga Muhe Musunhile hoyowagamba, “Nisagulileni Balinaba na Sauli kosoko yo mulimo woniwenangile.”
44013003	Kamei, wakamale kuwomba na kufunga, howowechila mikono howowaleka walute.
44013004	Kamei, Balinaba na Sauli wakafuluse kutumigwa na Muhe Musunhile, howadulika mpaka Seleukia, kulawa uko howokwila meli mpaka ku chisiwa cha Kuplo.
44013005	Wakafike Salami howohubili imbuli ya Mulungu mumasinagogi ge Chiyahudi. Yohana hakowa mutasi wasi wawo.
44013006	Howogenda kulawa ulwandi lumwedu lwe chisiwa mpaka Pafo, ulwandi lwa keli, na uko howomufika muhai yumonga Muyahudi yekwinangwa Bali Yesu, imwene yendeyokitenda fina mugonesi
44013007	Ayuno hakowa hamwedu na Seligio Paulo, no mukulu wa chicho ichisiwa, hokowa munhu yena umanyi lugano. Seligio Paulo hoyowenanga Balinaba na Sauli uleke yaihulike imbuli ya Mulungu.
44013008	Ninga ayo imuhayi Elima (foyendeyokwinangwa kunonga ye Chiyunani), hoyogesa kuwabesa uleke yamutende yuya imukulu we chisiwa yanghahuwile na kubiduchila dihuwi dye chiKilisito.
44013009	Baho, Sauli imwene yenangigwe kahi Paulo, yakameme Muhe Musunhile, hoyomukumhulila ameso gakwe imuhayi,
44013010	hoyogamba, “Agweye kwa mudasi lugano, kwechaka chawelu! Agweye kwa mwana wa luhoma! Agwe kwa mughondo wa chila chinhu chiya che chawelu; nghukuleka hata chimwedu kwaganisa si njila se Mundewa isigoloke.
44013011	Hambiya, umukono we Mundewa ukuwa muchanhya yako; ukuwa chipofu na nghukudaha kona ujelu we dijuwa kwa chigele.” Chimwande chila chinhu hochikuwa kifana ifunde na chisa ukwakwe, hoyokonga kugenda kuno na kuno yakuhananga munhu yamukole mukono yamulongose.
44013012	Ayuya imukulu we chiwa yakone nheifo, hoyobiduka, hoyohuwila; hoyokisina lugano amafuso goyahulike muchanhya ye Mundewa.
44013013	Kulawa Pafo, Paulo na wayagwe howokwila meli mpaka Pelga ya Pamfulia; ninga Yohana hoyowaleka hoyokuya Yelusalemu.
44013014	Ninga awene howogendelela ne inhambo kuwa Pelga mpaka mukaya ya Andiyokiya Pisidia. Dijuwa dye Sabato howokwingila mwi sinagogi howokwikala.
44013015	Gamale kusomigwa amasomo mu chitabu cha malagiso ga Musa ne chitabu cha Wagonesi, awakulu wa disinagogi howogelegela ne nonga ino, Wandugu hona mwina mbuli ya kuwatamila wanhu uleke muwagume moyo, longeni
44013016	Kamei Paulo hoyokwima, hoyowonesa kwa mukono, hoyokonga kulonga Anye wanhu wa Isilaelii na wamonga wose mukumogoha Mulungu tegeleseni!
44013017	Mulungu wa wanhu wano wa Isilaelii hakawasagula waBabasetu; hoyowagolosa wowe itaifa ikulu ugele fowowile kuya kuutumwa Misili. Mulungu hoyowaleusa uko kwa udaha wakwe mukulu.
44013018	Hoyowafinyilisa kwa minyaka makumi mane munyika.
44013019	Hoyowamala mataifa mafungate we isi ya Kanaani, hoyowengha awo awanhu wakwe isi iya yuwe yawo.
44013020	Hoyiloka minyaka magana mane na makumi mashano. Kamei hoyowengha walamusi kuwalongosa mpaka ugele we mugonesi Samweli.
44013021	Baho, howokwenda kuwa na Mundewa, Mulungu hoyowegha Sauli, mwana wa Kisha wa dikabila dya Benyamini, yowe Mundewa wawo kwa chigele cha minyaka makumi mane.
44013022	Hanyuma hoyomuleusa Sauli, Mulungu hoyomusagula Daudi kuwa Mundewa wawo. Mulungu hak kumufumila kwake hoyogamba: Nimona mwana wa Yese; ni munhu imwene moyo wangu wendesigwa naye, ni munhu yakwenda yagolosa agaya gose gonikwenda kugolosa.
44013023	Kwandamila ulukolo lwakwe munhu yuyu, Mulungu, fina foyalongile, kawegalila wana wa Isilaelii muhonya, no Yesu.
44013024	Ugele nghenati yeje Yesu, Yohana hakamulongolela yakuwahubilia wanhu wose wa Isilaelii fina ikuhanangigwa walambe na kubatisigwa.
44013025	Yohana foyamalagisage imbuli yakwe hakawagamba wanhu, Mukudoga aniye no nani? Aniye ni yuya yomukulangilila. Imwene yakwija hanyuma yangu na aniye sinogelwe hata kudohola sisigi se filwatu fyakwe.
44013026	Wandugu sangu, anyeye mu wana wo lukolo lwa Abulahamu, na wamonga wose mo mukumogoha Mulungu! Imbuli ino yo uhonya igaligwa ukwetu.
44013027	Kosoko awakaya wa Yelusalemu hamwedu na wakulu wawo wasamumanyile imwene kuwa Muhonya, kahiwasatangile simbuli sa wasungula sikusomigwa chila Sabato. Hata neifo hawagolosa simbuli sa wasungula simemeligwe kwa Yesu yakomigwe.
44013028	Ninga wasonile mbuli yoyose yoyabanile iikumutenda yakomigwe, fowamulongile Pilato yamuliganise yakomigwe.
44013029	Kamei wakafuluse kumemelesa gose agawandigwe kosoko ye mwene, howomuhulumusa kulawa mumusalaba howomwika muchilalo.
44013030	Ninga Mulungu hoyomwinula kulawa kuwafile.
44013031	Naye kwa majuwa mengi, hoyokiyonesa kuwa wakiyandamile naye kulawa Galilaya mpaka Yelusalemu. Awo no wahomelesi wakwe hambiya ku wanhu wa Isilaelii.
44013032	Naseye chija hano kumwigalilani imbuli swanu; imbuli iya Mulungu yoyawahuwise awaBabasetu.
44013033	Kamemelesa ukwetu seye chi wajukulu wawo kwa mwinula Yesu kulawa ku wafile fina foyiwandikwe Musabuli ya keli. Agweye kwa mwanangu, Aniye diyelo nigaluka Babako!
44013034	Na kukumwinula kulawa kuwafile, yanghadahe kahi kuya uko na kudoda. Mulungu hakagamba nhafi: Nikukwingha simboto sisunhile se chawelu sonamuhuwise Daudi.
44013035	Heye, nna musisehemu simonga se Sabuli yakugamba: Nghukumuleka isusunhile wako yadode
44013036	Daudi mwecho hakamemelesa foyakwenda Mulungu mu ugele wakwe; kamei hoyokufa hosikigwa habehibehi na wasehe wakwe, na uwili wakwe houdoda.
44013037	Ninga yuya yanuligwe na Mulungu kulawa kuwafile nghadodile.
44013038	Kwa nheifo, mumanye, wandugu sangu, fina kwe injila ye munhu yuno imbuli yo kulekeleligwa uwihi ikuhubihiigwa ukwenu;
44013039	na fina chila munhu yakumwihuwila Yesu yakulekeleligwa uwihi wose; chinhu ichene chisikudahika kwa malagiso.
44013040	Muchilangisise, mungheje mufikiligwa nagaya gowalongile awagonesi:
44013041	Tegeleseni anyeye mu wolubeso, jumeni mwagilile! Kosoko nikugolosa milimo aniye mumajuwa genu, ni chinhu ichene musikudaha kuhuwila hata munhu yanghamutamilani!
44013042	Paulo na Balinaba wokowe wakulawa mwisinagogi awaya awanhu howowagoneka weje kahi isabato ikwandamila, walonge wongesele simbuli siso.
44013043	Umulango wo ukahele, Wayahudi wengi na wanhu wa wamembe gamonga awabidukile idini ye Chiyahudi howowandamilla Paulo na Balinaba. Awo watumigwa howolonga nawo howagamba wagendele kwikala wakuhuwila dihewa dye Mulungu.
44013044	Isabato yandamile, kalibu ikaya yose hoyokwija kuhulikisa imbuli ye Mundewa.
44013045	Ninga Awayahudi wakone didyo ditewa dya wanhu, howomema wifu, howopinga goyalongage Paulo na kumuliga.
44013046	Hata nheifo Paulo na Balinaba howolonga kwa chigosi bila kogoha, wakugamba: Hayuwa fiswanu imbuli ya Mulungu imufikileni anye we kunghonga; ninga kosoko muilema na kiyona msagiligwe uwumi wa majuwa gose, aseye chikumulekani na kuwalutila awanhu wa mataifa gengi.
44013047	Kosoko Mundewa hakachilagisa nhafi: Nikwika gweye uwe ujelu ku wanhu wa wamembe, uleke nwegalile wanhu uhonya kose kuchilunga.
44013048	Awanhu wa wamembe gamonga wakahulike imbuli iyo huwosekelela, howowutunya ulongi wa Mulunguna waya awene wasaguligwe kupata uwumi wa majuwa gose, howohuwila.
44013049	Imbuli ya Mulungu hoikwenela kose kose mu isi iya.
44013050	Ninga Wayahudi howowasongesa awanawake wakulu wene fyeyo wa mataifa gengi na awene wende womogoha Mulungu na wagosi we kaya iyo. Howokonga kuwedasa Paulo na Balinaba, howowawinga kulawa mu sehemu yawo.
44013051	Kamei, watumigwa howokung'unha diluli mumigulu yawo, kuwa ushahidi ukwawo, kamei howoluta Ikonia.
44013052	Ninga awaya wahuwile howomema chinyemi na Muhe Musunhile.
44014001	Ako Ikonia simbuli hasuwa fina fosowile kuya Andiyokiya; Paulo na Balinaba howoluta kwi sinagogi dya Wayahudi howolonga kwa udaha mpaka Wayahudi wengi na Wayunani howohuwila.

44014003	Paulo na Balinaba hogendelela kwikala uko kwa udaha muchanhya ye Mundewa, naye Mundewa hoyowililila ulongi wo walongile muchanhya ye dihewa dyakwe, kwa wadahisa kugolosa ga majumo na gokisina.
44014004	Awanhu we kaya iyo howokitemanula: Wamonga howokifumilisa na Wayahudi, na wamonga howokuwa ulwandi lwa watumigwa.

44015001	Kamei wanhu wamonga hawafika Andiyokiya kulawa Uyahudi howokonga kuwafusa waya wandugu wakugamba, “Hona musigaligwe kwikumbi kwandamilo amahokelo na malagiso ga Musa musikudaha kuhonyigwa ng'oo.”
44015002	Imbuli ino hoikwiga kuwanga kukulu na Balinaba na Paulo wakalonge nao, howokifumilisa fina Paulo na Balinaba hamwedu na wahuwile wengi wa dikanisa dya Andiyokiya wakawona awaya watumigwa na wasehe muchanhya ye imbuli iyo.
44015003	Kamei dikanisa, hodiwelaga nawo wokowe wakulokela Foinike na Samalia howowatamila wanhu ifyene awamembe gamonga fowawamubidukile Mulungu. Simbuli siso hosiwendesa sana wandugu wawo wose.
44015004	Wakafike Yelusalemu howokalibishigwa na dikanisa, watumigwa na wasehe; nawo howowatamila gose goyagolose Mulungu hamwedu nawo.
44015005	Ninga wahuwile wamonga wowile we chitewa cha Mafalisayo, howokwima wakugamba, ikwendigwa wanhu wa wamembe gengi wegaligwe kwikumbi na kufusigwa kwandamila malagiso ga Musa.
44015006	Kamei, watumigwa na wasehe howogolosa mulundo wi waimwene uleke wailange imbuli iyo.
44015007	Wakamale masimulisi matali, Petulo hoyokwima, hoyogamba, “Wandugu sangu, mumanya fina kukonga Mulungu hakanisagula niye mugati yenu uleke awanhu wa wamembe wahulike imbuli Iswanu na kuhuwila kosoko ya mahubili gangu.
44015008	Naye Mulungu yamanyile miyoyo ya wanhu hoyokonesa fina kawafumila nawo kwa kuwengha Muhe Musunhile fina foyachinghile seye.
44015009	Nghagolose ubagusi wowose ukwetu na ukwawo, hakaisunha miyoyo kwa dihuwi.
44015010	Hambiya, nhani, kumugesa Mulungu kwa kuwatwika awo wahuwile musigo wene hata wababu setu, kahi aseye chilemeligwa kuwinula?
44015011	Inghowe nheifo, ninga, chikuhuwila fina aseye fina awene nawo, chikuhonyigwa kwa njila ya dihewa dye Mundewa Yesu.”
44015012	Chitewa chose hochinyamala twi, chikuwategelesa Balinaba na Paulo wakutamila majumo na kisina kwagohesigwe na Mulungu kwa mikono yawo mugati ya wanhu wa wamembe gengi.
44015013	Wakamale kulonga Yakobo hoyokonga kulonga: Wandugu sangu, nitegeleseni!
44015014	Simoni kachitamila fyene Mulungu kunghonga foyawagolosele wanhu wa wamembe gengi, hoyawasagula wamonga wawo wowe wanhu wakwe.
44015015	Imbuli ino iligana lugano na simbuli sa wagonesi fina mawandiko masunhile fogakulonga:
44015016	Hanyuma ya simbuli sino kukuya, nikwenda nijenge kahi aiya inyumba ya Daudi yuwile; Nikugolosa mahame gakwe na kuijenga kahi.

44015018	Nofo yakulonga Mundewa, iyagolosa imbuli ino dimanyike kulawa katali.
44015019	Kosoko iyo ulamusi wangu nowuno: Chinghawedase wanhu wa wamembe awakumubiduchila Mulungu.
44015020	Chiwawandikile baluwa wanghadiye fyakudiya vigumigwe wihi kwa kulafigwa kuwa filafwa ku sisanamu se milungu; waleke dihabwa, wanghadiye nyama yoyose iinyongigwe na wanghonywe sakame.
44015021	Kosoko simbuli sa Musa sendesihubiliwa mu chila isinagoti kwa kaya na kusomigwa mu masinagogi gose chila ijuwa dya sabato.
44015022	Watumigwa, wasehe na dikanisa dyose walamula kuwasagula wanhu wamonga mugati yawo na kuwatuma Andiyokiya hamwedu na Paulo na Balinaba. Kamei, howousagula Yuda iyakwinagwa kahi Balinaba, na Sila, wose wamanyikana lugano mugati ya wandugu.
44015023	Howowengha baluwa ino: Aseye watumigwa na wasehe wandugu senu chikuwalamusani anyeye wandugu wa wamembe gengi muwile ako Andiyokiya, Silia na Kilikia.
44015024	Chihulika fina wanhu wamonga kulawa kuno ukwetu wamidasani kwa simbuli sawo, wayiguma mimoyo yenu chiyangayanga. Ninga wagolosa bila kutumigwa na seye.
44015025	Chilamula hamwedu, chisagula wanhu wakefu na kuwatuma ukwenu hamwedu na wendigwa Balinaba na Paulo,
44015026	awene walafile uumi wawo kosoko ye disina dye Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito.
44015027	Kosoko iyo chikumutuma Yuda na Sila ukwenu, awano wakwenda wawatamileni awenyecho agano gochiwandike.
44015028	Muhe Musunhile naseye chikifumilisa chinghamutwikeni musigo kusuma agano gawagile mugamanye.
44015029	Munghadiye fyakudiya filafigwe kusisanamu; na kunywa sakame, munghadiye nyama inyongigwe; na muleke dihabwa. Mokuwa mugolose fiswanu munghaleka kugolosa simbuli so. Chikuwalamusani.
44015030	Wakamale chilagigwa awo awatumigwe, howoluta ulwandi lwa Andiyokiya, kowenange mulundo wa wahuwile, howowengha ibaluwa iyo.
44015031	Wakaisoma iyo ibaluwa, simbuli sakwe hosiwaguma moyo, howokonela lugano.
44015032	Yuda na Sila awene wowile wagonesi, howosimulila na wandungu wawo kwakuwaguma moyo na kuwasindamika kwa ugele mutali.
44015033	Wakamale kwikala uko kwa chigele chiguhi, wandugu wa Andiyokiya howowelaga, wakuwahangingila dihewa, kamei howokuya kuway awawatumile.
44015034	Ninga Sila hakalamula kusigala.
44015035	Paulo na Balinaba howosigala uko Andiyokiya kwa ugele muguhi, howofusa na kuhubili imbuli ye Mundewa hamwedu na wanhu wamonga.
44015036	Gakaloke majuwa mengi, Paulo hoyomugamba Balinaba, Chuye chikawagendele awaya wandugu mu chila kaya kochahubili imbuli ye Mundewa chikakiyonele fowakugendelela.
44015037	Balinaba hoyohananga wamulonde na Yohana yakwinangwa Mlk o,

44016001	Paulo hoyofika Delbe na Lisitila, koyekalage Mkilisito yomonga yakwinaningwa Timoseyo. Ing'ina imwene yawile muKilisito nheifia, hakowa Muyahudi; ninga iBabakwe hakowa Muyunani.
44016002	Timoseo hakowa na itunyo ikulu ku mugati ya wandugu wa Lisitila na Ikonia.
44016003	Paulo hakahananga Timoseyo yakiyandamile naye munhamo, kosoko iyo hoyomwigala kwikumbi. Hakagosa nheifo kosoko ya Wayahudi wose awekale ulwandi wa ukuya hawamanya fina iBabakwe hakowa Muyunani.
44016004	Ugele fowende wogenda musikaya siya hawawengha wanhu agaya malagiso galafigwe na watumigwa na wasehe akuya Yelusalemu howowagamba wagakole.

44016006	Howogenda ulwandi lwa Fulugia na Galatiya, Muhe Musunhile hakawalemes kuhubili imbuli iyo mu si isi sa Asia.
44016007	Wakafike kusimhaka sa Musia, howogesa kwingila ku si isi sa Bisinia, ninga Muhe wa Yesu hoyowalemesa.
44016008	Kamei, howolokela Musia howoluta mpaka Tulowa.

44016011	Kulawa Tulowa hochikwila meli mpaka Samatilake, nosiku yakwe hochiguma nanga Neapoli.
44016012	Kulawa uko, hochiluta Filipi, kaya ya Wilaya ya kunghonga ya Makedonia, yene nheifia ni utawala wa Chilumi. Hochikwikala mukaya iyo majuwa makefu.
44016013	Dijuwa dye Sabato hochilawa kunje ye kaya hochiluta kunghingi ye lwanda, hachigamba nhegela hanhu ha kufugila. Hochikwikala, hochilonga na wanawake wakitang'anyila baho.

44016015	Yakabatiswe mudala yuyu hamwedu ne nyumba yakwe, hoyochigoneka yakugamba, “Hona chawelu munyonile fina niye nikumuhuwila Mundewa, kalibuni ukaya ukwangu.” Hoyochidindilisa chilute.
44016016	Dijuwa dimonga fochalutage ahanhu ho kufugila, mundele yumonga yowile na dipepo dya kulagula hakatang'anyila nase. Mundele yowapatila wagoli wakwe fesa nyingi kwa kulagula kwakwe.

44016019	Awagoli wa yuya mundele wakone fina dihuwi dyawo dyokupata sawo dihela, howowakola Paulo na Sila, howowabulumula mpaka kuwanhu, kumwande ya wakulu.
44016020	Howowasongesa kuwalamusi wakugamba, “Wanhu wano Wayahudi wakwigala fujo mukaya yetu.
44016021	Wakufusa mahokelo agene aseye chi wanhu we Chilumi chikulemesigwa kusihokela kahikusandamila.”
44016022	Ditewa dya wanhu hodikihasa nawo howowatowa. Awaya watambiki howowadegela cha Paulo si suke sawo, howogamba watowigwe fiboko.

44016027	Musilikali wedigelesa foyenuke yakona imilango yose yamwasi, hoyogamba nhagela awafungwa wose hawowa watijile, kosoko iyo hoyosomola dipanga dyakwe na kuhananga kikoma.

44016034	Hanyuma hoyowalonda Paulo na Sila kunyumba yakwe, hoyowengha chakudiya. Imwene ne inyumba yakwe yose howogolosa shelehe kosoko hambiya hawowa wamuhuwile Mulungu.
44016035	Nosiku yakwe nosikusiku Mahakimu howowatuma awakulu wa wasilikali awene wakugamba, “Walekeni awanhu waya.”

44022010	Hoyogamba, ‘Nitende nhani Mundewa?’ iMundewa hoyonigamba, ‘Inuka ulute Damesiki na uko ukweda utamiligwe gose agekigwe kosoko yako ugagolose.’
44022011	Nikowe sikudaha kona kosoko ya ukali wa ujelu uya wonyonile, honilongosigwa kwa kukoligwa mukono na waya awowile hamwedu naniye hochikwingila Damesiki.
44022012	Uko hakuwa na munhu yakwinangigwa Ananiya, munhu yakumogoha Mulungu, yakwandamila malagiso getu, imwene yuyo hakowa munhu muswanu hakendigwa naWayahudi wose awekale uko,
44022013	hoyonijila hoyokwima habehi na niye, hoyonigamba, ‘Mundugusangu Sauli, hokela kona kwako na disaa didyo ameso gangu hogogubuka honikona.’
44022014	“Hoyogamba, ‘I Mulungu wa waBaba setu kakusagula agweye umanye inyenda yakwe, kumwona imutogomi wakwe yaliganile na kumuhulika imwene imwenecho yakulonga kwa mulomo wakwe;
44022015	kosoko ukuwa muhomelesi wakwe kuwanhu wose muchanhya ya gowonile na go uhulike.
44022016	Hambiya ukugoja choni? Inuka ubatisigwe, usunhwe uwihi wako kwa kwinanga disina dyakwe.’”
44022017	“Nikoye Yelusalemu ugele nikutasa mwihekalu, hanyona majumo, honimona yakulonga naniye,
44022018	Golosa chimwande uleuke Yelusalemu, kosoko wasikwenda wakuhulike uhomelesi wako muchanhya yangu.
44022019	Kamei hanigamba, ‘Mundewa, awene awenecho wamanya fina chila isinagogi haniwoha na kuwaguma mwigelesa awaya awakuhuwile,
44022020	na ugele isakame ya Sitefano imuhomelesi wako foyalafigwe, ani nayi hanyuwa nyimile baho, nikufumila, inghomigwa yakwe, na kulekeligwa sisuke sa waya wamukomage.’
44022021	“Hoyonigamba, ‘Leuka; kosoko nikukwigala kutali ku wamembe.’”
44022022	Kulawa kunghonga mpaka imbuli ino hawamutegelesa; kamei howekwinula amajwi gawo na kugamba, “Muleuse muchilunga! Kosoko nghagile kuwa mumi!”
44022023	Hawagendelele kujoja na kwinula sisuke na kutimula diluli muchanhya,
44022024	imukulu wa wasilikali wose hakalagisa wamukole Paulo wamwigale kwikigo kugati na kumujola mikotya uleke wamanye isoko iikuleka awanhu wakumujojoweka nheifo.
44022025	Ninga hawamoha ne mikowa ye singhingo, Paulo hoyolonga na mukulu we chitewa cha wasilikali igana dimwedu iyemila habehi naye, “Togola ikudahika kumujola imunhu iMulumi ugele nghenati yaliganiswe?”
