44022026	Ugele ayuya imukulu we ichitewa cha wasilikali wose, hoyomugamba, “Mukuhananga mugolose choni? Kosoko imunhu yuno ni Mulumi.”
44022027	Kosoko iyo imukulu wa wasilikali wose, hakeja na kumusa, “Nitamile agwe kwa Mulumi?” Hakagamba, “Heye.”
44022028	Imukulu wa wasilikali wose hakabidula, “Aniye nigula Ulumi kwa mapesa mengi.” Paulo hakagamba, “Aniye nyelekigwa Mulumi,”
44022029	Kosoko iyo awaya awanhu awahanangage wamusilise hawatimuka wose chimwandemwande; ayuya imukulu wa wasilikali wose naye hakogoha, kosoko hakatanga fina iPaulo hakowa Mulumi naye fina hakamoha.
44022030	Ninga ikowe nhosikusiku uleke yamanye ichalekile Wayahudi wamusongesa, hakamudohola, na kulagisa makuhani wakulu na dibalasa dyose wakitanganyile, hoyomwigala Paulo, hoyomwika kumwande yawo.
44023001	Paulo hoyowang'olela meso awaya awadibalasa, kamei hoyokonga kulonga, “Mpaka diyelo nafi nigendelela kwikala na moyo muswamu kumwande ye Mulungu.”
44023002	Baho iMutambiki mukulu Anania hoyowalonga awaya awemile habehi na Paulo wamutowe kofi mumulomo.
44023003	Kamei Paulo hoyomugamba, “Mulungu imwecho yakwenda yakutowe kofi agweye goufanile lukasi lubakigwe swakaya! Ukudahani kwikala baho uniliganise chishelia na gweye gomwecho ubana ishelia kwa kugamba nifowigwe?”
44023004	Awanhu awemile baho howomugamba Paulo, “Ukumuliga iMutambiki mukulu wa Mulungu?”
44023005	Paulo hoyobidula, “Wandugu sangu samanyile fina imwene ni kuhani mukulu. Kosoko amawandiko gagamba nhafi: ‘Unghalonge fihile muchanhya ye mutawala wa wanhu wako.’”
44023006	Ninga ugele uwo Paulo yakamanye fina wamonga wa wanhu wadibalasa diya ni Masadukayo na wamonga ni Mafalisayo. Kamei, hoyokwinula dijwi kumwande ya Dibalasa, “Wandugu sangu aniye na Mufalisayo. Aniye nigaliku balasa dya ulamusi, kosoko nikuhuwila fina awanhu wakawokwinuka.”
44023007	Yakalonge nheifo, howokonga kuwanga lugano Mafalisayo na Masadukayo, umukutano houkitemanuka matewa meli.
44023008	Isoko iyecho hayuwa aino, Masadukayo wakugamba kwichaka kwinuka wanhu wafile, kwichaka malaika, na kwichaka Muhe, ninga Mafalisayo wakuhuwila gose madatu.
44023009	Ichowe hochikongeseka wamonga wa walimu we shelia we chitewa cha Mafalisayo howokwima na kulafa malalamiko gawo kwa ludole. “Chisikona chochose chihile mwi munhu yuno; ikudahika nhagela Muhe au malaika kalonga naye?”
44023010	Kuwanga hokukuwa kwingi mpaka imukulu wa wasilikali we nghondo hoyokogoha fina wakudaha kumudega fihindihindi. Kosoko iyo hoyowatuma wasilikali wakwe wengile muchiligati cha ditewa diya, wamulafe Paulo na kumuwisa kugati ya digelesa.
44023011	Ichilo chandamile Mundewa hakema habehi na Paulo, hoyomugamba, “Kiinghe moyo! Kosoko fina founihomelela ahano Yelusalemu, ukwenda utende nheifo ukaya ya Lumi.”
44023012	Kukoche Wayahudi howogolosa chikalo cha chinyele. Howochilaha: Chisikudiya kahikunywa mpaka ma chimalile kumukoma Paulo.
44023013	Wanhu wafike makumi mane wakifumilise injama yo kugolosa nheifo.
44023014	Kamei howoluta kuwatambiki wakulu na wasehe, howogamba, “Aseye chichilaha fina chisikuwonja chochose kumilomo yetu mpaka baho ma chimalile kumukoma Paulo.
44023015	Hambiya, anyeye na Dibalasa mutume mbuli kwi mukulu wa dijeshi,” yamwigale Paulo ukwenu mukitende kifana mukuhananga kumanya simbuli sakwe chikamilifu ku imwene. “Chatayali kumukoma ugele yakali nghenati yafike habehi.”
44023016	Ninga imwana we munduguse wa Paulo hoyohulika simbuli umupango uwo; kwa nheifo hoyokwingila kwigelesa, hoyomutamila Paulo injama iyo.
44023017	Paulo hoyomwinanga yumwedu wa wasilikali hoyomugamba, “Mulonde mwanike yuno mwigale kwi mukulu wa dijeshi, kena mbuli yakumutamila.”
44023018	Musilikali homugala imwanike yuya hoyomulongosa mpaka kwi mukulu wa majeshi, hoyogamba, “Ayuya imufungwa Paulo kanyinanga hoyonitasa nimulete imwanike yuno ukwako kosoko kena mbuli ya kukutamila.”
44023019	Imukulu wa dijeshi homukola mukono imwanike yuya hoyoluta naye hanghanda, hoyomusa, Kwina choni chokunitamila?
44023020	Imwene hoyogamba, “Awayahudi wakifumilisa wakutase umwigale Paulo ku Dibalasa dikuhananga dipate simbuli sakwe fiswanu.
44023021	Ninga agweye unghafumile kosoko kwina wanhu wengi kusuma makumi mane wakiyohile kumukola kwa ludole. Wachilaha fina wasikudiya chinhu ama kunywa chinhu mpaka wowe wamalile kumukoma. Hambiya wakiyoha wagojela du ulamusi wako.”
44023022	Imukulu wa dijeshi hoyomuleka yalute hoyomusugula fina yanghamutamile munhu wowose fina kamwigalila imbuli iyo.
44023023	Baho, imukulu we dijeshi hoyowenanga wasilikali weli hoyowagamba, “Weke tayali wasilikali magana meli, na wakukwila si nyumbu makumi mufungate, na wasilikali magana meli we migoha, walute Kaisalia; muwe tayali kuleuka, ugele isaa tatu inghati ifike diyelo neichilo.
44023024	Ikeni nyumbu nghefu kosoko ya Paulo; mumwigale digoya kwa Felisi, imukulu we iyisi.”
44023025	Kamei hakawandika baluwa ku mbuli ino:
44023026	Aniye Kilaudio Lusia nikukuwandichila agweye mukulu Felisi: Mukulu we iisi Nikulamusa!
44023027	Wayahudi hawamukola munhu yuno na hawowa habehi na kukoma nanga satamiligwe fina ni mukaya wa Chilumi, kwa nheifo honiluta na wasilikali na honimuhonya.
44023028	Nikahanange kumanya imbuli ilekile womushitaki gawo muchanhya yakwe, honimwigala kwi Balasa dyawo dikulu.
44023029	Honikona fina mashitaka agecho hagowa ga kuwanga muchanhya ya finhu fingi fye sheliya yawo, kwa nheifo sonile fina kagolosa chochose chiya ichagile yakomigwe ama yohigwe mwigelesa.
44023030	Nikatamiligwe fina Wayahudi hawagolosa njila ya kumukoma, honilamula kumwigala ukwako. Honiwagamba awashitaki wakwe wagale mashitaka gawo kumwande yako.
44023031	Kamei awo awasilikali howomulonda Paulo fina fowalagisigwe. Howomwigalaichilo chicho mpaka Andipatili.
44023032	Nhosiku yakwe wasilikali we migulu howokuya kunghambi, howowaleka awaya awasilikali awakukwila si nyumbu wagendelele ne inhambo hamwedu na Paulo.
44023033	Wakafika Kaisalia howomwingha yuya imukulu we iisi ibaluwa iya na kumwika Paulo mu udaha wakwe.
44023034	Felisi yakamale kuisoma ibaluwa iya, hoyowosa Paulo kalawa iisi yaki. Yakatamiligwe fina kalawa iisi ya Kilikia,
44023035	hoyogamba, “Notegelesa imbuli yako ma wafulusekwija awashitaki wako.” Kamei hoyolagisa Paulo yekigwe wimilisi mwikumbo dya Helode.
44024001	Gakaloke majuwa mashano, iMutambiki mukulu Anania hoyokwija Kaisalia hamwedu na wasehe wakefu na wakili yumwedu wa shelia iyakwinangwa Telitulo. Howomulutila ayuya imukulu we iisi howomutamila amashitaka gawo muchanhya ya Paulo.
44024002	Paulo hoyokwinangigwa na Telitulo, hoyokumula mashitaka nhafi: Mukulu Felisi, ulongosi wako muswanu ugolosa mabadiliko agawagile mwitaifa dyetu chila hanu chihokela dino kwa moyo wa ilumbo.
44024003	Chila hanu na chila ugele chikuhokela dino kwa moyo wa ilumbo.
44024004	Ninga chinghagilise umuda wako kahi, chikukutasa ku uswanu wako, utegelese ulongi wetu.
44024005	Chitanga fina imunhu yuno niwakogoha lugano. Imwene yukukonga migogolo muchiligati ya Wayahudi chila hanhu, muchilunga chose kasi ni chilongosi we chitewa cha Wanasaleti.
44024006	Kahi hakagesi kuchafula dihekalu, nase hochimukola,
44024007	“Ninga Lisiya Ichilongosi hoyeja na kumuleusa mumikono yetu kwa ludole.”
44024008	Kwa kumusamusa agweye gomwecho ukwenda wone pwii simbuli sino sose isene sochikumushitaka.
44024009	Nawo Wayahudi howofumila fina chawelu foyalongile yuya amashitaka gago.
44024010	Kamei imukulu we iisi hoyomonesa Paulo kuwa yakudaha kulonga. Naye Paulo hoyogamba, “Nikonela kitetea kumwande yako, fina kosoko nimanya fina mulimo wa mulamusi wa ditaifa dino kwa minyaka mingi.
44024011	Ukudaha kuhananga ukweli fina gasilokile majuwa ikumi na meli du galokile fonalutile kufuga Yelusalemu.
44024012	Wayahudi wasinifikile nikuwanga na munhu wowose. Wasanifikile nikusongesa wanhu mwihekalu, ama mumasunagogi gawo, ama ahanhu hengi hohose mukaya iyo.
44024013	Hata wasikudaha kuhomelela amashitaka gowalafile muchanhya yangu.
44024014	“Ninga chino nochonikufumila kumwande yako: Aniye nikufuga Mulungu ku Njila yo wagumba ya usushi. Nikufuga Mulungu wa waBaba setu, nikuhuwila chila chinhu chiwandikigwe mu fitabu fye sheliya na fya wagonesi.
44024015	Aniye nikumuhuwila Mulungu imwene, awa nawo wakumuhokela, fina kwina kwinuligwa kwa wanhu wafile, awaswamu na wehile.
44024016	Kosoko iyo nikitahidi kuwa na moyo muswanu kwa Mulungu na kuwanhu.
44024017	“Nikekale kutali chipisi cha minyaka mikefu, honikuya Yelusalemu na kwigalila ditaifa dyangu sadaka na filafya.
44024018	Fonagolosage nheifo noho wanifikile mwihekalu nigolose difugilo dyo kitakasa. Kusowile na itewa dya wanhu kahimugogolo.
44024019	Ninga hakuwa Wayahudi kulawa iisi ya Asia; awo no yowile fiswanu wowe bahano kumwande yako na kulafa mashitaka gawo hona wena chochose chokulonga ku niye.
44024020	Ama waleke wano walonge dikosa dyowonile ukwangu fonyemile kumwande ya Dibalasa dyawo dikulu,
44024021	ninga simbuli sino sonalongile fonyemile kumwande yawo: ‘Mukuniliganisa diyelo dino kosoko yo kolelesa fina awafile wakawokwinuligwa.’”
44024022	Baho, Felisi imwecho hakaimanya oyo Injila iswanu, hoyokwimisa dishauli dyo. Hoyowagamba, “Nikanilafa ulamusi wangu muchanhya ye dishauli dino ugele Lusia mukulu wa dijeshi foyakwija hano.”
44024023	Kamei hoyomulonga ayuya chilongosi wa wasilikali we inghondo yamwike Paulo kugati, ninga yowe na uhulu chiyasi, na wambuya sakwe wanghalemesigwe kumwingha fyoyakuhitaji.
44024024	Gakaloke majuwa makefu, Felisi hoyofika hamwedu ne muke Dlusila, yowile Muyahudi. Holagisa Paulo yegaligwe, hoyomutegelesa yakulonga muchanhya ya kumuhuwila Yesu Kilisito.
44024025	Ninga Paulo foyakongile kulonga muchanhya ya kuliganila, kuwa na chiyasi, muchanhya ya uligaswe ukwija, Felisi hoyokogoha hoyogamba, “Kwa hambiya ukudaha kuluta; nokwinanga kahi ninghapata luneka.”
44024026	Ugele uwo yendeyohuwila fina Paulo komwingha fesa. Kosoko iyo hakagendelela kumwinanga na kusimulila naye chila ugele.
44024027	Ikaloke minyaka mili, Palikio Festo hoyolonda ahanhu ha Felisi, hoyokuwa mukulu we iisi. Kosoko hakenda kuwendesa Wayahudi, Felisi hoyomuleka Paulo mwigelesa.
44025001	Dijuwa dya kadatu yakafike Kaisali, Festo hoyoleuka kuluta Yelusalemu.
44025002	Watambiki wakulu na filongosi wa Wayahudi hawalonga naye muchanhya ya mashitaka gondeyoshitakiigwa Paulo. Howomutasa kwa dede, Festo
44025003	yawagolosele uswanu kwa kumwigala Paulo Yelusalemu. Howadiya njama wamukome hona yowile munjila.
44025004	Ninga Festo hoyobidula, Paulo yakusigala kuya Kaisalia mwigelesa ani nani nikwenda nilute uko majuwa si mengi.
44025005	Walekeni filongosi wenu walute uko hamwedu naniye wakafe mashitaka gawo hona yagolose dyodyose dihile.
44025006	Festo yakamale kwikala nawo, majuwa gafikile munana ama ikumi nhafi, kamei hoyoyokuya Kaisalia. Nhosiku yakwe hoyoluta kwi balasa hoyolagisa Paulo yegaligwe kugati.
44025007	Ugele Paulo yakeje, Wayahudi awalawile Yelusalemu howokonga kulafa mashitaka mengi, masito agene gowasadahile konesa fina ni chawelu.
44025008	Kukitetea Paulo hoyogamba: Aniye sigolose ikosa dyodyose muchanhya ye sheliya ye Chiyahudi, ama dihekalu, ama muchanhya ya Kaisali.
44025009	Festo hoyohananga kuwendesa Wayahudi, kwa nheifo hoyomusa Paulo Togola! Kokwenda kuluta Yelusalemu uleke ukahukumiigwe uko kumwande yangu muchanhya ya mashitaka gano?
44025010	Paulo hoyobidula, Nima hamwande ya mahakama ga Kaisali, na bahano no hanogele ninghigwe hukumu. Fina foumanyile fiswanu, siwagolosele Wayahudi uwihi wowose.
44025011	Ninga, hona nyoneke na ikosa dyodyose dinogele kufa, sikutasa kulekeleligwa kutendeligwa nheifo. Ninga hona kwichaka chawelu mu mashitaka, kwichaka yakudaha kuniguma mumiko yawo. Nikukanha lufaa kwa Kaisali!
44025012	Baho, Festo yakamale kusimulila na washauli wakwe, hoyomugamba Paulo, Kukanha lufaa kwa Kaisali, haya ukuluta kwa Kaisali.
44025013	Majuwa makefu hanyuma Mundewa Aglipa na Belinike howofika Kaisalia, uleke walafe heshima sawo kwa Festo.
44025014	Howokuwa uko majuwa makefu, naye Festo hoyomutamila Mundewa simbuli sa Paulo. Henamunhu yumonga hano imwene Felisi hakamuleka mwigelesa.
44025015	Nikalute Yelusalemu, watambiki wakulu na asehe wa Wayahudi howomushitaki na kunitasa nimuhukumu.
44025016	Ninga niye honiwabidula fina si jadi ya Walumi kumulafa munhu yenghigwe asabu ugele iyekushitakigwa nghenati yakitang'anyile na awashiliki wakwe chimeso meso na kwinghigwa luneka lwa kitekea muchanhya ya gago mashitaka.
44025017	Wakafike baho sachelewe, ninga honigolosa chikao kumahakama, nhosiku yakwe honilagisa imunhu yuyo yegaligwe.
44025018	Awashitaki howokwima lakini wasalafile mashika gehile fina fonendenidoga.
44025019	Ninga du howowa na lukani lwa mbili, si dini yawo na sa munhu yakwinangigwa Yesu yafile, ninga Paulo yakukolelesa fina ni mumi.
44025020	Nilemeligwa kumanya dyo kugolosa mu imbuli iyo. Kamei honimusa Paulo hona yakwenda kuluta kama hakama akuya Yelusalemu kosoko ya mashitaka gago.
44025021	Ninga Paulo hoyokanha lufa, hoyotasa yalekigwe mwigelesa mpaka ulamuso we imbuli iyo ulafigwe na Kaisali. Kosoko iyo hanidaha kumuleka mwigelesa mpaka ma nikudaha kumwigala kwa Kaisali.
44025022	Aglipa hoyomugamba Festo, Nokwenda kumuhulika imunhu yuyo aniye nimwecho. Festo hoyomugamba, “Komuhulika nhosiku.”
44025023	Kwa nheifo, nhosiku yakwe Aglipa na Belinike howokwija kwa chinyemi ku dikumbo dye mikutano wakilose na wakulu wa majeshi na filongosi we kaya. Festo hoyolagisa Paulo yegaligwe kugati.
44025024	Kamei hoyogamba, “Mundewa Aglipa na mose muwile hano hamwedu nase! Hano hamwande yenu hena munhu yuno, imwene aWayahudi wose wowile hano na kuya Yelusalemu, wakujoja fina nghawagilwa kuwa mumi kahi.
44025025	Ninga niye sonile fina kagolosa chochose chihile ichene chikumutenda yagiligwe kukomigwa; ninga kosoko imwecho hakakanha lufaa kwa Kaisali, nilamula kumwigala.
44025026	Ninga ku ulwandi ulwangu nichaka chinhu ichene chonikudaha kumuwandichila Kaisali muchanhya yakwe. Nochileka nimwigale hano kumwande yenu, na gano ukwako gweye, Mundewa Aglipa! Uleke munghamala kumusa Musa nipate mbuli ya kuwandika.
44025027	Kosoko ikuwa mbuli ya chibwalasi kwigala mufungwa, akuno hechaka amakosa gakwe goyagolose.”
44026001	Kamei Aglipa hoyomugamba Paulo, “Ukudaha kitetea.” Baho Paulo hoyogolola mukono wakwe hoyokitetea nhafi:
44026002	“Mundewa Aglipa, nikiyona nijaliwa diyelo kitetea kumwande yako muchanhya ya mashitaka gose agene Wayahudi walonga muchanhya yangu.
44026003	Chawelu kosoko gweye kumanya simila sa Wayahudi na migagolo yawo, nikukutasa unitegelese kwa ufumilifu.
44026004	“Awayahudi wamanya amaisha gangu gose kulawa udodo wangu fyene fonikale kulawa kunghonga ne ditaifa dyangu ako Yelusalemu.
44026005	Wanimanya kwa ugele mutali, na wakudaha kuhomelela, wanghenda fina kulawa kunghonga hanikala kifana munhu yumwedu wa waya awakolile lugano idini yetu, chitewa cha Mafalisayo.
44026006	Na hambiya nima hano nilamuligwe kosoko nikuhuwila dihuwi Mulungu dyoyawahuwise waBaba setu.
44026007	Diwi dyo nodidiya dikuhuwiligwa na makabila kumi na meli kupata fowakumufuga Mulungu chilo ne misi. Ku dihuwi dino nikushitakigwa na Wayahudi!
44026008	Mundewa, Nhani nyeye mukona isikudahika kwi Mulungu kwinula wanhu wafile?
44026009	Chawelu aniye nimwecho hanihuwila fina inyagila kugolosa mbuli nyingi kulema disina dya Yesu wa Nasaleti.
44026010	“Simbuli so, noso nagolose ako Yelusalemu, aniye nimwecho ugele wonenghigwe udaha kulawa ku watambiki wakulu, haniwaguma mwigelesa wengi wa wanhu wa Mulungu. Fowalamuligwe kukomigwa, aniye hanitowa kula ya kufumila.
44026011	Mikongho mingi haniwatenda wotowigwe mumasinagogi gose, honiwalonga kwa ludole wadikane dihuwilo dyawo. Inyono yangu ukwawo hoikuwa ghulu mpaka nende niwasaka sikaya sa kutali.”
44026012	“Kwe njila iyo honiluta Dameski ugele umoja, nina udaha na malagiso kulawa ku watambiki wakulu.
44026013	Mukulu, ugele fonowile munjila saa mutandatu ya nemisi, hanyona ujelu mukulu kusuma we dijuwa, ukwaka kulawa kulanga, hounisunguluta niye hamwedu na wachowanye munhambo.
44026014	Chose hochikugwa hasi, nani honihulika ijwi dikulonga nani kwa Chiebulaniya, ‘Sauli, Sauli! Nhani kunibulaga? Ukibulaga chaka kifana kutowa mundome ichuma chisongoke.’”
44026015	Honigamba, “Gwegwe nani Mundewa?” Naye Mundewa hoyobidula, “Aniye no Yesu imwene agweye ukubulaga.
44026016	Si chinhu, inuka hambiya, imanyima. Nikisololosa ukwako kosoko ino nikwike uwe mutumishi wangu kuhomelela ifyene fyo unyonile niye na simbuli sonikwenda nikiyonese ukwako.
44026017	Nikukuhonya kulawa ku wa Isilaelii na wanhu wa wamembe gamonga wonikwenda nikutume ukwawo.
44026018	Ukuwagubula meso gawo na kuwadahisa walawe muchisa na kwingila mu ujelu; walawe mu utawala wa Shetani, wamubidukile Mulungu kwa kumuhuwila kwawo, walekeleligwe uwihi na kulonda ahanhu hawo mugati ya waya awene wagaluke fina wanhu wa Mulungu.”
44026019	“Nheifo, Mundewa Aglipa, sibesile diwono didyo dya kulanga.
44026020	Ninga hanikonga kuhubili kunghonga ako Dameski, hanyuma ku waya wanhu wa Yelusalemu na wanhu wose wa Uyahudi na wa wamembe gamonga. Niwasonghesa wamubidukile Mulungu na konesa kwa sinhenda fina wabadilisha imiyoyo yawo.
44026021	Kosoko iyo Wayahudi hawanikola nuwile Mwihekalu, howohananga kunikoma.
44026022	Ninga Mulungu hoyonitasa; na kwa neifo mpaka diyelo nima chigosi nikuhomelela ku wose, ku wakulu na kuwadodo. Gonikulonga nogaya kuwagonesi na Musa wagamba gakagolawanisa:
44026023	Fina Kilisito yakusambasigwa na kokuwa wanghonga kwinuka kulawa kuwafile, uleke yafamile fina ujelu wa uhonya ukuwamulikia awanhu wose hambiya, Wayahudi na nheifiya wanhu wa wamembe gamonga.”
44026024	Paulo yakafike baho mukitetea kwakwe Festo hoyolonga kwa kwinula dijwi, “Paulo! Kwina chilalu!
44026025	Ninga Paulo nichaka chilalu Mukulu Festo, honikulonga ni chawelu muhala.
44026026	Agweye Mundewa kusimanya simbuli sino, kosoko iyo nikudaha kulonga nichaka chogoho kumwande yako. Nichaka manhonge fina aga gose gagoloseka gamanyika ukwako kosoko imbuli ino isigoloseke kwa chifiso.
44026027	Mundewa Aglipa, Togola ukuhuwila wagonesi? Nimanya fina ukuhuwila.”
44026028	Aglipa hoyomubidula Paulo, “Chidodogi du ukwenda unitende muKilisito?”
44026029	Paulo hoyobidula, Nikumutasa Mulungu, fina kwa chapangu chiguhi ama chitali, si gweye du ninga wose awakunihulika diyelo wowe fina niye fonuwile, ninga bila ino iminyolo.
44026030	Baho iMundewa mukulu we iisi, na Belinike, na waya wose wamonga wowile hamwedu nawo howokwinuka.
44026031	Wakaleuke howokiyusa wecho kwa wecho, Munhu yuno hakowa yadaha kulekeligwa howile ghakanhile lufaa kwa Kaisali.
44026032	Aglipa hakamugamba Fesito, “Imunhu yuno hakowa yakulekeleligwa woile ghatasile kuluta kwe Mundewa.”
44027001	Wakafuluse kulamula fina chilute mpaka Italia, howomwika Paulo hamwedu na wafungwa wamonga ku wimilisi wa akida we chikosi chikwinangwa Chikosi cha Kaisali.
44027002	Hochikwila meli ya Adilamito iyende iluta na kulokela musibandali sa mu iisi ya Asia, hochikonga lugendo. Alistaliko mukaya wa Makedonia, kulawa Sesaloniki hakowa hamwedu nase.
44027003	Nhosiku yakwe hochikwima kubandali ya Sidoni. Yuliyo hoyomutendela Paulo fiswamu kwa kumuleka yamone wambwiya sakwe na kupata ifinhu foyakuhananga.
44027004	Kulawa uko hochigendelela ne nhambo, ninga kosoko imheho yendeitowa kwa ludole kulawa kumwande yetu, hochilokela ulwandi lwe chisiwa cha Kupulo ukwene kusowile na mheho nyingi.
44027005	Hanyuma hochiloka ibahali ya Kilikia na Pamfulia, hochikwima Mula, ikaya ya Lukia.
44027006	Baho, ichilongosi wa wasilikali igana yuyo hoyofika meli imonga ya Alekisandilia iyendeluta Italia, kwa nheifo hoyochikiwisa kugati.
44027007	Kwa chipisi cha majuwa mengi hachigenda digaluga, na kwa fikugutu hochifika habehi na Nido. Na kosoko imheho isachinghile luneka hochiluta kumwande bila kubiduka, hochigenda ulwandi lwa Klete habehi na Salimone ukusowile na mheho nyingi.
44027008	Hochigenda kunghanda yakwe digaluga, hochifika hanhu hakwinangwa Bandali Swanu, habehi ne kaya ya Lasea.
44027009	Chipisi chitali hachuwa chilokile, hata dijuwa dyo kufunga hadyuwa dilokile. Hambiya hayuwa hatali lugano kugenda na meli. Kamei, Paulo hoyowasugula:
44027010	Wakulu, nikona fina inhambo ino ikuwa na mugogolo, kwagilila finhu fingi, si imisigo du yuwile mu meli, hata na kwa mwumi wetu.
44027011	Ninga ayuya ichilongosi wa waslikali igana hakahulikila simbuli sa ayuya iyakugendesa imeli na imwenye meli kusuma soyalongile Paulo.
44027012	Kosoko ibandali iyo isowile hanhu haswanu kwikala ugele we imheho ye inyota, uwengi huwosagula kugendelela ne inhambo kwa kubahatisha fina wakudaha kufika Foinike, bandali ya Kleti, hasi ya kuuswilo we dijuwa na kuchanhya ya kuuswile we dijuwa; na uko hawowa wakudaha kwikala uko ugele we inyota.
44027013	Kamei imheho ya kusini ikakonge kuputa fiswanu, howodoga fina wapata dowahanange, kosoko iyo howoleuka howoigenesa imeli habehi sana na mwani ya Klete.
44027014	Ninga, chisalokile chipisi chitati, imheho inghali ikwinangwa Mheho ya kasikasi haikonga kuputa kulanga kuchisiwa.
44027015	Imheho hoitowa imeli iya, na kosoko chisendechidaha kuisuma hochiileka ikwelegetigwe na iyo imheho.
44027016	Chisiwa chimonga chikwinangwa Kauda, hochichikinga chidodogi imheho iyo; na chikole kusini kwakwe hochisuma, hata nheifo kwa fikugutu kuhonya u munhumbwi uya wa imeli.
44027017	Awaya anamaji howowukweka umunhumbwi kugati, kamei howoisungulusila imeli lusigi na kuyoha kwa ludole. Awogoha fina wakudaha kwangamila kuchilo che bahali ku mwani ya Libiya. Kosoko iyo hawadulisa matanga na kuileka imeli ibulumuligwe ne imheho.
44027018	Umusukosuko hougendelela kuputa, na nhosiku yakwe howokonga kukubita kunje imisigo ya mumeli.
44027019	Dijuwa dya kadatu howokonga kuguma mumeji ifinhu fye imeli kwe mikono yawo awecho.
44027020	Kwa majuwa mengi chisadahile kona dijuwa ama sinyelesi; umusingisiko hugendela kuputa lugano. Hata dihuwi dyo kuhona hodichihelela.
44027021	Chikafuluse kwikala majuwa mengi bila kudiya chakudiya, Paulo hoyokwima mugati yawo hoyogamba, “Wakulu nanga yowile fiswamu nanga mwanitegelese na kuleka kugenda kulawa Klete. He mwatendile nheifo chosowile chikwingila mugogolo uno na si hasala sino sose.
44027022	Hambiya nikumutasani muwe na moyo, kwichaka hata yumwedu wenu yakwenda yagilise uumi wakwe; imeli du noikwende yagilile.
44027023	Kosoko digulo nechilo choikwinuchila diyelo, malaika we Mulungu imwene aniye na munhu wakwe, kahi nowo nikufuga, kanijila,
44027024	hoyonigamba, ‘Paulo, unghogohe, Inogela wine kumwande ya Kaisali, naye Mulungu kwa uswamu wakwe kakutendela maswanu kwa kukuhonya agweye na wose womuwaniye munhambo wanghagilile.’
44027025	Nheifo, mowanhu nye, kiingheni moyo! Kosoko nikumuhuwila Mulungu fina ikwende yuwe sawa fina fonitamiligwe.
44027026	Ninga hata nheifo chikwenda chikatagigwe muchiwa chingi.”
44027027	Ichilo cha dijuwa dya ikumi na ine, chendechikwigaligwa kuno na kuno mu bahali ya Adilia. Habehi na muchilo mugati, wanamaji howokona fina chuwa habehi na iisi.
44027028	Kwa nheifo howohananga chilinde che bahali uleke walagase ulusigi lohigwe chinhu chisito, howopata chilindi cha meta makumi mane, hanyuma howopima kahi howopata meta igana dimwedu na makumi madatu.
44027029	Kosoko ya kogoha kukwama kumawe, howodulisa nanga ine kunyuma ye imeli; howotasa usiku uche chimwande.
44027030	Wanamaji howohanga kutija na hawafulusa kudulisa auya umunhumbwi kumeji, wakitenda fina wakahulumusa si nanga kumwande ye meli.
44027031	Ninga Paulo hoyomulonga yuya akida wa dijeshi na wasilikali wakwe, Awano awanamaji wanghaleka kusigala amuno mu meli musikuhona.
44027032	Baho awasilikali waya howosidumula sisigi sakolelese au umunhumbwi, howouleka ulondigwe na meji.
44027033	Kukwende kuche, Paulo hoyowatasa wose wadiye chakudiya: Kwa majuwa ikumi na ine hambiya, hamuwa mumanhonge na musighati mudiye chinhu chochose.
44027034	Hambiya, nikumutasani mudiye chakudiya kosoko muchananga ikuhanangika mudiye uleke mudahe kugendelela kuwa womi. Kosoko hata lujwili lumwedu lwa matwi genu usikwagilila.
44027035	Yakamale kulonga nheifo hoyolonda mukate, hoyulumba kwa Mulungu, kumwande yawo wose hoyoubendula hoyokonga kudiya.
44027036	Baho wose howosindamala, howodiya chakudiya awecho.
44027037	Chose hamwedu hachuwa wanhu magana meli na makumi mufungate na mutandatu, mu meli.
44027038	Wose wakamale kudiya na kwiguta, howohungula usito mu meli kwa kutanga ingano mubahali.
44027039	Kukoche, wanamaji wasadahile kuitanga iisi iya ninga howokona hanhu hamonga hena mhwani na disanga, howolamula kuluta ne imeli uko mhwani inghahadahika.
44027040	Kwa nheifo hawosidumula si nanga na kusileka kubahali sisigi isohile ikukani, kamei howokwinula itanga dimwedu kumwande kukola imheho, howoluta imhwani.
44027041	Ninga howofika hanhu ahene mikondo mili ye bahali ikitang'anyila, ulwandi lwa kunyuma hoibenduka dibasibasi kusoko ya uludole lwa mawimbi.
44027042	Wasilikali howohananga kuwakoma awafungwa wose kwa kogoha fina wakudaha kogela mpaka mhwani na kutija.
44027043	Ninga kosoko yuya akida wa dijeshi hakahananga kumuhonya Paulo, hakawalemesa wanghatende nheifo. Hoyolagisa fina kunghonga awaya awakudaha kogela wajumhe kulawa mu meli na kogela mpaka mhwani,
44027044	na wamonga wendamile wakikolele mufibao au mufipande fye imeli ineneke. Nofo aseye chose chafikile mhwani.
44028001	Chikafuluse kufika kuisi hochimanya fina ichisiwa chiya chikwinangigwa Melita.
44028002	Wakaya wa baho howa waswanu sana ukwetu. Ifula yendeikonga kutonya na hakuwa na mheho, kosoko iyo howokwasa moto, howochikalibisha.
44028003	Paulo hoyodondola chisigo chidodogi cha figodi, ugele foyasigumange mumoto. Baho kosoko ya dijoto dya umoto hodilawa ijoka mufigodi hodikisinga mumukono wakwe hodinyalilila.
44028004	Awakaya wa baho wakone ichiyumbe chiya chikuning'inha mumukono wakwe, howokitamila kwa wecho, Chawelu imunhu yuno kakoma munhu hata kona yahonile kufila mubahali, ihaki isimulekile yowe mumi.
44028005	Ninga Paulo hodikung'unhila mumoto ichiyumbe chiya, na imwene nghabulagigwe hata chidodogi.
44028006	Awa wanhu wendewolangilila fina kofimba ama kokugwa hasi na kufa. Wakagojele kwa chipisi chitali bila kona Paulo yapatigwa na chinhu chochose ichene si cha kawaida, howobidula mafikili gawo muchanhya yakwe, howogamba fina ni mulungu.
44028007	Habehi na ahanhu baho hahowa na migunda ya Publio, imukulu we chisiwa chiya. Publio hoyochikalibisha chimbuya, hochikuwa wageni wakwe kwa majuwa madatu.
44028008	Hoyikuwa fina iBabakwe wa Publio hakowa mutamu wa mhungo na kahala, kagona mwisasi. Paulo hoyoluta kumwona na yakamale kuwomba, na yakamwikile mikono yakwe muchanhya yakwe hoyonona.
44028009	Kulawa dino kugoloseka, watamu wose muchisiwa howokwija howohonyigwa.
44028010	Howochingha finghwa fya hayo hayo, na ugele wochaleukage howochigumila mumeli ifinhu fyose fochendechihanga.
44028011	Ikaloke minyesi mitatu, hochileuka na meli yowile baho kosoko ye imheho mu chisiwa, meli ya Alekisandilia iikwinangwa, Wandugu mapasa (Milungu Mapasa)
44028012	Hochifika ikaya ya Silakusa, hochikwikala baho majuwa madatu.
44028013	Kulawa uko hachileuka hochisunguluta na kufika Legio. Dikaloke ijuwa dimwedu, imheho hoikonga kuputa kulawa kusini, kamei gakaloke majuwa meli hochifika bandali ya Potioli.
44028014	Uko hachifika wandugu wakefu awe wahanange chikale nawo kwa ijuma dimwedu. Nheifi nofo ehafikile Lumi.
44028015	Awandugu wa Lumi fowahulike simbuli setu, howokwija kuchihokela kwe soko dya Apio na Mikahawa midatu. Paulo yakawone hoyomulumba Mulungu, na hoyopata moyo.
44028016	Chikafike Lumi, Paulo hakalekeligwa yekale yemwene na musilikali yumwedu wa kumwimilisa.
44028017	Gakaloke majuwa madatu, Paulo hoyowenanga filongosi wose we Chiyahudi wa hanhu baho, wakakikonghole, Paulo hoyowagamba, “Wandugu sangu, aniye sagolose chochose chihile, kahikulema sijadi sa wasehe wetu, hamikoligwa akuya Yelusalemu na kugumigwa mumikono ya Walumi.
44028018	Wakanyusenyuse na kona fina nichaka wihi wowose, howohananga wanilekele.
44028019	Ninga Wayahudi wamonga howolema imbuli yo hoinigolosa nihanange lufaa kwa Kaisali, ninga niye sowile na mbuli yoyose ya kuwashitaki awaditaifa dyangu.
44028020	Kosoko iyo nihananga kiyona nanye na kusimulila nanye, kosoko nyohigwa iminyolo ku dihuwilo didyo dya Waislaeli.”
44028021	Nowo howomugamba fina, “Chisihokele baluwa sosose kulawa Uyahudi muchanhya yako, na kwichaka ndugu yeyose yejile hano yachitamile mbuli yoyose ihile ulwandi ulwako.
44028022	Ninga chikona inogela chihulike kulawa ukwako gomwecho foukona agweye; kosoko cho chimanyile muchanhya ye chitewa chino ni fina chila hanhu chikulongigwa fibi.”
44028023	Wakakifumilise dijuwa dyo kitang'anyila naye, howokwija hoyekalage wanhu wengi lugano. Hoyoyowatamila imbuli iyo kulawa nhosikusiku mpaka hegulo, yakuhomelela ku undewa wa Mulungu kuwonesa fina chawelu simbuli sa Yesu kulawa mu sheliya ya Musa na amanabii.
44028024	Wamonga wawo howofumila ku siya soyalongile, ugele uwo wamonga wasahuwile.
44028025	Howoleka kifumilisa wecho kwa wecho, howoleuka ugele Paulo yakagambe: “Muhe Musunhile hakowa sawa foyalongile kuwa Baba senu kwa njila ye mugonesi Isaya:
44028026	‘Luta ku wanhu wano, ukagambe, chaweli mukamuhulika ninga musikutanga ng'oo;
44028027	kosoko imisungu ya wanhu wano ibwalata, wahindi singhutwi sawo, wafinya meso gawo. Hona si nheifo, wowa wakona kwa meso gawo, hawahulike kwa singhutwi sawo, na kutanga kwe misungu yawo, na kunibiduchila, yakulonga Mundewa, nani nuwanikuwa honya.’”
44028028	Paulo hoyomalagisa kwa kugamba, “Mumanye fina uhonya uwo wa Mulungu.
44028029	wigaligwa kuwawamembe wakwende wahulike!”
44028030	Paulo hoyokwikala minyaka mili munyumba yakwe imwecho yendeyolihila kodi, yendeyowakalibisha wose wamwijilage.
44028031	Yakuhubili undewa wa Mulungu na kufusa muchanhya ya Mundewa Yesu Kilisito kwa udaha hechaka kulemesigwa.
45001001	Paulo, imutogomi wa Yesu Kilisito, kenangigwa kuwa Mutumigwa, yasaguligwe kosoko ye imbuli swanu ye Mulungu,
45001002	iyalaganisigwe ne Mulungu kulawa katali kupulutila awagonesi wakwe mumatulumo gasunhile,
45001003	imbuli swanu ni kosoko ya mwanagwe yalawile mulukolo lwa Daudi kwa chimutufi
45001004	na kutambusigwa kuwa Mwana we Mulungu hamwedu na ludole kosoko ya Muhe wo Usunhile kwa kwinuligwa kwakwe kulawa mudifa, Yesu Kilisito Mundewa wetu,
45001005	kulokela imwene chihokela dihewa, na utumigwa wo kwigala habehi ichihuliko che dihuwi mugati ya wose Amataifa kosoko ye disina dyakwe,
45001006	hamwedu na nyeye muwecho mwinangwe muwe wa Yesu Kilisito,
45001007	kuwose wendigwa ne Mulungu woile Loma wenangwe kuwa wasunhile:
45001008	Kunghonga, nikumulumba Mulungu wangu kulokela Yesu Kilisito kosoko yenu mose, kosoko ye dihuwi dyenu idikuhubiliigwa muchilunga chose.
45001009	kosoko iMulungu no muhomesi wangu, wonikumutogomela hamwedu ne muhe kwa kutamila imbuli swanu ye Mwanagwe, bila kuleka nigendelela kuwagelegela kwa kuwatasilani majuwa gose munhasa yangu,
45001010	nikutasa fina Mulungu yanghenda nidahe kwija ukwenu.
45001011	Kosoko nikusulumila niwoneni uleke niwengheni finghwa fye chimuhe na kuwagumani ludole,
45001012	uleke chuwe wakangasi wasindamafu kwa dihuwi dya chila munhu na miyagwe kosekose ukwenu na ukwangu.
45001013	Nikuhananga mumanye wandugu sangu fina mikangha mingi hanihananga kwija ukwenu (ninga hanilemesigwa) uleke nidahe kugola ugolaji ukwenu na nheifiya kifana kuwamembe wasigale.
45001014	Nikudaiigwa kuhubili Imbuli swanu kuwanhu wose Awayunani na Awasigendelele kuwene misungu na awabwalasi:
45001015	kosoko ya iyo nikuhananga kuhubili Imbuli swanu hata ukwenu nyeye muwile Loma.
45001016	Kosoko sikuyonela chinyala Imbuli swanu; ni ludole lwa Mulungu kwa uhonya wa chila munhu yene dihuwi, kwa Muyahudi kunghonga na kahi kwa Muyunani.
45001017	Kosoko kwa iyo ichawelu ye Mulungu igubuligwa kugendela dihuwi kwa dihuwi fina foitulumigwe kugamba; “Imuchawelu kokwikala kwa kulokela dihuwi”
45001018	Kosoko inyono ye Mulungu yonesigwa kulawa kulanga kuwanhu wose awasikwenda Mulungu na wihi wa awakukanhamisa ichawelu.
45001019	Kosoko iikudaha kumanyika muchanhya ye Mulungu ni chalinse ukwawo, kosoko iMulungu kayonesa ukwawo.
45001020	Kulawa kukumbigwa kwe chilunga inyuwa yakwe ye ludole yo kuleka koneka na udaha wa majuwa gose waumanya na kuona kulokela finhu fyumbigwe. Nong'amba wechaka chibalalilo.
45001021	Kosoko hawamumanya Mulungu, ninga wasimwinghile chogoho kifana Mulungu ama kumulumba, ninga hawagilila mudasi mumadoga gawo kamei misungu yawo hoigumigwa chisa
45001022	Wakidai wena misungu wagaluka, wabwalasi;
45001023	na kubidula ditunyo dye Mulungu idichaka ubani kuwa futa ye chimunhu iikubanika, na fidege na fikewe hamwedu na ifikutambala.
45001024	Kosoko ya iyo Mulungu kawengha mukusulumila mumimoyo yawo uwihi kuleka kiyogoha mumitufi yawo awecho
45001025	kosoko wabidula ichawelu ye Mulungu kuudasi na kufuga fyumbigwe na kufifugamila na kuleka Iyombile, imutunyigwa wa majuwa gose! Hano.
45001026	Kosoko ya iyo Mulungu kawengha usulumisi wichaka chogoho. Wanawake wao nawo wabidula sinhenda kulawa fosumbigwe kuluta kusisumbigwe,
45001027	nheifiya awagosi nawo, hawaleka sinhenda ifene foyumbigwe kuwa nawake sawo na kikola usulumisi wecho kwa wecho. Hata wagosi wagolosa mbuli sa chinyala na wagosi wayawo na kuhokela itoso dya nhenda sawo sihile.
45001028	Na kosoko wasonile fiswanu kumumanya Mulungu, Mulungu hakawaleka wandamile madoga gawo gehile agasiku hanangigwa wagolose.
45001029	Hawamema na chila ilalago dya wihi, ulwafu, usulumisi, chigiso, wamemile finju, ukomaji, unghondo, udanhilisaji, kubalalila, na walongaji we mbuli sa wamonga,
45001030	wakusigila wayawo, awasikumwenda Mulungu, wetogosi, weyoni, lubeso, wanhu wakudoga gehile, na awasikuhulika awaweleke,
45001031	wabwalasi, wechaka dihuwi, wakomaji wa mimoyo ya wanhu, wechaka ubasi na munhu.
45001032	Hata inghowa wamanyile ulamusi we Mulungu, fina awaya wakugolosa gago wagiligwa kufe, ninga siyo du wakugagolosa du kahi wakubwedelela wamonga nomowakugagolosa.
45002001	Hambiya kwichaka chibalalilo, kwawowose, nomo ukuliganisa wamonga; kosoko kwa kuwaliganisa wamonga ukilamula gomwecho, kosoko agweye gomulamulaji nagwe ukugolosa wihi uuya.
45002002	“Chimanya fina ulamusi we Mulungu kwa wayawakugolosa gago ni wachawelu”.
45002003	Ukudoga, gweye fina nomoukulamula awakugolosa gago kamei nagweye ukugagolosa nghukwija udaha kuitija inyono ye ulamusi we Mulungu?
45002004	Ama ukubesa uugoli we uwendo na ufinyilisi wakwe. Nghumanyile fina wendo we Mulungu wabaho kukulongosa gweye kukulamba?
45002005	Ninga kosoko youkugutu na kuleka kufinyilisa kwa umoyo wako ukiikila nyono muchanhya yako mwijuwa dye inyono ugele uliganiso we chawelu we Mulungu foukwija ukoneka
45002006	Kosoko Mulungu komuliha chila munhu fina foyaliganile:
45002007	Kuwanya awakufinyilisa mukugolosa maswanu wahananga kumutunya Mulungu na kumogoha na kowengha uumi wa majuwa gose;
45002008	na kuwamonga awakwandamila njila sao wenyecho na wasikwenda kuihulika ichawelu ninga uwihi, inyono ye Mulungu yofungha ukwawo.
45002009	Kokuwa na magayo na kutamigwa kwa chila iyakugolosa uwihi, kukongela kwa Muyahudi na kwe Muyunani,
45002010	ninga ditunyo na chogoho hamwedu na dihewa dyuwe kwa chila munhu iyakugolosa uswanu, kwa Muyahudi kunghonga kamei ne Muyunani naye.
45002011	Kosoko Mulungu kechaka kwendelela.
45002012	Kosoko awaya wose wagolose wihi bila dilagiso wakwagilila nheifiya bila dilagiso na wose wagolose wihi mudilagiso wolamuligwe ne dilagiso.
45002013	Kosoko siyo wakuhulika dilagiso nowene nhenda swanu hamwande ye Mulungu, ninga awagolosaji we dilagiso nowakwija wataliligwa nhenda swanu.
45002014	Nghona awamembe, awechaka dilagiso wakumanya chowakuhanagigwa wagolose, awano, awechaka dilagiso, wagaluka ilagiso awecho.
45002015	Wakonesa fina ichikuhanangigwa ne dilagiso chiyandikigwa mumimoyo yao, na madoga gawo gakuwahomelesa na kuwasongesa ama kuwabalalila
45002016	mwijuwa dye uliganiso fina imbuli yangu swanu foilongile, Mulungu kulokela Yesu Kilisito, yakwija yaliganisa amadoga gose agakifisile.
45002017	Ninga nghonaga ukiinanga Muyahudi na ukuhuwila dilagiso ukiyona kosoko ya Mulungu
45002018	na mumanya iMulungu choyakuhananga na kufumilisa ichiswanusi kosoko mulolesigwa mwilagiso,
45002019	na nghona umanyile fina kwamulongosaji wa wamudula na fina agweye no ujelu kwawaya woile muchisa,
45002020	ni mulolesaji wa wabwalasi na mufusaji wa wana wadodogi mumalagiso uwine umanyi we chawelu mugati yako,
45002021	agweye, goukufusa awamonga nghudaha kifusa gomwecho? Ukuhubili uhiji sambi gomwecho kahi ukuhija?
45002022	Agweye ukulemesa dihabwa, gomwecho ukugolosa ihabwa? Agweye ukudesekela fisikimunhu ukuhija mumahekalu?
45002023	Agweye ukitunyila mwilagiso, kahi ukumubesa Mulungu kwa kubena malagiso gakwe?
45002024	Kosoko, fina foitulumigwe, “Disina dye Mulungu dikutofuligwa mugati ya Wamembe kosoko yenu.”
45002025	Dikumbi dikuwa na chambusi nghona mukukola dilagiso amba nghona mukubana dilagiso mugaluka fina wanhu wasifinigwe.
45002026	Kosoko iyo, nghona munhu inghafinigwe yakukola malagiso kuleka kufunigwa kwakwe kusikugaluka kufinigwa?
45002027	Kamei na waya wasifinigwe chimutufi, ninga wakukola dilagiso wowalamula nyeye mwina umulundo wa matulumo na dikumbi, ninga mukubana dilagiso.
45002028	Kosoko iMuyahudi we chawelu nghakiyonesa kwa kunje, ama dikumbi dya chawelu siyo chinhu cha kunje ama cha chimutufi.
45002029	iMuyahudi wa chawelu no yuya iMuyahudi kwa kugati, na dikumbi dye chawelu dyuwa mumoyo, ayi ni mbuli ya chimuhe na siyo mawandiko du. Uleke munhu yahokele ditunyo siyo kulawa kuwanhu, ninga kwe Mulungu.
45003001	Kahi, iMuyahudi kena choni chongeseke ama ichambusi che dikumbi no chihoki?
45003002	Telele, chila hanhu. Kosoko kunghonga, Awayahudi hawenghigwa imbuli ye Mulungu.
45003003	Nhani ghona wamonga wasowile wanhu wakuhuwilika togoleni nonghamba kuleke kuhuwilika kwawo no kuleka kuhuwilika kwe Mulungu?
45003004	Gwe putu! Lekeni Mulungu yagendelele kuwa muchawelu hata nomowamonga wakuwa wadasi fina foitulumigwe, “Uleke utaliligwe chawelu musimbuli sako, na ukasume mwijuwa dyo uliganiso.”
45003005	Ninga inghowa wihi wetu unghagoloseka konesa ichawelu ye Mulungu, chigambeki kogamba Mulungu ni mwihi yakwigala nyono muchanhya yetu? (Nikulonga chimutufi.)
45003006	Gwe putu! Aho mbiya kodaha nhani Mulungu kuchiliganisa ichilunga?
45003007	Ninga inghowa kulokela udasi wangu ichawelu ye Mulungu yohigwa mwitunyo dyakwe, nhani nigendelele kuliganiswa kuwa mwihi?
45003008	Na nhani chinghalonge (kifana wamonga fowakuchisigila kwa kulonga gaya gochikulonga). “Chigolose gehile uleke maswanu geje?” Sigafu ye uliganiso wao ikuwagojela!
45003009	Chigambeki? Aseye Chiwayahudi chawaswanusi? Gwe putu! Kosoko nifulusa kuwalamula wose Awayahudi na Wayunani fina wowa hasi ya ludole lwe wihi;
45003010	fina foitulumigwe, kugamba, “Hechaka muchawelu, hechaka hata yumwedu
45003011	hechaka yamanyile, hechaka yakumuhananga Mulungu.
45003012	Wose wagilila, wose wagolosa wihi, hechaka hata yumwedu yakugolosa uswanu, hechaka hata yumwedu.”
45003013	“Malaka gawo ni makabuli gagubuligwe wakutumiya malimi gawo kudanhilisa.” “Usungu mukali wa majoka wuwa mumilomo yawo.”
45003014	“Milomo yawo imema kuligitisa na usungu lugano.”
45003015	“Migulu yawo ikubilima lumangho kwitila sakama;
45003016	Ubani na magayo gowa musinjila sawo,
45003017	na njila ye digoya wasiimanyile.”
45003018	“Wechaka chogoho cha Mulungu kumwande ya meso gawo.”
45003019	Hambiya chimanya fina chochose ichikulongigwa ne dilagiso, dikuwalonga waya wowile hasi ye dilagiso, uleke chila mulomo unyamale, na chilunga chose chilamuligwe ne Mulungu.
45003020	Kosoko “Hechaka munhu yene mutufi yakudaha kutaliligwa chawelu kwa kona” nhenda sa dilagiso, kosoko kulokela dilagiso no kwija kumanya kwe wihi.
45003021	Ninga hambiya, ichawelu ye Mulungu ifulusa konesigwa kahi kunje ye dilagiso, hata inghowa dilagiso ne wagonesi fikuhomelela imbuli ayi,
45003022	uchawelu we Mulungu kugendela dihuwi mwa Yesu Kilisito kwa wose wakuhuwila, kosoko kwachaka kubagula.
45003023	Kosoko awanhu wose wagolosa wihi na kuhungukiligwa ne ditunyo dye Mulungu;
45003024	wakutaliligwa chawelu chaka kwa njila ya dihewa, kulokela uhonya wuwile mugati ya Kilisito Yesu;
45003025	yalafigwe ne Mulungu kuwa maliho kwa sakama yakwe kwa waya wene dihuwi ukwakwe. Ayino hayuwa kosoko yo konesa uchawelu we Mulungu, kosoko muufinyilisi wakwe we chilungu nghaulangile uwihi wa katali;
45003026	hayuwa kuhomelela kwa chigele chino kuwa imwene imwecho ni muchawelu na yamutalile chawelu yuya iyakumuhuwila Yesu.
45003027	Kahi inyiyona yetu ikulawahi? Yahechaka. Kwa dilagiso dihoki? Kwa milimo ihoki? Ninga putu! Ninga kwa dilagiso dyuwile mwihuwi.
45003028	Kosoko chimanya fina munhu yakutaliligwa nhenda swanu ninga kwa ihuwi ninga siyo kwa kukola malagiso.
45003029	Ama iMulungu ni wa Wayahudi muhala? Si Mulungu wa Wamembe nheifiya? Heye na Wamembe nheifiya,
45003030	kosoko Mulungu ni yumwedu naye kawagolosa wechawelu wafinigwe kwa dihuwi dyawo, na wasifinigwe nawo kulokela dihuwi dyawo,
45003031	nong'amba chikubesa dilagiso kwa dihuwi dino? Putu! Ahanhu hakwe chikudimilila dilagiso.
45004001	Chilonge choni, kosoko ya Ibulahim iBaba yetu kwa chimutufi?
45004002	Kosoko inghowa Ibulahimu hakataliligwa nhenda swanu kwa njila ya milimo, kena chinhu cha kitunyila, ninga si hamwande ye Mulungu.
45004003	Kosoko matulumo gakugambaki? “Ibulahimu hakamuhuwila Mulungu, na haitaligwa kwe mwene fina Muchawelu.”
45004004	Hambiya kwa yuya yakutogoma mulimo, maliho siyo gakutaligwa kifana chinghwa, ninga kifana chinhu chimwagile.
45004005	Na kwa yuya inghakutogoma yakumuhuwila imwene iyakutalila wanhu awasimulungu, dihuwi dijo ditaligwa kifana uchawelu.
45004006	Nheifo Daudi yakulonga kwa kumotesa awaya wataliligwe chawelu ne Mulungu bila kugolosela milimo:
45004007	“Wamotesigwa wose awalekeleligwe wihi wao, na wihi wawo ugubikigwa.
45004008	Kamotesigwa munhu imwene Mundewa nghemutalila uwihi wakwe”
45004009	Togoleni mboto sino silongikwa ni kwa waya du wafinigwe ama na kwa wasifinigwe? Chikugamba, “Kwa Ibulahimu dihuwi dyakwe haditaligwa kuwa chawelu.”
45004010	Hakataliligwa finhani? Hayuwa foyowa yenghati yafinigwe? Hayowile ugele yafinigwe, ninga foyowile yekali.
45004011	Hakahokela chitangilo cha kufinigwa, mutojo wa ichawelu woyowile nawo kwa njila ya ihuwi chigele foyowa yekali kufinigwa. Hayuwa kumugolosa yowe Baba wa wose awakuhuwila hata ugele wasinati wafinigwe, ninga wena ichawelu yowataliligwe,
45004012	no nheifo yowe Baba wa waya wafinigwe, si kwa kufinigwa du ninga wandamile mbasi ye dihuwi adiya dyoyowile nadyo Baba yetu Ibulahimu chigele yenati yafinigwe.
45004013	Kwa dihuwiso dyoyakwija yahala, ichilunga hachilawile kwa Ibulahimu ama kwa lukolo lwakwe kwakulokela dilagiso, ninga kwa kulokela ichawelu ye dihuwi.
45004014	Kosoko inghowa awaya we dilagiso nowahasi, dihuwi digaluga dyachaka na dihuwiso nheifiya.
45004015	Kosoko dilagiso dikwigala nyono, ninga ahanhu hechaka ilagiso, basi hechaka ubanike.
45004016	Kosoko ya iyo dilagiso dima mwihuwi, uleke dihuwi dikale mwihewa na kuwa na nghinyo mulukolo wakwe wose, siyo du kwawakukola dilagiso, ninga kwa waya wakuhanga mwihuwi dya Ibulahimu (kosoko imwene ni Baba wa seye chose,
45004017	fina foitulumigwe, “Nikugolosa gweye uwe Baba wa mataifa mengi”) hamwande ye Mulungu imwene woyamuhuwile, iyakwinanga finhu ifisiuko na kufitenda fyuwe uko.
45004018	Yakuhuwila agasikuhuwilika, uleke yowe Baba wa mataifa mengi, “Kosoko yagaya galongigwe, no nheifo lukolo lwako usikwija utalika.”
45004019	Nghahunguke mwihuwi ugele foyadogage muchanhya ye mutufi wakwe, fowowile ufulusa kufa, (foyowa na minyaka kifana igana dimwedu) ne umusilatungulu we sinda se muke Sala.
45004020	Ghowile na manhonge muchanya ye dihuwiso dye Mulungu, ninga hakakula kwa ludole mwihuwi dyakwe na kumutunya Mulungu,
45004021	na kuhuwila fina Mulungu kogolosa gose goyamuhuwise.
45004022	Kamei “Hayitaligwa ukwakwe kuwa chawelu.”
45004023	Hambiya simbuli, “Haitaligwa ukwakwe,” haitulumigwe fina sikosoko yakwe muhala,
45004024	ninga naseye nase. Yotaliligwa na ukwetu naseye chikumuhuwila imwene yamwinule Yesu Mundewa wetu kulawa muchilalo,
45004025	iyalafigwe kufa kosoko ya wihi wetu na kwinuligwa kosoko ya kutaliligwa chawelu.
45005001	Hambiya, kosoko chitaliligwa chawelu kwa njila ya ihuwi, china digoya hamwedu ne Mulungu kulokela Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito,
45005002	kulawa muimwene chipata mboto mwiiyo chikwima; na chikitunyila dihuwi dyetu dyo kuhangila ditunyo dye Mulungu.
45005003	Na sididyo muhala, ninga kahi chikitunyila magayo, chimanya fina magayo gakwigala ufinyilisi,
45005004	na ufinyilisi ukwigala kupimigwa, na kupimigwa kukwigala ihuwi,
45005005	na dihuwi hadikudaha kumuleka munhu, kosoko wendo lwe Mulungu witiligwa mumimoyo yetu kwa njila ya Muhe Musunhile wochinghigwe.
45005006	Kosoko chigele fochahungukiligwe, muchigele chiswanu chikafike Kilisito hakofa kosoko ya wanhu awasimumanyile Mulungu.
45005007	Kosoko ni fikugutu munhu yafe kosoko ya muchawelu, ninga kosoko ya munhu muswanu yakudaha kufa.
45005008	Ninga Mulungu yakuchonesa wendo wakwe hata chigele fochowile wehi Kilisito hakofa kosoko yetu.
45005009	Ichikulu lugano hambiya, ni kutaliligwa chawelu kwa sakame yakwe, na chihonyigwa kulokela imwene ne inyono ye Mulungu.
45005010	Kosoko inghowa fochowile wanghondo hachilamuliligwa ne Mulungu kulokela difa dye Mwanagwe, nheifo chawelu lugano, kulamuliligwa, na kuhonyigwa kwa wumi wakwe.
45005011	Si nheifo du, ninga chikitunyila Mulungu kulokela Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito, muimwene hambiya chihokela ulamulo.
45005012	No nheifo, kifana wihi fowingile muchilunga kwa njila ya munhu yumwedu, na difa nadyo hadija kwanjila ya wihi, kamei difa hodikwenela kwa wose kosoko wose wagolosa wihi,
45005013	wihi hawuwa muchilunga hata chigele dilagiso disinati dije, ninga wihi usikutaligwa inghowa hechaka ilagiso.
45005014	Ninga difa hadyuwa uko kulawa Adamu mpaka Musa, na hadiwalongosa hata awasigolose wihi ufina wa Adamu umufano wa yuya yakwenda yeje.
45005015	Ninga ichighwa sichifanile wihi uya. Kosoko inghowa matewa wafa kosoko ya kubana kwa munhu yumwedu, nheifo chawelu dihewa dya munhu yumwedu Yesu Kilisito dyongeseka kosoko ya matewa.
45005016	Na ichinghwa chisikifanile wihi uya we munhu yumwedu. Kosoko uliganiso ukwandamila dikosa dye munhu yumwedu na kwigala uliganiso, ninga ichingwa ichene chikwandamila makosa mengi chikwigala kutaliligwa chawelu.
45005017	Kosoko inghowa kwa kubana kwa munhu yumwedu, difa dyenela kosoko ya yuya munhu yumwedu, yokuwa lugano kwawaya wakuhokela dihewa dimemile na chiya ichingwa che chawelu wohala uumi kwayuya munhu yumwedu, Yesu Kilisito.
45005018	Kahi fina uwihi wa munhu yumwedu fowigale difa kuwanhu wose, no nheifo igolosa ya uchawelu wa munhu yumwedu ikwigala uwumi na kulekeleligwa kuwanhu wose.
45005019	Kosoko ya kuleka kuwa na chogoho kwe munhu yumwedu wengi hawagolosa wihi, nheifiya kosoko ya chogoho cha munhu yumwedu wengi wokuwa wachawelu.
45005020	Ninga dilagiso hadingila, hamwedu nadyo ubani hawongeseka, ninga wihi fowongeseke dihewa dye Mulungu hadyongeseka lugano,
45005021	uleke kifana, wihi foukulongosa mudifa, nheifo dihewa nadyo dilongose mukutaliligwa chawelu, kwingila kuwumi wa majuwa gose kulokela Yesu Kilisito Mundewa wetu.
45006001	Togoleni chigambeki? Chigendelele muwihi uleke dihewa dyongeseke?
45006002	Gwe putu! Yokuwa nhani aseye chufile muwihi kahi chuwe womi muwihi?
45006003	Hamumanyile fina chose chibatisigwe mugati ya Kilisito Yesu hachibatisigwa mudifa dyakwe?
45006004	Kwanheifo hachisikigwa hamwedu naye kwa njila ya ubatiso mudifa, uleke kifana Kilisito foyenuke kulawa mudifa kwa itunyo dye Baba, ase nase chigende muusha we uwumi.
45006005	Hambiya halika chihanga naye mudifa kifana idyakwe, chohanga naye kahi mukwinuka kwakwe.
45006006	Chimanya fina unhu wetu wa katali usambasigwa hamwedu naye, uleke umutufi we wihi ubanigwe, uleke chinghowe watumwa wa wihi keli.
45006007	Kosoko imwene iyafile kalekeleligwa kutali ne wihi.
45006008	Ninga inghowa chufa hamwedu na Kilisito chikuhuwila chokwikala hamwedu naye.
45006009	Chimanya fina Kilisito, foyafulusa kwinuligwa mudifa, nghakufa keli; difa dichaka ludole muchanya yakwe keli.
45006010	Kosoko difa dyoyafile hakaufila wihi lumwedu du, ninga uumi woyowile nawo kenawo kosoko ye Mulungu.
45006011	Kosko iyo nanye dogeni muwecho kuwa wafile muwihi womi muKilisito Yesu.
45006012	Kwanheifo, munghaleke wihi ulongose mitufi yenu iikubanika na kuhulikisa sulumisi sakwe.
45006013	Munghagendelele kahi kulafa filungo fyenu fyuwe fiya fya kugolosa wihi, ninga kilafeni muwecho kwe Mulungu kifana wanhu walawile kudifa kwija kuwumi, na kulafa filungo fyenu kwe Mulungu fyuwe fiya fye ichawelu.
45006014	Kosoko iyo wihi wokuwa wichaka ulongosi mugati yenu, kosoko hamuwile hasi ye dilagiso ninga mudihewa.
45006015	Togoleni! Nong'amba chigolose wihi kosoko hachuwile hasi ye dilagiso, ninga hasi ye dihewa? Gwe putu!
45006016	Hamumanyile fina kwayuya wowose womukilafa ukwakwe kifana watumwa wakogoha, mugaluka watumwa ukwakwe wo mukogoha, hegu yuwe wihi ukulongosa kudifa ama chogoho ichikulongosa kuuchawelu?
45006017	Ninga yalumbigwe Mulungu kosoko anyeye, mowile watumwa wo wihi, mugaluka wanhu wakuhulika kulawa kufidoga kugati, amafuso ge umanyi uya womwekigwe hasi yakwe,
45006018	na mulekeleligwa kutali kulawa kuwihi, mugaluka mbiya watumwa we chawelu.
45006019	Nikulonga chimunhumunhu kosoko ye inyuwa yenu ye chimutufi. Kifana fomwakilafile filungo fyenu kuwa watumwa wa kugolosa mbuli so wihi mukulu na mukulusi, nheifo lafeni filungo fyenu fyuwe watumwa we kugolosa ichawelu kwa usunhile.
45006020	Kosoko fomowile watumwa wa wihi hamuwa kutali ne ichawelu.
45006021	Hamupata chotoko chaki majuwa gaya kwa kugolosa mbuli sa chinyala? Indumo ya mbuli aso ni difa.
45006022	Ninga hambiya mulekeleligwa kulawa wihi na kugolosigwa watumwa we Mulungu, chotoko cho mukupata ni usunhile. Na indumo yakwe uwumi wa majuwa gose.
45006023	Kosoko digelo dyo wihi ni difa, ninga ichinghwa che Mulungu ni uwumi wa majuwa gose mugati ya Kilisito Yesu Mundewa wetu.
45007001	Hamumanyile, wandugu sangu, kosoko nikulonga na waya awamanyile dilagiso, fina togoleni dilagiso dikumoha munhu nomo yemumi?
45007002	Ni kifana mwanamuke yatoligwe foyohigwe ne dilagiso kwe mulume nomo ye mumi; ninga mulume yanghafa yakuwa kalekeleligwa ne dilagiso muchanhya ye mulume.
45007003	No nheifo kokwinangwa kena ihabwa inghowa yakwikala na mulume yungi chigele mulume kabaho mumi. Ninga inghowa mulume yeja yafa, basi kalekeligwa ne dilagiso, na halika kotoligwa na mugosi yungi hakudaha yenangwe kena ihabwa.
45007004	No nheifo, wambuya sangu, hamufa mudilagiso kulokela mutufi wa Kilisito, uleke muwe kwa yungi ambaye no imwene yenuligwe mudifa uleke cheleke mamudyo kwe Mulungu.
45007005	Fochowa munhenda se chimutufi, musulumisi we wihi, ukulemana ne dilagiso hachitogoma milimo na kweleka mamudyo ga difa.
45007006	Ninga hambiya chilafigwa kulawa mudilagiso, mudifa idyachikolile muutumwa, uleke chitogome muusha na siyo munyuwa ya katali ye diwandiko, ninga mumikalile misha ye Muhe.
45007007	Hambiya chigambeki kahi? Togoleni idilagiso digaluka wihi? Du hata! Ninga woile si dilagiso sowile nikuumanya wihi, hata sowile nikumanya dilagiso dikugamba, “unghasulumile chinhu che miyago.”
45007008	Ninga wihi haupata luneka kwa diya dilagiso, na kweleka mugati yangu chila usulumisi wihile. Kosoko wihi muhala bila dilagiso ufa.
45007009	Hanuwa mumi fonowile nachaka dilagiso, ninga dikeje adiya dilagiso wihi winuka keli
45007010	kamei honikufa, kamei idilagiso dyonahuwile fina dyokwigala uwumi digaluka ifa ukwangu.
45007011	Kosoko wihi kwa kupata luneka mudilagiso, haunidanhilisa na kulokela didyo hounikoma.
45007012	Kosoko tolati isunhika kahi ne dilagiso ni isunhi na dyachawelu kahi iswanu.
45007013	Togoleni nong'amba idiswanu kahi digaluka ifa ukwangu? Gwe putu? Hawuwa wihi, wendeunikoma mugati yangu kulokela gaya maswanu, uleke wihi woneke fina ni wihi, na fina kulokela dilagiso uwe wihi wihise lugano.
45007014	Kosoko chimanya fina dilagiso ni kosoko ya kugati ye muhe; ninga aniye nuwa mumutufi, niguligwe muutumwa we wihi.
45007015	Sikimanya chonikugolosa nimwecho. Kosoko agaya gonikuhananga nigolosa sikugolosa, ninga nikugolosa agaya gonisikuhananga.
45007016	Hambiya inghowa nikugolosa agaya gonisikwenda, nikudifumila dilagiso fina ni swanu.
45007017	Ninga chawelu siniye nikwenda kugolosa gano, ninga uwihi uya wuwile mugati yangu.
45007018	Kosko nimanya fina mwichaka uswanu wowose ukwikala mugati yangu, uwile mumutufi wangu. Kugolosa diswanu dyonikuhananga, ninga sikudaha kudigolosa.
45007019	Kosoko sikugolosa diswanu dyonikuhananga, ninga dihile dyonisikwenda kugolosa.
45007020	Hambiya halika nikugolosa idyosikwenda, basi siniye muchidoga changu nikugolosa, ninga uwihi uya wuwile mugati yangu.
45007021	Hambiya nyona fina nomo nikuhanaga nigolose dilagiso, kwina dihile dikunijila.
45007022	Kosoko nikudibwedelela dilagiso dye Mulungu mugati yangu,
45007023	ninga nikona mufilungo fyangu ilagiso dingi dikitowa ne chidoga changu, na kunigolosa niye mutumwa kwilagiso dye wihi adiya dikwikala mugati ye filungo fyangu.
45007024	Usungu wangu mukiwa nikufilaki niye! Nani yakwenda yanihonye kulawa mumutufi awu we difa?
45007025	Nikumulumba Mulungu kulokela Yesu Kilisito Mundewa wetu! Hambiya inghowa nonheifo basi niye mumisungu yangu nikuditogomela dilagiso dye Mulungu, ninga mumutufi nigaluka namutumwa wa ilagiso dya wihi.
45008001	Hambiya hechaka uliganiso kwa waya woile mugati ya Kilisito Yesu.
45008002	Kosoko dilagiso dye Muhe we uwumi wuwile mugati ya Kilisito Yesu unika hatali ne dilagiso dye wihi ne difa.
45008003	Kosoko Mulungu kagolosa gahunguligwe ne dilagiso kosoko ye umutufi we chimunhu kwa njila ya kumwigala Mwanagwe imwecho kwa futa ya uunhu une wihi uleke yauleuse wihi na kuuliganisa chimutufi.
45008004	Uleke agakuhanangigwa mwilagiso gamemelekele mugati yetu seye, chikugenda si kwa mutufi, ninga kwa Muhe na kwika fidoga fyetu musimbuli se chimuhe.
45008005	Kosko awaya wakwandamila mitufi weka fidoga fyawo musimbuli se chimutufi, ninga awaya wakwandamila mutufi weka fidoga fyawo Mumuhe.
45008006	Kosoko chidoga che mutufi ni difa, ninga chidoga cha Muhe ni wumi na digoya.
45008007	Kosoko iyo, ichidoga chikwandamila mutufi ni chinghondo kwe Mulungu, kosoko hachikudaha kufumila dilagiso dye Mulungu na chisikwija chifumila.
45008008	Na wose awakwandamila mitufi wasikudaha kumwedesa Mulungu.
45008009	Ninga inghowa Muhe we Mulungu yakwikala mugati yenu, basi nyeye musikwandamila mutufi, ninga Muhe. Munhu wowose yechaka Muhe wa Kilisito ayo siyo wakwe..
45008010	Ninga inghowa Kilisito kowa mugati yenu, basi mutufi wufa kosoko ye wihi, na Muhe wa mumi kosoko ye ichawelu.
45008011	Inghowa Muhe wakwe imwene iyamwinule Yesu Kilisito muchilalo ukwikala mugati yenu, imwene iyamwinule Yesu Kilisito kulawa muchilalo komwinghani wumi mumitufi yenu yuwile mukufa kwa kulokela Muhe wakwe iyakwikala mugati yenu.
45008012	Hambiya wandugu sangu, chikudaigwa, siyo chimutufi, ninga chikale chimutufi,
45008013	kosoko inghowa ukugenda kwa kwandamila mutufi, mukuhananga kufa; ninga inghowa mukwandamila Muhe na kukoma nhenda sihile se chimutufi, mokuwa womi.
45008014	Kosoko wose wakulongosigwa ne Muhe we Mulungu awo no wana we Mulungu.
45008015	Kosoko musihokele muhe wa chitumwa na manhonge, ninga muhe wa kugoloswa wana. Nomo chikulila “Aba! Nong'amba Baba!”
45008016	Muhe imwecho yakuhomelela hamwedu ne fidoga fyetu, fina aseye cha wana we Mulungu,
45008017	na inghowa cha wana kahi cha wahasi, wahasi we Mulungu hamwedu na Kilisito, inghowa chikusambasika ni uleke chije chitunyigwe hamwedu na imwene.
45008018	Nikona fina magayo ge chigele chino gasifanile ne ditunyo dyonikwija nipata chigele cho kugubuligwa kwakwe ukwetu.
45008019	Kosoko fyumbe fyose fikugojela kwa nghwina lugano ulugubulo lwe wana we Mulungu;
45008020	Kosoko fiyumbe fyose hafikiigwa hasi ye uliganiso, siyo fofikwenda ifyecho, ninga foyakwenda imwene iyafikile hasi, mwihuwi.
45008021	Kosoko fyumbe ifyecho nafyo fyolekeleligwa kulawa muutumwa wo kudoda, uleke fipate indekelelwa ye ditunyo dya wana we Mulungu.
45008022	Chimanya fina fyumbe fyose fikugula usungu hamwedu mpaka hambiya;
45008023	ninga siyo du fiyumbe, ninga hata seye chiwecho, ichine mamudyo gaya ge nghonga ge Muhe, chikugula na kugojela kugoloswa kwetu, uhonya we mitufi yetu.
45008024	Kosoko kwa ihuwilo hachihonyigwa. Hambiya ihuwiso idikoneka si ihuwiso kahi, kosoko nani yakugendelele kuhuwila ichinhu chifuluse kwija?
45008025	Ninga inghowa chikuhuwila ichinhu ichisikoneka, basi chikuchigojela kwa ufinyilisi.
45008026	No nheifo na Muhe naye yakuchitasa mukuhungukiligwa kwetu; kosoko chisidahile kutasa ifene fo ikuhanangigwa, ninga Muhe imwecho yakuchitasila mbuli nghugutu na hata kwa kulila.
45008027	Na Imulungu iyakulanga mimoyo, kamanya ichidoga che Muhe kuwatasila wasunhile kwa kwandamila ifene foyakwenda Mulungu.
45008028	Chimanya fina musimbuli sose, Mulungu yakutogoma milimo hamwedu na maswanu na waya awakumwenda, awenangigwe kwa nyenda yakwe.
45008029	Kosoko awaya yawamanyile kulawa katali, hakawasagula, wowe futa kifana ye Mwanagwe, uleke yowe Nghulahanju mugati ya wandugu wengi.
45008030	Kahi awaya woyawasagule kulawa katali hakawenanga; na waya woyenange hakawatalila chawelu; na waya woyewatalile chawelu kahi hakawatunya.
45008031	Togoleni chigambeki musimbuli sino? iMulungu yanghowa ulwandi lwetu, nani yokuwa muchanhya yetu?
45008032	Imwene inghamulekelele Mwanagwe, ninga hakamulafa kosoko yetu, togoleni nghochinga chila chochikuhanaga?
45008033	Nani yakwenda yawalahe awasaguligwe ne Mulungu? iMulungu no ya watalilile chawelu.
45008034	Nani yakwenda yawaliganise? Si Yesu Kilisito yafile, heye, imwene yenuligwe muchilalo, yowile mukono we kulume we Mulungu, iyakuchitasila
45008035	Nani yakwenda yachibagule seye no wendo wa Kilisito? Wokuwa ukuguguti, ama tabu, hegu magayo, ama njala, au sakasa, ukomikomi, hegu ipanga?
45008036	Fina foitulumigwe kugamba, “Kosoko yako chikukomigwa chilo na misi; chikoneka kifana ngholo sa kuchinjigwa.”
45008037	Gwe putu, musimbuli sose sino aseye cha wasumi kahi kuloka awasumi kwa kulokela imwene iyachendile.
45008038	Kosoko hambiya nimanya fina sidifa, hegu wumi, ama malaika, kahi si mukulu wa isi, ifihambiya hegi ifikwija, hechaka udaha,
45008039	agekuchanhya kahi agehasi, ama chochose chumbigwe ichikudaha kunibagula ne wendo we Mulungu mu Kilisisto Yesu Mundewa wetu.
45009001	Nikulonga ichawelu mugati ya Kilisito, na ninga sikudanha; chidoga changu chikunihomelela ne Muhe Musunhile.
45009002	Nina usungu lugano na magayo agasikuhela mumoyo wangu.
45009003	Kosoko nikutasa hata niye nimwecho nidahe kusamisigwa na kutagigwa kutali na Kilisito kosoko ya wandugu sangu, wandugu we chimutufi.
45009004	Awano ni Waisilaeli, awagoloswe kuwa wana na wanhu we ditunyo ne dilagano, na kwinghigwa dilagiso, na kumufuga Mulungu, na mahuwiso gakwe;
45009005	awene no wene waBaba, na kulawa muwene kwa kwandamila mutufi nomo yalawile masihi iyejile muchanhya ya wose, iyakutunyigwa majuwa gose. Hano.
45009006	Siyo kugamba fina imbuli ye Mulungu idugikana. Kosoko si Waisilaeli wose ni walawile muisilaeli
45009007	na kahi siwose ni wana wa chawelu wa Ibulahimu; ninga, “Kwa kulokela Isaka wana wako wokwinangigwa.”
45009008	Ayino sikugamba fina wose wana we chimutufi ni wana we Mulungu, ninga awana we dihuwiso wakutaligwa fina ni wana wa welekwa.
45009009	Kosoko nhafi nofodikulonga dihuwiso kugamba, “Muchigele chikifane chino nokuya na Sala kokuwa na mwana.”
45009010	Ninga si nheifo du; chinhu chikifane chicho hachigoloseka kwa Lebeka, ugele foyowile na inda ye wanagwe kwe mugosi wakwe yumwedu, iBaba yetu Isaka.
45009011	Hata fowowile wekali kwelekigwa, na kugolosa mbuli yoyose swanu au ihile ( uleke nyenda ya Mulungu yo kusagula igendelele,
45009012	siyo kwa nhenda, ninga kwa lwinango lwakwe) mwanamuke yuya hakatamiligwa fina, “Mukulu komutogomela mudodo.”
45009013	Fina foitulumwe, “Nimwenda Yakobo ninga Esau nimudesekela.”
45009014	Togoleni hambiya chogambaki? Mulungu kena kwendelela? Du hata!
45009015	Kosoko hakamugamba Musa, “Nomonela ubasi ayuya wonikumonela ubasi, kahi nomonela usungu ayuya wonikumonela usungu.”
45009016	Hambiya siyo du kwa chimunhumunhu kahi kwa kwenda kwa munhu, ninga kwe Mulungu iyakonesa ubasi.
45009017	Kosoko matulumo gagamba kwa Falao, “Hanikwinula gweye kwasoko ya konesa udaha wangu ukwako, uleke disina dyangu ditagusigwe muchilunga chose.”
45009018	Hakamonesa ubasi wakwe kwa yuya woyasagule imwecho, na kuiguma ukugutu mimoyo ya waya woyasagule.
45009019	Wamonga wonigamba, “halika no nheifo nhani ho yekali yakulonga muchanhya ya wihi wa wanhu? Nonani yodaha kulemesa nyenda yakwe?”
45009020	Ninga agweye kwanani ukudaha kuwanga ne Mulungu? Togoleni Mumbi kodaha kuwanga ne ichumbo? Chumbo chigambe, “Nhani gweye unyumbile kifana nhafi?”
45009021	Ama imumbi nong'amba kechaka udaha muulongo, siyakuliganisa du awuno niugolosele chinhu achi na wuno nogolosele chiya cha itunyo?
45009022	Chogolosa choni inghowa Mulungu yanghamua konesa inyono yakwe ne udaha wakwe, kwa ufinyilisi mukulu hakakilondela na fiya fiya foyagolose fifuluse kubanigwa;
45009023	na yokuwa nhani ighowa kagolosa nheifo uleke yonese ugoli we ditunyo dyakwe kufiya fyoyonele ubasi, foyagolose kulawa katali fyuwe na itunyo;
45009024	hata seye si hakachinanga, siyo kwa Wayahudi du, ninga hata na Wamembe?
45009025	Hata nheifo yakugamba muchitabu cha Hosea, “Awaya wasowile wanhu wangu nowenanga wanhu wangu, na inghendigwe nomwinanga mwendigwa.”
45009026	“Kamei yokuwa ahanhu wenagwe, ‘Siyo wanhu wangu,’ wokwinangigwa wana we Mulungu ye mumi.”
45009027	Hata Isaya yakulila soko ya waisilaeli, “Chinghatala waisilaeli ni matewa kifana isanga ye bahali, ninga wakefu wakwija wahonyigwa,
45009028	kosoko Mundewa kogolosa fina foyalongile imbuli yakwe na kuimalagisa chimwande kwa chawelu.”
45009029	Na kifana Isaya foyagonese, “Inghowa Mundewa we inghondo woile nghachilekele cheleko hachisomigwa moto kifana Sodoma na kugolosigwa kifana Gomola.”
45009030	Togoleni hambiya chigambeki? Awamembe wanhu wasimanyile chawelu, waipata ichawelu kwa kulokela dihuwi;
45009031	ninga awaisilaeli wamanyile ichawelu, yuwile mudilagiso, wasumigwa kudimemelesa dilagiso diya.
45009032	Nhani? Ni kosoko hawandamile dilagiso diya kwa njila ya ihuwi, ninga kwa nhenda sawo. Watowa nghwalo mwiwe dya munghanda,
45009033	fina foitulumwe, “Langeni nikwika diwe Musayuni, iwe dikutowesa wanhu nghwalo, ikangalawe dikuwagolosa wogwe, kahi wowose yakumuhuwila imwene nghegumigwa chinyala.”
45010001	Wandugu sangu, kwenda kwe umoyo wangu ne inhasa kwe Mulungu ni kosoko yenu mudahe kuhonyigwa.
45010002	Kosoko nikudaha kuwahomelela fina, wena ludole kwe Mulungu, ninga wasigumigwe ujelu.
45010003	Kosoko inghowa hawaimanyile ichawelu ikulawa kwe Mulungu, na kuhananga kukongha chawelu yawo awecho, wamwichaka muchawelu ye Mulungu.
45010004	Kosoko Kilisito no ndumo ye dilagiso, uleke chila yakuhuwila yataliligwe chawelu.
45010005	Musa hakatuluma muchanhya ye ichawelu ikulawa mwilagiso, kugamba, “Munhu iyakugolosa didyo kokwikala na kugenda mudidyo.”
45010006	Ninga ichawelu iya ikulawa mwihuwi ikugamba, “Unghagambe kumoyo wako nani yokwila kulanga?” (uleke, yamwigale Kilisito hasi)
45010007	ama, “Nani yodulika mpaka hasihasisi?” (uleke yamukwise Kilisito kuchanhya kulawa kwa wafile).
45010008	Ninga igambigwaki? “Imbuli yahabehi nagwe, mumilomo yako na mumoyo wako.” (nong'amba, imbuli aiya ye dihuwi yochikutagusa);
45010009	Kosoko unghalamba kwa mulomo wako fina Yesu ni Mundewa na kuhuwila kugati yo moyo wako fina Mulungu hakamwinula kulawa muchilalo, kohonyigwa.
45010010	Kosoko kwa moyo munhu yakuhuwila na kupata ichawelu, na kwa mulomo yakulamba na kuhonyigwa.
45010011	Matulumo gakugamba nhafi, “Hechaka yamuhuwile kamei yagumigwa chinyala.”
45010012	Kosoko hechaka Muyahudi hegu Muyunani imwene ni Mundewa wa wose, yakuwengha wose wakumwinanga kwa undewa.
45010013	Kosoko, “Chila yakwinanga mwisina dye Mundewa kohonyigwa.”
45010014	Ninga womwinanga nhani munhu awasimuhuwile? Kahi womuhuwila finhani munhu wasimuhulike? Hata nheifo womuhulika nhani bila munhu kuwahubiliya?
45010015	Kahi wohubili nhani bila kwigaligwa? Fina foitulumigwe, “Ni miswanu lugano migulu yawo waya awakwigala imbuli swanu!”
45010016	Ninga si wose waihulikise imbuli swanu; kosoko mugonesi Isaya yakugamba, “Mundewa nani yahuwile simbuli setu?”
45010017	Hambiya nong'amba, dihuwi dikwija kwa njila ya kuhulika, na kuhulika kukwigaligwa ne imbuli ya Kilisito.
45010018	Ninga nikusa togoleni hawahulike? Du wahulika; kosoko, “Majwi gawo gahulikika muchilunga chose, na mbuli sawo kundumo ye chilunga.”
45010019	Keli kahi nikusa, waisilaeli wasimanyile? Kunghonga Musa hakagamba, “Nowaguma finju awanhu awasiditaifa; hamwedu na ditaifa dibwalate nowaguma nyono.”
45010020	Kamei Isaya yakulonga kwa nghinyo kugamba, “Nyonekana kuwanhu awasendewanikongha; nikionesa kwa wanhu wasinusile.”
45010021	Ninga kwa waisilaeli yakugamba, “Misi na chilo haniwanyooshela mikono yangu wanhu wasikuhulika na wechaka chihuliko.”
45011001	Hambiya, nikusa, togoleni Mulungu hakawalema wanhu wakwe? Gwe putu! Aniye du nimwecho namuisilaeli, mwana wa lukolo lwa Ibulahimu, nilawa mwikabila dya Benyamini.
45011002	Mulungu nghawalemile wanhu wakwe woyawamanyile kulawa katali. Nghumanyile matulumo fogakulonga muchanhya ya Eliya, ifene foyawasongese awaisilaeli hamwende ye Mulungu? Yakugamba,
45011003	“Mundewa wawakoma awagonesi wako, wamola ahanhu ho kufugila; nisigala niye niwaiyeka, nawo wanikongha wanikome.”
45011004	Ninga Mulungu hakamubidula nhani? “Niikikila fugasi ya wanhu figulu mutandatu awasikumufugamila Baali.”
45011005	Hambiya no nheifo kwa chigele chino cha hambiya, kwina wanhu wasigala, wasaguligwa kwa mboto.
45011006	Ninga inghowa kwa mboto, basi ichaka haja ya kutogomela milimo, hegu mboto ileke kuwa mboto.
45011007	Yanhani hambiya? Awaisilaeli wasumwa kupata chiya chowendewakonha. Ninga awaya wasaguligwe hawachipata, ninga wasigale hawowa wakugutu,
45011008	fina foitulumwe kugamba, “Mulungu hakawengha muhe wa ukugutu, wena meso ninga wasikona na nghutwi ninga wasikuhulika, mpaka diyelo.”
45011009	Kahi Daudi yakugamba, “Chakudiya chawo na chuwe italuma na mutego, hanhu ho kutowa nghwalo na maliho ukwawo;
45011010	meso gawo gowe lwisa uleke wanghone, ne migongo yawo igonje chigele chose.”
45011011	Hambiya nikusa, togoleni watowa nghwalo na kugwa? Gwe putu! Ninga kulokela kutowa nghwalo kwawo uhonya hauwijila wamembe, uleke kuwengha finju awaisislaeli.
45011012	Hambiya halika kutowa nghwalo kwawo, kwigala ugoli kuchilunga, basi na kusumwa kwawo kwigala ugoli Kuwamembe, hambiya siikuwa lugano kuumemi wawo!
45011013	Ninga nikulonga na nyeye Muwamembe. Foinimutumigwa wa Wamembe, nikutunya umulimo wangu
45011014	uleke niwagume finju Awayahudi wayangu, nhegele nohonya wamonga.
45011015	Kosoko inghowa kulema kwawo kwigala kulewanisa kwe chilunga, ninga kuhokeligwa kwawo yokuwa yoni halika siyo umi wawo chigele cho kufa!
45011016	Inghowa mamudyo ga kulafigwa kunghonga ni masunhile, nheifo ne mugunda wose ugaluka muswanu, kosoko inghowa idisina dye dibiki disunhika basi ne manhambi nago gasunhika.
45011017	Ninga inghowa manhambi gamonga hagadumuligwa, kamei agweye go museituni wa kumbago kuhandigwa mugati yawo, basi kugaluka muhangi nagwe ukuhanga umemi lwe ugoli we dibiki,
45011018	unghakitunyile mumanhambi. Kosoko unghakitunya, gelegela fina siyo no gweye ukudahisa idisina dye dibiki, ninga idisina idyecho no dikukudahisa gweye.
45011019	Nhegela kogamba, “Manhambi hagadumuligwa uleke nikigwe niye.”
45011020	Ayo ni chawelu. Kuwa hagadumuligwa kosoko ya kuleka kuhuwila kwawo, ninga gweye ukwima kosoko ye dihuwi du. Hambiya unghowe mwiyoni, ninga ukilangisise.
45011021	Kosoko inghowa Mulungu nghagalekile manhambi agecho ge dibiki, nhegela hakwanga yakuleke nagweye.
45011022	Uutange uswanu ne ufinyilisi we Mulungu: Ufinyilisi kuwanya wogwile, ninga uswanu we Mulungu ukwenu, ukuwagolosa nyeye mugendelele muuswanu wakwe; sinheifo nhegela anye nanye nhanga du mudumuligwe.
45011023	Hambiya hata awamonga muisilaeli, woile wahuwile nhanga wengisigwe, kosoko Mulungu kena ludole lwa kuwengisa keli.
45011024	Kosoko inghowa kudumuligwa kulawa hanhu howoile katali hene museituni wa kumbago na kwingisigwa kwingi kusikwawo, ninga kumuseituni umuswanu, siikuwa lugano kwawaya awemuseituni wawo wa katali kwingisigwa ukwawo.
45011025	Hambiya mungheje mukigamba mwina misungu kusuma fomuwile wandugu sangu, nikuhananga mumanye ichifiso chino fina ukugutu uwejila wanhu wa Isilaeli, mpaka Awamembe wowe wengi awakwingila.
45011026	Kwanheifo awaisilaeli wose wohonyigwa; fina foitulumigwe, “Mwihula kokwija kulawa Sayuni kobana isimbuli sihile kulawa kwa Yakobo;
45011027	na adino dyokuwa ilagano dyangu hamwedu nawo nomonikuwaleusila wihi wawo.”
45011028	Kosoko ye imbuli swanu wagaluka wanghondo we Mulungu, kosoko yenu; ninga kwa kusaguligwa wagaluka wendigwa kosoko ya waBaba sawo.
45011029	Kosoko fighwa ne lwinango lwe Mulungu lwichaka chibidubidu.
45011030	kifana katali fomowile mwichaka chihuliko kwe Mulungu, ninga hambiya muhokela ubasi kosoko ya kuwachaka chihuliko kwawo,
45011031	Hambiya wagaluka wasikwenda kuhulika, uleke kwa ubasi wonesigwe ukwenu nawo wauhokele.
45011032	Kosoko Mulungu kawomba wanhu wowe nheifo uleke yonese ubasi wakwe kwa wose.
45011033	Kusi ye ugoli no ubala ne misungu yakwe Mulungu! Isiikudaha kusakuligwa, nani yodaha kuumanya uliganiso lwakwe ne sinjila sakwe!
45011034	“Kosoko nonani yachimanyile ichidoga che Mundewa, ama nani yakudaha kuwa mulolesi wakwe?”
45011035	“Hegu nani yekudaha kumwingha ichinghwa yamuwisile?”
45011036	Kosoko kulawa muimwene na kulokela imwene finhu fyose fyumbigwa. Ditunyo dina imwene majuwa gose. Hano.
45012001	Hambiya nikuwatasani wandugu sangu, kwa ubasi wa Mulungu, lafeni mitufi yenu yuwe kifana nhambiko imumi isunhile, kahi ikuhokeligwa kwe Mulungu, ayo no ifuga yenu ye chimuhe.
45012002	Munghandamile mbuli se chilunga chino, ninga muwe washa mufidonga fyenu mudahe kutanga go yakwenda Mulungu, kahi goni amaswanu na gamemelekele.
45012003	Na kosoko ya mboto yo ninghigwe ne Mulungu, nikumuhananga chila munhu ukwenu yanghakiyone imwene munhu mukulu lugano kusuma foyakuhanangigwa yowe, ninga yakiyone musindamafu na yalamule ifene foikuhanagigwa mudihuwi dyoyenghigwe ne Mulungu.
45012004	Kosoko mumutufi umwedu china filungo fingi na filungo fyose fisikutogoma mulimo umwedu,
45012005	nheifo ase nase cha wengi ninga cha mutufi umwedu mugati ya Kilisito, chila munhu na miyagwe.
45012006	Chine ifinghwa fisiligane, kosoko ye imboto yakwe yo yachinghile chitogomele; inghowa ugonesi basi chiugolose kwa dihuwi dyetu
45012007	Inghowa kutogoma, chitogome na iyakufusa na yafuse,
45012008	iyakujama na yajame, iyakulafa na yalafe kwa undewa. Iyakutasa na yagolose yanghasoke; iyakonela wanhu ubasi na yagolose kwa chinyemi.
45012009	Wendo umeme, desekeleni wihi, koleni lugano amaswanu;
45012010	wendo lwe chindugu uwe mugati ya chila munhu na miyagwe, kiyoneseni chogoho nyenye kwa nyenye.
45012011	Munghowe wadoba, ninga muwe na ludole mumimuhe yenu kumutogomela Mulungu.
45012012	Bwedeleleni mwihuwi, muwe wafinyilisi mumagayo, wanhu wa mataso.
45012013	Lafeni finhu fyenu muwatase awasunhile, yuweni wandewa kuwageni.
45012014	Wamoteseni awaya wakuwasambasafibi; wamoteseni munghawaligitise.
45012015	Bwedeleleni na waya awakubwedelela, lileni na waya awakulila.
45012016	Mwikale kwa kifumilisa munhu na miyagwe, munghadoge makulu, ninga goloseni na amadodogi nago, yuweni waholo kahi munghakiyone fina mwina ubala kusuma wayenu.
45012017	Munghakilihe wihi kwa wihi, ninga amaswanu kumwande ya wanhu wose.
45012018	Inghadahika, kuulwandi lwenu, kaleni digoya na wanhu wose.
45012019	Wandugu, munghakilihe wihi nyenye kwa nyenye, ninga lekeni inyono ye Mulungu imwecho ilamule, kosoko itulumwa fina “Maliho ga wihi kwa wihi ni gangu nimwecho noliha, yakulonga Mundewa.”
45012020	Sinheifo du, “Ninga hata inghowa wanghondo wako wena njala wenghe chakudiya; wena nghilu wenghe meji, kosoko kwa kugolosa nheifo ukuwagumila moto wa makala mumatwi gawo.”
45012021	Munghasumwe ne wihi, ninga usumeni wihi kwa uswanu.
45013001	Chila munhu yawahulike awene ludole, kosoko hechaka ludole uusilawile kwe Mulungu; hata uya wibaho ulawa kwe Mulungu.
45013002	Hambiya munhu wowose yakulemana ne ludole uwo yakulemana ne Mulungu iyawikile, nawo wakulemana na uwo wohokela uliganiso.
45013003	Kosoko awakulongosa hawakutowa wanhu kosoko ya nhenda swanu, ninga sihile. Ukuhananga uwe munhu yechaka chogoho ne wasilikali? Golosa maswanu na kohokela ditunyo dyakwe;
45013004	Kosoko imwene ni mutogomi we Mulungu ukwako kosoko ya maswanu. Ninga inghowa ukugolosa gehile gowogoha, kosoko uludole wusikulonda dipanga bila mbuli ihile! Kosoko ni mutogomi we Mulungu yakumuliha chila imugolosa wihi.
45013005	Hambiya ukuhanangigwa uhulikise, siyo du kosoko ya kogoha, ninga kwa chidoga.
45013006	Kosoko ya iyo mukuliha kodi, kosoko awene ludole ni watogomi wa Mulungu wakiidasa musimbuli sino.
45013007	Liheni gose agakuhanangigwa na wene, munhu wa kodi mwingheni kodi yakwe, munhu wa ushulu mwingheni ushulu wakwe, munhu wa chogoho mwingheni chogoho.
45013008	Munghadaiigwe chinhu na munhu wowose ninga, kiyendeni nyenye kwa nyenye, kosoko iyakumwende miyagwe kamemelesa dilagiso.
45013009	Kosoko dilagiso digamba, “Unghagolose dihabwa, unghakome, unghahije; unghasulumile”; na malagiso goose gohigwa mwimbuli imwedu nayo ni “Mwende miyago fona foikiyenda gomwecho.”
45013010	Wendo lusikumugolosela munhu mbuli ihile, hambiya nong'amba wendo no umemesi we dilagiso.
45013011	Chinghaleka gago, ninga manyeni ichigele, fina ugele wo kugona hambiya uhela inukeni musinhongo. Kosoko uhonya uchisegelela hambiya kusuma fochowile chikali kuhuwila;
45013012	chilo chigendelela lugano, misi yahabehi. Chileke simbuli se chisa na kufala filama fye ujelu;
45013013	chigendeni kwa uswanu kifana wanhu wa hemisi, siyo kwa ukobo na ulefi wa gimbi, siyo kwa mbuli sihile na dihabwa, na kugomba na finju.
45013014	Ninga, mufaleni Mundewa Yesu Kilisito, na muunghaulange mutufi na kwaka kwa usulumisi wakwe wihile.
45014001	Wahokeleni waya wahungukiligwe mwihuwi, ninga munghalemane na madonga gawo.
45014002	Wamonga wakuhuwile kudiya chila chinhu, chigele wamonga wakwenda mboga muhala.
45014003	Awakudiya wanghawabese awasikudiya, naye inghakudiya yanghamubese inghadiile, kosoko Mulungu kamuhokela.
45014004	Agweye nonani ukwenda kumuliganisa mutogomi wa miyago? KweMundewa wakwe imwecho yakwima au yakugwa. Ninga kokwinuligwa kosoko Mundewa yakudaha kumwinula.
45014005	Wamonga wakuliganisa fina, dijuwa dimonga iswanu lugano kusuma dimonga, chigele wamonga wakuliganisa majuwa gose fina galigana. Chila munhu na yatange mumisungu yakwe imwecho.
45014006	Awaya wakukola majuwa, wakugakola na kugatunya kosoko ye Mundewa, na waya wakudiya wakudiya mwitunyo dye Mundewa, kosoko wakumwingha ilumbo Mulungu, na yuya inghakudiya nghadiile mwitunyo dye Mundewa, naye yakumulumba Mulungu.
45014007	Kosoko hechaka munhu mugati yetu iyakwikala kosoko yakwe imwecho, kahi hachikufa kosoko yetu chiwecho,.
45014008	Inghowa chikwikala chikwikala kosoko ye Mundewa, na inghowa chikufa chikufa kosoko ye Mundewa; basi hambiya, yuwe chufa ama chikwikala, aseye chawanhu wakwe Mundewa.
45014009	Kosoko Kilisito hakofa na kwinuka yekale keli, uleke yowe Mundewa wa fyose fyufile na ifyumi.
45014010	Nhani umuliganise imunduguso? Ama nhani gweye umubese munduguso? Kosoko chose chikwija chikwima hamwende ye uliganiso we Mulungu.
45014011	Kosoko itulumigwa, “Fina fonikwikala yakulonga Mundewa, chila ifindi dyofugama hamwande yangu, na chila ilimi dyotunya kulamba Mulungu.”
45014012	Basi hambiya, chila yumwedu wetu kolafa nhala yakwe kwe Mulungu.
45014013	Hambiya chileke kiliganisa chiwecho, ninga ibeka mulamule fina munhu yanghamukwakwalise miyagwe na kumukinya hegu kumuhindila njila.
45014014	Nimanya kahi, nitanga MwiMundewa Yesu fina hechaka chinhu chelekigwe chinyamafu, ninga chigaluka chinyamafu kosoko munhu kadoga fina ni chinyamafu, na chawelu ukwakwe munhu yo ni chinyamafu.
45014015	Inghowa mundugu sako yakubulagigwa ne fyakudiya fyoukudiya, kugaluka hukugenda muuwendo. Unghaleke fyakudiya fyoukudiya fimudese miyago, kosoko Kilisito hakofa kosoko ya yuyo naye.
45014016	Uswanu wako unghalongigwe kuwa wihi.
45014017	Kosoko undewa we Mulungu siyo kudiya na kunywa, ninga ichawelu ne digoya, kamei ne chinyemi mwiMuhe Musunhile.
45014018	Kosoko iyakumutogomela Kilisito mugago, ayo kahokeligwa ne Mulungu na kufumiligwa na wanhu.
45014019	Chandamile mbuli sa digoya, uswanu na mbuli sikujenga.
45014020	Unghaibane milimo ye Mulungu kosoko ya chakudiya. Chawelu fyose ni fiswanu, ninga fiha kwa yuya iyakuwakwakwalisa wayagwe kosoko ya fyakudiya fyakwe.
45014021	Yokuwa ibeka uleke kudiya, inghowa kudiya kwako kukuwakwakwalisa na kuwagolosa wayago wogwe.
45014022	Dihuwi diya dyowinadyo, uwe nadyo mumoyo wako gomwecho hamwande ye Mulungu. Ibeka awaya awechaka soko ya kiliganisa kosoko ya gaya gowakufumila.
45014023	Ninga waya wene manhonge waliganisigwa nomowakudiya, kosoko wasikugolosa kwa ihuwi. Na chila idisikulawa mwihuwi ni wihi.
45015001	Hambiya chikuhanangigwa seye chine ludole, chikilonde na waya wechaka ludole, na siyo kiendesa chiwecho du.
45015002	Chila yumwedu wetu yamwendese miyagwe uleke chijenge undugu.
45015003	Kosoko hata Kilisito nghakiyendese imwecho muhala, ninga fina foitulumwe, “Maligo gawo gowakuligile gweye haganugwila niye.”
45015004	Kosoko gose gatulumigwe chigele chilokile, hakatulumigwa kuchilolesa seye, uleke kwa ufinyilisi na kuguma moyo kwa njila ya matulumo chidahe kuwa na ihuwilo.
45015005	Mulungu we ufinyilisi na mugumi we moyo yawengheni kwikala muuhamwendu munhu na miyagwe, kifana Kilisito Yesu,
45015006	uleke kwa hamwedu na ijwi dimwedu mudahe kumutunya Mulungu na Baba we Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito.
45015007	Kihokeleni nyenye kwa nyenye, kifana Kilisito foyawahokeleni nyeye mwitunyo dye Mulungu.
45015008	Kosoko nikumutamilani fina Kilisito kagaluka mutogomi we dilagano dyo kufinigwa kosoko ye chawelu ye Mulungu uleke yadahe konesa mahuwiso galafigwe ne waBaba.
45015009	Kahi uleke Awamembe wadahe kumutunya Mulungu kwa ubasi wakwe. Fina foitulumigwe, “Kwanheifo nokulumba mugati ya Wamembe, na kwimba matunyo ge disina dyako.”
45015010	Kahi yakugamba, “Bwedeleleni, nyenye Muwamembe, hamwedu na wanhu wakwe;”
45015011	na kahi, “Mutunyeni Mundewa, anye mose Muwamembe, na wanhu wose wamutunye;”
45015012	Na kahi Isaya yakugamba, “Mulukolo lwa Yese kolawa munhu yokwinula na kulongosa Wamembe; umwakwe Wamembe wohuwila.”
45015013	Mulungu we dihuwi yawengheni mose chinyemi, ne digoya mukuhuwila, uleke mwikale mwihuwi kwa ludole lwa Muhe Musunhile.
45015014	Aniye nimwecho nifumiliswa muchanhya yenu nyenye wandugu sangu fina nyenye nanye mumema uswanu, na ubala wose, na fina mudaha kilolesa munhu na miyagwe.
45015015	Hata nheifo mbuli simonga niwawandikila kwa ludole lugano uleke kuwagelegesa, soko ye dihuwi diya dyoninghigwe ne Mulungu
45015016	kuwa mutogomi wa Kilisito Yesu Kuwamembe muutambiki nimugolosele milimo imbuli swanu ye Mulungu, uleke filafwa fya Wamembe fidahe kuhokeligwa, kwa kutambikiligwa na Muhe Musunhile.
45015017	Mu Kilisito Yesu, nina soko ya kitunyila milimo yangu kwe Mulungu.
45015018	Kosoko sikugesa kulonga mbuli ingi, ninga ayiya du yoyamalagise Kilisito, uleke Wamembe wafumile na kuhulika kwa mbuli ama kwa nhenda.
45015019	Kwa ludole lwa fitangilo na majumo, kulokela ludole lwe Muhe Musunhile, igaluka kulawa Yelusalemu mpaka Ililiko, nihubili lugano mbuli swanu ya Kilisito.
45015020	Kwanheifo nikiyoha lugano kuihubili mbuli swanu, ninga ninghaihubili hanhu Kilisito yafuluse kuhubiliigwa, uleke ninghajenge muchanhya ya nghindiso ya munhu yungi;
45015021	ninga fina foitulumigwe, “Awaya wasihubiliigwe mbuli sakwe wokona, na waya awasihulike womanya.”
45015022	Nochileka nikulemesigwa chila fonikuhananga kwija ukwenu.
45015023	Ninga hambiya nichaka hanhu kahi mumikowa ino, kwa chipisi chitali hambiya nikuhananga kwija ukwenu
45015024	nomonikuluta Hisipaniya. Kosoko nikuhuwila fina nowonani munhambo yangu na kwigaligwa na nyenye, hanuwa na chinyemi lugano kuwa hamwedu na nyenye kwa chipisi chiguhi.
45015025	Kwa hambiya, nikuluta Yelusalemu, nikawatogomele awasunhile;
