47003015	Heye mpaka diyelo ihanhu hohose ichitabu cha Musa hochikusomigwa imimoyo yawo ikuwa igubikigwa.
47003016	Amba imunhu yanghamubidukila iMundewa umutandilo ukuleusigwa.
47003017	Hambiya iMundewa no Muhe na ihena umuhe we Mundewa, hena kulekeleligwa.
47003018	Niinga aseye wose, china ifihanga fisigubikigwe awanhu wamonga wakudaha kona kupulutila aseye, iditunyo dye Mulungu, chikubiduligwa chikifane imwene na ditunyo dyetu dikuwa ikulusi, aino ikulawa kwe Muhe we Mundewa.
47004001	Ninga iMulungu kwa ubasi wakwe kachingha umulimo awu, na kosoko yo chisikusuhuka chidoga.
47004002	Aseye kwa ulwandi lwetu chilema simbuli sose se chinyala ne chifiso, chilema kudanha ama kwaganisa imbuli ye Mulungu, ninga kwa konesa chalinse uchawelu chodaha kwitogola chiweechokwa chila udaha wo kutagusa kumwande ye Mulungu.
47004003	Hata inghowa imbuli yetu swamu ifisigwe, ifisigwa du kwa waya iwagilile.
47004004	Awene wasikuhuwila kosoko iMulungu we chilunga achi kagaguma chisa amahala gawo wanghadahe kona chalinse ujelu we Imbuli swanu ye ditunyo dya Kilisito, iyakifane Mulungu.
47004005	Kosoko chisikuhubili chiweecho ninga Yesu Kilisito fina Mundewa wa wanhu wose, hamwedu na seye fina watumwa wenu kosoko ya Kilisito
47004006	Kosoko ni Mulungu yagambile, “Ujelu wake muchisa.” Imwene no yakuleka mimoyo yetu ikwaka na kuchingha ujelu wa umanyi we ditunyo dye Mulungu ukwakaika muchihanga cha Kilisito.
47004007	Ning chinawo ugoli awu mufiya fya ulongo, konesa fina udaha ukulu uwa kws Mulungu.
47004008	Chikubulagika ugele umonga, ninga chisikukanhamiswa, ugele umonga chikuwa na manhonge amba chisikusuhula chidoga;
47004009	Chikusambasika, ninga chisikulekigwa chiimwene, chikutowigwa ninga chisikubulagika.
47004010	Chila fonikugenda nikukomigwa chimutufi fina Yesu foyakomigwe, kosoko yo ugima wa Yesu udahe nawo kiyonesa mumitufi yetu.
47004011	Kosoko aseye chiwomi majuwa gose chikulafigwa chufe kosoko ya Yesu, kosoko ugima wa Yesu nawo ukiyonese mumitufi yetu iikufa.
47004012	Nonghamba, idifa dikugolosa milimo mugati yetu, amba mugati yenu mwina uumi milimo.
47004013	Kosoko china muhe yumwedu we dihuwi fina foitulumigwe, “Hanihuwila, na kosoko yo hanilonga,” na seye chikuhuwila na kosoko yo chikulonga,
47004014	chimanya ayuya yamwinule Mundewa Yesu kochinula seye nase kosoko cha hamwedu na Yesu na kochika kumwande yakwe hamwedu na nyeye.
47004015	Aga gose ni kosoko yo uwendowenu, kosoko fina dihewa fodikongeseka kuwanhu matewa kwa matewa, amalumbo nago gongeseke ku ditunyo dye Mulungu.
47004016	Kosoko yo chisikusuhuka chidoga, na hata inghowa mitufi ye chimunhumunhu ikubanika, imitufi yetu ye chimuhe ikubiduligwa chila ijuwa.
47004017	Kosoko amagayo gochikupata ni madodogi kahi ge chipisi chiguhi, ninga gochingha itunyo dikujumha maliganiso gose.
47004018	Kosoko chisikulanga kufinhu ifikoneka ninga kufinhu fisikoneka, kosoko ifinhu ifikoneka ni fya kuloka amba ifinhu fisikoneka ni fya majuwa gose.
47005001	Kosoko chimanya fina imitufi yetu ahano hachilunga ni kifana nyumba sa munyasi. Na inghofa, Mulungu kochingha nyumba ahanhu hakwe, iisigolosigwe na wanhu, amba igolosigwe ne Mulungu imwenecho na yokwikala majuwa gose.
47005002	Hambiya munamuna ayi chikugula akuno chikulangilila kwa nghwina kufasigwa inyikala yetu yuwile kulanga.
47005003	Chikuhanangigwa kufasigwa nhaifo kosoko chinghadahe koneka mwasi
47005004	Imitufi yetu ye chimunhumunhu iisikwikala majuwa gose. Chikulila kosoko ye magayo goikuhanangigwa ipate. Siyo chawelu fina chikuhananga chufe, ninga chikuhananga Mulungu yachibidule na kuchingha mutufimusha uukwikala majuwa gose. Nonghamba chikuhananga imitufi yetu ye chimunhumunhu ibiduligwe na kuwa umwedu uusikufa.
47005005	Iyachigolosele imbiduka ayi ni Mulungu iyachinghile iMuhe fina samana yetu.
47005006	China ng'inyo majuwa gose, na chimanya fina ugele wochikwikala mumutufi awu, chuwa kutali ne Mundewa,
47005007	kosoko chikwikala kwe dihuwi na siyo kwa kona.
47005008	China ng'inyo nghulu, na chikwendesigwa chiusame umutufi na kusamila kwe Mundewa.
47005009	Ninga kujumha chinhu chochose chiya, chikuhananga chimwendese imwene yuwe ch ikwikala ahano muchilunga ama uko.
47005010	Kosoko wose chikuhanangigwa choneke kwigoda dye ulamusi dya Kilisito, soko ya chila munhu yadahe kuhokela maswamu ama gehile gakumwendesa kosoko ye sinhenda sakwe mumutufi.
47005011	Ninga chimanya kumwogoha Mundewa, chikuwakwega wamonga, Mulungu kachimanya manyisi na nikuhuwila finamumimoyo yenu munimanya nheifiya.
47005012	Chisikitogola chiweecho ukwenu keli amba chotoko cha kitogola kosoko yetu, kosoko mudahe kuwabidula awaya wakiyona iweecho kosoko ye inyuwa yawo ya kunje kujumha fowali mumimoyo yawo.
47005013	Kosoko nghona choneka fina wabwalasi, ni kosoko ye Mulungu, na nghona china mahala ni kosoko yenu.
47005014	Uwendo wa Kilisito ukuchilongosa, na kosoko chimanya fina yumwedu kafa kosoko ya wanhu wose, nonghamba wose wakushiliki idifa dyakwe.
47005015	Hakofa kosoko ya wose, kahi awaya iwomi wanghekale kahi kosoko yawo, ninga kosoko ye imwene du yafile na kwinuligwa kosoko yawo.
47005016	Kulawa hambiya na kugendelela chisikumona munhu wowose kahi kwa inyona ye chimutufi, hata inghowa ugele umonga chamonile Kilisito nhaifo chisikumona nhaifo kahi.
47005017	Kosoko yo nghona yumonga yowile mu Kilisito, ni chumbigwe kasha, gakatali gapuluta langa! Amasha geja.
47005018	Aga gose gagoloseka ne Mulungu, imwene kupulutila Kilisito kachibidula seye kulawa wanghondo na kuwa wambwiya sakwe na kuchingha umulimo wa kuwagolosa awamonga nawo wowe wambwiya sakwe.
47005019	Nonghamba iMulungu hakawagolosa awanhu wose kupulutila Kilisito wambwiya sakwe; Mulungu nghatalile uwihi wawo, na kuchingha imbuli iikuchitamila yakuwagolosa nhani awamwiya sakwe.
47005020	Ninga seye cha watumigwa wa Kilisito.ne Mulungu imwenecho yakuchitumiya seye kumwidedelani anyeye, chikumutasani ahanhu ha Kilisito mwifumilise ne Mulungu.
47005021	Kilisito nghowile na wihi, ninga kosoko yetu Mulungu kamugolosa yahange uwihi wetu, na kosoko yo chidahe hamwedu naye kuhanga uchawelu we Mulungu.
47006001	Mumilimo yetu hamwedu ne Mulungu chikumwidedelani munghafumile kudyagilisa chaka dihewa dye Mulungu.
47006002	Kosoko hakagamba, “Muchigele chikufumilika haniwahulikisa, na kuwatasa mudijuwa dya uhonya.” Langa! Ugele ufumilike nowu, awu no ugele wo uhonya.
47006003	Chisikwika chikwakwaliso chochose munjila ya munhu wowose, kosoko idowa dyodyose dinghoneke mumilimo yetu.
47006004	ninga fina watumigwa we Mulungu chikitogola chiweecho kwa chila chinhu: Kwa kufinyilisa mu magayo gose.
47006005	Chitowigwa, chohigwa chihomigwa, chigolosa mulimo ya kusokesa, chisigonile na chisidiile
47006006	kwa usunhile we chidoga, umanyi, kufinyilisa na uchawelu, hamwedu na mamudyo ge Muhe Musunhile na uwendo we chawelu.
47006007	munonga ye chawelu na udaha kulawa kwe Mulungu, na uchawelu fina filama fyetu, fyo ulwandi wo kulume no kumoso
47006008	mu chogoho na kubesigwa ugele umonga wanhu wakuchitunya ugele umonga wakuchibesa. Wanhu wakuchilamula fina cha wadasi, ninga ugele wose chikulonga chawelu,
47006009	fina wanhu wasimanyike, hata nhaifo chimanyika fiswanu fina wanhu wakufa, langa cha wagima gimasi, wachisambasa amba lo wasichikomile;
47006010	fina wanhu wa usungu, amba chikubwedelelamajuwa gose, fina wakiwa amba chikugolosa wanhu matewa wagoli, fina wanhu wechaka chinhu amba china chila chinhu.
47006011	Chisiwafisile chochose mu wanhu Wakolinto chikumwendani kwa mimoyo yetu yose
47006012	Silo seye chisigubule mimoyo yetu ukwenu amba no nyeye musigubule mimoyo yenu ukwetu.
47006013	Na ahanhu hakwe, nikulonga na nyeye fina wana wadodogi, “Monese ukwetu uwendo fina uya wo chinawo ukwenu.”
47006014	Munghakihanangise na wasikuhuwila. Kosoko hena uhangi waki mugati ya uchawelu na uwihi? Ama chilo na misi fodaha kuwa hamwedu?
47006015	iKilisitone Luhoma fokifumilisa nhani? Ama imunhu inghakuhuwila kokuwa na choni cha hamwedu na iyakuhuwila?
47006016	Dihekalu dye Mulungu dina uhamwedu waki ne Milungu yo udasi? Kosoko aseye cha dihekalu dye Mulungu imumi, “Fina iMulungu foyagambile nokwikala na kuwa hamwedu nawo, na nokuwa Mulungu wawo na wene wokuwa wanhu wangu.
47006017	Kosoko yo muleguke ukwawo na mukitemanule nawo, yakulonga iMundewa, na munghakwafe chochose china uwihi, baho nomuhokelani;
47006018	na nokuwa Baba ukwenu na mokuwa wanangu we chigosi ne wachike, yakulonga iMundewa Mulungu.”
47007001	Kosoko chinaso siyahadi asi wendigwa wangu, lekeni chikisunhe chiweecho na chila uwihi we chimutufi ne chiloho na kuugolosa usunhile umemelekele na kwikala kwa kumogoha Mulungu.
47007002	Mukumhule imimoyo yenu ukwetu, chisimubanile munhu chinhu chochose, chisimubulage munhu wowose, chisimubanile munhu wowose chisimudanhilise munhu wowose.
47007003	Sikulonga nhafo kuwalamula nyeye kwa wihi, kosoko hanilonga kunghonga fina muwa mumimoyo yetu, chisitemanuligwa chuwe chufa ama womi.
47007004	Nina ng'inyo nghulu ukwenu, nikiyona kosoko yenu, mumagayo getu chihokela ihoso ikulu na ninyemuka lugano.
47007005	Hata fochafuluse kufika Makedoniya, chisapatile luneka lwa kubwihila, hachikidasika na gose, magomvi kuwamonga na ikeng'enha mufidoga fyetu.
47007006	Ninga iMulungu iyakuwahosa wasuhuke chidoga hakachihosa kwa kwija kwakwe Tito,
47007007	na siyo du kwa kwija kwakwe Tito, ninga kahi kosoko ye umoyo wowumwinghile anyeye, fina foyachitamile fomukuhananga kunyona, fomwina usungu, fomukuhananga kunimilisa kosoko yo nina nyemo lugano.
47007008	Kosoko hata inghowa ibaluwa iya yonyandike iwabulaga mufidoga aniye sikukalala (hata inghowa nakalale) kosoko nikona fina ibaluwa iwaguma usungu anyeye, hata inghowa kwa chipisi chiguhi.
47007009	Ninga hambiya nikubwedelela siyo kosoko hamudeseka ninga kosoko indeseka yenu iwagolosa mulambe, kosoko mukihulika usungu we chilungulungu, na soko yo musagilile kosoko yetu.
47007010	Kosoko usungu we Mulungu ukweleka kulamba kukulongosa kuuhonya, na kwichaka soko yo kujuta, amba usungu we chimunhumunhu ukweleka difa.
47007011	Hambiya mukudaha kona isoko yo kona usungu fina foyakuhananga Mulungu, langeni fomukiyonela ubasi, mukutinhuka na kogoha, mwikala hega kona ichawelu ikugoloseka, anyeye kwa chila njila mukiyonesa fina mwichaka dyomubanile.
47007012	Kosoko yo hata inghowa nyandike ukwenu, isowile kosoko ye imunhu yagolose uwihi kahikosoko ye imunhu yagoloseligwe uwihi ninga kosoko ikiyonese chalinse fina fomowile ne inghonya ukwetu kumwande ye Mulungu.
47007013	Nochonghone seye chagumigwe moyo lugano. Na kuleka ingumigwa yetu moyo chiweecho chikubwedelela lugano munyonela ya Tito, kosoko ichidoga chakwe chisindamala.
47007014	Aniye hanikiyona lugano kosoko yenu na sagumigwe chinyala, ninga fina chila chinhu chochawatamile fochowile chawelu, nonhaifo inyiyona yetu kwa Tito foni chawelu muhala.
47007015	Tito yakumwendani lugano anyeye mose, fina foyakugelegela ichogoho chenu mose, fomwamuhokele kwa chogoho na kuchichima.
47007016	Nikubwedelela kosoko nina ng'inyo iyecho ukwenu.
47008001	Chikuhananga mumanye Wakilisito weyetu, idihewa dye Mulungu dyonesigwe na makanisa ga Makedoniya,
47008002	hawagesigwa na magayo makulu, munyemuko yawo na ukiwa mukulu, hawowa wandewa kupulutisa.
47008003	kosoko hawalafa lugano fina fowadahile, hata kujumha fowadahile. Kwa kwenda kwawo aweecho.
47008004	Hawakidedela lugano wenghigwe luneka lwo kuwatasa awanhu we Mulungu.
47008005	Chisadogile fina wodaha kulafa nhaifo, hawakilafa aweecho kwa iMundewana seyekwa uwendo we Mulungu.
47008006	kosoko yo hachimutasa Tito fina fou yaukongesa umulimo awu, yakuhanangigwa yaumalagise umulimo awu we dihewa.
47008007	Mwina ugoli wa chila chinhu, mu dihuwi, udaha wo kulinga, umanyi, inghonya yose yakugolosa amaswanu, na uwendo wenu ukwetu kosoko mudihewa adi mudahe kupulutisa nheifiya.
47008008	Sikulongo dino fina ilagiso, ninga nikulonga du kuwonesa fina awamonga fowena inghanya yo kutasa, nidahe kumanya fina uwendo wenu foni wa chawehu.
47008009	Kosoko mumanya dihewa dye Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito, mugoli fina foyowile, kosoko yenu hakegolosa mukiwa, kosoko yawagolose wagoli kwa ukiwa wakwe.
47008010	Kosoko ye imbuli ayi nikuwenghan Maloleso: Ni fiswanu kwa nyeye hambiya kumalagisa chomukingile umwaka wa ulokile, hamukonga siyo kugolosa du amba chomusulumile.
47008011	Ninga hambiya mumalagise umulimo awo, na fina fomowile na ngwina mghulu yo kutasa, kahi konyeni nhaifo kuimalagisa kwa chiya chomwinacho.
47008012	Nghona chawelu mukuhananga klafa, iMulungu kohokela chila chomukudaha kulafa, nghakuhananga kujumha chomwinacho.
47008013	Nichaka mana fina awamonga wahungusiligwe na nyeye mukanhamisigwe,
47008014	niya ayo ni kosoko yo usawa, kosoko nyeye mwinafo fingi mugele awu ni fiswanu kuwatasa awaya wakuhananga. Kahi wanghowa nafyo fingi nanye muichaka, womutasani. Munamuna ayi wose mukuwa sawa.
47008015	Fina foitulumigwe “Iyakunjagise fingi nghowile nafyo kujumha foyahanange, na yakunjagise chidodogi nghahungukiligwe”
47008016	Malumbo kwe Mulungu yawagumile nghwina imwedu yo kutasa kosoko yenu mumoyo wa Tito.
47008017	Kosoko siyo du kafumila achiya chochimutasile kugolosa, ninga hakowa na ngwina lugano ya kutasa na kwa nyenda yakwe hakalamula kwija ukwenu.
47008018	Hamwedu naye chikumwigala imundugu setu iyasoweleke mumakanisa gose kosoko yo kuhubili mbuli swamu,
47008019	na siyo iyo du, amba kasaguligwa na makanisa kwilongosa na seye mumilomo ayi ye dihewa yochikugolosa, kosoko ye ditunyo dye Mundewa na konesa inyenda yetu swamu.
47008020	Chikuhananga kinega munhu wowose yangheje yechilaumu kosoko ye wimilisi wi isao ai.
47008021	Kosoko iniya yetu ikugolosa achiya ichiswamu siyo kwa Mulungu du, amba kwa wanhu nheifiya.
47008022	Na hamwedu na wanhu awo weli, chikumwigala imundugu setu wochimugesile mikangha itewa na kumona fina ugele wose ni munhu yena ngwina yo kutasa, ninga hambiya kena ngwina kusuma ugele wowose kosoko kena ng'inyo nghulu ukwenu.
47008023	Na kosoko ya Tito ni miyangu, mutogomi miyangu, chikugolosa milimo kosoko yenu, na kosoko ye wandugu wamonga awejile hamwedu naye, awo ni watumigwa we Makanisa, ditunyo dya Kilisito.
47008024	Ninga woneseni umemeleki wo uwendo wenu, na makanisa gose gone chawelu fina inyiyona yangu iikwenu siyo ya chaka.
47009001	Hechaka soko yo kwandika ukwenu kosoko ye filafwa ku Wakilisito wa Yelusalemu.
47009002	Kosoko nimanya fo mwina moyo wo kutasa, na hanikiyona kosoko yo ku wanhu wa Makedoniya, sikugamba Akaya hayuwa tayali kulawa mwaka ulokile ne unghwina yenu iwasonga matewa.
47009003	Ninga nikuwatuma awaKilisito weyetu kosoko inyitogola yetu kosoko inghowa ya chaka munonga ayi, kosoko muwe tayali, fina fonilongile mokuwa;
47009004	Ingheje ikuwa wanhu wa Makedoniya fowokawokwija na seye wafike musiwalafaji, chokuwa na chinyala chinhani, kuleka kulonga ichinyala chenu kosoko yo kuwa na ng'inyo.
47009005	Kosoko yo nyona fiswanu kuwatasa awaKilisito weyetu wachilongolele ukwenu, wadahe kwika tayali ifilafwa fyenu fomugambile molafa, nayo yonese fina chaweli ni mhongesi ilafigwe kwenda kahi siyo kwa kudindilisigwa.
47009006	Chonikulonga nochi; “Iyakuhanda chidodogi yakugola chidodogi na iyakuhanda chingi yakugola chingi”.
47009007	Chila muhu ikuhanangigwa yagolose fina foyalamule mumoyo wakwe, siyo kwa usungu ama kwa kudindilisigwa, kosoko iMulungu yakumwinda yakulafa kwa konela.
47009008	Na iMulungu yakudaha kuwingha nyeye chila mboto kwa wingi, kosoko mudase kuwa na chila chinhu chimemelekele majuwa gose, na mudahe kuwatasa wose wakuhananga.
47009009	Fina foitulumigwe, “Imwene yakulafa ku wakiwa, uchawelu wakwe ukwikala majuwa gose”.
47009010	Na iMulungu iyakulafa mbeyu kwe Muhandi ne chakudiya ku wanhu, kolafa nheifiya na kongesa kukugola kwenu kosoko muwatase awaya wakuhananga.
47009011	Momotesigwa kwa chila chinhu, kosoko wanhu wadahe kumulumba Mungu kwe simhongesi sowohokela kulawa ukwetu.
47009012	Kosoko fomukulafa utogomi awu musikulafa du kukuhananga kwa wanhu we Mulungu wa Yelusalemu, amba nheifiya haigolosa wanhu matewa wamulumbe Mulungu.
47009013	Na kosoko yo ulomelesi awu, momutunya Mulungu kwa kuihuwila mbuli swamu yaKilisito kahi kosoko yo undewa wo mukuwengha wanhu wa Yelusalemu na wanhu wamonga.
47009014	Kosoko yo kwa uwendo mukulu wowatasila nyeye kosoko ye dihewa dipulutise iMulungu dyoyonese ukwenu.
47009015	Chikumulumba Mulungu kosoko ye mhongesi yakwe iisikutagusika.
47010001	Aniye Paulo nimwenyecho hanyoneka, munhu wa ubasi na musindamafu wa Kilisito, hambiya aniye inimuholo ninghowa hamwedu na nyeye, namukali ninghowa kutali nanye.
47010002	Nikumutasani munghanigolose kuwa mukali ugele wonikuwa hamwedu na nyeye, hamwedu na nginyo fina fonitalile kwa kuwonesa awaya wadogage chikugolosa fina wanhu we chilunga.
47010003	Hata inghowa chikwikala muchilunga, ninga chisikitowa fina wanhu we chilunga.
47010004	Kosoko ifilama fochikutumiya siyo fya chimunhumunhu, ninga fina udaha we Mulungu uukubana singome(amakiga) sose
47010005	na kung'ola chila chikwakwaliso che kiyona ichikigwe kuilema umanyi we Mulungu, chikuteka chila madoga gaduha kumogoha Kilisito.
47010006	Munghafulusa kuwa mumemelekela muchogoho, aseye cha tayali kubana chila namuna ya kuleka kuwa na chogoho.
47010007	Mulange kuchuwile kumwande yenu. Nghona munhu wowose yena ng'inyo fina ni munhu wa Kilisito, imunhu ayo yakuhanangigwa yagelegele fina aseye nase cha Wakilisito fina imwene foyali.
47010008	Hata inghowa nipulutise mukiyona kwangu kosoko yo udaha uya woyachinghile iMundewa siyo wa kudimola dihuwi dyenu ninga kudijenga, sigumigwa chinyala kosoko yakwe.
47010009	Sikuhananga mone fina nikuwengha chogoho nyeye, kwe sibaluwa sangu.
47010010	Kosoko wakugamba, “Sibaluwa sa Paulo ni nghali na sina mbuli nsito, ninga imwecho yanghowa hamwedu na seye ni munhu muholo, na hata ugele woyakulonga simbuli sakwe kifana si chinhu.”
47010011	Leka munhu yo yamanye fina chochikulonga musibaluwa no gochigolosa ugele wochikuwa hamwedu na nyeye.
47010012	Kwa fyofyose chisikudaha kwiika ama kwiliganisa na waja wakitunya aweecho; Awanhu wakwigolosa wene kuwa chipimo cha kwipimila, na wanhu wakwiliganisa aweecho kwa eweecho ni wabwalasi.
47010013	Ninga chisikiyona na kupulutisa, amba kukiyona ko kosigala mumihaka ye imilimo yochinghigwe na Mulungu, aino ni hamwedu na imilimo yetu ukwenu.
47010014	Kosoko chisikujumha imihaka yochekiligwa ugele wochejile ukwenu; hachuwa we nghonga kwija ukwenu, chikumegalila imbuli swanu ya Kilisito.
47010015	Chisikiyona na kupulutisa kosoko ye milimo ya wanhu wengi, ninga dihuwi dyetu nodi, fina dihuwi dyenu fodikongeseka, imilimo yetu ukwenu yokongeseka lugano,
47010016	Baho chodaha kuhubili imbuli swanu muisi sa kutali na nyeye, na chisikiyona kosoko ye imilimo ifuluse kugolosigwa ni wanhu wengi.
47010017	Leka iyakiyona yakiyone kosoko ye Mundewa Kilisito.
47010018	Kosoko iyakuhoniligwa si si munhu iyakitunya imwenecho, amba imunhu yakutunyigwa ne Mulungu.
47011001	Nikona monifinyilisa chidodogi muubwalasi wangu. Dededeni munifinyilise!
47011002	Nikumonelani finju amba ni finju ya Mulungu, kosoko nimutumisani nyeye kwa Kilisito na nikumonani nyeye fina mwanamuke nghamanyile mugosi kwe mugosi wakwe yumwedu.
47011003	Ninga nikogoha fina dijoka fodimudanhilise Hawa kwa usugu wakwe, amadoga genu gobanigwa na kutowangisigwa na kuleka kuhuwilika kwenu kwa chawelu kwa Kilisito.
47011004	Kosoko yumwedu yangheja na kumuhubili Yesu yungi kusuma ayuya wochimuhubili, ama nghona muhokele muhe yungi kusuma yuya womuhokele, ama nghona muhokele mbuli swanu ingi kusuma aiya yomuhokele, ayo ifulusa kutosha kwiika hasi yakwe.
47011005	Sikudoga fina niye namudodogi kusuma awo watumigwa wo udasi.
47011006	Hata inghowa nikugugumila munonga, siyo muumanyi, kw njila yoyose chigagolosa gano chalinse ukwenu mufinhu fyose.
47011007	Togoleni! Hanigolosa wihi kwa kiidulisa nimwenecho kosoko anyeye mwinuligwe, kosoko hanihubili mbuli swanu ye Mulungu bila maliho.
47011008	Ugele wonagolo sage milimo ukwenu, nenda nilihigwa na makanisa gengi, chigambe nenda niwahijila kosoko ya kuwatasa nyenye.
47011009	Na ugele wongowile na nyenye na nakuhananga, samwighile musigo wowote kosoko ihananga yangu hailafingwa na wandugu wa Kilisito kulawa Makedonia. Hanikinegi nanokinega kuwa musigo kwa munhu wowote.
47011010	Fina uchawelu wa Kilisito fouwile mugati yangu, inyiyona yangu isinyamasisigwa mumukowa wa Akaya.
47011011	Na nhani? Kosoko sikumwendani? Imuhungu kamanya fina nikumwendani!
47011012	Na nogendelela kugolosa fina fonikugolosa, kosoko nighawenghe luneka awaya wakuhananga luneka lwa kiyona fina wakugolosa Milimo fina seye.
47011013	Kosoko awo ni watumigwa wo udasi, wotogomi we milimo wadasi, Wakiigolosa iweecho fina watumigwa wa Kilisito.
47011014	Na siyo ijimo kosoko hata Ihuhoma Yakiigolosa imwenecho fina malaika wo ujelu.
47011015	Kosoko yo siyo chinhu chigeni nghona awatumwa wakwe nawo wakiigolosa awecho fina watumwa wa uchawehu. Indumo yawo yoliganila ne iigolosa yawo.
47011016	Nifuhusa kuilonga, munhu wowose yanghadoge fina na mubwalasi, ninga hata mwonghadoga nhaifo, munihokele fina na mubwalasi, na kosoko yo aniya nani nikiyone chidodogi.
47011017	(Ichonikulonga sikulonga kwa udaha we Mundewa ninga fina mubwalasi, mung'inyo ino yenyitologa;
47011018	Kosoko wanhu matewa wakiyana kosoko ye finhu fye chilunga, aniye nani nokiyona.)
47011019	Kosoko mukuwafinyilisa kwa chinyemi iwabwalasi, anyeye mukiyona muwecho fina wanhu wa mahala.
47011020	Kosoko mukufinyilisa munhu yakuwongha, oma yakuwakanhamisa, ama yakuwabesa, ama yakuwatowa muchihanga.
47011021	Kwa chinyala nikugamba hachuwa ku finhu afo! Ninga nghonaga munhu wowose yakugesa kiyona kosoko ye chinhu chochose, nikulonga fina mubwalasi, na niye nikiyona.
47011022	Togoleni, awene ni Waibulania? Aniye nani nheifiya.Awene ni Waislaeli? Aniye nani nheifya. Awene ni welekwa wa Ibulahimu? Aniye nani nheifiya.
47011023	Awene ni watumigwa wa Kilisito? Aniye nikumutogomela Kilisito fiswanusi fina muchilahu aniye nitogoma milimo mikulusi nikala kwigelesa mikangha mingisi, nitowigwa mikangha mingisi na hanuwa habehi na kufa mikangha mingi.
47011024	Mikagha mishano hanitowigwa ne iya Mikotya makumi madatu na ikenda.
47011025	Mikangha midatu awaloma lawanitowa ne Mikotya, hanitowigwa na mawa kamwedu, mikangha midatu lanyuwa muhinhumbwi, Ugele wayabenekage mubahali. Kmwedu hanikala mumeji ijia dimwedu chilonemisi.
47011026	Musinhambo sangu sa chila ugele hangu wa muhatali ya mafahuko ya meji, mu hahatali ya wahiji, hatali hatali kulawa ku wamembwe, hatali mumakaya, hatali ya wandugu wo udasi.
47011027	Hanigolosa milimo mikugutu na kusoka, hamonga hanigona meso; hanyuwa na njala na nghilu, hanyuwa na mayeyo kosoko yo kuleka kuwa na suke simemelekele.
47011028	Na kuleka gago gose chila ijuwa nina manhonge kosoko ye makanisa gase.
47011029	Ugele yumwedu yechaka ludole nani nikihulika fina nechaka (yakulogosigwa) mu uwihi, nikumemigwa na usugu.
47011030	Nghona ninghanga kiyona, nokiyana kosoko ye finhu fikonesa fina nechaka ludole.
47011031	Imulungu ne Baba we Mundewa Yesu imwene yamotesigwe magiwa gose kamanya fina sikudanha.
47011032	Aa kuya Damasiki, imukulu wo mukowa yowile lasi ye Mundewa Aletasi hakeka wanhu kwimilisa ikaya kosoko wanikole.
47011033	Ninga hanihumulusigwa muchisage kupululila mwihengele dyowile mwikigo na kumuhija.
47012001	Nikuhanangigwa nikiyone, hechaka chinhu chonikwambulila kosoko yo, ninga nogendelela kusinjosi ne magubulo kulawa kwe Mundewa.
47012002	Nimumanya munhu yumwendu Mukilisto minyaka ikumi na mine yenuligwe kulanga, sikutanga nghona imunhu yo yowile ne mutufi wakwe ugele uwo, amba iMulungu chewelu kamaya.
47012003	Na nimanya fina imunhu ayu hakenuligwa kulanga, sikutanga ghona imunhu yo yowile ne mutufi wakwe egele uno, Mulungu kamanya.
47012004	na kuhulika finhu fe chifiso ifene fisikudaha kulongeka.
47012005	Mu hanhu he imunhu ayu, nokiyona, ninga sikiyona kosoko yangu, kulewa kiyona mukuleka kuwa na ludole.
47012006	Kosoko mhali nikuhananga kiyona sowile nikuwa mubwalasi hata chidodogi, kosoko hanyuwa nikulonga chawehu mahala ninga nikulema kugendelela kiyona, kosoko munhu wowose yangheje yedoga kusuma gaya goyakona na kuhulika kulawa ukwangu.
47012007	Na kunileusa kulawa kukiyona na kupulutisa kosoko ye simbuli asi singhulm se magubulo, kaninghigwa imuwa mumutufi wangu, mutumigwa wa huhoma, yakunitowa yakunileusa kulawa kunyiyonaya kupulutisa.
47012008	Hanikutasa Mundewa mikangha midatu kosoko ichinhu achi chinilawe;
47012009	ninga hakanigamba, “Imboto yangu ikutosha, kosoko uludole lwangu lukumemelekela mukuleka kuwa na ludole.” Nokuwa na nyemo nakiyona kosoko yo kuleka kwangu kuwa na ludole kosoko uludole lwa Kilisito lwikale muchanhya yangu.
47012010	Kosoko ya Kilisito nikwendesigwa na kuleka kuwa na ludole, maligo magayo; kosoko fonikuwa nichaka lodole no fonikuwa na ludole.
47012011	Ninga fina mubwalasi amba nyeye nomunidindilise kuwa nheifo, anye nomowile wanhu wokunitunya, kosoko hata inghowa aniye si chinhu simudodogi ng'o kuwawo “watumigwa wenu”
47012012	Ifitangilo fya Mutumigwa we chawelu hanigoloseka ukwenu kwa kufinyilisa, kwa majumo makulu.
47012013	Kosoko musahungukiligwe chinhu kusuma amakanisa gamonga, ila aniye nimwenyecho siwatwikile misigo, munilekelele kosoko haniwagoloselani fibi.
47012014	Langa hambiya lwa kadatu nifulusa kwija ukwenu. Na sikua musigo kosoko sikukongha fomuwile nafyo, ninga anyeye muwecho, kosoko awana wasikuhananga kuwekila aweweleke sigafu, ninga awaweleke nowakuhanangigwa wawekile sigafu.
47012015	Nokuwa na nyemo kutumiya fyose fyoninafyo kosoko yenu. Nghona nikuwenda nyeye lugano anyeye monyenda chidodogi.
47012016	Ninga mokifumilisa fina sowile musigo ukwenu amba yumwedu yakudaha kulonga kosoko Paulo ni musugu kawakochelesa!
47012017	Togoleni haniwongha kupulutila mutumigwa wowose wonimwigale ukwenu?
47012018	Hnimwinanga Tito na kumutuma, na hanimwigala imundu setu hamwedu naye Tito hakawongha nyeye? Sichigose na kulongoswa na chidoga chimwedu, chisigendile hamwedu.
47012019	Kowage mukudoga ugele wose mpaka hambiya, chendaga chikimilise chiwecho kumwande yenu, chikulonga chawelu kumwande ye Mulungu mu Kilisito, na gose gochikugolosa wendigwa wangu ni kosoko ya kuwajenga.
47012020	Kosoko nikogoha fina nikudaha kwija na kuwafika nyeye munyuwa yosikonela na kosoko yo mukudaha kunyona fina fomusikuhananga, kukudaha kuwa na kulemana, finju, nyono, nyiendesa, udasi, kulonga uwihi wa wanhu, kwanjasa udasi kuwanhu, na kuleka kuwa na dihewa mugati yenu.
47012021	Nikogoha kowage ugele wonikwija iMulungu kodaha kunigolosa nuwe na chinyala kumwande yenu, nani nohongesa kosoko ya wanhu wagolose wihi ugele ulokile na wasilambile kosoko yo wihi wawo.
47013001	Aluno ni lwa kadatu nikwija ukwenu. Chila mbuli ikulahigwa kwa uhomelesi lwa wanhu weli ama wadatu fina amatulumo fogakulonga.
47013002	Haniwajama awaya awagolose wihi ugele ulokile na wose wamonga nikuwajama hambiya ugele wonihechaka, fina fonagolose ugele wonowile bah one nija yangu ya keli, ugele wonikwija sikuwa na ubasi.
47013003	Kosoko mukuhananga mokiyonela muwecho fina Kilisito yakulonga kupulutila niye. Ukwenu Kilisito nghakuswela ludole ninga uludole lwakwe ukugolosa milimo mugati yenu.
47013004	Kosoko awanhu hawamukoma kwa kumutungika mumusalaba kosoko yo kuleka kuwa na ludole, ninga hambiya yakwikala kwe ludole lwe Mulungu. Kosoko nichaka ludole kwi mwene, amba ukenu nogendelela kuwa hamwedu naye kwa udaha we Mulungu.
47013005	Mukilangisise muwecho nghona mukwikala mwihuwi. Musikona fina Yesu Kilisito yakwikala mugati yenu? Nghona si nheifo basi nyeye muduga.
47013006	Nikuhuwila fina momanya fina sichidugile.
47013007	Chikumutasa Mulungu munghadahe kugolosa wihi, siyo kosoko choneka fina chifulusa kusuma, ninga mugolose maswanu hata inghowa aseye chikoneka fina chisumwa.
47013008	Kosoko chisikudaha kugolosa chochose kukana ichawelu, udaha wochinawo ni kugendelesa ichawelu.
47013009	Chikonela ugele wochichaka ludole anyeye mwina ludole. Chochikuwatasila mugaluke wanhu wamemelekele.
47013010	Nikwandika ibaluwa ino ugele ninghali kutali, kosoko ugele wonikwija ninghadindilisigwe kuwa mukali ukwenu kwa kutumiya auya udaha woninghigwe na Mundewa kosoko ya kujenga na sio kumola.
47013011	Hambiya lekeni nimalagise ibaluwa yangu kwa kumulagani. Goloseni sinjila senu, muhulikise amaloleso gangu, mukifumilise munhu ne miyagwe, ne iMulungu wo wendo ne digoya kukuwa hamwedu na nyeye.
47013012	Mukilamuse chila munhu e miyagwe kwa nyilamusa ye chiKilisito. Awanhu wose we Mulungu kuno wakuwalamusani.
47013013	Dihewa dye Mundewa Yesu Kilisito ne wendo we Mulungu na uhamwendu we Muhe Musunhile uwe hamwedu na nyeye mose.
48001001	Paulo Mutumigwa siyo na wanhu kahi kulawa kwa mwanadamu, ninga iYesu Kilisito imwecho ne Mulungu Baba, yamwinule kulawa muchilalo.
48001002	Awakilisito wose woile hano hamwedu na niye chikuwegalilani mulamuso kumakanisa gose gowile ako Galatiya:
48001003	Mulungu iBaba yetu na Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito na yamwingheni mboto yakwe ne idigoya,
48001004	uleke yachilekelele kulawa muchigele achi cho wihi. Kilisito hakakilafa imwenyecho kosoko yo wihi wetu, fina foyendile Mulungu iBaba yetu;
48001005	Ditunyo dina imwene chigele chose! Hano.
48001006	Aniye nikujuma! Nhani nheifo mukumuleka chimwande mwande iyamwinangileni mumboto ya Kilisito kamei mukubidukila Injila ingi.
48001007	Na ninga siyo fina kwina mbuli swanu ingi, ninga nikulonga nhafi kosoko kuna wanhu wakumwidasani na kuibidula Imbuli swanu ya Kilisito.
48001008	Ninga inghowa noseye ama Malaika kulawa kulanga yangheja yawahubili Imbuli swanu ingi ikulemana na aiya yochihubili aseye ukwenu, basi yaligitwe!
48001009	Fina fochilongile, na nikulonga lwakeli: Munhu yoyose iyakuwahubiliani Imbuli ikulemana na aiya yomuhokele na yaligitisigwe!
48001010	Aniye nikiyendesa kuwanhu ama kwe Mulungu? Ama nikituma kuwendesa awanhu? Kusigwa ninghali kwenda kuwendesa wanhu sinowile nikuwa mutogomi wa Kilisito.
48001011	Hambiya gojeni niwatamileni wandugu sangu fina imbuli aiya yonawahubili siyalawile kwa munhu.
48001012	Kahi siipatile kwa munhu wowose, kahi safuswa na munhu wowose ninga kwa kugubuliligwa na Yesu Kilisito.
48001013	Togoleni simuhulika niye fonowile imikalile yangu mudini ye Chiyahudi, fina fonidisambase dikanisa dye Mulungu bila ubasi na kugesa kudibana.
48001014	Aniye haniwalongolela wengi we disika dyangu kukola mafuso ge dini ya Chiyahudi, na kupiligala kukola mahokelo ga wasehe wetu.
48001015	Ninga iMulungu kwa imboto yakwe hakanisagula na kuninanga nimutumikie hata fonowa nikali kwelekwa. Yenda kunigubulila
48001016	imwanagwe, uleke nimuhubili kuwanhu wa mataifa wasimumanyile Mulungu, na simutasile munhu wowose ama kumusa fina nikonge nhani,
48001017	sakwila hata Yelusalemu kuwatumigwa wanilongolele kuwosa. Ila haniluta ningila mpaka Alabiya kunghonga, kamei kahi honikuya mpaka Damesiki.
48001018	Kamei foyaloka minyaka midatu hanikwila kahi mpaka Yelusalemu hanijamona Kefa ukuya, honikala ihakwe majua ikumi na mashano.
48001019	Sawonile hachikiyonile na awatumigwa wamonga ninga Yakobo du munduguse na Mundewa.
48001020	Aga gonikumwandikilani Mulungu kamanya fina sikuwandika udasi!
48001021	Kulawa baho haniluta kusitalafa sa iisi ya Silia na Chilikia.
48001022	Na ichigele cho samanyike kaa! Mumakanisa ga Wakilisito wa kuya Yudea.
48001023	Awanhu waya imbuli yowamanyile awene ni fina: Munhu yuya yendeyoliga na kuchitesa fibi kaumo naye yakuhubili dihuwi didino dyoyendayaliga!
48001024	Kamei hawamutunya Mulungu kosoko yangu.
48002001	Basi foyaloka minyaka ikumi na mine hanikwila kuluta Yelusalemu na Balinaba, kamei chalutanya na Tito.
48002002	Kuluta kwangu ni kosoko ya magubulo ge Mulungu. (Chuwile mu njama haniwatamila Filongosi) fina fonihubili Imbuli swanu muwanhu wa mataifa wamumanyile Mulungu. Hanigolosa nhaifo uleke milimo yangu ingheje ikuwa chaka.
48002003	Ninga hata imiyangu Tito iMuyunani, hadindiligwe kufinigwa,
48002004	ninga kosoko hakuwa na maKilisito ga udasi gendage gahananga gafinigwe. Mamunhu go hagakiingisa chinyemela, na kuhananga uhulu wetu wo chikilungise na wochuwile nawo mugati mwa Kilisito Yesu. Uleke wachingise muutumwa,
48002005	aseye hachilema lemilemi uleke ichawelu ye Mbuli swanu igendelele kusigala na nyenye.
48002006	Ninga wanhu wawo wakugambigwa Filongosi halika ni Filongosi ama hata, filongosi aniye ukwangu kaa; kosoko iMulungu hakulamula kwa kulanga futa. Wanhu wano hawowile na dyodyose dya kunongesela,
48002007	ninga chinyume chakwe fowona kwinghwigwa ne Mulungu mulimo wo kuhubili Mbuli swanu kuwamataifa kifana Petulo foyeng'igwe ikasi yo kuwahubiliya Wayahudi Mbuli swanu.
48002008	Kwa ludole lwa Mulungu nigoloswa Mutumi yatumigwe kuwamataifa, kifana Petulo foyagoloswa Mutumi kuwayahudi.
48002009	Wakone fina dihewa dyoninghigwe, Yakobo, Petulo na Yohana awowile mikiki hawafumi fina aniye ne Balinaba chilute ku wamataifa awene walute kuwanhu wafinigwe.
48002010	Ila nonga imwendu du yowachisigilile fina chiwagelegele awakiwa, mbuli iyo ayo hanuwa ludole nayo lugano.
48002011	Ila Petulo foyeja Andiyokiya, hanimugombela bila chifiso kosoko hakowe kena wihi.
48002012	Kosoko chigele wasinati hawanghati weje wanhu kulawa kwa Yakobo, yondeyodiya hamwedu na wanhu wamataifa. Kamei foyawonile wanhu waya wafika, hakakitenda kifana hadiyage nawo kosoko yendeyowogoha waya wafinigwe.
48002013	Nawo Awayahudi wamonga hawagolosa nheifiya mpaka Balanaba naye hakanegigwa na chimwefe chawo.
48002014	Aniye nikawone fina wasikugenda munjila inogile ye chawelu ye mbuli swanu, honimugombela iPetulo hamwande ya wanhu wose fina, Inghowa gweye go Muyahudi ukwandamila sijadi sa wamataifa; wanhu wasimanyile Mulungu kahi si Wayahudi. Nhani ukudindilisa wamataifa wandamile sa Wayahudi?
48002015	Aseye chiwecho Chiwayahudi kwa kwelekigwa kahi si wamataifa awena uwihi.
48002016	Kahi wamanyile fina imunhu nghekulaliligwanhenda sa chawelu kosoko yasinhenda sa malogiso ninga kosoko ya dihuwi mu Yesu Kilisito, hata na seye chihuwila mu Kilisito uleke chiteliligwe ichawelu kwa dihuwi mu Yesu, ninga si kwa sinhenda sa Malagiso, kosoko kwa sinhenda sa malagiso hechaka munhu wowose yakudaha kutaliligwa fina kena nhenda sa chewelu.
48002017	Hambiya inghowaga aseye chiwecho kwa kukonga kutaliligwa haki kwa njila ya Kilisito, hachoneka fina china wihi. Inghowa nonheifo togoleni nong'amba iKilisito yakutasa kwenesa uwihi? Chawelu ng'o!
48002018	Kosoko inghowa nikujenga gagaya kahi gonimonile, togoleni isikonesa finanimwecho nomubanaji.
48002019	Kosoko aniye kwa njila ya malagiso iyecho ganikoma, ila hambiya namumi kosoko ye Mulungu.
48002020	Nisambasigwa hamwedu na Kilisito kahi siniye ni mumi ninga Kilisito no mumi mugati yangu. Na uumi wo ninawo hambiya mumutufi, ninawo mwihuwi dye mwana we Mulungu, imwene yanyendile na kulafa chidoga chakwe kosoko yangu.
48002021	Sikwenda kuilema imboto ye Mulungu. Kosoko inghowa munhu yakutaliligwa nhenda sa chawelu kwa njila ya malagiso, basi Kilisito hakafa chaka!
48003001	Nhafo nyeye Muwagalatiya muwabwalasi! Nani yamulogileni inghowaga imanyika kumwande ya meso genu fina Yesu Kilisito katungikwa?
48003002	Nimuseni mbuli ayi imwedu: Hamuhokela Muhe kwa nhenda sa malagiso, hegu kwe kuhulika na kuihuwila?
48003003	Mwabwalasi lugano! Mukakonge na Muhe; hambiya mukuhananga Mulungu; ninga hambiya mukuhananga kwa chimutufi kumala?
48003004	Ninga gose gomugolose mutenda chaka? Chawelu chaka chakasi!
48003005	Je nong'amba iMulungu yamwinghileni Muhe na kugolosa majumo umwenu ago gose agakugoloseka kosoko ya nhenda sa malagiso ama kosoko hamuhulika Mbuli swamu na kuihuwila?
48003006	Hambia Ibulahimu hakamuhuwila Mulungu, na kutaliligwa fina muchawelu.
48003007	Nanye mumanye fina awanhu we dihuwi no wana wa Ibulahimu.
48003008	Matulumo gakone kumwande fina iMulungu yakwenda yawatalile ichawelu awamataifa kwa dihuwi, kahubili imbuli swamu kwa Ibulahimu yakugamba, “Umwako gweye amataifa gose gamotesigwa.”
48003009	Kwa nheifo awanhu we dihuwi wakumotesigwa hamwedu na Ibulahimu iyowile ne dihuwi.
48003010	Kosoko awaya awakwegamila lugano mumalagiso, awo wakwikala mumaligito makulu. Kosoko imbuli ye Mulungu ikugamba, “Munhu wowose nghakwandamila sose situlumigwe muchitabu che malagiso, basi kowa mwiligito ikulu!”
48003011	Hambiya imanyike lugano fina kwichaka munhu yakupata haki kwe Mulungu, kosoko yakwandamila malagiso kosoko matulumo gakugamba nhafi: No yuya du yene Dihuwi mwi Mulungu mumi.
48003012	Ninga amalagiso gasikwima mudihuwi. Iyakugagolosa yakwenda yowe mumi mugago.
48003013	Ninga kwa kugoloseka kuwa iligito iKilisito kachilegusa seye kulawa mwiligito, ligito dikwigaligwa ne malagiso; kosoko matulumo gagamba fina, Kaligitisigwa ne Mulungu imunhu yatungikigwe mwibiki.
48003014	Kilisito kagolosa gano gose uleke simboto se Mulungu soyalagane na Ibulahimu wasipate nawo awamataifa kwa njila ya Kilisito Yesu, uleke kwa njila ya kumuhuwila chihokele Muhe kwa ihuwi dye Mulungu.
48003015	Wandugu sangu, chinghalondela mbasi ye chimunhu munhu kifana wanhu weli nomowa kulagana mbuli na kikulumisa, hechaka yungi kahi yoibidulisa fingi.
48003016	Hambiya no nheifo kugamba dilagano dyagoloswa kwa Ibulahimu na lukolo lwakwe. Aino isigambigwe fina Milukolo ya wengi, ila igambigwa: Kulokela mulukolo lumwedu lwa Kilisito.
48003017	Chonikulonga hano nochi; Mulungu hakeka ilagano na Ibulahimu na kudigelegela. Dilagiso dyalafwa minyaka magana mane na makumi madatu ilokile isikudaha kubena Dilagano diya na kulegusa dilagano dye Mulungu.
48003018	Kosoko inghowa uhasi we Mulungu ukuhuwila ilagiso, basi ichaka haja ya ahadi. Ihuwi ninga iMulungu kamwingha ino Ibulahimu kwa njila ya dilagano.
48003019	Nhani mbiya yuwe ilagiso? Ni kosoko dilagiso hadija uleke konesa nhenda sihile mpaka lukolo lwa Ibulahimu, lukolo lwe dilagano wije. Dilagiso hadija kwa mikono ya malaika, ne munhu yengilile kifana mulamusi.
48003020	Ninga Imulamusi nghodaha kuwa yumwedu amba Imulungu ni yumwedu.
48003021	Aho, nong'amba dilagiso dikulemana ne siyahadi se Mulungu? Gwe hata! Kosoko woile dilagiso hadija uleke munhu yapate uumi, kahi ichawelu nayo hayuwa kwa njila ya dilagiso.
48003022	Ninga matulumo gagamba fina ichilunga chose chitawaligwa na ludole lwa sambi, na kosoko ya iyo basi uhasi wa ahidiigwe ukupatikana kwa njila ya ihuwilo, dikupatikana mwa Yesu Kilisito kwa waya wakuhuwila
48003023	Ninga chigele Dihuwi fodowa dikali kwija, aseye chose hachuwa muchifungo mpaka Dihuwi dino fodigubuligwe.
48003024	Nonghomba dilagiso hadichilongosagaa mpaka chigele Yesu foyeja, uleke chuwe we chawelu kwe Mulungu kulokela dihuwi.
48003025	Hambiya ugele we dihuwi no uno, ninga dilagiso dichaka chinhu ukwetu keli.
48003026	Kosoko muKilisito Yesu anyeye mose mwa wana we Mulungu kulokela dihuwi.
48003027	Ifene amatewa mugati yenu fowabatisigwa mu Kilisito wamufale Kilisito..
48003028	Aho lo hechaka Muyahudi kahiMuyunani, mutumwa ama si mutumwa, hechaka mugosi kahimwanamuke, kosoko mana anyeye mose mwa hamwedu mu Kilisito Yesu.
48003029	Inghowa nyeye mwa wanhu wa Kilisito mumanye fina mwawana wa Ibulahimu, kahi mwawahasi kuligana ne dilagano.
48004001	Nikugamba nhafi Imuhasi muugele woyekuwa mudodogi, kefana mutumwa, hamwedu nokuwa no Mundewa wa fyose.
48004002	Ninga yakuwa kowa hasi ya wanhu wakumulela na kumulangilila mpaka chigele iBabakwe foyakwija yamulekela ukulu.
48004003	Nheifo aseye nase fochowa chinghati chikule, hachuwa watumwa, we simbuli se chilunga achi.
48004004	Ninga chigele ichecho chikeje Mulungu hakamutuma mwanagwe. Imwene yelekwe na Mwanamuke, hakelekwa mwidilagiso dye Chiyahudi,
48004005	soko yawaleguse waya woile mwidilagiso, ili seye chinangwe wana wa Mulungu.
48004006	Na kosoko nyeye mwa wana wakwe, Mulungu hakamutuma Muhe we Mwanagwe kufidoga fyetu iyakulila Aba! Agwe Baba.
48004007	Hambiya kulokela Imulungu musikugendelela kuwa watumwa ning wana, na nghona ni wana kahi wahasi..
48004008	Katali fomowile munghati mumumanye Mulungu we chawelu, hamugendelelaga kufuga ifyumbigwe ifisowile Mulungu.
48004009	Ninga hambiya mumumanya Mulungu we chawelu, ama chigambe fina Mulungu mbiya kamumanyani nyeye, nhani mukuwila keli mafuso gasokile, mukuhananga muwe watumwa wani?
48004010	Mukukolelesa mbuli sa majuwa, minyesi, figele na minyaka.
48004011	Aniye to nikogoha seka ije yuwe nghiidasa chaka chakasi kosoko yenu.
48004012	Wandugusangu nikutasa lugano muwe kifana fonuwile niye. Kosoko niye nani nikifana nyeye ninga du musinigolosele dyodyose dihile.
48004013	Mumanya fina haniwahubili Imbuli swanu ichigele che inghonga, kosoko hanuwa na mutamu.
48004014	Hamwedu ihali yangu hayuwa Magesa ukwenu, musanibesile kahi kuniliga, ninga hamunihokela fina Malaika we Mulungu kifana Kilisito Yesu.
48004015	Fina hamuwa na chinyemi chikulu, mpaka hanidoga fina woile ikudahika kukumhula meso genu muninghe niye.
48004016	Togoleni nong'amba nigaluka mughondo wenu kosoko yo kuwatamilani ichawelu?
48004017	Awo wayenu wakonesa kifana wanogelelwa na nyeye, kumbeke wakuwahindilani kunje, uleke nyeye muwendese awene lugano.
48004018	Chawelu ni mbuli swanu kuwedasikila wamonga musimbuli si swanu siyo ugele wonibaho hamwedu nanye.
48004019	Mowangu wadodogi! Nikumonelani ubasi kifana imwanamuke nomaa yakukolwa no usungu wo kweleka, nani nikumonelani usungu mpaka Kilisito yombike mugati yenu.
48004020	Nikudoga nhanga nowile na nyeye lulu bahano, uleke nibidule dijwi dyangu kosoko nikona manhonge kosoko yenu.
48004021	Nikuhananga munitamile nyeye mukwenda kwikala mudilagiso: Musihulike fina dilagiso fodikulonga?
48004022	Fina Ibulahimu hakowa na wana weli, yumonga ni mwana we mwanamuke we chitumwa, kamei yumonga mwanamuke siwechitumwa.
48004023	Ayuno mwanagwe we chitumwa hakelekwa munjila ye chimutufi kifana wanhu wose, ninga yuno yumonga hayuwa kwa njila ya ihuwiso dye Mulungu imwecho.
48004024	Mbuli sino simanyika kifana mbasi: Kosoko wanawake wano weli wakonesa agaya malagano meli. Ayuya yene wana welekwe muutumwa, no Hajili, na ayuno yakonesa adiya dilagano dyagoloswa he tunda dya Sinai.
48004025	Hajili yuno yemile mwilagano dya mwitunda dya Sinai duwile ako Uwalabuni ni kifana mufano wa konesa dikaya dya Yelusalemu, kosoko dina wanagwe watumwa mpaka hambiya.
48004026	Ninga iYelusalemu ya kulanga siyo ye chitumwa, nayo iyo no ng'ina yetu seye.
48004027	Kosoko Itulumigwa nhafi: Sekelela gweye Musilatungulu go hukweleka! Inula dijwi dyako ujoje, agweye go winghati wone usungu wo kweleka! Kosoko wanagwe wa yuya yalekigwe ye mwene, wengisi kusuma yuya yene mugosi.
48004028	Hambiya wandugusangu, aseye nase cha wanagwe we Mulugu kwe chihuwi, fina Isaka foyowa.
48004029	Ninga kifana chigele chiya ayuya yelekigwe muutumwa foyamwidasage yuya yelekwa kwa njila ya muhe; noyuwile yuwile mpaka hambiya.
48004030	Ninga itulumwa nhani mwilago? Si ikugamba, “Muwingeni mwanamuke we chitumwa ne mwanagwe, kosoko imwana we chitumwa gwe hata nghodaha kuhala hamwedu ne mwana wa hakaya.”
48004031	Nhafo no chileka nikugamba aseye siyo cha wana wa mutumwa ila wana wa yuyo mwanamuke we hakaya.
48005001	Indekelelwa yochinayo chinghigwa na Kilisito Hambiya mwime ngwingwi mwinghowe hasi keli yo utumwa.
48005002	Tegeleseni! Aniye Paulo niwatamileni, Munhu yanghafinigwa yangheje yamanya fina Kilisito yakumutasa chinhu.
48005003	Kahi nikumujama chila munhu fina; yanghahananga kufinigwa yakuhanangwa yakole ne Itolati yose foikulonga.
48005004	Mubagulwa na Kilisito nyeye mukukola malagiso uleke noho mumwedese Mulungu. Ninga muwa kunje ne imboto ye Mulungu.
48005005	Ninga seye kwa Muhe chikugojela nhenda se chawelu ye Mulungu kwa njila ya dihuwi.
48005006	Kosoko kwa Kilisito kufinigwa na kuleka kufinigwa gose go gasikumutasa munhu chinhu chochose, ila kuwa na dihuwi dikugolosa mulimo kwa njila ya wendo.
48005007	Mwendemubilima fiswanu! Hambiya kahi nani yawagoloseni munghaifumile ichawelu? Iyamubilimiseni fibi nhafo nani?
48005008	Dilagiso dino sidikulawa kwa yuya iyamwinangileni.
48005009	“Unghaguma nungo hata inghowa ndodogi ikusasisa usage wose.”
48005010	Nikihulika nituna mwe Mundewa, nong'amba musilonda madoga gengi kusuma agangu, na wowose iyowedasa nyeye momwingha maliho gakwe hata yanghowa nani.
48005011	Ninga kwa ulwandi ulwangu halika nogendelela kuhubili fina kufinigwa ikuhanangigwa, nhani mbiya ho kudumangiswa? Woile fina no nheifo yuwile, basi kuhubili kwangu imbuli yo musalaba wa Kilisito kusowile kukuwa na lwidaso.
48005012	Ninga ibeka wawo wakumugumani manhonge walute wakafile kutali na nyeye.
48005013	Kosoko nyeye wandugu sangu hamwinangigwa mulekeleleligwe. Ninga mughasigolosele ndekelelwa yenu fibi kosoko mulekelelwa. Lekeni mukitase chila munhu na miyagwe.
48005014	Kosoko Malagiso gose muchitabu gamemelekela mwimbuli yiyo imwedu nayo: “Mwende miyago kifana foukiyenda gomwecho.”
48005015	Ninga munghowa kifana makewe, kiluma na kinghwakila, langisiseni mungheje mukimala.
48005016	Chonikulonga niye nochi, fina: Lekeni Muhe no umulongoseni mumikalile yenu, ninga hata nheifo simukwiguta usulumisi we mutufi.
48005017	Kosoko agaya agakwendigwa no umutufi, no gesikwendigwa na Muhe. Na agakwendigwa no Muhe no gasikwendigwa no mutufi. Awano weli Wanghondo, na ayino ikonesa fina musikudaha kugolosa muwecho gaya go mukwenda kugolosa.
48005018	Ninga inghowa mukulongosigwa na Muhe, aho nanga musuwile mumalagiso.
48005019	Na gose gakugolosigwa ne mutufi gamanyika du, mbona gamonga noga: Dihabwa, uwihi, nhenda sihile;
48005020	mafugo ge chikindikindi, uhayi, unghondo, kugomba, kiyonela gele, nyono, ukobo, kulemana, udasi;
48005021	chimesomeso, kunywa gimbi, ulefi, na goose gamonga kifana gago. Ayo lo nikumutamilani nghana fina: Wanhu wakugolosa ago, awo wasikwingila kulanga kwe Mulungu ng'o.
48005022	Ninga Dimudyo dye uMuhe we Mulungu nodi: Uwendo, ichinyemi, digoya, ufinyilisi, uunhu uswanu, kitasa, uchawelu,
48005023	uholosi, kechaka makulu. Musimbuli so, hechaka sheliya.
48005024	Na awaya woile mugati ya Kilisito wasabwalisa mutufi na madoga gakwe gehile.
48005025	Halika chikwikala na Muhe; basi na chigende na Muhe.
48005026	Chinghakitunye chiwecho chaka na chaka, na kiyanda sese kwa sese.
48006001	Wandugu sangu imiyenu wowose yanghagolosa wihi, nyeye mwichaka wihi mujameni miyenu na kumuwisa kwa moyo muswanu. Ninga kilangisiseni nanye muwenyecho mungheje mukugwila umo.
48006002	Kitaseni nyenye kwa nyenye, kosoko kwa njila ya kugolosa nhafo no kwandamila dilagiso dya Kilisito.
48006003	Munhu imwiyoni nomoo yakiyona imwenyecho ni chinhu kumbe siyo chinhu, yakidanhilisa imwecho.
48006004	Ninga chila munhu na yaisungilile imilimo yakwe imwecho. Kamei noho yowe na nonga ya kiyona nayo imwenyecho kuchidoga chakwe siyo kwe miyagwe.
48006005	Kosoko chila munhu yakwija yakwinula dikanda dyakwe imwecho.
48006006	Ninga iMufusigwa yakifusile mbuli swanu nayamutamile ne iMufusa wakwe.
48006007	Munghakidanhilise, Mulungu hakubesigwa. Kosoko chochose munhu cho ya kuhanda nocho yakwija yagola.
48006008	Iyakuhanda kwa kwandamila mbuli so mutufi wakwe, basi yakwija yagola difa kulawa umo mumutufi wakwe; lakini yuya yahandile kwa Muhe, yakwija yagola umo muMuhe uumi wa majuwa gose.
48006009	Ninga chinghasoke kugolosa maswanu; kosoko chikwija chigola kwa chigele chakwe, halika chokuwa hachilekile.
48006010	Hambiya nheifino nomaa chine luneka, basi chigendelele kugolosa maswanu kuwanhu wose ninga saidi lugano chiwagolosele wayetu wochuwanye mwikanisa.
48006011	Langeni ukulu lwa ulutulumo wo nitulume mubaluwa yangu ukwenu kwa mukono wangu ni mwecho!
48006012	Awaya wakwenda kiyonesa mitufi yawo fina wakugolosa nhenda swanu, nowene wakumulasimishani nyeye mufinigwe. Awakugolosa du nheifo uleke wanghadesigwe kosoko ya musalaba wa Kilisito.
48006013	Ninga du hata awecho wawo awakwenda kufinigwa, malagiso wasikuyakola, ila wakwanga nyeye nomufinigwe uleke wakitunyile umwenu fina langa lo! Wakukola malagiso fiswanu.
48006014	Ninga Aniye to, hata sikitunyila chinhu chochose ila musalaba wa Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito, kosoko kwa kulokela uwo ichilunga chisabwalisigwa ukwangu, na aniye nani nisabwalisigwa muchilunga.
48006015	Kosoko kufinigwa na kuleka kufinigwa gose sawa du; chikuhanangigwa usha wo moyo.
48006016	Na kwa wose wakuhanga wandamile gago, nikugamba kwimageni, ninga wagende digoya na ubasi we Mulungu ugende nawo ne wanhu we Mulungu Isilaeli!
48006017	Nikumalagisa kwa Kugamba: Kukongela hambiya nhafi munhu yanghanidase, fina nikulonda lubonoto lwa Yesu mumutufi wangu.
48006018	Wandugu sangu dihewa du ye Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito na dyuwe hamwedu ne mimoyo yenu. Hano.
49001001	Paulo mutumigwa wa Kilisito Yesu kwa nyenda ya Mulungu, ku wasunhile awene wakuhuwilika mu Kilisito Yesu:
49001002	Dihewa dyuwe ukwenu na idigoya kulawa Mulungu Baba yetu ne Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito.
49001003	Yatunyigwe Mulungu Baba we Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito imwene iyachimotese seye muKilisito hamwedu ne simboto sose se chimuhe kulanga,
49001004	hata foyachisagule chigele Ichilunga fochowa chisinati chumbigwe uleke chuwe wasunhile wechaka ilema ukwakwe.
49001005	Hakachisagula chuwe wanagwe kulokela Yesu Kilisito, kosoko ye nyenda yakwe.
49001006	Kuditunyo dyakwe dye nhogolwa dye dihewa fina hakachilekelela kulokela mwimwendigwa.
49001007	Umwakwe china uhonya kwanjila ya sakame yakwe, na kulekeleligwa wihi wetu ifene ugoli we dihewa dyakwe fowuwile.
49001008	Imwene hoyaching'ha ago mumemelesi,
49001009	kosoko hoyomanyika ukwetu kwa ubala na ujelu wose uwichaka chifiso kosoko no nheifo yendile mumakusudi gakwe goyakusudie fina galokele mwa Kilisito.
49001010	No nyenda yakwe fina ichigele fochimemelekela yafigale ifyumbigwe fyose umwakwe ifinhu fuwile kulanga na muchilunga.
49001011	Umwakwe ifinhu fyose fifuluka kugolosigwa kifana foyendile.
49001012	Aseye chi wanghonga mwihuwi dya Kilisito chasaguligwa na kwikigwa chikale chimutunye mwitunyo dyakwe.
49001013	Kulokela muimwene anye nanye hamuhulika imbuli ye chawelu, aiya mbuli swanu imwigalileni Uhonya wenu, kahi homuhuwila ninga homutoigwa lubonoto we dilagano dye Muhe musunhile,
49001014	iyo no dihuwiso dyo uhasi wetu, mpaka kuuhonya we wanhu wakwe Mulungu kunhogolwa ye ditunyo dyakwe.
49001015	Kosoko yo ninga hanihulika dihuwi dyenu mu Mundewa Yesu na wendo wenu kuwasunhile wose we Mulungu,
49001016	Sikuleka kulafa malumbo kosoko yenu na kuwagelegelani mumataso gangu,
49001017	fina Mulungu we Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito iBaba we ditunyo yawengheni Muhe we ubala na magubulo mumanyi wose uwile umwakwe.
49001018	Meso ga mimoyo yenu gowe majelu mudahe kumanya dihuwi dyomwinangiligwe na ifene ukulu wo ugoli wakwe fouwile mwitunyo dyo uhasi kuwasunhile wakwe.
49001019	ne ifene ukulu we udaha uusikudaha kupimika fouwile ukwetu seye chimuhuwile na kosoko ye milimo mikulu ine udaha yoyakutogoma.
49001020	Iyene iyo noijile imalagikila mwa Kilisito chigele foyamulafa muchilalo na kumugolosa yekale mumukono wakwe wa kulume kulanga.
49001021	Kuchanhasi ya undewa wose na udaha na ludole na ulongosi na kuchanhya ya chila isina idinangigwe siyo du muugele uno ninga na muchigele chikwija;
49001022	Naye keka finhu fyose hasi ye migulu yakwe, na kamugolosa imwene Kilisito kuwa no Ditwi dye finhu fyose kosoko ye dikanisa
49001023	no mutufi wakwe, umemelekele muimwene iyakumemelesa ifinhu fyose.
49002001	Hamuwa wanhu wafile kosoko ya sisambi senu.
49002002	hamwandamilaga mbuli sihile se chilunga achino, na kumwandamila Mundewa wo ludole we ulanga, muhe uya uukutogoma mlimo mpaka hambiya muwana wasikwenda kuhulika.
49002003	Na aseye chose hachuwa nheifo chigele cha kunyuma hachandamila nhenda sihile se mitufi yetu na gose madoga gehile na kugagolosa, hachuwa wana woile muihukumu ye nyono kifana awamonga.
49002004	Ninga iMulungu yamemile ubasi yene uwendo mukulu woyachendile seye,
49002005	hata chigele fochowa wanhu wasimumi kosoko ya makosa getu, imwene hakachigolosa womi kulokela Kilisito (ninga kwa mboto ye Mulungu muhonyigwa)

49002009	sikosoko ya milimo yoyose ninga munhu wowose yangheje yakitunya.
49002010	Kosoko seye no mulimo wakwe hachumbigwa mu Kilisito Yesu kosoko yo mulimo muswanu utandiligwe ne Mulungu kulawa kunghonga uleke chigende umo.
49002011	Hambiya mugelegele fina anyeye muugele uya hamuwa wamembe kwa chimutufi, mukwinangigwa wasifinigwe na waya wafinigwe, ikumbi dya mutufi dikugolosigwa na mikono,
49002012	ninga gelegeleni fina chigele chiya nyeye hamubaguligwa na Kilisito hamutemanhulwa kulawa mwisilaeli kahi wagenii mwi malagano ge dihuwiso, hamuwa mwichaka ihuwi kahi Mulungu muchilunga.
49002013	Ninga hambiya kulokela Kilisito Yesu anyeye mowile kutali ne Mulungu mugaligwa habehi kulokela sakame ya Kilisito.
49002014	Kosoko imwene no idigoya yetu, iyachigolose seye chuwe yumwedu, na kubena ulukasi woile hagatigati uchibagule.
49002015	Hoyalegusa ulukasii kwa mutufi wakwe no sisheliya malagiso na kugolosa muimwenyecho munhu musha yumwedu badala ya wanhu weli hoyegala idigoya lugano,
49002016	na yadahe kuchilamula chiweli kwe Mulungu kwanjila ya mutufi umwedu ahaya ho musalaba na kulegusa fikwakwaliso.
49002017	Hoyeja na kuhubili idigoya ukwenu nyeye mowile kutali kamei na waya woile habehi.
49002018	Kosoko kulokela imwene chose chipata luneka lwa kumufikila Baba kwa Muhe yumwedu.
49002019	Hambiya nyeye siyo mwa wageni keli, ninga siyo wagendanjila ninga mwa wakaya hamwedu na wasunhile wanhu wa hakaya he Mulungu,
49002020	mujengigwa mu munghindiso ya Watulumi na Wagonesi, iKilisito no sumbi ya hagatigati,
49002021	muimwene yuyo mujengo wose ukikolela hamwedu na kukula mpaka duwe ihekalu disunhile mwi Mundewa;
49002022	Muimwene umo anye nanye mukujengigwa uleke muwe kaya ya Mulungu kwa njila ya Muhe.
49003001	Kosoko ya iyo Aniye, Paulo, mohigwa kosoko ya Kilisito Yesu na kosoko yenu nyeye wamembe.
49003002	Dihuwi dyangu ni fina muhulika utogomi we mboto ye Mulungu wonenghigwe niye kosoko yenu.
49003003	Ifene foyanigubulile ichifiso na kugolosa imanyike na niye imbuli yakwe, kifana foniyandike chidodogi.
49003004	Nomo mukusoma aino motanga ifene fonimanyile ichifiso chakwe Kilisito,
49003005	ichifiso cho chisimanyike ne wana we wanhu we chigele chilokile kifana foigubuligwe hambiya muchigele achi ku watumigwa wakwe na wagonesi wasunhile kwa njila ya Muhe.
49003006	Ayo no ikuleka awamembe nawo niwahasi hamwedu na seye wakuhala hamwedu mu mutufi umwedu na wakuhangila na seye idihuwiso dyakwe dyuwile mwa Kilisito Yesu kulokela Mbuli swanu
49003007	Kosoko ya iyo Imbuli swanu aniye hanigoloswa mutogomi kwa chinghwa che imboto yakwe Mulungu cho neng'hingwa kosoko yo ludole lwe mulimo wakwe.
