49003009	na kuwagolosa wanhu wose wone na kumanya inyenda ye ichifiso chakifisile minyaka mingi ilokile mwe Mulungu yombile finhu fyose;
49003010	no kugamba fina kulokela dikanisa ubala we Mulungu hambiya umanyike na undewa wose na udaha muchilunga cha kulanga.
49003011	Adino haduwa soko ya minyaka na minyaka dyoyapangile mu Kilisito Yesu Mundewa wetu,
49003012	muimwene umo chichaka woga kahi chikihuwisa ku njila ya ihuwi dyetu umwakwe.
49003013	Ninga hambiya nikuwatasani munhofe mimoyo kosoko nikiidasa kosoko yenu na kwa itunyo dyenu.
49003014	Kosoko ya iyo nikufugama hamwande ya Baba,
49003015	Yuyo imwene ifinhu fyose kulanga na hasi fikutambuligwa,
49003016	uleke kugendela ugoli wakwe we ditunyo yakudaha kumwingha nyeye mudahe kuwa na ludole lwe ditunyo hamwedu na udaha kugendela Muhe wakwe mugati yenu,
49003017	na fina Kilisito yekale mumimoyo yenu kwa njila ya dihuwi; na ninga muwe na misisi na kugimbisigwa muwendo,
49003018	muwe na ludole lwa kutanga hamwedu na wasunhile amagalamu, matali, masisilii na gengile,
49003019	na mumanye uwendo wa Kilisito ambawo ni umanyi ulokile umanyike wose, ninga mumeme telele umemelesi wose we Mulungu.
49003020	Hambiya muimwene yene udaha ukugolosa mulimo mugati yetu kena ludole lwa kugolosa mengi kusuma gaya gochikutasa ama kugadoga,
49003021	ditunyo duwe kuimwene mwikanisa na mwa Kilisito Yesu kufyeleko fyose, minyaka na minyaka. Hano.
49004001	Aniye hambiya nimohigwa kosoko ye Mundewa, nikuwatasani mwikale mikalile kifana ya wanhu wenangigwe mulwinango womwinangwe,
49004002	hamwedu na uholo na ubasi, na ufinyilisi aku mukilondela chila munhu na miyagwe muuwendo,
49004003	hanangeni kukolelesa uumwedu we Muhe mohigwa nawo ne idigoya.
49004004	Kwina mutufi umwedu na Muhe nawo umwedu, kifana fomwinangigwe chila munhu mwihuwi dimwedu dye lwinango lwenu,
49004005	Mundewa yumwedu, dihuwi dimwedu, ubatiso umwedu,
49004006	Mulungu yumwedu naye no Baba wa wose yowile kuchanhya ya wose na muwowose.
49004007	Ninga mboto hachinghigwa chose kulokela chipimo cha ichingwa cha Kilisito.
49004008	Hambiya igambigwa, Foyapululuke kulanga hakalonda mateka kahi kalafa chinghwa kuwanhu.
49004009	(kugamba hakakwila togoleni ina maana yaki halika sikugamba imwene naye hakadulika hasi hasisi ye chilunga?
49004010	imwene yadulike no mwene kahi yapululuke kuchanya kutali lugano kuloka ulanga wose, uleke yamemese finhu fyose.)
49004011	Ne mwene hakalafa wamonga wowe watumi, wamonga wagonesi, wamonga wainjilisti, wamonga wadimi na wamonga wafusa,
49004012	uleke kuwatandila wasunhile wowe tayali kutogoma mulimo, wo kujenga mutufi wa Kilisito
49004013	mpaka chose fochikuhokela umwedu we dihuwi na umanyi we Mwana we Mulungu na kukula kuunhu we chipimo che disika dye umememelesi wa Kilisito;
49004014	uleke fina ching'agendelele kuwa fyana fikulondigwa londigwa ne mawingo ga mafuso gatungigwe na wanhu, muufundi wawo wo udasi.
49004015	Wakuleka kulonga gaya ge chawelu muuwendo, aseye chikule umwakwe imwene Kilisito ambaye no ditwi,
49004016	kosoko muimwene umutufi wose ukiyoha hamwedu na kikolela chila chilungo chakwe, chikutogoma mulimo wakwe noho umutufi ukule digoya na kijenga uwecho muuwendo.
49004017	Ninga nikulonga na kuhomelesa muMundewa fina anyeye kulawa hambiya munghekale mikalile kifana ya wamembe fowakwikala muubwalasi we mahala gawo gehile;
49004018	kosoko wakugumigwa lwisa mukutanga kwawo na waleusigwa na uumi we Mulungu kosoko yo ubwalasi uwile mugati yawo kamei na ukugutu we mimoyo yawo;
49004019	wofa mangete kahi wakiguma musimbuli so uwihi wo usulumisi uleke wagolose chila aina ya nhenda ihile,
49004020	ninga nyeye hamukifusile kwa Kilisito gago!
49004021	Nikuhuwila muhulika foifusigwe kuhusu imwene na ichawelu iya yuwile mwa Yesu.
49004022	Tageni nhenda senu sa katali isihile sikubanika sikwandamila umelo ukwenda mbuli sa udasi,
49004023	na goloseleni wanhu washa mufidoga fye sihakili senu.
49004024	Na faleni unhu usha wumbigwe kwa futa ye Mulungu muhaki ye chawelu na usunhi.
49004025	Kulawa hambiya nhafi lekeni udasi kamei chila munhu yalonge ichawelu ne miyagwe, kosoko cha filungo chila chilungo chikuhuwila miyagwe.
49004026	Ninga munghadeseka langisiseni mungheje mugolosa sambi; dijuwa ding'hoswe mwikali ne inyono,
49004027	mung'hamwinghe luhoma luneka.
49004028	Imuhiji hambiya yang'ahije keli, ibeka yalime na kutogoma milimo kwa mikono yakwe ulekeyowe na cha kuweng'ha wamonga awakuhananga.
49004029	Mbuli sihile sing'alawe mumilomo yenu, ninga siswanu na asiya sikudaha kuwatasa awakuhananga ili siweng'he mboto awakuhulika.
49004030	Ninga munghamudese Muhe Musunhile we Mulungu, ambaye muimwene umo hamutoigwa lubonoto, mpaka dijuwa diya dya uhonyi.
49004031	Usungu wose, nyono, kudeseka, chowe na maligo galeguke ukwenu, ne chila aina yo wihi,
49004032	yuweni na ubasi chila munhu na miyagwe na mimoyo ya kilekelela nyenye kwa nyenye kifana Mulungu kulokela Kilisito foyawalekeleleni nyeye.
49005001	Hambiya muwe wanhu wakugolosa fina Mulungu foyakugolosa kifana wana wendigwa.
49005002	Kamei gendeni muuwendo ifina Kilisito foyachendile seye hoyokilafa imwecho kufa kosoko yetu hakowa chilafwa che mhungile na kuwa nhambiko kwe Mulungu.
49005003	Ninga idihabwa na gose gehile mung'hagese hata kugataja ago gasikwendigwa kuwanhu we Mulungu.
49005004	Kunghowe chinyala, maligo, malumo, kahi ufumbi kosoko gasikuhanangigwa ukwenu, hanyuma yakwe du muwe wanhu wa kulumba.
49005005	Langisiseni lugano fina umo mugati yenu mwichaka muchilanga kahimunhu mwihi, ama yoyose musulumisi (mufugamila we sisanamu) yene uhasi muundewa we Kilisito na we Mulungu ayo lo kwichaka chakasi.
49005006	Munhu yang'awadanhilise kwa mbuli sakwe sibwalate. Mana nikumutamilani ni kosoko ya iino inyono ye Mulungu ikuwejila wana awasikuhulika.
49005007	Kahi munghakihase nawo,
49005008	kosoko chigele chiya hamuwa mulwisa ninga hambiya muwa muujelu we Mundewa; gendeni kifana wana we ujelu.
49005009	(kosoko dimudyo dye ujelu dikoneka nadyo ni; uswanu, haki ne chawelu)
49005010	mugese Kukonha agaya gakumwedesa Mundewa.
49005011	Ninga munghakihase na nhenda sihile se dichisa ambaso hasikweleka, ninga gagubuleni,
49005012	kosoko agakugoloseka ukwawo muchifiso ni chinyala hata kugalonga;
49005013	ninga gose gagubuligwe gakoneka munje muujelu, kosoko chila chikoneka chichoo no ujelu.
49005014	Ninga igambigwa, Handiko winuke gweye ugonile, winuke mudifa na Kilisito kokwingha ujelu.
49005015	Kilangisiseni fomukugenda siyo kifana wanhu wabwalasi ninga wabala
49005016	Togomeleni ugele fiswanu kosoko ichigele chino ni cha wihi.
49005017	Ninga munghowe wabwalasi bali tangeni agaya Mundewa goyakwenda.
49005018	Munghalewe gimbi na difai, kosoko umo mugati yakwe mwina wihi; ila memesigweni Muhe,
49005019	Kitamiliseni munhu na miyagwe aku mukwimba sabuli ne sinyimbo se tensi sa lohoni, aku mukwimba na kubwedelela Mundewa mufidoga fyenu fyose,
49005020	chila ijuwa na kwa chila chinhu lumbeni mudisina dye Mundewa watu Yesu Kilisito kwe Mulungu Baba.
49005021	Munghakibese munhuna miyagwe kosoko ya kumogoha Kilisito.
49005022	Anyeye muwanawake wahulikisiseni wagosi wenu kifana kumuhulika Mundewa,
49005023	kosoko mugosi no ditwi dye mwanamuke kifana Kilisito fo ye ditwi dye dikanisa mutufi na imwene no Mwihula.
49005024	kifana dikanisa fodikumuhulika Kilisito basi wanawake nawo wawahulike wagosi wawo kwa chila chinhu.
49005025	Anyeye wagosi wendeni wafele wenu, fina Kilisito foyajendile dikanisa mpaka yakilafa kosoko yakwe
49005026	uleke yakilafe kosoko yakwe na kudisunha kwa meji mwimbuli yakwe,
49005027	uleke yalafe ikanisa iswanu dichaka wihi kahi ilema dya wihi wowose ili duwe isunhile dichaka dyodyose dihile.
49005028	Awagosi wawende wanawake wawo kifana fowakuyenda imitufi yawo, imunhu yakumwenda imuke yakiyenda imwecho,
49005029	kosoko kwichaka munhu iyakuudesekela mutufi wakwe imwecho bali yakuwingha ndiya na kuutunduliya kifana Kilisito naye foyakudigolosela dikanisa.
49005030	kosoko seye cha filungo fya mutufi wakwe.
49005031	kosoko ya iyo mugosi yakuleka iBabakwe ne ing'ina na kiyandamila ne muke, nawo weli wakuwa mutufi umwedu.
49005032	Isili ino nghulu aniye to nikulonga du ikuhusu Kilisito na dikanisa;
49005033	Ninga chila munhu yamwende imuke fina foyakiyenda imwecho na imufele yanghaleke kumogoha imulume.
49006001	Muwana wahulikeni awaweleke mwi Mundewa, kosoko nhafo no fiswanu.
49006002	Wengheni chogoho awaBaba senu na awang'ina senu. (adino no dilagiso dye nghonga dine dilagano),
49006003	fina yokuwa mbuli inogile ukwenu, kamei mokwikala chigele chitali muchilunga,
49006004	Anye nanye waBaba munhu munghawande wana wenu, hadi wapate nyono, ninga waleleni mumafuso maswanu na maloleso ge Mundewa.
49006005	Anye muwatumwa wahulikeni awandewa wenu we chilunga kwa kogoha na kuchichima kwa chidoga chose fina fomukumugolosela Kilisito;
49006006	munghagolose du kosoko wawoneni na meso, na nyendesa ya meso du, ninga goloseni kifana watogomi wa Kilisito, awakugolosa kifa na Mulungu foyakwenda kulawa kumimoyo.
49006007	Goloseni milimo yenu kwa chinyemi, kifana mukumugolosela Mundewa ninga wanhu,
49006008	manyeni fina dyodyose diswanu dikugolosigwa na yoyose mutumwa ama simutumwa Mundewa yakwija yalafa maliho gakwe.
49006009	Anye nanye muwandewa wagoloseleni nheifo, lekeni kuweng'ha itisi manyeni fina anye nanye mwina Mundewa wenu kulanga ambaye no mukulu wawo nawo, na mugati yakwe mwichaka kubagula.
49006010	Kwa kumalagisa, nikugamba, imeni ngwingwi mwi Mundewa na kwa udaha we ludole lwakwe mukulu.
49006011	Faleni filama fyose fye Mulungu, noho mudahe kwima kitowa ne simhando sa Luhoma,
49006012	kosoko Inyisuma yetu seye siyo Nyisuma ye mitufi na sakame ninga ni udaha no ludole lwa wakulu we ichisa muchilunga achi, Ninga ni nghondo ya mhepo na wihi muchilunga cha muchanhya.
49006013	Hambiya londeni filama fyose fye Mulungu, uleke muwe na ludaha mwijuwa dya magesa, na fomukumala nheifo kwima imeni ngwi.
49006014	Hambiya mukwima nako imeni akuno mukifasa mukanda we ichawelu muchuno na kufala ngulo ye chuma ye chawelu muchifa,
49006015	na migulu yenu yuwe tayali kosoko ya mbuli swanu ye idigoya;
49006016	hamwedu na gago, londeni ne ngula ye dihuwi uleke sime umoto we misale ya luhoma.
49006017	Kamei londeni nghofiya ya wokofu ne dipanga dye Muye, nadyo no mbuli ye Mulungu.
49006018	Taseni chila ugele mu Muhe, kwa mataso gose na nhala. Muwe meso na munghofe mimoyo watasileni hata awamonga awanhu we Mulungu.
49006019	Ninga na niye nitasileni uleke Mulungu yaning'e mulomo uwechaka chogoho, mulomo wo kulonga chifiso che imbuli swanu imbuli yakwe.
49006020	Fina aniye nigaluka na munyamhala kosoko ye Imbuli swanu, ninga hambiya namuchifungo taseni uleke nilekeligwe nilonge imbuli yakwe fina fonikuhanangigwa nilonge mulamuso wo kumalagisa.
49006021	Hambiya manyeni fina fonuwile na fonikugolosa, fina iTikiko mundugusetu mwendigwa na mutogomi yahuwilike mwe Mundewa imwene yeja yawatamila chila chinhu.
49006022	Nimwigala ukwenu kosoko ya iyo du, ili mwije mumanye ifene fochuwile kamei yawagumeni moyo mufidoga fyenu.
49006023	Idigoya yuwe na nyeye wandugu, na uwendo, hamwedu ne dihuwi kulawa kwe Mulungu Baba na Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito.
49006024	Mboto yuwe na nyeye mose mukumwenda Mundewa Yesu Kilisito na kwa wendo usikufa.
50001001	Aniye Paulo na Timoseyo, watogomi wa Kilisito Yesu, Kuwasunhile wose mugati ya Kilisito Yesu awowile Filipi, hamwedu na maasikofu na mashemasi:
50001002	Dihewa dyuwe hamwedu nanye ne digoya dikulawa kwe Mulungu iBaba yetu ne Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito.
50001003	Nikumulumba iMulungu wangu chila fonikumugelegelani;
50001004	majuwa gose fonikumutasilani anyeye mose na kulonga sisala sangu kwa chinyemi,
50001005	nikulumba kosoko ya ulugota lwenu mung'endelesa imbuli swanu kulawa dijuwa dya bosi mpaka hambiya.
50001006	Na dyonihuwile fina chawelu nodino, iyakongese umulimo umuswamu mumimoyo yenu kowigala ku ndumiliso hata mwijuwa dya Yesu Kilisito.
50001007	Nhafo nofo nikwendigwa nimudogeni anyeye mose, kosoko muwa mumoyo wangu, kosoko chose chihangila imboto ino, iyokohigwa kwangu na umulimo wo kuimilisa na kuimilila imbuli ye Mulungu.
50001008	Kosoko iMulungu no muhomelesi wangu, ifene fonikumonelani nghwina anyeye mose muwendo wakwe Kilisito Yesu.
50001009	Diwombi dyangu nodino, uwendo wenu wongesekele kahi lugano, muumanyi ne misungu yose,
50001010	uleke mugafumile amaswanu lugano, kahi muwe na fidoga fiswanu mwijuwa dya Kilisito,
50001011	mumemesigwe mamudyo ge chelu, agekwija kwa njila ya Yesu Kilisito, kwa kutogolwa na kutunyigwa kwe Mulungu.
50001012	Nikuhananga anyeye wandugusangu mumanye fina gose aganipatile ganipata chawelu kosoko ya kuigendelesa mbuli swanu,
50001013	hata awasilikali na wamonga matewa wamanya fina inyohigwa yangu ni kosoko ya Kilisito;
50001014	na wengi wa wandugusangu wasindamikwa mugati ye Mundewa kosoko ye nyohigwa yangu na kugendelela kuwa wakangasi mu imbuli ye Mulungu wechaka chogoho.
50001015	Awamonga wekumuhubili Kilisito kwa chimwefe na nyisuma, ninga awamonga kwa fidoga fiswamu.
50001016	Awakeli wekumuhubili kwa wendo, wamanyile fina nyikigwa kosoko niimilile injili;
50001017	awenghonga wekumuhubili Kilisito kwa chimwefe, ng'o si kwa mimoyo mijelu, wamanyile fina wokongesa amagayo ge nyohigwa yangu.
50001018	Kahi choni? Amba kwa sinjila sose, yuwe kwa kiigilisa ama ye chawelu, Kilisito yakuhubiligwa; naniye nina chinyemi.
50001019	Heye, nobwedelela. Kosoko nimanya fina kwa njila ya mawombi genu ne utasi wa Muhe wa Yesu Kilisito agano gogaluka kulekeleligwa nyihulwa yangu,
50001020	ifene fonigojele na kuhuwila lugano fina sidaha kupata chinyala ng'o, amba kwa usindamiki mukulu fina majuwa gose Kilisito yakutunyigwa mumutufi wangu, inghowa kwa uwumi kahi kwa difa.
50001021	Kosoko ukwangu aniye kuwa mumi ni Kilisito, na kufa ni nyongesa.
50001022	Inghowa kuwa mumi chimutufi, ago no mamudyo go umulimo ukwangu. Nikali mumanhonge dyonikwendigwa nisagule sikutanga.
50001023	Nikanhamiswa hagati ya mabuli meli. Nikusulumila kuleuka nghekale na Kilisito, ayo no iswanu lugano.
50001024	Ninga kusigala chimutufi kukuhanangigwa lugano kosoko ya nyeye.
50001025	Nihuwile nheifo, nimanya fina nosigala na kugendelela nanyeye mose, ya magendelelo genu ne chinyemi mwihuwi,
50001026	uleke mudahe kongeseka kuwa ne itunyo mugati ya Kilisito Yesu, kosoko ye nyija yangu ukwenu kahi.
50001027	Ninga sinhenda senu suwe kifana Imbuli swanu ya Kilisito foikulagisa, uleke ningheja na kumonani anyeye, kahi nghona sijile, nihulike sinhenda senu, fina mwima ngwingwingwi mu Muhe yumwedu, na chidoga chimwedu kosoko ye dihuwi dye imbuli swanu,
50001028	munghogohe mbuli yoyose ya wanghondo wenu. Achino no chitangilo cha hajelu cho kwagilila kwawo, ninga uhonyi wenu uwukulawa kwe Mulungu.
50001029	Kosoko mwinghigwa anyeye kosoko ya Kilisito si kumuhuwila du, ninga na kudumangiswa kosoko yakwe,
50001030	mwingisigwa munghondo iya yomuyonile ukwangu, na hambiya mukuhulika fina ninayo.
50002001	Hambiya inghowa kwina sindamiko yoyose mugati ya Kilisito, ganghowa baho mahoso gogose ga wendo, unghowa baho lugota wowose we Muhe, nghona kwina ndekelela yoyose no ubasi,
50002002	memeleseni inyemo yangu, mudahe kuwa na chidoga chimwedu, wendo umwedu, moyo umwedu, mudoge hamwedu.
50002003	Munghagolose mbuli yoyose kwa kisuma ama kwa kiyona, ninga kwa uholo chila munhu yamone imiyagwe muswamu kusuma imwenecho.
50002004	Chila munhu yanghalongose simbuli sakwe, ninga yalongose simbuli sawayagwe.
50002005	Yuweni na chidoga chicho mugati yenu, ichuwile mugati ya Kilisito Yesu,
50002006	yuyo, iyowile kulawa kunghonga futa ya Mulungu nghonile inyuwa muliganyo ne Mulungu chinhu cha kikolelela nacho,
50002007	amba hakegolosa kechaka kulu, kuwa kefana mutumwa, kwelekwa kefana wanhu wose.
50002008	Kahe foyoneke kena futa ya munhu, hakakidulisa na kuwa muholo hata mwifa, mwifa dyo musalaba.
50002009	Hambiya iMulungu hakamukwisa lugano, na kumulugutisa disina dyakwe kusuma masina gose,
50002010	noho kwa disina dya Yesu chila ifindi difugame, dya ifinhu fyose fya kulanga na fye yisi na ifyuwile hasi ye yisi,
50002011	na chila ilimi digambe nhafi Yesu Kilisito no Mundewa kwa ukulu we Mulungu Baba.
50002012	Hambiya, wendigwa wangu, fina amajuwa gose fomugendelele kuwa na moyo wa chogoho, siyo ichigele chonyowile nanyeye du, amba hambiya lugano ichigele chosuwile nanye, togomeni kwa kogoha na kutetema kosoko yo uhonya wenu;
50002013	kosoko iMulungu noyekutogoma mulimo mugati yenu, kwenda kwenu na kutogoma kwenu, muumemelesi we nyenda yakwe.
50002014	Goloseni chila mbuli bila ya nghalasi ama nyiyusa,
50002015	mudahe kuwa wana we Mulungu mwichaka ilema, kahi udasi, mwichaka chinhu chochose chikumusigani mu cheleko chino cho ufudutu, ichagilile, chomukoneka anyeye mukwakaika muchilunga,
50002016	mukolelele imbuli yo uumi, nidahe kuwa na soko ya kitunya mwijuwa dya Kilisito, nhafi sabilime chaka ama sakiidasa chaka.
50002017	Hata ninghalafigwa uumi wangu kefana sadaka kosoko ye dihuwi dyenu kwe Mulungu, nokuwa na nyemo lugano, kahe nosangalala hamwedu nanye mu nyemo yiyo.
50002018	Anyeye nanye nheifo bwedeleleni kahe bwedeleleni hamwedu naniye.
50002019	Mundewa Yesu yanghenda, nikuhuwila kumutuma Timoseyo ukwenu chimwande, nidahe kugumigwa moyo nani ne simbuli se inyuwa yenu.
50002020	Kosoko nechaka munhu yungi ye hamwedu nani kefana imwene, iyodaha kumulangililani kwa moyo.
50002021	Kosoko awanhu wengi wekwenda simbuli sawo siyo sa Kilisito Yesu.
50002022	Anyeye mose mumumanya Timoseyo ne nyituma yakwe kefana mwana na Babakwe mumulimo we Injili.
50002023	Hambiya nikuhuwila kumutuma yuyo chimwande fonikanimanya agakanipata;
50002024	nani nimuhuwila Mundewa fina nokwija nimwenecho chimwande kahe.
50002025	Amba hanidoga yendesa kumutuma ukwenu Epafulodito, mundugusangu kahe mutogomi nani kahe chitung'ati miyangu, kahe mutumigwa wenu na mutogomi we finhu fonikwenda,
50002026	kosoko hakowa na nghwina nanye mose lugano, kuwa na usungu nanye lugano, kwasoko hamuhulika hakowa mutamu.
50002027	Chawelu hakowa mutamu, habehi na kufa. Ninga iMulungu hakamonela ubasi, kahe siyo ukwenu du amba no ukwangu nani, uleke ninghowe na sungu muchanhya yo usungu.
50002028	Hambiya nghitahidi lugano kumutuma, uleke munghamona kahi mumwayemwaye nani mhungulilwe usungu wangu.
50002029	Ninga muhokeleni imwene mugati ye Mundewa kwa nyemo yose; kahe muwe na chogoho na wanhu kefana imwene,
50002030	kosoko hakowa habehi kufa na kwangamisa uwumi wakwe kosoko yo mulimo wa Kilisito, uleke yamalagise agahunguke mu mulimo wenu ukwangu.
50003001	Kumalagisa, wandugusangu, bwedeleleni mwi Mundewa. Kuwawandikilani simbuli sisiya sonawandikile sikusoka kosoko sowatasa nyeye.
50003002	Kinegeni ne awanhu wefane mabwa, kinegeni na wekugolosa uwihi, kinegeni na wanhu awekitema mumitufi yawo.
50003003	Kosoko aseye chawalami we chawelu, ichikumufuga Mulungu mu muye, ne ditunyo dya Kilisito Yesu, na wanhu wesikihuwisila simbuli se chimutufi.
50003004	Ninga aniye nani nikudaha kihuwisila simbuli se chimutufi. Nghona hena munhu yakudoga yakudaha kihuwisila simbuli se chimutufi aniye ninaso itewa:
50003005	nafinigwa dijuwa dya munana, na munhu wa ditaifa dya Isilaeli, wa dikabila dya Benyamini, Muebulaniya nyelekwe na Waebulaniya; munghola itolati aniye na Ifalisayo,
50003006	kunyituma nadidumangisage dikanisa, muchawelu ye itolati hanyuwa namunjelu. Ninga amabuli gose gonyonage gena faida ukwangu, hanigawala hasala kosoko ya Kilisito.
50003007	Ninga amabuli gose gonyonage gena faida ukwangu, hanigawala hasala kosoko ya Kilisito.
50003008	Chawelu nikugatala amabuli gose kefana hasala kosoko yo uswamu wichaka muliganyo wo kumumanya Kilisito Yesu Mundewa wangu. Kosoko yakwe mhata hasala ya mabuli gose, nikugatala kefana chinhu chilemigwe uleke nimupate Kilisito
50003009	na koneka mwe imwene, nechaka chawelu yangu nimwenyecho, iikupatigwa kwa kwandamila sheliya, ninga iikupatigwa kwa kumuhuwila Kilisito, ichawelu iikulawa kwe Mulungu iihuwile dihuwi;
50003010	uleke nimumanye imwene na uludole wo kwinuka kwakwe muchilalo, na ulugota wa magayo gakwe, na kuliganiswa ne difa yakwe,
50003011	uleke inghadahika nani nije ninuligwe kulawa kwa wofile.
50003012	Sidaha kugamba ngaluka nisuma ama ngaluka memelekela; amba nikudoha uleke nidigolose dyuwe dyangu, kwasoko iKilisito Yesu kanigolosa nuwe wakwe.
50003013	Wandugusangu, sidaha kugamba ngaluka nidikola; amba imbuli imwedu yonikulonga noyino, kugasimilwa gose agowile kunyuma na kuchunyunhila ku agowile kumwande yangu,
50003014	nikudoha uleke nidipate digeleko idiswamu lugano dyo ulwinango mukulu we Mulungu mugati ya Kilisito Yesu.
50003015	Lekeni aseye chose chiwakangasi chidoge nheifo; hata munghadoga gengi mu mbuli yoyose, Mulungu kowagubulilani didyo nadyo.
50003016	Ninga chigendelele kuwa muchawelu yenele yochinayo.
50003017	Wandugusangu, munyandamile aniye, na kuwalanga awanhu awekwandamila umufano wochiwenghileni.
50003018	Kosoko awengi, wa awenele nigendelele kumutamilani kahe hambiya nikumutamilalani kwa masosi, wakwila kefana wanghondo wo musalaba wa Kilisito.
50003019	Indumo yawo ni kubanigwa, mulungu wawo ni sinda, kahi wekitunya mu chinyala chawo, awekudoga amabuli ge chilunga.
50003020	Ninga ukaya wetu aseye wuwa kulanga, kahi kulawa uko chikumugojela iMwihula, iMundewa Yesu Kilisito,
50003021	iyakayeubidula umutufi wetu uwichaka ludole, udahe kuliganila no mutufi wakwe we ditunyo, kwa udaha uwukumudahisa kufigolosa ifinhu fyose fyuwe hasi yakwe.
50004001	Hambiya, wandugusangu, wonikumwendani na kumonelani ngwina, inyemo yangu ne nghofiya yangu, gendeleleni kwima ngwingwingwimwe Mundewa wendigwa wangu.
50004002	Nikumutasa Ewudiya na Sindike wowe na chidoga chimwedu mwe Mundewa.
50004003	Kahe nikukutasa agwe nagwe, mwituma we chawelu, uwatase awanawake wano, kosoko hawagolosaga hamwedu naniye umulimo we mbuli swanu hamwedu na Kilemendi na awamonga wochagolosanyage umulimo, awandikwe masina gawo mu chitabu cho uwumi.
50004004	Bwedeleleni mwi Mundewa majuwa gose; kahi nikugamba, bwedeleleni.
50004005	Awanhu wose waumanye uholo wenu. iMundewa kamala keja.
50004006	Munghakiidase kwa mbuli yoyose, ninga kwa chila chinhu kwa kutasa na kufuga hamwedu ne dilumbo lekeni ifinhu fomukwenda fimanyike ne Mulungu.
50004007	Ne digoya dye Mulungu, idilokile umanyi wose, didime imimoyo yenu ne misungu yenu mu Kilisito Yesu.
50004008	Kumalagisa, wandugusangu, simbuli sose se chawelu, simbuli sose se chogoho, simbuli sose sichaka koneligwa, simbuli sose selile, simbuli sose so uyendo, simbuli sose se ditunyo diswamu, inghowa kwina chinhu chochose cha kutunya, dogeni simbuli senele siso.
50004009	Simbuli somukifusile na kuhokela na kuhulika na kona ukwangu, sigoloseni; ne iMulungu we toyoyo kokuwa hamwedu nanye.
50004010	Nina chinyemi mwe Mundewa lugano kosoko hambiya monesa ifyene fomowile hamwedu nani; hamuwa hamwedu nani chawelu, ninga hamuswela luneka.
50004011	Sikulonga gano kosoko nechaka chinhu nihungukiligwa; kosoko nghifusa kumemeswa na hali yoyose yoninayo.
50004012	Nimanya kuwa na finhu fikefu kahe nimanya kuwa na fingi; mu hali yoyose nikifusa isili yo kwiguta na kona njala, kuwanafyo na kuwa chaka.
50004013	Nina udaha wa kusuma simbuli sose mugati ye mwene iyekuniguma uludole.
50004014	Amba hamugolosa fiswamu, kwa kuwa hamwedu nani mumagayo gangu.
50004015	Kahe anyeye mo Wafilipi mowenyecho mumanya fina mu nghonga ye Injili, fonaleguke Makedoniya, hasowile na ikanisa dingi idyowile hamwedu nani mu ndafa na kuhokela ninga anyeye mwiwene;
50004016	kosoko hata kuya Sesalonike hamunigalila finhu fya kunisapusa siyo kamwedu amba majuwa itewa.
50004017	Munghagambe nikusulumila ifinhu fomwanyingile du; amba nikusulumila amamudyo ge nyongeseka yenu.
50004018	Ninafyo finhu fingi, na kongesekela; nimemelekela, mhokela kwa mukono wa Epafulodito ifinhu afiya ifilawile ukwenu, mhungile ya mafuta, sadaka yendeke, iikumwendesa Mulungu.
50004019	Ne Mulungu wangu yawamemeleseni chila chomukwenda ifyenele ugoli wakwe fouwile, mu ditunyo dhya Kilisito Yesu.
50004020	Kwe Mulungu wetu na Baba ditunyo dyuwe ukwakwe amajuwa gose. Hano.
50004021	Munamusile chila musunhile mugati ya Kilisito Yesu. Awandugusangu awowile na niye wekumulamusani.
50004022	Awasunhile wose wekumulamusani, awaya awowile mu nyumba ya Kaisali.
50004023	Dihewa dye Mundewa Yesu Kilisito dyuwe hamwedu ne fidoga fyenu.
51001001	Aniye Paulo mutumigwa wa Kilisito Yesu kwa wendo we Mulungu, na Timoseyo imundugusetu,
51001002	Kuwandugusangu awasunhile muchawelu ya Kilisito awowile Kolosai; Dihewa dyuwe nanye, ne idigoya dye Baba yetu Mulungu.
51001003	Chikumulumba Mulungu, iBabakwe we Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito amajuwa gose ichigele chochikuwatasila,
51001004	kosoko hachihulika dihuwi dyenu kwa Kilisito Yesu na uwendo womwinawo kuwasunhile wose,
51001005	kosoko ye dihuwi dyomwikiligwe kulanga. Mwihuwi didyo, hamuhulika katali simbuli sakwe se ichawelu ye Imbuli Swamu
51001006	iyafikile ukwenu, kifana foyowile muyisi yose, ikweleka mamudyo na kukula, kifana foyikukula ukwenu nako, kulawa dijuwa dyomwahulike na kumanya dihewa dye Mulungu muchawelu,
51001007	kifana fomwafusigwe na Epafula imwendigwa na mutumigwa miyetu. Kagaluka mutumigwa wa kuhuwilwa wa Kilisito ahanhu hetu
51001008	naye hakachitamila uwendo wenu ukwetu mu Muhe.
51001009	Kosoko yiyo, kukongela dijuwa dyochawahulike, chisilekile kumutasilani, kumutasa iMulungu yamumemeseni umanyi we isinhenda sakwe, no ubala womukwinghigwa ne Muhe wakwe.
51001010	Mugendelele kwikala ifene iMundewa foyakwenda na kugolosa gose agekumwendesa. Inyikala yenu yeleke mamudyo ge milimo yenu imiswamu kugendelela mu umanyi we Mulungu.
51001011	Mudahiswe no udahi wose, wo uludole wo ukulu wakwe, noho mudahe kufinyilisa na gose, hamwedu ne chinyemi;
51001012	mwingheni ilumbo iBaba iyachinghile kuhokela uhasi wa wasunhile mu ujelu.
51001013	Imwene hakachihonya muludole we chisa, na kuchisanyisila mu undewa we Mwanagwe mwendigwa;
51001014	iyekuchingha uhonya wo kulekeleligwa uwihi.
51001015	Imwene no futa ye Mulungu inghekoneka, mwelekwa we bosi we fyumbigwe fyose.
51001016	Kugendela imwene ifinhu fyose fyumbigwa, ifyuwile kulanga na ifyuwile muisi, ifikoneka na ifisikoneka; fyuwe fya magoda go undewa kahi magoda ga udaha, kahi ga ludole na udaha. Ifinhu fyose fyumbigwa kwa injila ye imwene kosoko ya imwene.
51001017	Naye yejayowa ugele ifinhu fyose na ifinhu fyose finghali fyuwe, na umwakwe ifinhu fyose fikikolelesa hamwedu.
51001018	Imwene no ditwi dyo umutufi, dikanisa; kahe imwene no nghonga, no mwelekwa we bosi wa awafile, imwene no chilongosi wa fyose.
51001019	Kosoko mugati yakwe hayendesa umemelesi wose we Mulungu wikale;
51001020	na kugendela imwene ifinhu fyose filamulwe foyafulusa kugolosa ihoso ne isakame yo musalaba wakwe; ifinhu fyose ifyuwile muisi na ifyuwile kulanga.
51001021	Anyeye, umowile aho bosi mulekigwa, kahe wanghondo mufidoga fyenu, kwe sinhenda senu sihile,
51001022	hambiha kamulamulani mumutufi wakwe, na kwa difa dyakwe, uleke yamwigaleni hamwande yakwe, wasunhile, mwichaka wihi,
51001023	mwikale mu dihuwi, mwikigwe muchanhya ye nghindiso, munghafumile kusingisigwa na kuleka dihuwi dye imbuli swamu iyahubiliigwe kwe ifyumbigwe fyose ifyuwile mu yisi; iyene aniye Paulo hanigaluka mutumigwa wakwe.
51001024	Hambiya nina chinyemi mu magayo goninago kosoko yenu; kahe nikugamemelesa mumutufi wangu amagayo agahunguke mumutufi wa Kilisito, kosoko yo umutufi wakwe, dikanisa,
51001025	dyonigaluke mutumigwa wo mulimo we Mulungu fina foninghigwe, kosoko yenu; umulimo wo kugolosa imbuli ye Mulungu inghamanyike.
51001026	Imbuli aiya iyafisigwe kulawa katali fyotoke ifyeleko fyose, hambiya igubuligwa ku wasunhile wose.
51001027	Mulungu iyendile kuwatamila ifene fouwile ugoli we ditunyo dye imbuli aino kuwamembe, uwo no Yesu mugati yetu dihuwilo dye ditunyo.
51001028	Yuyo nochikuwatamilisa imbuli yakwe, chikumujama chila munhu, na kumufusa chila munhu, mu umanyi wose uleke chimwigale chila munhu yamemelekele kwa Kilisito.
51001029	Nani nikiidasa kwa ludole lose kwe imbuli iyo, kwa udaha uukulawa ukwakwe uwuwile mugati yangu.
51002001	Kosoko nikuhananga anyeye mumanye ukulu we nyituma yangu kosoko yenu, na kosoko ya awoile Laodikiya, hamwedu na awanhu wose awasinimanyile;
51002002	uleke wahongesigwe mufidoga fyao, wakuhanganisigwa na uwendo, wakapate ugoli wose wa kumanya kwa chawelu, wamanye imbuli ifisigwe ye Mulungu na Kilisito imwenyecho,
51002003	iyina mugati yakwe ugoli wose wa ubala hamwedu no umanyi uwikigwe.
51002004	Nikumutamilani imbuli aino, imumhu yangheje yamudanhilisani kwa mbuli sa kukochelesa.
51002005	Hata ninghowa nahechaka chimutufi, mumanye fina nahamwendu nanye chimuhe, kwa nyemo kosoko ya kona ifene fomwimile chawelu mwihuwi dya Kilisito.
51002006	Hambiya fina fomumuhokele Kilisito Yesu, iMundewa, gendeleleni kwikala naye nhaifo;
51002007	mukijimbila na kujengwa naye; mugolosigwa ngwingwingwi mwihuwi, ifene fomufusigwe; na kugendelela mwi lumbo.
51002008	Langisiseni imunhu yanghawagolose kifana mwa watumwa kwa umanyi wakwe na udasi uwichaka chinhu, ifene awanhu we iyisi fowahokele, ifene amafuso age iyisi agakatali fogowile, nago ng'o si ga Kilisito.
51002009	Kosoko mugati yakwe mwina umemelesi wose we Mulungu, ifene fouwile mumutufi.
51002010	Nanye mumemelekela mugati yakwe imwene no ditwi dyo ukulu wose na undewa.
51002011	Mugati yakwe mufinigwa ku dikumbi disigolosigwe kwe imikono, kwa kuuhambula umutufi we inyama, kwa dikumbi digoloseke kwa njila ya Kilisito.
51002012	Kahe hamusikigwa hamwedu naye, mu ubatiso; na kwinuka hamwedu naye kwa kuhuwila uludole we Mulungu iyamwinule mudifa.
51002013	Nanye fomofile muwihi kuleka kufinigwa mumitufi yenu, hakawagolosa mwawomi hamwedu naye foyamalile kuchilekelela uwihi wetu wose;
51002014	foyamalile kuilegusa diwandiko dyoa uwihi wetu idyawandikwe kuchisongesa hoyailegusa inghowe baho kahi haibamandiligwa mumusalaba.
51002015	Foyamalile kuhambula ukulu na undewa na kusigubula kwa ludole, hakabwedelela naso mumusalaba uwo.
51002016	Hambiya imunhu yanghawaliganise nyeye mufyakudiya kahi ifinhu fyo kunywa, kahi kosoko ye sikukuu kahi kulawa ko umwesi kahi kosoko ye sabato.
51002017	Isimbuli aso hasuwa inyefu dya isimbuli isikwija; amba umutufi no Kilisito.
51002018	Imunhu yanghawahokeni digelo dyenu, kwa kinenela kwa kwenda kwake imwecho na kufuga malaika, kwa kigamba kwa magubulo gakwe na kiyona chaka kwa umanyi wakwe we chimunhu munhu;
51002019	kahe iyalekile kikolela ngwingwi mwitwi dyo umutufi. Kulawa imwene umutufi wose ukukula na kukoleleswa hamwedu ne ifilungo ne isinghwali, ukukula kwa udaha wa Mulungu.
51002020	Nghona mwafile hamwedu na Kilisito kulawa kumafuso agakatali agechilunga, nhani mukwikala kifana mwawanya muchilunga? Nhani mukugendelela kulongosigwa na malagiso,
51002021	Munghakole, munghawonje, munghakwafe
51002022	ifinhu afyo fyose fikubanika ugele wofikutumiigwa; na kugendelela kwandamila malagiso na mafuso ga awanhu?
51002023	Asino sikonesa kifana sina misungu, mumafugo gomukigolosele mowenyecho, na kufuga na kuudima umutufi kwa ukali; ninga gechaka ludole lwa kuwalemesa usulumisi wo mutufi.
51003001	Hambiya halika mwinuka muchilalo hamwedu na Kilisito, galangiseni agowile kuchanhya, koyowile Kilisito, kekala ku mukono wo kulume we Mulungu.
51003002	Dogeni agoile kuchanhya, siyo age muchilunga.
51003003	Kosoko hamufa, na uumi wenu ufisigwa hamwedu na Kilisito mwi Mulungu.
51003004	Ugele Kilisito foyawija yakoneke yuyo uwumi wetu, noho nanye mukwija mukoneka hamwedu naye mwitunyo dyakwe.
51003005	Kosoko yiyo, ikomeni chila mbuli iyihile ye chilunga iyuwile umwenu: Dihabwa, uwafu, kusulumila, magelegesi gehile, usulumisi wihile, na kufuga ifisikimunhu.
51003006	Kosoko ya gago inyono ye Mulungu ikwija.
51003007	Mugaga anyeye nanye hamugendela katali, fomowage mugago.
51003008	Amba hambiya gekeni kutali nanye ago gose: Inyono, fihi, uwihi, amaligo na amaligo mumilomo yenu.
51003009	Munghakidanhilise, kosoko mufulusa kuhambula uunhu wenu wa katali hamwedu ne sinhenda sakwe;
51003010	na kuufala uunhu musha, uukugolosigwa musha noho upate umanyi kifana imwenyecho iyawombile.
51003011	Aho hechaka Muyunani kahi Muyahudi, kufinigwa kahi kuleka kufinigwa, mugeni kahi mumataifa, mutumwa kahi isimutumwa, amba iKilisito no gose, na mugati ya gose.
51003012	Hambiya, kosoko mugaluka wanhu musaguligwe ne Mulungu, wasunhile umukwendigwa, faleni moyo wa ubasi, uswamu, unenenghesi, chogoho, uholo, na ufinyilisi,
51003013	mukitase na kilekelela, imunhu yanghowa kena mbuli ne miyagwe yamulekelele fina iMundewa foyawalekelele anyeye nanye mukilekelele nheifo.
51003014	Kahe, muchanhya yago gose kiyoheni uwendo no chifungo cha umemelesi.
51003015	Na digoya dya Kilisito dilamule mufidoga fyenu; nodyo mwenangiligwe, mumutufi umwedu, kahe muwe wanhu wa ilumbo.
51003016	Imbuli ya Kilisito ikale kwa umemelesi mugati yene, mukifuse na kijama chila munhu na miyagwe mu ubala wose, na kwimba sabuli na nyimbo, na nyimbo se Chimuhe; akuno mukumwimbila Mulungu kwe ilumbo dyose mufidoga fyenu.
51003017	Na chila chomukugolosa, kwa mbuli au kwa nhenda, goloseni gose mwisina dye Mundewa Yesu, akuno mukumulumba Mulungu Baba kugendela imwene.
51003018	Anyeye muwanawake muwahulike awalume senu, ifene foyagilwe mwi Mundewa.
51003019	Anyeye muwagosi, wendeni awake senu munghowe na ukali nawo.
51003020	Anyeye muwana wahulikeni awaBaba senu na awang'ina senu musimbuli sose; kosoko imbuli ayo ikumwendesa Mundewa.
51003021	Nanye muwaBabamunhu, munghawande awana wenu wangheje wafifihala mufidoga fyawo.
51003022	Anyeye muwatumwa muwahulike awakulu wenu we chilunga, musimbuli sose, siyo kiyonesa mumeso, kefana awekikomba kuwanhu, ninga kwa moyo muswanu akuno mukumogoha Mundewa.
51003023	Chila dyo mukugalosa goloseni kwa moyo, fina kwi Mundewa kahe si kwa wanhu,
51003024	mumanye nhafi mohokela kwe Mundewa uhasi kifana igelo dyenu; mukumutogomela Mundewa Kilisito.
51003025	Kosoko iyekupujila kohokela maliho go uwihi wakwe, kahe hechaka koneligwa.
51004001	Anyeye Muwakulu, wagoloseleni awatumwa wenu mu digoya na kuwengha foiwagile kwinghigwa, kosoko mumanye nanye fina mwina Mundewa kulanga.
51004002	Mugendelele lugano kutasa, na kuwa meso mu nhasa hamwedu na kulumba;
51004003	kahe muchitasile naseye, noho iMulungu yachikumulile mulango we imbuli yakwe, chilonge imbuli iyifisigwe ya Kilisito ilekile aniye nikohigwa,
51004004	noho nilonge, fonikwendigwa nilonge.
51004005	Muwe wabala na wose awowile kunje, na kugolosela digoya ichigele chomwinghigwe.
51004006	Isinonga senu suwe na ihewa amajuwa gose, sikolele munyu, mudahe kumanya foyagile kumubidula chila munhu.
51004007	iTikiko komutamilani simbuli sangu sose; imwene mwendigwa wangu kahe mutogomi yahuwilwe miyetu mu milimo ye Mundewa.
51004008	Nimutuma imwene ukwenu kosoko mumanye ifene fochuwile, kahi yawagumeni moyo,
51004009	kahe hamwedu na Onesimo, imundugusangu yahuwilwe, iyowile hamwedu nanye. Wowatamilani chila chinhu ichigoloseke ahano.
51004010	Alistaliko, iyohigwe hamwedu naniye, yakumulamusani; na Maluko imwihwawe wa Balinaba iyamwinghileni amalagiso yangheja ukwenu muhokeleni,
51004011	na Yesu iyekwinangigwa Yusito. Awo ni wanhu wafinigwe mugati ya watogomi wayangu kosoko yo undewa we Mulungu kahe wagendelela kunhasa lugano.
51004012	Epafula imwinya ukwenu, imutumigwa wa Kilisito Yesu, yekumulamusani, na kugolosa ludole majuwa gose kosoko yenu munhasa yakwe, uleke mwime ngwingwingwi na kugendelela chawelu kumwendesa Mulungu.
51004013	Kosoko nikumutamilani fina kagolosa kwa ludole kosoko yenu na kwa waya Laodikiya, na awoile Hielapoli.
51004014	Luka, imuganga mwendigwa, na Dema wekumulamusani.

51004016	Ibaluwa ino fomukufulusa kuyisoma, wengheni awayenu wa dikanisa dya Laodikiya waisome nawo; na ibaluwa iya yonawandikile awa Laodikiya wamwingheni nanye muisome.
51004017	Mugambeni Alikipo, Yakonye kuwugolosa umulimo woyenghigwe ne Mundewa.

52001001	Paulo, Siliwano na Timoteyo Kudikanisa dya Wasesalonike dye Mulungu Baba ne Mundewa Yesu Kilisito: Mboto ne dihewa dyuwe na nyeye.
52001002	Chikumulumba Mulungu majuwa gose kosoko ya nyeye mose, ninga hachikuleka kuwatajani nomo chikutasa.
52001003	Ninga chikugelegela dihuwi ne milimo yenu ye uwendo kamei na kufinyilisa kwenu ne dihuwilo dyenu mwiMundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito.
52001004	Kosoko chimanya wandugu setu wendigwa we Mulungu fina Mulungu yawasagula nyeye.
52001005	Kosoko imbuli yetu swanu haimwijilani nyeye si kwa nonga muhala ninga kwa ludole na Muhe Musunhile hamwedu na umanyi mukulu, kahi mumanya hachuwa wanhu wa aina yaki ukwenu,
52001006	nanye hamuwa wandamisi wetu na wandamilaji wa Mundewa kosoko ye imbuli iya yomuhokele kwa lwidaso mukulu, ninga kwa chinyemi chigumigwe na Muhe Musunhile;
52001007	Kamei homukuwa mufano muswanu ku Wakilisito wose woile Makedoniya na Akaya.
52001008	Ninga siyo kugamba imbuli ye Mulungu ikuhulikika ako ukwenu Makedoniya na Akaya du muhala ninga dihuwi dyenu mwi Mulungu dimanyike kose uleke seye chuwe chichaka dyokulonga
52001009	Kosoko awene awecho wakusimulila muchanhya yetu ifene fomwachihokele kamei fomwamubidukile Mulungu na kuleka kufuga fisikimunhu na kumutogomela Mulungu ye mumi ne wechawelu,
52001010	na kumugojela imwanagwe yakulawa kulanga imwene woyamulafile kulawa muchilalo, naye yuyo no Yesu iyakuchihonya seye na inyono inghulu ikwija.
52002001	Kosoko nyeye muwecho wandugu setu mumanya kwingila kwetu ukwenu fina kusowile chaka
52002002	ninga kwa kudumangisigwa na kugoloseligwa gehile kifana ako Filipi ni kosoko ye Mulungu du no ilekile chihubili imbuli swanu kwa njila ya magayo makulu.
52002003	Kosoko majamo getu gasilawile kwa makosa ama kwa wihi, na finju ihile,
52002004	ninga ni kosoko chipata luhusa kwe Mulungu na kuhuwilika ne inonga ye imbuli swanu hata nheifo chikulonga siyo kwa kwendesa wanhu ninga kwa kumwendesa Mulungu iyakugesa mimoyo yetu.
52002005	Fina fomumanyile ne Mulungu muhomelesi wetu hachejile kwa nonga sa kiyona ama ga uchoyo;
52002006	togoleni nong'amba hachija kiyonesa na kukongha kutogoligwa na wanhu, nikuwatamilani ninga si ukwenu kahi kuwamonga,
52002007	uleke chuwe watumigwa wa Kilisito. Na ninga hachuwa waholo mugati yenu kifana mwanamuke foyakulela chali chakwe imwecho.
52002008	Kwanheifo ase nase chikuwalelani nyeye na kuhangila siyo imbuli swanu du ye Mulungu ninga na fidoga fyetu nafyo, kosoko mugaluka wandugu lugano ukwetu.
52002009	Kosoko mukugelegela magayo getu na difuke wandugu setu hachitogoma milimo chilo na misi uleke chinghamutwike munhu wowose ikanda mugati yenu nomochikutamilisa imbuli swanu ye Mulungu.
52002010	Anyeye mwawahomelesi hamwedu ne Mulungu inyuwa yochowile nayo mugati yenu ya uswanu na moyo mujelu wichaka nonga ihile munghenda yetu ukwenu Wakilisito.
52002011	Fina fomumanyile hachimujama chila munhu mugati yenu kifana Baba yakulonga na wanagwe,
52002012	Hachiwagumo nghinyo na kuwatasani mwikale mikalile ikumwendesa Mulungu iyawenangileni muundewa wakwe imwecho we ditunyo.
52002013	Ase nase majuwa gose chikumulumba Mulungu kosoko yaiyo kosoko kulawa fomwaihokele imbuli ye Mulungu yomuhulike kulawa ukwetu hamuihokela siyo kifana mbuli ya munhu ninga ye ichawelu ye Mulungu iikutogoma milimo mugati yenu.

53001008	ne dililimba dye umoto kuwatosa awaya wamulemile Mulungu na awaya awasikwenda kuhulika imbuli swanu ye Mundewa wetu Yesu.

53001011	Hambiya chikutasa majuwa gose kosoko yenu uleke Mulungu wetu yawataleni fina mukufaha mu lwinango lwakwe yawamemeleseni chila chiswanu ne umulimo we dihuwi,
53001012	uleke disina dye Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito ditunyigwe.

54001001	Paulo, mutumigwa wa Kilisito Yesu ku dilagiso dye Mulungu Mwihula wetu na wa Kilisito dihuwi dyetu,
54001002	Ku Timoseyo gomwanangu we chawelu mwi huwi: Dihewa, ubasi ne digoya kulawa kwe Mulungu iBaba na Kilisito Yesu iMundewa wetu fyuwe nagwe.
54001003	Ifene fonakulagise gweye usigale Efeso ichigele chonalutage Makedoniya, uleke uwalemese awanhu wamonga wanghafuse mafuso gengi,

54001010	kahi awedihabwa, kahi awekuduwa na wanhu munjila ye cholo chikulu, awahijaji wa wanhu, kahi awadasi, kahi awekilaha kwa udasi, kahi na mbuli yoyose iisikifumilisa na na mafuso go uwumi,

54001014	kahi dihewa dye Mundewa wetu hadyongeseka lugano ukwangu hamwedu na dihuwi na uwendo ifyuwile mu Kilisito Yesu.
54001015	Ni mbuli ya chawelu kahi yagila kuhuwiligwa lugano, ing'amba Kilisito Yesu yeja muchilunga kuwehula awena sisambi. Aniye no we nghonga wa awena sisambi;
54001016	ninga hanipata ubasi kosoko ino, uleke mu niye we inghonga, Yesu Kilisito yonese umemelesi wo ufinyilisi wakwe, uwe ifuso ku wose awakawomuhuwila imwene kosoko yo uwumi wa majuwa gose.

54001019	uwe na dihuwi na chidoga chiswamu. Kwa kuleka ichidoga chiswamu, awanhu wamonga wogwa na kwagilisa dihuwi,
