54003016	Hechaka manhonge, isili ye ifuga igaluka nghulu: Hakoneswa mumutufi, na kumanyika mu Muhe, hakonigwa na wamalaika hakahubiliigwa muwamembe hakahuwiligwa muchilunga na kwinuligwa kuchanhya mwitunyo.
54004001	Hambiya iMuhe yakulonga bila chifiso nhafi ifigele fye indumo awamonga wokitemanula ne dihuwi na kuhulikisa imimuhe yo udasi na mafuso ga magini,
54004002	kwa udasi wa wanhu awekulonga udasi, akuno ifidoga fyawo fikwaka moto,
54004003	wakuwalemesa awanhu wanghakitole na kuwagamba wenege ne fyakudiya ifyumbigwe ne Mulungu fihokeligwe kwe ilumbo, na wose awena dihuwi kahi awamanyile ichawelu.
54004004	Kosoko chila chinhu chumbigwe ne Mulungu chigaluka chiswanu, kahi hechaka ichilemigwa chinghahokeligwa kwe ilumbo;
54004005	kosoko chihojojolwa ne imbulu ye Mulungu na kutasa.
54004006	Unghawengha amafuso gano awandugu, kokuwa mutogomi muswamu wa Kilisito Yesu, akuno ukugendelela musimbuli se dihuwi na mumafuso maswanu gowandamile.
54004007	Unghandamile sisimo se chibwalasi sa katali isichaka ulungu. Kifuse gomwenyecho imikalile ye chimulungu;
54004008	kosoko inghowa inyifusa amafuso ge chimutufi inoga, ninga inyifusa amafuso ge chimulungu inoga lugano musimbuli sose, kosoko ina ilagano dyo uwumi wa hambiya na uya we chigele chikwija.
54004009	Inonga ino ya chawelu kahi yagila kufumiligwa.
54004010	Kosoko mpaka kundumiliso ino chikiidasa na kupiligala, kosoko china ihuwi mwi Mulungu imumi, Mwihula wa wanhu wose, lugano awahuwile.
54004011	Lagisa kahi fusa simbuli sino.
54004012	Imunhu wowose yanghaubese ujelelo wako, ninga uwe chinhu cha kifusila kuwahuwile mu nonga na mumigendele na muwendo na mwihuwi na mumikalile miswanu.
54004013	Mpaka fonikwihja, piligala mu soma na kujama na kufusa.
54004014	unghaleke kuchitogomela ichise che Mulungu chuwile mugati yako, choninghigwe kwa ugonesi na kwa kwikiligwa mikono na wasehe.
54004015	Wandamila gano, wikale mugago, uleke wanhu wose wone ifene foukugendelela.
54004016	Kituse ne chidoga chako, na mafuso gako; gakolelese kosoko kwa kugolosa nheifo kodaha kihonya agweye gomwenyecho na wekukuhulikisa.
54005001	Unghamugombele imusehe, ninga mulolese kefana Babako; wagolosele awajelelo kefana wanduguso,
54005002	awadala kifana wang'inasako, awanawake wadodo kifana welumbuso muuya wose.
54005003	Uwe na chogoho ku wanawake wegane, awegane chawelu chawelu.
54005004	Imwanamuke mwigane yanghowa na wana ama wajukulu, leka wende kifusa simbuli se ifuga ukaya ukwawo kamei kamei wawagolosele digoya awaBaba sawo na wang'ina sawo; kosoko imbuli yo ifumiligwa ne Mulungu.
54005005	Ninga imwene imwigane chawelu chawelu, kalekigwa yemwene, yuyo keka dihuwi dyakwe mwi Mulungu, naye kogendelela mu kutasa na inhasa chilo ne misi;
54005006	ninga imwanamuke inghodaha kisisa imwenyecho kafulusa kufa hata yanghowa yekali mumi.
54005007	Uwenghe amalagiso gano, uleke wanghowe na ilema.
54005008	Imunhu wowose inghekuwatasa awanhu wo ukwakwe, nong'amba awanhu we inyumba yakwe kafulusa kulema dihuwi dyakwe kahi kagaluka mwihi kusuma imunhu inghahuwile.
54005009	Imwigane yanghawandikigwe mpaka yafike minyaka makumi mutandatu, naye hakowa muke wa mulume yumwedu;
54005010	naye yowe kahomelelwa sinhenda siswanu, yanghowa kakusa wanagwe fiswanu, iyawagolosele ihewa wageni, yanghowa kawanasha wasunhile migulu, yanghowa kawatasa awekudumangiswa, kahi iyakilafile kugolosa sinhenda siswanu.
54005011	Ninga lema kuwawandika awegane wa disika didido; kosoko wanghakolwa no usulumisi we chimutufi fonghekwenda Kilisito wohanga kutoligwa,
54005012	nawo wagila uliganiso kosoko wabena ichipingo chawo cha bosi.
54005013	Kahi hamwedu nag ago, wakifusa kuwa wadoba, kwa kusunguluta nyumba kwa nyumba, kahi si udoba du, ninga wagaluka wahehaji kahi wasakusaku, wakulonga simbuli isisiwagile kulonga.
54005014	Hambiya nikuhananga awegane we disika didodo watoligwe, walele wana, walongose sinyumba sawo, uleke wanghamwinghe imunghondo luneka lwa kuchitofula seye.
54005015	Kosoko awamonga wafulus kubiduka na kumwandamila Shetani.
54005016	Inghowa hena mwanamuke dikanisa dinghowe na musigo, uleke diwatase wamonga, awegane chawelu chawelu.
54005017	Awasehe awekulongosa fiswanu yagila wenghigwe maliho keli, nawo no waya awekutogoma umulimo wo kuhubili na kufusa.
54005018	Kosoko diwandiko dikugamba “Unghayowe mulomo ing'ombe youkutogomela umilimo wo kutowa uhemba mu chuga inghadiye simhule”, kahi “imutogomi yagila yahokele maliho gakwe.”
54005019	Unghafumile usongesi ku imusehe, ninga imbuli iyo ihomelelwe na wahomelesi weli hegu wadatu.
54005020	Awaya awekugendelela mu sambi, uwagombele mumeso ga wose, uleke wamonga wogohe.
54005021	Nikukulagisa mumeso ge Mulungu na Kilisito Yesu na wamalaika wasagulwe, ugolose gano bila kuliganisa chimwande hegu kwa konela.
54005022	Unghamwikile munhu mikono chimwande, kahi unghakigume musisambi wa wanu wamonga; ikala mikalile ye uuya.
54005023	Unghonywe meji muhala, ninga gimbi chidodogi kosoko ya sinda sako, ne sinhamu isikukwidasa chila chigele.
54005024	Sisambi sa wanhu wamonga sa hajelu, silongola ku uliganiso, ninga sisambi sa wamonga sikuwandamila ichigele chikwija.
54005025	Nheifo kahi sinhenda siswanu sa hajelu; kahi asiya isikoneka sisidaha kifisa.
54006001	Wose wowile hasi yo utumwa wawenghe chogoho awakulu wawo, uleke disina dye Mulungu dinghatofuligwe na mafuso getu.
54006002	Awaya awena wakulu awahuwile wanghawabese kosoko wagaluka ndugu; yagila wawatogomele muuswanu lugano wose, kosoko wose awekupata nyongesa kosoko yo mulima wawo wagaluka ndugu kahi wendigwa. Fusa kahi jama simbuli sino.
54006003	Imunhu wowose yanghafusa mafuso gengi kahi nghekufumila amafuso ge chawelu ge Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito, hegu mafuso ge ifuga yetu,
54006004	kamema nyiyona kahi nghamanyile mbuli yoyose; ninga muchilalu wa kudoga simbuli so kuwanga, isina mugati yakwe gele, lefi, usongesi, ubalalilaji,
54006005	na kugomba na wanhu wabanike mahala gawo, awaswelile ichawelu, awekudoga fina imikalile ye chimulungu ni luneka lwa kupatila ugoli.
54006006	Imikalile ye chimulungu ina ugoli mukulu kwa kumugolosa imunhu yegusigwe ne ifinhu foyenafyo;
54006007	kosoko sicheja na chinhu muchilunga kahi sichidaha kuleuka na chinhu kulawa muchilunga;
54006008	ninga chinghowa na chakudiya na suke chodaha kwigusigwa ne finhu fifyo.
54006009	Ninga wose awekwenda kuwa wagoli wakugwila mumagesa, na kugwila mumutego na usulumisi we chibwalasi kahi uukukoma, uukuwatubugisa awanhu mu uwagilisi na ubani.
54006010	Kosoko kwenda mapesa no musisi wo wihi wose; awanhu wamonga kwa kwenda lugano mapesa, waleka dihuwi dyawo na kihoma mumimoyo yawo kwa usungu mwingi lugano.
54006011	Ninga agweye, munhu wa Mulungu kinege na mabuli gano kongha ichawelu, mikalile ya chimulungu, dihuwi, uwendo, kugojela na upolo.
54006012	Lewa imilewo miswanu ye dihuwi; kolelesa uwumi wa maiwa gose wowenangiligwe ichigele fowalambile hamwande ya wahomelesi wengi.
54006013	Hamwande ye Mulungu iyekufingha ifinhu fyose uwumi, na hamwande ya Kilisito Yesu iyaihomelele na kuifumila ichawelu hamwande ya Pondiyo Pilato,
54006014	nikukulagisa ukolelese dilagiso dino bila ya ibando hegu ilema mpaka koneka kwakwe kwe Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito;
54006015	Kahi adino dikadikoneka bila ya chifiso muchigele chifumiligwe, ne imwene iyalugutisigwe kahi iyena ludole yemwene, Mundewa wa wandewa kahi Mukulu wa wakulu.
54006016	Yuyo ye imwene inghekufa, kahi iyekwikala muujelu uusikudaha kusegelelwa, inghenati yonigwe na munhu wowose hegu iyedaha kumona. Imwene yenghigwe chogoho na udaha majuwa gose. Hano.
54006017	Awagoli muchilunga chino, wagambe waleke kiyona, hegu wangheke ugoli uwichaka ichawelu, ninga wamuhuwile Mulungu iyekuchingha ifinhu fyose fingi uleke chifidiye kwa kubwedelela.
54006018	Wagolosele maswanu, uleke wowe wagoli wa kugolosa sinhenda siswanu, undewa na chise,
54006019	akuno wakiikile sigafu yuwe nghindiso swanu kosoko ye chigele ichikwija, uleke wapate uwumi we chawelu.
54006020	Agweye Timoseyo, kolelesa simbuli sose sowinghigwe. Kinege ne simbuli isichaka ulungu isichaka chuinhu na inyisuma ya misungu iikwinangigwa yo udasi,
54006021	kwa kuihomelela iyo awamonga waswela dihuwi. Dihewa dyuwe hamwedu nanye.
55001001	iPaulo, mutumigwa wa Kilisito Yesu kwa wendo we Mulungu, kosoko yo uumi uwuwile mugati ya Kilisito Yesu,
55001002	kwa Tinoseyo, imwanangu mwendigwa; Imboto, ubasi, na imheho kulawa kwe Mulungu Baba na Kilisito Yesu iMundewa wetu fyuwe hamwedu nagwe.
55001003	Nikumulumba Mulungu yonikumufuga kwa chidoga chelile, ifene fowagolosaga cha Baba, ichigele chose chonikukugelegela munhasa yangu.
55001004	Ifene fonikugelegela amasosi gako, nina ngwina lugano nechilo na nemisi ya kukona gweye, uleke memelesigwe ne chinyemi.
55001005	Nikugelegeswa na dihuwi dyako idichaka chimwefe, dihuwi idyowaga mwe imamako Loisi ne inghinako Eunike na ichigele chino nimanya fina dyuwa umwako.
55001006	Hambiha nikukugelegesa usonghelese ichipawa che Mulungu ichuwile mugati yako kwa kwikiligwa mikono yangu;
55001007	kosoko iMulungu nghachingha moyo we ikeng'enha ninga moyo wa ludole na wendo na ufinyilisi.
55001008	Hambiha unghawonele chinyala uhomelesi we Mundewa wetu, kahi unghanyonele niye chinyala nimufungwa wakwe, ninga ufinyilie agehile hamwedu nani kosoko ye Injili muludole we Mulungu,
55001009	iyachihonya seye na kuchinanga seye mu lwinango umusunhile, siyo kosoko ya sinhenda setu, amba kwasoko yo uwendo wakwe ne simboto soyachingha seye mugati ya Kilisito Yesu minyaka itewe iilongole.
55001010	na hambiya igubuligwa kwa kwija kwakwe Mundewa wetu Kilisito Yesu, iyasumile difa na kwigala umi na kubanika kuwa jelu kwa njila ya injili.
55001011	Kosoko ye injili nasagulwa nyuwe muhubili kahe mufusaji,
55001012	kahe hambiya nikudumangila fina fonyuwile. Ninga sikona chinyala, kosoko nimumanya yonimuhuwile, na nimanya fina kena ludole lwa kwikilisa ichinhu chonikiligwa mpaka Dijuwa diya.
55001013	kolelesa umufano we simbuli so uumi souhulike ukwangu, mwihuwi na uwendo uwuwile mugati ya Kilisito Yesu;
55001014	kolelesa imbuli ye chawelu yowinghigwe gweye ne Muye Musunhile iyowile mugati yetu.
55001015	Ifene foumanyile fina awanhu wose awowile Asiya, wafulusa kunileka, mugati yawo no cha Figelo na Helimogene.
55001016	iMundewa yawonele ubasi wose awowile munyumba ya Onesifolo, kosoko hakanisangalasaga figele fingi, na kuleka konela chinyala iminyolo yangu,
55001017	ninga foyafikile ahano Lumi hakanikongha kwa ludole hoyonyona.
55001018	Mundewa yamonele ubasi Mwijuwa diya, na agweye kumanya fiswanu ifene foyanihokele kwa mengi ako Efeso.
55002001	Hambiya gweye, mwanangu, wime chewelu mumboto iyuwile mugati ya Kilisito.
55002002	Na simbuli siya souhulike ukwangu hamwande ya mashahidi itewa uwenghe awanhu awahuilwe awodaha kuwafusa wamonga nawo.
55002003	Uwe mumagayo hamwedu nani kefana chitung'ati yahuwilwe na Kilisito Yesu.
55002004	Hechaka chitung'ati iyekitowa munghondo iyokiguma mu milimo ye chilunga, yadahe kumwendesa imukulu wakwe iyamwingise mumulimo.
55002005	Hata imunhu iyekisuma mumiseigo nghodaha kwinghingwa mhongesi yanghaleka kisuma muchawelu ifene foikwendigwa.
55002006	Yagila imulimi iyekituma mumulimo yowe wa nghonga kuhokela dikanda dya mamudyo agalawile mumugunda.
55002007	Kolelesa lugano gonikutamile, kosoko iMundewa kokwingha udaha wa kumanya chila chinhu.
55002008	Mugelegele Yesu Kilisito, iyenuke kulawa kwa wofile, iwo lukolo lwa Daudi, ifene foikulonga Injili yangu,
55002009	nani mu Injili iyo ndumangiswa mpaka kohigwa kefana ngolosa wihi. Ninga imbuli ye Mulungu isikudaha kohigwa.
55002010	Kosoko iyo nikufinyilisa simbuli sose, kosoko ya wanu wasagulwe, uleke nawo wapate uhonya uwuwile mugati ya Kilisito
55002011	Ni mbuli ya kuhuwiligwa: Inghowa chufa hamwedu naye, chokwikala hamwedu naye;
55002012	inghowa chofinyilisa, chokuwa wandewa hamwedu naye; chinghamulema imwene, naye kodaha kuchilema seye;
55002013	chinghaleka kuwa na ihuwi, imwene yakusigala wa kuhuwiligwa, kosoko ngodaha kilema imwenyecho.
55002014	Uwagelegese simbuli sino, na kuwajama hamwande ye Mundewa wanghowe na nyisuma ye simbuli isichaka chinhu chochose, amba sikuwagilisa awekusihulikisa.
55002015	Upiligale lugano ukiyonese fina kufumiligwa ne Mulungu, mtogomi we milimo iyechaka chinyala, iyakolelese imbuli ye chawelu ye Mulungu.
55002016	Kinege na mabuli agechaka dini, kosoko gakuwegala awanhu kutali ne Mulungu,
55002017	na dibuli dyokwenela kefana ilonda ndugu. Mugati yawo no cha Hinenayo na Fileto,
55002018	awaiswelile ichawelu, wekugamba nhafi indumo ifulusa kuloka. Howabidula dihuwi dya wamonga.
55002019	Amba umusingi we Mulungu uukangale ufulusa kwima, wina muhuli uno: iMundewa kawamanya wose awakwe na chila iyekutambula disina dya Mundewa yauleke uwihi.
55002020	Mugati ye inyumba inghulu siyo du mwina finhu fye sahabu na fesa amba mwina fya mabiki na fya ulongo; ifimonga fina heshima na ifimonga fichaka.
55002021	Hambiya inghowa imunhu kakikwema kwa kinega nawo, kokuwa chiya cha kwinghigwa heshima, ichisunhigwe, ichimwagile Mundewa, chigoloswa kwa chila mulimo muswamu.
55002022	Ninga utije usulumisi wo ujelelo na uikonghe ichawelu, dihuwi, uwendo, na itoyoyo hamwedu na wose awekwinanga iMundewa kwa chidogo chelile.
55002023	Ugaleme amaswali go ubwalasi agechaka mahala; umanyile fina gakwigala ulefi.
55002024	Na kwa uholo awekisuma naye. Mulungu kodah Imutogomi we Mundewa yakwendigwa yanghowe mulefi amba muholo kwa chila yumwedu, iyekudaha kufusa, mufinyilisi,
55002025	iyekudaha kuwajama kwa uholo awekisuma naye. Mulungu kodaha kuwatasa walambe na kuimanya ichawelu,
55002026	wadahe kinega no muheto wa luhoma, uwuwakolile, wagolose sinyenda sakwe.
55003001	Ninga umanye imbuli ino, nhafi amajuwa ge indumo kokuwa na figele fya kogohesa.
55003002	Kosoko awanhu wokuwa wakiyenda awenyecho, wakwenda mapesa, wakwenda kitunya, wakiyona, waligaji, wasikuwahulika awaBaba sawo na awang'ina sawo, wechaka ilumbo, wehi,
55003003	wasikuwenda awanhu wo ukwawo, wasikwenda kulamulwa, wasongesi, wechaka ufinyilisi, wakali, wasikwenda uswamu,
55003004	wahomelesi wo udasi, wafumbi, wekiyona, awekwenda amabuli gehile kuliko Mulungu,
55003005	wekigamba wamuhokela Mulungu amba awekukana uludole wakwe. Kinege na wanhu wo.
55003006	Kwasoko mugati yawo waumo wanhu awekwingila musinyumba sa wanhu na kuwalonda wanawake awechaka ludole, awena amakanda go uwihi wakoligwe no usulumisi wa mataho itewa,
55003007	awekituma kuhulikisa kwa chila munhu amba awesidaha kugafikila mahala ge chawelu.
55003008	Kefana Yanne na Yamble awamulemage Musa, awano nawo wakuilema ichawelu, wanhu wajugume matwi na awalemigwe na simbuli se dihuwi;
55003009	Ninga siwodaha kutowa nghanyo; kwasoko ubwalasi wawo wokonigwa na wanhu wose, kefana fowowile awuya wa wanhu weli. Mafuso ge ndumiliso
55003010	Ninga agweye kufulusa kona amafuso gangu, dihuwi dyangu, ufinyilisi wangu, uwendo wangu, umwimo wangu,
55003011	amagayo gangu, indumangiswa yangu, agamhatile Lisitila, amba hanifinyilisa kwa chila igayo; kahe mugago gose iMundewa hakamhonya.
55003012	Chawelu wose awekwenda kwikala ifene Kilisito Yesu foyekwenda wondumangiswa,
55003013	ninga awehi na wadasi wogendelela na kongeseka kuwa wehi, kudanha na kudanhiliswa.
55003014	Ninga gweye, ugendelele ne simbuli siya soufusigwe na kuhuiswa, kosoko kumanya kwifusa kwa che nani
55003015	na kulawa udodo wako kugamanya amawandiko masunhile, agodaha kukwingha mahala go kupata uumi kwa dihuwi idyuwile mugati ya Kilisito Yesu.
55003016	Amawandiko gose gena Muhe wa Mulungu kahe gena udaha wa kufusa, kugombela, kujama, kufusa mu chawelu,
55003017	uleke imunhu we Mulungu yamemelekele, yadahe kugolosa chila mulimo muswamu.
55004001	Nikukulagisa hamwande ye Mulungu na ya Kilisito Yesu iMulamusi wa wanhu awomi na wafile, na kwa kugubuligwa kwakwe no uumi wakwe:
55004002	tamilisa imbuli, wiyohe chigele chiswamu ne chihile, jama, gombela, na kulolesa kwa ufinyilisi wose na kufusa.
55004003	Kosoko chokwija chigele awanhu wakaalema mafuso go uumi, ninga kwa kwandamila sinyenda sawo awenyecho wodaha kupata wafusaji awekuwendesa,
55004004	nawo wokinega wanghahulike simbuli se chawelu na kubidukila sisimo so udasi.
55004005	Amba gweye, wiyohe majuwa gose, finyilisa mumagayo, togoma umulimo wo uinjilisti, togoma umulimo wako.
55004006	Kosoko aniye nyuwa muchigele cho kulafigwa nyuwe nhambiko; ichigele cha difa dyangu chisegelela.
55004007	Nilewa inghondo fiswamu, inhambo niimala, dihuwi nidimilisa;
55004008	kulawa baho nyikilwa mhongesi yo kusuma kwangu, yonikanikwinghigwa ne Mundewa, imulamusi we chawelu mwijuwa diya, kahe siyo niye muhala amba na wose awendile kwija ukwakwe.
55004009	Witahidi kwija ukwangu chimwandemwande.
55004010	Kosoko Dema kwa kwenda ichulunga chino hakandeka na kuluta Tesalonike; Kilesike kaluta Galatiya, Tito kaluta ku Dulumatiya.
55004011	Luka du noyowile naniye. Mulonde Maluko kamei mwijanye; kosoko yakunhasa lugano mumulimo.
55004012	Tikiko hanimwigala Efeso.
55004013	Ichigele chowukwija, wigale inghasu yangu yonalekile kwa Kalupo ku Tolowa, kahe wigale ifitabu fiya fye singhingo.
55004014	Alekisanda ayuya imulugulusaji we finhu fye shaba hakonesa winhi mwingi ukwangu; Mundewa komuliha ifene uwihi wakwe fowuwile.
55004015	Kinege naye, kosoko hakasilema lugano simbuli setu.
55004016	Munyinenela yangu ya bosi hechaka hata munhu yumwedu iyemile ulwandi lwangu; wose hawandeka niye. Nikutasa wanghawaliligwe itoso kwasoko yiyo!
55004017	Amba iMundewa hakema ulwandi lwangu na kunyingha ludole lwa kuitamilisa imbuli yose, uleke awamataifa nawo waihulike. Nani hanihuligwa mumulomo we simba.
55004018	iMundewa konihonya kulawa mu wihi wowose na kunhasa niufikile undewa wakwe wa kulanga. Ditunyo dyuwe ne mwene majuwa gose.
55004019	Walamuse cha Pilisika na Akila, hamwedu no ulukolo lwa Onesifolo.
55004020	Elasito yasigala Kolinto; Tulofimo hanimuleka mutamu ku Mileto.
55004021	Usunguse kwija ichigele che imheho chinati chikonge. Eubulo, Pude, Lino na Kilawudiya wose wakukulamusa.
55004022	iMundewa yowe hamwedu ne chidoga chako. Imboto yuwe nanye.
56001001	Paulo, mutogomi we Mulungu kahi mutumigwa wa Yesu Kilisito, kugendelesa dihuwi dya wasagulwe ne Mulungu no umanyi wawo we ichawelu iikufumila imikalile ye chimulungu,
56001002	mwihuwi dyo uwumi wa majuwa gose, uwene Mulungu, inghekudaha kudanha, hakaulaganisa minyaka mingi ilokile,
56001003	kahi muchigele chakwe haugubuligwa mumbuli yakwe kwa njila ya mahubili gonyenghigwe kwe dilagiso dye Mulungu iMwihula wetu.
56001004	Kwa Tito, gomwanangu we chawelu mwihuwi dyochihangile: Dihewa ne digoya kulawa kwe Mulungu iBaba na Kilisito Yesu iMwihula wetu fyuwe nagwe.
56001005	Nochanghone nakulekile ku Kilete, uleke ugolose digoya agasigale, na kuwasagula wasehe mu chila ikaya ifene fonakulagise,
56001006	nghona hena munhu munjelu, mulume wa muke yumwedu, kahi awanagwe wena ihuwi kahi wasikusongeswa na mbuli yoyose yo uwihi hegu kuleka kuwa na chogoho.
56001007	Kosoko iasikofu, kagaluka munyamhala we Mulungu, yagila yowe munhu inghekusongeswa na mbuli yoyose; yanghowe munhu iyakiyona, yanghowe munyono, yanghowe mulewaji wo ugimbi hegu mulefi hegu iyekilundila finhu itewa kosoko yakwe,
56001008	ninga yowe mundewa, iyekwenda uswanu, iyekiimila imwenyecho;
56001009	yekuhanangigwa yakolelese imbuli ye chawelu foifusigwe, uleke yadahe kulafa mafuso ge ichawelu, kahi kuwajama wose awekugalema.
56001010	Kosoko kwina wanhu wengi awechaka chogoho, wena mbuli sichaka chinhu, kahi wadasi, lugano awo ulwandi lwa wafinigwe;
56001011	wekuhanangigwa wanyamasigwe, kosoko wekuwabana awanhu we sikaya sose kwa mafuso gawo uleke wapate chinhu, amafuso gowasikwendigwa wafuse.
56001012	Yumwedu wawo, imugonese wawo yagamba “Awakilete wowaga wadasi majuwa gose malimu gehile, wadoba kahi wadiisaji”
56001013	Uhomelesi uno ni chawelu. Kosoko yo wagombele kwa ukali, uleke wadahe kuwa womi mwihuwi,
56001014	waleke kusitegelesa sisimo se Chiyahudi hegu amalagiso ga wanhu awekuilema ichawelu.
56001015	Ifinhu fyose fikugaluka fyela kuwanhu awelile, ninga kuwehi na awasikuhuwila hechaka chinhu chochose ichelile; amahala ne misungu yawo fibanika.
56001016	Wakigamba wamumanya Mulungu, ninga wakumulema kwa sinhenda sawo; wena ludeso, wechaka chihuliko, wasagile kwa nhenda yoyose iswanu.
56002001	Ninga gweye, fusa amafuso go uwumi.
56002002	Uwalagise awasehe wanghowe na makulu, ninga wowe wasindamafu, wowe na mahala, womi mwihuwi na muuwendo na mungojela.
56002003	Uwalagise kahi awadala wowe wasindamafu, wanghowe wasigilaji, hegu wonywaji wo ugimbi lugano; ninga awekufusa iswanu,
56002004	kahi na kuwafusa awanawake awadodogi wawende awalume sawo na wana,
56002005	wowe na chihuliko, usunhile, kutogoma milimo musinyumba sawo, waswamu, wowe na chihuliko kuwalume sawo, uleke imbuli ye mulungu inghatofuligwe.
56002006	Nheifo kahi, walolese awajelelo wakituse awecho.
56002007	Kiyonese gomwenyecho musimbuli sose chinhu cha kifusila sinhenda siswanu, kahi mumafuso gako yonesa uchawelu na usito,
56002008	na simbuli so uwumi isisidaha kutofuligwa uleke imunhu iyedaha kulema yengile chinyala, kwa kuswela mbuli ihile ya kulonga muchanhya yetu.
56002009	walagise awatumwa wowe na chogoho kuwakulu wawo, na kuwendesa musimbuli sose; wanghowe wabidulaji,
56002010	wanghowe wahiji, ninga wonese uchawelu wose, wagahambe amafuso fe Mwihula wetu Mulungu musimbuli sose.
56002011	Kosoko dihewa dya Mulungu digubuligwa uleke awanhu wose wehulwe,
56002012	nadyo dikuchifusa kuulema uwihi na usulumisi we chilunga, chidahe kwikala fiswanu, na mikalile yo kumogoha Mulungu muchilunga chino,
56002013	akuno nikudigojela dihuwidyetu idilugutisigwe, na magubulo ge ditunyo dye Mulungu wetu imukulu ne Mwihula Yesu Kilisito,
56002014	iyakilafa imwenyecho kosoko yetu kuchihula seye kulawa mu wihi wose na kisunhila imwenyecho wanhu wakwe awekupiligala musinhenda siswanu.
56002015	Longa simbuli sino; jama na kugombela kwa ludole. Munhu wowose yanghakubese.
56003001	Uwagelegese awanhu kinenenghesa kuwandewa na wena udaha, kuwa na chogoho, kuwa tayali kwa chila mulimo muswanu,
56003002	waleke kumulonga munu wowose, wakinege ne ing'omba, wowe waholo na konesa chogoho ku wanhu wose.
56003003	Kosoko ase nase katali hachuwaga chaka mahala, chichaka chogoho, chagiliswe, watumwa wo usulumisi wa mbuli nyingi, chikale mu wihi ne finju, chisuligwe na wanhu, nase chikisulile munhu na miyagwe;
56003004	ninga ichigele uswanu wakwe na uwendo wakwe Mulungu iMwihula wetu fowoneke,
56003005	hakachihonya seye, si kwa sinhenda setu, so uchawelu sochigolose, ninga kwa ubasi wakwe, kwa kusunhwa kwa kwelekigwa keli na kugoloswa usha ne Muhe Musunhile;
56003006	iyachitilile kwa ugoli wose kugendela Yesu Kilisito iMwihula wetu,
56003007	chidahe kutaliligwa ichawelu kwa dihewa dyakwe uleke chuwe wahasi mwihuwi dyo uwumi wa majuwa gose.
56003008	Ni nonga ya chawelu. Nikukuhananga gweye ulonge simbulisino kwa ludole uleke wose awamuhuwile Mulungu, wagendelele kusigala musinhenda siswanu; simbuli sino ni swanu kahi sina faida kuwanhu.
56003009	Ninga kinege ne sinonga se chibwalasi, sinonga sinhali sa wagono, ing'omba na iwanga kosoko ya malagiso, kosoko gechaka faida kahi gechaka chinhu.
56003010	Imunhu mudasi, yanghadaha kujamigwa ichigele cha bosi na cha keli, muleke,
56003011	umanye fina imunhu yefane yo kagilila kahi yakugolosa sambi; kafulusa kiliganisa imwenyecho.
56003012	Ichigele chonikanimutuma Alitema ukwako hegu Tikiko, piligala kwija ukwangu kuno Nikapoli, kosoko nilamula kwikala kuno ichigele che imheho.
56003013	Piligala kuwatasa Sena imulamusi na Apolo munhambo yawo; langisisa wanghahungukilwe na chinhu.
56003014	Leka awanhu wetu wefuse kusigala musinhenda siswanu, wadahe kuwatasa awechaka ichawelu, wanghaleke kulela mamudyo maswanu.
56003015	Awanhu wose awehamwedu nani wakukulamusa. Walamuse wose awekuchenda seye mwihuwi. Dihewa dyuwe hamwedu nanye mose.
57001001	Aniye Paulo, inyohigwe kosoko ya Kilisito Yesu, na Timoseyo imundugusetu. Chikukwandikila agweye Filemoni mwendigwa wetu, mwituma milimo miyetu,
57001002	na Afiya ilumbudyetu na Alikipo musilikali miyetu hamwedu ne dikanisa idikitang'anyila munyumba yako.
57001003	Dihewa dyuwe nanye, ne digoya idikulawa kwe Mulungu na kwe Mundewa Yesu Kilisito.
57001004	Nikumulumba lugano iMulungu wangu amajuwa gose, fonikuwagelegela munhasai yangu;
57001005	Ifene fonikuhulika isimbuli so uwendo wako, ne dihuwi dowinadyo mwe Mundewa Yesu na wasunhile wose.
57001006	Kahi nikutasa fina uumwedu wochinawo mwihui dyako dyongesele udaha wo kumanya maswanu gose muumi wetu mundugusangu mugati ya Kilisito.
57001007	Uwendo wako unyingha chinyemi lugano na kuhoswa! Kulawa muuwendo wako, fidoga fya wasunhile, fisangalaswa lugano kosoko yako.
57001008	Kosoko iyo nichaka chogoho mugati ya Yesu, kukulagisa ichikuhanangigwa ugolose,
57001009	ninga kosoko ya uwendo nikwenda kukutasa, (aniye Paulo nimusehe na hambiya mufungwa kosoko ya Kilisito Yesu).
57001010	Nikukutasa kosoko ye imwanangu Onesimo yonimweleke mwihuwi mugati ye inyohigwa yangu.
57001011	Iyowage katali munhu chaka ukwako mumilimo yakwe, amba hambiya kagaluka munhu munhusi ukwako na ukwangu.
57001012	Nikumuwisa ukwako kwa moyo wangu wose.
57001013	Hanyuwa nikwenda nisigale naye uleke yanhogomele ahanhu hako ugele nyuwile muchifungo kosoko ye mbuli swanu,
57001014	aniye sendile kugolosa mbuli yoyose yonghwendile agweye, kosoko yo uswamu wako unghowe fonghukwenda agweye, ninga foulamule gweye kwa kwenda kwako.
57001015	Nhagela nochileka yakulekile kwa chigele, uleke uwe naye kwa amajuwa gose,
57001016	hambiya, nghefane mutumwa du, amba imutumwa iyohigwe chawelu chawelusi mundugusangu mwendigwa ukwangu kosekose ukwako agweye chimutufi na kwe Mundewa.
57001017	Hambiya nghona ukunyona aniye chahamwedu nagwe, muhokele ayuno fina fowowile ukunihokela aniye.
57001018	Nghona yakugolosele mbuli yoyose ihile, kahi nghona ukumudai chilunhu chochose noliha niye.
57001019	Aniye Paulo nyandika, kwa mukono wangu nimwenyecho aniye noliha. (Sikulonga mbuli yoyose yonikukudai hata gweye gomwenyecho).
57001020	Heye mundugusangu nikuhananga nyongesa mwe Mundewa, kahi kusangalasa umoyo wangu mu Kilisito.
57001021	Kosoko mhuwila ichihuliko chako nochileka nikuwandikile nimanyile nhafi kogolosa kusuma agene gonilongile.
57001022	Ugele uwo munyikile ugono, kosoko nikuhuwila fina munhasa yenu modaha kunyona.
57001023	Epafula iyohigwe hamwedu naniye mu Kilisito Yesu, yekukulamusa;
57001024	hamwedu na Maluko, Alisitako, Dema, na Luka, awekugolosa imilimo hamwedi naniye.
57001025	Dihewa dye Mundewa Yesu Kilisito, dyuwe hamwedu ne ifidoga fyenu.
58001001	Katali iMulungu hakalonga na wababa setu kugendela wagonesi mikangha mingi na kwa njila se hayo hayo;
58001002	ninga majuwa gano kalonga nase kugendela iMwana, yoyamusagule yowe muhasi we finhu fyose, kahi kugendela imwene iMulungu kachumba ichilunga.
58001003	Imwene yakonesa ditunyo dye Mulungu kahi kena lubonoto lwe nyuwa yakwe, yakolelese ichilunga chose kwa ludole lwe mbuli yakwe. Foyagolose dihojojolo kosoko yo wihi, hakekala mumukono wo Ukulu uko kuchanhyasi,
58001004	Kagaluka mukulu muchanhya ya malaika kosoko disina dyoyapatile iswanu lugano kusuma agawo.
58001005	Kosoko kwina malaika yuhoki ugele wowose iyadaha kwinangigwa ne Mulungu, “Agweye kwa mwanangu, 2 diyelo nghweleka”? Ama kahi, “Aniye nokuwa Babakwe, 2 naye kokuwa ukwangu mwanangu.”
58001006	Na kahi, ugele foyekumwigala inhula hanju muchilunga, yekugamba, “Leka awamalaika we Mulungu wose wamufuge imwene.”
58001007	Na ku malaika yekugamba, “Iyekugolosa awamalaika wakwe wowe mheho, na watogomi wakwe malilimba ga moto.”
58001008	Ninga kwi mwana yekugamba, “Undewa wako, Go Mulungu, ni wa majuwa gose na ugele wose, nagwe ukudima digoya majuwa gose muundewa wako.
58001009	Agwe ukwenda ichawelu na kudesekela uwihi; 2 hambiya Mulungu, iMulungu wako kakubaka mafuta ga chinyemi kusuma awayago.”
58001010	Kahi, “Agweye, Mundewa nowejawomba iyisi kunghonga na ulanga ni mulimo we mikono yako;
58001011	nafyo fyobanika, ninga agweye kosigala; fyose fyodaha kulala kifana suke,
58001012	kofisinga kifana suke na fyo fyobiduka, nafyo fyobiduka. Ninga agweye kosigala fina fouwile, na iminyaka yako ichaka ndumo”
58001013	Ninga kwina malaika yuhoki yoyadaya kumugamba chigele chochose, “Ikala ulwandi lwo mukono wangu wo kulume, mpaka niweke awanghondo wako chigoda cha kwegamikila migulu”?
58001014	Nhafo awo si mimuhe watumigwe kutogoma, kosoko ya wanhu awakwija wahokela uhonya?
58002001	Hambiya chikuhanangigwa chikolelese lugano simbuli sose sochihulike, uleke chingheje chisiswela.
58002002	Kosoko inghowa imbuli iyalongigwe na malaika hayuwa ya chawelu na chila kubana hegu kuleka kuwa na chihuliko, hakuhokela maliho galiganile,
58002003	aseye nase chodaha kinega nhani chinghaulema uhonya uno umukulu? Haulongigwa kunghonga na Mundewa, na kuhomelelwa na wose ukwetu na wose awamuhulike imwende,
58002004	ugele iMulungu naye yakuwuhomelela kwa fitangilo na majumo na majumo gehayohayo na kwe chinghwa cho Muhe Musunhile ichikwinghigwa ifene imwenyecho foyekwenda.
58002005	Kosoko iMulungu nghachilekile ichilunga ichikwija chochikulionga chilongoswe na malaika.
58002006	Fina foihomeleligwe ahamonga, “Imunhu no nani hata umugelegele, hegu imwana we munhu, hata umulangilile imwene?
58002007	Kumugolosa mudodogi kusuma malaika kwa chipisi, kumufasa inghofiya ye ditunyo na chogoho,
58002008	kwika ifinhu fyose hasi ye migulu yakwe.” Hambiya munyika ifunhu fyose hasi yakwe, nghasigase chinhu isichuwile hasi yakwe. Fina foyuwile, chisinati chone chila chinhu chuwe hasi yakwe.
58002009	Ninga chikumona Yesu, imwene kwa chigele chiguhi hakagolosigwa mudodogi kusuma malaika yafasigwe ditunyo na chogoho kosoko ya magayo ge difa, uleke kwe dihewa dye Mulungu yadahe kunomola difa kosoko ya chila mumunhu.
58002010	Kosoko haimwagila imwene, imwenele na kugendela imwene ifinhu fyose fyabahano, munyigala wana itewa ku ditunyo, yamugolose chilongosi wo uwumi wao yaliganile kugendela magayo.
58002011	Kosoko iyakuhojojola na wose awakuhojojoligwa wena chotoko chimwedu. Nochanghone wena iYesu ighakona chinyala kuwenanga awene wanduguse
58002012	yakugamba “Notagusa disina dyako kuwandugu sangu muchiligati ye dikanisa nomutunya imwene.”
58002013	Na kahi, “Nomuhuwila imwene.” Na kahi, “Aniye nabahano na wana woninghigwe ne Mulungu.”
58002014	Hambiya kosoko wana wahangila mumutufi ne sakame, Yesu naye yowa nheifo uleke jugendela difa yadahe kumubana imwene yene udaha we difa, naye no luhoma,
58002015	na kuwehula awo wose woile mwibalangulu dya wose watumwa kosoko ye ditisi dye difa.
58002016	Kosoko ni chawelu fina Yesu nghejile kuwatasa malaika ninga icheleko cha Ibulahimu.
58002017	Hambiya haimwagila kuligana na wanduguse musimbuli sose uleke yadahe kuwa mutambiki mukulu yena ubasi akahi muchawelu mufuga ye Mulungu, yadahe kuwa iliho kwa wihi wa wanhu.
58002018	Kosoko imwene naye yahokela magayo na kugesigwa, kena udaha wa kuwatasa wose awekugesigwa.
58003001	Hambiya wandugu sangu wasunhile mukuhangila mulwinango lwa kulanga mugelegeleni Yesu imutumigwa na mutambi mukulu wo kulamba kwetu.
58003002	Yeja yowa muchawelu kwe Mulungu yamusagule imwene kifana Musa foyowile muchawelu munyumba ye Mulungu.
58003003	Kahi Yesu yataliligwa muchawelu iyena ditunyo lugano kusuma Musa ifene imujengaji we inyumba foyena ditunyo lugano kusuma inyumba iyecho.
58003004	( Kosoko chila nyumba ijengigwa na munhu yumonga, ninga imujengaji we finhu fyose ni Mulungu.)
58003005	Hambiya Imusa yeja yowa muchawelu munyumba yose ye Mulungu yefane mutogomi yowe muhomelesi we simbuli isikasilongigwa ichigele chikwija.
58003006	Ninga iKilisito yeja yowa muchawelu muchahya ye nyumba ye Mulungu kifana mwana, kahi aseye no sinyumba sakwe chinghakolelesa lugano ighinyo yetu na inyitogolela dihuwi dyetu
58003007	Hambiya fina Imuhe Musunhile foyakulonga, “Diyelo, munghahulika dijwi dyakwe,
58003008	munghaigolose imimoyo yenu yuwe mikugutu fina ichigele che ufuti fina dijuwa dyo kugesigwa kunyika,
58003009	ako konagesigwe na wababa senu na kona imilimo yangu,
58003010	kwa minyaka makumi mane. hambiya hanidesigwa ne cheleko chiya, na kugamba, ‘Majuwa gose ni wanhu wagilile mumimoyo yawo, wasisimanyile sinjila sangu.’
58003011	Fina fonikilahile munyono yangu, ‘Wasidaha kwingila muubwihilo wangu.’”
58003012	Wandugu sangu langisiseni, nghanghowe na yumwedu wenu imwihi yena umoyo uwichaka dihuwi uukulongosa kugwila kutali ne Mulungu imumi.
58003013	Ninga mukilolese munhu na miyagwe chila ijuwa, inangwa, “Diyelo,” uleke nghanghowe na yumwedu wenu yowe mukugutu kosoko ya kudanhiliswa na wihi.
58003014	Kosoko chihangila muKilisito chinghagendelesa kukolelela inghinyo yetu ye nghonga mpaka kundumo.
58003015	Kosoko hailongigwa, “Diyelo munghahulika dijwi dyakwe munghaigolose mimoyo yenu yuwe mikugutu kifana chigele cho ufuti.”
58003016	No chenani wahulike na kugendelela kuwa wafuti? Nhafo siwowile awaya wose awaleuke Misili ugele wo ulongosi wa Musa?
58003017	Kahi no chenani awamudesile kwa minyaka makumi mane? Siwaya wose awagolose wihi, awene mitufi yawo hayugwa mwibalangu?
58003018	Kahi no chenani welahile fina wanghengile mubwihilo wakwe ninga si waya awowile wafuti?
58003019	Hambiya chikona fina wasadahile kwingila kosoko ya kuleka kuhuwila kwawo.
58004001	Hambiya kosoko dihuwilo dyo kwingila muchinyemi chakwe dinghali baho, chogohe uleke yanghowe yumwedu wenu yaliganiswe kosoko ya kusuma kudifikila.
58004002	Kosoko imbuli iswanu haija ukwetu fina ukwawo, ninga imbuli yahubiliigwe ukwawo iswatasile, kosoko isahangile ne dihuwi dya wategelesage.
58004003	Kosoko aseye chihuwile chikwingila muubwihilo wakwe, kifana Mulungu foyalongile “Fina fonakilahile munyono yangu, Wasidaha kwingila mubwihilo wangu,” hata inghowa imilimo yakwe haihela ugele wo kwikigwa inghindiso ye chilunga.
58004004	Kosoko ahamonga kalonga simbuli se dijuwa dye mufungate, “Ne Mulungu hakabwihila dijuwa dyo mufungate kulawa kugolosa milimo yakwe yose.”
58004005	Na kahi ahanhu hano hakagamba, “Wasidaha kwingila mubwihilo wangu.”
58004006	Kosoko hambiya isigala kuwamonga kwingila umo, na wose awene kunghonga, hawahokela imbuli swanu ninga hawasumwa kwingila kosoko ya ufuti wawo,
58004007	kahi keka ijuwa dimonga, “diyelo” yakugamba kulokela Daudi minyaka mingi ilokile, musimbuli isamule kuwandikigwa, “Diyelo munghahulika dijwi dyakwe, munghaigolose imimoyo yenu yuwe mikugutu.”
58004008	Kosoko inghowa Yoshua hakamwinghani hanhu ha kubwihila iMulungu nghodaha kutambula hamwande dijuwa dingi.
58004009	Hambiya kahi ahaya isigala sabato dijuwa dyo kubwihila kwe Mwana we Mulungu!
58004010	Kosoko wowose iyakwingila muubwihilo we Mulungu yakubwihila munhogoma milimo yakwe fina Mulungu foyabwihile munhogoma yakwe.
58004011	Lekeni hambiya chipiligale chingile kuubwihilo uya, uleke hanghowe na yumwedu wetu yogwe kosoko yo ufuti uno.
58004012	Kosoko imbuli ye Mulungu nyumi, kahi ikutogoma milimo, nghali kusuma isunja, kahi ikuhoma mpaka ikutemanhula chidoga ne umuhe ne ifilungo fya umutufi ne umusopo, kumanya amadoga ne inyenda ye umoyo.
58004013	Kahi hamwande yakwe hechaka ichumbigwe chikifisile ninga fyoose fyahajelu na kugubuligwa mumeso gagwe imwene yena simbuli setu.
58004014	Kosoko hambiya china Imutambiki Mukulu iyengile kulanga, Yesu Imwana we Mulungu, chigendelele kukolelesa dihuwilo dyetu.
58004015	Kosoko chichaka Mutambiki Mukulu iyekuhanga nase musokesi wetu, ninga imwene naye hakahesigwa musinyuwa sose fina seye bila kugolosa wihi.
58004016	Chisegelele kwa nghinyo hegoda dye undewa dye dihewa, uleke chidahe kuhokela ubasi na dihewa dyo kuchitasa ugele wo chikuhananga.
58005001	Kosoko chila Mutambiki Mukulu yasaguligwe kulawa muwanhu, kekigwa yeme ahanhu ha wanhu yawatogomele musimbuli se Mulungu, kulafa filafwa na sinhambiko kosoko yo wihi.
58005002	Yekudaha kuwalondela kwa uholo awasimanyile na wokwagilila, kosoko imwene naye kowa musokesi.
58005003	Kosoko ino imwagila naye yalafe nhambiko kosoko yo wihi wakwe na wihi wa wanhu wamonga.
58005004	Na hechaka munhu yekiingha ditunyo dyo Utambiki Mukulu ninga ayuya iyenangigwe ne Mulungu, fina foyowile Haluni.
58005005	No nheifo kahi iKilisito naye nghakiinule imwenyecho kuwa Mutambiki Mukulu, ninga hakasaguligwa ne Mulungu yagambile, “Agwe no Mwanangu, diyelo nikweleka,”
58005006	fina foyakulonga ahanhu hamonga, “Agweye no mutambiki wa majuwa gose, anhanhu ho utambiki ha Melikisedeki.”
58005007	Mumajuwa gakwe goyekalage muchilunga, Yesu hakatasaga lugano na kutasilisa, kwa ijwi ikulu na masosi kwe Mulungu yena udaha wo kumuhonya kulawa mudifa, na hakahulikigwa kosoko ye chogoho che Mulungu ichowile umwakwe.
58005008	Hamwedu na gago hakowa Mwana, iyakifusile kuhulika kugendela amagayo goyapatile
58005009	naye foyakangasigwe hakagaluka chotoko cha uhonya wa majuwa gose kuwose awekumuhulika,
58005010	kahi imwene kasaguligwa ne Mulungu kuwa mutambiki mukulu ahanhu ha Melikisedeki.
58005011	Muchanhya yakwe china mbuli nyingi sa kulonga, ninga nghugutu kusilonga, kosoko anyeye hamukwenda kuhulika.
58005012	Kosoko hamwedu na gago muwagila muwe wafusaji mukuhananga munhu yun gi yawafuseni amafuso ge inghonga ge Mulungu. Mukuhananga mele siyo chakudiya chikugutu;
58005013	Kosoko chila munhu iyakwikala kwa ndiya ya mele nghamanyile imbuli ye chawelu, kosoko ni mwana na.
58005014	Ninga chakudiya chigugutu ni cha wakulu wagima, kosoko wose awene imisungu wakudaha kusagula diswanu na dihile.
58006001	Hambiya chileke amafuso ge nghonga agechikilisito na chandamile agakangale, chingheke nhindiso kahi: Kwa kulamba kulawa mumilimo yufile ninga chike dihuwi kwe Mulungu,
58006002	malagiso ge mbuli sa ubatiso na kwikiligwa mikono na kwinuka wafile na uliganiso wa majuwa gose.
58006003	Agano chogolosa Mulungu yenghenda.
58006004	Kosoko isikudahika kulamba kahi kwa wanhu awalekile dihuwi wowile muujelu na kunomola ichinghwa che Mulugu na kuwa na lugota na Muhe Musunhile,
58006005	na kufulusa kunomola uswanu we mbuli ye Mulungu na uludole we chigele chikwija,
58006006	na kuleka dihuwi isikudahika kuwowisa walambe kahi, kosoko wakumusambasa Imwana we Mulungu keli mufidoga fyawo na kumutofula kwa hajelu.
58006007	Kosoko isanga inyunyile ifula, itonyelwa chila ugele na kotesa mamudyo maswanu kwa yuya yakulima na kuhokela simboto kulawa kwe Mulungu.
58006008	Ninga inghotesa miwa na magugu, yokuwa chaka chambusi na kuwa habehi na kuhugutiswa; na kusomigwa kumoto.
58006009	Hata inghowa chikulonga nheifo, wendigwa wangu musimbuli senu chihuwila simbuli siswanu lugano so uhonya.
58006010	Kosoko Mulungu siyo mukugutu hata yaleke kona imilimo yenu na wendo womonese kosoko ye disina dyakwe, kuwatogomela awasunhile fina fomukugolosa hata hambiya.
58006011	Chikuhananga chila yumwedu wenu yonese upiligale uwo kwa kumanya umemelesi we dihuwi mpaka kundumiliso,
58006012	uleke munghowe wadoba, ninga awekuwandamila wose awena kulokela dihuwi na ufinyilisi wakuhala isilaganiswe.
58006013	Kosoko ichigele iMulungu foyamulaganise Ibulahimu, na kosoko nghowile hata na munhu yumwedu mukulu wa kilahila, hakelahila muimwecho,
58006014	yekugamba, “Chawelu nokumotesa gweye na kukongesa.”
58006015	Kamei Ibulahimu yakamale kufinyilisa, hakahokela choyalaganiswe.
58006016	Kosoko awanhu wakilaha kwa yuya imukulu kusuma awene, na nyilaha ukwawo no kumala simbuli sose.
58006017	No nheifo, Mulungu naye yakwenda konesa lugano awahasi we dihuwilo ifene amadoga gakwe fogechaka chibidubidu hakongesa mudihuwiso kilaha,
58006018	uleke kwa finhu fili ifisikudaha kubiduka mufifyo Mulungu nghodaha kulonga udasi, uleke aseye chibilimile chuwe na ludole lukangale kudikola dihuwi dikigwe hamwande yetu.
58006019	Chinadyo dihuwi dino, dye chawelu na dimile nghwi kifana chigingi che fidoga, ne dihuwi idikwingila mugati ye dipasiya,
58006020	Umo nomoyengile Yesu kosoko yetu, imwene noyachilongolele hakagaluka mutambiki mukulu wa majuwa gose kifana Melikisedeki.
58007001	Kosoko ayuno, “No Melikisedeki Mundewa wa Salemu, imutambiki we, Mulungu Iyekuchanhyasi, hakakitanyila na Ibulahimu foyendeyakuya kulawa kuwatowa wandewa na kumotesa,”
58007002	na kwe imwene yuyo Ibulahimu hakalafa, “Imwedu ye ikumi ya chila chinhu choyowile nacho,” itapita ye Disina dyakwe bosi ni, “Mundewa we chawelu,” keli ni mundewa wa Salemu, “Imwene ni mundewa we digoya.”
58007003	Munhu yo kechaka baba, ninga ng'ina, kechaka welekwa, hegu nghonga ama ndumo mulwikala lwakwe, ninga kaliganisigwa ne Mwana we Mulungu, imwene ni kuhani mwajuwa gose.
58007004	Langeni fonimukulu! Ibulahimu baba yetu hakamwingha imwedu ya kumi ye ifinhu ifilawile kunghonga.
58007005	Na wose awecheleko cha Lawi awakuhokela umulimo wo utambiki wene lusigililo mwilagiso fina walonde imwedu ya kumi kulawa kuwanhu wawo, kosoko nawo ni welekwa wa Ibulahimu.
58007006	Ninga munhu yuno siyo wa lukolo lwawo, hakahokela imwedu ya kumi kwa Ibulahimu na kumumotesa imwene yene dihuwiso.
58007007	Kahi imanyika fina imudodogi yakumotesigwa ne mukulu.
58007008	Na hata wanhu ambawo wakudaha kufa wakuhokela imwedu ya ikumi, ninga kwa Melikisedeki imwdu ya kumi haihokeligwa na kuhomeleligwa ne imwene imumi inghakudaha kufa.
58007009	Munhu yakudaha kugamba fina, Lawi imwenyecho, iyakuhokela imwedu ya kumi, hakaliha kugendela Ibulahimu,
58007010	kosoko hakowa mufyuno fye Babakwe ugele Melikisedeki foyakitang'anyile naye.
58007011	Hambiya inghowa ukangasi haupatagwa kwa njila ya utambiki we Chilawi, (kosoko hasi yakwe awanhu hawahokela malagiso), hahowa na soko yaki kahi ya mutambiki yungi yeme ahanhu ha Melikisedeki, kusuma hata yumwedu iyatambuligwe ahanhu ha Haluni?
58007012	Kosoko halika utambiki ukudaha kubiduka, yagila amalagiso nago gabiduke.
58007013	Kosoko umwene yalongigwe mugago hakowa muhangi wo ulukolo lwingi, ulwene hechaka hata yumwedu mulukolo lwalwo iyetuma mulimo wo utambiki hefugilo.
58007014	Kosoko imanyika chalinje fina iMundewa wetu yalawa mucheleko cha Yuda, mulukolo ulwene Musa nghalonga mbuli yoyose muchanhya yakwe musimbuli sa watambiki.
58007015	Adino digaluka dya chalinje lugano, ichigele mutambiki yungi yakwima kefana Melikisedeki,
58007016	iyagaluke mutambiki siyo kwa kwandamila inyenda ya malagiso ge chimutufi, ninga kwa ludole lwa uumi uusikubanika.
58007017	Kwasoko kahomelelwa fina “Agweye kwa mutambiki wa majuwa gose, ahanhu ha Melikisedeki.”
58007018	Kwa ulwandi lumonga dilagiso idilongole dikigwa hanghanda kosoko yo usokesi wakwe na kuleka kuwa na chakutogomelwa.
58007019	(Kosoko dilagiso sidyamemelese chochose); kwa ulwandi lumonga, dihuwilo diswanu hadinghiswa, uleke mugago chidahe kumusegelela Mulungu.
58007020	Kahi sidyowile nheifo bila ya kilaha.
58007021	Wose kunghonga awowile watambiki hawalonda mulimo uwo bila ya kilaha, ninga ayuno kenghigwa kwa kilaha, “Imundewa kakilaha kahi nghodaha kubidula chidoga chakwe, ‘Agweye no mutambiki wa majuwa gose.’”
58007022	kwa nheifo Yesu kagaluka mwimilisi we dilagano diswanu.
58007023	Lugano, awatambiki we nghonga hawowa wengi, kosoko hawakindisigwa ne difa wanghagendelele mumulimo;
58007024	ninga imwene kenawo utambiki wakwe uwichaka ndumo, kosoko ukugendelela majuwa gose.
58007025	Nochanghone ugele wose kena udaha wa kuwahonya wose awakumusegelela Mulungu kwa kulokela imwene, kosoko muchigele chakwe chose choyakwikala yakuwatasila.
58007026	Kosoko hayagila chuwe na mutambiki mukulu kifana yuyo, imusunhile yechaka ilema dyodyose, inghachafuke, iyakinega na uwihi, na yenuligwe kulanga.
58007027	hafanile, kifana awatambiki wamonga wakulu; kechaka haja kulafa nhambiko chila ijuwa, kunghonga kosoko yo wihi wakwe imwenyecho, keli kahi na kosoko yo uwihi wa wanhu wose; aga hakagagolosa malumwedu du kwa wanhu wose ichigele foyakilafile imweneyecho.
58007028	Kosoko dilagiso dikuweka wanhu wose awechaka ludole kuwa watambiki wakulu, ninga inonga ye nyilaha, iyejile kunyuma ye dilagiso haimusagula Mwana iyamemelekele majuwa gose.
58008001	Hambiya imbuli inghulu musose sochikulonga no ino: China mutambiki mukulu iyefane yuyo yekale mumukono wo kulume we digoda dye Undewa Mukulu ako kulanga,
58008002	imutogomi ahanhu hasunhile he dihema dye chawelu, idyekigwe siyo ne munhu, ninga Mundewa.
58008003	Kosoko chila mutambiki mukulu kasaguligwa uleke yalafe filafwa na nhambiko; kosoko ikuhanangigwa imutambiki naye yowe na chinhu cha kulafa.
58008004	Hambiya kusigwa yowile wamuchilunga nghowile yakuwa mutambiki hata chidodogi, kosoko hena watambiki awakulafa filafwa ifene dilagiso fodikulagisa.
58008005	Wakutogoma mulimo hanhu ha sunhile kifana futa na inyefu dya finhu fya kulanga; kifana Musa foyowile habehi kugolosa dihema, hakajamigwa kugambigwa, “Langa ukagolose finhu fyose kifana fowonesigwe akuya kwitunda.”
58008006	Ninga Yesu kapata mulimo muswanu lugano, na muchanhya ya iyo, imwene kakifana mulamusi we dilagano diswanu, kosoko dija kulokela mahuwiso maswanu.
58008007	Kosoko woile diya dye nghonga dyowile hadihunguke, kusowile kukuwa na soko ya kukongha dingi dya keli.
58008008	Mulungu hakona wihi kuwamonga nochinghone yakugamba, “Chawelu majuwa gakwija, yakulonga Mundewa, chigele chonikwija nikwiga ilagano isha ne nyumba ya Isilaeli na hamwedu na nyumba ya Yuda;
58008009	hadikuwa kifana dilagano diya dyonekile ne wababa sawo, mwijuwa dyonawalafage kwa mukono na kuwalongosa kuluta iisi ya Misili; kosoko hawagendelele mwilagano dyangu, na kwa nheifo naniye haniwadesekela, yakulonga Mundewa.
58008010	Adino no dilagano dyonikwenda nigolose hamwedu ne nyumba ye Isilaeli ganghaloka majuwa gago, yakulonga Mundewa, nikwenda nike malagiso gangu mumisungu yawo, na nowandika mumimoyo yawo, nani nokuwa Mulungu wawo, nawo wokuwa wanhu wangu.
58008011	Na wasikuwa wanhu wa kifusa munhu na miyagwe ama kwa kigamba, ‘Goloko mumanye Mulungu,’ kosoko wose wonimanya, kulawa mudodogi hata imukulu.
58008012	Kosoko nowonela ubasi kwa nhenda sawo sihile, na sikwijanigelegela wihi kahi.”
58008013	Munonga ye dilagano, lagano isha, nong'amba Mulungu kagolosa dye nghonga dyuwe disakala na ichinhu chisakale chahabehi na kwagilila.
58009001	Hambiya hata dilagano dye inghonga hadyuwa na nhenda sa kufuga na ahasunhile hakwe he chilunga.
58009002	Kosoko dihema hadigoloswa, idyakunje, idyekigwe chigwaso che itaa na imesa na imikate yo Konesa; hekwinangigwa Hanhu Hasunhile.
58009003	Kunyuma ye dipasiya dya keli hadima dihema dikwinangigwa Ahasunhile ha Hahasunhile,
58009004	dina chiya cho kufunghisila ubani chigoloswe kwa sahabu na disanduku dye dilagano digubikwe musisandi sose kwa shaba, umowile na dikopo dya sahabu idyowile na imana iya na imhando ya Haluni iyatugute ne fibawo fiya fye dilagano;
58009005	muchanhya ya disanduku hamuwa na makelubi ge ditunyo gakuguma inyefu mwigoda dyo ubasi. Ninga musimbuli sino chichaka luneka lwa kulonga kwa utali.
58009006	Ifinhu afyo finghafulusa kugoloswa, awatambiki wakugendelela kwingila mwihema didyo dye inghonga kutogoma imilimo yo kufuga;
58009007	ninga mwihema didyo dya keli dikwingiligwa ne mutambiki mukulu muhala, mukangha umwedu chila mwaka; kahi si bila sakame, yoyekuhanangigwa yalafe kosoko yakwe na kosoko ye sisambi sa kuleka kumanya sa wanhu awo.
58009008	Mu dino iMuhe Musunhile yakonesa fina injila yo kwingila ahanhu hasunhile hayuwa inhati ikumuligwe, kosoko dihema dya kunje hadyuwa dikali dimile
58009009	(idyowile chitangilo che chigele chino). Mugoloswa nheifi; filafwa ne sinhambiko ifisikudaha kumugolosa imunhu, iyekufuga yowe na misungu ikangale,
58009010	kosoko fikutogomela muhala ifyakudiya ne ifinhu fyo kungwa na uhojojolo we hayo hayo na malagiso ge chimutufi agekigwe mpaka ichigele chino.
58009011	Ninga ichigele Kilisito foyejile imutambiki mukulu we finhu fiswanu ifijile, kahi kugendela dihema dikulu, kahi idikangale lugano (idisigolosigwe kwe mikono, no ngamba, si dye cheleko chino)
58009012	hakengila kamwedu kosoko ya wose Ahanhu Hasunhile, yalondile isakame siyo yesimhene na sindama, ninga isakame yakwe imwenyecho na kuwa ne indekelela ya majuwa gose.
58009013	Kosoko inghowa isakame ye simhene na makambaku na difu dye sindama se singombe dyowetililigwe awanhu awena uwihi dikusunha na kukwema umutufi,
58009014	silugano isakame ya Kilisito, imwene kugendela iMuhe wa majuwa gose hakelafa imwenyecho kuwa chilafwa chichaka wihi, kuwasunha amadoga genu na sinhenda senu sufile mudahe kumufuga Mulungu wenu imumi.
58009015	Kosoko ino Kilisito noyekugolosa dilagano disha uleke wose awenangwe wadahe kuhokela uhasi uwuhuwisigwe wa majawa, kosoko ye difa digoloseke kuwaleusila uwihi wawo awowile hasi ye dilagano dhe nghonga.
58009016	Kosoko yagila ahena dilagano dyo uhasi, howe na ifa dya imunhu iyadigolose.
58009017	Kosoko dilagano dyo uhasi dina ludole ichigele imunhu foyekufa, amba foyekuwa yekali mumi dikuwa chaka ludole.
58009018	Ninga hata dilagano diya dya katali sidyakongesigwe bila ya sakame.
58009019	Kosoko chila ilagiso fodyalongigwe na Musa kuwanhu wose ifene foilongigwe mumalagiso, hakailonda isakame ya sindama na yesimhene na kuhanganisa mumeji na kuinyaga muchitabu cha malagiso na awanhu kwa sufi na kwa mahamba ge dibiki dikwinangigwa hisopo,
58009020	yekugamba, Ayino no sakame ye dilagano dye Mulungu dyoyamulagiseni.
58009021	Kahi nheifiya hakainyaka isakame yakwe mu fyose dihema na ifiya fyo kufugila.
58009022	Chawelu, hasi ya malagiso chila chinhu chikusunhigwa kwa sakame, na bila ya sakame kwachaka kulekeleligwa kwa wihi.
58009023	Ninga hayagila simbuli sose isasigale kulanga sisunhwe kwa kwandamila sinhenda sino, ninga simbuli isenyecho sa kulanga sisunhigwa kwa nhambiko siswanu kusuma sino.
58009024	Kosoko Kilisito nghengile ahanhu hasunhile ahagolosigwe ne mikono hefane chawelu ninga kulanga ukwenyecho, hambiya koneka hamwedu ne Mulungu kosoko yetu.
58009025	Kahi siyo yelafe kwa kuwila kuwila, imutambiki mukulu foyekwingilaga Ahanhu Hasunhile, chila mwaka kwe sakame siyo iyakwe;
58009026	Kusigwa no nheifo, hayuwa ikumwagila kusambasigwa mikangha mingi kulawa kwikigwa kwe isinghindisi se chilunga. Ama hambiya kamwedu du kwa umemelesi we figele, kagubuligwa, yauleuse uwihi wa wanhu kwe nhambiko yakwe imwenyecho.
58009027	Kahi kefana awanhu fowekiligwe kufa mukangha umwedu na fowekufa uliganiso,
58009028	no nheifo, Kilisito naye yakafuluse kulafigwa kamwedu kulonda uwihi wa wengi, kokwija mukangha wa keli, siyo kutogomela uwihi ninga kuwahonya wose awena inghilu ya kumugojela.
58010001	Kosoko dilagiso dina ninga inyefu dye finhu fiswanu ifikwija kahi si futa ye finhju ifyenyecho, isidaha kuwa, kwa sinhambiko senheifo isikugendelela kulafigwa munyaka kwa munyaka, kuwagolosa wamemelekele wose awekusegelela habehi.
58010002	Kusigwe si nheifo, sisowile sikulekigwa kulafigwa? Kusigwa awekufuga hawasunhwa kamwedu, wasowile wakugendelela kuwana madoga go wihi.
58010003	Ninga musinhambiko sino mwina ngelegelsi yo wihi munyaka kwa munyaka.
58010004	Kosoko isikudahika isakame ya makambaku ne simhene ilewuse uwihi.
58010005	Kosoko iyo ichigele iKilisito foyejile muchilunga, hakagamba, “Sinhambiko ne filafwa nghafyendile, ninga umutufi utandiligwa niye;
58010006	mufilafwa fyo kusoma mumoto na sinhambiko so wihi nghendesigwe naso.
58010007	kamei hakagamba, ‘Langa, nija kugolosa, sinyenda se Mulungu,’ ifene fosandikiligwe niye muchitabu cha dilagiso.”
58010008	Foyagambile hachanhya, “Nghasendile hegu konela sinhambiko ne ifilafwa na sinhambiko so kusoma mumoto na sinhambiko so uwihi” (asino sikulafigwa ifene dilagisoa fodikulonga),
58010009	kamei hakongesa “Langa, nija kugolosa sinyenda sako.”Yakulewusa isenghonga uleke yakongese isakeli.
58010010	na kwa nyenda iyo chisunhigwa kugendela ichilafwa cho umutufi wa Yesu Kilisito kamwedu kosoko ya wose.
58010011	Na chila mutambiki yakwina chila ijuwa mufuga yakwe, yakulafa kwa kuwila kuwila inhambiko ifane iyo, iyisidaha kulewusa uwihi.
58010012	Ninga ichigele Kilisito foyalafile nhambiko imwedu kosoko yo uwihi ye figele fyose, hakekala mumukono wo kulume we Mulungu,
58010013	kamei kugojela mpaka yaweke awanghondo wakwe chigoda cho kwegamikila imigulu yakwe.
58010014	Kosoko kwa nhambiko imwedu hakawagolosa wasunhile we figele fyose wamemelekele.
58010015	Kahi Muhe Musunhile yakuhomelela ukwetu; kwa kugamba,
58010016	Adino no dilagano dyonikanigolosa nawo ganghaloka majuwa gose, iMundewa yakugamba: Noguma amalagiso gangu mumimoyo yawo na kuwandika mumisungu yawo,
58010017	kamei yakongesa, “Sikanigelegela uwihi wawo na sinhenda sawo kahi.”
58010018	Ahena indekelelwa ya gano, hechaka kulafa chilafwa kosoko yo wihi.
58010019	Hambiya, wandugusangu, kosoko china nginyo yo kwingila ahasunhile kwa isakame ya Yesu,
58010020	kwa usha na injila inyumi yoyagubule kosoko yetu kugendela dipasiya, idyene, kugendela umutufi wakwe,
58010021	na kosoko china mutambiki mukulu muchanhya ye nyumba ye Mulungu,
58010022	chisegelele habehi na mimoho ye chawelu mwihuwiso dimemelekele dye dihuwi, china mimoyo inyunyisiligwe na kusunhwa kulawa mu madoga go wihi na imitufi yetu haisunhigwa kwa meji amaswanu.
58010023	Chikolelese ngwingwingwi kulamba kwe dihuwi dyetu bila ya kuleka, kosoko iyalaganise ni muchawelu;
58010024	na chikilangilile aseye kwa seye na kiguma moyo mu wendo no mulimo muswamu;
58010025	kahi chinghaleke kutanganyila hamwedu, ifene awamonga fowasowele, ninga kiguma moyo munhu na miyagwe, na gose lugano ifene fomukona Dijuwa disegela habehi.
58010026	Kosoko chinghagolosa wihi chigilagila chifuluse kuhokela umanyi we chawelu, hachaka nhambiko kahi yo wihi,
58010027	ninga kwina uliganiso wo kogohesa na ukali wo moto uwufuluse kwikiga kosoko ya wose awekulema.
58010028	Imunhu iyabanile dilagiso dya Musa yakufa bila ya ubasi kwa uhomelesi wa wanhu weli hegu wadatu.
58010029	Si uliganiso wilihile lugano wo mukudoga uwumwagile imunhu iyamubesile imwana we Mulungu, na kuitofula isakame ye dilagano iyamusunhile, na kumutofula Muhe we dihewa?
58010030	Kosoko chimumanya imwene iyagambile, Kuwisila ni kwangu, no kuwisila. Na kahi, iMundewa kowaliganisa awanhu wakwe.
58010031	Ni chinhu cha kogohesa kugwila mumikono ye Mulungu imumi.
58010032	Ninga gelegeleni amajuwa ga katali, fyomwamulikiligwe, hamufinyilisa inyisuma inghulu na magayo,
58010033	ichigele chimonga hamutofuligwa hajelu namagayo na ichigele chimonga chomwahasigwe na waya awagoloseligwe gago.
58010034	Kosoko hamuwonela ubasi awohigwe, kahi hamubwedelela kuhokigwa simali senu, mumanyile mufidoga fyenu fina mwina mali iswanu lugano kahi iyikwikala majuwa gose.
58010035	Hambiya munghatage inginyo yenu, iyina iliho ikulu.
58010036	Kosoko mukuhanangigwa mufinyilise, uleke mugolose inyenda ye Mulungu na kuhokela chomulaganisigwe.
58010037	Kosoko chisigala chipisi chidodogi lugano, imwene iyakwija yakwija kahi ngakusululuka;
58010038	ninga imuchawelu wangu kokwikala kwa ihuwi, kahi yanghoya kunyuma ichidoga changu sichikwendesigwa ne imwene.
58010039	Ninga sichifane awo awakuya kunyuma na kubanigwa, ninga wa wose awena dihuwi na kuhonya ifidoga fyawo.
58011001	Hambiya dihuwi ni kuwa na chawelu ye finhu ifikuhuwiligwa, ni inyuwa na dihuwi dya simbuli isisikoneka.
58011002	kosoko kwa didyo awanhu wa katali hawafumiligwa ne Mulungu.
58011003	Kwa dihuwi chimanya fina ichilunga hachumbigwa kwa mbuli ye Mulungu uleke hata ifinhu fikoneka hafigolosigwa kulawa mufinhu ifisikoneka.
58011004	Kwa dihuwi Habili hakamulafila Mulungu nhambiko iswanu lugano kusuma Kaini, iyamugolose yataliligwe uchawelu, iMulungu yakuhomelela kwa kufumila ifilafwa fyakwe; hakafa, ninga kugendela dihuwi dyakwe yenghali longa.
58011005	Kwa dihuwi Henoko yenuligwa kuchanhya uleke yanghone difa; na nghoneke, kosoka Mulungu hakamulonda. Hambiye ugele woyowile yenhati yalondigwe hakahomelelwa fina hakamwendesa Mulungu.
58011006	Kahi bila ya dihuwi isikudahika kumwendesa imwene. Kosoko wowose iyakumusegelela Mulungu yagila yahuwile fina kabaho na fina yakuwengha mageleko wose awekumuhananga imwene.
58011007	Kwa dihuwi Nuhu, yakafuluse kujamigwa ne Mulungu muchanhya ye simbuli isisinhati soneke hakamutegelesa Mulungu na kugolosa ngalawa kosoko ya kuwahonya awanhu we inyumba yakwe; kwa dino hakaliganisa ichilunga muhasi wo uchawelu uwukwija kwa dihuwi.
58011008	Kwa dihuwi Ibulahimu hakafumila foyenangigwe kuluta ahanhu hoyowile yakuhokela uhasi; na hakaleuka, nghamanyile koyekwija.
58011009	Kwa dihuwi hakekala muisi iya ye dihuwiso, kefana mugeni, yekale mumahema hamwedu na Isaka na Yakobo, wahasi hamwedu naye we dihuwiso difane didyo.
58011010	Kosoko hakalangaga kumwande ku kaya iyina singindiso, imujengaji na Mugolosaji wakwe ni Mulungu.
58011011	Kwa dihuwi Sala imwenyecho hakahokela ludole lwo usokesi, hamwedu hakaloka ichigele che cheleko hakamuhuwila imwene muchawelu iyahuwise.
58011012	Hambiya kugendela munhu yumwedu, na imwene hakowa munhu muswanu ninga yefane yafile, hachelekwa cheleko chingi kifana nyelesi sa kulanga kahi nghukudaha kutala kifanadisanga idyuwile mungingi ye bahali.
58011013	Awano wose hawafa mwihuwi wasinhati wahokele ichalaganiswe, ninga wafuluse kuchona na kubwedelela kwa kutali, na kumanya fina hawowa wageni na wagendaji muchilunga.
58011014	Kosoko awanhu awekulonga simbuli sifane siso wakonesa chalinje fina wakukongha iisi yawo yo kwikala.
58011015	Kusigwe hawadogaga kosoko ye iisi yiyo yowaleuke, hawowa wakuwa na luneka lwa kuya.
58011016	Ninga ifene foyuwile, wakuhananga iswanu, iyakulanga. Nochanghone Mulungu nghakona chinyala kwinangigwa Mulungu wawo, kosoko kawatandila kaya.
58011017	Kwa ihuwi Ibulahimu foyagesigwe, hakamulafa Isaka yowe nhambiko na imwene iyahokele amahuwiso hakafumila kumulafa imwanagwe yumwedu,

58011019	Hakadogaga fina Mulungu yakudaha kuwenula wanhu hata kulawa kuwafile; kamei kulonga kwa konesa, hakamupata imwene kunyuma.

58011022	Kwa dihuwi Yusufu, kundumiliso yo uwumi wakwe yatambula simbuli so kuleuka kwawo wana wa Isilaeli, na kulagisa muchanhya ya masiko gakwe.
58011023	Kwa dihuwi Musa, ichigele cho kwelekwa kwakwe hakafisigwa minyesi midatu ne babakwae ne ingina, kosoko hawona imwana hakowa muswanu lugano; kahi wasogohe dilakiso dye mundewa.

58011025	hakona ibeka yapate magayo hamwedu na wanhu we Mulungu kusuma kibwedesa muwihi kwa chipisi chidodogi.

58011029	Kwa dihuwi awanhu hawaloka ibahali ya Shamu, kifana muisi inyalile; Amba Awamisili fowagesile kulonga hawonywa munghabu wose.
58011030	Kwa dihuwi singhasi sa Yeliko hasugwa fosasungulitigwa majuwa mufungate.
58011031	Kwa dihuwi Lahabu we chilanga nghabanigwa hamwedu na waya awechaka chihuliko; kosoko hawanihokela kwa digoya awaya awasakulage.
58011032	Nani nongechoni kahi? Kosoko ye ichigele idikudahika kwigala simbuli sa Gidioni na Balaka na Samusoni na Yefuta na Daudi na Samwili na sa wagonesi
58011033	awene kugendela dihuwi hawasuma siisi isowage na wandewa, hawowa wachawelu, hawapasa ichahuwisigwe, hawagubika imilomo ye sisimba.
58011034	Hasima umoto na kwihuligwa mumakali ga mapanga. Hawagumigwa ludole kusuma usoka, hawowa fitungati munghondo, hawawinga amakingili ga wageni wowakitowage nawo.
58011035	Awanawake hawahokela wanhu wawo wafile wenuke mudifa awamonga hawasambasigwa wakulema kudoholeligwa, uleke wenuligwe fiswanu.
58011036	Awamonga hawagaya kwa kubesigwa na kutoigwa, kahi hata kwigaligwa kuchifungo.
58011037	Hwatoigwa mawe mpaka kufa, hawadumuligwa kwa misumeno hawakomigwa kwa ipanga hata kusanguligwa kifana ngholo na mhene foikusanguligwa inghingo yakwe, wagaya na kudumangila, na kona usungu,
58011038	wanhu ambawo chilunga chisagiligwe kuwa nawo. Hawasunguluta munyika na mumatunda, na mumapango na mashimo.

58012024	na kwa Yesu mulongesi we dilagano disha na kwe sekame inyunyisigwe iyikulonga maswamu kusuma isakame ya Habili.
58012025	Langisiseni munghamuleme iyekulonga. Kosoko inghowa wasakinegile ugele wowamulemile imwene iyawajamage muchilunga, lugano sichikudaha kwihuligwa aseye chinghakinega na imwene iyekuchijama kulawa kulanga.
58012026	Dijwi dyake kahi hadisingisa ichilunga mu ugele uwuya; ninga hambiya kalaganisa, “Kamwedu kahi nosingisa siyo ichilunga du ninga na ulanga.”

58013001	Uwendo we chindugu ugendelele.

58013022	Nikumutasani wandugusangu, mufumile imbuli ino ina maloleso kosoko nimuwandikilani kwa uguhi.

59003015	Ubala wo si uya uwukudulika kulawa kuchanhya, ninga we chilunga, we sinhenda se chimunhu, na Luhoma.
59003016	Kosoko ahena ifinju na ulefi no hena matemanuko, na chila nhenda ihile.
59003017	Ninga ubala uwukulawa kuchanhya, bosi ni swanu, kahi ni wa digoya, wa uholo, tayali kutegelesa simhuli sa wanhu, wina ubasi na mamudyo maswanu, wichaka, finju, wichaka unafiki.
59003018	Na dimudyo dyo uchawelu dikuhandigwa mu digoya na waya awekugolosa digoya.
59004001	Inghondo ikwigaligwa na choni, choni chikwigala kitowa mugati yenu? Singhamba usulumisi wenu muwecho wuwile mufilungo fye mitufi yenu?
59004002	Mukusulumila ninga musikupata gomukuhananga, hambiya mukoma na kusulumila kwa fibi, ninga musikupata hata mukitowa na kwika nghodo. Hamukupata kosoko musikutasa.
59004003	Mukutasa ninga musikupata kosoko mukutasa fibi, uleke mutumie musinhenda sso usulumiso wihile.
59004004	Anyeye mufiyumbe fisikuhuwilika! Musimanyile fina kikola mbuya ne chilunga ni kuwa munghondo ne Mulungu? Kosoko iyo wowose yakuhanaga kuwa mwimbuya ne chilunga yakigolosa imwecho kuwa munghondo we Mulungu.
59004005	au mumanya matulumo gakulonga chaka gagambile; Yuyo yakona finju muchanya ye muhe iyagolose kwikala mugati yetu?
59004006	Ninga yakulafa dihewa dingi; kwahiyo ikugamba Mulungu yakuwapinga awakiinula ninga yakuwengha dihewa awaholo.
59004007	Muhulikeni Mulungu. Mlemeni luhoma naye kuwatijani.
59004008	Msegeleleni Mulungu naye kowasegelela nyeye. Sunheni mikono yenu, anyeye mwine wihi, safisheni mimoyo yenu, anyeye wanhu we milomo mili.
59004009	Hongeseni na kulila. Chiseko chenu chuwe kuhongesa chinyemi chenu chuwe chililo.
59004010	Muwe waholo hamwende ye Mundewa naye kowenulani.
59004011	Munghakilonge fibi nyenye kwa nyenye. Kosoko imwene yakulonga gehile muchanya ye munduguse, yakudilonga dilagiso na yakuliganisa dilagiso. Ninga inghowa ukudiliganisa dilagiso basi gweye simugolosaji we dilagiso ninga mulamusi.
59004012	Kwina mulafaji we dilagiso yumwedu du kahi nomuliganisi imwene iyakudaha kuhonya na kubana. Ninga kwanani ukumulamula imiyago?
59004013	Wijeni hambiya anyeye mukugamba, Diyelo ama nhosiku choluta akuya na kukaya iya na kugolosa nhafi na nhafi na kugolosa biyashala;
59004014	ugele uwo musimanyile iyo inghousiku. Mikalile yenu ni choni, kosoko nyeye mwa maluwa gakubota kwa chipisi na kunyala.
59004015	Mukinhangagigwa mugambe Mundewa yanghenda chogolosa nhafi na kuluta nhafi
59004016	Kifana fomukitunya kitunya. Kitunya kose kwa namna ino kwiha.
59004017	Kosoko wowose yamanyile amaswanu ninga yakuduga kugagolosa, ukwakwe munhu yo ni sambi.
59005001	Tegeleseni nyeye muwagoli, lileni na kuhongesa kosoko ya magayo agakwanga gawejileni.
59005002	Ugoli wenu udoda kamei suke senu siidigwa na matele.
59005003	sahabu yenu ne ifesa ikola kutu na ikutu yakwe yokwija kuwadiyani ne mitufi yenu kifana moto. Mukiikila ugoli wenu mwijuwa dye ndumo.
59005004	Langeni mushahala wa awakulima wakugola migunda yenu, gomukiikile, ne chililo che wagolaji chimufikila Mundewa we inghondo.
59005005	Hamwikala muchilunga kwa mikalile ya anasa; munonesa mimoyo yenu muchanhya ye dijuwa dye kuchinjigwa.
59005006	Mulamula na kukoma we sinhenda siswanu, ninga nghawatendile chinhu.
59005007	Finyiliseni wandugu sangu mpaka kwija kwe Mundewa. Langeni kifana mukulima foyakugojela kugola kwa mafuno gakwe ge chilunga, mpaka gapate ifula ya nghonga ne ya ndumo.
59005008	Anye nanye muwe na ufinyilisi nheifo. Mwime mumimoyo yenu, kosoko dijuwa dyokwija Mundewa dyahabehi.
59005009	Munghakinghunghulikile nyenye kwa nyenye wandugu, uleke mungheje mulamuligwa; langeni, Imulamusi kema mumilango.
59005010	Uwe kifana nonga ya kwandamila ye magayo na ufinyilisi mukulu wa wagonesi wagonese mwisina dye Mundewa.
59005011	Langeni chikuwenanga ibeka awaya awafinyilisi. Hamuhulika ufinyilisi wakwe Ayubu, na hamona idikusudi dye Mulungu, ifene foniwahuluma na ubasi.
59005012	Ninga muchanhya ya gose wandugu sangu munghakilahe, kwa ulanga kahi kwa isi ama kilaha kwa namna yoyse iya, ninga heye yenu yowe heye na hata nayo yuwe hata, uleke mungheje mukugwila muulamusi.
59005013	Kwina munhu wowose yakwidasika mugati yenu? Na yatase. Kasangalala? Na yembe sinyimbo sa kutunya.
59005014	Mugati yenu mwina munhu mutamu? Na yawenange wasehe we dikanisa, wamutasile, wamubake na mafuta mwisina dye Mundewa;
59005015	na akuya kutasa kwa ihuwi komuhonya mutamu yuya, na hata inghowa hakagolosa wihi kolekeleligwa.
59005016	Hambiya lambeni wihi chila munhu kwe miyagwe, na kitasila nyenye kwa nyenye, uleke muhonyigwe. Kosoko mataso gemuchawelu gakwigala mabidulo makulu.
59005017	Eliya hakowa munhu fina seye, ninga hakatasa ifula inghatonye, na kwa minyaka midatu na minyesi mutandatu isilafile hata ditwenhe.
59005018	Kamei hakatasa lwa keli hoitonya na chilunga hochikweleka.
59005019	Wandugu sangu munhu wowose mugati yenu yanghagilila kutali kulawa kuchawelu kamei yumwedu wenu yamuwise,
59005020	manyeni fina ayuya yamuwise imwihi yuya kulawa musambi kohonya chidoga chakwe ne difa na sambi sakwe nyingi sogubikigwa.
60001001	iPetulo mutumigwa wa Yesu Kilisito kuwanhu wasaguligwe, wekale hayohayo musiisi so ugeni ako Ponto, Galatiya, Kapadokiya, na Asiya na Bisiniya,
60001002	awasaguligwe na kumanyigwa na Mulungu Baba na kusunhigwa na Muhe uleke wamuhulike Yesu Kilisito na kutwekeseligwa sakame yakwe: Mboto ne dihewa dimemelekele nanye.
60001003	Yatunyigwe Mulungu Baba we Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito! Iyacheleke lwa keli kwa kuchonela ubasi lugano uleke chuwe na ihuwi dine uumi wo kulawa kwakwe Yesu Kilisito muchilalo,
60001004	Chipate na ubasi uusikubanika wichaka wihi uusikunyala uwikigwe kulanga kosoko yenu.
60001005	Anyeye mukidimigwa kwa ludole lwe Mulungu kulokela mwihuwi, uleke mupate uhonyi ufuluse kugubuligwa muchigele che ndumo
60001006	Mokuwa na chinyemi lugano chigele chicho, ingawa hambiya kwa chipisi chidodogi soko ni lasima muwe mwichaka chinyemi kosoko ya magesa ge hayohayo.
60001007	Kosoko kugesigwa kwa dihuwi dyenu kwina maliho makulu kusuma sahabu ikwagilila ingawa ikugesigwa kwa moto, uleke konekane fina kwina ilumbo na itunyo na chogoho mukugubuligwa kwakwe Yesu Kilisito.
60001008	Ninga mukumwenda ingawa musimonile, hambiya mumuhuwila na kubweda kwa chinyemi chikulu chine lutunyo,
60001009	fina fomuhokele uhonyi we fidoga fyenu kulokela dihuwi dyenu.
60001010	Awagonesi awagonese imboto yenu hawaikongha na kuyusilisa na kuihananga imbuli yo kwihuligwa;
60001011	Wamanye no chigele chihoki choneswe ne Muhe we Kilisito mugati yawo, kugonesa magayo goyakwija yapata Kilisito ne ditunyo dyokwandamila.
60001012	Howagubulilwa fina sikosoko ya milimo yawo awecho, ninga kosoko ya nyeye mumbuli sino sikuhubiliigwa hambiya kulokela waya wawegalile imbuli swanu kwa Muhe Musunhile yalawile kulanga (mbuli sikwendigwa kulangigwa hata na Wasungula)!
60001013	Hambiya kiyoheni mumisungu yenu mufulise na kwika dihuwi dyenu mudihewa dyo mukwija mukwinangigwa ugele Yesu Kilisito foyakwija yagubuligwa.
60001014	Kahi kifana wana mukuhulika munghakiliganise na umelo wenu wakatali na ubwalasi.
60001015	Ninga kifana iyawenangeni fonimusunhi nanye yuweni wasunhile, mumikalile yose.
60001016	Kosoko itulumigwa kugamba “Mokuwa wasunhile kosoko niye namusunhile”.
60001017	Halika mukumwinanga Baba yuyo iyakulamula wanhu bila konelela basi gendeni kwa chogoho muchigele chenu kifana si wakaya.
60001018	Manyeni fina hamwihuligwa musinhenda sihile sa wababa senu si kwa finhu fikubanika kifana fesa na sahabu,
60001019	ninga kulokela sakame ya iliho ikulu ya Kilisito, kifana ye mwana we ngholo iyechaka chilema kahi ikofu,
60001020	imwene hakamanyika kulawa kunghali kumbigwa nghindisi se chilunga, kahi hakagubuligwa kundumo kosoko yenu nyeye.
60001021	Kulokela imwene mukihuwisa mwi Mulungu iyamwinuleni kulawa muchilalo na kumwinagha itunyo, uleke dihuwi dyenu ne nyihuwisa yenu fuwe mwi Mulungu.
60001022	Hambiya musunhigwa fidoga fyenu kwa njila ya kuhulika kwenu ichawelu kwa wendo mujelu we chindugu, kiyendeni nyenye kwa nyenye kwa moyo mujelu.
60001023	Kokoso mwelekwa lwa keli si mbeyu ikubanika ninga iisikubanika hata kwa kulokela mbuli nyumi imile mwi Mulungu.
60001024	Kosoko, “Mutufi wose ukifana manyasi na dituyo dyakwe dyose dikifana iluwa dya inyagala, manyagala gakubota maluwa kamei gakulagala.
60001025	Ninga imbuli ye Mundewa ikwima minyaka na minyaka.” Na imbuli yo noiya ihubiliigwe ukwenu.
60002001	Ninga tageni kutali wihi wose na hila, chimwefe, gele, na kisongesela, na maligo gose.
60002002	Kahi kifana wana wadodogi melemeleni mele amaswanu ge chimuhe, kosoko kulokela gago mokulila uhonyi wenu.
60002003	Kosoko chinomola uswanu we Mundewa.
60002004	Mulutileni imwene idiwe dimumi dilemigwe na wanhu, ninga kwe Mulungu disaguligwa kahi dya iliho ikulu.
60002005	Nanye kifana mawe ge mumi mujengigwa muwe nyumba ya Muhe ukuhani usunhile, mulafe sadaka sa Muhe sikwendigwa ne Mulungu kulokela Yesu Kilisito.
60002006	Kosoko itulumwa mumaandiko kugamba, “Langa nikwika Sayuni diwe dya munghanda disaguligwe dye diliho dikulu na chila iyakumuhuwila nghakupata chinyala.”
60002007	Ukwenu nyeye muhuwile kagaluka wa iliho ikulu ninga kwa wasikuhuwila, “Idiwe diya diya dilemigwe na wajensi digaluka iwe ikulu dya munghanda,”
60002008	Na kahi mawandiko gamonga nago gagamba: “Mudiwe umo wotowa nghwal, iwe dya ikangalawe” idikuwakinya kosoko wasendile kuhulika imbuli yowahanagwe kugolosa.
60002009	Ninga nyeye musaguligwa, lukolo lwe Undewa we chikuhani, ditaifa disunhile, mwa wanhu we Mulungu uleke mutamilise nhenda singhulu isakwe imwene yawenangileni kulawa mulwisa kwija kumwanga wakwe mukulu.
60002010	Ktali hamuwa siyo wanhu ninga hambiya wanhu we Mulungu, hamuwa mwichaka ubasi ninga hambiya muhokela ubasi.
60002011	Wandugu sangu nikuwatasani nyeye muwageni na wagendaji mwikale kutali ne sinhenda so umelo wo mutufi isikulemana na chidoga.
60002012	Muwe na igendele miswanu mugati ya wamembe uleke inghowa wakulonga gehile muchanhya yenu, fowakona sinhenda senu siswanu wamutunye Mulungu mwijuwa dyo kwija kwakwe Mundewa.
60002013	Hulikiseni wene ludole ne wasilikal; ikosoko ye Mundewa.
60002014	Ama awakutawala kosoko watumigwa ne Mulungu kuwatosa igelo awakugolosa nhenda sihile, na wawatunye wakugolosa maswanu.
60002015	Kosoko nofoyakwenda iMulungu fina kwa kugolosa maswanu mudahe kuulegusa uwihi na ubwalasi wa wanhu.
60002016	Ikaleni mundekeleligwa kifana wanhu walekeleligwe, ninga munghagolose wihi kosoko muwa mundekeleligwa, ninga kifana watumigwa we Mulungu.
60002017	Wahulikeni wanhu wose na wendeni wayenu wo mwinawo mwi kanisa, mogoheni Mulungu, hulikiseni wakulu, yandamileni magayo ga Kilisito
60002018	Anyeye watumwa wahulikiseni wakulu wenu kwa chogoho chose siyo du kwa waya waholo na waswanu ninga hata waya awakali.
60002019	Kosoko ni fiswanu munhu kufinyilisa magayo kosoko ye Mulungu nomo ukugaya wichaka dikosa.
60002020	Kosoko kwina iliho dyaki nomo ukufinyilisa magayo kosoko ya nhenda sako sihile? Ninga halika ukufinyilisa magayo kosoko ye Mulungu basi Mulungu imwecho kokumotesa.
60002021	Umo nomo mwinangiligwe kosoko Kilisito imwecho hakalokela umo mumagayo kosoko yenu, kawalekelani mbasi mwandamile.
60002022	“Ghagolose sambi kahi wihi usoneke mumulomo wakwe.”
60002023	Foyaligigwe nghowise iligo, foyasambasigwe nghatowile munhu. Ninga hakamuhuwila Mulungu imulamusi yechaka konelela.
60002024	Imwene imwecho hakenula sisambi setu mumutufi wakwe mumusalaba, uleke chufe musisambi na chuwe womi munhenda swanu. Kwa kutoigwa kwakwe anye muhona.
60002025	Kosoko hamuwa kifana ngholo sagilile, ninga hambiya muya kwe mudimi na mulangisisi we fidoga fyenu.
60003001	Anye nanye muwanawake wahulikeni wagosi wenu uleke halika wauko awasikwandamila imbuli wayandamile kwa kulanga nhenda swanu sa wanawake wawo,
60003002	nomoo wakona uswanu na chogoho mumikalile yenu.
60003003	Kahi kihamba kwenu kunghowe kunje yo mutufi kwa njwili sa sahabu na kufala fiswanu,
60003004	ninga uswanu wo kihamba kwenu uwe kulawa kusi ye fidoga fye mimoyo imiswanu ikwendesa hamwande ye Mulungu.
60003005	Nhafi nofo yowile kuwanawake awasunhile wene dihuwi kwe Mulungu wakihambage awecho na kuwahulika wagosi wawo,
60003006	kifana Sala foyamuhulika mugosi wakwe Ibulahimu na kumwinanga mundewa. Na hambiya nyeye mugaluka wanagwe munghagolosa maswanu bila itisi dyodyose.
60003007	Nheifo anye nanye muwagosi ikaleni fiswanu na wanawake senu na kumwingha mwanamuke chogoho kifana chinhu chichaka ludole kifana wahasi we imboto yo uumi, uleke kutasa kwenu kunghakindisigwe.
60003008	Kwa kumalagisa mose muwe na lugota wa chimuhe, ubasi, wendo munhu na miyagwe, moyo muswanu na uholo.
60003009	Munghakigolosele gehile kwa gehile ninga badala ya wihi kigoloseleni maswanu na kimotesa kosoko nogomwinangiligwe kumboto.
60003010	Kosoko iyakwenda uumi na kuwa na majuwa maswanu yakinege dilimi dyakwe dinghalonge gehile na milomo yakwe inghalonge wihi,
60003011	yabiduke kuuleka uwihi na kugolosa uswanu; yakonghe dihewa na kudyandamila.
60003012	Kosoko meso ge Mundewa gowa kuwena sinhenda siswanu na nghutwi sakwe sigubuka kutegelesa mataso gawo, ninga chihanga che Mundewa chuwa kwa waya wakugolosa wihi.
60003013	Nonani yakwanga yawabulage halika mukugolosa maswanu?
60003014	Ninga hata munghowa mukugaya kwa kugolosa maswanu momotesigwa, munghogohe gowakogoha.
60003015	Ninga mumimoyo yenu mwingheni Kilisito chogoho kifana Mundewa, majuwa gose yuweni meso mudahe kumutamila chila munhu dihuwi dyomwinadyo, kahi goloseni kwa uswanu na ujelu.
60003016	Yuweni wanhu waswanu na wakuhuwilika uleke nomowakumulongani fibi fowakona nhenda senu swanu sa Kilisito wapate chinyala.
60003017	Kosoko ni fiswanu kutabika soko ya maswanu mana ayo noyo yakwenda Mulungu kuliko kutabika kwa kugolosa wihi.
60003018	Soko Kilisito naye hakofa lumwedu du soko ya sambi, iyechaka wihi kosoko ya wene wihi uleke yachigale kwe Mulung, hakofa chimutufi ninga mumi chimuhe.
60003019	Hoyoluta kuhubiliya fidoga fuwile muchifungo.
60003020	Fidoga fifyo ifisendile kumuhulika Mulungu muchigele foyawagojele kulamba mumajuwa ga Nowa, kulawa kujengigwa disafina dingiligwe na wanhu wakefu, nawo ni munana muhala, awahonyigwe kulokela meji.
60003021	Aino ni mbasi ya ubatiso ukuwahonyani nyeye majuwa gano, siyo kulegusa wihi wa mutufi du, ninga uswanu we fidoga kulokela kulawa kwa Yesu Kilisito muchilalo,
60003022	iyalutile kulanga na kowa mukono wo kumoso we Mulungu hamwedu na malaika, uludole na udaha wose ukumuhulika imwene.
60004001	Hambiya kosoko Kilisito hakagaya mumutufi nanye kiyoheni muwecho mwidoga didyo, kosoko iyakugaya kalekana na sambi,
60004002	kosoko kulawa hambiya munghekale kahi munghenda se umelo se chimutufi ninga fina foyakwenda Mulungu.
60004003	chigele chomwikale munhenda senu sihile se chilunga sidumila hambiya, kosoko hamugenda muwihi, umelo wihi, ulefi, ukobo na kufuga masikimunhu.
60004004	Wakujuma kosoko wakona anyeye musikwandamila mbuli sawo sihile na kosoko iyo wakuwaligani.
60004005	Ninga wakwija walafa nghala ya chila mbuli kwe imwene Imulamusi we fyose fimumi na fufile.
60004006	Kosoko iyo nochileka imbuli swanu ihubiligwe mpaka kuwofile, uleke waliganiswe chimutufi kifana wanhu fowakuliganisigwa uleke wowe womi chimuhe kifana Mulungu fonimumi.
60004007	Ninga indumo ye chila mbuli yahabehi, basi mwikale meso na fiswanu na mumawombi genu muwecho.
60004008	Kwa kongesa mwikale muwendo kiyendeni nyeye kwa nyenye, kosoko uwendo ukugubika masambi mengi.
60004009	Kihokeleni musikaya senu nyenye kwa nyenye bila kukalala.
60004010	Yuweni wanhu waswanu mukitogomele chila munhu na miyagwe fina finafoyahokele chipawa kwe Mulungu.
60004011	Iyakulonga yalonge kifana yakulonga mbuli ya Mulungu, na iyakutogoma yatogome kwa ludole lwo yenghigwe ne Mulungu, uleke Mulungu yatunyigwe mugose kulokela Yesu Kilisito. Mwiimwene mwina itunyo na udaha wa majuwa gose. Hano.
60004012	Wandugu sangu munghone ijumo magayo gowile mugati yenu gakuwapata kuwagesani, kifana chinhu chisha.
60004013	Ninga sekeleleni kosoko mukuhangila magayo goyapata Kilisito uleke mwije muwe na chinyemi na kubwedelela mwitunyo dyo kugubuligwa kwakwe.
60004014	Inghowa mukuligigwa soko ye disina dya Kilisito, mwina ibeka, kosoko iMuhe we ditunyo imwene we Mulungu yakwikala muchanhya yenu. Ukwawo wene keha, ninga ukwenu, kena itunyo.
60004015	Ninga munghaleke munhu wa ukwenu yagaye kifana kakoma munhu, ama muhiji, au yagolose mbuli ihile, hegu kifana munhu yendeyogolosa mbuli sa wamonga.
60004016	Ninga inghowa yakutabika kosoko ni muKilisito basi yanghone chinyala, mutunye Mulungu kosoko nokwinula disina dyakwe uko.
60004017	Kosoko chigele chifika cho uliganiso we Mulungu kukongela munyumba yakwe, hambiya halika ukukongela ukwetu togoleni yokuwa nhani kuwanhu awasikwenda kuhulika imbuli swanu ye Mulungu?
60004018	Na, “Imuchawelu yanghahonyigwa kwa tabu togola yokuwanhani kwa yuya inghamumanyile Mulungu ne yene sisambi?”
60004019	Kosoko iyo basi waya awakugaya kusoko ye Mulungu wamwikile Mumbi imuchawelu dihuwi, nomowakugolosa maswanu.
60005001	Hambiya fina niye nani fonimusehe na muhomelesi wa magayo ga Kilisito, nheifiya kwa kuhangila ditunyo digubuligwe, nikuwatasa dedede wasehe woile ukwenu
60005002	kudima singholo se Mulungu suwile ukwenu, siyo kwa kudindilisigwa ninga kifana Mulungu foyakwenda mugolose
60005003	munghowe fitunghati kwa waya womukuwadima, ninga muwe ifuso kusingholo so mukudima
60005004	na mudimi mukulu foyakwijayasololekela mokwija mufasigwa nghofiya ye ditunyo iisikunyala.
60005005	Nheifo anye nanye muwajelelo mugahokele malamusi ga filongosi, mose kiyoheni uholosi uleke mukitase munhu na miyagwe, “Kosoko Mulungu yakulemana na awekiyona ninga yakuwengha mboto awaholo.”
60005006	Yugwileni hasi yo mukono mukulu we Mulungu uleke yawenuleni muchigele chakwe.
60005007	Mutwikeni imwene manghonge genu gose kosoko noyakuwalangilila.
60005008	Gendeni fiswanu na kuwa meso kosoko imulhi wenu luhoma kakifana simba yakugendagenda kumukongha munhu yamumese.
60005009	Mlemeni, imeni ngwi mwihuwi dyenu kosoko mumanye fina magayo gakumemelekela kuwandugu senu woile muchilunga.
60005010	Na fomukumala kutabika kwa chigele chidodogi Mulungu we imboto yose iyamwinangeni kuditunyo dyakwe dya minyaka na minyaka duwile muKilisito, yuyo imwecho kowoisilani, kowatasani, kowagumani ludole na kuwemisani.
60005011	Kwe imwene kwina ludole minyaka na minyaka. Hano Mulamuso wo kumalagisa
60005012	Kulokela Silowano wonikudoga fina ni munhu muchawelu, niwandika baluwa ino ndodogi kuwagumani ludole na kulonga fina ayino no mboto ye chawelu ye Mulungu imeni ngwi mu iyo.
60005013	Dikanisa duwile hano Babeli dikuwalamusani na mwanangu Maluko.
60005014	Kilamuseni munu na miyagwe kwa mulamuso wa wendo. Dihewa dyuwe nanye mose muwile mugati ya Kilisito.
61001001	Simoni Petulo imutumwa na Mutumigwa wa Yesu Kilisito, kuwose wena dihuwi fina idyetu duwile muchawelu ye Mulungu wetu ne Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito:
61001002	Imboto ne dihewa dyongeseke ukwenu muumanyi we Mulungu ne we Mundewa wetu Yesu.
61001003	Uludole lwe ulungu lwakwe uwetu uchingha finhu fyose muumi, na mwe chimulungu kulokela umanyi wakwe yachinangile mwitunyo dyakwe imwecho na uswanu wose.
61001004	Kwakuchingha iliho ikulu na ihuwiso ikulu, fina kulokela gano chidahe kinega uwihi wuwile muchilunga kosoko ya usulumisi, uleke muwe wahangi we iyasili ye chilungu.
61001005	Kosoko iyo goloseni chigosi kwima mwihuwi kwa nyikala swanu na nyikala swanu muumanyi,
61001006	na muumanyi hamwedu ne chiasi, ne chiasi hamwedu na ufinyilisi, na muufinyilisi umo ulungu,
61001007	na muulungu umo uwendo we chindugu, na uwendo we chindugu hamwedu na uwendo.
61001008	Kosoko finhu fino finghowa ukwenu na kumema, fikuwagolosa munghowe wadoba na awasikweleka mamudyo go umanyi we Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito.
61001009	Kosoko wowose iyakuhungukiligwa finhu fino ni mudula hakudaha kona finhu fuwile kutali kahi kasimilwa kusunhigwa kwa wihi wakwe uya wa katali.
61001010	Hambiya wandugu sangu, konyeni kumanya lwinango lwenu na kusaguligwa kwenu kosoko munghagolosa nheifo musikudaha kutoa nghwalo..
61001011	Kosoko kwa njila yiyo, mokwinghigwa luneka lwa kwingila muundewa we Mundewa wetu, Mwihula Yesu Kilisito.
61001012	Hambiya nowagelegesa simbuli asi, hata inghowa mufulusa kusimanya na kwenesigwa ne ichawelu ijile ukwenu.
61001013	Nani nikona fiswanu, muchigele nuwile mumutufi uno kuwagelegesa,
