61001014	kulawa fonamanya fina kufa kwangu kumala kwija kifana Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito foyanyonese fiswanu.
61001015	Na nogolosa chila ludole uleke kukuleguka kwangu anyeye mudahe kugelegela mambo gano.
61001016	Kosoko sichandamile mbasi situngigwe kwa ubala ugele fowumanyike ukwenu uludole na kwija kwe Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito, ninga chigaluka wahomeleswi wonile kwa meso ukulu wakwe.
61001017	Kosoko hakahokela chogoho na itunyo kulawa kwe Mulungu Baba chigele dijwi kulawa mwitunyo dikulu fodyalonga kugamba, “Ayuno no Mwanangu, Mwendigwa wangu wonyendesigwe naye lugano.”
61001018	Aseye chiwecho hachidihulika dijwi dijo kulawa kulanga, ugele wochowile naye mwitunda disunhile.
61001019	Hambiya china mbuli ye ugonesi uwecho ukangale. Kahi yokuwa fiswanu inghowa motega sighutwi mudidino kifana taa ikwaka mwichisa, mpaka dijuwa dilawe, na inyelesi ya kumugingu kumulika mumimoyo yenu.
61001020	Bosi ya gose mumanye dino, fina kwichaka ugonesi wa Mawandiko ulawile muutapita wa munhu imwenyecho,
61001021	kosoko hechaka ugonesi wowose winjile kwa nyenda ya munhu, ninga wanhu hawalonga kwa kulongoswa na Muhe Musunhile kulawa kwe Mulungu.
61002001	Ninga walimu wo udasi hawalawanisa mugati ya wanhu, kifana ukwenu fokukwanga nako kuwe na walimu wa udasi, awakwigisa kwa ubala madoga gakubana. Wakumulema mpaka Mundewa yawagulile na kiigalila awecho kwangamila kwa habehi.
61002002	Na matewa wokwandamila njila ya wihi, na kosoko ya walimu wano wo udasi injila ye chawelu yoligigwa.
61002003	Na mumelo wawo uwo wopata chinhu ukwenu kwa mbuli sa udasi. Uliganiso wawo ufuluka kulongigwa kulawa katali, siyo ya chaka na kwangamila kwawo hakukuleka.
61002004	Hambiya inghowa Mulungu hawalekile amalaika waya wagolose wihi, ninga hakawaguma kumoto na kuwoha muchifungo kusi ye dichisa mpaka uliganiso wije;
61002005	na inghowa hachilekile ichilunga chiya cha katali, hakamuhonya Nuhu, imuchawelu, hamwedu na wamonga mufungate chigele choyegale mafaluko muchilunga che wihi;
61002006	na kwa kubidula sikaya sa Sodoma na Gomola kuwa ifu hakawaliganisa uleke yuwe mbasi kuwanhu awesimumanyile Mulungu,
61002007	hakamuhonya Lutu, imuchawelu yendekwidasigwa ne wihi na awakubana.
61002008	( kosoko ayuya imuchawelu yekale nawo ijuwa mpaka ijuwa hakakiidasa muuchawelu wakwe muchidoga kosoko ya nhenda sawo fina hakona na kuhulika),
61002009	kahi Mundewa kamanya kuwahonya wanhu wakwe kulawa mumagesa, na kuweka wechaka Mulungu mumagayo mpaka dijuwa dye uliganiso
61002010	lugano awaya wakwandamila usulumisi ne wihi wo umutufi na kubesa udaha. Wanhu wene ludole na kwenda, wasikogoha kuliga imutunyigwa
61002011	ninga malaika, wakulu na udaha na ludole, hawakuwasongesela kuliganiso we Mundewa.
61002012	Wanhu wano wakifana manyama ga kumbago gechaka, misungu gelekwa na kukoligwa na kukomigwa. Wakuliga gowasimanyile, na wakwija wakwagilila kifana makewe ga kumbago,
61002013	kugaya kokuwa kwawo kosoko ya kugolosa gehile. Wakutala kulewa kwawo nhemisi ni chinhu chiswanu. Wagaluka matonhe na wihi, na chinyala mufyakudiya fyenu fyo uwendo nomowakudiya nanyeye.
61002014	wena meso gamemile chilanga, wasikuleka kugolosa wihi. Wakwagilisa fidoga ifichaka ludole. Wene mimoyo ifusigwe ukobo. Wana waligitisigwe!
61002015	Waleka injila igoloke na wagilila, wakwandamila njila ya Balaamu mwana wa Basoli, yendile maliho ge wihi,
61002016	ninga hakagombeligwa kosoko ya nhenda sakwe sihile, dipunda isidikudaha kulonga hadilonga kwa ijwi dye chimunhu na kulemesa ugonesi uya.
61002017	Awano ni nhyoko sichaka meji na mafunde gakwandamila mheho; wene wekiligwa dichisa ikulu.
61002018	Kosoko wakulonga nonga ghulu so kitapa, kwa usulumisi we chimutufi na wihi, wakuwadanhilisa wanhu wakongile kuwatija waya wakugenda mudasi.
61002019	Wakuwahuwisa undekelelwa, ninga awene awecho ni watumwa wa wihi; kosoko wanhu ni watumwa kwa yuya yakuwagendesa.
61002020	Kosoko inghowa, fowakumala kinega na wihi we chilunga kulokela umanyi we Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito, kamei wakoligwe keli na kusumwa basi inyuwa yawo ya ndumo ikuwa iha kusuma ye nghonga.
61002021	Kosoko hayuwa fiswanu ukwawo woile wasiimanyile njila ye chawelu kusuma kuimanya kamei kuleka dilagiso disunhile dijile ukwawo.
61002022	Ikuwa ni kifana imbasi ye chawelu ikugamba, “Dibwa dyuwila madeka gakwe,” na, “Nguluwe ikiyogile yuya kahi mumatope.”
61003001	Aino hambiya, no baluwa ya keli yonimwandikilileni wendigwa, na musose simbili nikwinusa misungu yenu kwa kuwagelegesa;
61003002	uleke mugelegele sinonga salongigwe na wagonesi wasunhile ne dilagiso dye Mundewa na dye Mwihula kulokela watumigwa wenu.
61003003	Iyilongelele sose mukuhanangigwa mumanyi nhafi, ku majuwa gwe ndumo wokwija wanhu wo lubeso no lubeso lwawo awekuwandamila usulumisi wawo awecho
61003004	na kugamba “dyuwahe dihuwiso dyo kwija kwakwe? Kosoko kukongela awaBaba setu wakagone, ifinhufyose figendelela nheifo fofyowile kulawa kunghonga yo kumba.”
61003005	Wakufinya meso gawo wanghone inonga ino fina kwa mbulu ya Mulungu ulanga hawuwa uko kulawa katali ne chilungu hachumbigwa kulawa mumeji,
61003006	ku gago ichilunga che chigele chiya hachagilila kwa meji.
61003007	Ninga kwa mbuli yiyo, ulanga ne chilunga cha hambiya chikigwa sigafu kwa moto, fikigwe mpaka dijuwa dyo uliganiso na kubanigwa kwa wanhu wasimumanyile Mulungu.
61003008	Ninga wendingwa munghaibese imbulu yino, kososo kwe Mundewa dijuwa dimwedu dikifana minyaka chigulu chimwedu, kahi minyaka chigulu chimwedu ikifana ijuwa dimwedu.
61003009	iMundewa nghakusululuka kwigala dihuwiso dyakwe, fina wamonga fowakudoka kusululuka, ninga yakuwagojelani kosoko nghakwenda munhu wowose yagilile ninga wose walambe.
61003010	Ninga dijuwa dye Mundewa dikwija fina muhiji, kamei ulanga woloka kwa sindo nghulu na finhu fyose folakasigwa kwa moto, na iisi na fyose fimemile umo fokwagilila.
61003011	Hambiya kosoko finhu fino fyose fikwija fibanigwa kwa nheifo, anyeye mukuhanangigwa muwe wanhu wa migendele ya usunhile na ya chimulungu,
61003012	mukugojela na kutegelesela inija ye dijuwa diya dye Mulungu, kosoko ulanga ukwija umoligwa na kosomigwa kahi finhu fikulakasigwa.
61003013	Ninga, kosoko ya dihuwiso dyakwe chikugojela ulanga musha na chilunga chisha, hanhu hokwikala wanhu wene nhenda swanu.
61003014	Hambiya wendigwa wangu kosoko mukugojela mbuli siso, konyeni monekane ne imwene fina muwa mudiigoya, mwichaka wihi;
61003015	na utaleni ufinyilisi we Mundewa wetu kuwa ni uhonya. Kamei kahi mundugu setu Paulo hakawandikilani kwa ubala woyenghigwe,
61003016	yakulonga sisino simbuli musibaluwa sakwe sose. Mwina mbuli simonga nghugutu kusimanya, mbuli so wanhu wechaka awasisomile na awasimile fiswanu wakwagilila awecho, fina fowakugolosa kumatulumo gamonga.
61003017	Hambiya nyeye, wendigwa, kulawa fomwajanjalusigwa langisiseni munghalondigwe ne ubani na kwagilisa kwima kwenu.
61003018	Ninga kulileni mwihewa na umanyi we Mundewa wetu ne Muhonya Yesu Kilisito. Ukwakwe kuwe itunyo hambiya na majuwa gose. Hano.
62001001	Chikumutamilani anyeye aiya yowile kulawa kunghonga, yochihuluke, yochonile na meso getu, yochilangile na kuikwafa kwe mikono yetu, muchanhya ya imbuli yo uwumi
62001002	uwumi auno hawonesigwa, na chiwona kahi chiuhomelela, na chikumutamilani ukwenu uwumi wa majuwa gose, uwowile na iBaba ninga hawonesigwa chimesomeso ukwetu
62001003	Chikumutamilani anyeye wochihulike na kona uleke nanye muwe na umwedu na seye; na umwedu wetu ni hamwedu na Baba na hamwedu na Imwanagwe Yesu Kilisito.
62001004	Chiwandika simbuli sino uleke ichinyemi chetu chimemelekele.
62001005	Ayino no mbuli yochihulike kulawa ukwakwe na kutamilisa ukwenu fina iMulungu ni ujelu na umwakwe mwachaka chisa chochose.
62001006	Chinghagamba china umwedu naye ugele chikugenda muchisa chikudanha kahi chisikugolosa ichawelu;
62001007	ninga chinghagenda mu ujelu fina imwene foyowile mu ujeleu, china umwedu chila yumwedu na miyagwe, kahi isakame ya Yesu iMwanagwe ikuchisunha kulawa mu uwihi wose.
62001008	Chinghagamba chichaka wihi, chikidanhilisa chiwecho, na ichawelu isuwile umwetu.
62001009	Chinghalamba uwihi wetu, imwene ni wakuhuwilika na chawelu yakwenda yachinenele uwihi wetu na kusunha na kubana kwetu kose.
62001010	Chinghagamba chisigolose wihi, chikumugolosa imwene fina mudasi, na imbuli yakwe umwetu yamwichaka.
62002001	Wanangu wadodogi, nikumwandikilani sino uleke munghagolose uwihi; imunhu wosose yanghagolosa wihi chenaye iyakuchitasila kwa Baba, Yesu Kilisito imuchawelu;
62002002	imwene no nhambiko yo uwihi wetu, si uwihi uwetu du muhala ninga kosoko ye wihi we chilunga chose.
62002003	Kwa njila ino chikuwa fina chawelu chimumanya, nghona chikolile amalagiso gakwe.
62002004	Ayuya iyekugamba, “Nimumanya,” ninga nghekogoha amalagiso gakwe, ni mudasi, kahi mwi mumhu yefane yo kechaka ichawelu,
62002005	ninga iyekogoha imbuli yakwe, chawelu mwi munhu yuno uwendo we Mungu umemelekela. Kwa nheifo chikumanya chawelu fina chuwa umwakwe.
62002006	Ayuya iyakugamba yakwikala umwakwe inogela yaligane lugano fina imwene foyowile iYesu.
62002007	Wendigwa, sikumwandikilani ilagiso disha, ninga ilagiso dya katali no imbuli yomwahulike.
62002008	Kahi nikumwandikilani ilagiso disha, dye chawelu umwakwe na umwenu, kosoko ichisa chikuleuka na ujelu we chawelu ukonga kumulika.
62002009	Ayuya iyakugamba fina kowa mu ujelu akuno yakumusuhila imunduguse yekali muchisa.
62002010	Ayuya iyakumwenda imunduguse yakwikala mu ujelu na kwachaka soko yoyose yakumukwakalisa.
62002011	Ninga yuya yakumusula imunduguse kowa muchisa na yakugenda muchisa, na nghamanyile koyakuluta kosoko ichisa chimutula meso.
62002012	Nikumwandikilani anyeye, wana wadodogi, kosoko uwihi wenu ulekeleligwa kosoko yakwe.
62002013	Nikumwandikilani anyeye, cha baba, kosoko mumumanya imwene yowile kulawa kung'onga. Nikumwandikilani anyeye, wajelelo, kosoko mumusuma ayuya yehile. Nikumwandikilani anyeye, wana wadodogi kosoko mumumanya iBaba.
62002014	Nikumwandikilani anyeye, cha baba, kosoko mumumanya imwene wa kulawa kunghonga. Nimwandikilani anyeye, wajelelo, kosoko mwina ludole, na imbuli ye Mulungu yuwa mugati yenu, na mumusuma iyehile.
62002015	Munghachende ichilunga hegu ifinhu fya muchilunga. Imunhu wowose iyakwenda ichilunga, uwendo wa Baba usimugati yakwe.
62002016	Kosoko gose gowile muchilunga, kukusulumila kwa umutufi na kusulumila kwa meso na kiyona kwo mutufi, si fya Baba ninga ni fye chilunga.
62002017	Ne chilunga chikuloka, na usulumisi wakwe; ninga ayuya iyakugolosa foyakwenda iMulungu yekwikala majuwa gose.
62002018	Mowana, Awuno no ugele we indumo; fina fomuhulike fina imunghondo wa Kilisito yakwija, hambiya wanghondo wa Kilisito wengi wafulusa kwija, kosoko iyo chimanya no ugele we indumo wahabehi kwija.
62002019	Hawaleuka wachileka seye, kosoko wasowile wayetu, kosoko nhanga wowile wayetu hawowa wakugendelela hamwedu nase, ninga hawaleuka uleke imanyike fina si wose wowile hamwedu nase.
62002020	Ninga anyeye mubakigwa mafuta ne Musunhile, nanye mose mumanya.
62002021	Nikumwandikilani, si kosoko musimanyile ichawelu, ninga muimanyile, na kumanya fina kwechaka udasi ukulawa muchawelu.
62002022	No nani imudasi ninga ayuya iyakukana fina Yesu si Kilisito? Ayuya no Munghondo wa Kilisito, imunhu iyekumukana iBaba na iMwana.
62002023	Wowose iyekumukana iBaba nghenaye iMwana. Iyakumufumila iMwana kenaye iBaba naye.
62002024	Aiya yomwahulike kulawa kunghonga ikale mugati yenu. Nghona yomuhulike kulawa kunghonga ikala mugati yenu, mokwikala mwi Mwana na mwi Baba
62002025	Ayino no mbuli yoyachilalaganise aseye Uwumi wa majuwa gose.
62002026	Nikumwandikilani sino kosoko ya waya wakuhananga kumudanhilisani.
62002027	Ninga kwa nyeye, amafuta gaya gomubakigwe kulawa ukwakwe gekala kugati yenu, kahi mwechaka soko ya munhu wowose kumufusani. Kosoko amafuta gaya gakuwafusa finhu fyose, kahi ni chawelu, ninga si udasi, fina fogamufusileni, ikaleni kugati yakwe.
62002028	Na hambiya mowana wadodogi, ikaleni mugati yakwe, uleke nghona yakwija yolawanisa chuwe na ng'inyo na si kumutija kosoko ya chinyala cho kwija kwakwe.
62002029	Nghona mumanyile fina imwene ni muchawelu mukumanya fina chila iyakugolosa maswanu kelekigwa naye.
62003001	Langeni, uwendo wochinghigwe na Baba, kachigolosa chinangigwe wana wa Mulungu, na nofo chuwile. Ichanghone ichilunga chisikuchimanya seye sichamumanyile imwene.
62003002	Wendigwa, chawana wa Mulungu hambiya; isikumanyika fochikwendigwa chuwe, ninga chimanya foyakasololoka chikachikuwa fina imwene, kosoko chikachimona foyowile.
62003003	Na wose awena dihuwi dino umwakwe wakisunha awenyecho, fina imwene fonimusunhile.
62003004	Chila munhu yakugolosa wihi yakubana amalagiso ge Mulungu; uwihi ni kuleka kwandamila amalagiso.
62003005	Mumanya fina hakeja uleke yaleuse uwihi, na umwakwe mwichaka wihi.
62003006	Hechaka wowose iyakwikala umwakwe yakugolosa wihi; kwichaka munhu iyakugolosa uwihi iyamonile hegu kumumanya.
62003007	Wana wadodogi, imunhu yanghamudanhiliseni. Imunhu iyakugolosa uswanu ni muswanu, fina imwene fonimuswamu.
62003008	Iyekugolosa uwihi ni mwana wa Luhoma, kosoko iLuhoma kagolosaga wihi kulawa kunghonga. iMwana we Mulungu hakeja kosoko iino, kubana imilimo ya Luhoma.
62003009	Hechaka iyelekigwe ne Mulungu yakugolosa wihi; kosoko inyuwa ye Mulungu yuwa uwakwe, kahi nghadaha kugolosa wihi kosoko kelekigwa na Mulungu.
62003010	Kwa nheifo ikudaha koneka, awana we Mulungu no wehoki na wana wa Luhoma no wehoki. Inghekugolosa maswanu si wa Mulungu, na yuya inghakumwenda imunduguse.
62003011	Kosoko ayino no mbuli yomwahulike kulawa kunghonga, fina chikiyende,
62003012	chinghowe fina Kaini iyowile wa yuya yehile iyakomile imunduguse. Hakamukoma kosoki yaki? Kosoko sinhenda sakwe imwenyecho hasuwa sihile, ninga se munduguse hasuwa swanu.
62003013	Wandugusangu munghajume, fina ichilunga chikumulemani.
62003014	Chimanya fina aseye chiloka kulawa mudifa na kwingila mu uwumi, kosoko chikuwenda awandugu. Ayuya iyechaka wendo kowa mudifa
62003015	Chila munhu inghakwenda munduguse ni mukomaji, na mumanya fina kwechaka imukomaji, yena uwumi wa majuwa gose umwakwe.
62003016	Kwa njila ino chimanya uwendo, kosoko hakalafa uwumi wakwe kosoko yetu; ichagula ase nase chilafe uwumi wetu kosoko ya wandugu.
62003017	Ninga imunhu wowose yangowa na finhu fyose fye chilunga chino na yakumona imunduguse kechaka chinhu, yanghagolosa ichidoga chakwe chuwe chikugutu yaleke kumwingha, uwendo we Mulungu ukwikala nhani umwakwe?
62003018	Wana wadodogi, chinghende kwa kulonga kwa mulomo du, ninaga kwa nhenda na kwa chawelu.
62003019	Kwa njila iyo chomanya fina aseye cha wachawelu, na kuwa chaka manhonge mufidoga fyetu kumwande yakwe
62003020	ugele wowose ifidoga fyetu nghona fikuchonesa wihi, kosoko iMulungu ni mukulu kusuma ifidoga fyetu na kumanya chila chinhu.
62003021	Wendigwa, nghona ifidoga fyetu fichikuchonesa china wihi, chikuwa chaka chinyala hamwande ye Mulungu;
62003022	na chikuhokela kulawa ukwakwe chochose chochikutasa, kosoko chikwandamila malagiso gakwe na kugolosa ifyene foyakwenda.
62003023	Na dino no dilagiso dyakwe, chidihuwile disina dye Mwanagwe Yesu Kilisito, na chikiyende fina foyachilagise.
62003024	Wose awakwandamila malagiso gakwe, wakwikala mugati yakwe, na imwene naye mugati yawo. Kwa njila iyo chimanya fina yakwikala mugati yetu, kwa njila ya Muhe woyachinghile.
62004001	Wendigwa, munghamuhuwile chila muhe, ninga igeseni imimuhe, kona nghona ni ya Mulungu; kosoko wagonesi wengi wo udasi wenela muchilunga.
62004002	Kwa njila ino mumanya Umuhe we Mulungu: Chila muhe uukufumila fina Yesu Kilisito keja mumutufi ni Muhe we Mulungu,
62004003	na chila muhe uukulema kufumila Yesu si wa Mulungu. Ayuno no Muhe iyakumulema Kilisito, womwahulike fina yakayokwija, na hambiya kafulusa kuwa muchilunga.
62004004	Wana wadodogi, anyeye mwa wa Mulungu, na muwasuma, kosoko ayuya iyowile kugati yenu ni mukulu kusuma yuya iyowile muchilunga.
62004005	Awene ni wanhu wa chilunga kosoko iyo sowakulonga ni sa chilunga na ichilunga chikuwategelesa.
62004006	Aseye cha wa Mulungu, wowose yamumanyile Mulungu yakuchitegelesa, ayuya isi wa Mulungu nghakuchitegelesa. Kwa njila iyo chikumanya muhe wa chawelu na muhe wo udasi.
62004007	Wendigwa, chikiyende; kosoko uwendo ni wa Mulungu.
62004008	Ayuya iyakwenda nhamumanyile Mulungu; kosoko Mulungu ni wendo.
62004009	Mu dino uwendo wa Mulungu wikigwa chalinje ukwetu, iMulungu kamwigala iMwanagwe we iwene, uleke chuwe womi mwi mwene.
62004010	Mu wendo uno, si fina hachimwenda Mulungu, ninga hakachenda seye na kumutuma iMwanagwe yowe no nhambiko yo uwihi wetu.
62004011	Wendigwa, iMulungu nghona yachendile nheifo; ase nase ikuchagila chikiyende.
62004012	Kwichaka munhu yamonile Mulungu; chinghakiyenda, iMulungu yakwikala kugati yetu na uwendo wakwe ukumemelekela umwetu.
62004013	Kwa njila ino chikumanya fina chikwikala kugati yakwe na imwene kugati yetu, kosoko kachingha umuhe wakwe imwecho.
62004014	Na chona kahi chikuhomelela fina iBaba kamwigala iMwanagwe kuwa muhonya we chilunga.
62004015	Wowose yakufumila fina iYesu ni Mwana wa Mulungu, iMulungu yakwikala mugati yakwe, na imwene mugati ya Mulungu.
62004016	Hambiya chimanya na kuhuwila uwendo woyenawo iMulungu ukwetu. Mulungu ni wendo, na yuya iyakwikala mu wendo yakwikala mwi Mulungu na iMulungu yakwikala mugati yakwe.
62004017	Mu dino uwendo wa Mulungu ukumemelesigwa ukwetu, uleke chuwe na usindamafu dijuwa dya ulamusi, kosoko fina foyowile nofochuwile aseye muchilunga.
62004018	Mu uwendo mwechaka woga, ninga uwendo umemelekele ukutanga kunje uwoga. Kosoko uwoga wina kuliganiswa, na wowose iyakogoha nghakangale mu wendo.
62004019	Chikwenda kosoko imwene hakakonga kuchenda seye.
62004020	Imunhu yanghagamba, “Nikumwenda Mulungu,” akuno yakumusula imunduguse imwene woyakumona, nghodaha kumwenda Mulungu wonghenati yamone.
62004021	Na dilagiso dino chenadyo kulawa ukwakwe, ayuya yekumwenda Mulungu yamwende ne munduguse naye.
62005001	Chila munhu iyakuhuwila fina Yesu no Kilisito ni mwana we Mulungu, na chila munhu iyakumwenda imweleka mwana, yakumwenda na imwana.
62005002	Kwa njila iyo chikumanya fina chikwenda wana we Mulungu, nghona chikumwenda Mulungu na kwandamila malagiso gakwe.
62005003	Kosoko auno no uwendo we Mulungu, nhafi chikwandamila amalagiso gakwe. Na malagiso si makugutu.
62005004	Kosoko chila yelekigwe ne Mulungu yakusuma ichilunga; na kuno nokusuma ichilunga, dihuwi dyetu.
62005005	No nani iyakusuma ichilunga ninga ayuya iyakuhuwila fina iYesu no Mwana wa Mulungu?
62005006	Ayuno no yuya iyejile kwa meji na kwa sakame, Yesu Kilisito si kwa meji muhala ninga ni kwa meji na kwa sakame.
62005007	Na Muhe no muhomelesi, kosoko Muhe no chawelu.
62005008	Kwina wahomelesi wadatu, u Muhe, ameji na kwa sakame; na wano wadatu wakifumilisa.
62005009	Nghona chikuhokela uhomelesi wa wanhu, uhomelesi we Mulungu ni Mukulu kusuma wose; auno no uhomelesi wa Mulungu woyahomelele muchanhya ye Mwanagwe.
62005010	Ayuya iyakuhuwila mwi mwana wa Mulungu kenawo uhomelesi uno umwakwe. Ayuya inghakumuhuwila Mulungu, kamugolosa Mulungu fina Mudasi kosoko nghauhuwile uhomelesi we Mulungu muchanhya ye Mwanagwe.
62005011	Na uno no uhomelesi, fina Mulungu kachingha uwumi wa majuwa gose, na uwumu uno wuwa mwi Mwanagwe.
62005012	Ayuya iyenaye iMwana kenawo uwumi; ayuya iyechaka iMwana we Mulungu kechaka uwumi.
62005013	Nikumwandililani sino anyeye mukuhuwila mudisina dye Mwana we Mulungu fina mwina wumi wa Majuwa gose,
62005014	Ayino no ng'inyo yochinayo umwakwe, fina chinghatasa chinhu chochose ifene foyakwenda imwene yakuchihulika.
62005015	Chinghamanya fina yakuchihulika mu gogose gochikumutasa, chimanya fina chihokela agaya gochimutasile.
62005016	Imunhu yanghamona imunduguse yakugolosa wihi iisikumwigala kudifa, kotasa, na Mulungu komwingha wumi kwa waya wakugolosa uwihi si we difa. Kwina wihi wa ifa; sikugamba fina imunhu yakudaha kutasa kosoko yo wihi wo.
62005017	Sinhenda sihile sose ni wihi, ninga kwina wihi uwene si wa ifa.
62005018	Chimanya fina chila munhu yelekigwe na Mulungu nghakugolosa wihi, ayuya yelekigwe na Mulungu yakumutasa, na yuya wo wihi nghakudaha kumukwafa.
62005019	Chimanya fina aseye cha wa Mulungu, na chilunga chose chuwa mu udaha wa yuya yehile.
62005020	Na chimanya fina iMwana we Mulungu keja na kachingha misungu, kumumanya ayuya we chawelu, iMwanagwe Yesu Kilisito. Imwene no Mulungu we chawelu na uwumi wa majuwa gose.
62005021	Wana wadodogi, munghandamile imilungu yo udasi.
63001001	Kulawa kwe musehe kwi Mudala na wanagwe wonikwenda lugano. Siyo andiye du ni mwene, ninga wose awaimanyile ichawelu wakumwendani,
63001002	kosoko ya ichawelu ikwikala umwetu nayo yokuwa hamwedu nase majuwa gose.
63001003	iMulungu Baba na Yesu Kilisito, iMwana wa Baba, yachinghe dihewa, ubasi na digoya, mu chawelu na uwendo.
63001004	Nikusekelela lugano kona fina awanago wamonga wakwikala mu chawelu, fina iBaba foyalagise.
63001005	Kosoko iyo nikukutasa gweye Mudala mwendigwa; chose chikiyende. Adino si ilagiso isha dyonikukwandikila ukwako; no dilagiso dyochowile nadyo kulawa kunghonga, chikiyende.
63001006	Uwendo uno wonikulonga ni chikale mukwandamila amalagiso ge Mulungu. Amalagiso ageno gomwahulike kulawa kunghonga ni fina mose mwikale mu uwendo.
63001007	Awadasi wengi wenela iisi yose, awanhu awasikufumila fina Yesu keja kwa mutufi wa chimunhu munhu wa nheifo ni mudasi na munghondo wa Kilisito.
63001008	Muwe meso, uleke munghagilise dyomugolosele milimo, ninga muhokele digelo dyenu dimemelekele.
63001009	Munhu wowose inghakwikala na mafuso ga Kilisito, ninga yakulokanisa, kechaka Mulungu. Wowose yuya yakwikala na mafuso gakwe kenawo wose iBaba na iMwana
63001010	Munhu wowose yanghakwijila inghekwigala amafuso gano, munghamuhokele musinyumba senu, kahi munghamulamuse;
63001011	kosoko munhu wowose yakumulamusa yakuwa miyagwe musinhenda sakwe sihile.
63001012	Ninago mengi ga kumwandikilani, nikona si fiswanu kumwandikilani kwa kalatasi na wino, ninga nikona nokwija nimwenyecho kumonani na kulonga nanye chimesomeso, uleke ichinyemi chetu chimemelesigwe.
63001013	Awana we lumbudyo musagulwa wakuwalamusani.
64001001	Kulawa kwe Musehe kwa mwendigwa Gayo, wonikwenda muchawelu
64001002	Mwendigwa, nikutasa Mulungu yakumotese kwa chila chinhu na uwe chaka matamu gogose; nimanya fina muchidoga chako mwina uswanu.
64001003	Kosoko hanisekelela lugano awandugu wamonga fowejile na kuhomelela ichawelu ya uwumi wako, fina chawelu foukwandamila ichawelu.
64001004	Kwechaka chinyemi chikulu fina chino, kukuhulika fina awanangu wakwandamila ichawelu.
64001005	Mwendigwa, ni mbuli ya ilumbo inhenda youkugolosa kuwatogomela awandugu, lugano, awageni,
64001006	awakuhomelela uwendo wako kwikanisa. Kogolosa fiswanu unghawatasa wagendelele munhambo yawo yo kumutogomela Mulungu.
64001007	Kosoko waleuka kukonga inhambo kahi wasihokele chochose kulawa kuwanhu awasikumuhuwila Mulungu.
64001008	Kwa nheifo ichagila kuwatasa fina wawo, uleke chuwe wayawo mumulimo we chawelu.
64001009	Niwandika chinhu chimonga kwi kanisa, ninga iDiyotelefe, iyekuhananga kwikusa kuwa chilongosi nghakufumila udaha wangu na ulongosi wangu,
64001010	Nghona nikwija nikwenda nike chalinje gose agene goyagolose na simbuli sihile soyagolose muchanhya yangu. Hamwedu na gago gose yakuwalemesa awaya awakwenda kuwahokela, na kuwawinga waleuke mwikanisa.
64001011	Mwendigwa, unghandamile gehile ninga wandamile amaswanu. Ayuya iyakugolosa maswanu ni wa Mulungu, iyakugolosa gehile nghamonile Mulungu.
64001012	Demeteliyo kena uhomelesi kulawa kwa chila munhu, na kulawa muchawelu iyenyecho, nikumuhomelela imwene kehi, na mumanya fina uhomelesi wangu wachawelu.
64001013	Hanuwa na mengi ga Kumwandikilani nyeye, ninga nikona fina ibeka ninghawandike na kalamu na wino;
64001014	Nikuhuwila kumonani chimwande, kahi chosimulila chimesomeso.
64001015	Digoya dyuwe nanye. Awambuya wakumulamusani. Walamuseni awambuya, chila yumwedu wenu.
65001001	Yuda mutogomi wa Yesu Kilisito na munduguse wa Yakobo, kwa wose wenangwe wendigwa mwi Mulungu iBaba na kudimigwa mu Yesu Kilisito.
65001002	Ubasi, dihewa na wendo wongeseke ukwenu.
65001003	Wendigwa fonahanangage lugano kuwaandikila imbuli ya uhonyi hanyona ihanangigwa niwaandikile kosoko ya dihuwi dilafigwe kuwasunhile wose.
65001004	Kosoko kwina wanhu wengisigwe kwa chifiso, wanhu waandikilwe uliganiso uno kulawa katali. Wanhu wasimumanyile iMulungu awakubidula imboto yuwe wihi na kumulema imwene mukulu Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito.
65001005	Hambiya nikuhananga nimugelegeseni hata inghowa hamufulusa kutamiligwa, fina ayuya iyawahonyile wanhu kulawa Muiisi ya Misili hakawakoma awaya awasamuhuwile.
65001006	Kahi malaika nawo awasakolile ahanhu hawo, ninga awalekile ukalo wawo wekigwa ne mwene muchifungo cha majuwa gose kuchisa na kuliganiswa mwijuwa dikulu.
65001007	No nheifo Sodoma na Gomola na makaya gasungulute fowagolosage gehile ge dihabwa kwandamila mutufi na kubidula uwunhu wawo nawo wekigwa muuliganiso lukulu we umoto wa majuwa gose.
65001008	Awano nawo nheifiya musinjosi sawo wakubana imitufi yawo, wakulema kulongosigwa na kuliga uswanu wakwe.
65001009	Ninga ichigele malaika mukulu Mikaeli fowakisumage na Luhoma wakuwanga kosoko yo umutufi wa Musa, nghendile kumusongesa kwa wihi ninga hakamugamba, “Mundewa na yakugombele!”
65001010	Ninga wanhu wano wakuliga finhu fofose fowasimanyile na kwa finhu fifo fowamanyile kwa misungu kifana makala ga kumbago gechaka misungu.
65001011	Usungu wawo! Kosoko wakugenda munjila ya Kaini, na kileusa awecho uleke wapate chinhu na kwagilila musinhenda sihile wihi wa Balamu uleke wapate na kwagilila munhenda sa kola.
65001012	Wanhu wano makala musisikukuu senu so uwendo nomo wakudiya nanyeye wechaka chogoho, wene wakifana wadimi awakidima awecho ni mafunde gechaka fula gakupululusigwa ne mheho, mabiki gechaka mamudyo, gofa mikangha mili na ninga gangholigwa kabisa;
65001013	Mawingo ga bahali gasikulongoseka, gakulafa chinyala chawo agecho kifana mafulo, nyelesi sikugendagenda sikiligwe dichisa kuwa nofugasi yawo.
65001014	No wawa walongigwe muugonesi wa Henoko we cheleko cha mutandatu kulawa Adamu yakugamba, “Langa Mundewa yakwija na figulu ikumi yakwe ye Musunhile wakwe,
65001015	uleke yagolose uliganiso kuwanhu wose, na kuwajama wose awasikumuhulika Mulungu kosoko ya nhenda sawo sikwagilisa na kosoko ya gose gehile ga awasikumuhulika Mulungu walongile muchanhya yakwe.”
65001016	Wanhu wano wakulonga mbuli chinyele na kukalala mbuli wakugenda kwa usulumisi wawo, Wakiyenda muluneka wawo. Majamo na Mafuso
65001017	Ninga nyeye, wendigwa wangu, mugelegele lugano agaya gomutamiligwe na watumigwa we Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito;
65001018	Kosoko hawawatamilani fina kumajuwa ge ndumo kwija kulawanisa wanhu wene kifana wano awakubesa na kwandamila usulumisi wawo wo kwagilisa
65001019	Wanhu wo wakwigala lutemanuko kahi ni wanhu we chilunga chino awechaka Muhe.
65001020	Ninga nyeye wendigwa wangu, kijengeni mwihuwi dyenu disunhile na kutasa mwi Muhe Musunhile.
65001021	Kaleni muwendo we Mulungu nomo mukugojela ubasi we Mundewa wetu Yesu Kilisito, na kupata uumi wa majuwa gose.
65001022	Woneleni ubasi awena manhonge;
65001023	Wahonyeni wamonga kwa kulafa mumoto na wamonga woneleni ubasi kwa kogoha na kudesekela hata isuke ichuchile mumutufi.
65001024	Imwene yakudaha kuwadima munghogwe na kuwemisani mwichaka wihi kumwande ye ditunyo dyakwe kwa chinyemi,
65001025	kwe Mulungu muhala iMwihula wetu kulokela Yesu Kilisito Mundewa wetu, Ditunyo dina imwene udaha, na uludole chigele chose hambiya na minyaka na minyaka. Hano.
66001001	Ugubulo waYesu Kilisito wo yenghigwe ne Mulungu konesa watogomi wakwe akakuhanangigwe gowe uko chimwande; hakagagolosa goneka kwa kumutuma malaika wakwe kwe mutumigwa wakwe Yohana,
66001002	imwene yahomelele imbuli ye Mulungu na kuuhomelesi wa Yesu Kilisito, na kwawaya wose woyonile.
66001003	Ibeka imunhu yuya iyakusoma simbuli so ugonesi wuno, kahi ibeka awakuhulika, na kukola agakuwandikigwa umo. Kosoko ugele wa habehi.
66001004	Yohana kumakanisa mufungate agowile ako Asia: Dihewa ukwenu ne digoya kulawa ukwakwe iyebaho, iyowile baho na iyekwija kahi kulawa kumimuhe mufungate wowile kumwande ye digoda dyakwe dye undewa,
66001005	na kulawa kwa Yesu Kilisito imuhomelesi we chawelu, imwelekigwa we inghonga wa wafile na mutawala wa wandewa wose we iisi. Ukwakwe imwene iyachendile na kuchilekelela na kuchisunha wihi wetu kwa sakame yakwe,
66001006	na kuchigolosa chuwe wandewa na makuhani watogomi we Mulungu wakwe na Baba, ukwakwe dyuwe itunyo na udaha majuwa gose. Hano.
66001007	Langa! Yakwija na mafunde; chila igiso dikwija dimona, hata awaya awamudomile; na makabila gose ge chilunga gokwijagalila kosoko yakwe kosoko nofoikwija ikuwa. Hano.
66001008	“Aniye no Alufa na Omega,” yakulonga Mundewa Mulungu, iyeuko na iyekwija, Iyene udaha wose.
66001009	Aniye Yohana, Mundugu senu iyekuhangila magayo muKilisito hamwedu nanye muundewa na ufinyilisi, hanuwa muchisiwa chikwinangwa Patimo kosoko ya imbuli ye Mulungu na uhomelesi wa Yesu.
66001010	Hanuwa mumuhe mwijuwa dye Mundewa, na hanihulika ijwi ikulu kunyuma yangu dikifana ijwi dya igunda
66001011	dikugamba, “Andika muchitabu goukona kamei ugegale kumakanisa mufungate kuile Efeso, Similina, Peligamu, Tilatila, Salidi, Filedefiya, na Laodikiya.”
66001012	Kamei honibiduka kulanga dijwi dilongile na niye, nikabiduke honikona figwaso fya kwikila taa mufungate fya sahabu,
66001013	na muchiligati che figwaso yumonga kifana mwana wa munhu kafala ikasu ijelu na mukowa wa sahabu kusunguluta muchifa chakwe;
66001014	Ditwi na sinjwili sakwe hasuwa njelu swee kifana pamba, na meso gakwe gakwakaika kifana ililimba dya moto
66001015	imigulu yakwe kifana shaba isunhugwe mumoto swanu lugano na dijwi dyakwe kifana ibumo dya meji mengi;
66001016	kakola nyelesi mufungate mumukono wakwe wo kulume, kumulomo wakwe kukulawa ipanga ikali dikutem kosekose, na ichihanga chakwe kifana dijuwa idikwakaika kwa singufu sakwe sose.
66001017	Nikamone honikugwa hamigulu yakwe kifana nufa. Ninga hoyonikola no mukono wakwe wo kulume, yakugamba, “Unghogohe; Aniye no we nghonga na we ndumiliso,
66001018	na ni mumu. Hanyufa, na langa, Namumi sakalakale, na nenaso sifunguo se Difa na se Kusimu.
66001019	Hambiya yandika gowonile, agebahano, na agakwenda galawanise hanyuma.
66001020	Agechifiso mu sinyelesi mufungate gowonile mumukono wangu wo kulume, na ifigwaso mufungate fye sitaa se sahabu, sinyelesi mufungate ni malaika na makanisa gaya mufungate na ifigwaso fiya mufungate ni makanisa gaya mufungate.”
66002001	“Kwimalaika wa Efeso wandika: Asino no simbuli sa yuya iyakolile sinyelesi mufungate mumukono wakwe wo kulume iyakugendagenda muchiligati che figwaso mufungate fye sitaa se sahabu:
66002002	Nimanya imilimo yako, kupiligala kwako na kufinyilisa kwako, na ninga nghukudaha kugendelela na wanhu wehile, ninga kuwagesa awaya wakiinanga watumigwa, ninga sichawelu na kuwatanga fina wadasi.
66002003	Kahi nimanya fina kwamufinyilisi kosoko ye disina dyangu na nghusokile.
66002004	Ninga nina nonga muchanhya yako gweye, kuleka wendo wowowile nawo kunghonga.
66002005	Gelegela ichikugwise, lamba na ugolose imilimo iya yowagolosage kunghonga, nghona sinheifo, nikukwijila na kuleusa ichigwaso che taa yako ahanhu hakwe unghaleka kulamba.
66002006	Achino chiswanu chowinacho ni fina nghukwenda imilimo ya Wanikolai, yene aniye nani sikuyenda.
66002007	Ayuya yene singhutwi yahulike, Imuhe foyakulonga kumakanisa. Kwayuya yakusuma nikumwingha kudiya kulawa mwibiki dyo uumi dyuwile kulanga kuswanu kwe Mulungu.”
66002008	“Na kwe malaika we dikanisa dyuwile Similina wandika: Asino ni nonga sakwe ye we bosi na we ndumo, iyafile na yenuke:
66002009	Nimanya amagayo gako na ukiwa wako, ninga kwa mugoli. Na nimanya amateto gawo waya wakigamba wene Wayahudi ninga siyo, ninga ni isinagogi dya Shetani.
66002010	Unghogohe amagayo agakukwijila chimwande, langa diluhoma dikwenda dimugumeni wamonga wenu mwigelesa na kwa majuwa ikumi mukuwa mumagayo, muwe wanhu we dihuwi mpaka kufa, nani nomwinghani ikofiya ye chindewa ye wumi, ya usumi wenhu.
66002011	Ayuya yena singhutwi yahulike iMuhe choyakulonga kumakanisa, ayuya yakusuma nghakwenda yabulagigwe ne difa dya keli.”
66002012	“Na kwamalaika we dikanisa dyuwile ako Peligamo wandika: Asino no simbuli sakwe imwene yene dipanga dikali dikutema akuno na kuno.
66002013	Nimanya houkwikala hedigoda dya Shetani. Nagwe kukolelela disina dyangu nghukanile dihuwi dyako ukwangu hata ugele wa Antipasi muhomelesi wangu, imuhuwilika wangu, yakomigwe mugati yenu, ahanhu hoyakwikala Shetani.
66002014	Ninga nina finhu fikefu fya kulonga muchanhya yako: Kwina wanhu baho awakolile mafuso ga Balaamu, iyamufusile Balaki kwigala chikwakwaliso kumwande ya waisilaeli, uleke wadiye fyakudiya filafigwe nhambiko kumasikimunhu, na kugolosa dihabwa.
66002015	Agwe nagwe kwinawo wamonga awakolile mafuuso ga wanikolao
66002016	Hambiya ulambe, amba unghaleka kulamba nikukwijila chimwande na kulewa nghondo nawo ne dipanga dye mulomo wangu.
66002017	Yene singhutwi yahulike Muhe foyakulonga nonga ino kumakanisa. Kwayuya iyakusuma nikumwingha imana ifisigwe, na nomwingha iwe ijelu, na isina disha diwandikigwe mudiwe na hechaka yadimanyile ninga imwene iyakudihokela.”
66002018	“Ku malaika we dikanisa dyuwile ako Siwatila wandika: Asino no simbuli se Mwana we Mulungu, iyena meso kifana ililimba dya moto, yena migulu kifana shaba isunhigwe, ikwakaika.
66002019	Nimanya imilimo yako ne migendelele yako na kufinyilisa kwako na fina milimo yako ye nyuma isuma iya ilongole.”
66002020	Ninga nina nonga muchanhya yako: “Ukugendelela kifinyilisa ne mwanamuke Yesebeli, iyekiinanga mugonesi iyakufusa na kuwagilisa watogomi wangu uleke wagolose dihabwa na kudiya fyakudiya fye nhambiko kufisikimunhu.
66002021	Hanimwingha chipisi uleke nghegela kolamba, ninga hoyolema kulamba dihabwa dyakwe.
66002022	Langa, nikwenda nimutage mwisasi, na wose awakugolosa dihabwa hamwedu naye nowaguma magayo makulu lugano, inghowa wasikulamba sinhenda sakwe.
66002023	Na nikwenda niwatowe na kuwakoma awanangwe. Na makanisa gose gomanya fina aniye noniimanyile imisungu kahi nonikumulika mbuli se mimoyo ya wanhu, na kumuliha chila munhu foifane milimo yakwe.”
66002024	Ninga kwa nyenye musigale ako Siwatila, anyeye musikolile amafuso gago, musikifusile wamonga gowakugamba, “Nni mafuso ga kugati lugano ga Shetani,” ukwenu nyeye nikugamba sikumwikilani musigo wingi.
66002025	mukolelese chomwinacho hata ugele fonikwija.
66002026	Ayuya yakusuma na yakolile milimo yangu, mpaka kukumalagisa, nikwenda nimwinghi udaha muchanhya ya mataifa;
66002027	kulongosa kwa mhando ya chuma, fina sinyungu sa ulongo fosikutulika.
66002028	Fina niye fonihokele udaha kulawa kwa Baba. Ayuya yakusuma nomwingha Inyelesi ya nhousikusiku.
66002029	Ayuya yena singhutwi yahulike iMuhe foyakulonga kumakanisa.
66003001	“Na kwa malaika we dikanisa dya Salidi wandika: Imbuli ya yuya yena imimuhe mufungate ye Mulungu ne sinyelesi mufungate, nimanya imilimo yako kwina isina dya uwumi, ninga gweye kufa.
66003002	Inuka kulafa mudifa, guma ludole mumilimo ihabehi kufa, kosoko sonile fina imilimo yako imemelekela hameso ge Mulungu wangu.
66003003	Gelegela sowahulike na sowahokele sikole na ulambe, unghaleka kwinuka nikukwijila kifana muhiji, na nghukwenda umanye chigele chinikwija.
66003004	Ninga kwinawo wanhu wakefu ako Salidi, awasichuchise sisuke sawo na wagenda hamwedu na niye, wafala suse sinjelu, kosoko wagiligwa.
66003005	Ayuya yakusuma yakwenda yafasigwe suke njelu, na sikuleusa disina dyakwe muchitabu cho uwumi, nikwenda nihomelele disina dyakwe kwa Baba na malaika wakwe.
66003006	Ayuya yena singhutwi yahulike iMuhe choyakulonga.”
66003007	“Na kwa malaika we dikanisa dyuwile ako Filedefiya wandika: Simbuli se Imusunhile iyena ifunguwo ya Daudi yekukumula na hechaka yakudaha kuhinda, na yakuhinda kahi hechaka yakudaha kukumula.
66003008	Nimanya imilimo yako, langa nikwingha mulango ukumuligwe, na hechaka munhu yakudaha kuhinda, nimanya fina kwina ludole ludodogi, hata nheifo kukola imbuli yangu na nghukanile disina dyangu.
66003009	Langa nikwenda niwagolose awaya we disinagogi dya Shetani awakigamba fina Wayahudi, kumbe si chawelu ninga wekudanha, langa nikwenda niwegale na wafugame hamigulu yako, na wakifuse fina nikukwenda gweye.
66003010	Kosoko kuikola imbuli yangu kwa kufinyilisa, ani nani nikwenda nikukolelese ugele wa magayo agakwija muisi, kuwagesa awaya awekale muchilunga.
66003011	Nikwija chimwande, chikolelese chowinacho uleke munhu wowose yangheje yalonde inghofiya yako ye chindewa yo kusuma.
66003012	Ayuya yekusuma, nikumugolosa sumbi mdihekalu dye Mulungu wangu, nghakulawa, kahi nghakulawa umo ugele wose na niwandika umwakwe disina dye Mulungu wangu na dye ikaya ye Mulungu, Yelusalemu Nyisha, ikulawa kuchanhya kwe Mulungu wangu na disina dyangu disha nimwecho.
66003013	Ayuya yena singhutwi na yahulike ifene Muhe foyakulonga kumakanisa.”
66003014	“Na kwa malaika we dikanisa dyuwile ako Laodikiya wandika: Simbuli sa Hano, imuchawelu na muhomelesi iyakuhuwilika, inghonga ye kumba kwe Mulungu.
66003015	Nimanya imilimo yako, nghwi mheho, kahi nghwi moto, ibeka hegu we mheho ama wi moto.
66003016	Hambiya kosoko, kwa lufufunghonde, nghwi mheho kahi nghwi moto nikwenda nikudeke kulawa kumulomo wangu.
66003017	Kosoko ukugamba aniye na mugoli, nichaka chinhu chonikuhananga; nghumanyile fina kwichaka chochose, kwa munhu wakoneligwa ubasi kwa mukiwa, kahi kwa mudula n akwa mwasi.
66003018	Ani nikukusugula ugule ukwangu, shabu isunhigwe ne moto uleke uwe mugoli na ufale suke njelu na kukuleusila chinyala chokuwa mwasi kwako koneka na kukubaka miti mumeso gako udahe kona.
66003019	Awaya wonikuwenda nikuwagombela na kuwatosa kosoko iyo upiligale na kulamba.
66003020	Langa nikwima hamulango na kugong'onda, imunhu wowose yakuhulika dijwi dyangu na kukumula umulango nikwingila ukwakwe na kudiya hamwedu naye imwene naye hamwedu na niye
66003021	Ayuya yakusuma, nikwikala naye mwigoda dyangu dya undewa, fina aniye fonasumile na kwikala hamwedu ne Baba mwigoda dyakwe dya undewa.
66003022	Ayuya yena singhutwi so kuhulika na yahulike iMuhe choyakulong kumakanisa.”
66004001	Sikaloke sino hanilanga, kumbe umulango wa kulanga hougubuka, idijwi dye nghonga dyonahulike dikulonga na niye dikifana igunda, dikugamba, “Wije kuno nikwenda nikonese agakwenda galawanise kulawa agano”
66004002	Chimwande hanuwa Mumuhe, kumbe kulanga kwikigwa igoda dye chindewa, na yumonga yekale umo.
66004003	Ayuya yekale umo koneka kifana alimasi, na diwe didunghu diswanu, na digoda dye undewa disungulutigwa na diwuta dye ifula difanile diwe dya alimasi dikwakaika.
66004004	Kusunguluta digoda dye undewa kwina magoda ge undewa makumi meli na mane na wekale mumagoda gago wasehe makumi meli na wane, wafasigwa makasu majelu na nghofiya sa chindewa sa sahabu mumatwi gawo.
66004005	Kulawa kwigoda dye undewa kwina fimuli fya ujelu na majwi na dibumo ikulu na kumwande ye digoda dye chindewa kwina fimuli mufungate fikumulikamulika moto imumuhe mufungate ye Mulungu,
66004006	kahi kumwande ye digoda dye undewa kwina chinhu chifanile bahali ya chikombe cha chiyoo, hameso ikoneka kifana meji gagandile na kusunguluta digoda dyo undewa chila ulwandi kwina fiyumbe fyumi fina meso kumwande na kunyuma:
66004007	chiyumbe che nghonga chakifana simba, ichiyumbe cha keli ichumi chakifana nghambaku ya ng'ombe, ichuyumbe cha kadatu china chihanga cha munhu ne chiyumbe cha kane chikifana numba ikupululuka.
66004008	Na ifyumbe fiya fine chila chimwedu china mabawa mutandatu fimema meso kunje na kugati na fisikuleka kwimba misi na chilo, kugamba, “Musunhile, musunhile, musunhile, ni Mundewa Mulungu wetu yena udaha wose, yowile baho, iyebaho na yekwija.”
66004009	Na chila ugele ifyumbe ifyumi fiya fikulafa ditunyo na chogoho kugamba, kwimange kwa ayuya yekale mwigoda dya undewa iyakwikala majuwa gose,
66004010	awaya wasehe makumi meli na wane wakugwa kumwande yakwe ayuya yekale mwigoda na kumufuga ayuya iyakwikala majuwa gose, aku wakutaga singhofiya sawo kumwande ye digoda dyo undewa na kwimba,
66004011	“Kwagiligwa gweye Mundewa na Mulungu wetu, kuhokela ditunyo na ukulu na udaha, kosoko gweye no wumbile ifinhu fyose na kwa kwenda kwako fyabaho na hafyumbigwa.”
66005001	Hanyona mumukono wa kulume wa yuya yekale mwigoda dye chindewa chitabu chiwandikigwe kunje na kugati nacho chohigwa na fikanhamiso mufungate;
66005002	Na honimona malaika mukulu yakulonga kwa ijwi ikulu kugamba, “Nona yagile kuchigubula ichitabu na kubena fikanhamiso fyakwe?”
66005003	Nhoneke hata yumwedu kulanga na hasi ye siisi yadahile kuchigubula ichitabu ama kuchilanga.
66005004	Honililila lugano kosoko nghoneke munhu wowose yawagilwe kuchigubula ama kuchilanga.
66005005	Yumonga wa wasehe hoyonigamba, “Unghalile Simba we dikabila dya Yuda Ulukolo lwa Daudi kasuma kosoko iyo yakudaha kuchigubula ichitabu na kufibena ifikanhamiso fyakwe.”
66005006	Hagati ye digoda dye undewa na fiya ifiyumbe fyumi mugati ya wasehe, honikona Mwana ngholo yemile kifana kachinjigwa kena mahembe mufungate na meso mufungate, isene so no mimuhe mufungate ye Mulungu itumigwe muchilunga chose.
66005007	Hakaluta na kuchilonda achiya ichitabu kulawa mumukono wo kulume wa yuya yekale mwigoda dye undewa.
66005008	Yakafuluse kuchilonda ichitabu ifiyumbe ifine na waya wasehe makumi na wane howomugwila yuya Mwana ngholo, chila yumwedu kakola ibwalimbwa na mabakuli ge sahabu gamemila ufumba na kutasa kwa wasunhile.
66005009	Wakwimba lwimbo lusha wakugamba: “Kwagiligwa agweye kulonda ichitabu na kubena ifikanhamiso fyakwe, kosoko agweye hakuchinjigwa na kwa sakame yako kuwagula wanhu wowe wa Mulungu, wanhu kulawa chila ikabila, nonga na mataifa gose;
66005010	na kuwagolosa wowe wandewa na makuhani wakutogoma kwe Mulungu wetu, na wakwenda watawale muchilunga.”
66005011	Kamei honilanga na kuhulika ijwi dya malaika matewa wakusunguluta digoda dye undewa na fiya fiyumbe ifyumi na wasehe; wasikudaha kutalika, figulu na figulu,
66005012	wakwimba kwa ijwi dya muchanhya lugano, “Kagiligwa Imwana ngholo iyachinjigwe kuhokela udaha na ugoli na ubala na kusuma chogoho na itunyo na mboto!”
66005013	Hanihulika chila chiyumbe kulanga na hasi ye iisi hata kubahali kose uko fikugamba, “Kwayuyo yekale mwigoda dye chindewa na kwe Mwana ngholo yuwe mboto na chogoho na itunyo na ludole majuwa gose hano!”
66005014	Kamei ifiyumbe fiya fine hofigamba, “Hano!” Kamei na wasehe wakugwa hasi na kufuga.
66006001	Kamei honikona Mwana ngholo yakukubula chimwedu che fikanhamiso mufungate, na kuhulika yumwedu wa fiyumbe ifine yakwinanga kwa ijwi ikulu ijwi kifa dya ibumo, “Wije!”
66006002	Na honikona langa falasi njelu, na iyasikwilile kena uta na kofiya ye chindewa yoyenghigwe hoyoluta kuchilunga na kosoko ya kusuma kwakwe na kusuma kahi.
66006003	Kahi foyagubule chikanhamiso cha keli hanimuhulika ichuyumbe ichumi cha keli, chikugamba, “Wije!”
66006004	Hoikwija falasi ingi ndunghu gu, iyakwilile hakenghigwa udaha wa kuleusa idigoya muchilunga, uleke awanhu wakikome chila munhu na miyagwe, hakenghigwa ipanga ikulu.
66006005	Yakakumule ichikanhamiso cha kadatu, hanihulika chiyumbe cha kadatu chikwinanga kwa ijwi ikulu, “Wije!” Hanilanga na kona Falasi ingi nhitu imunhu yakwilile hakowa na misani ya kupimila mumikono yakwe.
66006006	Kahi hanihulika chinhu kifana ijwi mugati ye fiyumbe fyumi ifine, ikugamba, “Chibaba chimwedu che usage we ngano kwa dinali na fibaba fidatu fye usage we shaili kwa dinali, ninga wanghabane mafuta ne difayi.”
66006007	Yakakumule ichikanhamiso cha kadatu, hanihulika dijwi dye chiyumbe china wumi cha kane chikugamba, “Wije!”
66006008	Honikona langa, ifalasi ina langi ya difu, ayuya yakwilile, yakwinangwa ifa na kusimu kukumwandamila hoyokwinghigwa udaha mulobo imwedu ye chilunga, kukoma kwa ipanga na njala na kwa matamu na kwa makala ge muchilunga,.
66006009	Yakakumule, ichikanhamiso cha shano, honikona hasi ye hefugilo fidoga fyawo wanhu wakomigwe kosoko ye imbuli ye Mulungu na uhomelesi wawo wowalongile,
66006010	howojoja kwa ijwi ikulu, “Agwe go Mundewa Mukulu musunhile na we chawelu, mpaka milaki ukuchiliganisa na kuwaliha chisasi che sakame yetu muchanhya ya wekale muchilunga?”
66006011	Kamei chila yumwedu hakenghigwa nghasu njelu na kugambigwa wagojele chidodogi, mpaka ifike inhala ya wayawo watumigwa fina wene, yuwe imemelekela, awene awakwenda wakomigwe fina awene fowakomigwe.
66006012	Yakakumule ichikanhamiso cha mutandatu, hanilanga na kona, isingisi ikulu na dijuwa hodikuwa ititu kifana iguniya, umwesi wose houkuwa kifana sakame.
66006013	Na sinyelesi sa kulanga hosilagala hasi fina umukuyu foukulagasa singhuyu sisikangale maukusingisigwa na uluputa lwa imheho ikupumunha ugele we inyota.
66006014	Ulanga haukikunja kifana kalatasi, na chila itunda na chisiwa hafileusigwa ahanhu hawo.
66006015	Kamei awandewa we chilunga awanhu wakulu na wakulu we selikali na wagoli na wena ludole na chila munhu mutumwa na isimutumwa, wakifisa mumapango na mumawe ga matunda
66006016	wakugamba amatunda na mawe, “Chugwileni ma muchifise kumwande ye chihanga chakwe ayuya yekale mwigoda dya undewa na inyono ye Mwana ngholo;
66006017	kosoko dijuwa dikulu dye inyono yawo difika nani yakwenda yadahe kwima hamwande yakwe?”
66007001	Ichinhu chandamile chonyonile hachuwa malaika wane wemile kulwandi sose ine se chilunga, waikolelese imheho inghapumunhe muchilunga na mubahali na mumabiki.
66007002	Honikona malaika yungi kulawa kulwandi we dijuwa kena chikanhamiso che Mulungu imumi. Hoyokwinanga kwa ijwi ikulu kumalaika awaya wane awenghigwe udaha wo kubana iisi ne bahali,
66007003	wakugamba, “Munghabane iisi hegu ibahali hegu mabiki, mpaka niwagume ifitangilo fye fikanhamiso awatumigwa we Mulungu mufihanga fyawo.”
66007004	Honihulika ihesabu yawo waya wagumigwe ifitangilo fye fikanhamiso, figulu makumi mane na wane kulawa chila ikabila dya wana wa Isilaeli:
66007005	Kulawa mwikabila dya Yuda wagumigwe chitangilo wanhu figulu ikumi na fili, mwikabila dya Leubeni figulu ikumi na fili, kulawa mwikabila dya Gadi figulu ikumi na fili,
66007006	kulawa mwikabila dya Asheli figulu ikumi na fili, dikabila dya Nafutali figulu ikumi na fili, dikabila dya manase figulu kumi na fili,
66007007	kulawa mwikabila dya Simionifigulu ikumi na fili. Mwikabila dya Lawi figulu ikumi na fili. Mwikabila dya Isakali figulu ikumi na fili,
66007008	kulawa mwikabila dya Sabuloni figulu ikumi na fili, kulawa mwikabila dya Yusufu figulu ikumi na fili na mwikabila dya Benyamini figulu ikumi na fili wagumigwe chitangilo
66007009	Chikaloke chino hanilanga ditewa dya wanhu awasikudaha kutalika fonu wengi, kulawa chila itaifa na makabila gose na kumwande ya digoda dya undewa na kumwande ye Mwana ngholo, wafasigwa nghasu njelu swee na matambi ge mitende mumikono yawo.
66007010	Kujoja kwa ijwi ikulu kugamba, “Uhonya uwa kwe Mulungu wetu yekale mwigoda dya undewa we kwe Mwana ngholo!”
66007011	Kamei malaika wose howokwima kusunguluta digoda dye undewa na wasehe ne fiyumbe fyose, howokugwa chifunhifunhi na kumufuga Mulungu,
66007012	wakwimba kugamba, “Hano! Imboto na ditunyo na ubala na malumbo na chogoho na uludole na udaha uwe ukwako Mulungu wetu wa majuwa gose! Hano.”
66007013	Kamei yumwedu wa wasehe hoyolonga na niye yakugamba, “Awano chenani woukona wafalile makasu majelu kahi walawa hoki?”
66007014	Honimugamba, “Mukulu kumanya gweye.” Kamei hoyonigamba, “Awano nowaya walawile mumagayo makulu lugano, wafuwa singhasu sawo na kusigolosa suwe njelu musakame ye Mwana we ngholo.
66007015	Kosoko iyo wowe kumwande ye digoda dyo undewa dye Mulungu, na wakumutogomela chilo ne imisi mwi hekalu dyakwe na yuyo yekale mwigoda dya undewa yakuwagubika na nyuwa yakwe baho.
66007016	Wasikuwa na njala kahi nghilu, dijuwa disikwenda diwasome, hegu kuwalakasa;
66007017	kosoko Mwana we ngholo yakuwa muchiligati ye digoda dyo undewa na kuwa mudimi wawo, naye kowalongosa kusinhyoko sa meji ga uwumi na Mulungu yakwenda yawahamuse chila isosi mumeso gawo.”
66008001	Ugele Mwana ngholo yakagubule ichikanhamiso che mufungate, kulanga hakunyamala posi kwa chigele cha nusu saa.
66008002	Kamei honikona malaika mufungate awakwima kumwande ye Mulungu, howokwinghigwa magunda mufungate.
66008003	Malaika yumonga kena chiya cho kusomela ubani cha sahabu na kwima hefugilo, hakenghigwa ubani mwingi yalafe hamwedu na mataso ge wasunhile wose, hamwande ye difugilo diya dye sahabu dyuwile hamwande ye digoda dyo undewa.
66008004	Kamei umosi wo ubani uya houkwila hamwedu na mataso ga wasunhile mpaka hamwande ye Mulungu kulawa mumukono wa yuya malaika.
66008005	Kahi malaika hakalonda ichiya cho kusomela ubani na hoyochimemesa, kamei moto kulawa hefugilo na kuukubita kuchilunga, hukukuwa na kudidima, chowe, imwemwe kupulika na disingisi dye chilunga
66008006	Kamei malaika mufungate awile na magunda mufungate howokonga kuyatowa magunda gawo.
66008007	Imalaika we nghonga hoyotowa digunda dyakwe kame haitonya fula ya mawe na moto ihasile ne sakame, hoitonya muchilunga kamei isehemu inghulu ye chilunga hailakala, na ulwandi lwa mabiki gago hogatikitila, ne nyasi yose ikwani hoyilakala fibi.
66008008	Imalaika wa keli hakatowa naye digunda dyakwe kamei hachilawanisa chinhu, kifana itunda ikulu dikwaka moto, hodikubitigwa kubahali.
66008009	hayuwa sakame mubahali kalibu fiyumbe fyose ifyumi mubahali hofikufa na simeli sose hasibanika.
66008010	Imalaika wa kadatu hakatowa naye digunda dyakwe, kamei, dinyelesi ikulu hadalagala kulawa kulanga dikwaka kifana imuli, hadilagala kalibu musisanda sose ne sinhyoko sa meji.
66008011	Disina dye dinyelesi diya ni Sungwi. Ameji kalibu gose hogagaluka sungwi na wengi howokufa kosoko ya meji gago kosoko hagowa ga usungu lugano.
66008012	Imalaika wa kane hakatowa naye digunda dyakwe, isehemu yose ye dijuwa haibanigwa ne mwesi wose ne sinyelesi, kamei fyose hofititihala, na imisi hoikuwa chilo.
66008013	Kamei hanilanga na kuhulika inumba dikulapa kwa ijwi ikulu ugele fodyapululukage mulanga dikugamba, “Usungu, usungu, usungu lugano kwa waya wekale muchilunga nemamagunda gamonga agehabehi kutoigwa nawaya malaika wadatu awasigale!”
66009001	Kamei malaika wa shano hakatowa naye digunda dyakwe, hanyona nyelesi ikulagala kulawa kulanga mpaka hasi, kamei hoikwinghigwa ifunguwo ikukumula dikolongo dya kusimu;
66009002	yakadikumule dikolongo diya, hakulawa mosi ukifane mosi wa ililimba dya moto kamei idijuwa ne ujelu we iisi hofititihala kosoko ya umosi.
66009003	Kamei kulawa muumosi uwo hakulawa sige muchilunga, sige siya hasinghigwa ludole kifana chisuswe.
66009004	Hosigambigwa singhabane imbago hegu chinhu chochose, ama mabiki ninga awanhu waya wechaka ichitangilo che chikanhamiso che Mulungu mufihanga fyawo.
66009005	Hasigambigwa siwasambase kwa chigele cha minyesi mishano, ninga singahwakome, usungu wakwe hawuwa kifana usungu wa munhu yalumigwe ne chisuswe.
66009006	Na ugele wa majuwa gago gose wohananga difa ninga wasikudipata, wosulumila wafe ninga difa dikwenda diwatije.
66009007	Na koneka kwawo sige siya sakifana falasi sikuluta kunghondo, mumatwi gawo sifala finhu kifana kofiya sa undewa sa sahabu, ifihanga fyawo fya kifana wanhu.
66009008	ubahila wawo wakifana njwili sa wanawake na meno gawo kifana ga simba;
66009009	hawowa na misani ikifane ngulo ya chuma mufiya fyawo, na ichowe che mabawa gawo hachuwa kifana chowe cha matuka mengi agekukwegigwa na falasi sikubilimila kunghondo.
66009010	Sina mikila kifana fisuswe, na ikuluma kahi ina uludole lwa kuwagaisa wanhu kwa minyesi mishano wowe mumikila yawo.
66009011	Wenaye mundewa wawo imalaika we dikolongo dye kusimu; disina dyakwe kwa Chiyebulaniya yakwinagwa Abadoni na Chiyunani yakwinangwa Apoliyoni.
66009012	Usungu we nghonga uloka, langa sikaili sungu mbili sikwija.
66009013	Kamei imalaika we mutandatu hoyotowa naye digunda dyakwe, hanihulika ijwi ikulu kulawa msimhembe ine se difugilo dye sahabu dyuwile hamwande ye Mulungu,
66009014	dikugamba, imalaika we mutandatu iyowile ne digunda, “Walekele amalaika wane wohigwe kulwanda uya mukulu lwa Fulati.”
66009015	Kamei malaika waya wane howalekeligwa, awafuluse kwikigwa kosoko ye chipisi, dijuwa, na mwesi, na mwaka, wakome cheleko kalibu chose cha wanhu.
66009016	Ihesabu ya awasilikali wakwilile sifalasi hayuwa; miliyoni magana meli, honihulika ihesabu yawo.
66009017	Nhafi nofonyonile sifalasi munyona yangu: Awapandile wafala mufifa fyawo ngulo se chuma sina langi ndunghu kifana moto, fikifane mawe ga ugoli mwingi, na matwi ge sifalasi siso gakifana matwi ga simba, na mumilomo yawo kukulawa moto na mosi kifana wa chibiliti.
66009018	Kwa magayo gano madatu sehemu nghulu ya wanhu haikomigwa, kwa umoto na umosi na chibiliti fikulawa kumilomo ye sifalasi siso.
66009019	Kosoko uludole lwe sifalasi luwa mumilomo yawo na mumikila yawo, imikila yawo ikifana majoka gena matwi na kwa matwi gawo gago gakubulaga.
66009020	Awanhu wasigale awasikomigwe ne mafa gago nowaya wasalambile imilimo yawo ye mikono yawo kahi kufuga simhepo ne milungu ye sahabu ne pesa na shaba na mawe na mabiki, iyene isikona hegu kuhulika, ama kugenda;
66009021	wasalambile, kukoma kwawo, ninga hata uhayi wawo na dihabwa dyawo na uhiji wawo.
66010001	Kahi hanyona malaika yungi wa ludole yakwija kulawa kulanga kafala difunde; ne diwuta dye ifula muchanhya ye ditwi dyakwe, na ichihanga chakwe hachuwa kifana ijuwa ne imigulu yakwe kifana sumbi sa moto.
66010002	Na mumukono wakwe hakowa na chitabu chidodogi, na hakajata umugulu wakwe wo kulume mubahali na umugulu wakwe wo kumoso muulongo kunje ye bahali,
66010003	hoyokwinanga kwa ijwi ikulu kifana disimba dikubuluma, yakenange imibumo mufungate hoihulikika.
66010004	kamei ikahulikike iya mibumo mufungate, nendenihananga niwandike, kamei hanihulika kahi ijwi kulwa kulanga dikugamba, “Kanhamisa ifikanhamiso fyako, isimbuli silongigwe ne mibumo unghawandike.”
66010005	Na imalaika yuya wonyonile yajatile mugulu umonga mubahali umonga muulongo kunje ye bahali, hakenula umukono wakwe wo kulume kulanga
66010006	na kilaha kwa yuya imumi wa majuwa gose yombile ulanga na fyose fyuwile muchilungana mubahali na fyose kahi fuwile umo, yakugamba, “Kunghowe na kusululuka,
66010007	ninga ugele wa majuwa go kutoigwa digunda na malaika mufungate, ichifiso che Mulungu chomemelekela, fina foyalongile kuwagonesi wakwe.”
66010008	Kahi ijwi, hanidihulika kulawa kulanga, dikunigamba, keli, gamba, “Luta londa ichitabu chigubuligwe mumukono we Malaika yuya yemile mugulu umonga mubahali na umonga kunje ye bahali.”
66010009	Kamei hanimulutila imalaika na kumugamba yaninghe chitabu chiya; naye hoyonigamba, “Chilonde na uchidiye, chokuwa chausungu kunda, ninga chamulile kifana uki mumulomo wako.”
66010010	Kamei honilonda kulawa mumukono we malaika ichitabu chiya, na kuchidiya, chawelu hachuwa chamulile hamulomo kifana uki, ninga nikamale kudiya kunda hakuwa kwausungu kifana sungwi.
66010011	Kamei hawanigamba, “Hambiya ukonge kugonesa lwa keli, muchanhya ye wanhu matewa na mataifa, ne sinonga kahi na wandewa.”
66011001	Kamei honikwinghigwa chibiki cha kupimila chikifana mhando, honigambigwa, “Wije na upime dihekalu dye Mulungu ne difugilo na wose awakufuga umo,
66011002	ninga unghapime dikumbo kunje ye dihekalu kosoko dyo dinghigwa awamataifa wakwenda waijate ikaya isunhile kwa minyesi makumi na mane na meli.
66011003	Nikwenda niwenghe wahomelesi weli udaha wo kutamila, chigele cha minyaka chigulu chimwedu magana meli naminyesi mutandatu wafalile maguniya.”
66011004	Agano no mabiki meli ge miseituni na figwaso fili fye sitaa fimile kumwande ye Mundewa we isi.
66011005	Na munhu wowose yanghenda kuwabulaga, moto kulawa mumilomo yawo ukuwalakasa awanghondo wawo; na wowose iyewakoma nhafo nofoyakwenda yatendigwe.
66011006	Wena udaha kuhinda ulanga, ifula inghatonye, uleke kunghowe na fula nomowakugonesa, kahi wena udaha muchanhya ya meji, kugabidula gowe sakame, na kuibulaga dunia na matamu fina fowakwenda.
66011007	Fowakumala uhomelesi wawo, dikala dkwenda dije kulawa kwikolongo dya kusimu na kulewa nghondo na kuwasuma na hata kuwakoma,
66011008	na mitufi yawo ikutagigwa munje mudikaya diya dikulu idifane Sodoma na Misili kwa chimuhe, ahanhu Mundewa wawo hoyasambasigwe.
66011009	Kwa chigele cha majuwa madatu na nusu, wandugu we wawo wafile, na makabila na chila nonga na mataifa wolanga mifimba yawo na kulema kuwasika;
66011010	na wakaya we chilunga wobwedelela kosoko yawo kwa chinyemi na kiingha fipengwa kosoko awaya wagonesi wawagaisa wanhu we chilunga.
66011011	Ninga gakaloke majuwa madatu, muhe wa Mulungu wija uwengila, na howokwima kwa migulu yawo, wanhu wawonile hawakolwa na itisi lugano.
66011012	Kamei hawahulika ijwi ikulu kulawa kulanga dikugamba, “Kwileni kuno!” Howokwila kulanga mwifunde chigele cho awanghondo wawo wakuwalanga.
66011013	Muchigele chicho hakuwa na isingisi dya chilunga, iisi na wasigale howokogoha na kumwingha itunyo Mulungu wa kulanga.
66011014	Usungu wa keli uloka. Usungu wa kadatu ukwija chimwande.
66011015	Kamei malaika wa mufungate katowa naye digunda dyakwe, hakuwa na ijwi ikulu kulanga, dikugamba, “Undewa we chilunga ungaluka ndewa wa Mundewa wetu ne Masihi wakwe, naye kulongosa minyaka kwa minyaka.”
66011016	Kamei wasehe waya makumi meli na wane awakwima hegoda dye undewa hamwande ye Mulungu wogwa wose hasi na kumufuga Mulungu,
66011017	wakwimba nhafi, “Chikukwingha malumbo, Mundewa Mulungu Mukulu, uwowile uko kahi ukwija kosoko kuulonda udaha wako mukulu kahi hakukonga kudima.
66011018	Amataifa hagadeseka, ninga nyono yako ija, na chigele cha kuwaliganisa wafile, kwa kuwaliha awatogomi wako na wagonesi na wasunhile na wose wendewogoha disina dyako, wose wakulu kwa wadodogi, na kuwabulaga waya awabulage ichilunga.”
66011019	Kamei dihekalu dye Mulungu kulanga hodikumuka kumu! Kamei disafina dye dilagano dyakwe hadyoneka mugati ye dihekalu; kahi hakuwa na fimuli fikumulika, na majwi kudidima, ne dimasingisa, na fula nghulu ya mawe.
66012001	Kahi chitangilo chikulu hachoneka, langa mwanamuke yafalile idijuwa na umwesi hasi ye migulu yakwe na mwitwi dyakwe nghofiya ina nyelesi ikumi na na mbili,
66012002	hakowa na inda na kosoko ya usungu umukali wo kidohola hakalila lugano.
66012003	Na chitangilo chingi hochikoneka kulanga, langa hakuwa na ijoka ikulu idunghu dina matwi mufungate na mahembe ikumi gena kofiya sa chindewa mufungate mwitwi dyakwe,
66012004	umukila wakwe houkwelegeta kalibu sinyelesi sose sa kulanga na kusilagasa hasi, na dijoka diya hadima habehi ne mwanamuke yuya yowile habehi na kweleka uleke dichimese ichali.
66012005	Mwanamuke yuya hakakidohola mwana wa chigosi, imwene iyakwenda yadime na kulongosa amataifa gose ne mhando ye chuma, kamei imwanagwe yuya hoyokwinuligwa mpaka kulanga kudigoda dye Mulungu.
66012006	Mwanamuke hakatijila kunyika kuwile na hanhu hekigwe ne Mulungu, nghakwinghigwa chakudiya kwa majuwa chigulu chimwedu na magana meli na makumi mutandatu.
66012007	Hambiya, inghondo haikonga kulanga, Mikaeli na malaika wakwe, wakulewa ne dijoka, nadyo dijoka nadyo na malaika sakwe hodilewa nawo nghondo. Ninga dijoka na wayagwe howotoigwa lugano,
66012008	kahi hawasumwa, na hakuwa kwichaka luneka kwa wene kahi kwikala kulanga.
66012009	Idijoka diya dikulu haditagigwa hasi, dijoka dya katali, dikwinagwa Luhoma na Shetani, imudasi we chilunga chose, hoyotagwa hasi kuchilunga, na malaika sakwe hamwedu naye.
66012010	Kamei hanihulika ijwi ikulu kulanga, dikugamba, “Hambiya uhonya ne ludole fija ne undewa we Mulungu wetu na udaha we Masihi wakwe, kosoko imusongesi we wandugu setu katagigwa hasi, iyendeyawasongesa misi na chilo hamwande ye Mulungu wetu.
66012011	Ninga howomusuma kwa sakame ye Mwanangholo na kwa mbuli ya uhomelesi wawo, kosoko hawendile nyikala yawo mpaka kufa.
66012012	Bwedeleleni hambiya, anyeye ulanga na waya wakwikala umo! Ninga usungu kwichilunga ne mubahali, kosoko luhoma katagigwa ukwenu kena nyono ikufungha, kosoko kamanya fina ugele wakwe mukefu!”
66012013	Hambiya ugele dijoka dikamanye fina ditagigwa hasi ye chilunga, hodikonga kumwidasa mwanamuke yuya yeleke imwana we chigosi.
66012014	Ninga mwanamuke yuya hakenghigwa mabawa meli ge dinumba dikulu uleke yapululuke kulawa hedijoka mpaka kunyika ku a hanhu hoyekiligwe yekale na kwinghigwa chakudiya kwa minyaka midatu na minyesi mutandatu.
66012015	Kamei dijoka hodilafa kulawa mumulomo wakwe meji kunyuma ye mwanamuke yuya, meji gaya hagowa kifana lwanda uleke gamukome kwa kunywa munghabu.
66012016	Ninga iisi hoikwija na kumutasa imwanamuke iisi hagubula mulomo wakwe na kuyonywa ameji gose dijoka godyalafile kumulomo wakwe.
66012017	Dijoka hadisuha ne mwanamuke yuya hadiluta na kulewa nghondo ne wanagwe kuwaya awakukola amalagiso ge Mulungu na kuhomelela muchanhya ya Yesu.
66012018	Kamei dijoka hodikwima munghingi, kusanga ye bahali.
66013001	Kamei hanyona ikala dyenuke kulawa mubahali dine mahembe ikumi na matwi mufungate, chila ihembe dina kofiya ya chindewa na isina dya kutofula muchanhya yakwe.
66013002	Na dikala diya dyonyonile dikifana duma, migulu yakwe kifana migulu ya idubu, na dilomo dyakwe dikifana ilomo dya simba, kamei idijoka hodidingha dikala diya udaha ana nghofiya yakwe ye chidewa na ludole mukulu.
66013003	Ditwi dyakwe dimonga dyoneka kifana dina ilonda ikulu dya kukoma, ninga dilonda dyakwe diya hadihona, na ichilunga chose hochidyandamila dikala diya kwa majumo.
66013004	Hawadifugamila dijoka diya, kosoko hadingigwa udaha wakwe kulawa kwe dikala, howodifuga dikala wakugamba, “Nonani yafanile gweye go dikala kahi nani yakudaha kitowa na gweye?”
66013005	Dikala hodikwinghigwa mulomo na kubwata mbuli sa kitogola na kutofula, hadilekeligwa konesa udaha wakwe kwa minyesi makumi mane na mili.
66013006	Hadigubula mulomo wakwe na kulonga matofulo kwe Mulungu, nqa kutofula disina dyakwe na wikalo wakwe na waya wakwikala kulanga.
66013007	Hodikwinghigwa udaha kulewa nghondo na wasunhile kahi hodiwasuma, kahi hadinghigwa udaha kuchila ikabila, chila wanhu, na chila nonga na chila itaifa,
66013008	na wose woile muchilunga wakwija wadifuga, chila munhu imwene disina dyakwe disiwandikigwe muchitabu che Mwana ngholo iyachinjigwe.
66013009	Munhu wowose yena singhutwi yahulike.
66013010	Munhu wowose yanghalondigwa kuwa mutumwa yakuluta kuutumwa; unghakoma kwa ipanga nagwe kuwagila ukomigwe kwa ipanga. Alono no lwinango lwo kufinyilisa ne dihuwi dya wasunhile.
66013011	Kahi hanyona ikala dingi dyasololoka muchilunga; haduwa na mhembe mbili sakifana mhembe sa ngholo na dilonga kifana ijoka.
66013012	Dikugolosa udaha wose wa diya dikala dye nghonga kumwande yakwe, na kuwagolosa we chilunga chose wafuge kwi kala diya dye nghonga, dyahonile dilonda dyakwe dyo kufa.
66013013	Dikugolosa majumo hata kwigala umoto kulawa kulanga kwija kuisi kumwande ya meso ga wanhu.
66013014	Na majumo gaya godyagolosage kumwande ye dikala, dikudanhilisa awekwikala muchilunga, diwalonga wagolosa sisanamu sa diya dikala dyowile na dilonda dyo kukoma dyabulagigwe ne dipanga ninga dikali dyumi,
66013015	hodikwinghigwa udaha kuguma muhe kudisanamu diya dye dikala mpaka kudaha kulonga na kuwagolosa waya awakulema kufuga wachijigwe.
66013016	Na kuwagolosa wanhu wose wadodogi na wakulu, awagoli na wakiwa awaya awatumwa na awasiwetumwa kugumigwa chitangilo mumukono wo kulume ama muchihanga,
66013017	uleke munhu wowose yanghadahe kugula hegu kwambasa, ninga ayuya du yene ichitangilo chicho che dikala diya ama ihesabu ye disina dyakwe.
66013018	Ayino ikuhananga ubala: Ayuya yena misungu yamanye ihesabu ye dikala, kosoko ni hesabu ya chimunhumunhu. Ihesabu yakwe ni magana mutandatu na makumi mutandatu na mutandatu.
66014001	Kamei hanilanga, na hahowa na Mwanangholo, yemile Mwitunda dya Sayuni! Hamwedu ne mwene wema wanhu figulu igana dimwedu na makumi mane na ine awowile ne disina dyakwe kamei ne disina dye Babakwe diwandikigwe mufihanga fyawo.
66014002	Hanihulika ijwi kulawa kulanga kifana ijwi dya meji mengi, na kifana ijwi ikulu dikudidima, dijwi diya dyonahulike hadyuwa kifana wanhu wakutowa fibwalimbwa fyawo,
66014003	wakwimba lwimbo lusha kumwande ye fiyumbe fine ifyumi na kumwande ya wasehe. Kwichaka munhu wowose yadahile kifusa kwimba ulwimbo uya ninga awaya du figulu igana dimwedu na makumi mane na wane awene awahonyigwe kulawa kuyisi.
66014004	Nowaya awasikibanile ne wihi we dihabwa, kosoko ni mabikila; awano no wamwandamile Mwanangholo kokose koyalutile. Wahonyigwa kulawa muwanhu wowe kifana mamudyo ge nghonga kwe Mulungu na kwe Mwanangholo,
66014005	na usoneka udasi wowose mumilomo yawo; wanhu wechaka ilema.
66014006	Kahi hanyona malaika yakupululuka muchiligati cho ulanga, kena mbuli swanu ye majuwa gose yakuhubili kuwaya awomi woile muchilunga kwa chila itaifa na ikabila, nonga na chila wanhu.
66014007	Yakulonga kwa ijwi ikulu lugano kugamba, “Mogoheni Mulungu kahi mwingheni itunyo, kosoko ugele we uliganiso wakwe wija; kahi mufugeni imwene yombile isi ne ulanga, bahali ne nhyoko sa meji.”
66014008	Kame malaika yungi wa keli, hakandamila, yakugamba, “Kugwa, kugwa, agweye Babeli go mukulu mugima! Iyawagolose mataifa wonywe difayi ye nyono ye dihabwa dyakwe.”
66014009	Kamei malaika yungi wa kadatu, hakawandamila, yakujoja kwa ijwi ikulu lugano yakugamba, “Imunhu wowose yakudaha kudifuga, dikala ne isanamu yakwe na kuhokela ichitangilo muchihanga chakwe ama mumukono wakwe,
66014010	naye yakwenda yonywe idifayi ya inyono ye Mulungu na yakwenda yalakasigwe na umoto we chibiliti kumwande ye malaika wasunhile na kumwande ya Mwanangholo.
66014011	Na umosi wo kulakala kwawo ukuluta kulanga minyaka na minyaka, na wasikubwihila misi na chilo wawo wafugile dikala na isanamu yakwe, na chila munhu iyakuhokela ichitangilo che disina dyakwe.”
66014012	Aluno ni lwinango lwa kufinyilisa, kosoko ya wasunhile awaya awakolile amalagiso ge Mulungu na dihuwi dya Yesu.
66014013	Honihulika kahi ijwi kulawa kulanga dikugamba, “Wandika dino fina. Ibeka awafile, awakufila mwihuwi dye Mundewa kulawa hambiya,” Heye yakulonga Imuhe, “Wabwihile kulawa mutabu yawo, kosoko nhenda sawo siligana nawo.”
66014014	Kamei hanyona, langa hahowa na ifunde ijelu, na yekale mwifunde didyo munhu yafane Mwana wa Munhu, kena nghofiya ya sahabu mwitwi dyakwe, na sengo nghali lugano mumukono wakwe!
66014015	Malaika yungi hakalawa kulawa kwihekalu, yakumwinanga yuya yekale mwifunde dijelu kwa ijwi ikulu lugano yakugamba, “Konga kusenga ne isengo yako ugole, kosoko ichigele cho kugola chifika, na kosoko indiya yokugola muisi ifulusa kukangala.”
66014016	Kamei ayuya yekale mwifunde, hoyoikubita isengo yakwe muchilunga, na fyechilunga hofigoligwa.
66014017	Kamei malika yungi hakalawanisa kulawa mwihekalu dya kulanga, naye hakakola sengo nghali lugano.
66014018	Kamei malaika yungi kahi hakalawanisa kulawa hefugilo, hakowa malaika yena udaha mukulu muchanhya ye moto, hoyomwinanga kwa ijwi ikulu ayuy yowile ne sengo inghali, “Guma isengo yako kudumula imisabibu yuwile mumigunda ye misabibu muisi kosoko sisabibu sifulusa kwifa.”
66014019	Baho iamalaika hoyotema ne sengo yakwe kulunda sisabibu sose muchilunga na kusiguma ahanhu hagolosigwe kukamila sisabibu ne inyono ye Mulungu;
66014020	na hokukamila sisabibu hahowa kunje ye ikaya, na isakame kulawa ahanhu haya hokukamila hoikwitika kifana lwanda lukulu lwa meji na kwingila hasi yendeifika musingo, kamei utali wakwe kifana maili magana meli.
66015001	Kamei hanyona chitangilo chingi kulanga, chikulu na cha ijumo, malaika mufungate na magayo mufungate ge kumalagisa, kosoko ya wawo inyono ye Mulungu imemelekela.
66015002	Na hanyona chinhu kifana bahali ifanile chiyoo chihangile na umoto, na awaya wadisumile dikala diya ne sanamu yakwe ne hesabu ye disina dyakwe, hawema munghingi ye bahali ye chiyoo wena fibwalimbwa fye Mulungu mumikono yawo.
66015003	Wakwimba lwimbo lwa Musa, mutogomi we Mulungu, na kwimba lwimbo lwe Mwanangholo kugamba: “Singhenda sako nghulu na sa majumo, Mundewa Mulungu Mukulu! Sinjila sako siliganila na sa chawelu, Mundewa wa mataifa!
66015004	Mundewa, nonani inghakwenda yogohe na kuditunya disina dyako? Kosoko agweye muhala no musunhile. Mataifa gose gokwija na kufuga hamwande yako, kosoko uliganiso wako ugubuligwa.”
66015005	Gakaloke gano hanilanga kahi na kona, dihekalu dye dihema dye uhomelesi dikumuligwa kulanga,
66015006	kulawa umo mwihekalu hawa malaika mufungate wena fililo mufungate wena suke sifanile bafuta sikwakaika na mufifa fyawo wafala mikanda ya sahabu.
66015007	Na yumwendu we fiyumbe ifyumi hakawengha malaika mufungate mabakuli ga sahabu gamemile inyono ye Mulungu ye kwikala majuwa gose,
66015008	na dihekalu hadimemesigwa mosi kulawa mwitunyo dye Mulungu na kulawa muludole lwakwe, na hechaka munhu yadahile kwingila kwihekalu kugati mpaka fililo mufungate fuya fya malaika mufungate fihele.
66016001	Kamei hanihulika ijwi ikulu kulawa kwihekalu dikuwagamba amalaika mufungate, “Luteni muketile kuchilunga amabakuli mufungate ge inyono ye Mulungu.”
66016002	Imalaika we nghonga hakaluta na kwitila dibakuli dyakwe muchilunga, awanhu hawapata malonda gehile awaya wose woile ne chitangilo che dikala ne wafugile isanamu yakwe.
66016003	Imalaika wa keli hoyokwitila dibakuli dyakwe mubahali, bahali hayuwa kifana sakame ye munhu yafile, na chila chowile umo hochikufa.
66016004	Imalaika wa kadatu haketila dibakuli dyakwe musisanda na musinhyoko, kamei hoikuwa sakame lugano.
66016005	Na hanihulika malaika we chililo cha meji yakugamba, “Agweye gouliganile mukuliganisa kwako, Agweyo musunhile, Agwe gowi baho, na wowile baho, kosoko kusiliganisa simbuli sino;
66016006	kosoko hawetila sakame ya wasunhile na wagonesi, na gweye kuwengha isakame kunywa. Nonheifo iwawagile!”
66016007	Kamei hanihulika dihekalu dikubidula kugamba, “Heye, Agweye Mundewa Mulungu, Mukulu mudaha wa fyose, uliganisi wako ni wachawelu na uliganila!”
66016008	Imalaika wa kane haketila dibakuli dyakwe mwijuwa, hodikuwa na ukali lugano hodisoma wanhu kwa moto,
66016009	wanhu howolakala lugano ne dililimba dyo moto, ninga hawaliga disina dye Mulungu, iyene udaha mumalilo gano na hawalambile hegu kumwingha itunyo
66016010	Imalaika wa shano haketila dibakuli dyakwe muchanhya ye digoda dye undewa we dikala diya, na muundewa wakwe wose homubanika lugano na kwingila chisa; wanhu hawaluma malimi gawo kwa usungu mukulu,
66016011	na kumuliga Mulungu wa kulanga kosoko yo usungu wawo na malonda gawo, ninga wasalambile singhenda sawo.
66016012	Imalaika wa mutandatu, haketila dibakuli dyakwe mulwanda uya mukulu lwa Efulata, na meji gakwe hoganyala, uleke kugolosa njila sa sa kuloka wandewa kulawa kundawilo ye dijuwa.
66016013	Kamei hanyona mhepo ndatu sihile kifana mabula sikulawa kumulomo we dijoka ne kumulomo we dikala na kumulomo we mugonesi yuya wo udasi.
66016014	Asino no simhepo isikutogoma fitangilo, fikuluta kuwandewa we chilunga chose, kuwagala hamwedu kwa nyitowa nghondo mwijuwa diya dikulu dye nghondo ye Mulungu Mukulu.
66016015	“Langa, nikwija kifana imuhiji nomayakwija hechilo! Ibeka ayuya yakwikala meso na yafalile suse, yanghoneke fina kechaka suke yanghapate chinyala.”
66016016	Howalunda hamwedu hanhu hakwinangwa munonga ya Chiyebulaniya Halimagedoni.
66016017	Imalaika we mufungate haketila dibakuli dyakwe mumheho muchanhya, kamei dijwi ikulu hodilawa kulawa kwihekalu, kwigoda dyo undewa dikugamba, “Ifuluka!”
66016018	Hakuwa na lumwemwe lukumulika, ujelu, kudidima na disingisi ikulu lugano.
66016019	Dikaya dikulu hoditemanhuligwa sandi ndatu na sikaya sa mataifa hosikugwa na Mulungu hakagelegela dikaya dikulu dya Babeli, kudigolosa dunywe na kumalagisa ichikombe che inyono ye Mulungu.
66016020	Chila chisiwa hachitija kutali, na hahowa hechaka cha itunda dyodyose dyasigale;
66016021	na ifula nghulu ya mawe ga usito wa kilo makumi mashano hogowalagalila wanhu kulawa kulanga, mpaka wanhu hawamuliga Mulungu kosoko ya digayo dye ifula ya mawe, adino haduwa igayo dya kogoha lugano.
66017001	Kamei yumwedu wa malaika waya yowile ne mabakuli mufungate hoyokwija na kunigamba, “Wije nikwenda nikonese uliganiso we mwanamuke we dihabwa dikulu iyekale mumeji mengi,
66017002	imwene hata awandewa we isi wagenda naye, na ugimbi wakwe wo kugenda na wagose wekale muisi walewa kosoko ya iyo.”
66017003	Kamei hakanilonda kwa muhe, mpaka kunyika, na uko honikona mwanamuke gowa hamwedu ne ikewe dimonga idunghu dimemile masina go kutofula, dikala diya haduwa na matwi mufungate, na mhembe ikumi.
66017004	Mwanamuke hakafala isuke dya usulunge na idunghudunghu, dihambigwe na fihambo fya sahabu na mawe ga maliho makulu, na lulu kamei mumukono wakwe kakola chikombe cha sahabu chimememile maligo na masinhu gehile na uwafu wose we dihabwa dyakwe,
66017005	na muchihanga chakwe mwanamuke yuya hamwandikigwa isina dya chifiso, dikugamba, “Babeli mukulu, ing'inamunhu mukulu we dihabwa na gehile gose ge chilunga.”
66017006	Hanyona fina mwanamuke yuya hakalewa na sakame ya wasunhile, ne sakama ya wahomelesi wa Yesu.
66017007	Ninga malaika yuya hoyonigamba, “Nhani ukujumha? Nokutamila ichifiso che mwanamuke yuno, ne dikala diya idine matwi mufungate ne simhembe ikumi.
66017008	Adiya dikala dyowonile haduwaga uko, ninga hambiya dyakwichaka, ndyo dikwenda kukwila kulawa kwikolongo dya kusimu na kuluta kukwangamila. Na awanhu wa muchilunga awene masina gawo gasiwandikwe muchitabu cho uwumi kulawa mukumbigwa chilunga, wojumha ugele fowakwija wakona dikala, kosoko haduwa uko na hambiya dyakwichaka, kahi dokwija.”
66017009	Mbuli ino ikuhananga misungu na ubala mukulu! Amatwi gaya mufungate gowonile ni matunda mufungate goyekale mwanamuke yuya; kahi hena wandewa mufungate,
66017010	muwawo washano wafa, yumwedu yekali mumi, na wamonga wekali kwija; na foyakwija kokwikala chipisi chiguhi du.
66017011	Na kwa diya dikala idyowile uko kame hambiya dyakwichaka ni dya munane mugati ya waya mufungate, nadyo dikuluta kukwagilia.
66017012	“Na simhembe ikumi sowonile, ni wandewa ikumi awekali kuhokela undewa wawo, ninga wohokela na kuwa wandewa kwa disaa dimwedu muhala, hamwedu na diya dikala.
66017013	Awano wa hamwedu, nawo wakudingha diya dikala ludole na udaha,
66017014	wakwenda wagolose nghondo ne Mwanangholo, ne Mwanangholo yakwenda yawasume, kosoko imwene ni Mundewa wa wandewa wose na Mukulu wa wakulu wose, na waya woile ne mwene wakwinangwa wasaguligwe na awakuhuwilika.”
66017015	Na hoyonigamba, “Ameji gaya gowonile, ahanhu haya howonile yekale imwanamuke yuya we dihabwa, ni wanhu na matewa na mataifa na nonga.
66017016	Na simhembe siya ikumi sowonile, awene na dikala womudesekela; womugolosa mukiwa na wakwenda wamuleke yemwene, kahi ye mwasi wodiya inyama yakwe na kumusoma mumoto.
66017017	Kosoko Mulungu kaguma gano mumimoyo yawo, kumemelesa agaya goyahanange kugolosa, kwa kifumilisa hamwedu na kudingha dikala diya undewa wawo, mpka mbuli se Mulungu simemelekele.
66017018	Imwanamuke wowumonile, ni dikaya diya dikulu dikulongosigwa na wandewa we chilunga.”
66018001	Gakaloke gag, hanyona malaika yungi yakulawa kulanga kena udaha lugano, ichilunga hochikwakaika kosoko ye ditunyo dyakwe.
66018002	Hakenanga kwa ijwi ikulu lugano kugamba, “Dyugwa, dyugwa dya, dikaya dikulu dya Babeli! digaluka lwikalo lwa simhepo, njila ya kugenda chila mamuhe gehile, njila ya kugendela chila idege dihile, njila ya kugenda chila ikewe dihile.
66018003	Kosoko amataifa gose galewesigwa idifayi yakwe we dihabwa na wandewa we chilunga wagendile naye, na wachulusi we chilunga wagaluka wagoli kosoko ye inyikala yakwe ye kibwedesa.”
66018004	Kahi hanihulika ijwi dingi kulawa kulanga dikugamba, “Laweni kunje yakwe, wanhu wangu, uleke munghahangile wihi wakwe, hegu kuwa na umwedu naye mufililo fyakwe;
66018005	kosoko uwihi wakwe ulundigwa chilundo chifikile kulanga, na Mulungu kagelegela uwihi wakwe wose.
66018006	Muliheni nheifiya fina foyamuliheni nyenye, kahi muliheni mikangha mili ifanile sinhenda sakwe; mumuhasile mikangha mili muchikombe choyahasile.
66018007	Ifene foyakitogole imwecho na kugolosa dihabwa mwinghe ichipimo chiliganile na kona usungu na kulila, kosoko ku moyo wakwe yakugamba, ‘Aniye namundewa fina malikiya; aniye si na mwigane hata, kahi sikwija nikona chililo.’
66018008	Hambiya malilo gakwe gomwijila ijuwa dimwedu utamu, ndilo ne njala naye kosomigwa mumoto; kosoko imukulu ni Mundewa Mulungu iyakwija yamulamula.”
66018009	Na awandewa we chilunga, wagolose dihabwa na kwikala mubwedelela hamwedu anye, wolila na kuhongesa lugano muchinhya yakwe nomowakwija wakona umosi wo kulakala kwakwe;
66018010	wokwima kutali kosoko ya usungu na magayo ge mwanamuke yuyo, nawo wogamba, “Usungu, usungu agweye go dikaya dikulu dyoludole dya Babeli, ni chipisi cha disaa dimwedu ulamusi ukwija.”
66018011	Na wachulusi we chilunga wakulila kosoko yakwe, kosoko hechaka munhu kahi yakukugula ifinhu fyakwe,
66018012	ikanda dye sahabu, fesa ne mawe ge maliho makulu, suke sa bafuta, samawi, halili na suke ndunghu, na chila fiswanu na finhu figolosigwe na simbali sa simhembe, finhu fya diyombe dikulu, fya mabiki, shaba, chuma, na masambalawe,
66018013	mudalasini, filungo, ubani, manemane, wudi, difayi, mafuta, usage wa ngano, ng'ombe na ngholo, falasi na mikokoteni, na watumwa, nong'amba ifidoga fya wanhu.
66018014	“Isigafu sahuwiligwe ne moyo wako siluta kutali na gweye, na ugoli wose ne ditunyo dyako fifulusa kuleuka ukwako, hafikuya keli!”
66018015	Awachulusi wawo wapatile finhu fyo ugoli kosoko ye imwene wokawakwima kutali kosoko yo kogoha amagayo gakwe wakulila na kuhongesa wakujoja wakugamba,
66018016	“Usungu, usungu, ikaya iya inghulu, ifasigwe suke swanu, sowile ne udunghudunghu, ihambigwe ne sahabu, hamwedu ne masambaluwe gakwakaika!
66018017	Kosoko kwa chipisi chiguhi ugoli wose uya wagilila!” Na awena simeli, na wose wakugenda mumeji na awachulusi wakwe wose wokwima kutali
66018018	ma kulila kwa usungu fowakona umosi ukumusoma, “Hena kaya yaki ifanile ikaya ino inghulu?”
66018019	Howokitilila diluli mumatwi gawo, fowakulila na kuhongesa, na kugamba, Usungu mukulu, usungu mukulu ikaya iya inghulu, umo nomowanhu wose wapatile ugoli kwa ugoli wakwe! Kosoko kwa chipisi chimwedu kahi chiguhi fyose fyagilila.
66018020	Bwedelela gweye Go ulanga kosoko yakwe, anyenye muwasunhile na muwatumigwa na wagonesi!
66018021	Kamei malaika yumonga we ludole kenula iwe difanile iwe dya lwala lukulu na kudikubita mubahali na kugamba, “Nheifo nofonikwenda nikukubite agweye go dikaya dikulu dya Babeli na nghukwija ukoneka keli;
66018022	kamei ijwi dye wakutowa ifibwalimbwa ne figoma, awekutowa sifuluti na magunda gasikwenda gahulikike kahi ukwako;
66018023	ujelu we itaa usikwenda woneke ukwako kahi, ninga dijwi dya bwana halusi au bibi halusi disikwenda dihulikike ukwako; awachulusi wako na wowile wakulu we chilunga na wanhu wose hawadanhilisigwa na uganga wako.”
66018024	Umwakwe umo hayoneka sakame ya wagonesi na ya wasunhile na wose wakomigwe muchilunga.
66019001	Gakaloke gano, honihulika chinhu, chowile kifana ijwi, matewa ga wanhu kulanga wakugamba, “Haleluya! uhonya na ditunyo na udaha wina Mulungu wetu,
66019002	kosoko uliganisi wakwe ni wa chawelu na uliganila, kumuliganisa iwe dihabwa dikulu, iyabanile iisi yose ne dihabwa dyakwe, na kumulamula imwene kuligana ne isakame ya watumigwa wakwe.”
66019003	Kahi hawajija wakugamba, “Haleluya! Umosi kulawa umwakwe ukufililika majuwa gose.”
66019004	Na wasehe makumi meli na ine na ifyumbigwe fine ifyumi hawogwa hasi kumufuga Mulungu, yekale mwigoda dye undewa wakugamba, “Hano. Haleluya!”
66019005	Na kulawa kudigoda dyo undewa hodihulikika dijwi dikugamba, “Yatunyigwe Mulungu wetu, anye moose muwatogomi wakwe, anye mukumogoha, wadodo na wakulu.”
66019006	Kamei hanihulika chinhu chowile kifana chowe cha itewa ikulu, kifana ijwi dya meji mengi, na kifana ijwi na madidimo ga ludole, gakugamba, “Haleluya! Kosoko iMundewa wetu Mulungu Imukulu no yakudima.
66019007	Haya chisekelele na kumwinula na kumwingha ditunyo, kosoko utole we Mwana we nholo ufika, na ibibi halusi wakwe kafulusa kitandila
66019008	hoyokwinghigwa kufala suke swanu sa bafuta njelu sikwakaika kahi swanu” kosoko sisuke siswanu se bafuta no sinhenda siswanu sa wasunhile.
66019009	Kamei imalaika hoyonigamba, “Wandika dino: Wamoteswe no waya awegonekwe kuchakudiya che halusi cha Mwana ngholo.” Hakanigamba, “Asino ni mbuli sa chawelu se Mulungu.”
66019010	Kamei hanugwa hamigulu kumufuga, ninga hakanigamba, “Unghagolose nheifo aniye namutogomi miyago hamwedu nagwe, na wanduguso wose awena uhomelesi wa Yesu mufuge iMulungu! Kosoko uhomelesi wa Yesu ni muhe wa ugonesi.”
